Inkohliso yaseBerners Street yenziwa umlobi uTheodore Hook eWestminster (manje eyingxenye yeLondon) ngo-1810. Ngemva kwamasonto ambalwa ezilungiselela wenza ukubheja ngokuzenzakalelayo nomngane wakhe ukuthi angashintsha noma iyiphi indawo ibe ikheli okukhulunywa ngalo kakhulu eLondon. UHook wachitha amasonto ayisithupha ethumela izincwadi eziphakathi kwenkulungwane nezine kubahwebi namabhizinisi e-oda ukulethwa kwezimpahla zabo nezinkonzo ku-54 Berners Street, eWestminster, ngezikhathi ezihlukahlukene ngomhla ka-27 November 1810. Abantu abaningana abaziwayo nabo bamenywa ukuba bavakashele ikheli, kuhlanganise nosihlalo BeBhange LaseNgilandi kanye Nenkampani Yase-East India, uMbusi WaseLondon Mayorce kanye noMbusi waseGlou Mayorce. 

UHook nabangane bakhe baqashe amagumbi endlini ebhekene nenombolo 54 ukuze babuke okuqhubekayo. Abashanela bakashimula baqala ukufika ekhelini ngo-5:00 ekuseni ngalolo suku, balandelwa amakhulu abameleli bemisebenzi yezandla namabhizinisi amaningana, kuhlanganise nabadayisi, abangcwabi, abadayisa ukudla, abadayisi, ababhaki, abapheki bekhekhe nezingcweti zokudansa; ukulethwa kwezimpahla bekuhlanganisa izitho zomzimba, ifenisha, amalahle, amakhekhe omshado, ukudla, iziphuzo kanye nebhokisi. Amaphoyisa abizwe ukuthi azozama ukulawula isixuku kodwa awakwazanga ukususa umgwaqo kwaze kwaba ngemva kokutheleka kokugcina kwezivakashi ngo-5:00 ntambama: izisebenzi zasendlini ezazicabanga ukuthi zizohlolelwa umsebenzi. 

U-Hook wayengaziwa ngaleso sikhathi, kodwa wavuma ukuzibandakanya kwakhe kunoveli ye-semi-autobiographical eyanyatheliswa eminyakeni engamashumi amabili nanhlanu ngemva komcimbi. Umkhonyovu waphindwa kulo lonke elaseBrithani naseParis, waphinde waxoxwa esiteji, ngengoma nangabadwebi bamakhathuni. 

Isendlalelo kanye nokwakhiwa 
kwe-Etching of Hook eneminyaka engaba ngu-22. Ugqoka ingubo ehloniphekile futhi ubheka ngqo kumbukeli. 
Theodore Hook, umenzi wenkohliso, c. Ngo-1810 
uTheodore Hook wayengumbhali wama-comic opera kanye nama-farces esiteji kanye nombhali wamanoveli amaningana. Wayenohlangothi olubi emvelweni yakhe futhi wayaziwa njengomgiliqili nomkhohlisi.[1] Isazi-mlando uJudith Flanders siphawula ukuthi wayaziwa kakhulu ngamahlaya akhe awusizo njengoba ayaziwa ngokubhala kwakhe.[2] Ngesikhathi sokukhohlisa kukaBerners Street wayeneminyaka engama-22 ubudala. 

Ukuhlelwa kukaHook ngale nkohliso kwaqala ngo-October 1810, emasontweni ayisithupha ngaphambi komcimbi, futhi wayenabangane ababili ababezomsiza ngakho.[4] Akwaziwa ukuthi obani ababehambisana naye—owesilisa nowesifazane oyedwa—kodwa kucatshangwa ukuthi omunye wabo kamuva waba umlingisi odumile.[5] Inombolo enkulu yezincwadi yathunyelwa kubahwebi, abahlinzeki kanye nabaziwayo kusetshenziswa izaba ezahlukene; izilinganiso zenani lezinhlamvu ziyahlukahluka kusukela "okungenani kwenkulungwane"[6] kuya ezinkulungwaneni ezine.

Izaba ezisetshenzisiwe zashintsha kuye ngokuthi ubani owayethintwa, kodwa bonke babeneziqondiso ezifanayo: ukubiza uNksz Tottenham, umhlali we-54 Berners Street. abanye bayalela ukuba kuthuthwe, bethi "ucela ukuthi i-post-chaise kanye [namahhashi] amane kube sekhaya ... ukuze amdlulisele esigabeni sokuqala ebheke eBath". Amanothi kosomabhizinisi afundeka ngokuthi “wayefisa ukukhuluma naye ngezindaba ezibalulekile”;[8] inguqulo eyathunyelwa kothisha bomdanso yabacela “ukuba bambize kusasa, phakathi kwehora lesibili nelesithathu, njengoba efisa ukuba amadodakazi akhe athole iziyalezo”.[9] Kuthunyelwe izincwadi kusihlalo weBhange lase-England kanye ne-East India Company zibacela ukuthi bashayele ukuze bezwe imininingwane yokukhwabanisa okuthinta izinhlangano zabo. UMbusi waseGloucester wathunyelwa inothi emcela ukuba ahambele umbhede wokufa womgcini womndeni. 

NgoNovemba 1810 Hook nomngane babehamba behla ngoBerners Street lapho ekhomba, ebonakala nje ngokungahleliwe, endlini engunombolo 54 futhi wabheja ukuthi angenza indawo ikheli okukhulunywa ngalo kakhulu eLondon. Umngani wakhe wamkhwelisa ebhejini kanti ibheja yayisethelwe igwinya elilodwa. 

Isigameko 
Isigcawu esicatshangelwe kusukela ngosuku lokukhohlisa. UBerners Street ugcwele amakalishi, osomabhizinisi, abadayisi, abafana abadilivayo kanye nababukele. 
I-Berners Street hoax 
Hook nabangane bakhe babeqashe amagumbi endlini ebhekene no-54 Berners Street ukuze babone okwenzekayo ngosuku.[2][13] Ngo-5:00 ekuseni ngomhla zingama-27 kuNovemba 1810 uhide lwabashanela bakashimula bangqongqoza emnyango wenombolo 54, bethi babethunyiwe. Balandelwa inqwaba yezinqola zamalahle, ziletha impahla yazo ezikhumulweni zemikhumbi zasePaddington; ngaso leso sikhathi, kwaqhamuka ababhaki abayishumi nambili bezoletha amakhekhe omshado anemininingwane eminingi, kulandelwa uchungechunge lwabakhi bezicathulo.[5][6][14] Ngokwe-Times, alandelwa “izimpahla zokugqoka izigqoko ezithwele izinqola, izitho zomzimba, ama-pianoforte, ilineni, ubucwebe kanye nayo yonke enye incazelo yefenisha, [eyayi]fakwe eduze ngangokunokwenzeka emnyango weNo. Njengoba igagasi ngalinye elisha lifika, isixuku esasizungeze le ndawo sasikhula, njengoba abaningi babehlale bebukele ukuthi ubani owayezofika. Osihlalo BeBhange LaseNgilandi kanye Nenkampani Yase-East India, kanye noMbusi WaseGloucester, bonke bafike emini, kanjalo nomngcwabi owayephethe ibhokisi lomngcwabo elenziwe ezilinganisweni zikaNkk Tottenham. 

Imephu yase-Westminster enophawu olubonisa indawo ye-54 Berners StreetMap yase-Westminster enophawu olubonisa indawo engu-54 Berners Street54 Berners Street 
Indawo eseduze ye-54 Berners Street, London
Ngaphandle kwabathengisi bezinhlanzi abangamashumi amane—abafika nama-lobster nama-cod—nabadayisi abangamashumi amane, ngamunye enomlenze wenyama yemvu, kwakukhona abapheki bekhekhe abangamashumi amahlanu nama-raspberry tarts angu-2 500. UJoshua Smith, iNkosi iMeya yaseLondon—egqoke ingubo egcwele futhi egibele inqola yakhe esemthethweni—wafika, kodwa akazange ame. Kunalokho waya eNkantolo yeMantshi yaseMarlborough Street ukuze athumele amaphoyisa endaweni yesigameko.[5][10][18] Ngokombiko we-Times, njengoba la maphoyisa efika kuBerners Street athola “amadoda ayisithupha ayizidlakela ephethe isitho somzimba, ezungezwe abathwali bewayini abanezimvume, abagundi bezinwele befake amawigi, abenzi be-mantua bephethe amabhokisi okubhendi, [kanye] nodokotela bamehlo bephethe izinto ezihlukahlukene zomsebenzi wabo”.[15] I-Morning Post iphinde yabika ngabalandelayo ababekhona: "abadwebi, abadwebi bezinyo, abapenda abancane, abadwebi bazo zonke izincazelo, abadayisi, abangcwabi, abadayisa ukudla, abadayisi, ama-post-chaise, amakhoshi okuzila, izinkukhu, onogwaja, amajuba, &c".[19] Ezama ukunqanda lesi simo, amaphoyisa avimbe izinhlangothi zombili zomgwaqo, kodwa abantu babelokhu befika lapho bezoqashwa, okuhlanganisa, ngo-5:00 ntambama, inqwaba yezisebenzi zasendlini, zonke ezazicabanga ukuthi zizohlolelwa umsebenzi.[15][20] Akuphelanga sikhathi esingakanani kwase kuhwalala izivakashi zayeka ukuqhamuka nezinkumbi zabantu zahlakazeka. Amaphoyisa 

ase-Aftermath 
athungatha isigebengu futhi anikezwa umklomelo, kodwa kwanhlanga zimuka nomoya.[21] UHook wacabanga ukuthi kuwukuhlakanipha ukushiya idolobha elikhulu futhi wahlala amasonto ambalwa emaphandleni.[6] Ngo-1812 uHook wasolwa ngokukhohlisa; wavuma ngakho encwadini yakhe ye-semi-autobiographical yango-1835 ethi Gilbert Gurney 

[T]nakhu akukho okumnandi - yini enye eyenza umphumela kuBerner's Street? Ngiyindoda - ngikwenzile ... kopisha ihlaya, futhi liyayeka ukuba linye; - noma yisiphi isiphukuphuku singalingisa isibonelo esake sabekwa - kodwa ngokuqondene nomcabango nokuklama, ngicabanga ukuthi lokho bekuphelele. 

Inkohliso yaphindwa nakwamanye amadolobha aseBrithani kanye naseParis.[23] Yaba umthombo wogqozi lwama-comic ballads namakhathuni futhi kwakhulunywa ngayo kuma-pantomime iminyaka eminingana.[24] Ngemva kokufa kukaHook ngo-1841 umngane wakhe uNancy Matthews—unkosikazi womlingisi uCharles Matthew—wathi kwakungeyena uHook owayebangela leli nkohliso kodwa “insizwa esencane, manje ... engomunye wabefundisi abaqine kakhulu embusweni”.[2] Uqhube wathi nakuba uHook engazange enze inkohliso ku-Berners Street, ngaphambili wayeke wenza umgilingwane ofanayo esikalini esincane ku-Bedford Street. 

Akukaze kube nencazelo yokuthi kungani kwenziwa umkhonyovu, noma ngokukhethwa kukaNkk Tottenham—owesifazane ocebile onokuma okuhle emphakathini—njengesisulu sezehlakalo.[24][7] U-Graeme Harper, ebhala ku-Oxford Dictionary of National Biography ngo-2008, uthi ukukhetha kwenziwa ngokungahleliwe.[1] Intatheli nombhali uRobert Chambers wabhala ngo-1879 ukuthi kwakukhona intukuthelo phakathi kukaNkk Tottenham noHook nabangane bakhe, kodwa akazange anikeze imininingwane.




u-heodore Edward Hook (22 Septhemba 1788 - 24 Agasti 1841) wayengungqondongqondo nomqambi wesiNgisi futhi kafushane eyisisebenzi sikahulumeni eMauritius. Waziwa kakhulu ngamahlaya akhe angokoqobo, ikakhulukazi inkohliso yaseBerners Street ngo-1810. Iposikhadi lokuqala emhlabeni latholwa nguHook ngo-1840; cishe wazithumelela yona. 

Umlando 
wempilo yasekuqaleni 
uHook wazalelwa eCharlotte Street, eBedford Square, eLondon. Uyise, uJames Hook (1746–1827), wayengumqambi; umfowabo omdala, owayebizwa nangokuthi uJames Hook (1771–1828), waba yiDini yaseWorcester. 

Uchithe unyaka e-Harrow School futhi ngemuva kwalokho waphothula umatikuletsheni eNyuvesi yase-Oxford. Uyise wakuthokozela ukubukisa ngezipho zomculo nezemethrikhi zomfana, kanti uTheodore owayesengaphambili waba isilwane esifuywayo segumbi eliluhlaza. Lapho eneminyaka engu-16, ehlangene noyise, uthole impumelelo emangalisayo nge-The Soldier's Return, i-opera yamahlaya, futhi yalandela uchungechunge lwezinhlelo ezithandwayo noJohn Liston noCharles Mathews, kuhlanganise noTekeli. 

UHook wabe eseba ihlaya elidlalayo kanye nehlaya elisebenzayo elaziwa kakhulu ngenkohliso yaseBerners Street ngo-1810 lapho ahlela khona inqwaba yabahwebi, nabagqamile njengeNkosi Mayor yaseLondon, uMbusi weBhange LaseNgilandi, uSihlalo we-East India Company kanye noDuke waseGloucester ukuthi bavakashele uNkk Tottenham e-54 Berners Street ukuze anqobe enkulumweni yendlu enkulu. isonto. 

Enye i-prank ephawulekayo ye-Hook yadlalwa kumlingisi uRobert ("Romeo") Coates, eminyakeni embalwa kamuva. Ngaleso sikhathi iNkosana i-Prince Regent yayiphethe "udumo oludlulele" eCarlton House, kanye noCoates "enkazimulweni yakhe ebulala uShakespeare eHaymarket"; elingisa umbhalo wesandla ka-Chamberlain, uHook wakhiqiza ithikithi "elala ukuba khona kuka-Signor Romeo" futhi, egqoke ingubo ebomvu ebomvu, waletha lesi simemo esithophayo kodwa esiyimbumbulu ku-Coates mathupha. UHook walinda ukuze abukele u-Coates egibela umcimbi enqoleni yakhe, "elalele konke okucolisekileyo, ngenkemba enesici sedayimane nomoya kaLouis le Grand". U-Coates wamenywa ukuba angene, kodwa ngesikhathi ehlola ithikithi "wabikelwa ngesizotha ukuthi kwenzeke iphutha", wahoxa. Ngemva kokuthumela inqola yakhe, waphoqeleka ukuthi alinde esitobhini sikaHackney. INkosana, ngokungazi, ihileleke ezenzweni zikaHook, yazisola ngokuthi uCoates wayejikiswe, embona “eyindoda engafanele” futhi ephawula nokuthi “ukuba khona kwakhe kwakungase kujabulise izihambeli eziningi, futhi kwakungeke kulimaze muntu.” UMntwana wathumela unobhala wakhe ngakusasa, wamema uCoates ukuba eze azobheka "amalungiselo nemihlobiso" eyayisamile yonke; UCoates wahamba ngokufanelekile. Kwaphawulwa ukuthi, "ukumenzela ubulungisa", Hook, ekuyilandeni kabusha,"Angikaze ngixoxe indaba ngaphandle kwezimpawu zokuthi uyathinteka. 

Umsebenzi
Wahlala eSt Mary Hall, e-Oxford University, washiya ngemuva kwamatemu amabili ukuze aqhubeke nempilo yakhe yangaphambili. Isipho sakhe sezingoma ezithuthukisayo sathakazelisa u-Prince Regent wakhipha isimemezelo sokuthi kukhona okumele kwenziwe kuHook, owaqokwa waba umgcinimabhuku-jikelele kanye nomgcinimafa waseMauritius ngeholo lika-£2,000 ngonyaka (£142,325; US$194,771 ngokwemibandela yango-2021). Wayeyimpilo nomphefumulo wesiqhingi kusukela ekufikeni kwakhe ngo-Okthoba 1813, kodwa kwatholakala ukushoda okukhulu kuma-akhawunti we-treasury ngo-1817, futhi waboshwa futhi walethwa eNgilandi ngecala lobugebengu. Isamba esingaba ngu-£12,000 (£1,054,500; US$1.44 million ngokwemibandela yango-2021) sikhishwe iphini lesikhulu, futhi uHook wathweswa icala. 


Hook, c. Ngo-1810 
Ngesikhathi sokucutshungulwa kwebhodi lokucwaningwa kwamabhuku, wayehlala ngokucashile futhi ezinakekela ngokubhalela omagazini namaphephandaba. Ngo-1820, wethula iphephandaba uJohn Bull, iqhawe leToryism ephezulu kanye nomshushisi ononya weNdlovukazi uCaroline. Ukugxekwa okuhlakaniphile kanye ne-invective engenaluzwela kuvikele ukusakazwa okukhulu, futhi iHook yathola, ngonyaka wokuqala okungenani, imali engenayo engu-£2,000. Waboshwa nokho okwesibili ngenxa yesikweletu sakhe kuhulumeni, angenzanga mzamo wokusikhokha. 

Ngenkathi evalelwe endlini yesiponji kusukela ngo-1823 kuya ku-1825, wabhala imiqulu eyisishiyagalolunye yezindaba kamuva eyaqoqwa ngaphansi kwesihloko esithi Izinkulumo Nezenzo (1824-1828). Ekuqaleni kwawo-1820, wasiza umculi uMichael Kelly ukuba ahlanganise Inkumbulo yakhe, ehlanganisa imininingwane yokusebenza noMozart. Eminyakeni engu-23 esele yokuphila kwakhe, wakhipha imiqulu engu-38 ngaphandle kwezihloko, ama-squibs nemidwebo. Amanoveli akhe anezigaba ezijwayelekile zokulandisa okuhlazisayo kanye nesithombe esicacile. Bahlanganisa uMaxwell (1830), isithombe somngane wakhe uMfundisi E. Cannon; Uthando Nokuziqhenya (1833); i-autobiographical uGilbert Gurney (1835) kanye noGurney Married (1838); UJack Brag (1837) noPeregrine Bunce (1842). Akazange awuqedele umsebenzi wokuphila komuntu kaCharles Mathews. Inoveli yakhe yokugcina kwakungu-Births, Marriages and Deaths (1839). 

Iposikhadi elidala kunawo wonke emhlabeni lathunyelwa ku-Hook ngo-1840, [1] liphethe isitembu sikaPenny Black. Kungenzeka ukuthi u-Hook wadala futhi wathumela ikhadi kuye njengehlaya elisebenzayo enkonzweni yeposi, njengoba isithombe siyi-caricature yabasebenzi baseposini. Ngo-2002, ikhadi leposi lathengiswa ngerekhodi elingu-£31,750. 

Kamuva ukuphila nokufa 
Umsebenzi wawusuqalile kakade ukulimaza impilo yakhe lapho uHook ebuyela emikhubeni yakhe yakudala futhi umzamo wesikhathi eside wokuhlanganisa imboni kanye nokuqothulwa kwaphumela ekuvumeni ukuthi wenziwa esikhwameni, engqondweni nasemzimbeni, futhi, ekugcineni. Washonela ekhaya eFulham ngomhla zingama-24 kuNcwaba 1841 eneminyaka engama-52. Ifa lakhe lathathwa nguMgcinimafa. Akazange ashade kodwa wayehlala noMary Anne Doughty; babenezingane eziyisithupha.

I-Hook ikhunjulwa njengenye yezibalo ezigqamile kakhulu zezikhathi zaseGeorgia. Ugqugquzele abalingisi bakaLucian Gay encwadini kaBenjamin Disraeli ethi Coningsby kanye noMnu Wagg kuVanity Fair kaThackeray. Isitayela sakhe sadlalwa ngabakwaSmith kumakheli Anqatshiwe (1812). UColeridge umncome ngokuthi "ungumuntu ohlakaniphile njengoDante". 













Ukuze uthole indawo ebanzi yaseLondon, bheka iDolobha laseWestminster. Ukuze uthole okunye ukusetshenziswa, bheka i-Westminster (disambiguation). 
I-Westminster 

Westminster iyindawo enkulu yokuhlala yeDolobha laseWestminster eCentral London, eNgilandi. Isuka eMfuleni iThames iye ku-Oxford Street futhi inezimpawu zomhlaba eziningi ezidumile, okuhlanganisa iSigodlo saseWestminster, iBuckingham Palace, iWestminster Abbey, iWestminster Cathedral, iTrafalgar Square kanye nengxenye enkulu yesikhungo samasiko saseWest End okuhlanganisa nendawo yokuzijabulisa yaseWest End yaseshashalazini. 

Igama (IsiNgisi Esidala: Westmynstre) [1] lisuka encazelweni engakahleleki yesonto le-abbey kanye nenqaba yasebukhosini yaseSt Peter's (Westminster Abbey), entshonalanga yeDolobha laseLondon (kuze kube yiNguquko yamaNgisi kuphinde kube khona i-Eastminster abbey, ngakolunye uhlangothi lweDolobha laseLondon, eMpumalanga End of London). Imvelaphi ye-abbey isukela phakathi kwekhulu lesi-7 nele-10, kodwa yanyukela ekuveleleni kuzwelonke lapho yakhiwa kabusha u-Edward the Confessor ngekhulu le-11. Ngokuthuthukiswa kwesigodlo esidala eduze kwe-abbey, iWestminster ibiyikhaya likahulumeni waseNgilandi kusukela cishe ngo-1200, futhi kusukela ngo-1707 uHulumeni wase-United Kingdom. Ngo-1539, yaba idolobha. 

I-Westminster ivamise ukusetshenziswa njengegama-ntonye ukubhekisa ePhalamende lase-United Kingdom, elihlala esigodlweni saseWestminster. 

I-Geography 
Physical Geography 
IDolobha neNkululeko yase-Westminster kanye nezinye izikhungo zokuphatha zase-Westminster zomlando (ngaphandle kweDolobha lesimanjemanje lase-Westminster, i-London Borough eyakhiwa ngo-1965) yanwetshwa isuka eMfuleni iThames yaya emgwaqeni omdala waseRoma osuka eDolobheni uye entshonalanga yeNgilandi, manje osekuyi-Oxford Street. 




I-Westminster ngaphambi kokuya emadolobheni. Umgwaqo waseRoma (u-Oxford Street wesimanje) ukhonjiswa phezulu oya ngasentshonalanga. 
I-Thorney Island yayiphakathi kwezingalo zoMfula iTyburn wangaphambili ekuhlanganeni kwawo noMfula iThames, kuyilapho umngcele osentshonalanga ne-Chelsea wakhiwa uMfula iWestbourne owalahleka ngokufanayo.[2] Ulayini womfula usakha (nokubuyekezwa okuncane kakhulu) imingcele yesifunda sesimanje esineRoyal Borough yaseKensington kanye neChelsea. 


Amapherishi nezindawo zeDolobha kanye neNkululeko yase-Westminster. I-Westbourne engezansi yakha ingxenye yomngcele osentshonalanga, kanye no-Oxford Street enyakatho. 
Enyakatho, kude nomfula, iWestminster yayihlanganisa umhlaba nhlangothi zombili zeWestbourne,ikakhulukazi i-Knightsbridge (kuhlanganise nezingxenye ze-Hyde Park entshonalanga yechibi i-Serpentine (ekuqaleni eyakhiwe ngokucekela phansi umfula) kanye neningi le-Kensington Gardens).


I-Westminster ihlanganisa izifunda ezingaphansi kwe-Soho, i-St James, i-Mayfair, i-Covent Garden (eyabiwe ne-Camden engumakhelwane), i-Pimlico, i-Victoria, i-Belgravia ne-Knightsbridge (yabiwe ne-Kensington engumakhelwane). 

Idolobha langaphambili laseWestminster lahlangana nezindawo ezingomakhelwane zasePaddington kanye neMarylebone ngo-1965 ukwakha idolobha elikhulu lesimanje. Lezi zindawo ezingomakhelwane (ngaphandle kwendawo encane yasePaddington engxenyeni ye-Kensington Gardens), zisenyakatho yomgwaqo u-Oxford kanye nokuqhubeka kwawo ngasentshonalanga, u-Bayswater Road. 


















IBerners Street iyindawo esenyakatho yomgwaqo u-Oxford eDolobheni laseWestminster eWest End of London, eyasungulwa okokuqala njengomgwaqo wokuhlala abantu maphakathi nekhulu le-18 ngumakhi wezakhiwo uWilliam Berners, futhi kamuva yanikezelwa ezakhiweni ezinkulu zezentengiselwano nezama-semi-industrial noma ezindlini zamafulethi. Inobudlelwane noCharles Dickens, futhi bekuyindawo yabenzi bezinsimbi zomculo okuhlanganisa amapiyano namahabhu, kanye nefenisha nabakhi bamafilimu. 


UBerners Street uhamba cishe amamitha angu-315 ubheke enyakatho ukusuka enhlanganweni yomgwaqo u-Oxford kanye noWardour Street ukuze uhlangane noMortimer Street (owayekade enguCharles Street) kanye nesibhedlela sangaphambili iMiddlesex (manje esibizwa ngokuthi iFitzroy Place). Umgwaqo usendaweni eyaziwa ngeFitzrovia futhi uthathwa ngokomlando ukuthi use-East Marylebone. Izihlahla ezingamashumi amabili nanye zengezwa ku-Berners Street ngo-2012 


Berners Street ekuqaleni yathuthukiswa njengendawo yokuhlala yi-Berners Estate phakathi nekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalombili. 

UJohn Slater, umhloli we-Berners Estate, wabhala ngo-1918

Ngomhla zingama-21 kuNhlaba 1738, uWilliam Berners wavumela iminyaka engamashumi ayisishiyagalolunye nesishiyagalolunye kuThomas Huddle indawo yonke engaphambili engamafithi angu-655 ukuya ku-Oxford Street namafidi angu-100 ukujula (ngaphandle kobubanzi obudingekayo emigwaqweni emisha emibili ehlongozwayo - okuzoba imigwaqo yamanje kaBerners kanye neNewman kanye nokwandiswa kwe-Wells Lane) ngenani eliphelele lerenti engu-4. ngonyawo ngonyaka. U-Huddle wayezodiliza zonke izakhiwo ezindala futhi amise ezintsha, kanti uBerners wayezokwakha ipayipi lendle elisuka e-Wells Lane liye e-Rathbone Place. U-Huddle waqala ukwakha izindlu ku-Oxford Street ngesikhathi esisodwa, futhi wahlukanisela amarenti lapho, indawo yokuqala yokuqashisa iminyaka engamashumi ayisishiyagalolunye nesishiyagalolunye yanikezwa ngo-1739. Isamba semali yerenti yonyaka eyatholwa ifa yezindlu ze-Oxford Street yayingu-£135 8s. kwaze kwaba okokugcina kokuqashisa okudala kwehla ngo-1838. Indle okukhulunywa ngayo isahamba ngaphansi kwezinye zezindlu ekuBerners Street naku-Wells Street, kodwa manje ayisasetshenziswa. Phakathi kuka-1750 no-1763 kwabekwa imigwaqo ekhona e-Estate: eyokuqashisa yokuqala eyanikezwa ku-Newman Street yangonyaka ka-1750, kuCharles Street, manje obizwa ngokuthi uMortimer Street, ngo-1759, ku-Castle Street no-Wells Street ngo-1760, ku-Berners Street ku-1763, futhi ku-Building on 1763 Suffolk, manje ebizwa ngokuthi i-Suffolk 6. ngokushesha, ngoba ngo-1773 kwakunezindlu ezingamashumi ayisithupha eziqediwe ezikhona ku-Berners Street, ezingamashumi amabili nantathu kuCastle Street, ezingamashumi amathathu nanhlanu kuMortimer Street, ngaphandle kweSibhedlela saseMiddlesex, ezingamashumi ayisishiyagalolunye kuNewman Street, nezingamashumi amabili nantathu kuNassau Street. Izindlu eziningi zikhombisa ngokunamandla ithonya labafowethu u-Adam, kanti ezinye izisilingi, ezinhle kakhulu, cishe zazisuka emiklamo yazo yasekuqaleni. Isivumelwano seminyaka engama-999 sanikezwa iSibhedlela saseMiddlesex ngo-1754 

u-Edward Walford, wabhala e-Old and New London (Umqulu 4), eyanyatheliswa ngo-1878 

Berners Street, ebizwa kanjalo ngesihloko somndeni womninindlu waso, udlulela enyakatho kancane empumalanga ye-Wells Street. Yakhiwa cishe maphakathi nekhulu leminyaka elidlule, futhi ibilokhu igujwa “njengekhaya nendawo” yabadwebi, abadwebi, nabaqophi. Phakathi kwezakhamuzi zakhona zangaphambili kuzobalwa u-Opie, uFuseli, kanye noSir William Chambers, laba bakamuva esesibabalile mayelana neSomerset House. U-Opie wangcwatshwa e-St. Paul's Cathedral. Umkakhe wesibili, u-Amelia, i-Quakeress efundile, wayaziwa kakhulu ngemibhalo yakhe, "Tales of Real Life," "Izinkondlo," "Izinganekwane Ezilula," njll. Kulo mgwaqo bekuyibhange uFauntleroy, umgunyazi, ayenguzakwethu 

uWalford eqopha ukwanda kwezikhungo ezisiza abantulayo kanye nezokwelashwa kuBerners Street ngekhulu le-19.

I-Berners Street yakha inhloko yezikhungo eziningana zakwamanye amazwe neziphayo, ezinye zazo ezisungulwe kusukela ekhulwini leminyaka elidlule. Ngo-1788 kwasungulwa i-Society for the Relief of Widows and Orphans of Medical Men. I-Medical and Chirurgical Society yasungulwa ngo-1805, futhi yahlanganiswa ngo-1834, ukuze kutshalwe futhi kukhuthazwe imithi nokuhlinzwa. Umphakathi unomtapo wezincwadi omuhle, onemiqulu engaba ngu-25,000. Nalapha futhi, kune-Obstetrical Society of London, eyasungulwa ngo-1858; kanye ne-Pathological Society, eyasungulwa ngo-1846. Umphakathi oqanjwe igama lokugcina wasungulwa ukuze kuboniswe futhi kuhlolwe izibonelo, imidwebo, amalungiselelo amancane, ama-casts noma amamodeli ezingxenye ezigulayo, nezincazelo ezibhaliwe noma zomlomo ezihambisana nayo, ezibonisa isayensi ye-pathological. Yonke imiphakathi yezokwelapha eshiwo ngenhla, kanye nenye ebizwa ngokuthi i-Clinical Society of London, ihlaliswa endlini efanayo (No. 53). Eduze kwalesi sakhiwo (No. 54) kunesibhedlela iSt Peter's for Stone. Lesi sikhungo sosizo sasungulwa ngo-1860, futhi inhloso yaso ukuhlomula ngenani elikhulu ngangokunokwenzeka kwabampofu ngokubanikeza, ngaphandle kwencwadi yokuncoma, izinzuzo ngendawo yokuhlala esibhedlela; ukwenza ngcono ulwazi lwezokwelapha nokuhlinzwa ezifundweni ezilashwe ngokukhethekile lapha, ngokuhlanganisa inani elikhulu leziguli eziphethwe yilezo zifo, ngaleyo ndlela kunikezwe amathuba okubhekwa nokuhlukaniswa; futhi, ezimeni zeziguli ezihlushwa amatshe, ukuze kuphenywe izindlela ezingcono kakhulu zokufeza ukususwa kwalo ngengozi encane kakhulu empilweni yesiguli, futhi, noma nini lapho kungenzeka, esikhundleni se-lithotrity ye-lithotomy. Umkhuba wesibhedlela uvuleleke kubo bonke abafundi namalungu omsebenzi. KuNombolo 22 kunamahhovisi eLadies' Sanitary Association, kanye neNhlangano Yokukhuthaza Ukuqashwa Kwabesifazane. KuNombolo 9 kune-Berners Women's Club—olunye lwesivivinyo sokuqala kuleli cala. Endlini efanayo kunamahhovisi eKomiti Enkulu yeNational Society for Women’s Suffrage. I-London Association for the Protection of Trade inehhovisi layo kuNombolo 16. 

Eziningi zalezi zikhungo ezikhula eduze neSibhedlela SaseMiddlesex.

Ku-Charles Street, phezulu ku-Berners Street, ukubuka phansi lapho iyala, i-Middlesex Hospital. Isakhiwo, esenziwe ngezitini, futhi sibanzi kakhulu, sihlanganisa isikhungo namaphiko; ifakwe okugeza, imisebenzi yaselabhorethri, shaft yokufaka umoya, futhi, ngempela, zonke izinto ezidingekayo zokunethezeka, njll. Lesi sibhedlela sisukela eminyakeni engaba yishumi noma engamashumi amabili ngemuva kwefa elihle likaThomas Guy, umthengisi wezincwadi ongenalutho kuLombard Street. Yasungulwa okokuqala, ngo-1745, ku-Windmill Street, Tottenham Court Road, eyabagulayo nabakhubazekile, kanye neyabesifazane abashadile abalele. Yasuswa, ngo-1755, yayiswa endaweni yayo yamanje, lapho yema phakathi kwamasimu aluhlaza nemizila. Kusukela ngo-1807 iziguli ezibelethisayo, zifinyelela inani elicishe libe yinkulungwane ngonyaka, esikhundleni sokwamukelwa njengeziboshwa, zihanjelwa izikhulu zezokwelapha zesibhedlela emakhaya azo. Amawadi omdlavuza asungulwa ngesipho sika-£ 4,000 esivela kuMnu. Samuel Whitbread, ngo-1807, lapho ezinye izipho kanye namafa engeziwe. Isigameko esiphawulekayo emlandweni wesibhedlela ukuthi ngo-1793 saba isiphephelo sabafuduki abaningi basebukhosini baseFrance abaxoshwa eFrance yi-Jacobin Reign of Terror. Izakhiwo zandiswa ngamaphiko amasha akhiwa ngo-1775, futhi futhi ngo-1834. U-Lord Robert Seymour, umngane oshisekayo nomubi walesi sikhungo, wathola ngenxa yaso uxhaso lobukhosi lukaGeorge IV., oluqhutshwa nguMkhulu wakhe wamanje. Isikole sezokwelapha, esasungulwa ngo-1835, sinedumela eliphakeme; ifakwe umnyuziyamu wamaqoqo abalulekile. Lesi sibhedlela sinemibhede yeziguli ezingaphezu kwamakhulu amathathu. Kulaba abangamashumi amabili nesithupha bazinikele ekusungulweni komdlavuza, owasungulwa ngonyaka we-1791, lapho isiguli sivunyelwe ukuhlala "kuze kube yilapho sikhululwa ngobuciko noma sikhishwe ngokufa; eziyisishiyagalombili zabelwe abesifazane abaphethwe izifo ezithinta ubulili babo; ingxenye esele yemibhede ibekelwe amacala ahlukahlukene. Abesifazane abashadile abangaphezulu kwamakhulu ayisishiyagalolunye abalele ezindaweni zabo, kanti iziguli ezingaphandle eziyizinkulungwane eziyishumi nesishiyagalombili ziyakhululeka minyaka yonke. Isibhedlela asinawo amafa. Izikhokhelo zonyaka zifinyelela ku-£2,355, kanti eminyakeni edlule izindleko zinyuswe ngemisebenzi ethile yokuthuthukisa edingekayo. Lesi sibhedlela sibalwa nodokotela abahlinzayo nodokotela abavelele kakhulu emkhakheni wezokwelapha; ngaphandle kwalokho kube yisizinda semisebenzi eminingi evelele ekuhlinzeni. 

U-Edward Walford uvusa okuthile kwesimo semakethe yasemgwaqweni ekhoneni likaBerners Street noCharles Street okwachazwa ngokucacile nguHenry Mayhew ngeminyaka yawo-1840s kanye nama-50s.

Uhlangothi oluseningizimu yoMgwaqo u-Charles, oqhutshekwa ngo-Goodge Street ku-Tottenham Court Road, luveza ukubonakala okumatasa, ikakhulukazi ngoLwesihlanu nangoMgqibelo kusihlwa; futhi njengenye yezimakethe zomgwaqo ezimbalwa ezisele eNtshonalanga, futhi okungenzeka ukuthi izonyamalala ngokushesha, ingase ifune isaziso esifushane. Ohlwini olude lwabagcini bezitolo ohlangothini lwalo oluseningizimu, ababonisa izitolo zabo zezinhlanzi, izithelo, nemifino kumabhala wezandla nobhasikidi, nasezilebheni ezinyakazayo, singasebenzisa amazwi ka-Henry Mayhew:—“Indawo kulezi zingxenye inesimo esingaphezu kwesemakethe. Kunamakhulukhulu ezitolo, futhi yonke indawo inesibani saso esisodwa noma ezimbili esimhlophe; Isibani segesi esizikhiqizela sona, noma sikhanyiswa ilangabi elibomvu elishunqayo lezibani zamafutha zasendulo, enye indoda iveza ikhandlela layo elinamathiselwe emnyameni wezinkuni zokubasa; uye wagingqa idiphu yakhe ephepheni elimnyama, elivutha amakhandlela elibomvu elinomlilo okhanya emigodini engaphansi kwesitofu se-chestnut esibhakiwe. indiza emoyeni njengamafulege amalangabi, ithela isikhukhula sokukhanya, kangangokuthi kude umkhathi ngenhla kwendawo uyathuthumela sengathi umgwaqo uyasha e- 

Jamaica 
Ngomhla zi-2 kuNovemba 1756, u-Richard Bathurst wahambisa incwadi yakhe yokwesula eBhodini leSibhedlela saseMiddlesex, ngakho-ke 

Madoda, Ngokuphoqeleka Ngesibopho Sokuthola Isidingo Sesibili, I-Jamica. ukubuya, ngicela ukuthi kusukela ngalolu suku nizothatha indawo yami esibhedlela senu njengengenamuntu angeke ngikwazi ukwenza lokhu kwesula ngaphandle kokubuyisa ukubonga kwami ​​ngokwahluka engikhethwe ngawo, Umusa engivunyelwe ngawo ukungabikho kwami ngezikhathi ezithile, kanye nemiphakathi engiyitholile ngiyohlala ngifisela Impumelelo eSibhedlela futhi abangeke besakukhumbula ngayo yonke i-Gratitude. Madoda. Inceku yenu ebophezeleke kakhulu futhi ethobeke kakhulu, uRichard Bathurst 

Isazi sozalo u-Anne M. Powers ubhale ucwaningo ngokushintshana phakathi kwe-Jamaica yekhulu le-18 ne-London mercantile encwadini yakhe kanye nebhulogi ethi 'A Parcel of Ribbons', enikeza ukuqonda okuthile ngo-Berners Street ngezikhathi zamakholoni.

Lapho uRobert Cooper Lee ebuyela eNgilandi esuka eJamaica nomndeni wakhe ekupheleni kuka-August 1771, bahlala isikhashana ku-Old Bond Street eLondon. Kodwa phakathi namasonto ambalwa uRobert wathola indlu kuBerners Street lapho asayina khona isivumelwano sokuqashisa iminyaka engamashumi amathathu. Namuhla eBrithani noma ubani ongakwazi ukuthenga indlu ubuye athenge indawo yokuhlala mahhala ngakho-ke ungumnikazi wendlu kanye nomhlaba omi kuwo. ELondon ekhulwini le-18 isimo esinjalo sasingavamile. Ngisho nabacebe kakhulu bangasayina isivumelwano sokuqashisa indlu nganoma yini kusukela ezinyangeni ezimbalwa (ukuya enkathini yezenhlalo yaseLondon) kuya esikhathini seminyaka. Iminyaka engamashumi amathathu yayivamile kodwa kungaba noma yini kuze kube iminyaka engamashumi ayisishiyagalolunye nesishiyagalolunye. ILondon umndeni wakwa-Lee obuyele kuyo yabe isikhule kakhulu emashumini amabili eminyaka selokhu uRobert ehambile. Kwakukhona amabhuloho amasha amabili ngaphesheya kweThames - Westminster Bridge eyayisakhiwa lapho ehamba yavulwa ngo-1750, iBlackfriars Bridge yavulwa ngo-1769. Ibhuloho laseLondon lase lilahlekelwe yinqwaba yezindlu nezitolo zenkathi ephakathi ngo-1757 futhi lathola isisekelo esisha nesinhle sase-Italy. Ngaphezu kokwakhiwa kwamabhuloho amasha, iLondon yayisabalala ngokushesha ngaphandle, ihlanganisa izindawo ezaziyizinkundla nje ebusheni bukaRobert, futhi inani labantu lalikhule lisuka cishe ingxenye yesigidi ngo-1750 laya ezingxenyeni ezintathu kwezine zesigidi emashumini amabili eminyaka kamuva. Kwake kwaba izindawo ezinemfashini njengeCovent Garden zase zehlile futhi manje zase zigcwele amasela nezifebe. Izakhamuzi zawo zangaphambili zathuthela entshonalanga, futhi izindawo ezinkulu ezisenyakatho naseningizimu yomgwaqo u-Oxford zabona ukuthuthukiswa kwemigwaqo nezikwele ezinhle, eziningi zazo ezisazigcina okungenani ezinye zezindlu zazo zaseGeorgia. U-Berners Street uhamba ngama-engeli angakwesokudla ku-Oxford Street, ngaleso sikhathi owawusaziwa ngokuthi u-Oxford Road, futhi ngenkathi kamuva wathola idumela njengendawo yamaciko nababhali, kwakukhona imindeni eminingi enama-Jamaican axhumene nayo eyahlala lapho futhi abahlala khona ngokuvamile babecebile futhi bexhumene kahle. Izindlu bezizintsha - zinhle, izitezi zaseGeorgia ezinokufinyelela ngemuva ezitebeleni zazo ngeBerners Mews. Indlu ka-Lee enenombolo yamashumi amabili nesithupha yachazwa njengenamagumbi ombhede aphakeme anomoya anomoya omuhle, amagumbi ezisebenzi kanye nenqwaba yamakhabethe, igumbi lokudweba eliphakeme elinesikhala esinocezu lukashimula oluhle kanye ne-stucco cornice, igumbi lokudlela elikhulu nendawo yokuphumula esemaceleni, umtapo wolwazi, ihholo lokungena eliphakeme, namahhovisi anamathiselwe afanele ahlelwe kahle, futhi ahlinzekwa ngamanzi; emi amakalishi amabili, stabling amahhashi amahlanu futhi omile arched cellaring. Umlando wokuthuthuka kwalendawo uhlehlela emuva maphakathi nekhulunyaka elandulela lapho, ngo-1654, uJosias Berners ethenga indawo endaweni yesifunda sase-St Marylebone ngo-£970 kuSir Francis Williamson wase-Isleworth. Ukuthuthukiswa okukhulu kwenziwa engxenyeni yokuqala yekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalombili nguWilliam Berners, ngakho-ke umndeni waqamba igama lawo emgwaqweni.Umndeni wakwaBerners wawuxhunywe eJamaica izikhathi ezintathu ngomndeni wakwaJarrett. Abazukulu abathathu bakaWilliam Berners bashada noJarretts wase-Orange Valley, uTrelawny – uMaria Berners washada noHerbert Newton Jarrett (ongowesithathu kulelo gama), umfowabo uWilliam washada noRachel Allen Jarrett (owesibili kulelo gama) kwathi umfowabo uHenry Denny Berners washada noSarah Jarrett. USarah noRachel babengodadewabo, uHerbert wayengumfowabo omncane kayise. Kodwa ukubuyela kuBerners Street! Indlela evamile yentuthuko ekhulwini leshumi nesishiyagalombili kwakuwukuthi umnikazi womhlaba aqashe iziqephu zomhlaba ukuze zithuthukiswe kubakhi abaqagelayo ababezokwakha iqoqo lezindlu bese beziqashisa kubaqashi. Ngezinye izikhathi umakhi wayemane agxumeke igobolondo futhi ukuqedela ingaphakathi kwenziwe ngomunye umuntu, ngokuvamile ngaphansi kokuqondisa kwalowo oqashelwe ukuqasha. Kwakungekho mfuneko yokungaguquguquki ekubukeni kwezindlu, nakuba imfashini yezilinganiso zakudala ngokwezinga elithile yayikhuthaza. Ngokungafani nanamuhla kwakungekho mvume yokuhlela edingekayo futhi kwaba nemithethonqubo embalwa yokwakha yokulawula ikhwalithi yesakhiwo. Kwakunemithetho ethile ehlobene ngokwesibonelo nezinto zokwakha kanye nobubanzi bemigwaqo eyayilandelwe kusukela eMlilo Omkhulu waseLondon ngo-1666. Kungalesi sizathu ukuthi lezi zindlu zikanokusho zaseGeorgia zazivame ukwakhiwa ngezitini, umhlaba wezitini umbiwa emigodini emikhulu yobumba ezungeze iLondon. Isibonelo idolobhana elincane laseWare eHertfordshire lalinezindawo zezitini ezinkulu kanye nolayini omuhle wokuthutha izitini ukuya eLondon ngesikebhe phansi ngomgwaqo we-Lea (ekugcineni kwayo namuhla okumi i-Olympic Park). Phakathi kwabanikazi bomhlaba eMarylebone kwakunababusi baseChandos, baseDevonshire nasePortland amagama abo akhunjulwa namuhla emigwaqweni nasezigcawini zayo. Ungafunda incazelo yangaleso sikhathi yentuthuko yendawo eyabhalwa ekupheleni kwekhulu le-18 nguDaniel Lysons oNdawo yakhe yaseLondon iwumthombo omangalisayo wolwazi ngekhulu le-18 leminyaka laseLondon. Izinga lokuzinza kwamalungu ePlantocracy endaweni lifakazelwa yizinombolo zamarekhodi ezincwadini zepherishi yase-St Marylebone, ngemibhabhadiso, imishado kanye nokungcwatshwa kwabo. Kamuva ekhulwini leminyaka laba bahlali abacebile bathuthela kancane kancane bebheka enyakatho njengoba intuthuko yayiqhubeka phezu kweMarylebone Gardens endala, eyake yaba indawo enhle yokuhamba ngezinyawo kodwa manje eseyidlulwa yinzuzo ezotholakala ngentuthuko. Ngisho noRobert Cooper Lee waqhubeka. Yize asigcinile isivumelwano sokuqashisa emzini kaBerners Street, wathuthela e-Bedford Square esanda kuqedwa, nayo ehlala abantu bakudala baseJamaican abanjengoMarchant Tubb, kanye namalungu omndeni wakwaHibbert. Nakuba i-Bedford Square ... ingashintshile kakhulu, indlu kaRobert Cooper Lee kaBerners Street kade yahamba, kanye nengxenye enkulu yekhulu le-18 eLondon, yathathelwa indawo amafulethi ama-Victorian, acaba ngamabhomu ngesikhathi sempi,yakhiwe kabusha ngemva kwempi futhi yathathelwa indawo yingilazi namabhulokhi ensimbi.

Berners Street Hoax 
Umgwaqo wanikwa idumela ihlaya elingokoqobo, elaziwa ngokuthi i-Berners Street hoax, eyenziwa umlobi uTheodore Hook ngo-1810. [7] UHook wenze ukubheja nomngane wakhe, uSamuel Beazley, ukuthi angakwazi ukuguqula noma iyiphi indlu eLondon ibe ikheli okukhulunywa ngalo kakhulu phakathi nesonto, okuyinto ayithola ngokuthumela izinkulungwane zezincwadi egameni likaNkk Tottenham, owayehlala ku-54 Berners Street, ecela ukudiliva, izivakashi, nosizo. UHook uzimise endlini ebhekene ngqo no-54 Berners Street, lapho yena nomngane wakhe bachitha khona usuku bebuka isiphithiphithi. Indawo eku-54 Berners Street manje isithathwe ihhotela i-Sanderson. 

UCharles Booth 
Ngo-Okthoba 1898, uCharles Booth wathatha uhambo olulandelanayo noConstable RJ French waseTottenham Court Road ehlukaniswe ingxenye yamaphoyisa ophiko lwamaphoyisa luka-D futhi waqopha akubona ebhukwini lakhe le-Life and Labor of the People of London. Ngomhla zingama-21 kuMfumfu wahamba ne-PC French ezungeza "Isifunda sesi-3" kuhlanganise nendawo "eboshwe eNyakatho ngo-Mortimer Street kanye ne-Goodge St. eMpumalanga ngo-Charlotte St. kanye ne-Rathbone Place, eNingizimu ngo-Oxford Street futhi eNtshonalanga yi-Regent St. iyingxenye yezifunda ze-All Souls and All Saints." Ephuma ekhoneni likaGoodge Street kanye noCharlotte Street wahamba waya enyakatho e-Berners Street ephawula kuphela "izitolo ezingu-4 1/2, isikhungo sezikhungo zomculo, upiyano, insimbi, abashicileli bomculo njll. 


Ubuciko 
uWilliam Chambers, umakhi wezakhiwo kanye nomhlobisi wangaphakathi, wakwazi ukuzakhela indlu "ngokuqagela kwakhe", e-13, Berners Street, kanye nezindlu ezimbili ze-1 no-James 1 no-1 cent. UThomas Rouse, konke kwaqala ngo-1764. Ngokombhali wakhe wokuphila kwabantu uJohn Harris, “Ingadi kaChambers inqanyulwe esitebeleni futhi eseduze negumbi elikhulu okumelwe ukuthi kwakuyihhovisi lakhe lokudweba, elivumela abasizi ukuba bangene emigwaqweni. Ingemuva lendlu yakhe lalihlotshiswe nge-papier mâché 'ngesitayela', mhlawumbe i-Chinoiserie,."[9] Izithombe zezinye zezinto zangaphakathi ze-Chambers zigcinwe emtatsheni wezincwadi we-RIBA. 
UThomas Collins, umkhandi wokuhlobisa owayesebenzela, futhi wayengumngane kanye nozakwethu ka-Sir William Chambers. 
UJohn Opie, umlando, u-Henry Berners Street kuze kube ngu-8 umculi we-8 u- 
Henry Berners Street (8 ) Umdwebi waseSwitzerland nomdwebi (13, Berners Street, ikhaya langaphambili likaWilliam Chambers) 1803

UBerners Street uhlotshaniswa kakhulu nombhali uCharles Dickens. Ubabekazi kaDickens, uNkz Charles Charlton, wayenendlu yokulala ku-16 Berners Street, kanti u-Dickens wayevame ukuthathwa lapha ngunina, futhi wathola umsebenzi ngo-1827. Omunye wababehlalele kwakungummeli osemusha okuthiwa u-Edward Blackmore, owahlatshwa umxhwele yilo mfana futhi wamqasha njengommeli e-Ellisn 1 Blackmore (iholo elingaphezu kokuphindwe kabili kweholo likaDickens, umsebenzi wefekthri owesatshwayo, nowagcina edumile). 

KwakukuBerners Street lapho, esengumfana, uDickens abona khona owesifazane owayezulazula, okwakusekelwe phezu kwakhe umlingiswa onguMiss Havisham ovela ku-Great Expectations. U-Dickens wamchaza "njengesidalwa esidala esizidlayo, esibandayo futhi esihlelekile" "esasigqoke ngokuphelele esimhlophe sinokwekwe okumhlophe okwesabekayo ekhanda laso nasebusweni ngaphakathi kwebhonethi yaso emhlophe." Wengeza ngokuthi "wahlanya ngenxa yezizathu zakhe eyedwa - ngokungangabazeki ngenxa yokuthi isicebi somQuaker sasingafuni ukumshada. Lena ingubo yakhe yomshado. Uhlale ehambela lapha… sibona esinyathelweni sakhe esicwebezelayo neso eliwufifi ukuthi uhlose ukumbulala." Lokhu kwakusendatshana yakhe ethi, “Lapho Sayeka Ukukhula” eyanyatheliswa ku-Household Words ngo-1 January 1853. 

Kamuva ekuphileni, e-31 Berners Street, u-Dickens wafaka isithandwa sakhe esincane esiyimfihlo, umlingisi u-Ellen Lawless Ternan (ogama lakhe linguNelly), owathi eneminyaka engu-19 wayemncane ngeminyaka engu-27 kuye, futhi eneminyaka efanayo nendodakazi yakhe endala. KwakunguSeptember 1858 lapho engena ephelezelwa unina uFrancis, owayengumlingisi, nodadewabo ababili, uMaria, omunye umlingisi, noFanny, umculi. Ngemva kwenyanga nje u-Ellen noMaria babika kuye ukuthi babehlushwa iphoyisa, uDickens ayesola ukuthi lalifumbathiswe indoda enesithakazelo sobulili kubo bobabili noma kubo bobabili. Ukhale ngalokhu “kuziphatha okungavamile, okuyingozi nokungafuneki kwephoyisa” acabanga ukuthi kufanele lichithwe. Kodwa ukwesaba ukwaziwa kwamvimbela ukuba aqhubeke nalo. Mhlawumbe yingakho bonke bathutha ngoMashi 1859 baya e-Ampthill Square. U-Ellen wayenomkhuba wokugqoka ama-geranium abomvu ne-heather emhlophe ezinweleni zakhe. Wagqugquzelwa ukuthi ayeke ukubambela uDickens ngo-Agasti 1859, futhi wathola izinkokhelo ezivamile ku-akhawunti yakhe yaseCoutts Bank. Lapho eshona eneminyaka engu-75 ubudala, wangcwatshwa eSouthsea, eduze nalapho uDickens azalelwa khona. 

U-Ellen Ternan, umlingisi kanye nenkosikazi kaCharles Dickens (31, Berners Street) 
USamuel Taylor Coleridge, imbongi (71, Berners Street) 
Ezinye izakhamuzi 
uRobert Cooper Lee (26, Berners Street) iminyaka engu-30 eqashisa ngo-1771, wabe esethuthela e-Bedford Square[16] 
uJohn Slater, FRSA, umklami we-4. Berners Street 1891
Ekupheleni kwekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalolunye indawo ezungeze uBerners Street yayingaseyona indawo yokuhlala ngokuphelele futhi iziza zentuthuko zase zihlanganiswa ukuze kwakhiwe izakhiwo ezinkulu zezohwebo kanye nezincane zezimboni noma amabhlogo ezithabathaba zamafulethi. Izibonelo zalawo mabhuloki ezithabathaba zifaka izithabathaba zemigwaqo yase-Edwardian Berners (34–36, Berners Street) kanye neNkantolo yaseLancaster.

u-Elizabeth Crawford waphawula emsebenzini wakhe we-Women's Suffrage Movement:
 
Ngo-1871 ikomidi leBerners Club lalihlanganisa uFrancis Power Cobbe noBarbara Bodichon. Iklabhu lapho okubhaliselwe khona konyaka kwakungu-10s, yayivulwa kusukela ngo-8 ekuseni kuze kube ngu-10.30 ebusuku phakathi nezinsuku futhi kusukela ngo-9 ekuseni kuze kube ngu-10.30 ebusuku ngamaSonto. Ikilabhu ibinegumbi lokufunda, elihlinzekwe ngamaphephandaba kanye nezincwadi; igumbi lokudweba lomphakathi nengxoxo, kanye negumbi lokudlela. Ikilabhu yayingakhethi nhlobo, futhi yayivulekele amalungu angaphandle kanye namaNgisi. Ikomiti lalifuna ilungu ngalinye elingase libe khona ukuba linikeze ireferensi ngokuhlonishwa. I-Berners Club yayingasekho ngo-1898.

abenzi 
bomculo abangu -19 etholakala kuBerners Street phakathi kuka-1820 no-1860, okuhlanganisa:[28] 



Thomas Dodd, umenzi wamahabhu. UThomas Dodd uvela emndenini wabenzi bezinsimbi - iminsalo ye-violin ye-Dodd yayidumile kusukela maphakathi no-1700. Uyise u-Edward washona ngo-1810 eneminyaka ehlonipheke kakhulu engu-95. U-Dodd wayengumthengisi wezinsimbi kusukela ngo-1809 kuya ku-1823, lapho ethuthela ku-Berners Street wabe esethanda amahabhu. Ubuye futhi ku-Berwick Street ngo-1827 ngaphambi kokubuyela ku-Berners Street. UThomas washona cishe ngo-1830, futhi ibhizinisi laqhubeka kwaze kwaba ngu-1846 - mhlawumbe ngokusebenzisa amadodana akhe amabili (bona u-Edward Dodd, 3, Berners Street). Kukhona i-patent ye-1822 yentamo e-laminated. 
Haarnack, umenzi wamahabhu (53 Berners Street). Kwakukhona izizukulwane ezimbalwa ze-Haarnack ezisukela maphakathi nawo-1920s. Ibhizinisi laliku-Charlotte Street futhi kwakukhona indawo yombukiso eFitzroy Square. Okwesikhashana nabo beseku-53 Berners Street ezansi nomgwaqo osuka eDodds. Owokuqala kulayini wayengumakhenikha omkhulu e-Erards ngo-1808. I-Haarnack yayingabakhi bokugcina abaqhubeka nokuhweba futhi yayinebhizinisi eliphumelelayo lokulungisa. UMarie Goosens ukhuluma ngokuhlangana nezizukulwane ezi-3 esitolo sabo encwadini yakhe ethi "Life on a Harpstring". 
I-Erat's Harp Saloon yayiku-23 Berners Street kusukela ngo-1820 kuya ku-1858, futhi amakhonsathi omphakathi ayebanjelwe lapho. Ngawo-1920s kuya kuma-1950s uRudall, Carte & Co, umkhiqizi wezinsimbi zokhuni nezethusi, wayetholakala ku-23 Berners Street. 
I-Music Sales Group eshicilela 
umculo ingumshicileli womculo ophrintiwe omkhulu kunayo yonke e-Europe, enendlunkulu eku-Berners Street, e-London. Iphethe amalungelo ezingoma ezingamakhulu ezinkulungwane, izigxivizo zombili zezincwadi nomculo weshidi, isebenzisa uchungechunge lwezitolo zomculo ezinkulu kunazo zonke e-UK, futhi ithengisa umculo wamakhasi, izinsimbi kanye nezinsiza ngokuqondile nge-Musicroom.com.
I-Novello & Co (1, Berners Street, 1867-1906) yinkampani yokushicilela umculo ophrintiwe ezinze eLondon egxile emculweni wakudala, ikakhulukazi umculo wamakhwaya. Yasungulwa ngo-1811 nguVincent Novello.
I-Performing Rights Society for Music (29–33 Berners Street), phambilini eyayiyiNhlangano Yelungelo Lokwenza, eyasungulwa ngo-1914, ingumphakathi wase-UK oqoqa amalungelo okukopisha kanye nenhlangano yamalungelo okusebenza eqhuba ukuphathwa kwamalungelo eqoqo lemisebenzi yomculo. I-PRS Yomculo yasungulwa ngo-1997 njenge-MCPS-PRS Alliance, ihlanganisa izinhlangano ezimbili zamaqoqo: I-Mechanical-Copyright Protection Society (MCPS) kanye ne-Performing Right Society (PRS).
