Bourne kanye neHollingsworth 
Bourne & Hollingsworth kwakuyisitolo somnyango ekhoneni lika-Oxford Street kanye noBerners Street. Isakhiwo sayo sakhiwa ngasekupheleni kwekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalolunye, futhi isitolo sathuthela esakhiweni ekuqaleni kwawo-1900, sahlala lapho kwaze kwaba yilapho sivalwa ngo-1983. I-Bourne & Hollingsworth ifakwe kwifilimu ye-Adelphi yango-1954 ethi The Crowded Day, elandela usuku olulodwa empilweni yeqembu labasebenzi besitolo somnyango futhi yadutshulwa ingxenye endaweni ngaphakathi nangaphandle kwesitolo. 
































IBhange LaseNgilandi yibhange elikhulu lase-United Kingdom kanye nemodeli okusekelwe kuyo amabhange amakhulu esimanje. Isungulwe ngo-1694 ukuze isebenze njengomabhange kanye nomphathi wezikweletu kuHulumeni wamaNgisi, futhi isengomunye wabamabhange kahulumeni wase-United Kingdom, iyibhange elikhulu lesibili elidala emhlabeni.

Ibhange laliphethwe ngasese ngabanikazi bamasheya kusukela ekusungulweni kwalo ngo-1694 laze lafakwa ngaphansi kombuso ngo-1946 yinkonzo yase-Attlee.[4] Ngo-1998 yaba inhlangano yomphakathi ezimele, ephethwe ngokuphelele nguSolicitor Wezezimali egameni likahulumeni, [5] enegunya lokusekela izinqubomgomo zezomnotho zikahulumeni wangaleso sikhathi, [6] kodwa ezimele ekugcineni ukuqina kwamanani.[7] Ngekhulu lama-21 ibhange lathatha umthwalo wemfanelo owengeziwe wokugcina nokuqapha uzinzo lwezezimali e-UK, futhi liya ngokuya lisebenza njengomlawuli osemthethweni. 

Ikomkhulu laleli bhange lisesifundeni esikhulu sezimali saseLondon, iDolobha laseLondon, kusukela ngo-1694, kanye naku-Threadneedle Street kusukela ngo-1734. Ngezinye izikhathi laziwa ngokuthi "I-Old Lady of Threadneedle Street", igama elithathwe kukhathuni ehlekisayo ka-James Gillray ngo-1797. Impambano yomgwaqo ngaphandle yaziwa ngokuthi i-Bank Junction. 

Ibhange, phakathi kwezinye izinto, lingumgadi wezinqolobane zegolide ezisemthethweni zase-United Kingdom (nalezo zakwamanye amazwe angaba ngu-30).[10] Kusukela ngo-Ephreli 2016, ibhange labamba amathani angaba ngu-5,134 (amathani angama-5,659) egolide, abiza u-£141 billion. Lezi zilinganiso ziphakamisa ukuthi i-vault ingabamba cishe u-3% wamathani ayi-171,300 egolide ambiwa kuwo wonke umlando wesintu. 

Imisebenzi 
Ngokuvumelana ne-strapline yalo, inhloso eyinhloko yebhange 'ukuthuthukisa okuhle kwabantu base-United Kingdom ngokugcina uzinzo lwezimali nezezimali'. Lokhu kufezwa ngezindlela ezihlukahlukene: 

Ukuzinza kwezimali 
Izintengo ezizinzile nezindlela zokukhokha ezivikelekile yizindlela ezimbili eziyinhloko zokuzinza kwezimali. 

Amanani aqinile 
Izintengo ezizinzile zigcinwa ngokufuna ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ukwenyuka kwamanani kufinyelela imigomo kaHulumeni yokwehla kwamandla emali. Ibhange lihlose ukufeza lokhu okuhlosiwe ngokulungisa izinga lenzalo eliyisisekelo (elaziwa ngokuthi izinga lasebhange), elinqunywa iKomidi Lenqubomgomo Yezimali yebhange (MPC). (I-MPC inikeze umthwalo wemfanelo wokuphatha inqubomgomo yezimali; UMnyango Wezezimali we-HM unamandla agodliwe okunikeza imiyalo ekomitini "uma idingeka ngokwentshisekelo yomphakathi kanye nezimo zezomnotho ezimbi kakhulu", kodwa iPhalamende kufanele ligunyaze leyo miyalo zingakapheli izinsuku ezingama-28.) 

Kusukela ngo-2024 umgomo wokwehla kwamandla emali u-2%; uma lokhu okuhlosiwe kweqiwe uMbusi kudingeka abhale incwadi evulelekile eya kuShansela Womnyango Wezimali echaza isimo futhi aphakamise amakhambi.[15] Ngaphandle kokusetha izinga lenzalo eliyisisekelo, ithuluzi eliyinhloko elisetshenziswa yibhange kulokhu ukuncishiswa komthamo.
 
Vikela izindlela zokukhokha
Ibhange linegunya phezu kodaba lwamanothi eNgilandi naseWales futhi lilawula ukukhishwa kwamabhange ngamabhange ezentengiselwano eScotland naseNyakatho Ireland. (Amabhange ase-Scottish nase-Northern Irish agcina ilungelo lokukhipha ama-banknotes awo, kodwa kufanele axhaswe umuntu ngamunye ngediphozithi ebhange, ngaphandle kwamaphawundi ayizigidi ezimbalwa amelela inani lamanothi ayenawo ngo-1845.) 

Ngaphezu kwalokho ibhange liqondisa ezinye izinhlelo zokukhokha, ezisebenza njenge-ejenti yokukhokhelana kanye nezinhlelo ze-Real-time settlement ze-CHAPS.[18] Ngo-2024 ibhange lalikhokha imali elinganiselwa ku-£500 billion phakathi kwamabhange usuku nosuku. 

Ukuzinza kwezezimali 
Ukugcina uzinzo kwezezimali kuhilela ukuvikela abongi base-UK, abatshalizimali kanye nababolekayo ekusongelweni kohlelo lwezezimali lulonke.[8] Izinsongo zitholwa umsebenzi webhange wokugada nezobunhloli bemakethe, futhi zisingathwa ngokusebenza kwezezimali nokunye (kokubili ekhaya naphesheya). Iningi lalezi zindlela zokuvikela zafakwa ngemuva kwenkinga yezimali yango-2008: 

Umthetho 
Ngo-2011 i-Prudential Regulation Authority yebhange yasungulwa ukuze ilawule futhi yengamele wonke amabhange amakhulu, izinhlangano zokwakha, izinyunyana zezikweletu, izinkampani zomshuwalense kanye namafemu okutshala izimali e-UK ('i-microprudential regulation').[19] Ibhange liphinde libe neqhaza elisemthethweni lokuqondisa mayelana nengqalasizinda yezimakethe zezimali. 

Ukulawulwa kobungozi 
Ngesikhathi esifanayo, iKomidi Lenqubomgomo Yezezimali (i-FPC) yebhange lamiswa ukuze lihlonze futhi liqaphe ubungozi ohlelweni lwezezimali, futhi lithathe izinyathelo ezifanele lapho kunesidingo ('imithethonqubo ebanzi'). I-FPC ishicilela lokho ekutholile (kanye nezinyathelo ezithathiwe) Kumbiko Wokusimama Kwezezimali waminyaka yonke kabili ngonyaka. 

Amasevisi ebhange 
Ibhange lihlinzeka ngezinsizakalo zamabhange amakhulu kuHulumeni wase-UK (kanye namabhange amakhulu angaphezu kwekhulu aphesheya kwezilwandle).[22] Iphatha I-Akhawunti Ye-Exchange Equalization yase-UK egameni lika-HM Treasury futhi inakekela i-akhawunti kahulumeni Yesikhwama Esihlanganisiwe.[23] Iphinde ilawule izindawo zokushintshiselana ngemali yangaphandle futhi ingumlondolozi wezinqolobane zegolide zase-UK (kanye nabanye). 

Ibhange liphinde linikeze 'ukwesekwa kwezimali kanye nezinye izinsiza emabhange nakwezinye izikhungo zezezimali'.[13] Amabhange ezentengiselwano ngokuvamile agcina ingxenye enkulu yezimali zawo ezigciniwe lapho efakwa eBhange LaseNgilandi. Lezi zimali ezigciniwe zamabhange amakhulu zisetshenziswa amabhange ukukhokhelana izinkokhelo zodwa;[25] (ngalesi sizathu iBhange LaseNgilandi ngezinye izikhathi libizwa ngokuthi 'ibhange lababhange').[26] Ezimweni ezingavamile, iBhange lingase libe ngumbolekisi wendlela yokugcina ngokwelula isikweletu uma kungekho esinye isikhungo esingakwenza.

Njengomlawuli kanye nebhange elikhulu, iBhange LaseNgilandi alikaze linikeze izinsiza zebhange zabathengi iminyaka eminingi, kodwa lisalawula ezinye izinkonzo ezibhekene nomphakathi (njengokushintshana ngemali yamanothi ebhange athathelwe indawo).[27] Kuze kube ngu-2017, izisebenzi zeBhange zazinelungelo lokuvula ama-akhawunti amanje ngokuqondile neBhange LaseNgilandi futhi zanikezwa ikhodi yohlobo eyingqayizivele ethi 10-00-00. 

Isinqumo 
Ngaphansi kwemigomo yoMthetho Wamabhange ka-2009 ibhange liyiSigungu Seziphathimandla sase-UK sanoma yiliphi ibhange noma umphakathi wezakhiwo ohlulelwa 'mkhulu kakhulu ukuba ungahluleka'; ngalokho inikwa amandla okwenza uma kwenzeka ibhange lihluleka 'ukuvikela izinsiza ezibalulekile zezezimali zase-UK nokuzinza kwezezimali'. 

Izinsizakalo zomlando nezibopho 
Phakathi kuka-1715 no-1998, iBhange LaseNgilandi laliphethe Izitokwe Zikahulumeni (ezakhe ingxenye enkulu yesikweletu sikazwelonke): ibhange lalinomthwalo wemfanelo wokukhipha amasheya kubanikazi bamasheya, ukukhokha izinzuzo kanye nokugcina irejista yokudluliswa kwemali;[26] nokho ngo-1998, ngemva kwesinqumo sokunikeza isikweletu, ukuphathwa kwebhange kwakunomthwalo wemfanelo wokudlulisa ukuzimela kweHhovisi elisha. iphinde yathatha i-Exchequer yokuphatha imali kanye nesibopho sokukhipha izikweletu zikaMgcinimafa ebhange ngo-2000.[30] I-Computershare ithathe isikhundla sokubhalisa amabhondi kahulumeni wase-UK (izibambiso eziqinile noma 'ama-gilts') ebhange ekupheleni kuka-2004. Ibhange, nokho, liyaqhubeka nokusebenza njenge-ejenti yokukhokhela izikweletu zeHhovisi Lokuphathwa Kwezikweletu kanye nomgcini wezibambiso zalo. 

Kusukela lasungulwa ngo-1694, leli bhange lalihlinzekele uHulumeni insizakalo yamabhange okudayisa; nokho ngo-2008 yanquma ukuhoxa ekunikezeni lezi zinsizakalo, manje ezihlinzekwa uhla lwezinye izikhungo zezimali futhi ezilawulwa yi-Government Banking Service. 

Kuze kube ngu-2016, ibhange belihlinzeka ngezinsizakalo zebhange lomuntu siqu njengelungelo lezisebenzi.[28] Ngaphambilini, ibhange beligcina ama-akhawunti angasese nawezohwebo azo zonke izinhlobo zamakhasimende, okuhlanganisa abantu ngabanye, amabhizinisi amancane kanye nezinhlangano zomphakathi; kodwa ukushintsha kwenqubomgomo okwalandela iMpi Yezwe Yokuqala kwabona ukuthi ibhange liya ngokuya lihoxa kulolu hlobo lwebhizinisi ukuze ligxile ngokucace kakhulu endimeni yalo yamabhange. 


I-banknote ebhalwe ngesandla yango-1697, yasayinwa 'YoMbusi NeNkampani YeBhange LaseNgilandi' nguCashier Wesibili URobert Hedges 
Phakathi Nempi Yeminyaka Eyisishiyagalolunye, iRoyal Navy yanqotshwa Umbutho Wamasosha Wasemanzini waseFrance ngo-1690 Battle of Beachy Head, okwabangela ukudideka kuhulumeni kaWilliam III waseNgilandi. Uhulumeni wamaNgisi wanquma ukwakha kabusha iRoyal Navy ibe ibutho elalikwazi ukubekela amaFulentshi inselele ngokulingana; nokho, ikhono labo lokwenza kanjalo laphazanyiswa ukuntuleka kwezimali zomphakathi ezitholakalayo kanye nesikweletu esincane sikahulumeni. Lokhu kuntuleka kwesikweletu kwenza uhulumeni wamaNgisi angakwazi ukuboleka imali engu-£1.5m ayefuna ukuyisebenzisela ukwandisa iRoyal Navy.[32]


Ngo-1691, uWilliam Paterson wayehlongoze ukusungula ibhange likazwelonke njengendlela yokuqinisa ezezimali zomphakathi.[33] Njengoba kamuva abhala epheshaneni lakhe elithi A Brief Account of the Intended Bank of England (1694): 

“...kwahlongozwa eminyakeni ethile edlule ukuthi iSikhwama Semali Senzalo esidluliselwa emphakathini kufanele sisungulwe yiPhalamende, senze kube lula ukuthola amarisidi kanye nezinkokhelo emadolobheni aseLondon naseWestminster; futhi kwakhiwe iNhlangano Yabantu Abanemali ukuze banikeze uhulumeni Izabelo zabo. Fund, ngazo zonke izidingo" 

Nakuba uhlelo lwakhe lungazange lusukunyelwe ngokushesha, lunikeze isisekelo soMqulu wokuqala webhange kanye nomthetho owenze ukuthi ukusungulwa kwalo kube nokwenzeka 

Abanye abantu ababili ababalulekile ekwakhiweni kwebhange kwakunguCharles Montagu, ILungu LePhalamende laseMaldon, owabamba iqhaza elibalulekile ekuqondiseni iziphakamiso ngePhalamende (futhi kamuva waqokwa njengoShansela weSigungu Somthetho); kanye noMichael Godfrey, owasiza ekunxenxeni abezimali beDolobha ngezinzuzo zalo (futhi kamuva wakhethwa ukuba abe iPhini LoMbusi wokuqala webhange) 

Kuphinde kwafunwa (ngu-WR Scott, phakathi kwabanye) [35] ukuthi uWilliam Phips wadlala indima efike ngesikhathi, uma kwenzeka kwenzeka: umkhankaso wakhe oyimpumelelo wokubuyisa impango egalaji laseSpain elalicwile (imakethe yase-Nuestra i-Seestra yase-Nuestra isiza ukwakha ibhange lase-Nuestra foundation: ukugcwala imakethe ngenkunzi yemali nokudala umdlandla wokwenza amabhizinisi ahlanganyelwe 

Umthetho u- 

Charles Montagu ubambe iqhaza elikhulu ekusunguleni umthetho wokusungulwa kweBhangengodla futhi uliqondise ku-House of Commons. 
Isiphakamiso sikaPaterson sasidinga ukuthi uHulumeni asungule isikhwama okwakuzokhokhwa kuso inzalo kwababhalisile. Kwanqunywa ukuthi lokhu kuzohlinzekwa ngemali engenayo evela ku-tonnage, neminye imisebenzi ethile yokuthumela ekhokhiswa njalo i-HM Exchequer; ngakho-ke iPhalamende ligunyaze ukusungulwa kwebhange ngoMthetho we-Tonnage Act 1694[37] ('uMthetho wokunikeza Izikhulu Zazo Izilinganiso Nemisebenzi eminingana phezu kokuThuthukiswa Kwemikhumbi Nemikhumbi kanye naphezu kwe-Beere Ale nobunye Utshwala ukuze kutholwe Izinzuzo Nezinzuzo ezithile kulo Mthetho oshiwo kuBantu abayizinkulungwane eziyikhulu njengoba kufanele kuthuthukiswe izinkulungwane zabantu. ukuqhubeka neMpi ngokumelene neFrance') 

Ukuze kutholwe ukubhalisela imali ebolekiwe, ababhalisile kwakufanele bahlanganiswe negama Lombusi kanye Nenkampani Yebhange LaseNgilandi. Izimali zikahulumeni zazisesimweni esibi kakhulu ngaleso sikhathi[39] kangangokuthi imibandela yokubolekwa kwemali (njengoba ibekwe eMthethweni Wephalamende) yayiwukuthi yayizosetshenzwa ngenani lama-8% ngonyaka; bekuphinde kube nenkokhelo yesevisi engu-£4,000 ngonyaka ekhokhelwa ibhange ngokuphatha imali ebolekiwe.

Umthetho ukhawulele ukutshalwa kwezimali kwababhalisi ukuba kufike ku-£10,000 lilinye ekuqaleni, kanye no-£1,200,000 isiyonke (kwakucatshangwa ukuthi i-Exchequer izonyusa ama-£300,000 asele ngezinye izindlela zokuboleka) Ukuvalwa 

Kokuhlanganiswa 

KweBhange Lase-England Charter (1694), ngu-Lady Janel05 
wase-England, i-Lady Janel05 yase-England. yanikezwa ngomhla zingama-27 kuNtulikazi 1694, izinyanga ezintathu ngemuva kokuphasiswa koMthetho 

. 1,268 abantu ababhalisile. Izimpahla zabo zaziwa ngokuthi I-Bank Stock (I-Bank Stock yaqhubeka nokuba ngaphansi kobunikazi obuzimele kwaze kwaba ngu-1946 lapho iBhange LaseNgilandi ligunyazwa ukuba libe ngaphansi kombuso).[40] Iningi lababhalisi bokuqala 'babengabesigaba esimaphakathi se-mercantile sase-London' (nakuba abahwebi nezingcweti nabo babhalisele ukubhalisa).[41] Iningi (ngaphezulu kokubili kokuthathu) linikele ngaphansi kuka-£1,000. Njengengxenye yenani eliphelele eliqoqiwe, u-25% uvela ku-'esquires', u-21% uvela kubathengisi futhi u-15% uvela ezikhundleni eziphakeme. Amaphesenti ayishumi nambili ababhalisile bokuqala kwakungabesifazane.[41] INkosi uWilliam kanye neNdlovukazi uMary (ngokuhlangene) batshale u-£10,000, isamba esiphezulu esivunyelwe, njengoba kwenza nedlanzana labanye (kuhlanganise noSir John Houblon) 

Ukutshalwa kwezimali ebuthweni lasolwandle kwenzeka ngendlela efanele. Njengomphumela ongemuhle, umzamo omkhulu wezimboni odingekayo (okuhlanganisa nokusungula izinsimbi ukwenza izinzipho ezengeziwe kanye nenqubekela phambili[ukucaciswa okudingekayo] kwezolimo ukondla amandla aphindwe kane ebutho lasolwandle) waqala ukuguqula umnotho. Lokhu kwasiza uMbuso omusha weGreat Britain - iNgilandi neScotland zahlanganiswa ngokusemthethweni ngo-1707 - ukuba zibe namandla. Amandla eRoyal Navy enza iBrithani yaba umbuso wezwe obusayo ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-18 nasekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19 

Ukubusa 
Umbusi wokuqala webhange kwakunguJohn Houblon, kanye nePhini LoMbusi wokuqala uMichael Godfrey. (Eminyakeni engama-330 kamuva, ngo-1994, ibhange lalizokhipha inothi lika-£50 elibonisa u-Houblon ukuthi aphawule i-tercentenary yayo.) 


Incwadi yokuqala yeBhange LaseNgilandi, enophawu lwe-Britannia, esayinwe yi-Chief Cashier, u-Thomas Madockes, futhi yango-1699 
ukuBusa kwanikezwa uMbusi, iPhini lakhe kanye 'noMqondisi Wenkantolo' (owayenguMqondisi Wenkantolo Enkulu). aqashwe eDolobheni); Abaqondisi bakhethwa minyaka yonke 'yiNkantolo Jikelele' yabo bonke abanikazi bamasheya ababhalisiwe beBhange (bebonke abaziwa ngokuthi 'Abanikazi'). Uphawu oluvamile lweNkantolo Yabaqondisi, olwamukelwa mhla zingama-30 kuJulayi 1694, lubonisa 'i-Britannia ihlezi futhi ibheke Ibhange Lemali'; I-Britannia ibiwuphawu lwebhange kusukela ngaleso sikhathi.

INkantolo yaqoka izikhulu eziphezulu ezintathu, kanye noMbusi kanye nePhini LoMbusi, ababenomthwalo wemfanelo ekusebenzeni kwayo kwansuku zonke kwebhange: Unobhala kanye Nommeli, Obambe iqhaza WokuQala kanye Nomphathi Wezimali Wokuqala. (Abalandela esikhundleni, uNobhala, uMgcini-zimali Omkhulu kanye noMphathi Omkhulu Wezimali, baqhubekile nokuhola izigaba eziyinhloko zokusebenza kwebhange eminyakeni engu-250 elandelayo: Umphathi Wezimali Omkhulu kanye noMgcini-zincwadi Omkhulu babephethe 'uhlangothi lwemali' kanye 'nohlangothi lwesitokwe' sebhange, ngokulandelana, kuyilapho uNobhala eqondise ukuphathwa kwalo kwangaphakathi.) 

Ngaphandle kwalezi zikhulu, i-1694 yabasebenzi basebhange beyi-1694 kanye nabasebenzi ababili basebhange. abalindisango. 

Izakhiwo 
Ibhange ekuqaleni lalingenaso isakhiwo salo, lavulwa okokuqala mhla lu-1 kuNcwaba 1694 eMercers' Hall eCheapside. Lokhu kodwa kwatholakala kukuncane kakhulu futhi kusukela zingama-31 kuZibandlela 1694 ibhange lasebenza lisuka eHholo LaseGrocers (elalisendaweni yasePoultry ngaleso sikhathi), lapho lalizohlala khona iminyaka ecishe ibe ngu-40.[47] (U-Houblon uke wasebenza njengoMphathi Wenkampani Yokuthenga Ukudla ngo-1690–1691.) 

Umsebenzi 
Umthetho Wephalamende wenqabela ibhange ukuthi lihwebe ngezimpahla noma impahla yanoma yiluphi uhlobo, nakuba lalivunyelwe ukuhwebelana ngegolide nesiliva, kanye nezikweletu zokushintshanisa.[48] Kungakabiphi, ibhange lase likhulisa inzuzo yalo ngokukhipha ama-banknotes, lithathe amadiphozithi futhi libolekise ngemali yokubambisa. 

Ezinsukwini zalo zakuqala ibhange lenza ukulahlekelwa okukhulu, hhayi okungenani ngokwamukela izinhlamvu zemali ezisikiwe ukuze lithole imali yalo engamaphepha.[48] Ukusungulwa kweBhange Lomhlaba (nguJohn Asgill kanye noNicholas Barbon) ngo-1695, kanye nokushoda kwemali okwabangelwa yi-Great Recoinage ka-1696, kokubili kwasongela isikhundla sebhange; [26] kodwa iPhalamende langenelela, lashaya omunye uMthetho ngalowo nyaka, owagunyaza ibhange ukuthi lenyuse inhlokodolobha yalo ibe ngaphezu kuka-£2.2 wezigidi ngokukhuliswa kwesitoko esisha. I-Dividend Day 

yekhulunyaka le-18 

eBhange, 1770. Ihholo Lokukhokha lika-1732 lalingelinye lamabhilidi okuqala eBhange ku-Threadneedle Street. (Ngesinye isikhathi abanikazi bamasheya kwakudingeka bazifikele mathupha ukuze bakhokhele izabelo zikaHulumeni; lo mkhuba waqedwa ngo-1910). 
Ngo-1700, i-Hollow Sword Blade Company yathengwa iqembu losomabhizinisi ababefisa ukusungula ibhange lamaNgisi eliqhudelanayo (ngesenzo namuhla esizobhekwa "njengohlu lwangemuva"). Ukubusa kweBhange LaseNgilandi okokuqala ebhange laseNgilandi kwakuzophelelwa yisikhathi ngo-1710. Nokho, esikhundleni salokho lavuselelwa, futhi inkampani yeSword Blade yahluleka ukufeza umgomo wayo.

Umbono kanye neqiniso lesikweletu sikazwelonke kwavela ngalesi sikhathi, futhi lokhu kwakulawulwa kakhulu yibhange. Ngomthetho we-1715 Ways and Means Act, iPhalamende lagunyaza ibhange ukuthi lithole izikhokhelo zokukhishwa kukahulumeni kwama-annuities angu-5%, okuklanyelwe ukuqongelela u-£910,000;[50] lokhu kwaphawula ukuqala kwendima yebhange ekuphatheni Izitokwe Zikahulumeni, okwakuyindlela yokuthi abantu batshale imali esikweletini sikahulumeni (ngaphambilini ukuboleka kukaHulumeni kwakuphethwe yi-Excher ngokuqondile).[46] Ibhange lalibophezelekile ngokoMthetho ukuthi likhokhe izabelo zengxenye yonyaka kanye nokugcina irekhodi lencwadi yakho konke ukudluliselwa (njengoba lase lijwayele ukukwenza kakade maqondana neSitoko Salo Sebhange). 

Ibhange lalingenawo amandla okuboleka uhulumeni, nokho: I-South Sea Company yasungulwa ngo-1711, futhi ngo-1720 nayo yaba nesibopho sengxenye yesikweletu sikazwelonke sase-UK, yaba imbangi enkulu yeBhange LaseNgilandi. Ngenkathi inhlekelele ye-"South Sea Bubble" iqala ngokushesha, inkampani yaqhubeka nokuphatha ingxenye yesikweletu sikazwelonke sase-UK kwaze kwaba ngu-1853. I-East India Company nayo yayingamaboleki okuzikhethela kuhulumeni. 

Ngo-1734 kwakunabasebenzi abangamashumi ayisishiyagalolunye nesithupha ebhange.[46] I-charter yebhange yavuselelwa ngo-1742, futhi futhi ngo-1764. Ngomthetho we-1742 ibhange laba ukuphela kwenkampani yamasheya evunyelwe ukukhipha amanothi ebhange edolobheni elikhulu. 

I-Threadneedle Street 

A Perspective View yeBhange Lase-England (eyanyatheliswa ngo-1756): ibhange ekuqaleni belithatha indawo ewumngcingo ngemuva kwengaphambili ku-Threadneedle Street. 
IBhange LaseNgilandi lathuthela endaweni yalo yamanje, endaweni yendlu nengadi kaSir John Houblon ku-Threadneedle Street (eduze nesonto lika-St Christopher le Stocks), ngo-1734. [52] (Ifa lalithengiwe eminyakeni eyishumi ngaphambili; uHoublon wayeshone ngo-1712, kodwa umfelokazi wakhe wahlala endlini waze washona ngo-1731, okwathi ngemva kwalokho indlu yabhidlizwa futhi kwaqala ukusebenza ebhange.)
 
Le ndawo eyayisanda kwakhiwa, eyaklanywa uGeorge Sampson, yayisendaweni eyingcingo (engaba amafidi angu-80 (cishe amafidi angu-80 (24 m) onwetshiwe enyakatho yoMthaladi ongu-24.[] Isakhiwo esingaphambili sasinamahhovisi okudlulisa imali esitezi sokuqala, ngaphansi kwawo kwakunekhothamo lokungena eliholela egcekeni. Kubheke ngasemnyango 'kwakuyisakhiwo esikhulu' sebhange:[54] iHholo elikhulu (79 ft × 40 ft (24 m × 12 m)) lapho amanothi ebhange akhishwa khona futhikushintshaniswa,[55] nalapho amadiphozithi kanye nokuhoxiswa kungenziwa.[41] (Ihholo Elikhulu likaSampson, kamuva elaziwa ngokuthi i-Pay Hall, lahlala likhona futhi lisetshenziswa kwaze kwaba yilapho u-Herbert Baker ehlanganisa ukwakhiwa kabusha okuphelele kwawo-1920s.)[56] Ngale kweHholo kwakukhona unxantathu wezakhiwo ezivale 'igceke leNkantolo ebanzi nenesizotha' (kamuva elaziwa ngokuthi iBullion Court). Ohlangothini oluseningizimu lonxantathu kwakukhona iGumbi Lenkantolo kanye neGumbi LeKomiti, ohlangothini olusenyakatho kwakukhona iHhovisi Lokugcinwa Kwamabhuku Ezimali elikhulu; nhlangothi zombili kwakunemizila yokuhamba, enamakamelo ezikhulu eziphezulu, kuyilapho ezitezi ezingaphezulu zinamahhovisi namafulethi.[53] Ngaphansi kwe-quadrangle kwakunamakamelo angaphansi ('anezindonga eziqine kakhulu namasango Ensimbi, Okulondoloza Imali'); ukungena egcekeni kwakuhlinzekiwe, ngendlela yephaseji eliholela 'esangweni elikhulu' ku-Bartholomew Lane, labaqeqeshi nezinqola 'ezifika njalo zilayishwe Igolide Nesiliva'.[54] Uhlangothi olungaphezu komnyango weHholo elikhulu lwaluhlotshiswe ngomfanekiso oqoshiwe we-alto relievo waseBritannia (owayevele ocingweni oluvamile lwebhange kusukela ngomhla ka-30 Julayi 1694); [57] umqophi wezithombe kwakunguRobert Taylor, owaqokwa njengomakhi, ngokulandelana kukaSampson, ngo-1764. III,[58] edunyiswa embhalweni wesiLatini ohambisana naso njengomsunguli webhange (i-conditor);[48] ngakolunye uhlangothi, iwindi elikhulu laseVenice lalibheke egcekeni lesonto likaSt Christopher. 

Ukunwetshwa 

I-Threadneedle Street front ngo-1773, ngemva kokwengezwa kophiko lukaTaylor olusempumalanga kodwa ngaphambi kokubhidlizwa kweSt Christopher le Stocks (kwesobunxele)
Engxenyeni yesibili yekhulu le-18 ibhange lathola kancane kancane iziza zomhlaba ezingomakhelwane ukuze likwazi ukunwetshwa, futhi ngemva kuka-1765 izakhiwo ezintsha zaqala ukungezwa ngumdwebi webhange owayesanda kumiswa uRobert Taylor. Enyakatho-ntshonalanga ye-Pay Hall, ebheke egcekeni lesonto lika-St Christopher eningizimu, u-Taylor wakhela Abaqondisi bebhange isudu yamagumbi agxile eGumbi Lenkantolo (elikhudlwana) kanye neGumbi Lekomidi (Ngesikhathi ibhange lakhiwa kabusha ngeminyaka yawo-1920s-30s, lawa magumbi asuswa endaweni yawo yokuqala eyisitezi futhi aphinde akhiwa kabusha asetshenziswa esitezi sokuqala seNkantolo; Ikomidi Lenqubomgomo Yezezimali ngokulandelanayo.).[59][60] EMpumalanga ye-Pay Hall, u-Taylor wakha uchungechunge lwamahholo namahhovisi anikezelwe ekuphathweni kwamasheya nezabelo, okuphindaphindeka kakhudlwana noma ngaphansi kobukhulu bendawo yebhange (ukunweba kuze kufike e-Bartholomew Lane).[41] Lawa makamelo ayegxile eRotunda enkulu, eyaziwa nangokuthi i-Brokers' Exchange, lapho ukuthengiswa kwe-Government Stock kwenzeka khona; nxazonke kwahlelwa amaHhovisi Okudlulisa Amakhulu amane, ngalinye lihambisana nesikhwama esihlukile (njengoba kuchazwe ngeminyaka yawo-1820: 'Ehhovisi ngalinye ngaphansi kwezinhlamvu ezimbalwa zezinhlamvu, kuhlelwa izincwadi okubhaliswe kuzo amagama abo bonke abantu abanempahla ezikhwameni, kanye nemininingwane yezintshisekelo zabo'). [48] Wonke lawa mahhovisi ayekhanyisiwe, ukugwema isidingo samafasitela ezindongeni ezingaphandle. 


Ibhange ngo-1797: amaphiko asempumalanga nasentshonalanga ngu-Sir Robert Taylor flank Sampson's centerpiece ka-1733. 
Ngo-1782 isonto lika-St Christopher le Stocks labhidlizwa, okwavumela ibhange ukuthi linwebele ngasentshonalanga ku-Threadneedle Street. Uphiko olusha olusentshonalanga lwaqedwa ekwakhiweni kukaTaylor ngo-1786 (ingaphambili lalo elifana nephiko likaTaylor elisempumalanga): lalihlala iHhovisi Le-Reduced Annuities Office, i-Check Office kanye ne-Dividend Warrant Office (phakathi kokunye). Ngokushesha enyakatho kwakukhona indawo yesonto yangaphambili yase-St Christopher le Stocks, eyayigcinwe ngaphakathi kwezakhiwo njengengadi (eyaziwa ngokuthi 'Inkantolo Yengadi'). Enyakatho yeNkantolo yaseBullion, uTaylor wakha umtapo wolwazi omusha onezitezi ezine, ozogcina iqoqo lebhange elikhulayo lezingobo zomlando. 

I-Bank Picquet 
Ukubhidlizwa kwebandla kudalwe izibhelu zika-1780 Gordon, lapho kubikwa ukuthi izibhelu zagibela esontweni zizojikijela amabhilidi ebhange. Phakathi nezibhelu, ngo-June 1780, iNkosi Mayor yaseLondon yanxusa uNobhala Wezwe ukuba athumele unogada wezempi ukuze avikele ibhange kanye ne-Mansion House.[61] Kusukela lapho unogada wasebusuku ('i-Bank Picquet') wanikezwa amasosha e-Household Brigade (umkhuba owaqhubeka kwaze kwaba ngu-1973). Ukuze kuhlaliswe unogada u-Taylor wakha inkambu (okungenwa kuyo ngomnyango ohlukile ku-Princes Street) ekhoneni elisenyakatho-ntshonalanga yesiza.

Ukwakhiwa kabusha kukaJohn Soane
I-Bank of England Site Act 1793 

Ihhovisi le-Dividend njengoba lakhiwa kabusha ngu-John Soane 
Sir Robert Taylor washona ngo-1788 futhi esikhundleni sakhe ibhange laqoka u-John Soane njengoMklami kanye noMhloli (uzohlala esikhundleni kuze kube ngu-1827). Ngaphansi kokuqondisa kwakhe, ibhange laphinde lanwetshwa futhi lakhiwa kabusha kancane kancane, kodwa kwaba uhlelo oluhlangene. Ukuhlolwa kwezakhiwo, okwenziwa ekuqaleni kokubusa kwakhe, kuhlonze izinkinga ezithile, ezalungiswa ngokushesha nguSoane: isibonelo ngo-1795 wakha kabusha iRotunda kanye namaHhovisi Okudluliselwa Kwamabhilidi amabili aseduze (iHhovisi Lezimali Zebhange kanye ne-Four Per Cent Office), esikhundleni sophahla lukaTaylor, olwaluvuza, ngamatshe aqinile.[62] Ngesikhathi esifanayo uSoane wanikwa umsebenzi wokuthenga izindawo enyakatho-mpumalanga, ngamandla okuthenga ayimpoqo anikezwe iBank of England Site Act 1793 (33 Geo. 3. c. 15), ukuze ibhange likwazi ukunwebeka ngalolo hlangothi kuze kufike eLothbury. Phakathi kuka-1794 no-1800 waklama isethi ehlangene yezakhiwo ngaphakathi kwendawo entsha emise ngendlela engavamile: walungisa kabusha i-Bullion Court futhi wanikeza indlela entsha yokungena yezimoto ezivela enyakatho, eyaqanjwa ngokuthi iNkantolo yaseLothbury;[63] entshonalanga yalokhu wakha ihhovisi elisha likaCashier Omkhulu, kanye namakamelo kaNobhala noMgcini-zincwadi Omkhulu; empumalanga wakha ibhulokhi entsha yoMtapo Wezincwadi futhi wengeza Ihhovisi Lokudluliswa Kwezinto Lesihlanu (iHhovisi Lokudluliswa Kwama-Consols) enyakatho kwamanye amane. 

I-Brokers' Exchange e-Bank 

Soane's Rotunda, isasetshenziswa njengendawo yokuhweba (1804) 
Ekupheleni kwekhulu le-18 nasekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19, ngaphambi kokusungulwa kweLondon Stock Exchange, i-Rotunda eBhange LaseNgilandi yayisetshenziswa njengendawo yokuhweba 'lapho abadayisi, abadayisi, nabanye abantu, behlangana khona ngenjongo yokwenza imali yomphakathi'5. Ukusuka e-Rotunda 'kwabe ngamahhovisi abelwe abaphathi besitoko ngasinye' aqukethe izincwadi ezibonisa isithakazelo esibhalisiwe somuntu ngamunye esikhwameni. Ukusetshenziswa kwe-Rotunda ekuhwebeni kwaphela ngo-1838, kodwa yaqhubeka nokusetshenziselwa ukukhishwa kwezincwadi ezigunyaza izabelo zezabelo. 

Izingxabano kanye nezinkinga zezikweletu 

Ikhathuni yeSatirical ephikisana nokwethulwa kwemali yephepha, nguJames Gillray, 1797. "I-Old Lady yaseThreadneedle St" (ibhange elenziwe samuntu) lihlukunyezwa nguWilliam Pitt Omncane. 
Inkinga yezikweletu yango-1772 ichazwe njengenkinga yokuqala yesimanje yamabhange ebhekene neBhange LaseNgilandi.[65] Lonke iDolobha laseLondon laba nesiphithiphithi lapho u-Alexander Fordyce kumenyezelwa ukuthi akanamali.[66] Ngo-August 1773, iBhange LaseNgilandi lasiza i-EIC ngemalimboleko.[67] Ubunzima bemali egciniwe yeBhange LaseNgilandi aluzange lwehliswe kwaze kwaba sekupheleni konyaka. 

Ngesikhathi seMpi Yokuzimela yaseMelika, ibhizinisi lebhange lalihle kakhulu kangangokuthi uGeorge Washington wahlala engumnikazi wamasheya kuso sonke isikhathi.

Ngokuvuselelwa kwe-charter yebhange ngo-1781, laliphinde libe yibhange labamabhange - ligcina igolide elanele ukukhokha amanothi alo lapho lifunwa khona kuze kube umhla zingama-26 kuNhlolanja 1797 lapho impi isinciphe kakhulu imali egciniwe yegolide kangangokuthi - kulandela ukuhlasela okwabangelwa yiMpi Yezinhlanzi ezinsukwini ngaphambili - uhulumeni wenqabela ibhange ukuthi likhokhe nge-bank17 Restrition Act of the bank17 Restrition Act. kwaze kwaba ngu-1821. 

Ngo-1798, phakathi Nezimpi Zenguquko YaseFrance, kwasungulwa i-Corps of bank Volunteers (yamadoda aphakathi kuka-450 no-500) ukuvikela ibhange uma kwenzeka lihlaselwa. Yahlakazwa ngo-1802, kodwa yaphinde yakhiwa kabusha ngonyaka olandelayo ekuqaleni Kwezimpi ZaseNapoleonic. Amasosha alo ayeqeqeshwa, uma kwenzeka ehlaselwa, ukuba akhiphe igolide nesiliva emagumbini angaphansi aliyise endaweni eqhelile, kanye nemishini yokunyathelisa yemali engamaphepha namarekhodi athile abalulekile.[70] Kwanikezwa indawo yezikhali endaweni eku-Threadneedle Street ukuze bathole izingalo zabo nezinto zabo.[48] I-Corps yagcina yahlakazwa ngo-1814. 

I-19th Century 

View of the Bank of England ithathwe engxenyeni esenyakatho-ntshonalanga njengoba yakhiwa ngo-1805 (JM Gandy, 1825) 
Ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19 uhlelo lwenziwa u-John Soane ukuze kunwetshwe indawo yebhange, kulokhu kuya enyakatho-ntshonalanga ye-Street, i-routing entsha ye-Princess Street. endaweni). Indawo enkulu yesandiso esisha yathathwa ngomshini wokunyathelisa osebenza ngesitimu ukuze kunyatheliswe imali engamaphepha (amanothi aqhubeka enyatheliswa endaweni kwaze kwaba yiMpi Yezwe Yokuqala, lapho isibhedlela sangaphambili sase-St Luke's sitholwa futhi saguqulwa saba imisebenzi yokunyathelisa yebhange).[71] USoane waqhubeka nomsebenzi kwaze kwaba ngu-1833; eminyakeni yokugcina ngaphambi kokuthatha umhlalaphansi wakhe waphothula ukwakha kabusha uphiko lukaTaylor olusempumalanga futhi walungisa kabusha amafaçade abheke emgwaqeni ka-Sampson no-Taylor ukuze enze yonke i-perimeter ye-complex iphelele. 

Ngo-1811, 'iwashi elakhiwe ngobuhlakani' yi-Thwaites & Co. lafakwa ngenhla kweHholo Lokukhokha:[72] kanye nokushaya amahora nekota, lalidlulisa isikhathi ukude (ngezinduku zethusi ezinweba isamba esingamafidi angu-700 (210 m) ubude) ekushayeleni okutholakala emahhovisi ahlukene ayishumi nesithupha endaweni.

 
I-Pay Hall (lapho amanothi ashintshwa khona ngezinhlamvu zemali, futhi okuphambene nalokho) efanekiselwa ngo-1866.
'Uvalo lwango-1825' lwagqamisa ubungozi obukhona ekuhlukaniseni izindlela ezintathu kwebhange: kubanini bamasheya, kuHulumeni (futhi ngalokho nasemphakathini), kanye nakumakhasimende alo amabhange ezentengiselwano. Ngo-1825-26 ibhange lakwazi ukunqanda inkinga yokuswelakala kwemali ngesikhathi uNathan Mayer Rothschild ephumelela ukulihlinzeka ngegolide;[74] nokho, ngemva kwale nkinga, amabhange amaningi ezwe kanye nezifundazwe ahluleka ukubangela ukuqothuka okuningi kwezentengiselwano.[75] Ukuphasiswa kwe-Country Bankers Act 1826 kwavumela ibhange ukuthi livule amagatsha ezifundazwe ukuze kusatshalaliswe kangcono imali yalo engamaphepha (ngaleso sikhathi amabhange amancane ezwe, amanye awo ayengenamali eningi kakhulu, ekhipha amanothi awo); ekupheleni konyaka olandelayo amagatsha ayisishiyagalombili eBhange LaseNgilandi ayesemiswe ezweni lonke. 


I-Bank Stock yeBhange LaseNgilandi, eyakhishwa zingama-25 kuMasingana 1876 
I-Bank Charter Act 1844 yabophela indaba yamanothi ezinqolobaneni zegolide futhi yanikeza iBhange LaseNgilandi kuphela amalungelo maqondana nokukhishwa kwemali engamaphepha eNgilandi. Amabhange azimele ngaphambili ayenalelo lungelo aligcina, inqobo nje uma indlunkulu yawo ingaphandle kwaseLondon futhi efaka isibambiso kumanothi awakhiphile; kodwa banikezwa ithuba lokuliyeka leli lungelo. (Ibhange elizimele lokugcina eNgilandi ukukhipha alo amanothi kwakuyibhange likaThomas Fox, iFowler kanye neNkampani eWellington, elakhula ngokushesha laze lahlanganiswa neLloyds Bank ngo-1927. Ahlala ethenda esemthethweni kwaze kwaba ngu-1964. (Kusele amanothi ayisishiyagalolunye; elinye ligcinwe eTone Dale House, eWellington.)) 

Ibhange ligcine ukusebenza68 njengokwethuka okokuqala ngqa. 

Ikhulu lama-20 

Inothi leBhange elimhlophe lopondo amahlanu lahlala lisetshenziswa kwaze kwaba ngu-1957. 
Kwaze kwaba ngu-1931 iBrithani yayisezingeni legolide, okusho ukuthi inani le-sterling lalinqunywa inani legolide. Ngalowo nyaka, iBhange LaseNgilandi kwadingeka lisuse iBrithani ezingeni legolide ngenxa yemiphumela yokucindezeleka Okukhulu okusakazekela eYurophu. 

Ngo-1913 ukuzama ukuqhunyiswa kwamabhomu 
Bheka futhi: Umkhankaso wokuqhunyiswa kwamabhomu kanye nokushiswa kwe-Suffragette 

Amabhomu amabili e-suffragette aboniswe e-City of London Police Museum ngo-2019. Ibhomu elingakwesobunxele lasetshenziswa ekuzameni ukuqhuma kwamabhomu ngaphandle kwebhange ngomhla ka-4 ku-April 1913, ukuhlasela okungenzeka kwadala ukulimala okuningi ukube akuzange kuvinjwe. 
Kwazanywa ibhomu lamaphekula ngaphandle kwebhilidi laseBhange LaseNgilandi ngomhla ka-4 Ephreli 1913. Kwatholakala ibhomu lishunqa futhi selilungele ukuqhuma eduze kwezinsimbi ngaphandle kwebhilidi.[78][79] Ibhomu lalifakwe njengengxenye yomkhankaso wokuqhunyiswa kwamabhomu kanye nokushiswa kwempahla, lapho i-Women's Social and Political Union (WSPU) yethula uchungechunge lwamabhomu kanye nokuhlasela okugqugquzelwa yipolitiki ezweni lonke njengengxenye yomkhankaso wabo wokulwela amalungelo abesifazane.[79][80] Ibhomu lanqanyulwa ngaphambi kokuba liqhume, endaweni ngaleso sikhathi eyayingomunye wemigwaqo yomphakathi ephithizelayo enhloko-dolobha, okungenzeka ukuthi ivimbele abantu abaningi abalimalayo.[79][81] Ibhomu lalifakwe ngosuku olulandelayo umholi we-WSPU u-Emmeline Pankhurst egwetshwe iminyaka emithathu ebhadla ejele ngokuqhumisa ibhomu emzini kasopolitiki uDavid Lloyd George.

Izinsalela zaleli bhomu, elakhelwe endaweni yokusebenzela ubisi, manje seziyabukiswa e-City of London Police Museum. 

Ukuhlela Kabusha Nokwakha Kabusha 
Ngesikhathi sokuphatha kukaMontagu Norman, kusukela ngo-1920 kuya ku-1944, ibhange lenza imizamo eqondile yokusuka emabhange okuhweba libe yibhange elikhulu. Umbusi wakamuva, uRobin Leigh-Pemberton, wasichaza 'njengesikhathi soshintsho olusheshayo, lapho saqala khona ukuqhela emasikweni abefundisi beminyaka engu-200 [...] futhi samukele uchwepheshe, umshini kanye neziyalo zokuphatha zesimanje'.[46] Osomnotho kanye nezibalo baqale ukuqashwa ebhange ngenani elikhulayo. Ngo-1931 'Ikomidi Lepigogo', elasungulwa ukuze leluleke ngokuthuthukiswa kwenhlangano, lashicilela izincomo ezihlanganisa ukuqokwa kwabaqondisi abakhulu abakhokhelwayo (kanye namalungu endabuko angewona aphethe eNkantolo). Iphinde yancoma ukumiswa kabusha kwezinhlaka zomnyango ezijwayelekile zebhange. 


Ibhange lika-Baker elakhiwe kabusha limi ngemuva kodonga lwamakhethini luka-Soane olugcinelwe ingxenye 
Umsebenzi webhange usukhule kakhulu kusukela ekupheleni kweMpi Yezwe Yokuqala, futhi isinqumo sathathwa sokunwetshwa. Phakathi kuka-1925 no-1939 indlunkulu yebhange ku-Threadneedle Street yakhiwa kabusha ngokuphelele ngu-Herbert Baker. (Lokhu kwakuhilela ukubhidlizwa kwezakhiwo eziningi zikaSir John Soane, isenzo esichazwe isazi-mlando sezokwakha u-Nikolaus Pevsner “njengobugebengu obukhulu kakhulu bezakhiwo, eDolobheni laseLondon, ekhulwini lamashumi amabili.)[82] Ekuqaleni icebo bekuwukugcina amahholo amabhange ka-Soane ngemuva kodonga lwamakhethini, kodwa lokhu kwafakazela inselele futhi kwaba inselele. Ukubhidliza nokwakhiwa kabusha kwenzeke ngezigaba, abasebenzi besuka kwenye ingxenye yesakhiwo beya kwenye (noma, kwezinye izimo, bayohlala endaweni yesikhashana e-Finsbury Circus). Inkunzi nezibambiso zahlala endaweni yonke. Ngesikhathi kwakhiwa kabusha izinsalela zabantu eziphathelene negceke lesonto elidala lase-St Christopher le Stocks zambiwa futhi zangcwatshwa kabusha emathuneni aseNunhead. 
Ngo-1939 kwethulwa i-Exchange Controls e-United Kingdom ngesikhathi kugqashuka iMpi Yezwe Yesibili; lezi zazilawulwa yibhange.[46] Phakathi ne-WWII, ngaphezu kwe-10% yenani lobuso lokuzungeza imali yamaphepha e-Pound Sterling kwakungamanga akhiqizwa yiJalimane.


Isithombe sika-Ariel nguCharles Wheeler
Isakhiwo sika-Baker esiwuhlaka lwensimbi sinezitezi eziyisikhombisa ukuphakama, nezinye izitezi ezintathu ezinwebeka ngaphansi kwezinga eliphansi. Ihlotshiswe ngezithombe eziqoshiwe nezethusi kaCharles Wheeler, i-plasterwork ka-Joseph Armitage kanye ne-mosaic ka-Boris Anrep.[83] Ibhange namuhla liyibhilidi elibhalwe uGrade I. 


Inani lemisebenzi yebhange kanye nabasebenzi bathuthelwe eHampshire ngesikhathi sempi, okuhlanganisa nemisebenzi yokunyathelisa (eyathuthela e-Overton), uMnyango Wezimali (owaya e-Hurstbourne Park) namanye amahhovisi ahlukahlukene. Labo abasala ku-Threadneedle Street, kuhlanganise nabaqondisi, bathuthele amahhovisi abo ezindaweni ezingaphansi komhlaba. 

Ukwenziwa ngaphansi kombuso ngemuva kwempi 
Ngo-1946, ngemuva nje kokuphela kokuphatha kukaMontagu Norman, leli bhange lafakwa ngaphansi kukahulumeni wabasebenzi. Ngaso leso sikhathi isibalo sabaQondisi sehliswa saba ishumi nesithupha (abane kubo bekungabaqondisi abakhulu besikhathi esigcwele). 

Ibhange laphishekela imigomo eminingi yezomnotho zaseKeynesian ngemuva kuka-1945, ikakhulukazi "imali elula" kanye namazinga enzalo ephansi ukusekela ukufunwa okuhlanganisiwe. Izamile ukugcina izinga lokushintshanisa okungaguquki futhi yazama ukubhekana nokwehla kwamandla emali kanye nobuthakathaka be-sterling ngezilawuli zekhredithi kanye nokuhwebelana. 


I-Bank of England New Change (ngezansi kwesokudla) njengoba ibonakala e-St Paul's 
Ngemva kwempi, uMnyango Wezezimali omkhulu kakhulu (owayephethe uhlangothi lwesitoko sebhange) wabuyela e-London usuka eHampshire. Indawo yayo yehhovisi emisiwe ku-Threadneedle Street, nokho, ngaleso sikhathi, yayisithathwe ihhovisi le-Exchange Control. Umnyango esikhundleni salokho wanikezwa indawo yokuhlala yesikhashana (ephinde e-Finsbury Circus), kusalindwe ukwakhiwa kwebhilidi elisha, elizothatha indawo yebhomu engamahektare amabili empumalanga ye-St Paul's Cathedral. 'I-Bank of England New Change' yaklanywa u-Victor Heal futhi yavulwa ngo-1957 (ngaleso sikhathi kwakuyiphrojekthi enkulu yaseLondon yokwakha kabusha ngemva kwempi);[86] isakhiwo esisha sasiqukethe izinsiza zabasebenzi ezimbalwa eceleni kwehhovisi lokuhlala futhi, ezingeni lomgwaqo, amayunithi okudayisa avunyelwe ukuhlukahluka kwamabhizinisi. Ibhange lalinesakhiwo esinesivumelwano sokuqashisa seminyaka engu-200; kodwa ngokufika kwezinombolo zabasebenzi bekhompyutha zehliswa kakhulu ngeminyaka yawo-1980-90s; izingxenye zesakhiwo zavunyelwa kwezinye izimboni (ikakhulukazi inkampani yabameli i-Allen & Overy). Ibhange ladayisa lesi sakhiwo ngo-2000 kwathi ngo-2007 sabhidlizwa; Ushintsho Olusha Olulodwa manje lumi kusayithi. 

I-"10 bob note" yebhange yahoxiswa ekusetshenzisweni ngo-1970 kulungiselelwa uSuku lweDesimali ngo-1971. 


Amabhondi ase-United Kingdom

  1 unyaka

  1 inyanga 
Bheka futhi: Ijika lesivuno esihlanekezelwe
Ngo-1977 ibhange lasungula inkampani ephethwe ngokugcwele ebizwa ngokuthi i-Bank of England Nominees Limited (BOEN), okuyinkampani ezimele engasekho, enamasheya ayo amabili e-£1 akhishiwe. Ngokwememorandamu yayo yenhlangano, izinhloso zayo bekuwukuthi: "Ukusebenza njengoPhathiwe noma i-ejenti noma ummeli ngokuhlanganyela noma ngokuhlanganyela nabanye, kunoma yimuphi umuntu noma abantu, ubambiswano, inkampani, inhlangano, uhulumeni, umbuso, inhlangano, umbuso, isifundazwe, igunya, noma inhlangano yomphakathi, nanoma yiliphi iqembu noma inhlangano yabo". I-Bank of England Nominees Limited inikezwe ukukhululwa ngu-Edmund Dell, Unobhala Wezohwebo Wezwe, ezimfuneko zokudalulwa ngaphansi kweSigaba 27(9) soMthetho Wezinkampani 1976, ngenxa yokuthi "kwakubhekwa njengokungathandeki ukuthi izimfuneko zokudalulwa kufanele zisebenze ezigabeni ezithile zabanikazi bamasheya". IBhange LaseNgilandi futhi livikelwe yisikhundla salo sombuso kanye noMthetho Wezimfihlo Ezisemthethweni.[87] I-BOEN bekuyimoto yohulumeni nezinhloko zezifundazwe ukuthi batshale izimali ezinkampanini zase-UK (kuncike ekugunyazweni kukaNobhala Wezwe), inqobo nje uma bezibophezela "ukungabi nomthelela ezindabeni zenkampani".[88] Eminyakeni yayo yakamuva, i-BOEN yayingasakhululekile ezimfuneko zokudalulwa komthetho wenkampani.[89] Nakuba kuyinkampani ethule,[90] ukuhlala kahle akuvimbeli inkampani esebenza ngokugcwele njengomnikazi wamasheya oqokiwe.[91] I-BOEN yayinabanikazi bamasheya ababili: iBhange LaseNgilandi, kanye noNobhala WeBhange LaseNgilandi. 

Imfuneko egciniwe yokuthi amabhange abambe ingxenye encane emisiwe yezimali ezifakwayo njengezigodlo eBhange LaseNgilandi yaqedwa ngo-1981: bheka imfuneko ye-Reserve § United Kingdom ukuze uthole imininingwane eyengeziwe. Ushintsho lwamanje olusuka kwezomnotho lwaseKeynesian luye kwezomnotho lwaseChicago lwahlaziywa nguNicholas Kaldor encwadini ethi The Scourge of Monetarism. 

Ukunikezelwa kwenqubomgomo yezimali ebhange kwaba ipulani eliyinhloko lenqubomgomo yezomnotho ye-Liberal Democrats okhethweni lukazwelonke lwango-1992.[94] Ilungu le-Conservative MP u-Nicholas Budgen naye wayephakamise lokhu njengomthethosivivinywa welungu elizimele ngo-1996, kodwa lo mthethosivivinywa wehluleka njengoba wawungasekelwanga uhulumeni noma abaphikisayo. 

Uhulumeni wase-UK washiya i-European Exchange Rate Mechanism ebizayo ukuze igcinwe ngo-September 1992, isenzo esabiza i-HM Treasury ngaphezu kwe-£3 billion. Lokhu kuholele ekutheni kube nokuxhumana phakathi kukahulumeni naleli bhange. 


Umlando we-inflation yase-UK kusukela ngo-1960 
Bheka futhi: 1976 sterling crisis 
Ngo-1993, ibhange lakhiqizela uhulumeni umbiko walo wokuqala we-Inflation, ochaza kabanzi ngezimo zokwehla kwamandla emali kanye nezingcindezi. Lo mbiko okhiqizwa minyaka yonke uhlala ungomunye wezincwadi ezinkulu zebhange.[84] Impumelelo yokuqondisa ukwehla kwamandla emali e-United Kingdom kudalwe ukugxila kwebhange ekwenziweni kwezinto obala.[95] IBhange LaseNgilandi libe ngumholi ekukhiqizeni izindlela ezintsha zokudlulisela ulwazi emphakathini, ikakhulukazi ngombiko walo Wokukhuphuka Kwamanani Emali,okuyinto amanye amabhange amakhulu amaningi alingise.

Ibhange lagubha usuku lwalo lokuzalwa lamakhulu amathathu ngo-1994. 

Ngo-1996, ibhange lakhiqiza i-Financial Stability Review yokuqala. Le ncwadi yonyaka yaziwa ngokuthi i-Financial Stability Report ngo-2006. [84] Futhi ngalowo nyaka, ibhange lasungula uhlelo lwalo lwe-real-time gross settlement (RTGS) ukuze lithuthukise ukukhokhelana okungenabungozi phakathi kwamabhange ase-UK. 

Mhla ziyisi-6 kuNhlaba 1997, kulandela ukhetho lukazwelonke lwango-1997 olwabeka uhulumeni Wezabasebenzi okokuqala ngqa kusukela ngo-1979, kwamenyezelwa nguShansela we-Exchequer, uGordon Brown, ukuthi ibhange lizonikezwa inkululeko yokusebenza phezu kwenqubomgomo yezimali.[97] Ngaphansi kwemigomo yoMthetho weBhange LaseNgilandi ka-1998 (owaqala ukusebenza mhla lu-1 kuNhlangulana 1998) iKomidi Lenqubomgomo Yezimali (MPC) lanikezwa umthwalo wemfanelo wodwa wokusetha izilinganiso zenzalo ukuze kuhlangatshezwane nemigomo yokwehla kwamandla emali kaHulumeni ye-Retail Prices Index (RPI) engu-2.5%. [98] Okuhlosiwe kushintshile kwaba ngu-2% kusukela Inkomba Yentengo Yabathengi (CPI) ithathele indawo Inkomba Yezintengo Zokudayisa njengenkomba yokwehla kwamandla emali yoMgcinimafa.[99] Uma ukwehla kwamandla emali kweqa noma kwehlisa okuhlosiwe ngaphezu kuka-1% uMbusi kufanele abhalele uShansela we-Exchequer incwadi echaza ukuthi kungani, nokuthi uzosilungisa kanjani lesi simo. 

Amabhange amakhulu azimele asebenzisa i-inflation target aziwa ngokuthi ama-Friedmanite central banks. Lolu shintsho kupolitiki Yezabasebenzi lwachazwa ngu-Skidelsky kwethi Ukubuya Kwengcweti[101] njengephutha futhi njengokwamukelwa kwenkolelo-mbono yokulindela okunengqondo njengoba yamenyezelwa u-Alan Walters.[102] Izinhloso zokwehla kwamandla emali kuhlanganiswe nokuzimela kwamabhange amakhulu kuphawulwe njengesu "lokubulala isilo" elidala ukuntuleka kwemali embonini kahulumeni. 

ngoJuni 1998 umsebenzi wokulawula nokuqondisa amabhange kanye nezimboni zomshwalense wasuswa ebhange wayiswa ku-Financial Services Authority. Imemorandamu yokuqonda ichaze imigomo ibhange, uMnyango Wezezimali, kanye ne-FSA ezosebenzela ngaphansi kwayo ukuze kufezeke inhloso efanayo yokwandisa uzinzo kwezezimali.[103] (Eminyakeni eyishumi kamuva, nokho, ngemva kwenhlekelele yezimali yango-2008, umthetho omusha wamabhange wadlulisela umthwalo wemfanelo wokulawula nokuqondisa izimboni zamabhange nezomshwalense emuva eBhange LaseNgilandi). 

Ikhulu lama-21 

2013: kusukela ngekhulu le-18 abalindisango bebhange bebegqoka 'opinki' (i-livery ehlotshaniswa no-Sir John Houblon).[104] 
Ibhange lanquma ukudayisela u-De La Rue umsebenzi walo wokunyathelisa imali ngo-December 2002, ngaphansi kweseluleko se-Close Brothers Corporate Finance Ltd. 

UMervyn King waba uMbusi WeBhange LaseNgilandi ngo-30 June 2003.

Ngo-2009, isicelo esenziwa kuMgcinimafa we-HM ngaphansi kwe-Freedom of Information Act safuna imininingwane mayelana ne-3% yesitoko saseBhange lase-England esiphethwe abanikazi bamasheya abangadalulwanga igama labo ibhange elingenankululeko yokudalula.[106] Encwadini yempendulo yangomhla ziyi-15 kuMfumfu wezi-2009, uMgcinimafa wakwa-HM wachaza ukuthi "Ezinye ze-3% yesitoko sikaMgcinimafa esasetshenziswa ukunxephezela abanikazi bangaphambili besitoko sasebhange asikahlengwa. Nokho, inzalo ikhokhwa kabili ngonyaka futhi akusikhona ukuthi lokhu bekunqwabelana futhi kuhlanganiswe. I-

  ngonyaka futhi akunjalo ukuthi lokhu bekunqwabelana futhi 
kuhlanganiswe . futhi: Ijika lesivuno esihlanekezelwe 
Ngo-2010, iShansela engenayo yamemezela inhloso yayo yokuhlanganisa i-Financial Services Authority ibuyele ebhange Ngo-2011 kwasungulwa iKomidi leNqubomgomo Yezimali yesikhashana (i-FPC) (njengekomidi lesibuko leKomidi Lenqubomgomo Yezimali) ukuze lihole igunya elisha lebhange mayelana nokusimama kwezezimali, i-FPC kanye nemisebenzi ye-Financial Services I-Prudential Regulation Authority (PRA), kanye namandla amaningi okuqondisa abahlinzeki bengqalasizinda yemakethe 

yezezimali Isakhamuzi soMbuso kodwa kusukela ngaleso sikhathi sinikezwe ubuzwe Ngesicelo sikaHulumeni, isikhathi sakhe sanwetshwa saya ku-2019, saphinde safika 

ku 
- 

2020 

. yasebenza, kusukela ngoJanuwari 2009, i-Asset Purchase Facility (APF) yokuthenga "impahla yekhwalithi ephezulu exhaswe yi-Treasury bills kanye nemisebenzi yokuphatha ukheshi ye-DMO" futhi ngaleyo ndlela ithuthukise i-liquidity ezimakethe zezikweletu.[112] I-MPC Kanye nokuphatha izimali ze-QE, ezazingu-£895 bn phezulu, i-APF iyaqhubeka nokusebenzisa izakhiwo zayo zezinkampani Zombili zenziwa inkampani engaphansi kweBhange LaseNgilandi, i-Bank of England Asset Purchase Facility Fund Limited (BEAPFF).

I-QE yaklanywa ngokuyinhloko njengethuluzi lenqubomgomo yezimali. Indlela yokusebenza yayidinga ukuthi iBhange LaseNgilandi lithenge amabhondi kahulumeni emakethe yesibili, ekhokhelwa ngokudala imali entsha yasebhange eliphakathi. Lokhu kuzoba nomthelela wokwenyusa izintengo zempahla yamabhondi athengiwe, ngaleyo ndlela kwehlise isivuno futhi kwehliswe izinga lenzalo lesikhathi eside. Inhloso yale nqubomgomo ekuqaleni bekuwukudambisa imikhawulo yemali etholakalayo ohlelweni lwe-sterling reserves kodwa yashintsha yaba umgomo obanzi wokuhlinzeka ngesikhuthazo somnotho. 

I-QE yenziwe ngezigaba eziyisithupha phakathi kuka-2009 no-2020. Ekuphakameni kwayo ngo-2020, iphothifoliyo yafinyelela ku-£895 billion, ehlanganisa u-£875 billion wamabhondi kahulumeni wase-UK kanye no-£20 webhiliyoni wamabhondi okuhweba ezinga eliphezulu. 

NgoFebhuwari 2022, iBhange LaseNgilandi lamemezela inhloso yalo yokuqala ukuvala iphothifoliyo ye-QE.[113] Ekuqaleni lokhu bekuzofezwa ngokungashintshi izilinganiso zamabhondi avuthwayo, futhi kamuva kwakuzosheshiswa ngokuthengiswa kwebhondi okusebenzayo. 

Ngo-Agasti 2022, iBhange Lase-England laphinda laphinda inhloso yalo yokusheshisa ukwehla kwe-QE ngokuthengisa okusebenzayo kwebhondi. Le nqubomgomo yaqinisekiswa ngokushintshana kwezincwadi phakathi kweBhange LaseNgilandi kanye Neshansela lase-UK le-Exchequer ngoSepthemba 2022.[114] Phakathi kukaFebhuwari 2022 noSepthemba 2022, isamba esingu-£37.1bn wamabhondi kahulumeni avuthwa, ehlisa isitoko esisele sisuka ku-£875.0bn ekupheleni kuka-2021 saya ku-£837.9bn. Ngaphezu kwalokho, isamba esingu-£1.1bn samabhondi ezinkampani sivuthwe, sehlisa isitoko sisuka ku-£20.0bn saya ku-£18.9bn, kanti ukuthengiswa kwesitoko esisele kuhlelwe ukuthi kuqale ngomhla zingama-27 kuSepthemba. 

Imibhalo yemali 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Iphepha lebhange lase-England likhipha 

inothi elingu-£1 langonyaka ka-1797 (futhi elamakwa ngokuthi likhokhwe ngo-1928) 
Ibhange likhiphe amanothi kusukela ngo-1694. Amanothi ayebhalwa ngesandla ekuqaleni; nakuba zanyatheliswa ngokwengxenye kusukela ngo-1725 kuqhubeke, osokheshi kwakusadingeka basayine inothi ngalinye futhi babenze bakhokhele othile. Amanothi anyatheliswa ngokugcwele kusukela ngo-1855. Kuze kube ngu-1928 wonke amanothi "Amanothi Amhlophe", aphrintiwe ngombala omnyama futhi angenalutho. Ngekhulu le-18 nele-19, Amanothi Amhlophe akhishwa ngamahlelo ka-£1 no-£2. Phakathi nekhulu lama-20, Amanothi Amhlophe akhishwa ngamahlelo aphakathi kuka-£5 no-£1000. Kuze kube kuphasiswa uMthetho Ojwayelekile Wegolide ka-1925 ibhange lalibophekile ukuthi likhokhe uma lifunwa inani lemali yemali yegolide kumphathi walo. 

Ngo-1724 ibhange langena esivumelwaneni no-Henry Portal waseWhitchurch, eHamphire ukuhlinzeka ngephepha lezinga eliphezulu lokunyathelisa imali engamaphepha.[115] Ukunyathelisa ngokwako kwenziwa yizinkampani ezizimele zokunyathelisa; izingcwecwe zethusi zazigcinwa egumbini elingaphansi, futhi phakathi nesikhathi sazo emshinini wokunyathelisa ngumabhalane wasebhange (owayezobhala inani lamakhophi enziwe); uma komile babezohanjiswa ebhange. Umsebenzi wokunyathelisa walethwa emagcekeni ebhange (nakuba wawusengaphansi kwenkontileka yangasese) ngo-1791; ngo-1808 yalethwa ngokugcwele endlini.


Iphepha lemali lase-One Guinea, elakhishwa iGloucester Old Bank ngo-1813 
Kuze kube maphakathi nekhulu le-19, amabhange ezentengiselwano ayevunyelwe ukuba akhiphe awawo amabhange, futhi amanothi akhishwa izinkampani zamabhange zesifundazwe ayevame ukusakazwa.[116] I-Bank Charter Act 1844 yaqala inqubo yokukhawulela udaba lwamanothi ebhange; amabhange amasha ayenqatshelwe ukukhipha awawo amaphepha emali, futhi amabhange akhona akhipha amaphepha ayengavunyelwe ukwandisa udaba lwawo. Njengoba izinkampani zamabhange zezifundazwe zazihlangana ukuze zenze amabhange amakhulu, zalahlekelwa ilungelo lazo lokukhipha amanothi, futhi imali yangasese yaseNgilandi yagcina inyamalele, kwashiya ibhange nomthwalo wemfanelo wezindaba zamanothi eNgilandi naseWales. Ibhange lokugcina elizimele ukukhipha awalo amanothi e-England naseWales kwakunguFox, Fowler and Company ngo-1921.[117] Kodwa-ke, ukulinganiselwa koMthetho we-1844 kuthinte kuphela amabhange aseNgilandi naseWales, futhi namuhla amabhange amathathu okuhweba eScotland namathathu aseNyakatho Ireland ayaqhubeka nokukhipha ama-banknotes awo, alawulwa yibhange. 


Inothi likaMgcinimafa losheleni abayishumi (eyaqala ngo-1914), elasayinwa ngu-John Bradbury 
Ekuqaleni kweMpi Yezwe Yokuqala, uMthetho Wezimali Namanothi Ebhange waphasiswa, owanikeza amandla esikhashana kuMgcinimafa we-HM okukhipha imali engamaphepha enanini lika-£1 no-10/- (amasheleni ayishumi). Amanothi kaMgcinimafa abenesimo esigcwele samathenda asemthethweni futhi abengaguqulwa abe yigolide ngebhange; bashintsha uhlamvu lwegolide olusakazwayo ukuze bavimbele ukusetshenziswa kwe-sterling futhi bakwazi ukuthenga impahla eluhlaza ukuze kukhiqizwe izikhali. La manothi abe nesithombe seNkosi uGeorge V (Amanothi eBhange laseNgilandi awazange aqale ukubonisa isithombe senkosi kuze kube ngu-1960). Amagama anothi ngalinye ayethi: 

UNITED KINGDOM OF GREAT BRITAIN AND IRELAND – Amanothi emali ayiThenda Elisemthethweni lokukhokhwa kwanoma iyiphi isamba – Likhishwe OKhomishana Bamakhosi BoMgcinimafa Wobukhosi Bakhe ngaphansi Kwegunya Lomthetho Wephalamende 

Amanothi Omgcinimafa akhishwa kwaze kwaba ngu-1928 lapho Umthetho Wokubuyiswa Kwemali Namanothi Asebhange8182 Umthetho Wokukhokhiswa Kwezimali182 IBhange LaseNgilandi lakhipha amanothi osheleni abayishumi kanye nophawundi olulodwa okokuqala ngqa ngomhla zingama-22 kuNovemba 1928. 


Iphepha elithi 'Operation Bernhard' £50, elaqanjwa iziboshwa ekamu lokuhlushwa laseSachsenhausen 
Phakathi neMpi Yezwe Yesibili, umkhankaso waseJalimane u-Operation Bernhard wazama ukwenza amahlelo mbumbulu phakathi kuka-£5 no-£50, okwenza imali engu-500,000 ibe yimali ye-parachu yenyanga ngayinye e-UK. umzamo wokuthunaza umnotho waseBrithani, kodwa kwatholakala kuwusizo kakhulu ukusebenzisa amanothi ukukhokhela ama-agent aseJalimane asebenza kulo lonke elaseYurophu. Nakuba iningi lawela ezandleni zama-Allied ekupheleni kwempi, amaphutha ayevame ukuvela iminyaka eminingi kamuva, okwaholela ekutheni amahlelo emali engaphezu kuka-£5 asuswe ekusakazweni. 

Ngo-2006, imali engamaphepha engaphezulu kuka-£53 million yebhange yebiwa edepho e-Tonbridge, e-Kent.

Ngo-1917 ibhange lase lithuthe umsebenzi walo wokunyathelisa layiswa eSt Luke's Printing Works, okwakuyisibhedlela sangaphambili; ngo-1958 yathuthela eDebden. Amanothi esimanje aphrintwa ngenkontileka neDe La Rue Currency eLoughton, Essex. 

Amahhovisi egatsha 

iBhange LaseNgilandi, e-King Street, eLeeds: esinye sezakhiwo eziningi zegatsha ezinonya esavulwa ekuqaleni kwawo-1970. 
Esikhathini esiningi sekhulunyaka leshumi nesishiyagalolunye namashumi amabili ibhange lalinamagatsha amaningi eLondon nakwamanye amadolobha aseNgilandi. 

Amagatsha okuqala avulwa ngo-1826 (ngomfutho onikezwe ukuphasiswa kwe-Country Bankers Act, okwavumela okokuqala ukusungulwa kwamabhange esitoko ngaphandle kwaseLondon).[75] Ibhange lalibheke ukuthi uxhaxha olusha lwamagatsha 'luzokwandisa ukusetshenziswa kwama-Bank Notes, lunikeze ibhange ukulawula okuphelele kakhulu kuwo wonke amaphepha asakazwayo, futhi livikele ibhange emiqhudelwaneni yezinkampani zamabhange ezinkulu'.[121] Igatsha ngalinye laliqondiswa i-Agent (umuntu 'onolwazi lwezentengiselwano, onolwazi lwasendaweni').[75] Ngo-1829 kwakunamagatsha ayishumi nanye asebenza (ayishumi eNgilandi nelilodwa eWales). Amanye amagatsha angenanzuzo encane awahlali isikhathi esifushane, kodwa amanye aqhubeka nokusebenza kwaze kwaba ngawo-1990. 

Ngo-1997 amagatsha amahlanu okugcina asele avalwa; ama-Agent, nokho, agcinwa, ngohlaka lwama-Regional Agencies adalwe (kulo lonke elase-UK), amanye awo ayezinze ezakhiweni zamagatsha zangaphambili.

INkantolo Yabaqondisi iyibhodi elihlangene elinomthwalo wemfanelo wokubeka isu lenhlangano nesabelomali kanye nokwenza izinqumo ezibalulekile mayelana nezinsiza nokuqokwa. Linamalungu amahlanu aphezulu avela ebhange (uMbusi kanye namaPhini Obabusi abane, ngamunye wabo wengamela indawo ehlukile yokusebenza kwebhange), kanye namalungu angewona ayisi-9 angaphethe, wonke aqokwa nguBukhosi. IShansela likhetha uSihlalo Wenkantolo phakathi kwamalungu angewona amalungu esigungu esiphezulu. INkantolo idingeka ukuthi ihlangane okungenani izikhathi eziyisikhombisa ngonyaka. 

UMbusi usebenza isikhathi esiyiminyaka eyisishiyagalombili, amaSekela-Babusi iminyaka emihlanu, kanti amalungu angeyona ingxenye yesigungu esiphezulu kuze kube iminyaka emine.

Umqondisi 
Webhange Lase-England. unomthwalo wemfanelo wokubusa nokuziphatha kwamabhange: 'Unomthwalo wemfanelo wokuqinisekisa ukuthi inhlangano iphathwa kahle futhi weluleka iNkantolo yethu Yabaqondisi [...] Uphinde abe yisikhulu sethu sezinkinga zokungqubuzana futhi weseka uHulumeni lapho eqoka amakomiti ethu enqubomgomo kanye Nenkantolo Yabaqondisi'. 

Kusukela ngo-2013, ibhange libe nesikhulu sokusebenza (COO) esinesikhundla kanye neholo lePhini likaMbusi. Kusukela ngo-2024, i-COO yebhange nguBen Stimson; unomthwalo wemfanelo wokusebenza kwansuku zonke kwebhange, okuhlanganisa i-Human Resources, Property, IT and Security. NgoMashi 2025, iBhange LaseNgilandi laqoka uSarah John njengoMphathi Omkhulu Wezokusebenza. UJohn uke wasebenza njengoMphathi Omkhulu Webhange. 

Abaqondisi abakhulu abangaba ngamashumi amabili basebenza kanye namaGovernors, bakha 'ithimba labaphathi abakhulu'. Phakathi kwenani labo kukhona nosomnotho omkhulu webhange (i-Huw Pill kusukela ngo-2021), kanye nomphathi wezimali.




Ukuze uthole indawo yamanje, bheka i-England. Ngombuso kusuka ku-1707 kuya ku-1800, bheka i-Kingdom of Great Britain. Ngombuso kusukela ngo-1801 kuya ku-1922, bheka i-Kingdom of Great Britain ne-Ireland. Ukuze uthole izwe elizimele lamanje, bheka i-United Kingdom.
