Polities izwe elizimele esiqhingini saseGreat Britain kusukela ngekhulu le-10, lapho lihlanganiswa emibusweni ehlukahlukene yama-Anglo-Saxon, kwaze kwaba umhla ka-1 Meyi 1707, lapho lihlangana neScotland ukwakha uMbuso WaseBrithani, owawuzoba yi-United Kingdom. UMbuso WaseNgilandi wawuphakathi kwezifunda ezinamandla kakhulu eYurophu phakathi nenkathi ephakathi neyokuqala yesimanje. 
Kusukela ngonyaka wama-886 [4] u-Alfred Omkhulu waphinde wahlala eLondon esuka kumaVikings aseDenmark futhi ngemva kwalesi senzakalo wazimemezela njengeNkosi yama-Anglo-Saxon, kwaze kwaba sekufeni kwakhe ngo-899. Phakathi nenkathi yokuqala yekhulu leshumi, imibuso ehlukahlukene yama-Anglo-Saxon yahlanganiswa inzalo ka-Alfred u-Edward Omdala 89 (wabusa 9) 924–939) ukwakha uMbuso wamaNgisi. Ngo-927, u-Æthelstan wanqoba umbuso wokugcina wamaViking owawusele, e-York, wamenza umbusi wokuqala wama-Anglo-Saxon kulo lonke elaseNgilandi. Ngo-1016, lo mbuso waba yingxenye yoMbuso WaseNyakatho Yasolwandle waseCnut the Great, inyunyana yomuntu siqu phakathi kweNgilandi, iDenmark neNorway. I-Norman Conquest ngo-1066 yaholela ekudlulisweni kwenhloko-dolobha yamaNgisi kanye nendawo yokuhlala yasebukhosini isuka kweyase-Anglo-Saxon eseWinchester yayiswa eWestminster, futhi iDolobha laseLondon lazisungula ngokushesha njengesikhungo sezohwebo esikhulu kunazo zonke saseNgilandi futhi esiyinhloko. 
Imilando yoMbuso WaseNgilandi kusukela ekunqotshweni kukaNorman ka-1066 ngokwejwayelekile ihlukanisa izikhathi eziqanjwe ngezizukulwane ezibusayo ezilandelanayo: uNorman/Angevin 1066–1216, iPlantagenet 1216–1485, iTudor 1485–1603 kanye noStuart 1603–1707 (iphazanyiswe 16-160 ephazanyiswe ngo-160). Wonke amakhosi angamaNgisi ngemva kuka-1066 agcina ehla ephuma kumaNorman, futhi ukuhlukaniswa kwamaPlantagenet kuyinto evamile—kusukela ngoHenry II (wabusa ngo-1154–1189) kusukela ngaleso sikhathi, amakhosi ase-Angevin aba “amaNgisi kakhulu ngokwemvelo”; izindlu zaseLancaster nase-York zombili zingamagatsha e-Plantagenet cadet, uzalo lwakwaTudor lwathi luphuma ku-Edward III ngo-John Beaufort kanye no-James VI kanye mina we-House of Stuart sathi siphuma ku-Henry VII ngo-Margaret Tudor.



Ukuqedwa kokunqotshwa kweWales ngu-Edward I ngo-1284 kwabeka iWales ngaphansi kokulawula komqhele wamaNgisi. U-Edward III (wabusa ngo-1327–1377) waguqula uMbuso WaseNgilandi waba ngelinye lamandla ezempi asabekayo eYurophu; ekubuseni kwakhe kwabona nentuthuko ebalulekile emithethweni nakuhulumeni—ikakhulukazi intuthuko yePhalamende lamaNgisi. Kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1340s, izimangalo zamaNgisi ezithatha isihlalo sobukhosi saseFrance zabanjwa ngokuzenzisa, kodwa ngemva kweMpi Yeminyaka Eyikhulu nokugqashuka Kwezimpi ZaseRoses ngo-1455, amaNgisi ayengasenasimo sokuphishekela izimangalo zawo zesiFulentshi futhi alahlekelwa yiwo wonke umhlaba wawo ezwenikazi, ngaphandle kukaCalais. Ngemuva kweziyaluyalu zeziMpi zamaRoses, ubukhosi bakwaTudor babusa ngesikhathi seNkathi Yokuzalwa KwamaNgisi futhi baphinde banweba amandla obukhosi baseNgilandi ngaphezu kweNgilandi ngokufanele, kwafinyelela inyunyana ephelele yeNgilandi kanye noBukhosi baseWales ngaphansi kweMithetho yaseWales IzEnzo 1535-1542. UHenry VIII wengamele iNguquko YamaNgisi, kanye nendodakazi yakhe u-Elizabeth I (wabusa ngo-1558-1603) i-Elizabethan Religious Settlement, ngaleso sikhathi esungula iNgilandi njengamandla amakhulu futhi ebeka izisekelo zoMbuso WaseBrithani ngokusebenzisa amakoloni aseMelika. 

Ukungena kukaJames VI kanye nami ngo-1603 kwaphumela eNyunyana YamaCrown, nobukhosi bakwaStuart obubusa imibuso yaseNgilandi, eScotland nase-Ireland. Ngaphansi kweStuarts, iNgilandi yangena ezimpini zombango, eyafinyelela umvuthwandaba ngokubulawa kukaCharles I ngo-1649. Ubukhosi babuya ngo-1660, kodwa iMpi Yombango yayisungule isibonelo sokuthi inkosi yaseNgilandi ayinakubusa ngaphandle kwemvume yePhalamende. Lo mqondo wamiswa ngokomthetho njengengxenye yeNguquko Ekhazimulayo ka-1688. Kusukela ngalesi sikhathi umbuso waseNgilandi, kanye nezwe owalandela esikhundleni i-United Kingdom, wasebenza njengombuso ongokomthethosisekelo.[a] Ngomhla lu-1 kuNhlaba 1707, ngaphansi kwemibandela ye-Acts of Union 1707, amaphalamende, futhi ngenxa yalokho, imibuso, kokubili iNgilandi neScotland yaqedwa. Izimpahla zabo nezindawo zabo kuhlangene 'phakade, eMbusweni ngegama leGreat Britain', kwakha uMbuso WaseBrithani Omkhulu kanye nePhalamende LaseGreat Britain.[7][8] 

Igama 
Isihloko esikhulu: Igama laseNgilandi 
Ama-Anglo-Saxon azibiza ngokuthi i-Engle noma i-Angelcynn, ekuqaleni amagama ama-Angles. Babiza izwe labo ngokuthi i-Engla izwe, okusho ukuthi "izwe lamaNgisi", elibhalwe ngu-Æthelweard Latinized Anglia, elivela ku-Anglia vetus yasekuqaleni, izwe okucatshangwa ukuthi lidabuka e-Angles (elibizwa ngokuthi u-Angulus ngo-Bede).[9] Igama elithi Engla land laba yiNgilandi nge-haplology ngesikhathi sesiNgisi esiPhakathi (Engle-land, Engelond).[10][ikhasi elidingekayo] Igama lesiLatini kwakuyi-Anglia noma i-Anglorum terra, isiFulentshi Esidala kanye ne-Anglo-Norman eyodwa i-Engleterre.[11]

Isihloko esijwayelekile samakhosi asuka e-Æthelstan kuze kube uJohn kwakunguRex Anglorum ("Inkosi YesiNgisi"). UCnut, waseDane, waba ngowokuqala ukuzibiza ngokuthi "iNkosi yaseNgilandi". Ngesikhathi samaNorman u-Rex Anglorum wahlala esezingeni, ngokusetshenziswa ngezikhathi ezithile kwe-Rex Anglie ("Inkosi yaseNgilandi"). Kusukela ekubuseni kukaJohane kuqhubeke zonke ezinye iziqu zagwenywa zivuna uRex noma uRegina Anglie. Ngo-1604 uJames I, owayezuze njengefa isihlalo sobukhosi samaNgisi ngonyaka owandulele, wathatha lesi sihloko (manje esivame ukuhunyushwa ngesiNgisi kunesiLatini) iNkosi yaseGreat Britain.[b] 


UMbuso WaseNgilandi wavela ekuhlanganisweni kancane kancane kwemibuso yasendulo yama-Anglo-Saxon eyaziwa ngokuthi i-Heptarchy: East Anglia, Mercia, Northumbria, Wessexssex, Sussex, Kent. Ukuhlasela kwamaViking kwekhulu lesi-9 kwaphazamisa ibhalansi yamandla phakathi kwemibuso yamaNgisi, nempilo yomdabu yama-Anglo-Saxon ngokuvamile. Amazwe amaNgisi ahlanganiswa ngekhulu le-10 ekuthathweni kabusha okwaqedwa ngo-927.[5] 

Ngesikhathi se-Heptarchy, inkosi enamandla kunazo zonke phakathi kwemibuso yama-Anglo-Saxon ingase yamukelwe njengoBretwalda, inkosi ephakeme phezu kwamanye amakhosi. Ukuwohloka kweMercia kwavumela i-Wessex ukuba ibe namandla kakhudlwana, yathatha imibuso yaseKent neSussex ngo-825. Amakhosi aseWessex aya ngokuya ebusa eminye imibuso yaseNgilandi phakathi nekhulu lesi-9. Ngo-827, i-Northumbria yathumela ku-Egbert wase-Wessex e-Dore, okwenza u-Egbert abe inkosi yokuqala ukubusa phezu kweNgilandi ebumbene.[13] 

Ngo-886, u-Alfred Omkhulu waphinde wathatha iLondon, ngokusobala ayeyibheka njengenguquko ekubuseni kwakhe. I-Anglo-Saxon Chronicle ithi "bonke abantu abangamaNgisi (bonke abakwa-Angelcyn) ababengekho ngaphansi kwamaDanes bazithoba eNkosini u-Alfred." [14] U-Asser wengeza ngokuthi "u-Alfred, inkosi yama-Anglo-Saxon, wabuyisela idolobha laseLondon ngobuhle ... futhi walenza ukuba kuhlale kulo futhi." ukwakha izikhumulo ngasemfuleni iThames, nokubeka ipulani elisha lomgwaqo wedolobha. [16] [ikhasi elidingekayo] 

Ngomhla ziyi-12 kuJulayi 927 amakhosi aseBrithani ahlangana e-Eamont eCumbria ukuze ahloniphe i-Æthelstan njengenkosi yamaNgisi.[5] Isihloko esithi "Inkosi YamaNgisi" noma i-Rex Anglorum ngesiLatini, saqala ukusetshenziswa ukuchaza i-Æthelstan kwenye yezincwadi zakhe ngo-928. Isihloko esijwayelekile samakhosi asuka e-Æthelstan kuze kube uJohane "iNkosi yamaNgisi". Phakathi neminyaka elandelayo i-Northumbria yashintsha ngokuphindaphindiwe izandla phakathi kwamakhosi angamaNgisi nabahlaseli baseNorway, kodwa ngokuqinisekile yalethwa ngaphansi kokulawulwa kwamaNgisi ngu-Eadred ngo-954, eqedela ukuhlanganiswa kweNgilandi.[17] Ngonyaka we-1018, uLothian, ingxenye yengxenye esenyakatho yeNorthumbria Bernicia yanikelwa eMbusweni waseScotland.[18][19]

 
Ukubusa kwe-Cnut (1014–1035)
INgilandi iye yahlala isebunyeni bezombangazwe kusukela ngaleso sikhathi. Ngesikhathi sokubusa kuka-Æthelred the Unready (978-1016), igagasi elisha lokuhlasela kwe-Danish lahlelwa ngu-Sweyn I waseDenmark, okwafinyelela umvuthwandaba ngemva kwekhulu lesine lempi ekunqobeni i-England yaseDenmark ngo-1013. Ngo-1015, indodana kaSweyn u-Cnut (owaziwa kakhulu ngokuthi uCanute) wethula ukuhlasela okusha. Impi eyalandela yaphela ngesivumelwano ngo-1016 phakathi kukaCanute no-Edmund Ironside owalandela esikhundleni sika-Æthelred, sokuhlukanisa iNgilandi phakathi kwabo, kodwa ukufa kuka-Edmund ngo-30 November walowo nyaka kwashiya iNgilandi ihlangene ngaphansi kombuso waseDenmark. Lokhu kwaqhubeka iminyaka engu-26 kwaze kwaba sekufeni kukaHarthacnut ngoJuni 1042. Wayeyindodana kaCanute no-Emma waseNormandy (umfelokazi ka-Æthelred the Unready) futhi engenazo izindlalifa ezingokwakhe; walandelwa umfowabo ngamzali munye, indodana ka-Æthelred, u-Edward the Confessor.[20] 

Norman Conquest 
Isihloko esikhulu: Norman Conquest 
Ukuthula kwahlala kwaze kwashona u-Edward owayengenamntwana ngo-January 1066. Umlamu wakhe wathweswa ubukhosi njengeNkosi uHarold, kodwa umzala wakhe uWilliam uMnqobi, uMbusi waseNormandy, wathatha isihlalo sobukhosi ngokushesha. UWilliam waqala ukuhlasela iNgilandi futhi wafika eSussex ngomhla zingama-28 kuMandulo 1066. UHarold nebutho lakhe babeseYork kulandela ukunqoba kwabo abaseNorwegian e-Battle of Stamford Bridge (25 September 1066) ngenkathi lezi zindaba zifika kuye. Wanquma ukuphuma ngaphandle kokulibala futhi wabhekana nebutho lamaNorman eSussex lahamba laya eningizimu ngaso leso sikhathi, naphezu kokuba amasosha ayengaphumuli kahle kulandela impi namaNorwegian. Amabutho kaHarold noWilliam abhekana e-Battle of Hastings (14 October 1066), lapho amabutho amaNgisi, noma uFyrd, anqotshwa khona, uHarold nabafowabo ababili babulawa, kwathi uWilliam waba ngumnqobi. UWilliam wabe esekwazi ukunqoba iNgilandi ngaphandle kokuphikiswa okuncane. Nokho, wayengahlelile ukungenisa uMbuso eMbusweni WaseNormandy. Njengombusi nje, uWilliam wayekweleta ukwethembeka kuPhilip I waseFrance, kanti eMbusweni ozimele waseNgilandi wayengabusa ngaphandle kokuphazanyiswa. Wathweswa umqhele ngomhla zingama-25 kuZibandlela 1066 eWestminster Abbey, eLondon. [21] 

I-High Middle Ages 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: I-England ngeNkathi Ephakathi Ephakeme 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Umbuso wase-Angevin, ukuhlasela kukaNorman eWales, kanye Nokunqotshwa kweWales ngu-Edward I.
Ngo-1092, uWilliam II wahola ukuhlasela kweStrathclyde, umbuso wamaCeltic endaweni manje eyiningizimu-ntshonalanga yeScotland neCumbria. Ngokwenza kanjalo, wanamathisela lokho manje osekuyisifunda saseCumbria eNgilandi. Ngo-1124, uHenry I wanikela lokho manje osekuyiningizimu-mpumalanga yeScotland (ebizwa ngokuthi iLothian) eMbusweni waseScotland, ukuze abuyisele ukwethembeka kweNkosi yaseScotland. Lesi sivumelwano sokugcina sasungula lokho okuzoba imingcele yendabuko yaseNgilandi ehlale ingashintshile kusukela ngaleso sikhathi (ngaphandle kwezinguquko zesikhashana nezesikhashana). Le ndawo yomhlaba phambilini ibiyingxenye yoMbuso Wama-Anglian waseNorthumbria. ILothian yayiqukethe lokho kamuva okwaba inhloko-dolobha yaseScotland, i-Edinburgh. Leli lungiselelo kamuva laphothulwa ngo-1237 yiSivumelwano Sase-York.[22] 


INkosi uJohn isayina uMagna Carta eRunnymede ngo-1215, ezungezwe yi-baronage yakhe. Illustration from Cassell's History of England, 1902. 
Ukuhlasela kwama-Anglo-Norman e-Ireland kwenzeka ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-12, lapho ama-Anglo-Normans kancane kancane enqoba futhi ethola izindawo ezinkulu ezivela kubantu base-Ireland, okwathi ngaleso sikhathi iNgilandi yazisholo ubukhosi, konke okwakusolwa ukuthi kwakugunyazwe uPapa inkunzi uLaudabiliter.[23] Ngaleso sikhathi, iGaelic Ireland yayakhiwe imibuso eminingana, neNkosi Ephakeme eyayithi ubukhosi phezu kwamanye amakhosi amaningi.[24] 

I-Duchy of Aquitaine yangena ebunyeni bomuntu siqu neNgilandi lapho kubusa uHenry II, owayeshade no-Eleanor, uDuchess wase-Aquitaine. Bahlala bebumbene kwaze kwaba yilapho uJohn Lackland, indodana kaHenry II kanye nesizukulwane sesine sozalo lukaWilliam uMnqobi, elahlekelwa yimpahla yezwekazi kuPhilip II waseFrance ngokushesha ngemva kweMpi YaseBouvines ngo-1214. Izinsalela ezimbalwa zaseNormandy, kuhlanganise neziQhingi Zesiteshi, zasala esandleni sikaJohn, kanye neningi lamaDuchy of Aquitaine.[2] 

Ukunqotshwa kweWales 
Kuze Kube Ukunqotshwa kukaNorman waseNgilandi, iWales yayihlale ingxenye enkulu izimele emibusweni yama-Anglo-Saxon, nakuba amanye amakhosi aseWales ayeyivuma iBretwalda ngezinye izikhathi. Nokho, ngokushesha ngemva kokunqotshwa kukaNorman waseNgilandi, ezinye izinduna zamaNorman zaqala ukuhlasela iWales. Bayinqoba futhi babusa izingxenye zayo, bevuma ubukhosi bamakhosi amaNorman aseNgilandi kodwa ngokuzimela okukhulu kwendawo. Eminyakeni eminingi lezi "Marcher Lords" zanqoba kakhulu i-Wales, ngokumelene nokuphikiswa okukhulu okuholwa yizikhulu ezihlukahlukene zase-Wales, nazo ezivame ukuvuma ubukhosi bamakhosi ase-Norman aseNgilandi. [26] [ikhasi elidingekayo] 

u-Edward I wanqoba uLlywelyn ap Gruffudd, futhi wanqoba ngempumelelo i-Wales, ngo-1282 wadala iNkosana yakhe yesibili, u-Edward we-Wales yakhe ezayo. 1301. Ukunqoba kuka-Edward I kwakunonya futhi ukucindezelwa okwalandela kwaba kukhulu, njengoba kufakazela izinqaba ezinhle zaseWales ezinjengeConwy, Harlech, kanye neCaernarfon.[27] 

I-Late Middle Ages 
I-athikili eyinhloko: i-England kuma-Late Middle Ages
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Izimpi ZaseRoses, Impi Yeminyaka Eyikhulu, kanye Nokuwohloka Okukhulu (ngekhulu le-15) 

Incanyana yekhulu leshumi nanhlanu ebonisa ukunqoba kwamaNgisi phezu kweFrance eMpini Yase-Agincourt 
U-Edward III wayeyinkosi yokuqala yamaNgisi ukubanga isihlalo sobukhosi saseFrance. Ukuphishekela kwakhe isimangalo kwaphumela eMpini Yeminyaka Eyikhulu (1337–1453), eyaxabanisa amakhosi amahlanu aseNgilandi eNdlu yasePlantagenet namakhosi amahlanu aseFrance eCapetian House of Valois. Ukuhlasela okukhulu kwemikhumbi yempi kwenziwa yizo zonke izinhlangothi phakathi nempi, ngokuvamile kuhilela abantu abazimele abafana noJohn Hawley waseDartmouth noma iCastilian Pero Niño. Nakuba amaNgisi anqoba izikhathi eziningi, awakwazanga ukunqoba inani eliphakeme lamaFulentshi kanye nokusebenzisa kwawo amasu ezikhali zesibhamu. INgilandi yahlulwa e-Battle of Formigny ngo-1450 futhi ekugcineni e-Battle of Castillon ngo-1453, yagcina idolobha elilodwa kuphela eFrance, eCalais. [28] 

Ngesikhathi seMpi Yeminyaka Eyikhulu kwaqala ukukhula ubuwena besiNgisi esikhundleni sokuhlukana kwangaphambilini phakathi kwamakhosi amaNorman kanye nezifundo zawo ze-Anglo-Saxon. Lokhu kwaba umphumela wobutha obuqhubekayo kumaFulentshi ayekhula ngobuzwe, amakhosi awo kanye nabanye abaholi (ikakhulukazi uJoan wase-Arc onobungane) basebenzisa umuzwa okhulayo wobunikazi baseFrance ukuze basize ukudonsela abantu kunjongo yabo.[29] 

Umbuso wawunesikhathi esincane sokululama ngaphambi kokungena eziMpini ZaseRoses (1455-1487), uchungechunge lwezimpi zombango zokuba nesihlalo sobukhosi phakathi kweNdlu yaseLancaster (ophawu lwayo lwe-heraldic kwakuyirose elibomvu) kanye neNdlu yaseYork (ophawu layo kwakuyirose elimhlophe), ngayinye iholwa ngamagatsha ahlukene enzalo ka-Edward III. Ukuphela kwalezi zimpi kwathola isihlalo sobukhosi esiphethwe ngenzalo yelungu elingekho emthethweni ekuqaleni leNdlu yaseLancaster, eshade nendodakazi endala yeNdlu yase-York: uHenry VII no-Elizabeth wase-York.[30] 

Isikhathi sika-Tudor 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Isikhathi sika-Tudor, inkathi ka-Elizabethan, inkathi ka-Stuart, neNguquko YesiNgisi 
Bheka futhi: Ukunqoba kukaTudor kwe-Ireland 
I-Wales igcine uhlelo oluhlukile lwezomthetho nokuphatha, olwasungulwa ngu-Edward I ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-13. Izwe lahlukaniswa phakathi kwe-Marcher Lords, eyanikeza ukwethembeka emqheleni, kanye noBukhosi baseWales. Ngaphansi kobukhosi bakwaTudor, uHenry VIII washintsha imithetho yaseWales wafaka leyo yaseNgilandi (ngaphansi kweMithetho yaseWales IzEnzo 1535–1542). I-Wales yafakwa eNgilandi, futhi kusukela manje yabe imelwe ePhalamende.[31] 


Isithombe sika-Elizabeth I esenziwe ukuze kukhunjulwe ukunqotshwa kwe-Armada yaseSpain (1588), eboniswe ngemuva. Amandla ka-Elizabeth omhlaba wonke afanekiselwa isandla esihlezi emhlabeni.
Phakathi neminyaka yawo-1530, uHenry wagumbuqela amandla eSonto LamaKatolika embusweni, ethatha isikhundla sikapapa njengenhloko yeSonto lakhe lamaNgisi futhi wathatha nezindawo zeSonto LamaKatolika, ngaleyo ndlela wenza kube lula ukudalwa kokwehluka kobuKatolika okwaba ubuProthestani ngokwengeziwe ngokuhamba kwesikhathi. Lokhu kwaba nomphumela wokuqondanisa iNgilandi neScotland, nayo eyamukela kancane kancane inkolo yobuProthestani, kuyilapho imibuso yezwekazi ebaluleke kakhulu, iFrance neSpain, yahlala ingamaKatolika.[32] 

"Ukunqotshwa kukaTudor" (noma ukubuyisela kabusha) kwe-Ireland' kwenzeka ngaphansi kobukhosi bakwaTudor. Ngemva kokuhlubuka okuhlulekile ngokumelene nomqhele nguSilken Thomas, u-Earl waseKildare, ngawo-1530, uHenry VIII wamenyezelwa njengeNkosi yase-Ireland ngo-1542 ngokomthetho wePhalamende lase-Ireland, ngenhloso yokubuyisela igunya eliphakathi nendawo njengoba lalilahlekile ezweni lonke phakathi namakhulu amabili eminyaka adlule.[33] 

ICalais, indawo yokugcina yoMbuso esele yezwekazi, yalahleka ngo-1558, phakathi nokubusa kukaPhilip noMary I. Umlandeli wabo, u-Elizabeth I, wahlanganisa iSonto LamaProthestani laseSheshi elisha nelalandayo. Waphinde waqala ukwakha amandla emikhumbi yombuso, ezisekelweni uHenry VIII ayezibekile. Ngo-1588, ibutho lakhe elisha lasemanzini lase liqine ngokwanele ukuba linqobe i-Spanish Armada, eyayifuna ukuhlasela iNgilandi ukuze imise ukusekelwa kwamaNgisi kumavukelambuso amaDashi futhi ibeke inkosi yamaKhatholika esihlalweni sobukhosi esikhundleni sayo.[34][35][36] 

Umlando wasendulo wesimanje 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Isikhathi sasendulo saseBrithani kanye nesikaStuart 
Indlu kaTudor yaphela ngokushona kuka-Elizabeth I ngomhla zingama-24 kuNdasa 1603. UJames I wathatha isihlalo sobukhosi saseNgilandi futhi walethela ebunyeni bomuntu siqu noMbuso waseScotland. Naphezu kwe-Union of the Crowns, imibuso yahlala ihlukene futhi izimele: isimo sezindaba esathatha iminyaka engaphezu kwekhulu.[37] 

I-Civil War kanye ne-Interregnum 
Ama-athikili abalulekile: I-English Civil War, English Interregnum, English Commonwealth, kanye ne-English Protectorate 

Cromwell e-Dunbar. U-Oliver Cromwell wahlanganisa zonke iziQhingi zaseBrithani ngenkani futhi wadala i-Commonwealth yaseNgilandi. 
Amakhosi akwa-Stuart alinganisela ngokweqile amandla obukhosi bamaNgisi, futhi axoshwa yiPhalamende ngo-1645 nango-1688. Okokuqala, ukwethulwa kukaCharles I kwezinhlobo ezintsha zentela ngokudelela iPhalamende kwaholela eMpini Yombango YamaNgisi (1641-1645), lapho inkosi yanqotshwa khona, nasekuqedweni kombuso ka-Oliver Cromwell. 1649–1660.[38]

Ngemva kokuqulwa kwecala nokubulawa kukaCharles I ngoJanuwari 1649, iPhalamende laseRump laphasisa isenzo esimemezela ukuthi iNgilandi iyiNhlangano Yezizwe Ezihlangene ngoMeyi 19 1649. Ubukhosi kanye neNdlu Yamakhosi kwaqedwa, ngakho-ke iNdlu Yezikhulu yaba yindlu yomthetho ebumbene enomzimba omusha, uMkhandlu Wombuso waba isigungu esiphezulu. Kodwa-ke, iButho Lezempi lahlala liyisikhungo esivelele e-republic entsha futhi ujenene ovelele kwakungu-Oliver Cromwell. I-Commonwealth yalwa izimpi e-Ireland naseScotland ezanqotshwa futhi zafakwa ngaphansi kombuso wezempi weCommonwealth.[39]

Ngaleso sikhathi, ubudlelwano neDutch Republic base buwohlokile. Naphezu kokusekelwa kokuqala kwamaNgisi phakathi neMpi Yenkululeko YamaDashi ngokumelene namaSpanishi, kwaphakama ukungezwani njengoba i-Dutch Republic ivela njengembangi eyinhloko yezohwebo nezempi yase-England. Maphakathi nekhulu le-17, lase liyizwe elihamba phambili kwezohwebo. Ephendula amaNgisi, ethuswe ukuncintisana kwawo okunciphayo, asebenzisa izinqubomgomo zokuhweba eziqinile ukuze anqande ukubusa kwamaDashi. Impi yokuqala yamaNgisi namaDashi eyalandela, nokho, yehlulekile ukuxazulula izinkinga zezentengiso.[40][41] 

Ngo-April 1653 uCromwell kanye namanye amaGrandees e-New Model Army, ekhungathekile ngamalungu ePhalamende laseRump ayengafuni ukuphasisa umthetho wokuhlakaza iRump futhi avumele iphalamende elisha elimele ukuba liqokwe, bamisa iseshini kaRump futhi bamemezela ukuthi iRump ihlakazekile.[42] 

Ngemva kokuhlolwa koMkhandlu Okhethiwe (iPhalamende LaseBarebone), amaGrandees eButhweni lezempi, ngokusebenzisa uMkhandlu Wombuso wabeka uhlelo olusha lomthethosisekelo ngaphansi komthethosisekelo obhaliwe obizwa ngokuthi i-Instrument of Government. Ngaphansi kweThuluzi likaHulumeni amandla aphezulu ayenoMvikeli Wenkosi (ihhovisi elalizogcinwa impilo yakhe yonke ophethe) futhi kwakuzoba namaPhalamende aminyaka emithathu, okuzohlala okungenani izinyanga ezinhlanu. Isigaba sama-23 seThuluzi likaHulumeni sathi u-Oliver Cromwell wayezoba uMvikeli WeNkosi wokuqala. Ithuluzi likaHulumeni lathathelwa indawo umthethosisekelo wesibili (Isikhalazo esithobekile kanye nezeluleko) lapho iNkosi uMvikeli ayengaqoka khona ozongena esikhundleni sakhe. UCromwell uqoke indodana yakhe uRichard owaba yiNkosi uMvikeli ekufeni kuka-Oliver ngomhlaka-3 Septhemba 1658. [43] 

Ukubuyiselwa Nenguquko Ekhazimulayo 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Ukubuyiselwa (eNgilandi) kanye Nenguquko Ekhazimulayo 

UCharles wahamba ngomkhumbi esuka ekudingisweni eNetherlands waya ekubuyiselweni kwakhe eNgilandi ngoMeyi 1660. Umdwebo ngu-Lieve Verschuier. 
URichard wabonakala engasebenzi futhi akakwazanga ukulondoloza ukubusa kwakhe. Washiya phansi isikhundla sakhe futhi washiya phansi endaweni ongaziwa. IPhalamende laseRump labuyiselwa emuva futhi kwaba nesikhathi sesibili lapho amandla okuphatha alele kuMkhandlu wombuso. Kodwa lokhu kubuyiselwa kokubusa kweCommonwealth, okufana nalokho ngaphambi koMvikeli, kwabonakala kungazinzile, futhi ummangali owayedingisiwe, uCharles II, wabuyiselwa esihlalweni sobukhosi ngo-1660.[44]

Ngo-1665 izinkinga zezentengiselwano ezingakaxazululwa namaDashi zaholela eMpini Yesibili YamaNgisi namaDashi, eyafinyelela umvuthwandaba ngeRaid eyinhlekelele eMedway futhi yaphoqelela uCharles owayethotshisiwe ukuba enze isivumelwano sokuthula esingesihle. Lesi sivumelwano saqeda izinkinga eziningi osekunesikhathi eside zikhona, futhi esikhathini eside senza ukuthi la mazwe womabili ahlangane ngokumelene nezinqubomgomo zokwandisa ezazilandelwa uLouis XIV waseFrance. Nokho, esikhathini esifushane, isifiso sikaCharles sokuphindiselela lokhu kuvinjelwa saholela eMpini Yesithathu YamaNgisi NamaDashi ngo-1672. Naphezu kokuthola ukusekelwa kwamaFulentshi ngalesi sikhathi, impumelelo yezempi yamaDashi yenza iPhalamende lingazimisele ukusekela impi kaCharles, futhi waphinde waphoqeleka ukuba enze ukuthula.[45] 

Ngemva kokubuyiselwa kobukhosi ngo-1660, umzamo kaJames II wokubuyisela ubuRoma Katolika—ikhulu leminyaka ngemva kokucindezelwa kwabo amaTudor—waholela ekuVukeleni Okukhazimulayo kwango-1688, lapho adingiswa khona inkosana yamaDashi uWilliam wase-Orange. UWilliam nomkakhe uMary babe sebethweswa umqhele yiPhalamende.[46] UWilliam walungisa kabusha inqubomgomo yezangaphandle yaseNgilandi ukuze isekele i-Dutch Republic ezimpini zayo ezilwa noLouis XIV waseFrance.[c][47] 

Union with Scotland 
Endabeni yaseScotland, izinto ezihehayo zaziyingxenye yezezimali futhi ngokwengxenye zihlobene nokususa unswinyo lokuhweba lwamaNgisi olwabekwa ngoMthetho we-Alien 1705. AmaNgisi ayekhathazeke kakhulu ngokulandelana kobukhosi. Ukushona kukaWilliam III ngo-1702 kwakuholele ekubekweni kukadadewabo kadadewabo u-Anne esihlalweni sobukhosi saseNgilandi naseScotland, kodwa ingane yakhe okuwukuphela kwayo eyayisindile yashona ngo-1700, futhi uMthetho Wokuhlaliswa KwamaNgisi 1701 wawunikeze ukulandelana komqhele wamaNgisi eNdlu yamaProthestani yaseHanover. Ukuthola ukulandelana okufanayo eScotland kwaba yinto eyinhloko yokucabanga kwamasu amaNgisi ngaseScotland. Ngo-1704, i-Union of the Crowns yayisenkingeni, ngoMthetho Wezokuphepha WaseScotland uvumela iPhalamende laseScotland ukuba likhethe inkosi ehlukile, okungase kuholele kunqubomgomo yangaphandle ezimele phakathi nempi enkulu yaseYurophu.[48] 

ISivumelwano SeNyunyana kwavunyelwana ngomhla zingama-22 kuJulayi 1706, futhi ngokulandela iMithetho yeNyunyana ka-1707, eyadala uMbuso WaseBrithani Enkulu, ukuzimela kwemibuso yaseNgilandi naseScotland kwaphela mhla lu-1 kuNhlaba 1707. I-Acts of Union yakha inyunyana yamasiko kanye nenyunyana yezimali futhi yahlinzeka ngokuthi noma yimiphi “imithetho nemithetho” ephikisana nemithetho noma ephikisana nemithetho ehambisana nemithetho noma ephikisana nemithetho. "phela futhi ube yize." [49]

IPhalamende lamaNgisi nelaseScottish lahlanganiswa laba yiPhalamende LaseGreat Britain, eliseWestminster, eLondon. Kuleli qophelo iNgilandi ayizange ibe khona njengenhlangano yezombangazwe ehlukile, futhi kusukela lapho ayizange ibe nohulumeni kazwelonke. Imithetho yaseNgilandi ayizange ithintwe, amandla angokomthetho aqhubeka nokuba ngoweNgilandi naseWales, kuyilapho iScotland yaqhubeka nokuba nemithetho yayo nezinkantolo zomthetho. Lokhu kwaqhubeka ngemva kokuhlangana kwango-1801 phakathi kwemibuso yeGreat Britain ne-Ireland, kwakha i-United Kingdom of Great Britain kanye ne-Ireland. Ngo-1922 iFree State yase-Ireland yazihlukanisa ne-United Kingdom, okwaholela ekutheni leyakamuva iqanjwe kabusha ngokuthi i-United Kingdom of Great Britain kanye ne-Northern Ireland.[50] Izindatshana eziyinhloko 

zikahulumeni 
: Uhulumeni eNgilandi yasendulo kanye nohulumeni wase-Elizabeth 
Olunye ulwazi: Umlando wobukhosi bamaNgisi 
Izigaba zendawo 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Izifunda zomlando zaseNgilandi, Uhlu lwezindawo zase-Earldom, i-Domesday Book, i-County palatine, imilando yesifunda saseNgilandi, kanye ne-English feudal 
barony Ayeka ukusetshenziselwa ukuphatha kuphela ngokudalwa kwezifunda zokuphatha ngo-1889.[51][52] 

Ngokungafani nezifunda ezizibusayo ngokwengxenye ezazihlanganisa izindawo zasemadolobheni, izifunda zeNgilandi yasendulo zazikhona ngokuyinhloko njengendlela yokuphoqelela amandla kahulumeni omaphakathi, okwenza amakhosi akwazi ukulawula izindawo zendawo ngabameleli bawo abakhethiwe - ekuqaleni osherifu futhi kamuva ama-lord-lieutenants - kanye namajaji abo okuthula angaphansi.[53] Izifunda zazisetshenziswa ekuqaleni ukuze kuphathwe ubulungisa, ukuqoqwa kwezintela kanye nokuhlela amasosha, futhi kamuva kuhulumeni wasekhaya nokukhetha ukumeleleka ephalamende.[54][ikhasi elidingekayo] Ezinye izifunda ezingaphandle ngezikhathi ezithile zazinikezwa isikhundla se-palatine ngemisebenzi ethile yezempi kanye nekahulumeni oyinhloko enikezwa isicukuthwane noma umbhishobhi wendawo. Okokugcina, i-County Palatine yaseDurham, ayizange ilahlekelwe yilesi simo esikhethekile kwaze kwaba sekhulwini le-19. [55] [ikhasi elidingekayo] 

Nakuba yonke iNgilandi yahlukaniswa yaba izingxenye ngesikhathi se-Norman Conquest, ezinye izifunda zakhiwa kamuva kakhulu, kwaze kwaba sekhulwini le-16. Ngenxa yemvelaphi yazo ehlukene izifunda zazihlukahluka kakhulu ngobukhulu. Imingcele yesifunda yayimile kahle phakathi kwezenzo zeMithetho yekhulu le-16 e-Wales kanye noMthetho Wohulumeni Wasekhaya 1888.[56] I-shire ngayinye yayinomthwalo wemfanelo wokuqoqa intela kuhulumeni omkhulu; ukuzivikela kwendawo; kanye nobulungisa, ngokusebenzisa izinkantolo.[57][ikhasi elidingekayo]

Amandla ama-feudal barons okulawula ubunikazi bawo bomhlaba aba buthaka kakhulu ngo-1290 ngomthetho we-Quia Emptores. Ama-feudal baronies mhlawumbe aphelelwa yisikhathi (kodwa awazange ashabalale) ekuqedweni kokubusa phakathi neMpi Yombango, njengoba kuqinisekiswe uMthetho Wokuqedwa Kwezindawo Zokuhlala 1660 owaphasiswa ngaphansi kokubuyiselwa okwasusa insizakalo yama-knight namanye amalungelo omthetho. Ukuqashwa kwe-knight-service kwaqedwa futhi kwakhishwa futhi imihlaba embozwe yilezo zikhathi, okuhlanganisa ama-feudal baronies, kusukela manje kuqhubeke aphethwe yi-socage (okungukuthi, ngokuhwebelana ngemali). I-English Fitzwalter Case ngo-1670 yakhipha isinqumo sokuthi ukuhlukunyezwa ngokubusa kwase kunqanyulwe iminyaka eminingi futhi noma yiziphi izimangalo kunontanga ngaleso sisekelo, okusho ukuthi ilungelo lokuhlala eNdlu Yenkosi, kwakungafanele zivuselelwe, nanoma yiliphi ilungelo lokulandelana elisekelwe kuzo.[58] 

ISitatimende SaseRhuddlan ngo-1284 salandela ukunqotshwa kweWales ngu-Edward I waseNgilandi. Yathatha amazwe aphethwe yiNkosana yaseGwynedd ngaphansi kwesihloko esithi "Prince of Wales" njengengxenye esemthethweni yezwe laseNgilandi, futhi yasungula izifunda ze-shire ngemodeli yesiNgisi kulezo zindawo. Ama-Marcher Lords ayeboshelwa kancane kancane emakhosini amaNgisi ngokunikezwa kwezindawo nobukhosi eNgilandi. I-Council of Wales kanye ne-Marches, elawulwa kusukela e-Ludlow Castle, yaqala yasungulwa ngu-Edward IV waseNgilandi ukuze ilawule amazwe aphethwe ngaphansi koBukhosi baseWales ngo-1472.[59] 

Ngaso leso sikhathi uMkhandlu WaseWales wasungulwa ngo-1472, kwamiswa uMkhandlu WaseNyakatho wezifunda ezisenyakatho yeNgilandi. Ngemva kokungasasetshenziswa, yaphinde yamiswa ngo-1537 futhi yaqedwa ngo-1641. UMkhandlu WaseNtshonalanga owahlala isikhathi esifushane wawukhona naseWest Country phakathi kuka-1537 no-1540.[60] 

Intela 
Ngesikhathi se-Anglo-Saxon, intela ye-geld noma yendawo yaqale yakhokhiswa ukuphendula ukuhlasela kwe-Danish kodwa kamuva yaba intela evamile. Iningi lemali engenayo yenkosi etholakala ku-royal demesne kanye "nepulazi" lonyaka eliphuma ku-shire ngayinye (isamba esinqunyiwe esikhokhwa osherifu ngelungelo lokuphatha nokwenza inzuzo emazweni asebukhosini). Amakhosi nawo athola imali ngezinhlawulo zokwahlulela nokulawula ukuhweba.[61] Abantu babekweleta inkosi inkonzo ye-trinoda necessitas—inkonzo ye-fyrd, i-burh building, kanye nokwakhiwa kwebhuloho.[62] 

Ngemuva kokunqotshwa kwe-1066, amaNorman aqhubeka nokuqoqa i-geld njalo. Baphinde bethula imithombo emisha yemali engenayo esekelwe emicabangweni ye-feudalism. Inkosi yayinelungelo lokuqoqa usizo lwe-feudal lapho indodana yayo endala ilwa, indodakazi yayo endala ishada, noma uma inkosi kudingeka izikhokhele isihlengo sayo. Indlalifa yenkosana kwakudingeka futhi ikhokhele inkosi isinxephezelo ngaphambi kokuba ithathe ifa layo. Inkosi futhi yayinelungelo lenkonzo yezempi engaphansi kwayo, kodwa izikhulu zazikwazi ukukhokhela ukuxoshwa esikhundleni.[63] Imibhalo Eyinhloko 

Yezempi 
: Ibutho LesiNgisi Nomlando weRoyal Navy (ngaphambi kuka-1707)
Esikhathini sama-Anglo-Saxon, iNgilandi yayingenamasosha amile. Inkosi nezikhulu zagcina amasosha asekhaya aqeqeshiwe (bheka i-housecarl), futhi wonke amadoda akhululekile ayebophekile ukwenza inkonzo yezempi endaweni. Ngaphezu kwalokho, abanikazi bezindawo zamabhuku babenesibopho sokuhlinzeka ngenani elithile lamadoda ngokusekelwe enanini lezikhumba abanazo.[64] 

Ngemuva kwe-Norman Conquest, amabutho endlu yenkosi ahlala ephakathi kwanoma yiliphi ibutho lasebukhosini. I-Anglo-Saxon fyrd nayo yahlala isetshenziswa. Kodwa amaNorman aphinde wethula isici esisha sombuso embuthweni wezempi wamaNgisi. Abaqashi benkosi (izinduna zakhe) babenesibopho sokuhlinzeka ngamaqhawe agibele amahhashi ukuze asebenze ebuthweni lasebukhosini noma amise izinqaba zasebukhosini. Isamba senani lama-knights ayekweletwa lalibizwa ngokuthi i-servitium debitum (ngesiLatini: "inkonzo ekweletwayo"), futhi isazi-mlando uRichard Huscroft silinganisela ukuthi leli nani lalilinganiselwa ku-5,000. Eqinisweni, i-servitium debitum yayinkulu kunanoma iyiphi inkosi engayidinga ngempela ngesikhathi sempi. Inhloso yayo enkulu bekuwukuhlola ukuthi singakanani isikweleti esikweletwa yinkosi. I-scuage yasetshenziselwa ukukhokhela amasosha, ayeyingxenye ebalulekile yanoma yiliphi ibutho lamaNorman.[65] 



"Uhulumeni Wobukhosi Bakhe" kanye "noHulumeni Wobukhosi Bakhe" uqondise kabusha lapha. Ukuze usebenzise leli gama, bheka Uhulumeni Wobukhosi (itemu). 
Le ndatshana imayelana nesiphathimandla esiphezulu sase-UK. Kubantu abakuhulumeni wamanje waseBrithani, bheka ibhentshi likaHulumeni WaseBrithani. Ukuze uthole uhlelo olubanzi lwezepolitiki lwase-UK, bheka Ipolitiki yase-United Kingdom.
