Amanye amazwe 
vte
Uhulumeni Wobukhosi Bakhe, [a] esifushaniswe kuHulumeni we-HM[b] noma ngenye indlela uHulumeni wase-UK, uyisiphathimandla esiphezulu se-United Kingdom of Great Britain kanye ne-Northern Ireland.[4][5] Uhulumeni uholwa ngundunankulu (uKeir Starmer kusukela ngomhlaka-5 Julayi 2024) oqoka bonke abanye ongqongqoshe. Izwe libe nohulumeni Wezabasebenzi kusukela ngo-2024. Undunankulu kanye nongqongqoshe bakhe abakhulu bangamalungu ekomidi eliphezulu elithatha izinqumo, elaziwa ngokuthi yiKhabhinethi.[5] 

Ongqongqoshe boBukhosi banesibopho seNdlu abahlala kuyo; benza izitatimende kuleyo Ndlu futhi bathathe imibuzo kumalungu aleyo Ndlu. Kongqongqoshe abaningi abaphezulu lokhu kuvame ukuba yiNdlu Yezikhulu Ezikhethiwe kuneNdlu Yamakhosi. Uhulumeni uncike ePhalamende ekwenzeni umthetho oyinhloko, [6] futhi ukhetho lukazwelonke lubanjwa njalo eminyakeni emihlanu (okungenani) ukuze kukhethwe iNdlu Yezikhulu Ezintsha, ngaphandle uma undunankulu eluleka inkosi ukuthi ihlakaze iPhalamende, lapho ukhetho lungase lubanjwe ngokushesha. Ngemva kokhetho, inkosi ikhetha njengondunankulu umholi weqembu okungenzeka kakhulu ukuthi alawule ukwethenjwa yiNdlu Yezikhulu, ngokuvamile ngokuba namaLungu EPhalamende amaningi.[7] 

Ngaphansi komthethosisekelo waseBrithani ongagunyaziwe, igunya eliphezulu likunkosi, nakuba leli gunya lisetshenziswa kuphela ngemva kokuthola iseluleko se-Privy Council.[8] Undunankulu, iHouse of Lords, umholi wamaqembu aphikisayo, kanye namaphoyisa kanye nezikhulu zezempi zisebenza njengamalungu nabeluleki benkosi eMkhandlwini Wangasese. Ezikhathini eziningi ikhabhinethi isebenzisa amandla ngokuqondile njengabaholi beminyango kahulumeni, nakuba ezinye izikhundla zeKhabhinethi ziyizicucu ngezinga elikhulu noma elincane (ngokwesibonelo iShansela ye-Duchy of Lancaster noma i-Lord Privy Seal). 

Uhulumeni kwesinye isikhathi ubizwa ngegama elithi "Westminster" noma "Whitehall", njengoba amahhovisi akhe amaningi ekhona. Lawa mamenymem asetshenziswa ikakhulukazi amalungu kaHulumeni waseScotland, uHulumeni waseWales kanye neNorthern Ireland Executive ukuze bahlukanise uhulumeni wabo kuHulumeni Wobukhosi Bakhe. 

Umlando 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Umlando womthethosisekelo wase-United Kingdom kanye Nomlando Wobukhosi e-United Kingdom 
I-United Kingdom iwumbuso wasebukhosini ongokomthethosisekelo lapho inkosi ebusayo (okungukuthi, inkosi noma indlovukazi eyinhloko yombuso nganoma yisiphi isikhathi) ingenzi noma yiziphi izinqumo zezombusazwe ezivulekile. Zonke izinqumo zezepolitiki zithathwa uhulumeni nePhalamende. Lesi simo somthethosisekelo siwumphumela womlando omude wokuphoqa nokunciphisa amandla epolitiki enkosi, kusukela ngoMagna Carta ngo-1215.

Kusukela ekuqaleni kokubusa kuka-Edward VII ngo-1901, ngomhlangano, undunankulu ubeyilungu elikhethiwe lePhalamende (MP) futhi ngaleyo ndlela aziphendulele kwiNdlu Yezikhulu, nakuba kwakukhona amasonto amabili ngo-1963 lapho u-Alec Douglas-Home eqala ukuba yilungu leNdlu Yenkosi futhi ngemva kwalokho engekho indlu. Ingqungquthela efanayo iyasebenza esikhundleni sikashansela we-exchequer. Ushansela wokugcina we-Exchequer ukuba yilungu leNdlu Yenkosi kwakunguLord Denman, owakhonza inyanga eyodwa ngo-1834.[9] 

I-Powers 
Royal Prerogative 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ilungelo Lasebukhosini e-United Kingdom 
Inkosi yaseBrithani iyinhloko yezwe kanye nobukhosi, kodwa hhayi inhloko kahulumeni. Empeleni, iNgonyama ngokuvamile ayihlanganyeli ngokuqondile ekubuseni izwe futhi ayithathi hlangothi ezindabeni zezombangazwe. Kodwa-ke, igunya lombuso elinikezwe umbusi, owaziwa ngokuthi uMqhele, lisewumthombo wamandla okuphatha asetshenziswa uhulumeni. 

Ngaphezu kwegunya elisemthethweni elicacile, umqhele uphinde ube nendikimba yamandla ezindabeni ezithile ezihlangene ezaziwa ngokuthi igunya lobukhosi. Lawa mandla asukela egunyeni lokukhipha noma lokuhoxisa amaphasipoti kuya ekumemezeleni impi. Ngokwengqungquthela osekunesikhathi eside ikhona, iningi lala mandla lisuke lidluliselwe kuMkhosi kongqongqoshe abehlukene noma ezinye izikhulu zoBukhosi, ezingawasebenzisa ngaphandle kokuthola imvume yePhalamende. 

Undunankulu naye uba nemihlangano yamasonto onke neNgonyama. Okushiwo kule mihlangano kuyimfihlo ngokuphelele; nokho, ngokuvamile zihilela izindaba zikahulumeni nezombangazwe inkosi enegunya “nomsebenzi” wokuphawula ngayo.[10] Ukuphawula okunjalo akubophi nokho futhi iNkosi kufanele ekugcineni ihambisane nezinqumo zikahulumeni.[11] 

Amandla obukhosi ahlanganisa, kodwa awagcini nje kulokhu okulandelayo: 

Amandla asekhaya 

iNdlovukazi u-Elizabeth II ethola uNdunankulu uTony Blair ngemva kokuwina ihlandla lesithathu ehhovisi ngomhla ziyisi-6 kuNhlaba wezi-2005 
Amandla okuqoka nokuxosha undunankulu. Lawa mandla asetshenziswa yinkosi uqobo. Kodwa-ke, okokugcina inkosi yasebenzisa ukuqonda kwayo lapho isebenzisa la mandla kwakungu-1834, nomhlangano wesimanje abawuqoka (futhi okulindeleke ukuba uqoke) umuntu okungenzeka kakhulu ukuthi akwazi ukubusa iningi eNdlu Yezikhulu.[12] 
Amandla okuqoka nokuxosha abanye ongqongqoshe. Lawa mandla asetshenziswa yiNgonyama ngokweseluleko sikandunankulu. 
Amandla okugunyaza nokushaya imithetho ngokunikeza imvume yobukhosi emithethwenisivivinyo ephasiswe yiPhalamende, edingekayo ukuze umthetho usebenze (isenzo). Lokhu kwenziwa yinkosi, nayo ngokweqiwa ukuthi inamandla okwenqaba imvume, yize kungekho nkosi eyenqabile ukuvuma umthethosivivinywa owaphasiswa yiPhalamende kusukela iNdlovukazi u-Anne ngo-1708. 
Amandla okunikeza kanye nokukhipha amakhomishana ezikhulwini ezithunyelwe eMbuthweni Wezempi. 
Amandla okuyala amaButho. Lawa mandla asetshenziswa uMkhandlu Wezokuvikela egameni leSilo. 
Amandla okuqoka amalungu oMkhandlu Wangasese.
Amandla okukhipha, ukumisa okwesikhashana, ukukhansela, ukukhumbula, ukubopha, ukuhoxisa, noma ukuhoxisa amaphasipoti ase-British kanye namandla ajwayelekile okuhlinzeka noma ukunqabela izinsiza zamaphasipoti waseBrithani kwizakhamizi zase-British kanye nezakhamuzi zase-British. Lokhu kwenziwa e-United Kingdom (kodwa hhayi e-Isle of Man, Channel Islands noma British Overseas Territories) ngunobhala wezasekhaya. 
Amandla okuxolela noma yikuphi ukugwetshwa (ilungelo lobukhosi lesihe). 
Amandla okunikeza, ukukhansela kanye nokuchitha noma yikuphi ukuhlonishwa. 
Amandla okudala izinkampani (okuhlanganisa nesimo sokuba idolobha, nenhlangano yalo) ngomthethosisekelo wasebukhosini, kanye nokuchibiyela, esikhundleni kanye nokuhoxisa ama-charter akhona. 
Amandla angaphandle 

Ihhovisi Lezangaphandle, I-Commonwealth kanye Nentuthuko, i-Whitehall 
Amandla okwenza nokuqinisekisa izivumelwano. 
Amandla okumemezela impi futhi aqedele ukuthula nezinye izizwe. 
Amandla okutshala Amasosha phesheya kwezilwandle. 
Amandla okubona izifundazwe. 
Amandla esikweletu nokwamukela amanxusa. 
Nakuba kungekho mibhalo esemthethweni ebeka amalungelo, uhulumeni washicilela lolu hlu olungenhla ngo-Okthoba 2003 ukuze kwandiswe obala, njengoba amanye amandla asetshenziswa egameni leNgonyama ayingxenye yelungelo lobukhosi.[13] Kodwa-ke, ubukhulu obuphelele bamandla obukhosi abuzange bubekwe ngokugcwele, njengoba amaningi awo avela esikweni lasendulo kanye nenkathi yobukhosi obuphelele, noma ashintshwa ngomkhuba womthethosisekelo wakamuva. 

Ongqongqoshe neminyango 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Uhlu longqongqoshe bakahulumeni base-United Kingdom kanye neMinyango Kahulumeni wase-United Kingdom 
Kusukela ngo-2019, kukhona ongqongqoshe bakahulumeni ababalelwa ku-120[14] abasekelwa abasebenzi bakahulumeni abangu-560,000[15] nabanye abasebenzi abasebenza eminyangweni yongqongqoshe engama-24[16] nezinhlaka zabo eziphezulu. Kukhona neminyango eyengeziwe engama-20 engeyona eyezongqongqoshe enohlu lweminye imisebenzi. 

Ngokombono, ungqongqoshe kahulumeni akudingekile ukuba abe yilungu lanoma iyiphi iNdlu yePhalamende. Nokho, empeleni, umhlangano uthi ongqongqoshe kufanele babe amalungu eNdlu Yezizwe noma ENdlu Yamakhosi ukuze baziphendulele ePhalamende. Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi, ondunankulu baqoka abangewona amalungu ePhalamende njengongqongqoshe. Eminyakeni esanda kudlula izikhonzi ezinjalo ziye zabekwa eNdlu Yezinkosi.[17] 

Uhulumeni ePhalamende
 
Imibuzo KaNdunankulu, 2024
Uhulumeni udingeka ngokomhlangano nangezizathu ezingokoqobo zokugcina ukuzethemba kweNdlu Yezikhulu. Kudinga ukusekelwa yiNdlu Yezizwe ukuze kugcinwe ukunikezwa (ngokuvota ngezabelomali zikahulumeni) kanye nokuphasisa umthetho oyinhloko. Ngokwengqungquthela, uma uhulumeni elahlekelwa ukwethenjwa yi-House of Commons kufanele asule noma kwenziwe ukhetho lukazwelonke. Ukwesekwa kwamakhosi, nakuba kuwusizo kuhulumeni ukuze kuphasiswe umthetho wakhe ngaphandle kokulibala, akubalulekile. Akudingeki ukuthi uhulumeni esule esikhundleni noma engasethembi amakhosi futhi ehlulwe ngamavoti abalulekile kuleyo Ndlu. Ngakho-ke i-House of Commons iyindlu enomthwalo wemfanelo. 

Undunankulu uzoziphendulela ngesikhathi semibuzo kaNdunankulu (PMQs) enikeza ithuba kumalungu ePhalamende kuzo zonke izinhlangothi ukuthi abuze uNdunankulu nganoma yisiphi isihloko. Kuphinde kube nemibuzo yomnyango uma ongqongqoshe bephendula imibuzo ephathelene nemininingwane yabo yomnyango. Ngokungafani nama-PMQ, bobabili ongqongqoshe bekhabhinethi bomnyango kanye nongqongqoshe abancane emnyangweni bangaphendula egameni likahulumeni, kuye ngesihloko sombuzo. 

Ngesikhathi sezinkulumo-mpikiswano ngomthetho ohlongozwa uhulumeni, ongqongqoshe—imvamisa abanomthwalo wemfanelo womnyango kulo mthethosivivinywa—bazohola inkulumo-mpikiswano kahulumeni futhi baphendule amaphuzu ashiwo ngamaLungu ePhalamende noma aMakhosi. 

Amakomidi[18] awo womabili eNdlu Yezizwe kanye neNdlu Yenkosi abamba uhulumeni ukuthi aziphendulele, acubungule umsebenzi wawo futhi ahlole ngokuningiliziwe iziphakamiso zomthetho. Ongqongqoshe bavela phambi kwamakomiti ukuze banikeze ubufakazi futhi baphendule imibuzo. 

Ongqongqoshe bakahulumeni nabo kudingeka ngokwengqungquthela kanye neKhodi yoNgqongqoshe,[19] lapho iPhalamende lihlezi, benze izitatimende ezinkulu mayelana nenqubomgomo kahulumeni noma izindaba ezibalulekile kuzwelonke ePhalamende. Lokhu kuvumela amalungu ePhalamende noma aMakhosi ukuthi abuze uhulumeni ngesitatimende. Lapho uhulumeni esikhundleni salokho ekhetha ukwenza izimemezelo kuqala ngaphandle kwePhalamende, kuvame ukugxekwa kakhulu amaLungu ePhalamende kanye nosomlomo weNdlu Yezizwe Ezivamile.[20] 

Indawo 

Isango lokungena elikhulu lika-10 Downing Street, indawo yokuhlala esemthethweni kanye nehhovisi leNkosi Yokuqala Yomnyango Wezezimali, osengundunankulu namuhla Undunankulu 
uzinze ku-10 Downing Street eWestminster, eLondon. Imihlangano yeKhabhinethi nayo iba khona lapha. Iminyango eminingi kahulumeni inekomkhulu layo eduze kwaseWhitehall. 

Imikhawulo yamandla kahulumeni 
Bheka futhi: Umthetho Wephalamende (UK) kanye Namandla kandunankulu wase-United Kingdom
Amandla kahulumeni ahlanganisa amandla okuphatha jikelele kanye nawomthetho, imithetho ephathisiwe, namandla amaningi okuqoka kanye nokuxhasa. Kodwa-ke, ezinye izikhulu ezinamandla nezinhlaka, (isb. amajaji e-HM, iziphathimandla zendawo, namakhomishana ezinhlangano ezisiza umphakathi) zizimele ngokusemthethweni noma kancane kuhulumeni, futhi amandla kahulumeni alinganiselwe ngokusemthethweni kulawo agcinwe Ubukhosi ngaphansi komthetho ovamile noma anikezwe futhi anqunyelwe ngokomthetho wePhalamende. Kokubili imikhawulo eqinile kanye nenqubo iphoqelelwa ezinkantolo ngokubuyekezwa kobulungiswa. 

Noma kunjalo, izimantshi nezimeya basengaboshwa futhi baquliswe amacala enkohlakalo, futhi uhulumeni unamandla okufaka amakhomishana kumasipala wendawo ukuze angamele umsebenzi wawo, futhi akhiphe iziqondiso okufanele zilandelwe umkhandlu wendawo uma umkhandlu wendawo ungathobeli izibopho zawo ezingokomthetho.[21] 

Ngokuphambene, njengasemazweni angamalungu e-European Union (EU), izikhulu ze-EU azikwazi ukushushiswa nganoma yiziphi izenzo eziqhutshwa ngokulandela imisebenzi yazo esemthethweni, futhi osomaqhinga bamazwe angaphandle (nakuba kungenjalo abasebenzi babo) kanye namalungu angaphandle ePhalamende LaseYurophu[22] avikelekile ekushushisweni ezifundazweni ze-EU ngaphansi kwanoma yisiphi isimo. Ngenxa yalokho, izinhlangano ze-EU noma osomaqhinga akufanele bakhokhe intela, ngoba ngeke kwenzeke ukuba bashushiswe ngenxa yokweqa intela. Lapho i-UK iyilungu le-EU, lokhu kwadala ingxabano lapho inxusa laseMelika e-UK lithi inkokhiso yokuminyana yaseLondon iyintela, hhayi inkokhiso (naphezu kwegama), ngakho-ke kwakungadingeki ukuthi ayikhokhe—isimangalo i-Greater London Authority esaphikiswana nayo. 

Ngokufanayo, inkosi ivikelekile ekushushisweni ngobugebengu futhi ingamangalelwa kuphela ngemvume yayo (lokhu kwaziwa ngokuthi i-sovereign immunity). Inkosi, ngokomthetho, ayidingeki ukuthi ikhokhe intela yeholo, kodwa iNdlovukazi u-Elizabeth II wayikhokha ngokuzithandela kusukela ngo-1993 kwaze kwaba sekupheleni kokubusa kwayo ngo-2022, futhi yakhokha nentela yendawo ngokuzithandela. Kodwa-ke, ubukhosi buphinde bathola uxhaso olukhulu luvela kuhulumeni, Isibonelelo Sikahulumeni Sokusekela, kanye nefa leNdlovukazi u-Elizabeth II kunina, iNdlovukazi u-Elizabeth Indlovukazi Umama, yayingakhokhiswa intela yefa. 

Ukwengeza emandleni okushaya umthetho, uHulumeni Wobukhosi unamandla amakhulu kuziphathimandla zasekhaya nezinye izinhlaka ezisungulwe yiwo, ngamandla ezezimali nezibonelelo. Imisebenzi eminingi eyenziwa iziphathimandla zendawo, njengokukhokha izinzuzo zezindlu kanye nezinzuzo zentela yomkhandlu, ixhaswa noma ingxenye enkulu ixhaswa uhulumeni omkhulu.

Uhulumeni omkhulu noma iziphathimandla zendawo azivunyelwe ukumangalela noma ubani ngokwehlisa isithunzi. Osopolitiki ngabanye bavunyelwe ukumangalela abantu ngokwehlisa isithunzi ngokomuntu siqu futhi ngaphandle kokusebenzisa izimali zikahulumeni, kodwa lokhu kuyivelakancane uma kuqhathaniswa (nakuba uGeorge Galloway, owayeyilungu lePhalamende le-backbench ingxenye yesine yekhulu, uye wamangalela noma wasabisa ngokufaka icala lokudicilela phansi isithunzi izikhathi eziningana). Kodwa-ke, kuyicala lobugebengu ukwenza isitatimende esingamanga nganoma yimuphi umuntu ongenele ukhetho ngesikhathi sokhetho, ukuze kuncishiswe inani lamavoti abawatholayo (njengama-libel, imibono ayibali). 

Itemu 

Umhlangano wekhabhinethi eGumbi leKhabhinethi, 10 Downing Street 
Nakuba uhulumeni eyiqembu lamanje longqongqoshe (ibhentshi eliphambili likaHulumeni waseBrithani), ngezinye izikhathi uhulumeni ubonakala ngokubanzi njengohlanganisa abantu noma izinhlangano ezisebenzela ongqongqoshe. Izisebenzi zikahulumeni, nakuba 'zizimele kuhulumeni',[23] ngezinye izikhathi zichazwa njengengxenye kahulumeni,[24][25][26][27] ngenxa yokusondelana kokusebenza kwazo nongqongqoshe, ukubaluleka, ukubeseka, nokusebenzisa izinqumo zabo zokuphatha. Abanye abantu abasebenzela ongqongqoshe banalo ngisho negama elithi 'Hulumeni' ezihlokweni zabo, njengethi Government Actuary kanye noGovernment Chief Scientific Adviser, kanjalo nezinhlangano zezisebenzi zikahulumeni ezifana ne-Government Statistical Service, i-Government Legal Profession, neHhovisi Likahulumeni Lesayensi. Izinkampani eziphethwe nguhulumeni zingabonakala njengezingxenye zikahulumeni, njenge-UK Government Investments[28] kanye ne-HS2 Ltd.[29] 

Ngokufanayo, oNobhala Abazimele bePhalamende ababona ongqongqoshe ngakho abayona ingxenye kahulumeni.[30] Kodwa-ke, baboshwe izingxenye zekhodi yongqongqoshe, bayingxenye yevoti labakhokhelwayo, futhi bangabonakala 'njengabasesigabeni sokuqala sesitebhisi songqongqoshe'.[31][32] Kwesinye isikhathi bachazwa njengengxenye kahulumeni.[33][34][35] 

Izimpawu 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ijazi lezikhali lase-United Kingdom 

Izikhali ezincane ezisetshenziswe kusukela ngo-2024 
Uhulumeni wase-UK usebenzisa uhlobo olwenziwe lula lwe-Royal Arms njengophawu olubizwa ngokuthi izingalo ezincane. Ivamise ukushiya i-helm kanye ne-mantling, inciphisa i-crest ibe umqhele wodwa, futhi ayinakho igumbi.[36] Nakuba ukukhanya kwezikhali kungashintshile kusukela ngo-1837, kwakhiwa isithombe esisha se-Royal Arms ekubuseni ngakunye okusha.[36]

Ukusetshenziswa Kwezikhali Zasebukhosini yiminyango nezinhlaka zikahulumeni kulawulwa yiHhovisi leKhabhinethi.[37] I-Royal Arms itholakala kuyo yonke iMithetho YePhalamende, kumalogo eminyango kahulumeni, esembozweni sawo wonke amaphasipoti ase-UK (namaphasiphothi akhishwa kwezinye izindawo zaseBrithani nokuncika kwawo), njengengxenye yokunganqamuki emafulegeni enxusa lamaNxusa aseBrithani, kanye naku-The London Gazette. Ibuye isetshenziswe e-British Overseas Territories, okungukuthi kuzo zonke izenzo ze-Anguilla House of Assembly kanye nabaphathi be-Akrotiri ne-Dhekelia, i-Pitcairn Islands, ne-South Georgia kanye ne-South Sandwich Islands. 

Eminye iminyango isebenzisa uphawu oluhlukile njengezizathu ezingokomlando zophawu lwayo, okuhlanganisa neHhovisi LaseScotland, Ihhovisi Lasekhaya, Umnyango Wezokuvikela kanye Nomnyango Webhizinisi Nohwebo.[37] 

Ohulumeni Abadaluliwe 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukwehliswa kwezimali e-United Kingdom 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Uhulumeni wase-Scottish, I-Northern Ireland Executive, kanye noHulumeni Wase-Wales 
Kusukela ngo-1999, izindawo ezithile zikahulumeni omkhulu zinikezelwe kohulumeni abaphendulayo e-Scotland, Wales naseNyakatho Ireland. Laba abayona ingxenye kaHulumeni woNgangezwe Lakhe, futhi baphendule ngokuqondile ezikhungweni zabo, negunya labo ngaphansi koBukhosi; ngokuphambene, akekho uhulumeni kazwelonke ohlukanisiwe waseNgilandi, nakuba amandla athile kahulumeni omaphakathi edluliselwe ku-Greater London Authority kanye neziphathimandla ezihlangene. 

Uhulumeni wasekhaya 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Uhulumeni wasekhaya eNgilandi, eScotland, eWales, naseNyakatho Ireland 
Kuze kufike ezigabeni ezintathu zeziphathimandla zendawo ezikhethiwe (ezifana nemiKhandlu yesifunda, yesifunda kanye neyepherishi) zikhona kuzo zonke izingxenye ze-United Kingdom, kwezinye izindawo ezihlanganiswe zaba yiziphathimandla ezihlangene. Banamandla alinganiselwe endawo okunyusa intela. Ezinye iziphathimandla nama-ejensi amaningi nawo anamandla angokomthetho, ngokuvamile angaphansi kokuqondisa kukahulumeni othile. 



UClement Attlee wamenywa yiNkosi uGeorge VI ukuthi enze inkonzo yokuqala ka-Attlee e-United Kingdom ngomhla zingama-26 kuJulayi 1945, [1] elandela uWinston Churchill njengondunankulu wase-United Kingdom. I-Labour Party yayinqobe ngamalengiso okhethweni lukazwelonke lwango-1945, futhi yaqhubeka nokwenza izinqubomgomo zalokho okwaziwa ngokuthi ukuvumelana kwangemva kwempi, okuhlanganisa ukusungulwa kombuso wezenhlalakahle kanye nokufakwa kuzwelonke kwamaphesenti angama-20 omnotho wonke.[2] Ukuphatha kukahulumeni esikhundleni kwaphawulwa yizinyathelo zokunciphisa emuva kwempi; ukuchotshozwa kwezinhlangano ezilwela inkululeko kanye namakhomanisi eMalaya; ukunikezwa kokuzimela kweNdiya, iPakistan, iCeylon, neBurma; ukubandakanyeka eMpini Yomshoshaphansi ngokumelene nobuKhomanisi baseSoviet; kanye nokwakhiwa kweNational Health Service (NHS) yezwe.

U-Attlee waqhubeka nokuwina iningi elincane okhethweni lukazwelonke lwango-1950, akha inkonzo yesibili ka-Attlee.[3] Ezinyangeni ezingamashumi amabili nje ngemva kwalolo khetho, u-Attlee wabiza ukhetho olusha lwangomhla zingama-25 kuMfumfu 1951, kodwa wahlulwa kancane yi-Conservative Party, okwathumela iLabour esikhathini esiyiminyaka eyi-13 bephikisana. 

Abaholi 
ILabour Party yangena emandleni kulandela ukunqoba kwayo okungalindelekile okhethweni lukazwelonke lwangoJulayi 1945. Umholi weqembu uClement Attlee waba undunankulu esikhundleni sikaWinston Churchill ngasekupheleni kukaJulayi. U-Ernest Bevin wayenguNobhala Wezangaphandle kwaze kwaba ngaphambi nje kokufa kwakhe ngo-April 1951. U-Hugh Dalton waba nguShansela we-Exchequer (nakuba kwadingeka asule ngo-1947), kuyilapho u-James Chuter Ede enguNobhala Wezangaphakathi. 

Ezinye izibalo eziphawulekayo kuhulumeni zazihlanganisa: U-Herbert Morrison, iPhini likaNdunankulu kanye noMholi weNdlu Yezikhulu, owangena esikhundleni sikaBevin njengoNobhala Wezangaphandle ngoNdasa 1951; USir Stafford Cripps ekuqaleni wayenguMongameli Webhodi Lezohwebo kodwa wathatha isikhundla sika-Dalton njengoShansela we-Exchequer ngo-1947; U-Hugh Gaitskell ubambe izikhala ezimbalwa ezincane ngaphambi kokuthatha uCripps njengoShansela ngo-1950; U-Aneurin Bevan wayenguNgqongqoshe Wezempilo; U-Arthur Greenwood wayengu-Lord Privy Seal kanye no-Paymaster General ngenkathi uNdunankulu wakusasa u-Harold Wilson eba yilungu elincane kunawo wonke lekhabhinethi ekhulwini lama-20 (eneminyaka engu-31) lapho enziwa uMongameli weBhodi Lezohwebo ngo-1947. Ophawuleka kakhulu kumalungu ambalwa wesifazane kahulumeni kwakungu-Ellen Wilkinson, owayenguNgqongqoshe Wezemfundo kwaze kwaba yilapho eshona ePowaiesr47 ekuqaleni 
kwesihloko saseBrithani 

. (1945-1979) 

Ikhathuni yangaleso sikhathi kumagazini wasePoland we-satirical i-Szpilki igxeka inkonzo ka-Attlee 
Kwakuyinkathi "yokuzilibazisa", njengoba ukulinganisa ngesikhathi sempi kwakuqhubeka naphezu kokunqoba kwe-Allied Forces, futhi kwaze kwanwetshwa ukuze kufakwe nesinkwa. Izimo zokuphila zazimpofu; esikhundleni sokwanda, umsebenzi wezwe wawuwukuthatha indawo yengcebo yezwe eyachithwa noma eyasetshenziswa phakathi nempi. Ukuwohloka Okukhulu Komnotho akuzange kubuye, futhi kwaqashwa ngokugcwele. Omakadebona ababuyayo baphinde bafakwa ngempumelelo emphakathini wangemva kwempi.[5] Uhulumeni wase-Attlee wenza kuzwelonke cishe u-20% womnotho, okuhlanganisa amalahle, izitimela, ezokuthutha emgwaqeni, iBhange LaseNgilandi, izindiza zomphakathi, ugesi negesi, nensimbi. Yayincane imali yokutshalwa kwezimali ukuze lezi zimboni zibe zesimanje, futhi ukulawulwa kwakugcinwa nguhulumeni, kunokuba kudluliselwe kumalungu enyunyana. Uhulumeni wase-Attlee wandisa kakhulu isimo senhlalakahle, ngoMthetho Wenkonzo Yezempilo Kazwelonke we-1946, owafaka izibhedlela ezweni lonke futhi wahlinzeka ngokunakekelwa kwezempilo kwamahhala emhlabeni wonke. Umthetho Womshuwalense Kazwelonke we-1946 unikeze izinzuzo zokugula kanye nokungasebenzi kubantu abadala, kanye nezimpesheni zomhlalaphansi.

Uhlelo Losizo Lukazwelonke olwasungulwa ngaphansi koMthetho Wosizo Kazwelonke we-1948 (11 & 12 Geo. 6. c. 29) luhlinzekele ukwengezwa okukhethekile masonto onke ukuze kuhlangatshezwane nezimo ezikhethekile ezifana nezindleko zokudla kanye nelondolo, ngesikhathi ngokubona kweBhodi Losizo Likazwelonke 'Izibonelelo zezidingo Eziyingqayizivele' (isamba esiyisamba sezinkokhelo zezindleko ezitholakalayo ukuze kuhlangatshezwane nezidingo ezikhethekile ezitholakalayo. Ngaphezu kwalokho, "Irenti yayibhekwa njengento ehlukile yemfuneko: abaninikhaya ngokuvamile babethola irenti yabo yonke ngokugcwele, kuyilapho abangewona abanikazi bezindlu bezothola 'isabelo esizwakalayo' serenti ekhokhwa umninikhaya, kuncike emikhawulweni ephezulu nephansi."[6] I-National Assistance (Ukunqunywa Kwesidingo) Imithetho ka-1948, njengezabelo ezingaboni kahle, ezibekwe ezilinganisweni ezihlukile zabazuzi abahlukahlukene. iziguli kanye nokuhlinzekwa kwabafake izicelo ezindlini zomasipala. Isamba samasonto onke mayelana nezidingo zerenti yavunyelwa, leyo emithethweni eshiwo "emalini yerenti yamasonto onke, noma ingxenye yayo, efanele isonto, ngaphandle kwezikweleti zayo, kanye nengxenye yamasonto onke yemali ephumayo ethwalwa umninikhaya okuhlanganisa, ikakhulukazi, amarates, isibonelelo esizwakalayo kunoma yiziphi izindleko ezidingekile zokulungisa noma ukukhokhwa kwengxenye yemali ekhokhwayo ngesikhathi saleyo ngxenye yemali ekhokhwayo. isikweletu sendlu ebolekwayo noma isibambiso esitholakalayo esikhokhiswa indlu lapho umninikhaya ehlala khona, noma ngenzalo yalutho kuyo."[7]

Kuphinde kwenziwa ukunganakwa okuhlukene ngaphansi kweNational Assistance Act 1948, okuhlanganisa nanoma yisiphi isibonelelo sokufa esikhokhelwa umuntu ngaphansi kwezinhlinzeko zesigaba samashumi amabili nambili seNational Insurance Act 1946, noma yisiphi isibonelelo sokubeletha lapho owesifazane anelungelo lokusithola ngaphansi kwesigaba seshumi nane soMthetho Womshuwalense Kazwelonke we-1946, osheleni abayishumi bokuqala kanye nenkokhelo ye-6 noma inkokhelo yokuqala yenhlangano yabasebenzi ethola ishumi ngesonto. eziyisithupha ngesonto "zanoma iyiphi inkokhelo yempesheni noma izinkokhelo zempesheni mayelana nenkonzo yangaphambilini noma umsebenzi lapho umemukeli ashiye khona umhlalaphansi noma esula emsebenzini (kungakhathaliseki ukuthi ikhokhwa umqashi wangaphambili noma cha), engeyona inkokhelo noma izinkokhelo— (i) ngenxa yempesheni ngaphansi koMthetho Wezimpesheni Zabadala, 1936 noma ngaphansi noma ngegunya le-Old Age and Ortribution, Conphages 1936 kuya ku-1941, noma ngaphansi kwanoma yimuphi umthetho osulwe yinoma yimiphi leyo Mithetho, noma (ii) ngenxa yempesheni yomhlalaphansi ngaphansi koMthetho Womshuwalense Kazwelonke, 1946," noma iyiphi inkokhelo "mayelana nomholo noma impesheni encike kuyo isigaba seshumi nesithupha [9 & 10 Geo] 5. c. isibonelelo esihambisana nempesheni enjalo," noma iyiphi inkokhelo "mayelana nempesheni yokukhubazeka ekhishwa ngaphansi koMthetho [2 & 3 Geo 6. c 82.] Personal Injuries (Emergency Provisions) Act, 1939, okuhlanganisa, ukukhushulwa kwempesheni enjalo maqondana nababondliwa," noma iyiphi inkokhelo yamasonto onke "ngendlela yokunxeshezelwa" nganoma iyiphi indlela yokunxeshezelwa ngomsebenzi. ukuhlomula ngaphansi kwesigaba seshumi nambili soMthetho Womshuwalense Kazwelonke (Industrial Injuries) Act, 1946."[8] 

Kwakhiwa izindlu zomkhandlu ezengeziwe, futhi kwenziwa izinhlelo ngoMthetho Wamadolobha Amusha 1946 (9 & 10 Geo. 6. c. 68) ukuze kukhule izindawo ezingaphansi kwedolobha, kanye nokunciphisa ukuminyana emadolobheni amakhulu njengeLondon neGlasgo. Njengoba kwakunemali encane yokuhlela okuningiliziwe, uhulumeni wamukela i-Keynesianism, eyayivumela ukuhlela ngomqondo wokulawula konke okushodayo kanye nensalela kazwelonke.[9][10][11] 

Umthetho Wezokuthutha wango-1947 wasungula iKhomishana Yezokuthutha YaseBrithani, eyathatha izintambo zokulawula ujantshi kusukela ku-Big Four—Great Western Railway, London, Midland and Scottish Railway, London and North Eastern Railway and the Southern Railway—ukuze kwakhiwe iBritish Railways.[12] 

Ezindabeni zakwamanye amazwe, uhulumeni wayesebenza eNhlanganweni Yezizwe Ezihlangene futhi waxoxisana ngemali ebolekwa ngamaRandi ayizigidi eziyizinkulungwane ezingu-5 evela e-United States naseCanada ngo-1946. Wajoyina ngokulangazela i-Marshall Plan ngo-1948. Wayengasenakukwazi ukusekela uhulumeni waseGreece phakathi neMpi Yombango YamaGreki futhi wakhuthaza i-US ukuthi ithathe indawo yayo nge-Truman Doctrine ngo-1947. Yathatha indima esebenzayo e-United States ekuhlanganiseni i-NATO. Yanikeza inkululeko eNdiya, ePakistan,ECeylon naseBurma futhi bathuthela ekuqiniseni iBritish Commonwealth.[13] 

Amaphrojekthi okwenziwa kuzwelonke
1945–51 
I-Labour Party iqala ukubusa ngohlelo lokwenza imikhakha ebalulekile yezomnotho ibe ngaphansi kukahulumeni, eminye yayo eyayintekenteke ngesikhathi sempi: ezezimali, izimboni ezinzima kanye nemithombo yemvelo, kanye nengqalasizinda yezokuxhumana nezokuthutha.[14][15][16] 
1946 
Imboni yamalahle ngaphansi kweBhodi Likazwelonke Lamalahle.[17] 
Ibhange laseNgilandi.[18] 
Isevisi Yezempilo Kazwelonke idaliwe (namayunithi ahlukene e-England, Wales, naseScotland naseNyakatho Ireland) ithatha izibhedlela nokwenza izinsiza zezokwelapha zibe mahhala. I-NHS yaqala ukusebenza ngo-1948.[19][20] 
1947 
British Electricity Authority kanye namabhodi kagesi wendawo.[21] 
Ikhebula Nokungenantambo.[22] 
1948 
Isitimela sikaZwelonke, ezokuthutha zamanzi ezingaphakathi nezwe (hhayi zasolwandle), ukuthutha okuthile emigwaqeni, ukuthutha abagibeli bomgwaqo kanye noThomas Cook & Son ngaphansi kweKhomishini Yezokuthutha YaseBrithani. Izinto ezihlukene zisebenza njengeBritish Railways, British Road Services, kanye neBritish Waterways.[23] 
1949 
Iziphathimandla zendawo zokuhlinzeka ngegesi e-England, Scotland naseWales.[21] 
1951 
Iron and Steel Corporation of Great Britain (yangasese Uhulumeni Wokulondoloza Imvelo ngo-1955, futhi yashintshwa kabusha ngabaSebenzi ngo-1967 njengeBritish Steel Corporation).[24][25][26] 
Izinqubomgomo zezenhlalakahle 
I-Health 

Trafford General Hospital, eyaziwa njengendawo yokuzalwa kukaNgqongqoshe 
Wezempilo we-NHS Attlee, u-Aneurin Bevan, walwa kanzima ngokumelene nokungavunyelwa okuvamile kokusungulwa kwezokwelapha, kuhlanganise neBritish Medical Association, ngokudala iNational Health Service ngo-1948. Lokhu kwakuwuhlelo lokunakekelwa kwezempilo oluxhaswe ngumphakathi, olwanikeza ukwelashwa kubo bonke, kungakhathaliseki ukuthi yini engenayo, mahhala endaweni yokusetshenziswa. Ibonisa isidingo sokuvala osekunesikhathi eside sikhona sezinkonzo zezokwelapha, i-NHS yelapha iziguli zamazinyo ezingaba ngu-8,500,000 futhi yakhipha amapheya angaphezu kuka-5,000,000 ezibuko phakathi nonyaka wayo wokuqala isebenza.[27] 

Ababonisi bahlomula ohlelweni olusha ngokukhokhelwa amaholo ayenikeza izinga lokuphila elamukelekayo ngaphandle kwesidingo sokuba baphendukele emisebenzini yangasese.[28] I-NHS ilethe intuthuko enkulu empilweni yabantu besigaba sabasebenzi, kwathi ukufa ngenxa ye-diphtheria, inyumoniya, nesifo sofuba kwehle kakhulu.[29] Nakuba kwakuvame ukuba nezingxabano mayelana nenhlangano kanye noxhaso lwazo, amaqembu ezombusazwe aseBrithani aqhubeka nokuzwakalisa ukusekela kwawo jikelele i-NHS ukuze aqhubeke ekhethwa.[30]

Emkhakheni wokunakekelwa kwezempilo, izimali zabelwa ukuthuthukiswa kwezinhlelo zesimanje kanye nokwelulwa okuhloswe ngazo ukuthuthukisa ukusebenza kahle kwezokuphatha. Kwenziwa ngcono indawo yokulala yabahlengikazi ukuze kuqashelwe abahlengikazi abengeziwe futhi kuncishiswe ukushoda kwezisebenzi okwakugcina imibhede engu-60,000 ingasasebenzi, futhi kwenziwa imizamo yokunciphisa ukungalingani “phakathi kwemibhede yomkhuhlane nesifo sofuba (TB) ngokweqile kanye nokuntuleka kwemibhede yokubeletha”.[31] 

Imithi yokugoma ye-BCG yethulwa ukuze kuvikelwe abafundi bezokwelapha, ababelethisi, abahlengikazi, nokuxhumana neziguli ezinesifo sofuba,[32] kwasungulwa uhlelo lwempesheni lwabasebenzi be-NHS esanda kusungulwa,[33] I-National Health Service (Superannuation) Regulations 1947 yabeka inani lezinhlinzeko kwabahlomulayo okuhlanganisa impesheni yesikhulu, impesheni, impesheni kanye nenkonzo yokuhoxiswa. i-gratuity, impesheni yomfelokazi, kanye nezinkokhelo ezengeziwe uma kwenzeka kuba nezigaba ezikhethekile zezikhulu. Kwenziwa nelungiselelo lokwabiwa kwengxenye yempesheni noma yesibonelelo sokulimala kumlingani wobondliwa.[34] 

I-Radioactive Substances Act 1948 ibeka imibandela evamile yokulawula izinto ezikhipha imisebe.[35] Kwaphinde kwethulwa izinguquko eziningi ezincane, ezinye zazo ezazuzisa kakhulu izingxenye ezithile zomphakathi waseBrithani, njengabakhubazekile ngokwengqondo nezimpumputhe.[36] Phakathi kuka-1948 no-1951, uhulumeni ka-Attlee wenyusa ukusetshenziswa kwemali kwezempilo kusuka ku-£6,000,000,000 kuya ku-£11,000,000,000: ukwanda okungaphezu kuka-80%, futhi kusuka ku-2.1% kuya ku-3.6% we-GDP.[37] 

Ezenhlalakahle 
Uhulumeni waqala ukusebenzisa izinhlelo ze-Beveridge Report ngesikhathi sempi ukuze kwakhiwe isimo senhlalakahle 'esizangcwaba', futhi amise uhlelo olusha ngokuphelele lokuvikeleka komphakathi. Phakathi kwemithetho ebaluleke kakhulu kwakukhona uMthetho Womshuwalense Kazwelonke we-1946, lapho abantu abasebenzayo babekhokha inani eliphelele lomshwalense kazwelonke. Ngokubuyisela, bona (kanye nabafazi babanikeli besilisa) babefanelekela impesheni yezinga eliphansi, inzuzo yokugula, inzuzo yokungasebenzi, kanye nenzuzo yomngcwabo.[38] Kufakwe izinhlinzeko ezehlukene kuMthetho Womshuwalense Kazwelonke we-1946 okuhlanganisa ukungasebenzi kanye nenzuzo yokugula, isibonelelo sokubeletha kanye nesibonelelo sokuya esikoleni, isibonelelo sokubeletha, umhlomulo womfelokazi, impesheni yomfelokazi ezimweni ezikhethekile, impesheni yomnakekeli, impesheni yomhlalaphansi, kanye nesibonelelo sokufa.[39] UMthetho Kazwelonke Womshuwalense Ka-1951, njengoba kwaphawulwa okunye ukuhlola, “wethula imali ekhokhwa kanye nezinzuzo zabafelokazi ngengane ngayinye ebondliwayo emkhayeni.”[40] 

Eminye imithetho ehlukahlukene ehlinzekelwe ukuhlomula kwezingane nokondla abantu abangenawo omunye umthombo wemali engenayo.[38] Ngo-1949, ukungasebenzi, ukugula kanye nezinzuzo zokubeletha zakhululwa ekukhokhisweni intela.[41]

Uxhaso lwebhulokhi olwethulwa ngo-1948 lwasiza izinsizakalo zezenhlalakahle ezihlinzekwa iziphathimandla zendawo.[42] Izinkonzo Zezenhlalakahle Zomuntu Siqu noma izinsizakalo zezenhlalakahle zathuthukiswa ngo-1948 kulungiselelwa umuntu ngamunye kanye nemindeni jikelele, ikakhulukazi amaqembu akhethekile afana nabaphazamisekile ngokwengqondo, izingane ezintulayo, abantu abadala, nabakhubazekile.[43] 

Uhulumeni wase-Attlee wenyusa izimpesheni nezinye izinzuzo, kwathi izimpesheni zaphakanyiswa ukuze zibe yimali yokuziphilisa kunanini ngaphambili. Izimpesheni zempi kanye nezibonelelo (zazo zombili iziMpi Zomhlaba) zenyuswa ngesenzo sika-1946 [ikuphi?] esanikeza indoda eyayilimele isabelo somkayo nezingane uma ishada ngemva kokulimala, ngaleyo ndlela isusa isikhalo seminyaka engaphezu kwamashumi amabili imile.[44] Kwenziwa okunye ukuthuthukiswa kwezimpesheni zempi ngesikhathi u-Attlee engundunankulu. Isibonelelo Esiqhubekayo Sokuba khona saphindwa kathathu, Isibonelelo Sokungaqashwa saphindwa kathathu sisuka kwabaneminyaka engu-10 kuya kwengama-30 ngesonto, futhi kwethulwa nesibonelelo sobunzima esikhethekile esingafika ku-£1 ngesonto. Ngaphezu kwalokho, iSabelomali sango-1951 senza okunye ukuthuthuka ezinkolelweni ezingeziwe zabaningi abahola impesheni ezimpini. Kusukela ngo-1945 kuqhubeke, izicelo zempesheni ezintathu kwezine zibe yimpumelelo, kanti ngemva kweMpi Yezwe Yokuqala kwavunyelwa isicelo esisodwa sempesheni kwezintathu.[45] Ngaphansi koMthetho Wokuhoxiswa Kwempesheni (Izihlinzeko Ezixubile) ka-1948, abasebenzi bendikimba emele iziphathimandla zendawo noma izikhulu zeziphathimandla zendawo zingamukelwa "ngemibandela efanele esikhwameni sempesheni yomkhandlu wendawo".[46] Ngo-1951, kwethulwa imali yokunethezeka eyakhokhelwa ngokuzenzekelayo abahola impesheni zempi "abathola isengezo sokungaqashi kanye nesibonelelo sokuya njalo".[47] 

AbakwaPersUkulimala komlomo (Izakhamuzi) Uhlelo luka-1947 lwaluhlanganisa izinzuzo ezihlukahlukene njengezinga eliphakeme elikhethekile lesibonelelo sokuhlala njalo sama-40s ngesonto, kanye nesibonelelo sokuguga nokuklebhuka kwezingubo ezibangelwa ukusetshenziswa kwezitho nezimpahla zikagesi. Ukwengeza, izibonelelo ezikhokhwayo ngenkathi ohola impesheni elashelwa esibhedlela "ngokujwayelekile azisakhonjelwe ekubanjweni kwemali maqondana nokwehla kwezindleko zekhaya." Izinguquko ezehlukene zenziwa maqondana nabantu abaqashwe ngendlela ezuzisayo kanye namavolontiya okuvikela umphakathi athole ukulimala ezimpini. Lokhu kwakuhlanganisa ukuhlinzekwa kwezibonelelo zenkosikazi nezingane zabantu abalimele abathola isibonelelo sokulimala noma impesheni yokukhubazeka, izichibiyelo ezinhlinzekweni zesibonelelo somuntu ohola impesheni othathwa njengongaqashiwe ngenxa yokukhubazeka kwakhe kwempesheni "ukuze aqinisekise ukuthi uyayithola isamba semali yokungasebenzi kanye nanoma yiziphi izinzuzo zensizakalo yezenhlalakahle ezifanele ukunyuselwa impesheni okungenani ngeviki," 20. imali ekhokhelwa umfazi womuntu othola isibonelelo sokwelashwa, isibonelelo sokungasebenzi noma sokulimala ngaphansi kwemibandela ethile futhi "uma kungekho mali ekhokhwayo yomfazi, isibonelelo singanikezwa umuntu omdala obondliwayo," kanye nesibonelelo sobunzima bomphakathi samadoda akhubazeke ngokwengxenye "ukuthi, nakuba engaqashiwe, evinjwa ngokuthatha kwakhe ukukhubazeka ayekusebenze ekuqaleni noma ukuthatha umsebenzi wakhe wangaphambili wokukhubazeka." Futhi, “Lapho indoda ifa ngenxa yokulimala okufanelekayo, umfelokazi wayo angase aklonyeliswe impesheni (kanye nezibonelelo zezingane zakhe) ngaphandle kokubheka usuku lomshado.”[48] 

Uhulumeni wase-Attlee wawusungulwe uhlelo olubanzi kakhulu lwezinzuzo zenhlalakahle yomphakathi, olwafeza lukhulu ekunciphiseni ukuntula umphakathi. Umthelela onqwabelene wezinqubomgomo zezempilo nezenhlalakahle zikahulumeni ka-Attlee wawuthi zonke izinkomba zempilo (njengezibalo zezokwelapha zesikole noma izikhulu zamazinyo, noma izikhulu zezempilo zezempilo) zibonise izimpawu zentuthuko, ngokuthuthukiswa okuqhubekayo kwamazinga okusinda kwezinsana kanye nokwenyuka kweminyaka yokuphila kwasebekhulile.[42] Impumelelo yomthetho wenhlalakahle kaHulumeni ka-Attlee ekunciphiseni ubumpofu kwaba ukuthi, okhethweni lukazwelonke lwango-1950, ngokocwaningo oluthile, "Inkulumo-ze yezabasebenzi ingenza isimangalo esikhulu sokuthi ukuvikeleka komphakathi kwakuqede ukuswela okunzima kakhulu kwawo-1930".[27] 

Ezezindlu nokuhlela
Umthetho wamaDolobha AseNew 1946 (9 & 10 Geo. 6. c. 68) wamisa izinhlangano zentuthuko ukuze zakhe amadolobha amasha, kuyilapho uMthetho Wokuhlela Amadolobha Nezwe 1947 wayala imikhandlu yezifunda ukuthi ilungise izinhlelo zentuthuko futhi inikeze namandla okuthenga ayimpoqo.[49] Uhulumeni wase-Attlee wabuye welula amandla eziphathimandla zendawo ekufuneni izindlu nezingxenye zezindlu, futhi wenza ukuthathwa komhlaba kwaba nzima kakhulu kunakuqala.[50] I-Housing (Scotland) Act 1949 inikeze izibonelelo ze-75% (87.5% e-Highlands and Islands) ezindlekweni zesimanje ezikhokhelwa uMnyango Wezezimali kuziphathimandla zendawo.[51] 

Ngo-1949, iziphathimandla zendawo zanikwa amandla okuhlinzeka abantu abahlushwa impilo ebuthaka ngezindlu zomphakathi ngerenti yomxhaso.[52] 

Ukuze kusizwe ubunikazi bendlu, umkhawulo enanini lemali abantu ababengayiboleka kuziphathimandla zendawo ukuze bathenge noma bakhe umuzi wakhushulwa kusukela ku-£800 kuya ku-£1,500 ngo-1945, futhi kuya ku-£5,000 ngo-1949.[53] Ngaphansi kwe-National Assistance Act 1948 (11 & 12 Geo. 6. c. 29), iziphathimandla zendawo zazinomsebenzi "wokuhlinzeka ngendawo yokuhlala yesikhashana ephuthumayo emindenini engenamakhaya ngaphandle kwephutha layo".[54] 

Uhlelo olukhulu lokwakha izindlu lwenziwa ngenhloso yokuhlinzeka izigidi zabantu ngezindlu ezisezingeni eliphezulu.[27] Isenzo sezezindlu sandise uxhaso lukaMgcinimafa ukuze kwakhiwe izindlu zeziphathimandla zendawo eNgilandi naseWales.[49] Izindlu ezine kweziyisihlanu ezazakhiwe ngaphansi kwabasebenzi kwakuyizindawo zomkhandlu ezakhiwe ngendlela ecace kakhulu kunangaphambi kweMpi Yezwe Yesibili, futhi uxhaso lwanciphisa irenti yomkhandlu. Sezizonke, lezi zinqubomgomo zinikeze izindlu zomkhakha womphakathi ukuthuthuka okukhulu kunakho konke okwake kwaba khona kuze kube yileso sikhathi, kuyilapho abahola kancane bezuza kakhulu kulezi zinguquko. Nakuba uHulumeni wase-Attlee ehlulekile ukuhlangabezana nemigomo yawo, ngokuyinhloko ngenxa yezinkinga zezomnotho, amakhaya amasha angaphezu kwe-1,000,000 akhiwa phakathi kuka-1945 no-1951 (impumelelo enkulu ngaphansi kwezimo) eyaqinisekisa ukuthi izindlu ezihloniphekile, ezithengekayo zazitholakala emindenini eminingi ehola kancane okokuqala ngqa.[27] 

Amalungelo entuthuko enziwa ngaphansi kombuso ngesikhathi uhulumeni ezama ukuthathela umbuso yonke inzuzo yentuthuko. Kwamiswa iziphathimandla eziqinile zokuhlela ukuze zilawule ukusetshenziswa komhlaba, futhi zakhipha iziqondiso zeziqondiso ezazigcizelela ukubaluleka kokuvikela umhlaba wokulima. Kwamiswa uchungechunge oluqinile lwamahhovisi ezifunda ngaphakathi kwenkonzo yokuhlela ukuze lunikeze ukuhola okuqinile kuzinqubomgomo zokuthuthukiswa kwesifunda.[55] I-Comprehensive Development Areas (CDAs), okuyigama elingaphansi koMthetho WokuHlelwa Kwedolobha Nezwe ka-1947, ivumele iziphathimandla zendawo ukuthi zithole indawo ezindaweni eziqokiwe zisebenzisa amandla okuthenga okuyimpoqo ukuze zihlele kabusha futhi zithuthukise izindawo zasemadolobheni ezihlushwa ukulimala kwedolobha noma ukulimala kwempi.[56] 

Abesifazane nezingane
Kwaqalwa izinguquko eziningana ukuze kuthuthukiswe izimo zabesifazane nezingane. Ngo-1946, izibonelelo zomndeni ezijwayelekile zethulwa ukuze zinikeze usizo lwezimali ezindlini zokukhulisa izingane.[57][58] Lezi zinzuzo zazishaywe umthetho ngonyaka owandulele ngokomthetho we-Churchill's Family Allowances Act 1945. I-Conservatives kamuva izogxeka i-Labour ngokuthi "yashesha kakhulu" ukwethula izibonelelo zomndeni.[50] 

Umthetho Wabesifazane Abashadile (Ukuzithiba Lapho Kulindeleke) uMthetho we-1949 waphasiswa ukuze "ulingane, unikeze noma yimiphi imigoqo engasebenzi lapho kulindelwe noma ukuhlukaniswa okuhambisana nokuthokozelwa kwempahla ngowesifazane", kuyilapho uMthetho Wabesifazane Abashadile (Isondlo) we-1949 washaywa ngenhloso yokuthuthukisa ukwanela kanye nobude bemihlomulo yabesifazane abashadile.[59] 

Umthetho weCriminal Law (Amendment) Act 1950 wachibiyela uMthetho Wokuchibiyela uMthetho Wobugebengu 1885 ukuze ulethe abaqwayizi emthethweni futhi ubavikele ekuthunjweni nasekuhlukunyezweni.[60] UMthetho Wezobulungiswa Bobugebengu 1948 wawubekela umkhawulo ekuboshweni kwezingane futhi waletha intuthuko ezinhlelweni zesikhungo sokuvivinywa kanye nesejele, kuyilapho ukuphasiswa kwe-Justice of the Peace Act 1949 kwaholela ekuguqulweni okubanzi kwezinkantolo zikamantshi.[61] Uhulumeni wase-Attlee uphinde waqeda imishado kuHulumeni, ngaleyo ndlela wavumela abesifazane abashadile ukuthi basebenze kuleso sikhungo.[62] 

Ngo-1946, uhulumeni wasungula i-National Institute of Houseworkers njengendlela yokuhlinzeka ngemisebenzi yasekhaya ehlukahlukene yentando yeningi. [63] 

Ngasekupheleni kuka-1946, kwamiswa izindinganiso zokuqeqesha okwakuvunyelwene ngazo, okwalandelwa ukuvulwa kwendlunkulu yokuqeqesha nokuvulwa kwezikhungo zokuqeqesha eziyisishiyagalolunye ezengeziwe eWales, eScotland, kwase kuba kulo lonke elaseGreat Britain. UMthetho Kazwelonke Wenkonzo Yezempilo ka-1946 waveza ukuthi usizo lwasekhaya kufanele luhlinzekwe emakhaya lapho lolo sizo ludingeka khona “ngenxa yokuba khona kwanoma yimuphi umuntu ogulayo, olele endlini, umama okhulelwe, okhubazekile ngokwengqondo, ubudala noma ingane engadluli iminyaka yesikole eyimpoqo”. Ngakho-ke 'usizo lwasekhaya' lwaluhlanganisa ukuhlinzekwa kosizo lwasekhaya lwabahlengikazi nomama abakhulelwe kanye nomama abanezingane ezineminyaka engaphansi kwemihlanu, futhi ngo-1952 abesifazane abangaba ngu-20,000 bahlanganyela kule nkonzo.[64]
 
Amalungelo abasebenzi
Izinyathelo ezehlukene zenziwa ukuthuthukisa izimo emsebenzini. Ilungelo lekhefu lokugula lanwetshwa kakhulu, futhi kwaqaliswa izinhlelo zokuhola abagulayo kubaphathi basekhaya, abasebenzi abangochwepheshe kanye nabasebenzi bezobuchwepheshe ngo-1946 kanye nezigaba ezihlukahlukene zabasebenzi bezandla ngo-1948.[65] Ukunxeshezelwa kwabasebenzi nakho kwaba ngcono kakhulu.[66] Kwethulwa uMthetho Womshuwalense Kazwelonke (Industrial Injuries) Act 1946 owawuhlanganisa izinhlinzeko ezihlukahlukene njengenzuzo yokulimala, inzuzo yokukhubazeka, ukukhushulwa kwempesheni yokukhubazeka ezimeni zokungasebenzi, ubunzima obukhethekile, ukuba khona njalo, nangesikhathi sokwelashwa okugunyaziwe esibhedlela, kanye nokukhushulwa kwenzuzo yokulimala kanye nempesheni yokukhubazeka maqondana nezingane kanye nabantu abadala abondliwa.[67] Ngaphansi Komshwalense Kazwelonke (Industrial Injuries) (Prescribed Diseases) Amendment Regulations of 1948, abahlomuli lapho bethola izimpesheni zokukhubazeka ze-byssinosis babenelungelo ezimweni ezithile zokwenyuswa kwempesheni maqondana nobunzima obukhethekile, kuyilapho inzuzo yokukhubazeka maqondana ne-pneumoconiosis yandiselwa emacaleni amaningi.[68] 

I-Fair Wages Resolution yango-1946 yayidinga noma yimuphi usonkontileka osebenza kuphrojekthi yomphakathi ukuthi okungenani afane nezinga lokuhola nezinye izimo zokuqashwa ezibekwe esivumelwaneni seqoqo esifanele.[69][70][71] Ngo-1946, i-Purchase Tax yasuswa ngokuphelele ezintweni ezifakwa ekhishini nasezitsheni, kuyilapho izinga lehliswa ezintweni ezihlukahlukene zasengadini.[63] Umthetho Wokuqashwa Nokuqeqeshwa 1948 wawuhlanganisa izinhlinzeko ezifana nezinhlinzeko ezinjengokuqeqeshwa kokuqashwa kanye nezinkokhelo zezindleko zokususa nokuhlalisa kabusha abasebenzi[72] 

Umthetho Wezinkonzo Zomlilo 1947 wethula uhlelo olusha lwempesheni lwabacishi bomlilo,[73] kuyilapho uMthetho Wezogesi we-1947 wethula izinzuzo ezingcono zokuthatha umhlalaphansi zabasebenzi kuleyo mboni.[74] Umthetho Wesinxephezelo Sabasebenzi (Isengezo) 1948 futhi wethula izinzuzo kubasebenzi abanezifo ezithile ezihlobene ne-asbestos ezazenzeke ngaphambi kuka-1948.[75] Umthetho Wokuthuthwa Kwemikhumbi ka-1948 kanye Nomthetho Wokuhamba Ngemikhumbi Komthengisi (Ingqungquthela Yokuphepha) we-1949 waphasiswa ukuze kuthuthukiswe izimo zamatilosi. IShops Act 1950 yahlanganisa umthetho wangaphambili owawuhlinzeka ngokuthi kungabikho muntu ongaqashwa esitolo amahora angaphezu kwayisithupha ngaphandle kokuphumula okungenani imizuzu engama-20. Umthetho wawudinga nekhefu lesidlo sasemini okungenani lemizuzu engu-45 kunoma ubani osebenza phakathi kuka-11:30am no-2:30pm, kanye nekhefu letiye lesigamu sehora kunoma ubani osebenza phakathi kuka-4pm no-7pm.[76] Uhulumeni uphinde waqinisa iSinqumo Semiholo Elungile, ngesigatshana esasidinga ukuthi bonke abaqashi bathole izinkontileka zikahulumeni ukuze bahloniphe amalungelo abasebenzi babo okujoyina izinyunyana.[77]

I-Trades Disputes Act 1927 yachithwa, kwathi ngo-1947 kwethulwa i-Dock Labour Scheme ukuze kuqedwe uhlelo oluvamile lokuqasha abasebenzi ezikhumulweni zemikhumbi.[78] Lolu hlelo lunikeze amadokodo abhalisiwe ilungelo elisemthethweni lomsebenzi omncane nezimo ezihloniphekile. Ngokusebenzisa Ibhodi Likazwelonke Labasebenzi Bemikhumbi (lapho izinyunyana zabasebenzi nabaqashi babenokumelwa okulinganayo) izinyunyana zathola ukulawula ekuqasheni nasekuxoshweni. Amadokodo abhalisiwe adilizwa abaqashi ngaphakathi kweSikimu babenelungelo lokuthathwa ngomunye, noma lesinxephezelo esikhulu.[79] Wonke amadokodo ayebhaliswe ngaphansi kwe-Dock Labour Scheme, ebanika ilungelo elingokomthetho lomsebenzi omncane, amaholide kanye nenkokhelo yokugula.[80] 

Amaholo amalungu ombutho wamaphoyisa anyuswe kakhulu.[81] Ukwethulwa koMqulu Wezimayini ngo-1946 kwasungula isonto lokusebenza lezinsuku ezinhlanu kubavukuzi kanye nesakhiwo samaholo osuku esimisiwe, [42] kwathi ngo-1948 kwagunyazwa i-Colliery Workers Supplementary Scheme, ihlinzeka ngezibonelelo ezengeziwe kubasebenzi bamalahle abakhubazekile kanye nalabo ababethembele kubo.[82][83] Izinzuzo ezihlukahlukene zanikezwa ngaphansi kwalolu hlelo, okuhlanganisa inzuzo yokulimala eyengeziwe, impesheni yokukhubazeka maqondana nengozi ye-colliery noma isifo esibuhlungu, izinzuzo zokufa, kanye Nezibonelelo Ezingeziwe.[84] 

Ngo-1948, kwasungulwa uhlelo lwempesheni ukuze kuhlinzekwe izinzuzo zempesheni kubasebenzi be-NHS entsha, kanye nalabo abathembele kubo.[85] Ngaphansi Kwemithetho Yemboni Yamalahle Kazwelonke (yeSuperannuation) ka-1950, kwasungulwa uhlelo lwempesheni yabasebenzi basezimayini.[86] Ukuthuthukiswa kwamaholo abasebenzi basemapulazini kwenziwa ngcono,[45] kanye neBhodi Yemiholo Yezolimo ngo-1948 ayizange nje ivikele amazinga amaholo, kodwa futhi yaqinisekisa ukuthi abasebenzi bahlinzekwa ngendawo yokuhlala.[87]

Imithetho eminingana okuhloswe ngayo ukuvikela impilo nokuphepha kwabantu emsebenzini yethulwa ngesikhathi sika-Attlee. Imithetho yakhishwa ngoFebhruwari 1946 eyayisebenza ezimbonini ezithintekayo "nokukhiqiza amabrikhethi noma amabhulokhi kaphethiloli ahlanganisa amalahle, uthuli lwamalahle, i-coke noma i-slurry ene-pitch njengento ebophayo," futhi ephathelene "nothuli nokungena komoya, izindawo zokuwasha nendawo yokuhlala yezingubo, ukuvikelwa kwesikhumba kanye nokuhlolwa kwesikhumba kanye nokuhlolwa [8] I-General Mines (Ventilation) Imithetho Ejwayelekile yangomhla ziyi-17 kuNhlaba 1947 "yenza izincomo zeKhomishana Yasebukhosini Yezokuphepha Ezimayini Zamalahle mayelana nezihloko ezimbili eziyinhloko: izindlela zokuhlola ngezikhathi ezithile izinga elijwayelekile lokungena komoya kanye nezindlela zokunciphisa ukuvuza komoya. Izinhlinzeko zibekwe phansi ngokuphathelene nokunqunywa kokuqukethwe kwe-firedamp nezindlela ezinqunywa ngazo le mithetho." 30 June 1948, "elawula ukungeniswa, ukukhiqizwa, ukuthengiswa, ukugcinwa kanye nokusetshenziswa kwezinto ezinomsakazo, kuhlanganisa izinhlinzeko ezinikeza uNgqongqoshe amandla okukhipha imithetho yokuvimbela ukulimala empilweni okubangelwa imisebe ye-ionizing kanye nokuqinisekisa ukulahlwa okuphephile kwemikhiqizo yemfucuza ekhipha imisebe."[90] I-Dry Cleaning Special Regulations, 49bit yaqala ngo-1949 ukuthi kusetshenziswe uketshezi lwe-9 ku-November 1949. enephuzu elikhanyayo elingaphansi kuka-32°C. (90°F.) ekubeni isetshenziselwe ukuhlanza okomile ngaphandle kokubona."[91] Imithetho Ekhethekile Yokuqhunyiswa (I-Castings kanye Nezinye Izihloko) 1949, "iyakwenqabela ukuqhunyiswa kwesihlabathi futhi ibhekane nendawo ebiyelwe ukuqhuma, ukuhlanzwa kwe-abrasive esetshenzisiwe, imboni yokukhipha umoya, ukuhlolwa, ukuhlanza, ukuhlanza okomuntu siqu okokusebenza kanye nokugcinwa kwemishini yokuvikela, ukugcinwa kwezinto zokuvikela kanye nokuqashwa komuntu siqu, kanye nokugcinwa kwezinto ezisetshenziswayo kanye nokugcinwa kwemishini esetshenziswayo. abantu, kanye nokubikwa kokukhubazeka kumshini wokuqhumisa isihlabathi akuvunyelwe eSigabeni sesi-5, esifundeka kanje: "Asikho isihlabathi noma enye into equkethe i-silica yamahhala ezokwethulwa njenge-abrasive kunoma iyiphi into eqhunyiswa yizinto eziqhumayo." 1948 "kubandakanya ukukhushulwa nokuthwala imithwalo ngabesifazane nabantu abasha, ukungena komoya, izinga lokushisa kanye nomswakama, inhlalakahle, ukwakhiwa nokusetshenziswa kwemishini nokudayiswa kanye nokuqashwa kwemishini".[90]

I-Magnesium (Ukugaywa Kwezinto Ezidlalwayo kanye Nezinye Izihloko) (Imithetho Ekhethekile) ka-December 1946 yayiqukethe izinyathelo ezikhethekile “eziphathelene nokugcinwa kwezitshalo nezinto zokusebenza; izinyathelo zokuphepha ezingabangela izinhlansi; ukunqanyulwa nokususwa kothuli; ukusebenza okuzenzakalelayo kwemishini; izingubo zokuzivikela; kanye nokuvinjelwa kokubhema, izibani ezivulekile nemililo". Kulabo basebenzi abenza izinqubo zokukhanyisa, i-Factories (Luminising) Special Regulations (1947) yenqabela ukuqashwa kwalabo abaneminyaka engaphansi kwe-18 futhi yayala "ukuhlolwa kokuqala kodokotela okufanele kwenziwe ngaphambi kosuku lwesikhombisa lomsebenzi; ukuhlolwa okulandelayo kufanele kwenziwe kanye ngenyanga".Ngaphansi kwemibandela Yokuqhunyiswa (Izici Ezikhethekile Ezingu-194) Eziqukethe Izimiso Zamahhala Ezingu-194 " i-silica kufanele isetshenziswe kunoma iyiphi inqubo yokuqhuma", kuyilapho i-Foundries (Parting Materials) Special Regulations (1950) yenqabela ukusetshenziswa kwezimpushana ezithile zokuhlukanisa "okubangela ingozi enkulu ye-silicosis".[93] 

I-Building (Ukuphepha, Impilo Nenhlalakahle) Regulations 1948 yayidinga ukuthi izinyathelo kufanele zithathwe ukuze kuncishiswe ukuchayeka othulini olungase lube yingozi noma intuthu,[94] kuyilapho i-Pottery (Health) Special Regulations (1947) ikwenqabela ukusetshenziswa "ngaphandle kokwenziwa kwamathayela acwebezelisiwe" azo zonke "izinqubo ezicwebezelayo ezingaba yingozi noma ezicwebezelayo ezingaphansi noma eziphansi. noma i-quartz akufanele iqashwe." [93] I-Pottery (Impilo Nezenhlalakahle) Imithetho Ekhethekile Ka-1950 yenza inhlinzeko yezempilo nokuphepha kwabasebenzi abaqashwe ezimbonini "lapho kwenziwa khona ukwakhiwa noma ukuhlobisa izitsha zobumba noma abakhiqizi noma izinqubo ezithile ezihlangene".[95] 

Umthetho 
Izinguquko ezihlukahlukene zomthetho nazo zenziwa uhulumeni ka-Attlee. Umthetho weCriminal Justice Act 1948 uhlinzekele izindlela ezintsha zokubhekana nezaphulamthetho, futhi waqeda ukusebenza kanzima, ukugqilazwa yizijeziso, ukuhlukana kwamajele kanye nokubhaxabulwa.[96] Umthetho we-Law Reform (Personal Injuries) Act 1948 wavumela abasebenzi ukuba bamangalele abaqashi babo ezimeni lapho bethole ukulimala ngenxa yobudedengu bomsebenzi wabo.[97] I-Legal Aid and Advice Act 1949 yethula uhlelo losizo lukahulumeni ukusiza labo ababengakwazi ukukhokhela izinsiza zomthetho.[98] I-The Witnesses Allowances Regulations 1948 ihlinzekela ukukhokhwa kwemali yofakazi abaqeqeshiwe, imali yasebusuku, kanye nesabelo sofakazi abangochwepheshe ezimweni ezithile.[99] 

Ukuvumelana kwangemva kwempi 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukuvumelana kwangemva kwempi
Izazi-mlando eziningi ziphikisa ngokuthi izinqubomgomo eziyinhloko zasekhaya (ngaphandle kokwenziwa kwensimbi kuzwelonke) zibonise ukuvumelana okubanzi kwama-bipartisan. Ukuvumelana kwangemva kwempi kuyimodeli yosomlando yesivumelwano sezepolitiki kusukela ngo-1945 kuya ngasekupheleni kwawo-1970. Ngo-1979 uNdunankulu osanda kukhethwa uMargaret Thatcher wakulahla futhi wakuhoxisa.[100] Umqondo uthi kwakukhona ukuvumelana okusabalele okuhlanganisa ukwesekwa kwephakethe lezinqubomgomo ezibumbene ezathuthukiswa ngeminyaka yawo-1930, ezathenjiswa phakathi neMpi Yezwe Yesibili, futhi zamiswa ngaphansi kuka-Attlee. Izinqubomgomo zibhekane nomnotho oxubile, i-Keynesianism, kanye nezwe lenhlalakahle elibanzi.[101] Eminyakeni yamuva nje izazi-mlando ziye zaphikisana ngokufaneleka kwencazelo. 

Imodeli yezazi-mlando yokuvumelana kwangemva kwempi yathuthukiswa ngokugcwele nguPaul Addison.[102] Ingxabano eyisisekelo iwukuthi ngeminyaka yawo-1930, ongqondongqondo beLiberal Party ababeholwa uJohn Maynard Keynes kanye noWilliam Beveridge bakha uchungechunge lwezinhlelo ezakhanga kakhulu njengoba uhulumeni wesikhathi sempi wathembisa iBrithani engcono kakhulu yangemva kwempi futhi babona isidingo sokubandakanya yonke imikhakha yomphakathi. Uhulumeni womfelandawonye phakathi nempi, owawuholwa uChurchill no-Attlee, wasayina uchungechunge lwamaphepha amhlophe ayethembisa iBrithani izwe lenhlalakahle elithuthuke kakhulu. Ngemva kwempi, izithembiso zazihlanganisa uMnyango Wezempilo Kazwelonke, nokwandiswa kwemfundo, izindlu, kanye nenani lezinhlelo zezenhlalakahle. Ayizange ifake ukufakwa kuzwelonke kwensimbi nensimbi, okwavunywa kuphela yi-Labour Party. 

Imodeli ithi kusukela ngo-1945 kuze kufike u-Thatcher ngo-1979, kwaba nokuvumelana okubanzi kwezinhlaka eziningi kazwelonke mayelana nenqubomgomo yezenhlalakahle nezomnotho, ikakhulukazi mayelana nesimo sezenhlalakahle, izinsizakalo zezempilo zikazwelonke, ukuguqulwa kwezemfundo, umnotho oxubile, umthethonqubo kahulumeni, izinqubomgomo ze-macroeconomic zaseKeynesian, kanye nokuqashwa okugcwele. Ngaphandle kombuzo wokufakwa ngaphansi kukahulumeni kwezinye izimboni, le migomo yamukelwa kabanzi yizinhlangano ezintathu ezinkulu, kanye nezimboni, umphakathi wezezimali kanye nenhlangano yabasebenzi. Kuze kube ngawo-1980, izazi-mlando ngokuvamile zazivumelana ngobukhona nokubaluleka kokuvumelana. Ezinye izazi-mlando ezinjengo-Ralph Miliband zazwakalisa ukudumala ngokuthi ukuvumelana kwakuyiphakheji elinesizotha noma ngisho nelokulandela umthetho elivimbe umphakathi ohlalisana ngokugcwele.[103] Isazi-mlando u-Angus Calder sakhononda kabuhlungu ngokuthi izinguquko zangemva kwempi zaziwumvuzo onganele wokuzidela ngesikhathi sempi, kanye nokukhaphela ngendlela engafanele kwethemba labantu lomphakathi onobulungisa kakhudlwana wangemva kwempi.[104] Eminyakeni yamuva nje, kuye kwaba nenkulumompikiswano yezomlando mayelana nokuthi kwake kwaba khona yini ukuvumelana okunjalo.[105] 

Isiphetho
Okhethweni lukazwelonke lwangoFebhuwari 1950 iLabour Party yagcina ngokulambisa iningi layo ngezihlalo ezi-5 kuphela. Lokhu bekungenele ukuphatha nokho, ngenxa yokuhlukana kukaBevanite okudale ukungezwani eqenjini. Olunye ukhetho lukazwelonke lwabizwa ngo-1951 ukuzama ukwandisa iningi labo. Nokho, okhethweni lukazwelonke lwango-October 1951 amaConservative abuyela emandleni ngaphansi kukaWinston Churchill. Umsebenzi wawuzohlala ungekho esikhundleni iminyaka eyishumi nantathu elandelayo, kuze kube ngu-1964, lapho uHarold Wilson eba undunankulu. 


Ukuzinza kwezezimali wukungabikho kweziqephu zesistimu lapho kuvela khona inkinga yezezimali futhi ibonakala njengomnotho onokuntengantenga okuncane. Kuphinde kubandakanye ukukhuthazela kwengcindezi yezinhlelo zezezimali ukuze ukwazi ukubhekana nakho kokubili izikhathi ezinhle nezimbi. Ukuzinza kwezezimali kuyinhloso yohulumeni abaningi namabhange amakhulu. Inhloso akukona ukuvimbela inhlekelele noma ukumisa izinqumo ezimbi zezimali. Ikhona ukuze kubambe umnotho ndawonye futhi kugcinwe uhlelo luhamba kahle ngesikhathi imicimbi enjalo isenzeka. [1] 

Isisekelo sokuzinza kwezezimali ukudalwa kwesistimu ekwazi ukumunca zonke izehlakalo ezinhle nezingezinhle ezenzeka emnothweni nganoma yisiphi isikhathi. Akuhlangene nokuvimbela abantu noma amabhizinisi ukuthi ahluleke, alahlekelwe yimali, noma aphumelele. Isiza nje ekwakhiweni kwezimo zokuqhubeka nokusebenza kahle kwesistimu lapho kubhekene nezenzakalo ezinjalo.[2] 

Umnotho yilowo olokhu ushintsha futhi ukhula, futhi ugcwele amabhizinisi aqalayo, akhula, futhi ahluleka: imisebenzi evamile yomjikelezo webhizinisi. Izimakethe zezimali nezikhungo zezezimali zibhekwa njengezizinzile lapho zikwazi ukuhlinzeka amakhaya, imiphakathi, namabhizinisi ngezinsiza, izinsizakalo, nemikhiqizo eziyidingayo ukuze itshale, ikhule, futhi ibambe iqhaza emnothweni osebenza kahle. Izikhungo zezimali zihlanganisa amabhange, ukonga nemalimboleko, neminye imikhiqizo yezezimali nabahlinzeki bezinsizakalo.[2] Uhlelo lwezezimali oluhlangabezana nezidingo zemikhaya namabhizinisi ajwayelekile ukuboleka imali yokuthenga indlu noma imoto, ukonga umhlalaphansi, noma ukukhokhela ikolishi kubhekwa njengokuzinza kwezezimali. Ngendlela efanayo, amabhizinisi kufanele athathe imali ebolekiwe ukuze andise, akhe izimboni, aqashe abasebenzi abasha, futhi ahole.

Ikhono lokwaba izinsiza ngendlela ephumelelayo, ukuhlola nokuphatha izingozi zezimali, ukugcina amazinga okuqashwa eseduze nenani elingokwemvelo lomnotho, kanye nokuqeda ukunyakaza kwentengo okuhlobene kwezimpahla zangempela noma zezimali okuzothinta ukuzinza kwezimali noma amazinga okuqashwa yizo zonke izici zesistimu ezinzile ngokwezezimali. Ukungalingani kwezezimali okuvela ngokwemvelo noma ngenxa yezehlakalo ezimbi kakhulu nezingalindelekile kuyaqedwa lapho uhlelo lwezezimali lusebangeni lokuzinza. Uma uhlelo luzinzile, luzodonsa ngokuyinhloko ukushaqeka ngezindlela zokuzilungisa, luvimbele izehlakalo ezimbi ekuphazamiseni umnotho wangempela noma ezinye izinhlelo zezezimali. Ngenxa yokuthi iningi lemisebenzi yomhlaba wangempela yenzeka ngohlelo lwezezimali, ukuzinza kwezezimali kuyadingeka ukuze kwandiswe umnotho.[1][3] 

Izinyathelo ezisetshenziswayo 
Izinyathelo zokuzinza zezinga eliqinile 
I-z-score ye-Altman isetshenziswa kakhulu ocwaningweni lokuhlola njengesilinganiso sokuzinza kwezinga lenkampani ngokuhlobana kwayo okuphezulu nethuba lokuzenzakalelayo. Lesi silinganiso siqhathanisa amabhafa (i-capitalization kanye nembuyiselo) nengcuphe (ukuntengantenga kwembuyiselo) futhi senze kahle ekubikezeleni ukuqothuka phakathi neminyaka emibili. Naphezu kokuthuthukiswa kwamanye amamodeli okubikezela ukuzinza kwezezimali imodeli ka-Altman isalokhu isetshenziswa kakhulu.[4][5] 

Enye imodeli esetshenziselwa ukukala ukuzinza kwezinga lesikhungo imodeli ye-Merton (ebizwa nangokuthi imodeli yenani lempahla). Ihlola ikhono lefemu lokuhlangabezana nezibopho zayo zezezimali futhi ikala ukuthi kungenzeka yini ukuthi ihluleke. Kule modeli, ukulingana kwesikhungo kuthathwa njengenketho yocingo ezimpahleni zaso eziphethwe, kucatshangelwa ukuntengantenga kwalezo zimpahla. I-Put-call parity isetshenziselwa ukubiza inani lenketho ethi “beka” eshiwo, emele ingcuphe yekhredithi yenkampani. Ekugcineni, imodeli ikala inani lezimpahla zefemu (ezilinganiselwe ngenxa yokuguquguquka) ngesikhathi lapho abanikazi bezikweletu basebenzisa “inketho yabo yokubeka” ngokulindela ukubuyiselwa imali. Ngokusobala, imodeli ichaza okumisiwe njengalapho inani lezikweletu zenkampani lidlula lelo lezimpahla zayo libala amathuba okuzenzakalelayo kwekhredithi. Ekuphindaphindweni okuhlukile kwemodeli, ileveli yempahla/yesikweletu ingasethwa kumaleveli omkhawulo ahlukene. 

Ocwaningweni olwalandela, imodeli ka-Merton ishintshiwe ukuze ithwebule uhlu olubanzi lwemisebenzi yezezimali kusetshenziswa idatha yokushintshashintsha okuzenzakalelayo kwekhredithi. Isibonelo, i-Moody's iyisebenzisa kumodeli ye-KMV kokubili ukubala amathuba okuphutha kwekhredithi nanjengengxenye yohlelo lwabo lokulawula ubungozi besikweletu. I-Distance to Default (DD) ingesinye isilinganiso esisekelwe emakethe sengozi ezenzakalelayo yebhizinisi esekelwe kumodeli kaMerton. Ikala kokubili ubungozi be-solvency kanye nobungozi be-liquidity ezingeni eliqinile. 

Izinyathelo ezihlelekile zokuzinza 
Ngeshwa, ayikabi khona imodeli eyodwa, esezingeni yokuhlola ukuzinza kwesistimu yezezimali kanye nokuhlola izinqubomgomo.

Ukuze kulinganiswe ukuzinza kwesistimu, izifundo eziningi zizama ukuhlanganisa izinyathelo zokuzinza zezinga lenkampani (i-z-score nebanga ukuya kokumisiwe) zibe ukuhlola okubanzi kwesistimu kokuzinza, ngokuthatha isilinganiso esilula noma ukukala isilinganiso ngasinye ngosayizi ohlobene wesikhungo. Kodwa-ke, lezi zinyathelo ezihlanganisiwe ziyehluleka ukulandisa ngezingozi ezihlobene phakathi kwezikhungo zezezimali. Ngamanye amazwi, imodeli iyehluleka ukubheka ukuxhumana phakathi kwezikhungo, nokuthi ukwehluleka kwesikhungo esisodwa kungaholela ekuthelelekeni. 

Amathuba Okuqala Okumisiwe, noma amathuba okubona ukwehluleka okukodwa phakathi kwenani lezikhungo, kuhlongoziwe njengesilinganiso sobungozi obuhleliwe eqenjini lezikhungo ezinkulu zezezimali. Lesi silinganiso sibheka amathuba azenzakalelayo angathathi hlangothi ekusakazekeni kokushintshashintsha kwekhredithi. Ngokungafani nezinyathelo zebanga ukuya kokumisiwe, amathuba abona ukuxhumana phakathi kokuzenzakalelayo kwezikhungo ezahlukahlukene. Kodwa-ke, izifundo ezigxile emathubeni okuzenzakalelayo zivame ukunganaki umthelela we-ripper obangelwa ukwehluleka kwesikhungo esikhulu. 

Okunye ukuhlola kokuzinza kwesistimu yezezimali yi-Systemic Expected Shortfall (SES), ekala umnikelo wesistimu yengozi yesikhungo ngasinye. I-SES icubungula izinga lesilinganiso somuntu ngamunye futhi ikala izinto zangaphandle ezidalwe emkhakheni wamabhange lapho lezi zikhungo zingaphumeleli. Imodeli ifaneleka kakhulu ukuhlonza ukuthi yiziphi izikhungo ezihambisana nohlelo futhi ezingaba nomthelela omkhulu emnothweni uma wehluleka. Esinye isici esibi sendlela ye-SES ukuthi kunzima ukunquma ukuthi izikhungo ezibalulekile ngokwesistimu zingase zehlule nini.[6] 

Ukuze kuthuthukiswe amandla okuqagela, isilinganiso se-SES se-retrospective sanwetshwa futhi salungiswa ocwaningweni lwakamuva. Imodeli ethuthukisiwe ibizwa nge-SRISK, ehlola ukushoda kwemali okulindelekile kwenkampani esesimweni esibucayi. Ukuze ubale le SRISK, umuntu kufanele aqale anqume Ukushoda Okulindelwe Kwesikhathi Eside (LRMES), esikala ubudlelwano phakathi kwembuyiselo yezabelo zenkampani kanye nembuyiselo yemakethe (okulinganiselwe kusetshenziswa ukuguquguquka kwe-asymmetric, ukuhlobana, ne-copula). Bese, imodeli ilinganisela ukwehla kwevelu yokulingana yenkampani uma imakethe ehlanganisiwe iba nokwehla okungama-40% noma ngaphezulu esikhathini esiyizinyanga eziyisithupha ukuze kunqunywe ukuthi ingakanani imali edingekayo ukuze kuzuzwe inzuzo engu-8% yesilinganiso senani lempahla. Ngamanye amazwi, i-SRISK inikeza imininingwane ngephesenti lefemu lokushoda kwengqikithi yemali yomkhakha wezezimali. I-SRSK % ephezulu ibonisa abahluleki abakhulu kakhulu lapho kuvela inhlekelele. Omunye umthelela wenkomba ye-SES ukuthi inkampani ibhekwa “njengeyingozi ngokwesistimu” uma ibhekene namathuba aphezulu okushoda kwezimali lapho umkhakha wezezimali ubuthakathaka.[7]

Esinye isilinganiso sokuzinza kwezezimali ukusatshalaliswa kokulahlekelwa okuhlelekile, okuzama ukugcwalisa ezinye izikhala zezinyathelo ezishiwo ngenhla. Lesi silinganiso sihlanganisa izici ezintathu ezibalulekile: amathuba okuba isikhungo ngasinye singaphutha, usayizi wokulahlekelwa onikezwe ukwehluleka, kanye nokusuleleka okubangelwa izikhungo ezixhumene ngokuzenzakalelayo.[8] 


Ukulawulwa kwezezimali kuyisethi ebanzi yezinqubomgomo ezisebenza emkhakheni wezezimali ezindaweni eziningi, ezivunyelwa izici ezimbili eziyinhloko zezimali: ubungozi besistimu, okusho ukuthi ukwehluleka kwamafemu ezezimali kuhilela ukucatshangelwa kwentshisekelo yomphakathi; kanye ne-asymmetry yolwazi, ethethelela imingcele yenkululeko yenkontileka ezindaweni ezikhethiwe zezinsizakalo zezezimali, ikakhulukazi lezo ezihilela amakhasimende ezitolo kanye/noma izinkinga ze-ejenti eyinhloko. Ingxenye ebalulekile yokulawulwa kwezimali ukugadwa kwamafemu ezezimali aqokiwe nezimakethe yiziphathimandla ezikhethekile njengamakhomishana ezibambiso nabaphathi bamabhange. 

Kwezinye izindawo, izici ezithile zokuqondisa kwezezimali zithunyelwe ezinhlanganweni ezizilawulayo. Ukulawulwa kwezezimali kwakha isigaba esisodwa kwezintathu ezingokomthetho ezihlanganisa okuqukethwe komthetho wezezimali, ezinye ezimbili kuyimikhuba yemakethe kanye nomthetho wamacala.[1] 

Umlando 
[isithonjana]	 
Lesi sigaba sidinga ukunwetshwa. Ungasiza ngokungeza kukho. (November 2023) 
Ekuqaleni kwenkathi yesimanje, amaDashi ayengamavulandlela ekuqondisweni kwezimali.[2] Ukuvinjelwa kokuqala okurekhodiwe (umthethonqubo) wokuthengisa okufushane kwenziwa iziphathimandla zase-Dutch ekuqaleni kuka-1610. 

Izinjongo zokulawula 
Izinjongo zabalawuli bezezimali ngokuvamile yilezi:[3] 

ukuzethemba kwemakethe - ukugcina ukuzethemba ohlelweni lwezezimali 
ukuzinza kwezezimali - okunikela ekuvikelweni nasekuthuthukiseni ukuzinza kohlelo lwezezimali 
ukuvikelwa kwabathengi - ukuthola izinga elifanele lokuvikelwa kwabathengi. 
ukunciphisa ubugebengu bezezimali 
lawula ukubamba iqhaza kwamanye amazwe 
Isakhiwo sokuqondisa 
Imithetho inika amandla izinhlangano, uhulumeni noma okungezona ezikahulumeni, ukuqapha imisebenzi kanye nokuphoqelela izenzo.[4] Kukhona ukusethwa okuhlukahlukene nezinhlanganisela ezikhona zesakhiwo sokulawula ezezimali emhlabeni wonke.[5][6] 

Umthetho wemakethe yezibambiso 
I-athikili eyinhloko: Ikhomishana yezibambiso 
Izenzo zokushintshanisa ziqinisekisa ukuthi ukuhweba endaweni yokuhwebelana kwenziwa ngendlela efanele. Okugqama kakhulu inqubo yokubeka amanani, ukwenziwa kanye nokuxazululwa kohwebo, ukugadwa kohwebo okuqondile nokuphumelelayo.[7][8]

Abalawuli bezezimali baqinisekisa ukuthi izinkampani ezisohlwini nabahlanganyeli bemakethe bathobela imithetho ehlukahlukene ngaphansi kwemithetho yokuhweba. Izenzo zokuhweba zidinga ukuthi izinkampani ezisohlwini zishicilele imibiko evamile yezezimali, izaziso zesikhashana noma ukusebenzelana kwabaqondisi. Nakuba abahlanganyeli bemakethe kudingeka ukuthi bashicilele izaziso ezinkulu zabanikazi bamasheya. Inhloso yokuqapha ukuthobela kwezinkampani ezisohlwini nezidingo zazo zokudalula iwukuqinisekisa ukuthi abatshalizimali bayakwazi ukufinyelela olwazini olubalulekile nolwenele ukuze kwenziwe uhlolo olunolwazi lwezinkampani ezisohlwini nezibambiso zazo.[9][10][11][12] 

Ukugadwa kokuphathwa kwempahla noma izenzo zokutshalwa kwezimali kuqinisekisa ukusebenza okungenantambo kwalezo zimoto.[13] 

Ukugadwa kwamabhange nabahlinzeki bezinsizakalo zezezimali 
Isihloko esikhulu: Imithetho yebhange 
Imithetho yasebhange ibeka imithetho yamabhange okufanele ayibheke lapho esungulwa nalapho eqhuba ibhizinisi lawo. Le mithetho yakhelwe ukuvimbela intuthuko engamukelekile engaphazamisa ukusebenza kahle kohlelo lwamabhange. Ngaleyo ndlela kuqinisekisa uhlelo lwamabhange oluqinile nolusebenzayo.[14][15] 




Le ndatshana imayelana nesikhungo somlando kanye nesifunda samabhizinisi esimaphakathi saseLondon. Ukuze uthole idolobha elikhulu elibanzi, elakha inhloko-dolobha yaseNgilandi nase-UK, bheka iLondon. Ukuze uthole okunye ukusetshenziswa, bheka iDolobha laseLondon (disambiguation).
