Idolobha laseLondon (elivame ukubizwa ngokuthi iDolobha noma i-Square Mile), yidolobha, isifunda esinemikhosi kanye nesifunda sikahulumeni wasekhaya eNgilandi. Isungulwe amaRoma cishe ngo-47 AD njengeLondinium, yakha isikhungo esingokomlando sedolobha elikhulu laseLondon. Lizungezwe isifunda semikhosi yesimanje saseGreater London, lapho lihlala lihlukene khona, iDolobha liyindawo ehlukile yabaphathi bendawo ephethwe yiDolobha laseLondon Corporation, eliholwa yiNkosi Mayor yaseLondon; nakuba iyingxenye yesifunda esiphethwe yi-Greater London Authority. 

Eqanjwe ngokuthi i-Square Mile, iDolobha laseLondon linendawo engu-1.12 sq mi (716.80 acres; 2.90 km2), okulenza libe idolobha elincane kunawo wonke e-United Kingdom. Yayinabantu abangu-8,583 ekubalweni kwabantu kwango-2021, [1] [2] nokho bangaphezu kuka-500,000 abantu abaqashwe kule ndawo kusukela ngo-2019.[3] [4] 

Ngokubambisana neCanary Wharf kanye neWest End, iDolobha laseLondon lakha isifunda samabhizinisi esimaphakathi saseLondon, okungesinye sezikhungo zezezimali ezihamba phambili emhlabeni. IBhange LaseNgilandi kanye neLondon Stock Exchange zombili zizinze eDolobheni. Imboni yomshwalense iphinde ibe khona kakhulu endaweni, kanti ukuba khona kweNdlu Yezinkantolo Emngceleni osentshonalanga yeDolobha kuyenze yaba isikhungo somkhakha wezomthetho. 

Idolobha lamanje laseLondon lakha iningi leLondon ukusuka lapho lihlala khona amaRoma ngekhulu lokuqala AD kuya eNkathini Ephakathi. Iqukethe iziza ezimbalwa ezinomlando, okuhlanganisa iSt Paul's Cathedral, iRoyal Exchange, Mansion House, Guildhall, Old Bailey, Smithfield Market, Monument to the Great Fire of London, kanye nezinsalela zoDonga lwaseLondon lasendulo. 

Umlando Isihloko esiyinhloko: Umlando 
Wemvelaphi 
YaseLondon 
Isihloko esikhulu: Londinium 
Isigqoko Sokuzivikela SaseWaterloo, c. 150–50 BC, etholakala eMfuleni iThames

 
Isiqephu esasinda soDonga lwaseLondon, olwakhiwa cishe ngo-AD 200, eduze neTower Hill.
Amabutho aseRoma asungula indawo eyaziwa ngokuthi "i-Londinium" endaweni yamanje yeDolobha laseLondon cishe ngo-AD 43. Ibhuloho layo phezu koMfula iThames laguqula leli dolobha laba indawo yomgwaqo kanye nechweba elikhulu, elisebenza njengesikhungo esikhulu sezohwebo eBrithani yaseRoma kwaze kwaba yilapho ilahlwa phakathi nekhulu lesi-5. Isazi semivubukulo u-Leslie Wallace siphawula ukuthi, ngenxa yokuthi ukuvubukula okubanzi akukavezi noma yiziphi izimpawu zokuba khona okubalulekile kwangaphambi kweRoma, “izimpikiswano zesisekelo samaRoma kuphela saseLondon sezivamile futhi azinampikiswano.”[5] 

Ekuphakameni kwalo, idolobha laseRoma lalinabantu abangaba ngu-45,000–60,000. I-Londinium kwakuyidolobha elihlukene ngokwezizwe, elinabantu abavela kuwo wonke uMbuso WaseRoma, kuhlanganise nabomdabu baseBritannia, ezwekazini laseYurophu, eMpumalanga Ephakathi, naseNyakatho Afrika.[6] AmaRoma akha uDonga lwaseLondon esikhathini esithile phakathi kuka-AD 190 no-225. Imingcele yedolobha laseRoma yayifana naleyo yeDolobha laseLondon namuhla, nakuba iDolobha lidlulela entshonalanga kuneLudgate yaseLondinium, futhi umfula iThames wawungancishisiwe futhi waba banzi kunalokho oyikho namuhla, nogu lwaseLondinium olusenyakatho kancane nogu lwedolobha olukhona. AmaRoma akha ibhuloho ngaphesheya komfula, kusukela ngo-AD 50, eduze nebhuloho lanamuhla laseLondon. 

Ukuncipha 
Ngesikhathi kwakhiwa uDonga LwaseLondon, ingcebo yaleli dolobha yancipha, futhi lalibhekene nezinkinga zesifo esiwumshayabhuqe nomlilo. UMbuso WaseRoma wangena esikhathini eside sokungazinzi nokuncipha, kuhlanganise nokuvukela kweCarausian eBrithani. Ngekhulu lesi-3 nelesi-4, idolobha lalihlaselwa abahlaseli basePicts, Scots, nabaseSaxon. Ukwehla kwaqhubeka, kokubili eLondinium kanye noMbuso, futhi ngo-AD 410 amaRoma ahoxa ngokuphelele eBrithani. Izakhiwo eziningi zomphakathi zaseRoma eLondinium ngalesi sikhathi zase ziwohlokile futhi zingasasetshenziswa, futhi kancane kancane ngemva kokuhoxa ngokusemthethweni idolobha lacishe lacishe lahlala (uma kungenjalo, ngezinye izikhathi, ngokuphelele) lingasahlali muntu. Isikhungo sezohwebo kanye nenani labantu sasuka e-Londinium ebiyelwe ngodonga saya eLundenwic ("imakethe yaseLondon"), indawo yokuhlala esentshonalanga, cishe endaweni yanamuhla yaseStrand/Aldwych/Covent Garden.[catation needed] 

Ukubuyiselwa kwe-Anglo-Saxon 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Anglo-Saxon London 
Ngesikhathi se-Anglo-Saxon indawo yase-Anglo-Saxon kwafika ngaphansi kwe-London Heptarchy, i-London Heptarchy, kamuva ne-Essence Heptarchy, i-London Heptarchy. I-Wessex, nakuba kusukela maphakathi nekhulu lesi-8 yayivame ukusongelwa ukuhlaselwa ngamaqembu ahlukene okuhlanganisa namaViking.

 
I-Plaque eduze kwaseSouthwark Bridge ephawula imisebenzi ngesikhathi seNkosi u-Alfred
U-Bede ubhala ukuthi ngo-AD 604 uSt Augustine wangcwelisa uMellitus njengombhishobhi wokuqala embusweni wama-Anglo-Saxon wase-East Saxons kanye nenkosi yawo, uSæberht. Umalume kaSæberht kanye nenkosi, u-Æthelberht, inkosi yaseKent, wakha isonto elinikezelwe eSt Paul eLondon, njengendawo yokuhlala yombhishobhi omusha.[7] Kucatshangelwa, nakuba kungenabufakazi, ukuthi leli sonto lokuqala le-Anglo-Saxon limi endaweni efanayo naleyo yakamuva kanye namasonto akhona manje 

. yathatha izingxenye zeNgilandi. Indawo yokuhlala eqinile yama-Anglo-Saxon yaziwa ngokuthi ("London Fort", isifunda). Isazi-mlando u-Asser sathi “u-Alfred, inkosi yama-Anglo-Saxon, wabuyisela idolobha laseLondon ngokukhazimulayo ... futhi walenza ukuba kuhlale kulo futhi.”[8] “Ukubuyisela” kuka-Alfred kwakuhlanganisa ukuhlala kabusha nokuvuselela idolobha laseRoma elibiyelwe elicishe lasala dengwane, ukwakha izikhumulo zemikhumbi ngasemfuleni iThames, kanye nokubeka ipulani yomgwaqo entsha yedolobha.[9] 

Ukuthatha kuka-Alfred iLondon kanye nokwakhiwa kabusha kwedolobha laseRoma elidala kwaba inguquko emlandweni, hhayi nje kuphela njengokusungulwa unomphela kweDolobha laseLondon, kodwa futhi njengengxenye yomzuzu wokuhlanganisa ekuqaleni kweNgilandi, lapho i-Wessex yaba umbuso wamaNgisi ophethe kanye nokuxosha (ngezinga elithile) kokuhlala nokuhlasela kwamaViking. Ngenkathi iLondon, kanye neNgilandi ngempela, kamuva yabhekana nezinye izikhathi zokuhlasela kwamaViking namaDanish, kwanqoba ukusungulwa kweDolobha laseLondon kanye noMbuso WaseNgilandi.[10] 

Ngekhulu le-10, i-Athelstan yavumela ukuba kusungulwe iminti engu-8, uma kuqhathaniswa neziyisithupha enhloko-dolobha yayo, iWinchester, okubonisa ingcebo yedolobha. Ibhuloho laseLondon, elase liwele enxiweni kulandela ukuphuma kwamaRoma kanye nokushiywa kweLondinium, lakhiwa kabusha amaSaxon, kodwa lacekelwa phansi ngezikhathi ezithile ukuhlasela kwamaViking neziphepho. 

Njengoba ukugxila kwezohwebo kanye nenani labantu kwabuyiselwa emuva ngaphakathi kwezindonga zakudala zaseRoma, indawo endala yaseSaxon yaseLundenwic yashiywa kakhulu futhi yathola igama lika-Ealdwic ("indawo endala"). Igama lisekhona nanamuhla njenge-Aldwych ("indawo yemakethe endala"), igama lomgwaqo nendawo yeDolobha laseWestminster phakathi kweWestminster neDolobha laseLondon. 

I-Medieval era 

Map of London in about 1300 

Umcimbi obalulekile ngesikhathi sokuvukela kwabalimi, 1381: umholi wabo u-Wat Tyler ugwazwe nguWilliam Walworth, iNkosi Mayor. 
Bheka futhi: I-Norman ne-Medieval London 
Ngemva kweMpi yaseHastings, uWilliam uMnqobi wamasha eLondon, waze wafika eSouthwark, kodwa wehluleka ukuwela iLondon Bridge noma ukunqoba abaseLondon. Ekugcineni wawela uMfula iThames eWallingford, waphanga izwe njengoba ehamba. Esikhundleni sokuqhubeka nempi, u-Edgar the Ætheling, u-Edwin waseMercia noMorcar waseNorthumbria bazinikela eBerkhamsted. UWilliam wanika izakhamuzi zaseLondon umqulu ngo-1075; idolobha lalingesinye sezibonelo ezimbalwa zokuthi amaNgisi agcine igunya elithile. Idolobha alizange lihlanganiswe ne-Domesday Book. 

UWilliam wakha izinqaba ezintathu ezizungeze idolobha, ukuze agcine abantu baseLondon benqotshiwe: 

i-Tower of London, okuseyisikhungo esikhulu. 
I-Baynard's Castle, engasekho kodwa eqanjwe isigceme sedolobha. 
Montfichet's Tower or Castle on Ludgate Hill, eyadilizwa futhi yathengiswa ngekhulu le-13.
Cishe ngo-1132 iDolobha lanikezwa ilungelo lokuqoka osherifu balo kunokuba kube nosherifu abaqokwa yinkosi. Osherifu abakhethiwe baseLondon baphinde basebenza njengosherifu besifunda saseMiddlesex. Lokhu kwakusho ukuthi iDolobha kanye ne-Middlesex bathathwa njengenye kwezokuphatha ukubhekana nobugebengu kanye nokugcina ukuthula (hhayi ukuthi isifunda sasingaphansi kwedolobha). Osherifu baseLondon baqhubekile nokusebenzela iMiddlesex kwaze kwaba yilapho isifunda sinikezwa osherifu baso futhi kulandela uMthetho Wohulumeni Wasekhaya we-1888.[11][12] Ngo-1141 yonke indikimba yesakhamuzi yayibhekwa njengomphakathi owodwa. Lo 'mhlangano' wawungumsuka we-City of London Corporation futhi izakhamuzi zathola ilungelo lokuqoka, ngemvume yenkosi, imeya ngo-1189-kanye nokukhetha ngokuqondile umeya kusukela ngo-1215. 

Kusukela ezikhathini zasendulo, leli dolobha liye lakhiwa amawadi asendulo angu-25, ngalinye liphethwe i-alderman, ehlala njalo ngonyaka e-Wardmotes. I-Folkmoot, yeDolobha lonke ebibanjelwe esiphambanweni esingaphandle se-St Paul's Cathedral, nayo ibike yabanjelwa. Amahhovisi amaningi enkathi ephakathi namasiko ayaqhubeka kuze kube namuhla, ebonisa isimo esiyingqayizivele seDolobha kanye neNhlangano yalo. 

Ngo-1381, ukuvukela kwabalimi kwathinta iLondon. Amavukela-mbuso athatha iDolobha noMbhoshongo waseLondon, kodwa ukuhlubuka kwaphela ngemva kokubulawa komholi wawo, u-Wat Tyler, phakathi nengxabano eyayihlanganisa iNkosi iMeya uWilliam Walworth. Ngo-1450, amabutho amavukelambuso aphinde athatha iDolobha ngesikhathi sokuvukela kukaJack Cade ngaphambi kokuxoshwa yizakhamuzi zaseLondon kulandela impi eyachitha igazi eLondon Bridge. Ngo-1550, indawo eseningizimu yeLondon Bridge eSouthwark yaba ngaphansi kokulawulwa yiDolobha ngokusungulwa kwesigceme saseBridge Without. 


Imephu ye-"Woodcut" yaseLondon, esukela ngeminyaka yawo-1560s 

Imephu ekhombisa izinga loMlilo Omkhulu waseLondon, owacekela phansi cishe amaphesenti angama-80 eDolobha 

Umlilo Omkhulu Wango-1666 njengoba ukhonjiswe emdwebeni wekhulu le-17: ubonisa i-Old London Bridge kwesokunxele, amasonto, izindlu, kanye noMbhoshongo waseLondon kwesokudla, njengoba kubonakala esikebheni eduze kwase-W Towerharf. 
Idolobha lashiswa kanzima izikhathi eziningana, okubi kakhulu kwaba ngo-1123 kanye noMlilo Omkhulu WaseLondon ngo-1666. Yomibili le mililo yabizwa ngokuthi uMlilo Omkhulu. Ngemuva komlilo wango-1666, kwadwetshwa inqwaba yezinhlelo zokulungisa kabusha idolobha kanye nephethini yalo yomgwaqo libe idolobha lesitayela sokuvuselela elinamabhulokhi asemadolobheni ahleliwe, izikwele kanye nama-boulevards. Lezi zinhlelo cishe azizange zenziwe ngokuphelele, futhi iphethini yomgwaqo yenkathi ephakathi yaphinde yavela cishe ngokuphelele. 

Isikhathi sokuqala sanamuhla 
Ngeminyaka yawo-1630s iCrown yafuna ukuthi i-Corporation of the City of London inwebe amandla ayo ezindaweni ezizungezile. Kulokho ngezinye izikhathi okubizwa ngokuthi "ukwenqaba okukhulu", iNhlangano yathi cha eNkosini, okuyingxenye yesakhiwo sayo sikahulumeni esiyingqayizivele kuze kube manje.[13]

Ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-16, iLondon yaya ngokuya iba isikhungo esikhulu samabhange, uhwebo lwamazwe ngamazwe kanye nezohwebo. I-Royal Exchange yasungulwa ngo-1565 nguSir Thomas Gresham njengesikhungo sezohwebo kubathengisi baseLondon, futhi yazuza ukusekelwa kweRoyal ngo-1571. Nakuba ingasasetshenziselwa injongo yayo yasekuqaleni, indawo yayo esekhoneni lika-Cornhill kanye ne-Threadneedle Street iyaqhubeka nokuba isikhungo sendawo yomgogodla wedolobha webhange elikhona kanye nesayithi lase-England elibhekene ne-73 ye-Exchange yasebhange kanye nesayithi lezezimali elibhekene ne-73 yezezimali. Ngokushesha eningizimu yeCornhill, uLombard Street kwakuyindawo kusukela ngo-1691 ye-Lloyd's Coffee House, eyaba yimakethe yomshwalense ehamba phambili emhlabeni. Umkhakha womshwalense waseLondon uyaqhubeka nokuba khona endaweni, ikakhulukazi kuLime Street. 

Ngo-1708, umsebenzi wobuciko kaChristopher Wren, iSt Paul's Cathedral, waqedwa ngosuku lwakhe lokuzalwa. Inkonzo yokuqala yayibanjwe zi-2 kuZibandlela 1697, eminyakeni engaphezu kweyi-10 ngaphambili. Yathatha indawo yeSt Paul's yasekuqaleni, eyayicekelwe phansi ngokuphelele eMlilo Omkhulu waseLondon, futhi ibhekwa njengelinye lamahholo ombhishobhi amahle kakhulu eBrithani futhi iyisibonelo esihle sezakhiwo zeBaroque. 

Ukukhula kweLondon 
Ikhulu le-18 kwakuyinkathi yokukhula okusheshayo kweLondon, ebonisa ukwanda kwenani labantu bezwe, izisusa zakuqala zeNguquko Yezimboni, kanye nendima yaseLondon enkabeni yoMbuso WaseBrithani owawuthuthuka. Indawo yasemadolobheni yanwetshwa yadlula imingcele yeDolobha laseLondon, ikakhulukazi ngalesi sikhathi ibheke eWest End naseWestminster. 

Ukwanda kwaqhubeka futhi kwashesha kakhulu ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19, iLondon ikhula kuzo zonke izinhlangothi. EMpumalanga ichweba laseLondon lakhula ngokushesha phakathi nekhulu leminyaka, ngokwakhiwa kwezikhumulo zemikhumbi eziningi, ezidingekayo njengoba umfula iThames eDolobheni wawungakwazi ukumelana nomthamo wokuhweba. Ukufika kwezitimela kanye neTube kwakusho ukuthi iLondon inganwebeka endaweni enkulu kakhulu. Maphakathi nekhulu le-19, njengoba iLondon isakhula ngokushesha ngesibalo sabantu nendawo, iDolobha lase liyingxenye encane yedolobha elikhulu.
 
Ikhulu le-19 nelama-20
Umzamo wenziwa ngo-1894 neRoyal Commission on the Amalgamation of the City and County of London ukuze kuqedwe umehluko phakathi kwedolobha nesifunda esiseduze saseLondon, kodwa ukuguqulwa kukahulumeni eWestminster kwasho ukuthi inketho ayizange ithathwe. Idolobha njengepolitiki ehlukile lasinda naphezu kwesikhundla salo endaweni yaseLondon kanye nezinguquko eziningi kuhulumeni wasekhaya. Isekela lesi simo, idolobha laliyisifunda sephalamende esikhethekile esakhetha amalungu amane eNdlu Yezikhulu ezingaguquki, agcinwa ngemva kweReform Act 1832; zehliswe zaba ezimbili ngaphansi koMthetho Wokwabiwa Kabusha Kwezihlalo 1885; futhi yayeka ukuba yisifunda esihlukile ngaphansi koMthetho Wokumela Abantu 1948. Kusukela lapho idolobha liyidlanzana (ngokwesibalo sabantu nendawo) lamaDolobha aseLondon naseWestminster. 


I-St Paul's Cathedral (esesithombeni sango-1896) ibibusa isibhakabhaka seDolobha amakhulu eminyaka - isakhiwo salo samanje sikaChristopher Wren saqedwa ngo-1706, ngemva kokuba owandulelayo wenkathi ephakathi eshise ingxenye enkulu yeDolobha eMlilo Omkhulu wango-1666. 
Inani labantu baleli dolobha lehla ngokushesha ngekhulu le-19 njengoba abantu besuka eLondon besuka cishe kuwo wonke ama-20 ekhulwini. udedangendlale wamadolobha, nezakhiwo eziningi zokuhlala zadilizwa ukuze kwakhiwe amahhovisi. Njengezindawo eziningi zaseLondon nakwamanye amadolobha aseBrithani, iDolobha laba yizisulu zokuqhunyiswa kwamabhomu emoyeni okulimaza kakhulu phakathi neMpi Yezwe II, ikakhulukazi eBlitz. Ngenkathi iSt Paul's Cathedral yasinda kulokhu kuhlasela, izindawo ezinkulu zendawo azizange futhi ukuhlasela okunamandla kwasekupheleni kukaDisemba 1940 kwaholela esivunguvungwini esibizwa ngokuthi i-Second Great Fire yaseLondon. 

Kwakukhona uhlelo olukhulu lokwakha kabusha emashumini eminyaka alandela impi, kwezinye izingxenye (njengaseBarbican) kwashintsha ngokuphawulekayo isimo sasemadolobheni. Kodwa ukucekelwa phansi kwendwangu endala yomlando kuvumele ukwakhiwa kwentuthuko yesimanje kanye nezinga elikhulu, kanti kulezo zingxenye ezingathintekile kangako ngenxa yokulimala kwamabhomu iDolobha ligcina isimilo salo esidala sezakhiwo ezincane. Iphethini yomgwaqo, okuseyinkathi ephakathi, yashintshwa kancane ezindaweni, nakuba kunomkhuba wakamuva wokubuyisela emuva ezinye zezinguquko zesimanje zangemuva kwempi ezenziwe, njengasePaternoster Square. 

IDolobha labhekana nokuhlasela kwamaphekula okuhlanganisa ukuqhuma kwamabhomu eBishopsgate (IRA) ngo-1993 kanye nokuqhuma kwamabhomu eLondon ngomhlaka-7 Julayi 2005 (Islamist). Ukusabela ekuqhunyisweni kwamabhomu kwango-1993, uhlelo lwezithiyo zomgwaqo, izindawo zokuhlola kanye namakhamera okuqapha okubizwa ngokuthi “indandatho yensimbi” iye yagcinwa ukuze kulawuleke izindawo zokungena edolobheni.

Ngawo-1970 kwakhiwa izakhiwo ezinde zamahhovisi okuhlanganisa i-600-foot (183 m), i-NatWest Tower enezitezi ezingu-47, i-skyscraper yokuqala e-UK. Ngawo-2010, ukuthuthukiswa kwendawo yamahhovisi kwase kushubile eDolobheni, ikakhulukazi maphakathi, enyakatho nasempumalanga, kunezakhiwo eziphakeme ezihlanganisa i-30 St. Mary Ax ("the Gherkin"), Isakhiwo seLeadenhall ("i-Cheesegrater"), i-20 Fenchurch Street ("i-Walkie-Talkie"), i-Broadgate Tower kanye ne-Broadgate Tower. 

Ingxenye enkulu yokuhlala yeDolobha namuhla iBarbican Estate, eyakhiwa phakathi kuka-1965 no-1976. I-Museum yaseLondon yazinze lapho kwaze kwaba ngoMashi 2023 (ngenxa yokuthi izovulwa kabusha eWest Smithfield ngo-2026), [14] kuyilapho inani lezinye izinsiza ezihlinzekwa yinhlangano zisagcinwa eBarbican Estate. 

I-Governance 

Guildhall iyisikhungo semikhosi nokuphatha sedolobha. 

I-Mansion House iyindawo yokuhlala esemthethweni yeNkosi Mayor. 

John Stuttard, Lord Mayor of the City of London 2006–2007, during the Lord Mayor’s Show of 2006 
Bheka futhi: Idolobha LaseLondon Corporation kanye Nomlando Wohulumeni Wasekhaya 
eNgilandi Ngokomlando uhlelo lwayo lukahulumeni lwalungeyona into engavamile, kodwa aluzange luguqulwe uMthetho Wezinkampani Zomasipala 1835 futhi lwashintshwa kancane yizinguquko zakamuva, ukuze kube ukuphela kukahulumeni wendawo e-UK lapho ukhetho lungaqhutshwa ngesisekelo sevoti elilodwa laso sonke isakhamuzi esikhulile. 

Iphethwe yiDolobha laseLondon Corporation, eholwa yiNkosi Mayor yaseLondon (akumele kudidaniswe neMeya yaseLondon ehlukene, ihhovisi elakhiwa ngonyaka wezi-2000 kuphela), elibhekele imisebenzi eminingi futhi elinentshisekelo emhlabeni ongaphezu kwemingcele yedolobha. Ngokungafani nezinye iziphathimandla zendawo zamaNgisi, le nhlangano inezinhlaka ezimbili zomkhandlu: iNkantolo ye-Aldermen (manje eyimikhosi) kanye neNkantolo Yomkhandlu Ovamile. INkantolo Yase-Aldermen imele izigceme, nesigceme ngasinye (kungakhathaliseki ubukhulu) sibuyisela i-alderman eyodwa. Isikhulu esiphezulu seNhlangano sinehhovisi lasendulo likaMabhalane Wedolobha laseLondon. 

Idolobhana liyisifunda semikhosi esineKhomishana Yezobulungiswa eholwa yiNkosi Mayor esikhundleni se-Lord-Lieutenant futhi inamaSheriff amabili esikhundleni se-High Sheriff (bheka uhlu lwaSheriffs baseLondon), amahhovisi ezomthetho aqokwe izinkampani ezithengisa impahla, uhlelo lwezepolitiki lwakudala olusekelwe ekumelelweni nasekuvikelweni kwezentengiselwano (izinhlangano). Amalungu aphezulu ezinkampani ezikhiqiza ama-livery aziwa ngokuthi ama-liverymen futhi akha i-Common Hall, ekhetha u-lord meya, osherifu nezinye izikhulu ezithile. Isihloko 

seWards 
Main: Wards of the City of London
Idolobha lakhiwe amawadi angama-25. Bangabasinde ohlelweni lukahulumeni wenkathi ephakathi olwavumela indawo yendawo ukuba ibe khona njengendawo ezibusayo ngaphakathi kwedolobha elibanzi.[15] Angachazwa njengokwehlukana kwezokhetho/kwezombusazwe; izinhlangano zemikhosi, indawo kanye nezokuphatha; izigatshana zedolobha. Isigceme ngasinye sine-Alderman, okwathi kwaze kwaba phakathi nawo-1960[16] yabamba ihhovisi impilo yakhe yonke kodwa yazinikela ekukhethweni kabusha okungenani njalo ngemva kweminyaka eyi-6, futhi iwukuphela kwama-Aldermen akhethwa ngokuqondile e-United Kingdom. Izigceme zisaqhubeka nokuba ne-Beadle, isikhundla sakudala manje esesiyingxenye yomkhosi umsebenzi wawo oyinhloko osele uwukuqhutshwa kwe-Wardmote yaminyaka yonke yabavoti, abameleli kanye nezikhulu.[17] E-Wardmote u-Alderman wesigceme uqoka okungenani iPhini elilodwa lonyaka ozayo, kanti ama-Wardmotes nawo abanjwa ngesikhathi sokhetho. Isigceme ngasinye futhi sineKlabhu Yewadi, efana nenhlangano yabahlali.[18] 

Izigceme ezakudala futhi isibalo sazo sesishintshe izikhathi ezintathu kusukela kudala: 

ngo-1394 iFarringdon yahlukaniswa yaba yiFarringdon Ngaphakathi neFarringdon Without 
ngo-1550 kwasungulwa isigceme saseBridge Without, eningizimu yomfula, isigceme saseBridge eba yiBridge Ngaphakathi;[19] 
ngo-1978 lezi zigceme zeBhuloho zahlanganiswa njengesigceme seBridge.[20] 

Imephu yezigceme njengoba yayinjalo ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19 

Imephu yezigceme kusukela ngo-2003 
Ngemva kokushintshwa kwemingcele ngo-1994, kanye noshintsho lwakamuva lwevoti lebhizinisi edolobheni, kwaba nomngcele omkhulu nokumeleleka kokhetho lokubukezwa kwezigceme ngo-2003, futhi zabuyekezwa futhi ngo-2010 ukuze kube noshintsho olumangalisayo ngo-2. Ukubuyekezwa kwenziwe izikhulu eziphezulu zenhlangano kanye namajaji aphezulu e-Old Bailey;[21] izigceme zibuyekezwa yile nqubo ukuze kugwenywe ukungahambisani kahle. Inqubo yokubuyekeza ihlukile e-United Kingdom njengoba ingenziwa Ikhomishana Yokhetho noma ikhomishana yemingcele kahulumeni wasekhaya njalo ngemva kweminyaka eyi-8 kuya kweyi-12, okuyinto eyenzeka kuwo wonke amanye amawadi e-Great Britain. Amasonto athile, amahholo ezinkampani ezidayisa ukudla kanye nezinye izakhiwo ezinomlando nezakhiwo zihlotshaniswa nesigceme, njengeSt Paul's Cathedral neCastle Baynard, neLondon Bridge eneBridge; izinguquko zemingcele ngo-2003 zasusa okunye kwalokhu kuxhumana okungokomlando.

Isigceme ngasinye sikhetha i-alderman eNkantolo Yase-Aldermen, kanye nabavamile (iDolobha elilingana nekhansela) eNkantolo YoMkhandlu Ovamile wenhlangano. Abavoti kuphela abangama-Freemen baseDolobheni lase-London abafaneleka ukungenela ukhetho. Isibalo sabantu abavamile isigceme esibathumelayo kuMkhandlu Kazwelonke siyahluka sisuka kwababili siye kweshumi, kuye ngenani labavoti esigcemeni ngasinye. Kusukela ekubuyekezweni kuka-2003 kuvunyelwene ngokuthi ezinye izigceme ezine zokuhlala: Portsoken, Queenhithe, Aldersgate kanye neCripplegate ndawonye zikhethe abantukazana abangama-20 kwabayi-100, kuyilapho insalela egcwele amabhizinisi ikhetha abantukazana abasele abangama-80. Izinguquko zemingcele zika-2003 kanye no-2013 zikhulise ukugcizelelwa kwezindawo zokuhlala ezigcemeni ezine ezibaluliwe. 

Idatha yokubalwa kwabantu ihlinzeka ngezigceme eziyisishiyagalombili kunezigceme zangempela ezingama-25, zonke ezinobukhulu obuhlukahlukene kanye nenani labantu. Njengoba ngaphansi kokuqanjwa kabusha nokuchazwa nganoma isiphi isikhathi, lezi 'zigceme' zokubalwa kwabantu ziphawuleka ngokuthi izigceme ezine kweziyisishiyagalombili zibalelwa ku-67% 'we-square mile' futhi ziphethe u-86% wabantu, futhi lezi empeleni zazifana futhi zaqanjwa ngezigceme ezine zeDolobha lase-London: 

Ingcaphuno 'yezigceme' zokubalwa kwabantu lapho cishe ingaphansi kwezigceme ezingaphansi kwezingu-2

Ukhetho 
Idolobha linohlelo olukhethekile lokhetho. Iningi labavoti bayo bangabamele amabhizinisi nezinye izinhlaka ezihlala ezakhiweni zedolobha. Izigceme zakhona zasendulo zinezibalo ezingalingani kakhulu zabavoti. Okhethweni, womabili amabhizinisi azinze edolobheni kanye nezakhamizi zeDolobha bayavota. 

I-City of London Corporation ayizange iguqulwe uMthetho Wezinkampani Zomasipala 1835, ngoba yayinemvume yokhetho eningi ukwedlula noma yimuphi omunye idolobha noma idolobha; empeleni, yakwandisa lokhu ngokuqhubekayo ngomthetho wayo ofanayo ovumela ukuthi umuntu abe ngumuntu okhululekile ngaphandle kokuba umdlwenguli. Ngo-1801, leli dolobha lalinabantu ababalelwa ku-130,000, kodwa ukwanda kwentuthuko yedolobha njengesifunda samabhizinisi emaphakathi kuholele ekutheni lehle libe ngaphansi kuka-5,000 ngemuva kweMpi Yezwe Yesibili. Ngo-2009, ivoti lebhizinisi lalilinganiselwa ku-24,000, lidlula kakhulu abavoti bezindawo zokuhlala. [23] Njengoba i-City of London Corporation ingazange ithintwe eminye imithetho kamasipala phakathi nesikhathi kusukela lapho, umkhuba wayo wokhetho usuya ngokuya uxaka. Ngokuhlukile okhethweni lwamadolobhakazi noma lwesifunda, ukhetho lwalo luhlala luzimele.

Ibhizinisi noma "ivoti okungelona elokuhlala" laqedwa kolunye ukhetho lomkhandlu wendawo wase-UK yi-Representation of the People Act 1969, kodwa lalondolozwa eDolobheni laseLondon. Isizathu esiyinhloko esinikezwe ohulumeni base-UK abalandelanayo ngokugcina le ndlela yokunikeza amabhizinisi ukumelwa, ukuthi idolobha “ngokuyinhloko liyindawo yokwenza ibhizinisi”.[24] Cishe abantu abangaba ngu-330,000 abangezona izakhamuzi bakha inani labantu besikhathi sasemini futhi basebenzisa iningi lezinsizakalo zabo, izakhamuzi ezidlula kude, ezibalelwa ku-7,000 (2011). Ngokuphambene, abamelene nokugcinwa kwevoti lebhizinisi baphikisa ngokuthi kuyimbangela yokungasebenzi kwesikhungo.[25] 

Umthetho Wedolobha LaseLondon (Ukhetho Lwezigceme) ka-2002 (c. vi), okuyisenzo sePhalamende sendawo, [26] uguqule uhlelo lokuvota futhi wandisa kakhulu i-franchise yebhizinisi, kwavumela amabhizinisi amaningi ukuba amelwe. Ngaphansi kohlelo olusha, isibalo sabavoti okungezona izakhamuzi sesiphindeke kabili sisuka ku-16,000 saya ku-32,000. Amafemu ayekade enqanyulwe amalungelo (kanye nezinye izinhlangano) anelungelo lokuqoka abavoti, ngaphezu kwalabo asebevele bamelwe, futhi zonke izinhlaka ezinjalo manje kudingeka zikhethe abavoti bazo ngendlela ebamele. Izindikimba eziqasha abantu abangaphansi kwe-10 zingaqoka umvoti oyedwa; labo abaqasha abantu abayi-10 kuya kwabangu-50 umvoti oyedwa kubasebenzi aba-5; labo abaqasha abantu abangaphezu kwama-50 abavoti abayi-10 kanye nomvoti oyedwa owengeziwe kubasebenzi abangama-50 ngamunye ngaphezu kwalabo bokuqala abangama-50. Umthetho uphinde washintsha ezinye izici zesenzo sangaphambili esiphathelene nokhetho edolobheni, kusukela ngo-1957. Isihloko 

seThempeli 
Eliyinhloko: Ithempeli, iLondon 
Inner Temple kanye neThempeli eliPhakathi (okungumakhelwane komunye nomunye) esigcemeni esisentshonalanga ye-Farringdon kanye nedolobha elicatshangelwayo ama-enclaves azimele. Zimbili kwezimbalwa ezisele zenkululeko, igama elidala lesigaba sendawo esinamalungelo akhethekile. Ziyizindawo ezingenangqondo, [27] ngokomlando aziphethwe yiDolobha laseLondon Corporation[28] (futhi namuhla zithathwa njengeziphathimandla zendawo ngezinjongo eziningi[29]) futhi ngokulinganayo zingaphandle kwegunya lesonto likaMbhishobhi waseLondon. 

Eminye imisebenzi 

I-Leadenhall Market iyimakethe yomlando ephakathi kukaGracechurch Street kanye ne-Lime Street. 
Ngaphakathi kwedolobha, i-Corporation ingumnikazi futhi iqhuba iMakethe yaseSmithfield neLeadenhall Market. Iphethe umhlaba ongaphezu kwemingcele yayo, okuhlanganisa nezindawo ezivulekile (amapaki, amahlathi nezindawo ezivamile) ngaphakathi nasezindaweni ezizungezile iGreater London, okuhlanganisa neningi le-Epping Forest kanye neHampstead Heath. I-Corporation ingumnikazi we-Old Spitalfields Market kanye ne-Billingsgate Fish Market, endaweni engumakhelwane yase-London Borough of Tower Hamlets. Ingumnikazi futhi isiza ngezimali i-Old Bailey, iNkantolo Yobugebengu Emaphakathi yase-England nase-Wales, njengesipho esizweni, njengoba isiqale njenge-City and Middlesex Sessions. Umhlonishwa I-Irish Society, indikimba exhumene kakhulu nenhlangano, nayo ingabanikazi bezindawo eziningi zomphakathi eNyakatho ye-Ireland.

Idolobha linamaphoyisa alo azimele, Amaphoyisa Edolobha LaseLondon—uMkhandlu Ovamile (indikimba eyinhloko yenhlangano) uyigunya lamaphoyisa.[30] Le nhlangano iphinde iphathe i-Hampstead Heath Constabulary, i-Epping Forest Keepers kanye nezinkampani zemakethe zeDolobha laseLondon (amalungu azo angasafakazelwanga njengoconstable kodwa agcina isihloko esingokomlando). Iningi le-Greater London lingamaphoyisa ophiko lwamaphoyisa eMetropolitan, oluzinze eNew Scotland Yard. 

Idolobha linesibhedlela esisodwa, iSt Bartholomew's Hospital, esaziwa nangokuthi 'Barts'. Yasungulwa ngo-1123, itholakala eSmithfield, futhi ivuselelwa isikhathi eside ilindelwe ngemuva kokungabaza ngokuqhubeka nokusetshenziswa kwayo ngeminyaka yawo-1990. 

Idolobha lingelesithathu ngobukhulu e-UK umxhasi kwezobuciko. Yengamela i-Barbican Centre futhi ixhase izinkampani ezimbalwa ezibalulekile ezidlalayo. 

I-London Port Health Authority, okuyisibopho senhlangano, inesibopho sayo yonke imisebenzi yezempilo echwebeni engxenyeni yomfula i-Thames, okuhlanganisa nechweba laseLondon kanye nezikhumulo zemikhumbi ezihlobene nayo, kanye ne-London City Airport.[31] I-Corporation yengamela iBridge House Estates, egcina iBlackfriars Bridge, iMillennium Bridge, iSouthwark Bridge, iLondon Bridge kanye neTower Bridge. Ifulege leDolobha lindizela phezu kwe-Tower Bridge, nakuba kungekho zinyawo ezifika edolobheni.[32] 

Umngcele weDolobha 

laseLondon umaka womngcele uma usondela eLondon Bridge 
Ubukhulu bedolobha bebuvinjwe udonga oluyisivikelo, olwaziwa ngoDonga lwaseLondon, olwakhiwa amaRoma ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-2nd ukuvikela idolobha labo eliyichweba. Nokho imingcele yeDolobha laseLondon ayisahambisani nodonga lwedolobha elidala, njengoba iDolobha lanweba indawo yalo yokulawula kancane ngokuhamba kwesikhathi. Ngesikhathi seNkathi Ephakathi, indawo yokulawula yedolobha inwebeka ngasentshonalanga, yeqa umngcele ongokomlando osentshonalanga wendawo yokuqala—i-River Fleet—egudle uFleet Street kuya e-Temple Bar. Idolobha liphinde lathatha eminye “imigoqo yeDolobha” eyayingalé kwendawo endala ebiyelwe ngodonga, njengaseHolborn, e-Aldersgate, eWest Smithfield, eBishopsgate nase-Aldgate. Lawa kwakuyiminyango ebalulekile yedolobha futhi ukulawula kwawo kwakubalulekile ekulondolozeni amalungelo akhethekile edolobha emisebenzini ethile yezohwebo. 


Isithombe sikadrako etsheni lesikhumbuzo Lebha Yethempeli, eliphawula umngcele phakathi kweDolobha laseLondon neDolobha lase-Westminster 
Iningi lodonga lunyamalele, kodwa izingxenye ezimbalwa zisabonakala. Ingxenye eseduze neMnyuziyamu yaseLondon yembulwa ngemva kokucekelwa phansi kokuhlasela kwezindiza ngomhlaka-29 Disemba 1940 ekuphakameni kweBlitz. Ezinye izingxenye ezibonakalayo ziseSt Alphage, futhi kunezigaba ezimbili eduze noMbhoshongo waseLondon. I-River Fleet yenziwa imisele ngemva koMlilo Omkhulu wango-1666 kwase kuthi ngezigaba kwenziwa ngezitini futhi kusukela ngekhulu le-18 bekungomunye "wemifula noma imifudlana" elahlekile yaseLondon, namuhla engaphansi komhlaba njengomfula wesiphepho.

Umngcele wedolobha awuzange ushintshe kwaze kwaba yilapho kushintsha umngcele omncane ngomhla ka-1 Ephreli 1994, lapho unwebeka kancane waya entshonalanga, enyakatho nasempumalanga, uthatha amaphasela amancane omhlaba eLondon Boroughs yaseWestminster, eCamden, e-Islington, eHackney naseTower Hamlets. Inhloso eyinhloko yalezi zinguquko kwakuwukuqoqa umngcele lapho wawusuphelelwe yisikhathi ngenxa yezinguquko endaweni yasemadolobheni. Kulolu hlelo idolobhakazi liphinde lalahlekelwa yizindawo ezincane zomhlaba, nakuba kube nenzuzo isiyonke (iDolobha lakhula lisuka ku-1.05 laya ku-1.12 square miles). Okuphawuleka kakhulu, izinguquko zabeka (ngaleso sikhathi esisanda kuthuthukiswa) ifa le-Broadgate edolobheni ngokuphelele.[33] 

ISouthwark, eningizimu yedolobha ngaphesheya koMfula iThames, yayingaphakathi kweDolobha phakathi kuka-1550 no-1899 njengeSigceme Sebhuloho Ngaphandle, isimo esihlobene neGuildable Manor. Umthwalo wemfanelo wokuphatha wedolobha lapho washabalala ngesikhathi maphakathi nenkathi ye-Victorian njengoba izici ezihlukahlukene zikahulumeni wedolobha elikhulu zanwetshwa ezindaweni ezingomakhelwane. Namuhla iyingxenye yeLondon Borough of Southwark. Umbhoshongo waseLondon ubulokhu ungaphandle kwedolobha futhi ungena ngaphansi kweLondon Borough of Tower Hamlets. 

Izikhali, isiqubulo kanye nefulegi 
Izihloko ezisemqoka: Ijazi lezikhali leDolobha lase-London kanye nefulegi leDolobha lase-London 

Idolobha lase-London lihlome ngengubo yesihlalo, njengoba kubonakala ngaphandle kwe-Royal Courts of Justice ngesikhathi sombukiso we-Lord Mayor's Show, 2011 
Inhlangano Yedolobha Lase-London iphumelele ngokugcwele ekuthwaleni izikhali okuhlanganisa isihlangu esibekwe phezu kwesihlangu, kubekwe phezu kwesihlangu. abalandeli nhlangothi zombili kanye nesiqubulo esivezwe emqulwini ongaphansi kwezingalo.[34][35][36] 

Ijazi lezikhali "liqoshwe kudala" eKolishi Lezikhali. Izingalo zihlanganisa ihawu elisiliva elinesiphambano esibomvu esinenkemba ebomvu eqondile engxenyeni yokuqala. Bahlanganisa izifanekiselo zabangcwele abangabavikeli baseNgilandi naseLondon: Isiphambano saseSt George nophawu lokufel’ ukholo lukaSaint Paul.[35][36] Inkemba ivame ukubizwa ngephutha ukukhumbula ukubulawa komholi we-Peasants' Revolt u-Wat Tyler yi-Lord Mayor yaseLondon uWilliam Walworth. Kodwa-ke izingalo zazisetshenziswa ezinyangeni ezithile ngaphambi kokufa kukaTyler, futhi isiko elivezwa inkemba ka-Walworth kungenzeka ukuthi isukela ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-17.[35][37][38][39] 

Isiqubulo sesiLatini saleli dolobha sithi "Domine dirige nos", esihumusha ngokuthi "Nkosi, siqondise". Kucatshangwa ukuthi yamukelwa ngekhulu le-17, njengoba irekhodi layo lakudala lingo-1633.[36][38] 

Isibhengezo sezingalo (umklamo osesihlangu) sindiza njengefulegi. 

IJografi
IDolobha laseLondon liyisifunda semikhosi esincane kunazo zonke eNgilandi ngendawo nangesibalo sabantu, kanti ingeyesine enabantu abaningi kakhulu. Ezifundeni ezingama-326 zamaNgisi, ingeyesibili ngobukhulu ngesibalo sabantu, ilandela iziQhingi zaseScally, futhi incane kakhulu ngendawo. Futhi iyidolobha elincane lamaNgisi ngenani labantu (futhi eBrithani, amadolobha amabili kuphela eWales mancane), kanye namancane kunawo wonke e-UK ngendawo. 

Ukuphakama kweDolobha kusuka ezingeni lolwandle emfuleni iThames kuye kumamitha angu-21.6 (71 ft) ekuhlanganeni kweHigh Holborn kanye neChancery Lane.[40] Amagquma amabili amancane kodwa aphawulekayo angaphakathi komlando, iLudgate Hill ngasentshonalanga kanye neCornhill empumalanga. Phakathi kwabo kwakugijima i-Walbrook, omunye wemifula eminingi "elahlekile" noma imifudlana yaseLondon (enye i-Fleet). Imingcele 

ye-Boundary 

Modern yeDolobha laseLondon, ekhombisa izindawo ezizungezile zaseLondon kanye nomngcele wangaphambi kuka-1994 (lapho ushintshiwe khona) ngokubomvu. Indawo ehlanganiswe yiThempeli elingaphakathi neliphakathi imakwe ngokuluhlaza. 
Kusukela entshonalanga, lapho iDolobha elisemngceleni we-Westminster, umngcele unqamula i-Victoria Embankment usuka e-Thames, udlulele ngasentshonalanga yeThempeli eliPhakathi, bese ujikela ibangana elifushane eduze ne-Strand futhi eduze ne-Temple Bar bese ukhuphuka ukhuphuka i-Chancery Lane, lapho umngcele weCamden. Ijikela empumalanga ngase-Holborn ukuya e-Holborn Circus bese iya enyakatho-mpumalanga ku-Charterhouse Street. Njengoba inqamula uFarringdon Road iba umngcele one-Islingt on. Iqhubekela e-Aldersgate, iye enyakatho, bese ijikela empumalanga ibe yimigwaqo engemuva ngemuva nje kokuthi i-Aldersgate ibe nguGoswell Road, kusukela ngo-1994 yamukela yonke i-Golden Lane Estate yale nhlangano. Lapha, e-Baltic Street West, yizinga elisenyakatho kakhulu. Umngcele uhlanganisa yonke i-Barbican Estate futhi uqhubeka usempumalanga eduze no-Ropemaker Street futhi ukuqhubeka kwawo ngaphesheya kwe-Moorgate, uba yindawo eseNingizimu. Iya enyakatho, ifinyelele emngceleni noHackney, bese isempumalanga, enyakatho, empumalanga emigwaqweni engemuva, i-Worship Street yenza umngcele osenyakatho, ukuze ifake i-Broadgate estate. Umngcele ube usuphendukela eningizimu eNorton Folgate futhi uba umngcele neTower Hamlets. Uqhubekela eningizimu ungene e-Bishopsgate, futhi uthatha imigwaqo engemuva iye ku-Middlesex Street (Petticoat Lane) lapho uqhubeka ubheke eningizimu-mpumalanga bese useningizimu. Khona-ke ijikela eningizimu-ntshonalanga, inqamule iMinories ukuze ingahlanganisi uMbhoshongo waseLondon, bese ifika eMfuleni iThames. 

Umngcele ube usukhuphukela enkabeni yomzila onamagagasi aphansi oMfula iThames, ngaphandle kokuthi iBlackfriars Bridge (okuhlanganisa nomfula ongaphansi nomhlaba osekugcineni kwayo eningizimu) iyingxenye yeDolobha ngokuphelele, okwenza iDolobha kanye neBorough yaseRichmond phezu kweThames kube ukuphela kwezifunda zaseLondon ezihamba ngasenyakatho naseningizimu yomfula. I-span kanye ne-southern abutment ye-London Bridge iyingxenye yedolobha ngezinjongo ezithile[41] (futhi ngaleyo ndlela iyingxenye yesigceme seBridge).[42]

Imingcele imakwe ngamabhola amnyama anophawu lwedolobha, kanye nezimpawu zomngcele kadrako ezindaweni zokungena ezinkulu, njengaseHolborn naseningizimu yeLondon Bridge. Itshe lesikhumbuzo elikhulu kakhulu liphawula umngcele e-Temple Bar kuFleet Street. 

Kwezinye izindawo, isifunda sezimali sidlulela ngale kwemingcele, ikakhulukazi enyakatho nasempumalanga, siye ezindaweni zaseLondon iTower Hamlets, Hackney kanye ne-Islington, futhi ngokungakahleleki lezi zindawo zithathwa njengengxenye ye-"Square Mile". Kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1990s umngcele osempumalanga, udlulela eHackney naseTower Hamlets, ulokhu ugxile kakhulu ekuthuthukisweni kwamahhovisi amakhulu ngenxa yokutholakala kwezindawo ezinkulu uma kuqhathaniswa nangaphakathi kwedolobha. 

Izingadi nobuciko bomphakathi 
Bheka futhi: Uhlu lobuciko bomphakathi eDolobheni LaseLondon 

I-Finsbury Circus, indawo enkulu kunazo zonke evulekile yomphakathi, ebonwa kusukela ku-Tower 42 
Idolobha alinawo amapaki amakhulu ngaphakathi komngcele walo, kodwa linoxhaxha lwenani elikhulu lezingadi nezindawo ezincane ezivulekile, eziningi zazo ezinakekelwa yinhlangano. Lezi zisukela ezingadini ezisemthethweni njengale eseFinsbury Circus, equkethe i-bowling eluhlaza kanye ne-bandstand, kuya emagcekeni esonto afana no-St Olave Hart Street, ukuchelela izici nemisebenzi yobuciko emagcekeni nasezindleleni zabahamba ngezinyawo.[43] 

Izingadi zifaka phakathi:

Kunenqwaba yezingadi ezizimele nezindawo ezivulekile, ngokuvamile ngaphakathi kwamagceke entuthuko enkulu yezentengiselwano. Ezimbili ezinkulukazi yilezo zeThempeli elingaphakathi kanye neThempeli eliPhakathi Inns laseNkantolo, eningizimu-ntshonalanga ekude. 

Umfula iThames kanye nohambo lwawo oseceleni komfula kuya ngokuya kwaziswa njengezindawo ezivulekile futhi eminyakeni yamuva nje kwenziwa imizamo yokwandisa ikhono labahamba ngezinyawo ukuze bakwazi ukungena nokuhamba eduze komfula. 

Isimo Sezulu 
Isiteshi sezulu esiseduzane ngokomlando bekuyi-London Weather Center e-Kingsway/Holborn, nakuba ukubonwa kwanqamuka ngo-2010. Manje i-St. James Park inikeza ukufundwa okusemthethweni okuseduze.

Idolobha linesimo sezulu solwandle (i-Köppen "Cfb") esilungiswe yisiqhingi sokushisa sasemadolobheni esimaphakathi neLondon. Lokhu ngokuvamile kubangela ubuncane besikhathi sasebusuku esiphezulu kunezindawo ezingaphandle. Isibonelo, isilinganiso sika-August sisho ubuncane[45] sika-14.7 °C (58.5 °F) siqhathaniswa nesibalo esingu-13.3 °C (55.9 °F) se-Greenwich[46] ne-Heathrow[47] kuyilapho singu-11.6 °C (52.9 °F) e-Wisley[48] maphakathi ne-Metropolitan yamakhilomitha-skwele ambalwa. Zonke izibalo zibhekisela esikhathini sokubuka sika-1971–2000. 

Ngokunjalo, isiteshi sezulu siphethe irekhodi lezinga lokushisa elincane lase-UK elifudumele ebusuku, elingu-24.0 °C (75.2 °F), elaqoshwa ngomhla ka-4 Agasti 1990.[49] Umkhawulo ngu-37.6 °C (99.7 °F), usethwe ngomhla ka-10 Agasti 2003.[50] Ubuncane obuphelele[51] besiteshi sesimo sezulu bungu-−8.2 °C (17.2 °F), uma kuqhathaniswa nokufunda cishe ku-−15.0 °C (5.0 °F) ngasemaphethelweni eLondon. Ngokungajwayelekile, lelizinga lokushisa laliphakathi nesikhathi sokubanda okunomoya neqhwa (maphakathi no-January 1987), kunokuba kube nobusuku obubandayo obucwathile—kuboshwa umoya obandayo ngenxa yodedangendlale wendawo yasemadolobheni ezungeze idolobha. 

Isiteshi siphethe irekhodi lezinga eliphezulu lokushisa lanyanga zonke laseBrithani,[52] 24.5 °C (76.1 °F) (okushiwo ubuningi obungu-29.2 °C (84.6 °F), kusho ubuncane obungu-19.7 °C (67.5 °F) phakathi noJulayi 2006). Nokho, ngokwezinga lokushisa eliphezulu emini, i-Cambridge NIAB[53] kanye ne-Botanical Gardens[54] enesilinganiso esiphezulu esingu-29.1 °C (84.4 °F), kanye ne-Heathrow[55] eno-29.0 °C (84.2 °F) konke kudlule lokhu.

Izinsiza zomphakathi 

Idolobha laseLondon ijazi lezikhali emgwaqweni 
Amaphoyisa nokuphepha 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Ubugebengu eLondon 

Imoto yamaphoyisa yaseDolobheni laseLondon eBlackfriars Bridge
Idolobha liyindawo yamaphoyisa futhi linamaphoyisa alo, iDolobha Lamaphoyisa aseLondon, ahlukene neMetropolitan Police Service ehlanganisa iningi leGreater London. Phambilini amaPhoyisa eDolobha abeneziteshi zamaphoyisa ezintathu, eSnow Hill, Wood Street naseBishopsgate. Manje bagcine kuphela i-Bishopsgate kanye nendlunkulu yokuphatha e-Guildhall Yard East.[57] Umbutho unamaphoyisa angama-735 kuhlanganisa nabaseshi abangu-273.[58] Ingamaphoyisa amancane kunawo wonke e-England nase-Wales, kuzo zombili izindawo kanye nenani lamaphoyisa. 

Lapho iningi lamaphoyisa aseBrithani enamabheji anombala wesiliva, lawo Amaphoyisa Edolobha LaseLondon amnyama negolide afaka iCity Crest. Ibutho linamabhande angamakepisi anoshekhasi abomvu namhlophe angavamile kanye namabhande anemigqa eyingqayizivele ebomvu nemhlophe emikhonweni yamajazi oconstable nosayitsheni (imibala ebomvu nemhlophe okuyimibala yedolobha), okuthi kwamanye amabutho amaningi aseBrithani amnyama nokumhlophe. Osayitsheni bamaphoyisa edolobha noconstable bagqoka izigqoko zokuvikela abaqaphi ngesikhathi behamba ngezinyawo. Lezi zigqoko zokuzivikela azifaki uMqhele waseSt Edward noma i-Brunswick Star, ezisetshenziswa kwezinye izigqoko zamaphoyisa eNgilandi naseWales. 

Isikhundla sedolobha njengesikhungo sezimali sase-United Kingdom kanye nengxenye ebucayi yomnotho wezwe, esinikela cishe ngama-2.5% womkhiqizo kazwelonke wase-UK, [59] siholele ekutheni libe yizisulu zodlame lwezepolitiki. I-IRA Yesikhashana yaqhuma amabhomu ambalwa ekuqaleni kwawo-1990, okuhlanganisa nokuqhuma kwamabhomu e-Bishopsgate yango-1993. 

Le ndawo kuphinde kukhulunywe ngayo njengendawo okungase kubhekiswe kuyo i-al-Qaeda. Isibonelo, lapho ngoMeyi 2004 uhlelo lwe-BBC's Panorama luhlola ukulungela kwabezimo eziphuthumayo baseBrithani ukuhlasela kwamaphekula ngesilinganiso sokuhlasela kwangomhla ziyi-11 kuSeptemba 2001, balingisa ukuqhuma kwamakhemikhali eBishopsgate empumalanga yedolobha. "I-Ring of Steel" yasungulwa ngemuva kokuqhuma kwamabhomu e-IRA ukuze kuvikelwe izinsongo zamaphekula. 

I-Fire Brigade 
Isihloko esikhulu: I-London Fire Brigade 
Idolobha linezingozi zomlilo ezakhiweni eziningi ezinomlando, okuhlanganisa i-St Paul's Cathedral, i-Old Bailey, i-Mansion House, i-Smithfield Market, i-Guildhall, kanye nezakhiwo eziningi eziphakeme kakhulu. Kunesiteshi esisodwa saseLondon Fire Brigade edolobheni, e-Dowgate, esinomshini wokumpompa owodwa.[60] IDolobha lithembele eziteshini ezisezindaweni ezizungezile zaseLondon ukulisekela kwezinye izigameko. Izicishamlilo zokuqala ziba khona cishe emizuzwini emihlanu ngokwesilinganiso, eyesibili uma kudingeka ngemizuzu engaphezudlwana kwemihlanu nesigamu.[60] Kwakunezehlakalo ezingu-1 814 eDolobheni ngo-2006/2007—eziphansi kunazo zonke eGreater London. Akekho owashona esigamekweni esibangelwe umlilo eminyakeni emine eyandulela indawo 

Amandla 
Kunesiteshi sikagesi esiku-Charterhouse Street esihlinzeka ukushisa kwamanye amabhilidi aseduze.[61]

Imithombo: Ihhovisi Lezibalo Zikazwelonke[62][63] 
Ihhovisi Lezibalo Zikazwelonke laqopha inani labantu ngo-2011 njengabangu-7,375;[64] liphakeme kancane kunobalo lwabantu lwangaphambilini, ngo-2001,[65] futhi lilinganisela ukuthi inani labantu maphakathi no-2016 lalingu-9,401. Ekubalwa kwabantu kwango-2001 ukwakheka kohlanga kwakungama-84.6% Abamhlophe, 6.8% abaseNingizimu Asia, 2.6% Abamnyama, 2.3% Abaxubile, 2.0% amaShayina kanye no-1.7% afakwe ohlwini "njengabanye".[65] Inani labantu laliphakathi kuka-120,000 kanye ne-140,000 engxenyeni yokuqala yekhulu le-19, lehla kakhulu lisuka ku-1851 laya ku-1991, nokwanda okuncane phakathi kuka-1991 no-2001. Okuwukuphela koshintsho lwemingcele oluphawulekayo kusukela ekubenilwa kwabantu kokuqala ngo-1801 kwenzeka 

ngeviki eligcwele abasebenzi basemadolobheni ngo-1994. khokha kunaseLondon naseGreat Britain (eNgilandi, eWales naseScotland): £773.30 uma kuqhathaniswa no-£598.60 kanye no-£491.00 ngokulandelana. [66] Kunokungalingani okukhulu kwemali engenayo phakathi kobulili (£1,085.90 emadodeni uma kuqhathaniswa no-£653.50 kwabesifazane), futhi lokhu kungachazwa ngohlobo lomsebenzi kanye nobude bokuqashwa ngokulandelana.[66] I-Census yango-2001 yabonisa idolobha njengesifunda esiyingqayizivele phakathi kwezifunda ezingama-376 ezahlolwa eNgilandi naseWales.[65] Idolobhakazi libe nokwanda okulinganiselwe kwesibalo sabantu, imindeni yomuntu oyedwa, abantu abaneziqu ezingeni leziqu noma ngaphezulu kanye nezinkomba eziphakeme kakhulu zokuminyana.[65] Iqophe ingxenye ephansi kakhulu yemizi enezimoto noma amaveni, abantu abaya emsebenzini ngemoto, imindeni yabashadile kanye nesilinganiso esiphansi sobukhulu bendlu: abantu abangu-1.58 kuphela.[65] Iphinde yakleliswa endaweni ephakeme kakhulu phakathi kweGreater London endaweni ngamaphesenti abantu abangenayo inkolo kanye nabantu abasebenzayo.[65] 

Ukuwohloka Kwezibalo Zezibalo Zedolobha LaseLondon (1981-2021) 
Umnotho 
Bheka futhi: Umnotho waseLondon 

IBhange LaseNgilandi, eku-Threadneedle Street, yibhange elikhulu lase-United Kingdom.
Idolobha laseLondon liqhudelana ne-Lower Manhattan yaseNew York City ukuthola umehluko wesikhungo sezimali esivelele emhlabeni. ILondon Stock Exchange (amasheya namabhondi), i-Lloyd's yaseLondon (umshwalense) kanye neBhange LaseNgilandi zonke zizinze edolobheni.[72] Amabhange angaphezu kuka-500 anamahhovisi edolobheni. I-Alternative Investment Market, imakethe yokuhweba ngezabelo zamafemu amancane, iyintuthuko yakamuva. Ngo-2009, iDolobha laseLondon laba ngu-2.4% we-GDP yase-UK.[73] 

Imakethe yokushintshiselana ngemali yangaphandle yaseLondon ichazwe ngabakwaReuters 'njengegugu eliyigugu lomkhakha wezezimali waseLondon'.[74] Ku-$3.98 trillion nsuku zonke emhlabeni jikelele, njengoba kwalinganiswa ngo-2009, ukuhwebelana eLondon kwaba nenani elilinganiselwa ku-$1.85 trillion, noma u-46.7% yenani eliphelele.[73] I-pound sterling, imali yase-United Kingdom, iwuhlobo lwemali lwesine oluhweba kakhulu emhlabeni jikelele[75] kanye nemali egcinwe endaweni yesine ephethwe kakhulu.[76] 

ICanary Wharf, eqhele ngamakhilomitha ambalwa empumalanga yeDolobha e-Tower Hamlets, okuhlala amabhange amaningi nezinye izikhungo ezazitholakala e-Square Mile, kusukela ngo-1991 isibe esinye isikhungo semboni yezinkonzo zezezimali yaseLondon. Nakuba ukukhula kuqhubekile kuzo zombili lezi zindawo, [okungaqondakali] futhi kube nokuthuthwa kuzo zombili izinhlangothi, iNhlangano ibone ukuthi izinqubomgomo zayo zokuhlela kungenzeka ukuthi bezibangela amafemu ezezimali ukuthi akhethe i-Canary Wharf njengendawo.[ecashunwa] 

Ngo-2022, u-12.3% wezakhamizi zaseDolobheni lase-London zazinikezwe isimo sokungeyona indawo yokuhlala ukuze zigweme ukukhokha7 intela e-UK.[7] 

Indlunkulu 

iPaternoster Square, kusukela ngo-2004 ikhaya leLondon Stock Exchange 
Izinkampani eziningi ezinkulu zomhlaba zinekomkhulu lazo edolobheni, okuhlanganisa i-Aviva, [78] BT Group, [79] Lloyds Banking Group, [80] Quilter, Prudential, [81] Schroders, [82] Standard Chartered, [83] kanye ne-Unilever, [83] 

Izinkampani eziningi zezomthetho ezinkulu emhlabeni zinekomkhulu kuleli dolobha, okuhlanganisa nezinkampani zabameli ezine zeMagic Circle (Allen & Overy, Freshfields Bruckhaus Deringer, Linklaters and Slaughter & May), kanye namanye amafemu afana no-Ashurst, DLA Piper, Eversheds Sutherland, Herbert Smith Freehills kanye noHorbert Smith. 

Eminye imikhakha 

Barbican Center
Nakuba umkhakha wezezimali, kanye namabhizinisi nezikhungo ezihlobene, zisaqhubeka nokubusa, umnotho awugcini kulowo mkhakha. Umkhakha wezomthetho unobukhona obuqinile, ikakhulukazi entshonalanga nasenyakatho (okungukuthi, ngaseZindlini Zokulala Ezinkantolo). Amabhizinisi okudayisa ake abalulekile, kodwa kancane kancane athuthela eWest End yaseLondon, nakuba manje kuyinqubomgomo yeNhlangano ukukhuthaza ukudayisa kwezinye izindawo, isibonelo eCheapside eduze kwaseSt Paul's. Idolobha linezindawo eziningi eziheha izivakashi, ikakhulukazi ezisuselwa kumagugu alo omlando kanye neBarbican Center kanye neMuseum eseduze yaseLondon, yize ezokuvakasha okwamanje azibambeleli kakhulu emnothweni noma kumlingisi wedolobha. Idolobha linezindawo eziningi zokucima ukoma, imigoqo kanye nezindawo zokudlela, kanti umnotho "wasebusuku" uyabonakala endaweni yaseBishopsgate, ngaseShoreditch. Imakethe yenyama eSmithfield, ngaphakathi kwedolobha lonke, isaqhubeka nokuba enye yezimakethe ezinkulu zaseLondon (eyodwa esele enkabeni yeLondon) kanye nemakethe yenyama enkulu kunazo zonke yezwe. Empumalanga kuneMakethe yaseLeadenhall, imakethe yokudla okusha nayo eheha izivakashi. 

Ukudayisa kanye nezindawo zokuhlala 
Umkhuba wokuthuthukiswa kwamahhovisi kuphela usuqala ukuhlehla njengoba iNhlangano ikhuthaza ukusetshenziswa kwezindawo zokuhlala, nakuba intuthuko iyenzeka uma ivela ezindaweni ezifashisayo. Idolobhakazi linomgomo wokwengeza izindlu zokuhlala ezingama-90 ngonyaka.[85] Enye indawo yokuhlala eyengeziwe isezakhiweni ezincane ezisohlwini lwangaphambi kweMpi Yezwe II, ezingakulungele ukuhlalwa yizinkampani ezinkulu manje esezihlinzeka ngemisebenzi eminingi yedolobha. Intuthuko yezindawo zokuhlala yakamuva ihlanganisa "iHeron", ibhilidi eliphakeme lokuhlala endaweni yaseMilton Court eduze neBarbican, kanye nentuthuko yeHeron Plaza eBishopsgate kulindeleke ukuthi ifake nezindawo zokuhlala. 

Kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1990, iDolobha liye lahluka ekusetshenzisweni kwamahhovisi okukhethekile ngezinye izindlela. Isibonelo, amahhotela amaningana kanye nesitolo sokuqala savulwa ngeminyaka yawo-2000s. Inxanxathela yezitolo isanda kuvulwa e-One New Change, e-Cheapside (eduze kwase-St Paul's Cathedral) ngo-Okthoba 2010, evulwa izinsuku eziyisikhombisa ngesonto. Kodwa-ke, izingxenye ezinkulu zihlala zithule ngezimpelasonto, ikakhulukazi engxenyeni esempumalanga, futhi kuyinto evamile ukuthola izitolo, izindawo zokudlela kanye nezindawo zokudlela zivaliwe ngalezi zinsuku. 

Izimpawu Zezindawo 
Izakhiwo zomlando 
Umlilo, ukuqhuma kwamabhomu kanye nokuthuthukiswa kabusha kwangemva kweMpi Yezwe II kusho ukuthi idolobha, naphezu komlando walo, linezakhiwo zomlando ezimbalwa ezingaguquki kunalokho umuntu angase akulindele. Noma kunjalo, kusele inqwaba yezakhiwo ezinhle (ikakhulukazi ezase-Victorian kanye ne-Edwardian), ngokuvamile ngesitayela somlando kanye ne-neoclassical. Zihlanganisa iSikhumbuzo Somlilo Omkhulu waseLondon ("isikhumbuzo"), iSt Paul's Cathedral, iGuildhall, iRoyal Exchange, iDokotela Johnson's House, Mansion House kanye namasonto amaningi amakhulu, amaningi aklanywa nguSir Christopher Wren, naye owaklama iSt Paul's.

I-Prince Henry's Room kanye ne-2 King's Bench Walk bangababhali abasinde ekuqhunyisweni kwamabhomu okunamandla endaweni yeThempeli, esakhiwe kabusha ngendlela engokomlando. Esinye isibonelo sendawo eyalinyazwa ibhomu esibuyiselwe iStaple Inn eseHolborn. Izingxenye ezimbalwa ezincane zoDonga LwaseRoma lwaseLondon zikhona, isibonelo eduze neTower of London kanye nendawo yaseBarbican. Phakathi kwezakhiwo ezisohlwini zangekhulunyaka lamashumi amabili kukhona i-Bracken House, okuyizakhiwo zokuqala zangemuva kweMpi Yezwe Yesibili ezweni ezinikezwe isivikelo esingokomthetho, kanye nayo yonke iBarbican neGolden Lane Estate. 

I-Tower of London ayikho edolobheni, kodwa iyindawo ephawulekayo eheha izivakashi ezilethela izivakashi eningizimu-mpumalanga yedolobha. Ezinye izakhiwo eziyingqophamlando ezinomlando obalulekile zifaka iBhange LaseNgilandi, i-Old Bailey, iCustom House, iSmithfield Market, iLeadenhall Market kanye nesibhedlela iSt Bartholomew. Izakhiwo zangaleso eziphawulekayo zihlanganisa nenani lezakhiwo eziphakeme zesimanje (bheka ingxenye engezansi) kanye nesakhiwo sikaLloyd. 


IBhange LaseNgilandi (kwesobunxele) kanye neRoyal Exchange (maphakathi) yizakhiwo ezimbili kweziningi ezibalulekile eDolobheni laseLondon. 
Amabhilidi namabhilidi amade 
Bheka futhi: Uhlu lwezakhiwo ezinde kunazo zonke eLondon 

Isibhakabhaka seDolobha ngo-2021, kuhlanganisa no-20 Fenchurch Street, i-Leadenhall Building, 30 St Mary Ax & 22 Bishopgate, isakhiwo eside kunazo zonke eDolobheni laseLondon. Ibhuloho laseLondon phansi kwesokunxele. 
Kuqediwe 
Inani elikhulayo lamabhilidi amade namabhilidi asetshenziswa ngokuyinhloko umkhakha wezezimali. Cishe zonke zitholakala ohlangothini olusempumalanga eduze kwaseBishopsgate, Leadenhall Street kanye noFenchurch Street, emnyombweni wezezimali wedolobha. Enyakatho kuneqoqo elincane elihlanganisa imibhoshongo emithathu emide yokuhlala yaseBarbican Estate kanye nombhoshongo wezohwebo weCityPoint. Ngo-2007, kwabhidlizwa isakhiwo se-Drapers' Gardens esibude obuyi-100 m (328 ft) sathathelwa indawo umbhoshongo omfishane. 

Izakhiwo zedolobha okungenani eziyi-100 m (328 ft) ukuphakama yilezi: 



UJames Gillray (13 Agasti 1756 [1][2] - 1 Juni 1815) wayengumdlali we-caricaturist waseBrithani kanye nomshicileli odume ngokubhuqa kwakhe kwezepolitiki nezenhlalo, okushicilelwe ikakhulukazi phakathi kuka-1792 no-1810. Iningi lemisebenzi yakhe e-Gay National Portrait eLondon. 

U-Gillray ubizwa ngokuthi "uyise wopopayi wezombusazwe", nemisebenzi yakhe ehlekisa uGeorge III, uNapoleon, ondunankulu nojenene. [3] Ethathwa njengomunye wabadwebi bopopayi ababili abanethonya elikhulu, omunye kunguWilliam Hogarth, ubuhlakani namahlaya kaGillray, ulwazi lokuphila, ukuvunda kwezinsiza, umuzwa ojulile wokuhlekisa, nobuhle bokubulawa, ngaso leso sikhathi kwamnikeza indawo yokuqala phakathi kwabadlali be-caricatur.[3][4][5] 

Isiqalo sokuphila
Wazalelwa e-Chelsea, eLondon. Uyise wayeke wakhonza njengesosha; walahlekelwa ingalo e-Battle of Fontenoy ngo-1745 futhi wangeniswa, okokuqala njengesiboshwa futhi kamuva njengomuntu ohola impesheni yangaphandle, esibhedlela sase-Chelsea. UGillray waqala ukuphila ngokufunda ukubhala ngohlamvu, lapho asheshe waba nekhono khona. Ethola lo msebenzi unzima, wabe esezulazula isikhashana nenkampani yabadlali abahamba ngezinyawo. Ngemva kokuhlangenwe nakho okulinganiselwe, wabuyela eLondon futhi wamukelwa njengomfundi eRoyal Academy, ezisekela ngokuqopha, futhi mhlawumbe ekhipha inqwaba yama-caricatures ngaphansi kwamagama aqanjiwe.[6] 

I-caricatures yakhe cishe yonke i-etching, enye nayo ine-aquatint, kanti abambalwa basebenzisa ubuchwepheshe be-stipple. Ayikho engachazwa ngendlela efanele njengeqoshiwe, nakuba leli gama livame ukusetshenziselwa ukuzichaza ngokukhululekile. Imisebenzi kaHogarth yayiyinjabulo nokufunda eminyakeni yakhe yokuqala. I-Paddy on Horseback, eyavela ngo-1779, i-caricature yokuqala okungeyakhe ngokuqinisekile. Ama-caricatures amabili ekunqobeni kwemikhumbi yempi ka-Admiral Rodney e-Battle of the Saintes, eyakhishwa ngo-1782, ayephakathi kwezokuqala ochungechungeni olukhumbulekayo lwemidwebo yakhe yezombangazwe.[6][7] 

Impilo Yabantu Abadala 

Very Slippy-Weather (1808) 
Igama lomshicileli nomthengisi wamaphrinti kaGillray, u-Hannah Humphrey – isitolo sakhe saqale saba ku-227 Strand, saba ku-New Bond Street, saba ku-Old Bond Street, futhi ekugcineni ku-St James's Street - lihlotshaniswa ngokungenakuhlukaniswa nelomculi we-caricaturist ngokwakhe. UGillray wayehlala noMiss (ovame ukubizwa ngokuthi uNkk) Humphrey phakathi nayo yonke inkathi yodumo lwakhe. Kukholakala ukuthi izikhathi eziningana wacabanga ukumshada, nokuthi ngesinye isikhathi laba bobabili babesendleleni eya esontweni, lapho uGillray ethi: "Lokhu kuwubuwula, ucabanga, Nkosazana Humphrey. Siphila ngokunethezeka kakhulu ndawonye; kungcono siyeke." Nokho, abukho ubufakazi obusekela izindaba ezaqanjwa abenzi bamahlazo ngobudlelwano babo.[6] Eminye yemibhalo kaGillray, ethi, "Twopenny Whist", iwumfanekiso wabantu abane abadlala amakhadi, kanti umlingisi oboniswe owesibili ukusuka kwesokunxele, intokazi esikhulile enezibuko zamehlo kanye nebhonethi, kukholakala kabanzi njengomfanekiso onembile kaMiss Humphrey. 

Amapuleti kaGillray avele obala efasiteleni lesitolo sikaHumphrey, lapho izixuku ezimagange zaziwahlola khona.[6] Enye yamaphrinti akhe akamuva, i-Very Slippy-Weather, ibonisa isitolo sikaMiss Humphrey ku-St. James's Street ngemuva. Efasiteleni lesitolo inani lemibhalo ka-Gillray eshicilelwe ngaphambilini, efana no-Tiddy-Doll the Great French Gingerbread Maker, Drawing Out A New Batch of Kings; Indoda Yakhe, uTalley Mixing up the Dough, ukubhuqa mayelana nokwenza inkosi kukaNapoleon, kuboniswe efasiteleni lesitolo. 


I-L'Assemblée Nationale (1804) yayibizwa ngokuthi "i-caricature enethalente kakhulu eyake yavela", ngokwengxenye ngenxa "yokufana kwayo okuncomekayo".INkosana YaseWales yakhokha isamba semali ukuze icindezele futhi ipuleti layo licekelwe phansi.[8]
Amehlo kaGillray aqala ukuphelelwa amandla ngo-1806. Waqala ukugqoka izibuko kodwa ayengagculisi. Engakwazi ukusebenzela izindinganiso zakhe eziphakeme zangaphambili, uJames Gillray wacindezeleka futhi waqala ukuphuza kakhulu. Wakhiqiza umbhalo wakhe wokugcina ngo-September 1809. Ngenxa yokuphuza kwakhe kakhulu u-Gillray waphathwa yi-gout kukho konke ukuphila kwakhe kwakamuva. 

Umsebenzi wakhe wokugcina, ovela kumklamo ka-Bunbury, unesihloko esithi Interior of a Barber's Shop in Assize Time, futhi wangonyaka ka-1811. Ngesikhathi esathembisene umshado wawo wasangana, nakuba ayenezikhathi ezithile zokuhlanzeka, azisebenzisa emsebenzini wakhe wokugcina. Ukusondela kobuhlanya kungenzeka ukuthi kwakusheshiswa imikhuba yakhe yokungabi nasimilo.[6] 

NgoJulayi 1811 uGillray wazama ukuzibulala ngokugxuma efasiteleni le-attic ngaphezu kwesitolo sikaHumphrey kuSt James's Street. U-Gillray wawela ekuhlanyeni futhi wabhekwa nguHannah Humphrey waze washona mhla lu-1 kuNhlangulana 1815 eLondon; wangcwatshwa egcekeni lesonto laseSt James, ePiccadilly. 

Ubuciko be-caricature 

I-Reception of the Diplomatique (i-Macartney) kanye ne-Suite yakhe, eNkantolo yasePekin, eyanyatheliswa ngo-September 1792. 
Inqwaba yezingoma zakhe ezihlukumezayo ziqondiswe kuGeorge III, okwathi, ngemva kokuhlola ezinye zemidwebo kaGillray, wathi "Angiziqondi lezi zithombe." UGillray waziphindiselela ngalokhu kukhuluma nge-caricature yakhe enesihloko esithi, A Connoisseur Examining a Cooper, akwenza esebenzisa ikhandlela elithi "save-all", ukuze umdwebo odwetshiwe uhleke ngokushesha ukuzenzisa kwenkosi kolwazi lobuciko kanye nemikhuba yayo yobuxhwanguxhwangu. 

Phakathi neNguquko YaseFrance, uGillray wathatha isimo sokulandela, futhi wakhipha i-caricature ngemuva kwe-caricature egcona amaFulentshi namaNapoleon (evamise ukusebenzisa uJacobin) futhi ekhazimulisa uJohn Bull. Okuningi kwalokhu kushicilelwe ku-Anti-Jacobin Review. Nokho, akufanele abhekwe njengomuntu oshisekayo wezepolitiki weqembu le-Whig noma le-Tory; ama-caricatures akhe ayegculisa amalungu azo zonke izinhlangothi zomkhakha wezombangazwe.[6] 


Ama-Monstrous Craws, edilini elisha le-Coalition (1787)
Izikhathi uGillray ayephila kuzo zazithandeka ngokukhethekile ekukhuleni kwesikole esikhulu se-caricature. Impi yeqembu yayiqhutshwa ngamandla amakhulu futhi hhayi kancane kancane; futhi ubuntu babezitika ngokukhululekile nhlangothi zombili. Ukuhlakanipha nokuhleka kukaGillray okungenakuqhathaniswa, ulwazi lokuphila, ukuvunda kwensiza, umuzwa ojulile wokuhlekisa, nobuhle bokubulawa, ngaso leso sikhathi kwamnikeza indawo yokuqala phakathi kwama-caricaturists. Uhlukaniswa emlandweni we-caricature ngokuthi imidwebo yakhe iyimisebenzi yobuciko yangempela. Imibono equkethwe kweminye yayo mihle kakhulu futhi muhle ngokwenkondlo ngokuqina kwencazelo yayo, kuyilapho ukungagwegwesi - abanye abaye bakubiza ngokuthi ukukhohlakala - abanye abakubonisayo kuwuphawu lwenkululeko evamile yokwelapha evamile kuyo yonke iminyango yezobuhlakani ekhulwini le-18. Ukubaluleka okungokomlando komsebenzi kaGillray kuye kwaqashelwa abafundi abaningi abaqaphelayo bomlando. Njengoba kuye kwaphawulwa kahle: “INkosi uStanhope iphendule uGillray njengentatheli yezinkulumo eqotho, kanye nomdwebi osikisela wezenzakalo.”[4] 


IVoluptuary Under the Horrors of Digestion (1792) 

Temperance Enjoying a Frugal Meal (1792) 
Ubufakazi bakhe besikhathi esidlule uBay ethonyeni lezombangazwe kusukela ku-3 November 2014 1798. "Abaphikisayo", ebhalela uGillray, "baphansi ngendlela esingabafisa ngayo. Ube nenkonzo engapheli ekwehliseni, futhi ubenze inhlekisa." Imboni ka-Gillray engavamile ingase ithathwe eqinisweni lokuthi cishe ama-caricatures angu-1000 afakwe kuye; kuyilapho abanye bembheka njengombhali wezincwadi eziningi ezifinyelela ku-1600 noma 1700. Ngokwe-Encyclopædia Britannica Eleventh Edition, “uGillray ubaluleke kakhulu kumfundi wemikhuba yesiNgisi njengakumfundi wezombangazwe, ehlasela ubuwula bezenhlalo yangaleso sikhathi ngokubhuqa okuhlabayo; futhi akukho lutho olumbalekelayo, ngisho noshintsho olukhulu oluncane oluncane lwemfashini ewubukhazikhazi. noma isiphi isihloko silingana kuphela nesiphetho esihle semidwebo yakhe—enhle kunayo yonke efinyelela ubuhle obumangalisayo kanye ne-Miltonic sublimity yokukhulelwa."[4]

Ama-caricatures ka-Gillray ngokuvamile ahlukaniswe amakilasi amabili, uchungechunge lwezepolitiki kanye nezenhlalo, nakuba kubalulekile ukuthi singabaluli igama elithi "uchungechunge" noma yimuphi umqondo wokuqhubeka noma ukuphelela. Imidwebo yezombangazwe ihlanganisa ingxenye ebalulekile neyigugu yomlando osekhona wengxenye yokugcina yokubusa kukaGeorge III. Azisakazwanga eBrithani kuphela kodwa nakulo lonke elaseYurophu, futhi zaba nethonya elinamandla kokubili eBrithani nakwamanye amazwe. Emibhalweni yezombangazwe, uGeorge III, unkosikazi kaGeorge u-Queen Charlotte, iNkosana yaseWales (kamuva owaba yisikhulu senkosi, kwase kuba yiNkosi uGeorge IV), uFox, uPitt Omncane, uBurke noNapoleon Bonaparte bangabantu abavelele kakhulu.[4] Ngasekupheleni kokuphila kwakhe, uNapoleon wakhala ngokuthi ama-caricatures kaGillray athi wayemfushane ngokungavamile “wenze okungaphezu kwawo wonke amabutho aseYurophu ukungiwisa.”[9] 

Ngo-1788, kwavela ama-caricatures amabili amahle kaGillray. Igazi Ekudumeni eligudla uLwandle Olubomvu limele u-Lord Thurlow ethwele u-Warren Hastings olwandle olushisayo: U-Hastings ubukeka enethezeke kakhulu, futhi uphethe izikhwama ezimbili ezinkulu zemali. I-Market-Day ifanekisela ongqongqoshe bangaleso sikhathi njengezinkomo ezithengiswayo.[4] 


Ngemfashini ngaphambi kokukhululeka; - noma, - Umthethosisekelo omuhle owahlatshelwa iFomu le-Fantastick (1793), u-James Gillray wenza i-Paine eqinisa i-corset yase-Britannia futhi ephuma ephaketheni lejazi lakhe yiteyiphu yokulinganisa ebhalwe ukuthi "Amalungelo Omuntu" 

I-Plumb-pudding in Danger (1805). Umhlaba uqoshwa waba yimikhakha yethonya phakathi kukaPitt noNapoleon. NgokukaMartin Rowson, “cishe iwumdwebo opopayi wezombangazwe odume kunayo yonke ezikhathini zonke, iye yebiwa ngokuphindaphindiwe abadwebi bamakhathuni kusukela ngaleso sikhathi.”[10] 

I-Cow-Pock—noma—Imiphumela Emangalisayo Yokujova Okusha! (1802). Ikhiqizwe ngemuva kokuthi u-Edward Jenner enikeze umgomo wokuqala, umsebenzi ka-Gillray waveza ukwesaba ukuthi iziguli zazigonyelwe ingxibongo nge-cowpox ukuthi kwakuzozenza zihlume izinto ezisetshenziswa njengenkomo. 
Phakathi kokuhlekisa kuka-Gillray ngoGeorge III kukhona: Umlimi uGeorge noMkakhe, amapuleti ahamba naye amabili, kwelinye lawo inkosi ithosa ama-muffin ekudleni kwasekuseni, kanti kwelinye indlovukazi ithosa ama-sprats; Ama-Anti-Saccharites, lapho umbhangqwana wasebukhosini uhlongoza ukukhipha ushukela, ekwesabeni okukhulu komndeni; Isazi Esihlola I-Cooper; amapuleti abhanqiwe A Voluptuary under the Horrors of Digestion and Temperance ejabulela Isidlo Esihle, ehlekisa ngokweqisa kweNkosana Regent (kamuva owaba nguGeorge IV wase-United Kingdom) kanye nobuxhwanguxhwangu bukayise, uGeorge III wase-United Kingdom ngokulandelana; I-Royal Affability; Isifundo kumadombolo e-apula; kanye Nezingulube Eziphethwe.[4]

Amanye ama-caricatures ezombusazwe ahlanganisa: I-Britannia phakathi kuka-Scylla no-Charybdis, isithombe lapho u-Pitt, ovame kakhulu u-Gillray's butt, enza khona ukukhanya okuhle; Ubusuku Bomakoti; I-Apotheosis of Hoche, egxilisa ukweqisa kweNguquko YaseFrance ngombono owodwa; I-Nursery with Britannia reposing in Peace; I-Kiss Yokuqala Kule minyaka Eyishumi (1803), enye inhlekisa ngokuthula, okuthiwa yamhlekisa kakhulu uNapoleon; Umbhalo Wesandla Odongeni; I-Confederated Coalition, ukuswayipha kumfelandawonye owasusa inkonzo yase-Addington; Ukukhipha i-Old Sherry; I-Plumb-pudding esengozini (mhlawumbe umbhalo wepolitiki owaziwa kakhulu owake washicilelwa); Ukwenza Okuhloniphekile; Ukunethezeka Kombhede Wezimbali; Ukubuka kwamaHustings eCovent Garden; Phathon Alarmed; noPandora evula Ibhokisi lakhe.[4] 

Kanye nokukhuluma ngokungagwegwesi ekuphawuleni kwakhe, u-Gillray angaba nobuqili obumangalisayo, futhi abhoboze ubuze ngendlela ehlakaniphe ngendlela emangalisayo. Isibonelo esivelele salokhu ukuphrinta kweFashion Contrasts;—noma—Isicathulo esincanyana sika-The Duchess's yeilding [sic] to the Magnitude of the Duke's Foot. Lesi kwakuyisithombe esidabukisayo esiqondiswe ku-sycophancy engenangqondo eqondiswe abezindaba kuFrederica Charlotte Ulrica, u-Duchess wase-York, kanye nokubukeka kwezinyawo zakhe. Ukuphrinta kubonise kuphela izinyawo namaqakala kaDuke noDuchess base-York, besesimweni esisobala sokukopishana, izinyawo zikaDuke zikhulisiwe futhi izinyawo zamaDuchess zidwetshwe zincane kakhulu. Lokhu kuphrinta kuthulise unomphela i-sycophancy yabezindaba mayelana nenyunyana yamaDuke namaDuchess. 

Uchungechunge oluxubile lwama-caricatures, nakuba lungenakho ukubaluleka komlando wochungechunge lwezepolitiki, luqondakala kalula, futhi luyahlekisa nakakhulu. Phakathi kwezinhle kakhulu yilezi: Shakespeare Sacrificed; I-Two-Penny Whist (ebonisa isithombe sika-Hannah Humphrey); Sengathi le nyama eqine kakhulu ingancibilika; I-Sandwich-Izaqathi; I-Gout; Induduzo kuMmbila; Begone I-Dull Care; I-Cow-Pock, enikeza inkulumo ehlekisayo ekwesabeni okudumile kokugoma; I-Dilletanti Theatres; kanye Nokuvumelana Kwangaphambi Komshado Nokuvumelana Komshado—imidwebo emibili ephambene ngobudlova.[4] 

I-Flemish Characters (1793), eyanyatheliswa ngu-G. Humphrey, 27 St James's Street, 1 January 1822 
Flemish Characters (1793), eshicilelwe nguG. Humphrey, 27 St James's Street, 1 January 1822 
Flemish Characters 
 
, eshicilelwe nguG. Humphrey, 1821 January Streacters, 221 James St. nguG. Humphrey, 27 St James's Street, 1 January 1822 
Izinguqulo ezidumile 
Ukukhethwa kwemisebenzi kaGillray kwavela kuJames Gillray: The Caricatures eyanyatheliswa phakathi kuka-1818 namaphakathi nawo-1820 futhi yanyatheliswa nguJohn Miller, Bridge Street kanye noW. Blackwood, Edinburgh. Kwakhululwa izingxenye eziyisishiyagalolunye. Uhlelo olulandelayo kwaba lukaThomas McLean, olwanyatheliswa ngokhiye, ngo-1830.

Ngo-1851 uHenry George Bohn wakhipha uhlelo, olusuka emapuletini okuqala ephepheni lendlovu elihle, elinemidwebo eqinile—eyaziwa ngokuvamile ngokuthi “Amapuleti Acindezelwe”—eyanyatheliswa ngomqulu ohlukile. Kulolu hlelo uThomas Wright noRobert Harding Evans babhale ukuphawula, umlando wezikhathi ezamukelwa ama-caricatures. Amakhophi amaningi e-Bohn Edition ahlukaniswe abe amashidi ngamanye futhi adluliswa njengawokuqala (bona Ukuqoqa ngezansi). Nakuba imiqulu emibili ye-Bohn Edition ivame ukumelelwa njengeqoqo eliphelele lemisebenzi ka-Gillray, akunjalo: isibonelo, i-Doublûres of Characters ayifakiwe kunoma iyiphi ivolumu. Lokhu kungenzeka kakhulu ngoba lokhu okuphrintiwe akuzange kushicilelwe u-Hannah Humphrey, kodwa ngu-John Wright we-Anti-Jacobin Review kanye Nomagazini. 

Uhlelo olulandelayo, olunesihloko esithi The Works of James Gillray, the Caricaturist: With the Story of his Life and Times (Chatto & Windus, 1874), kwakuwumsebenzi kaThomas Wright, [11] futhi wethula uGillray emphakathini omkhulu. Lolu hlelo, oluphelele kumqulu owodwa, luqukethe izithombe ezimbili zika-Gillray, nemifanekiso engaphezu kuka-400.[4]
