Umthelela 
uGillray usahlonishwa njengomunye wabalingisi bezombangazwe abanethonya kunabo bonke abake baba khona, futhi phakathi kwabadwebi bamakhathuni abahamba phambili esigabeni sezombusazwe e-United Kingdom namuhla, bobabili uSteve Bell noMartin Rowson bayamamukela ngokuthi cishe nguyena owayenethonya elikhulu kunabo bonke ababengaphambi kwabo kuleyo nkundla ethile [catation needed]. USolwazi uDavid Taylor, uchwepheshe weNyuvesi yaseToronto kwezombangazwe, wathi ngo-2013, "Ngaphandle kokungabaza, ukube umdwebi wamakhathuni ohamba phambili ngaleso sikhathi-uJames Gillray-wayebonise uRob Ford wayezoba nesihe kakhulu kunanamuhla. 

" Umdwebi wekhathuni waseNew Zealand wangekhulu lama-20 uDavid Low uchaze uHogarth njengomkhulu futhi uGillray uyise wopopayi wezombusazwe.[3] Ubuso buka-Court Flunkey kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1980/1990s umbukiso kamabonakude kamabonakude waseBrithani ohlekisayo we-Spitting Image uyi-caricature ka-Gillray, okuhloswe ngayo ukuhlonipha ubaba womdwebi opopayi wezombusazwe.[13] 

Esihlokweni esinesihloko esithi A Rousseauian Reading of Gillray's National Conveniences uJohn Moores wabhala, "Njengoba iNational Conveniences and The Fashionable Mamma show, uGillray wayenesithakazelo emibonweni kaRousseau, umsebenzi wakhe wathonywa yiwo, futhi, njengoba imiklamo yakamuva yenguquko kanye ne-radicalism ibonisa, wabamba uRousseau ngokuhlonishwa okuphezulu kunamanye amasu okuguquguquka okuguquguqukayo. emifanekisweni yakhe yemibhalo kaRousseau.





Umdwebi wekhathuni uyiciko elibonakalayo eligxile kukho kokubili ukudweba nokubhala[1] opopayi (izithombe ngazinye) noma amahlaya (izithombe ezilandelanayo). Abadwebi bamakhathuni bayahluka kubabhali bamahlaya noma abadwebi/abaculi bamahlaya ngoba bakhiqiza kokubili izingxenye zemibhalo nezithombe zomsebenzi njengengxenye yokwenza kwabo. 

Abadwebi bamakhathuni bangase basebenze ngezindlela ezihlukahlukene, okuhlanganisa izincwajana, imidwebo yamahlaya, izincwadi zamahlaya, opopayi abahlelayo, amanoveli ayingcaca, amamanuwali, opopayi begag, amabhodi wezindaba, amaphosta, amahembe, izincwadi, izikhangiso, amakhadi emikhonzo, omagazini, amaphephandaba, amakhasi ewebhu, kanye nokupakishwa kwegeyimu yevidiyo. 

Amagama Amagama 
Bheka futhi: Umqambi Wamahlaya 
Isiyalo somdwebi wamakhathuni sihlanganisa kokubili imikhakha egunyaziwe neyokubhala [1] (bona ubuciko bemikhakha eyahlukene). Amagama athi "umdwebi wamahlaya", "umculi wamahlaya", noma "umculi wencwadi yamahlaya" abhekisele engxenyeni yokwenza izithombe yomkhakha wokudwetshwa kopopayi[2] (bona umdwebi). Nakuba wonke "umdwebi wamakhathuni" angase athathwe "njengomdwebi wamahlaya", "umculi wamahlaya", noma "umculi wencwadi yamahlaya", hhayi wonke "umdwebi wamahlaya", "umculi wamahlaya", noma "umdwebi wezincwadi zamahlaya" "umdwebi wamakhathuni". 

Ukungaqondakali kungase kuvele lapho abadwebi nababhali babelana ngemisebenzi yomunye nomunye ekugunyazeni umsebenzi.[3] 

Umlando 
Opopayi Abahleli 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ikhathuni yokuhlela 
Umdwebi wezithombe oyiNgisi kanye nomdwebi wekhathuni ongumhleli uWilliam Hogarth, owavela ekhulwini le-18, wahlekisa ngezombusazwe namasiko angaleso sikhathi; imifanekiso yesitayela esinjalo ngokuvamile ibizwa ngokuthi "iHogarthian".[4] Kulandela umsebenzi kaHogarth, opopayi bokuhlela/bezepolitiki baqala ukuthuthuka eNgilandi engxenyeni yokugcina yekhulu le-18 ngaphansi kokuqondisa kwabahlaziyi bayo abakhulu, uJames Gillray noThomas Rowlandson, bobabili baseLondon. U-Gillray wahlola ukusetshenziswa kwendlela yokwenza i-lampooning kanye ne-caricature, ebiza inkosi (uGeorge III), ondunankulu nojenene ukuba balandise, futhi uye wabizwa ngokuthi uyise wopopayi wezombusazwe.[5] 


I-Joyina, noma i-Die ka-Benjamin Franklin (May 9, 1754), ebizwa ngokuthi ikhathuni yokuqala eyanyatheliswa ephephandabeni laseMelika 
Umsuka e-US 
Nakuba engakaze abe ngumdwebi wekhathuni ochwepheshe, uBenjamin Franklin uhlonishwa ngekhathuni yokuqala eyanyatheliswa kuyi-Pennsylvania Gazette ngoMeyi 9, 1754: Joyina, noma Die, ebonisa amakoloni aseMelika njengengxenye [6].[6] Ekhulwini le-19, abadwebi bamakhathuni abangochwepheshe abanjengoThomas Nast, umsebenzi wabo owavela kuyi-Harper's Weekly, bethula ezinye izimpawu zezombangazwe zaseMelika ezaziwayo, njengendlovu yaseRiphabhulikhi.[6] 

Isiqephu samahlaya 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Isiqephu samahlaya Isithonjana 
Amahlaya 



Ingosi ye 
-vte 
Amapheshana amahlaya athole ukusatshalaliswa okusabalele emaphephandabeni avamile ngamaqembu.[8]

U-Calum MacKenzie, esanduleleni sakhe sekhathalogi yombukiso, Abadwebi Bopopayi baseScottish (Igalari Yesitudiyo Sokuphrinta I-Glasgow, 1979) bachaza indlela yokukhetha: 

Umehluko phakathi komdwebi wekhathuni nomdwebi wawufana nomehluko phakathi kosomahlaya nomlingisi wamahlaya—owokuqala bobabili baletha imigqa yabo futhi bathatha isibopho esiphelele ngenxa yabo ngaso sonke isikhathi. 
Imichilo eminingi yayiwumsebenzi wabantu ababili nakuba kwakuboniswe isiginesha eyodwa kuphela. Ngokushesha ngemva kokuba uFrank Willard eqale uMoon Mullins ngo-1923, waqasha uFerd Johnson njengomsizi wakhe. Sekungamashumi eminyaka uJohnson engatholi sikweletu. UWillard noJohnson bahamba cishe eFlorida, eMaine, eLos Angeles naseMexico, bedweba umucu ngenkathi behlala emahhotela, ezindlini nasezindlini zamapulazi. Esiqongweni sawo sokuthandwa phakathi neminyaka yawo-1940 kanye nawo-1950, lesi siqephu sasiphuma emaphephandabeni angama-350. Ngokusho kukaJohnson, ubelokhu enza i-strip solo okungenani iminyaka eyishumi ngaphambi kokufa kukaWillard ku-1958: "Babeka igama lami kuwo ngaleso sikhathi. Ngangikade ngikwenza cishe iminyaka engu-10 ngaphambi kwalokho ngoba uWillard wayenesifo senhliziyo kanye nemivimbo kanye nazo zonke lezo zinto. Umzuzu igama lami laqhubeka kuleyo nto futhi igama lakhe lahamba, amaphepha e-25 alahla umdwebo. Lokho kwakubonise ukuthi igama le-10 lisho ukuthi, nakuba iminyaka eyishumi isho lokho 









. ubuciko buyizinhlobo zobuciko ezifana nokudweba, ukudweba, ukuphrinta, ukubaza, izitsha zobumba, izithombe, ividiyo, izithombe, ukwenza amafilimu, ukuklama, imisebenzi yezandla, nezakhiwo. Imikhakha eminingi yobuciko efana nobuciko obudlalwayo, ubuciko bomqondo, nobuciko bendwangu, iphinde ibandakanye izici zobuciko obubonakalayo, kanye nobuciko bezinye izinhlobo. Ngaphakathi kwezobuciko obubonakalayo,[1] ubuciko obusetshenzisiwe,[2] obufana nedizayini yezimboni, idizayini yezithombe, idizayini yemfashini, idizayini yangaphakathi, nobuciko bokuhlobisa[3] nakho kufakiwe. 

Ukusetshenziswa kwamanje kwegama elithi "ubuciko bokubukwayo" kufaka phakathi ubuciko obuhle kanye nobuciko obusetshenzisiwe noma bokuhlobisa nemisebenzi yezandla, kodwa lokhu bekungenjalo ngaso sonke isikhathi. Ngaphambi kwe-Arts and Crafts Movement eBrithani nakwezinye izindawo ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, igama elithi 'iciko' kwase kungamakhulu eminyaka lilinganiselwe kumuntu osebenza kwezobuciko (njengokupenda, ukubaza, noma ukwenza ukuphrinta) hhayi ubuciko bokuhlobisa, imisebenzi yezandla, noma imidiya yobuciko obubonakalayo. Umehluko wagcizelelwa abaculi be-Arts and Crafts Movement, ababezazisa izinhlobo zobuciko zezilimi zomdabu ngendlela esezingeni eliphezulu.[4] Izikole zezobuciko zenze umehluko phakathi kobuciko obuhle nemisebenzi yezandla, zagcina ukuthi umuntu odwebayo wayengenakubhekwa njengomsebenzi wobuciko.

Ukuthambekela okwandayo kwelungelo lokudweba, kanye nezinga elincane lokubaza, ngaphezu kobunye ubuciko kube isici sobuciko baseNtshonalanga kanye nobuciko baseMpumalanga Asia. Kuzo zombili izifunda, ukudweba kuye kwabonwa njengokuncika ngezinga eliphezulu kakhulu emcabangweni womdwebi futhi kube yiyona esuswe kude kakhulu emsebenzini wezandla - emdwebeni waseShayina, izitayela ezaziswa kakhulu yilezo "zokudweba komfundi", okungenani ngokombono owenziwe ngabayizimfundamakhwela. Isigaba saseNtshonalanga sezinhlobo zezinhlobo sabonisa izimo zengqondo ezifanayo. 

Imfundo nokuqeqeshwa 
I-athikili eyinhloko: Imfundo yobuciko obubonakalayo 
Ukuqeqeshwa kwezobuciko obubonwayo ngokuvamile kube ngokwehlukahlukana kwezinhlelo zabafundi abafunda umsebenzi kanye nezinhlelo zokucobelelana ngolwazi. EYurophu, inhlangano yeRenaissance yokwandisa udumo lweciko yaholela ohlelweni lwezemfundo lokuqeqesha amaciko, futhi namuhla iningi labantu abaphishekela umsebenzi wokuqeqeshwa kwezobuciko ezikoleni zobuciko emazingeni emfundo ephakeme. Ubuciko obubonakalayo manje sebuphenduke isihloko esikhethwayo ezinhlelweni eziningi zemfundo.[5][6] 

E-East Asia, imfundo yobuciko yamaciko angewona umsebenzi ngokuvamile igxile ekuxubeni; i-calligraphy yayibalwa phakathi koBuciko obuyisithupha bamadoda obukhosi bakwaZhou baseShayina, futhi umbhalo we-calligraphy nomdwebo wamaShayina wawubalwa phakathi kobuciko obune bezikhulu zezazi eChina yobukhosi.[7][8][9] 

Izwe elihamba phambili ekuthuthukisweni kwezobuciko eLatin America, ngo-1875 lakha iNational Society of the Stimulus of the Arts, eyasungulwa ngabadwebi u-Eduardo Schiafino, u-Eduardo Sívori, nabanye abaculi. Inhlangano yabo yaphinde yaqashwa njengeNational Academy of Fine Arts ngo-1905 futhi, ngo-1923, ngomzamo womdwebi nomfundi u-Ernesto de la Cárcova, njengomnyango eNyuvesi yaseBuenos Aires, iSuperior Art School of the Nation. Njengamanje, inhlangano ehamba phambili yezemfundo yezobuciko ezweni yi-UNA Universidad Nacional de las Artes.[10] 

Ukudweba 
Isihloko Esiyinhloko: Ukudweba 
Umdwebo onemininingwane yeqhawe lesifazane onesihloko esithi 'Extinction' ngu-Christiaan Tonnis, owadalwa ngo-1981 ngamapensela egraphite namapensela anemibala, ukulinganisa okungu-13.6 x 18.5 amayintshi. Oka-Kunstverein Familie Montez kusukela ngo-December 2010.  
U-Christiaan Tonnis - Iqhawe Lowesifazane #14 'Extinction', ipensela nepensela enemibala ephepheni, 1981
Ukudweba kuyindlela yokwenza isithombe, umfanekiso noma umfanekiso usebenzisa noma yimaphi ahlukahlukene amathuluzi namasu atholakala ku-inthanethi futhi ungaxhunyiwe ku-inthanethi. Ngokuvamile kuhilela ukwenza amamaki endaweni engaphezulu ngokusebenzisa ingcindezi evela ethuluzini, noma ukuhambisa ithuluzi endaweni ethile kusetshenziswa imidiya eyomile njengamapensela e-graphite, ipeni noyinki, amabhulashi anoyinki, amapensela ombala we-wax, amakhrayoni, amalahle, ama-pastel, namakaki. Amathuluzi edijithali, okufaka phakathi amapeni, i-stylus, elingisa imiphumela yalezi nazo zisetshenziswa. Izindlela eziyinhloko ezisetshenziswa ekudwebeni yilezi: ukudweba umugqa, ukuchanyuselwa, ukuchanyuselwa, ukuchanyuselwa okungahleliwe, ukufiphaza, ukuklwebha, ukugoqa, nokuhlanganisa. Umdwebi owenza kahle kakhulu ekudwebeni ubizwa ngokuthi umdwebi noma umdwebi.[11]
 
Ukudweba nokudweba kuhlehlela emuva emashumini ezinkulungwane zeminyaka.[12] Ubuciko be-Upper Paleolithic buhlanganisa ubuciko obungokomfanekiso obuqala okungenani eminyakeni engu-40,000 edlule.[13] Imidwebo emigedeni engeyona engokomfanekiso ehlanganisa ama-stencil ezandla kanye nokwakheka kwejiyomethri elula midala nakakhulu.[12] Izethulo zomhume wePaleolithic wezilwane zitholakala ezindaweni ezifana neLascaux, France, Altamira, Spain, [14] Maros, Sulawesi e-Asia,[15] naseGabarnmung, Australia.[16] 

EGibhithe lasendulo, imidwebo kayinki ku-papyrus, ngokuvamile ebonisa abantu, yayisetshenziswa njengezibonelo zokudweba noma ukubaza.[17] Imidwebo yamavazi esiGreki, ekuqaleni kwejiyomethri, kamuva yathuthukiswa yaba sesimweni somuntu ngezitsha zobumba ezinomfanekiso omnyama phakathi nekhulu lesi-6 BC.[18] 

Njengoba iphepha selivame kakhulu eYurophu ngekhulu le-14, [19] umdwebo wamukelwa ongcweti abafana noSandro Botticelli, uRaphael, uMichelangelo, noLeonardo da Vinci, ngezinye izikhathi ababephatha ukudweba njengobuciko ngokwabo, kunokuba kube yisiteji sokulungiselela ukudweba noma ukuqopha.[20] 

Ukupenda 
I-athikili Eyinhloko: Ukupenda 
Umdwebo othathwe njengoba unjalo umkhuba wokufaka umbala wombala olengiswe kusithwali (noma okuphakathi) kanye ne-ejenti ebophayo (ingcina) endaweni (okusekela) njengephepha, indwangu noma udonga. Kodwa-ke, uma kusetshenziswa ngomqondo wobuciko kusho ukusetshenziswa kwalo msebenzi uhlanganiswe nomdwebo, ukwakheka, noma okunye ukucatshangelwa kobuhle ukuze kubonakale inhloso ecacile nenengqondo yomsebenzisi. Ukudweba kusetshenziselwa ukuveza izinhloso nemibono engokomoya; amasayithi alolu hlobo lwemidwebo asukela emisebenzini yobuciko ebonisa imifanekiso yezinganekwane ezitsheni zobumba kuya eThe Sistine Chapel, kuya emzimbeni womuntu ngokwawo.[21] 

Umlando 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umlando wokudweba 
Umsuka kanye nomlando wakuqala 

Umdwebo we-Lascaux u- 

Nefertari no-Isis 
Njengomdwebo, ukudweba kunemvelaphi yakho ebhaliwe emigedeni nasebusweni bamadwala.[22] Imidwebo yakudala eyaziwayo yasemhumeni, ephakathi kweminyaka engu-32,000-30,000 edlule, itholakala emhumeni wase-Chauvet eningizimu yeFrance;[23] imidwebo yasendongeni ye-polychrome edumile yaseLascaux isukela eminyakeni engaba ngu-17,000–15,500 edlule.[24] Emithunzini ebomvu, ensundu, ephuzi nemnyama, imidwebo esezindongeni nosilingi iveza inyamazane, izinkomo (ama-auroch), amahhashi nezinyamazane.[25] 

Imidwebo yemifanekiso yabantu ingatholakala emathuneni aseGibhithe lasendulo. Ethempelini elikhulu likaRamesses II, uNefertari, indlovukazi yakhe, uboniswa eholwa u-Isis.[26] AmaGreki aba nesandla ekudwebeni kodwa umsebenzi wawo omningi ulahlekile. Esinye sezethulo ezihamba phambili ezisele yizithombe zomama ze-Hellenistic Fayum. Esinye isibonelo siwumfanekiso we-Battle of Issus ePompeii, okungenzeka wawusekelwe emdwebeni wamaGreki. Ubuciko bamaGreki namaRoma baba nesandla ebucikweni baseByzantium ngekhulu lesi-4 BC, obaqala isiko lokudweba imifanekiso.[27] Isihloko esikhulu 

seRenaissance 
: Umdwebo we-Italian Renaissance
Ngaphandle kwemibhalo yesandla ekhanyisiwe eyakhiqizwa izindela phakathi neNkathi Ephakathi, umnikelo olandelayo obalulekile kwezobuciko baseYurophu wawuvela kubadwebi bokuvuselela kabusha base-Italy. Kusukela e-Giotto ngekhulu le-13 kuya kuLeonardo da Vinci kanye no-Raphael ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-16, lesi kwakuyinkathi ecebe kakhulu kwezobuciko base-Italy njengoba amasu e-chiaroscuro asetshenziswa ukudala inkohliso yesikhala esingu-3-D.[28] 

Abadwebi basenyakatho yeYurophu nabo bathonywa isikole sase-Italy. U-Jan van Eyck waseBelgium, u-Pieter Bruegel Omdala wase-Netherlands kanye no-Hans Holbein Omncane wase-Germany baphakathi kwabadwebi abaphumelele kakhulu bezikhathi. Basebenzise inqubo yokucwebezela ngamafutha ukuze bathole ukujula nokukhanya. 

Ochwepheshe base-Dutch 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Umdwebo we-Dutch Golden Age 
Umdwebo ka-Rembrandt Ebusuku Buka amadoda amabili eqhubekela phambili nesixuku 
Rembrandt: I-Night Watch, 1642 
Ikhulu le-17 labona ukuvela kwezingcweti ezinkulu zama-Dutch ezifana no-Rembrandt oguquguqukayo owakhunjulwa kakhulu ngezithombe zakhe nezigcawu zeBhayibheli, kanye no-Vermeer owayenezigcawu ezikhethekile zokuphila zaseDutch. 

I-Baroque 
Main article: I-Baroque 
I-Baroque yaqala ngemva kweRenaissance, kusukela ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-16 kuya ekupheleni kwekhulu le-17. Abaculi abakhulu beBaroque bahlanganisa uCaravaggio, owasebenzisa kakhulu i-tenebrism. UPeter Paul Rubens, umdwebi waseFlemish owafunda e-Italy, wasebenzela amasonto endawo e-Antwerp futhi wapenda uchungechunge lukaMarie de' Medici. U-Annibale Carracci wathatha amathonya e-Sistine Chapel futhi wadala uhlobo lomdwebo owenziwe ngophahla ongekho emthethweni. Intuthuko enkulu eyenzeka eBaroque yayingenxa yeNguquko YamaProthestani kanye nomphumela we-Counter Reformation. Okuningi okuchaza i-Baroque ukukhanya okumangalisayo kanye nokubonwayo okuphelele.[29] 

Impressionism 
Isihloko esikhulu: Impressionism 
I-Post-impressionism 
Isihloko esikhulu: I-Post-Impressionism

UClaude Monet: Impression, Sunrise (1872) 
Impressionism yaqala eFrance ngekhulu le-19 ngenhlangano exegayo yamaciko ahlanganisa uClaude Monet, Pierre-Auguste Renoir noPaul Cézanne abaletha isitayela esisha esixutshwe ngokukhululekile ekupendeni, ngokuvamile ekhetha ukudweba izigcawu ezingokoqobo zempilo yesimanje ngaphandle kunestudiyo. Lokhu kwafezwa ngokuvezwa okusha kwezici zobuhle ezikhonjiswe ngokushaywa kwamabhulashi kanye nombono weqiniso. Bazuze ukudlidliza kombala okunamandla ngokusebenzisa imibala emsulwa, engaxutshiwe kanye nemivimbo yebhulashi emifushane. Ukunyakaza kube nomthelela wobuciko njengento eguquguqukayo, ehamba phakathi nesikhathi nokulungisa amasu amasha kanye nombono wobuciko. Ukunaka imininingwane kuye kwaba yinto ehamba phambili ekufezeni, ngenkathi kuhlolwa umbono ochemile wezindawo nemvelo iso leciko.[30][31] 

Ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19, abadwebi abaningana abasebasha baqhubekisela phambili i-impressionism, besebenzisa amafomu ejiyomethri nombala ongewona owemvelo ukukhombisa imizwa kuyilapho belwela ukuthola izimpawu ezijulile. Okuphawuleka ngokukhethekile uPaul Gauguin, owathonywa kakhulu ubuciko base-Asia, e-Afrika naseJapane, uVincent van Gogh, umDashi owathuthela eFrance lapho adweba khona ukukhanya kwelanga okunamandla eningizimu, noToulouse-Lautrec, akhunjulwa ngemidwebo yakhe ecacile yokuphila ebusuku esifundeni saseParis saseMontmartre.[32] 

I-Symbolism, i-expressionism kanye ne-cubism 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ubuciko besimanje 
u-Edvard Munch, umdwebi waseNorway, wasungula indlela yakhe engokomfanekiso ekupheleni kwekhulu le-19, egqugquzelwa i-French impressionist uManet. I-Scream (1893), umsebenzi wakhe odume kakhulu, uhunyushwa kabanzi ngokuthi umele ukukhathazeka kwendawo yonke yomuntu wanamuhla. Ngokwengxenye ngenxa yethonya likaMunch, inhlangano yokukhuluma yaseJalimane yaqala eJalimane ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20 njengoba abaculi abafana no-Ernst Kirschner no-Erich Heckel baqala ukuhlanekezela iqiniso ngomphumela womzwelo. 

Ngokuhambisanayo, isitayela esaziwa ngokuthi i-cubism sathuthukiswa e-France njengamaciko agxile kumthamo nesikhala sezakhiwo ezibukhali ngaphakathi kokuqanjwa. UPablo Picasso noGeorges Braque babengabasekeli abahamba phambili bale nhlangano. Izinto ziyahlukaniswa, zihlaziywe, futhi zihlanganiswe kabusha ngendlela efingqiwe. Ngawo-1920, lesi sitayela sase sithuthuke saba yi-surrealism ngo-Dali kanye no-Magritte.[33] 

Ukuphrinta 
Isihloko Esiyinhloko: Ukwenza Ukuphrinta 
Umbhalo oqoshiwe waseShayina wasendulo wabadlali bezinsimbi besifazane 
Umbhalo wasendulo waseShayina wabadlali bezinsimbi besifazane 
Ukwenza ukuphrinta kudala, ngezinjongo zobuciko, isithombe ku-matrix esidluliselwa endaweni enezinhlangothi ezimbili (eyisicaba) ngoyinki noma enye indlela yokwenza umbala.[34] Ngaphandle esimweni se-monotype, i-matrix efanayo ingasetshenziswa ukukhiqiza izibonelo eziningi zokuphrinta.[35]

Ngokomlando, amasu amakhulu (abuye abizwe ngokuthi imidiya) ahilelekile ukuqoshwa kokhuni,[36] ukuqoshwa komugqa,[37] etching,[38] lithography,[39] nokuphrinta isikrini,[40] (serigraphy, ukuhlola usilika) futhi kukhona nezinye eziningi, kuhlanganise namasu edijithali.[41] Ngokujwayelekile, okuphrintiwe kuphrintwa ephepheni,[19] kodwa ezinye izisetshenziswa zisukela endwangu kanye nevellum,[42] kuye ezintweni zesimanjemanje.[43] 
 
Umlando waseYurophu 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukuphrinta okuyinhloko kwakudala
Amaphrinti esiko laseNtshonalanga akhiqizwa ngaphambi kuka-1830 aziwa ngokuthi ama-master prints amadala. EYurophu, kusukela cishe ku-1400 AD, ukuqoshwa kwezinkuni, kwakusetshenziselwa ukuphrinta okuhle ephepheni kusetshenziswa amasu okuphrinta athuthukiswe emhlabeni waseByzantine kanye namaSulumane. UMichael Wolgemut wenza ngcono i-woodcut yaseJalimane kusukela cishe ngo-1475, kanti u-Erhard Reuwich, umDashi, waba ngowokuqala ukusebenzisa i-cross-hatching. Ekupheleni kwekhulu leminyaka u-Albrecht Dürer waletha umhume waseNtshonalanga esigabeni esingakaze sidlulwe, ekhulisa isimo sokunqunywa kweqabunga elilodwa.[44] 

Umsuka nokusebenza kwamaShayina 
I-Chinese Diamond Sutra, incwadi yokunyathelisa ye-Woodblock endala kunazo zonke emhlabeni kusukela ngo-868 CE 
I-Chinese Diamond Sutra, incwadi endala kunazo zonke emhlabeni enyathelisiwe (868 CE) 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukunyathelisa kwe-Woodblock 
E-China, ubuciko bokwenza amaphrinta bathuthukiswa eminyakeni engaba ngu-1,100 edlule njengemifanekiso ehambisana nombhalo osikwe ezigxotsheni ukuze unyatheliswe ephepheni. Ekuqaleni izithombe zazingokwenkolo kodwa ebukhosini beNgoma, abaculi baqala ukusika izindawo. Phakathi nezizukulwane ze-Ming (1368-1644) kanye ne-Qing (1616-1911), le ndlela yapheleliswa kukho kokubili okuqoshiwe kwezenkolo nokobuciko.[45][46] 

Ukuthuthukiswa e-Japan, 1603–1867 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukuphrinta kwe-Woodblock e-Japan 
Hokusai color print "i-Red Fuji yaseningizimu umoya ocwebile ekuseni" kusukela Emibukweni Engamashumi Amathathu Nesithupha yeMount Fuji 
Hokusai: I-Fuji Ebomvu kusukela Emibukweni Engamashumi Amathathu Nesithupha e-Mount Fuji (1830–1832) 
I-Woodblock printing eJapane, i-Hakunga yaseJapane inqubo eyaziwa kakhulu ngokusetshenziswa kwayo ohlotsheni lwezobuciko ukiyo-e; nokho, yabuye yasetshenziswa kabanzi ekunyatheliseni izincwadi ezinemifanekiso ngaleso sikhathi. Ukunyathelisa kwe-Woodblock kwakusetshenziswe eShayina amakhulu eminyaka ukuphrinta izincwadi, kudala ngaphambi kokufika kwezinhlobo ezinyakazayo, kodwa kwamukelwa kabanzi eJapane ngesikhathi se-Edo (1603-1867).[47][48] Nakuba ifana nokusika ukhuni ekunyatheliseni okusentshonalanga kokunye, i-moku hanga ihluke kakhulu ngokuthi i-inki esekelwe emanzini isetshenziswa (ngokungafani ne-Western woodcut, esebenzisa i-inks esekelwe uwoyela), okuvumela ububanzi bombala ogqamile, ukucwebezela kanye nokubonakala kombala.
 
Ngemuva kokuncipha kwe-ukiyo-e kanye nokwethulwa kobuchwepheshe bokuphrinta besimanje, ukuphrinta kwe-woodblock kwaqhubeka njengendlela yokunyathelisa imibhalo kanye nokukhiqiza ubuciko, kokubili ngaphakathi kwezindlela zendabuko ezifana ne-ukiyo-e kanye nezinhlobonhlobo zezindlela eziqinile noma zaseNtshonalanga ezingase zithathwe njengobuciko besimanje. Ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, i-shin-hanga eyahlanganisa isiko le-ukiyo-e nezindlela zemidwebo yaseNtshonalanga yaduma, futhi imisebenzi ka-Hasui Kawase kanye no-Hiroshi Yoshida yazuza ukuduma emhlabeni wonke.[49][50] Izikhungo ezifana ne-"Adachi Institute of Woodblock Prints" kanye ne-"Takezasado" ziyaqhubeka nokukhiqiza ukuphrinta kwe-ukiyo-e ngezinto nezindlela ezifanayo ezasetshenziswa esikhathini esidlule.[51][52] 

Ukuthatha izithombe 
Isihloko esikhulu: Izithombe
Ukuthatha izithombe kuyinqubo yokwenza izithombe ngokwenza ukukhanya. Amaphethini okukhanya aboniswa noma akhishwa ezintweni aqoshwa endaweni ebucayi, noma i-chip yesitoreji, ngokuchayeka okunesikhathi.[53] Inqubo yenziwa ngezivalo zemishini[54] noma ukuchayeka ngesikhathi ngekhompuyutha kwamafotoni emshinini wokucubungula amakhemikhali noma emishinini yokwenza idijithali eyaziwa ngokuthi amakhamera.[55] 

Igama livela kwelesiGreki elithi φῶς ''phos'' (“ukukhanya”) kanye no-γραφή ''graphê'' (“ukudweba” noma “ukubhala”), ngokwezwi nezwi okusho “ukudweba ngokukhanya”.[56] Ngokwesiko, umkhiqizo wokuthatha izithombe ubizwa ngokuthi isithombe; igama elithi ''isithombe'' liyisifinyezo futhi nakuba abaningi bezibiza ngokuthi “izithombe,” igama elithi “isithombe” seliya ngokuya lithatha indawo “yesithombe,” ebonisa ukuthwebula nge-elekthronikhi kanye nomqondo obanzi wokumelwa kwesithombe ku-optics nakukhompyutha.[57] 

I-Architecture 
Bheka futhi: Uhlu lwesofthiwe ye-BIM 

Izindlu ezinohlaka lwe-Timber e-Brittany 
Architecture yinqubo kanye nomkhiqizo wokuhlela, ukuklama, nokwakha izakhiwo nanoma yiziphi ezinye izakhiwo.[58] Imisebenzi yezakhiwo, ngendlela yezakhiwo, ivame ukubonwa njengezimpawu zamasiko nemisebenzi yobuciko.[59] Izimpucuko zomlando zivame ukuhlotshaniswa nempumelelo yazo esekhona yezakhiwo.[60] 

Umsebenzi obhaliwe wokuqala osekhona wezokwakha yi-De architectura, eyabhalwa umakhi waseRoma u-Vitruvius ekuqaleni kwekhulu lokuqala AD.[61] NgokukaVitruvius, isakhiwo esihle kufanele senelise izimiso ezintathu: firmitas, utilitas, venustas, okuhunyushwa ngokuthi ukuqina, impahla, kanye nenjabulo.[62] Okulingana nesiNgisi sesimanje kungaba: 

Ukuqina - isakhiwo kufanele siqine futhi sihlale sisesimweni esihle. 
Utility - kufanele ilungele izinhloso ezisetshenziselwa zona.  
Ubuhle - kufanele bube buhle ngobuhle.[63]
Ukwakha kuqale kwavela ekushintshashintsheni phakathi kwezidingo (indawo yokuhlala, ukuvikeleka, ukukhonza, njll.) kanye nezindlela (izinto zokwakha ezitholakalayo namakhono omsizi).[64] Njengoba amasiko athuthukile nolwazi luqala ukwenziwa lube semthethweni ngamasiko nezinqubo zomlomo, ukwakha kwaba ubuciko, futhi “izakhiwo” yigama elinikezwa izinguqulo ezisemthethweni kakhulu zalowo msebenzi.[65] 

Ukwenziwa Kwefilimu 
Isihloko Esiyinhloko: 
Ukwenziwa Kwefilimu Ukwenza ifilimu kuyinqubo yokwenza isithombe esinyakazayo, kusukela ekuqanjweni kokuqala kanye nocwaningo, ngokubhala umbhalo, ukuthwebula nokuqoshwa, ukugqwayiza noma eminye imiphumela ekhethekile, ukuhlela, umsebenzi womsindo nomculo futhi ekugcineni ukusabalalisa izethameli; isho kabanzi ekwakhiweni kwazo zonke izinhlobo zamafilimu, ahlanganisa idokhumentari, izinhlobo zetiyetha nezincwadi zefilimu, kanye nemikhuba yobunkondlo noma yokuhlola, futhi ngokuvamile isetshenziselwa ukubhekisela nasezinqubweni ezisekelwe kuvidiyo. 

Ubuciko bekhompyutha 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ubuciko bekhompyutha 
Bheka futhi: Ubuciko bedijithali 

u-Desmond Paul Henry, Isithombe Ngomshini Wokudweba 1, c. 1960
Amaciko abonakalayo awasagcini kumidiya yezobuciko obubonakalayo bendabuko. Amakhompiyutha asetshenziswe kwezobuciko bokubukwa kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1960.[66] Ukusetshenziswa kuhlanganisa ukuthwebula noma ukudala izithombe namafomu,[67] ukuhlelwa kwalezo zithombe (okuhlanganisa nokuhlola okuqanjwe okuningi)[68] kanye nokukhishwa kokugcina noma ukuphrinta (okuhlanganisa ukuphrinta kwe-3D).[69] 

Ubuciko bekhompiyutha yinoma yibuphi amakhompiyutha adlala indima ekukhiqizeni noma ekubonisweni.[70] Ubuciko obunjalo bungaba isithombe, umsindo, opopayi, ividiyo, i-CD-ROM, i-DVD, umdlalo wevidiyo, iwebhusayithi, i-algorithm, ukusebenza noma ukufakwa kwegalari.[71] 

Imikhakha eminingi yendabuko manje ihlanganisa ubuchwepheshe bedijithali, ngakho imigqa phakathi kwemisebenzi yobuciko evamile nemisebenzi emisha yemidiya edalwe kusetshenziswa amakhompuyutha ayicaciswanga.[72] Isibonelo, umdwebi angase ahlanganise umdwebo wendabuko nobuciko be-algorithmic nezinye izindlela zedijithali.[73] Ngenxa yalokho, ukuchaza ubuciko bekhompiyutha ngomkhiqizo wayo wokugcina kungaba nzima. Noma kunjalo, lolu hlobo lobuciko luvela emibukisweni yasemnyuziyamu yobuciko, kodwa lungabonakala njengethuluzi, kunokuba lubonakale njengomdwebo.[74] Ngakolunye uhlangothi, kukhona imisebenzi yobuciko esekelwe kukhompuyutha eyingxenye yomqondo omusha kanye ne-postdigital strand, ethatha ubuchwepheshe obufanayo, nomthelela wayo kumphakathi, njengento yophenyo.[75] 

Ukusetshenziswa kwekhompyutha kufiphaze umehluko phakathi kwabadwebi bezithombe, abathwebuli bezithombe, abahleli bezithombe, abamodela be-3-D, nabaculi bezandla.[76] Isofthiwe esezingeni eliphezulu yokunikezela nokuhlela iholele kubathuthukisi bezithombe abanamakhono amaningi. Abathwebuli bezithombe bangase babe amaciko edijithali.[77] Abadwebi bangase babe opopayi. Imisebenzi yezandla ingase isize ngekhompyutha noma isebenzise izithombe ezikhiqizwe ngekhompuyutha njengesifanekiso.[78] Ukusetshenziswa kobuciko beziqeshana zekhompiyutha kwenze umehluko phakathi kobuciko obubonakalayo nesakhiwo sekhasi ungabi sobala ngenxa yokufinyelela kalula nokuhlela ubuciko bokunamathisela ohlelweni lokuphega umbhalo.[79] 

Ubuciko bePlastiki  
Isihloko esikhulu: Ubuciko bePlastiki
Ubuciko bepulasitiki yitemu lezinhlobo zobuciko ezibandakanya ukukhohliswa ngokomzimba kwendawo yepulasitiki ngokuyibumba noma ukwenza imodeli efana nokubaza noma izitsha zobumba. Leli gama liphinde lasetshenziswa kukho konke ubuciko obubonwayo (obungabhalwanga, obungezona ezomculo).[80][81] 

Izinto ezingaqoshwa noma ezilolongekile, njengetshe, ukhuni, ukhonkolo, noma insimbi, nazo ziye zafakwa encazelweni encane, njengoba, ngamathuluzi afanele, izinto ezinjalo nazo ziyakwazi ukushintshashintsha.[82] Lokhu kusetshenziswa kwegama elithi “ipulasitiki” kwezobuciko kwehlukile ekusetshenzisweni kukaPiet Mondrian, futhi nangomnyakazo awubiza ngokuthi, “Neoplasticism.”[83][84] 

Sculpture 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukuqopha
Ukubaza kungumsebenzi wobuciko onezinhlangothi ezintathu odalwe ngokubumba noma ukuhlanganisa izinto eziqinile noma zepulasitiki, umsindo, noma umbhalo kanye noma ukukhanya, ngokuvamile itshe (kungaba idwala noma imabula), ubumba, insimbi, ingilazi, noma ukhuni. Eminye imifanekiso idalwe ngokuqondile ngokuthola noma ngokubaza; ezinye ziyaqoqwa, zakhiwe ndawonye futhi zishiswe, zishiselwe, zibunjwe, noma ziphonswe. Izithombe zivame ukupendiwa.[85] Umuntu owenza izithombe eziqoshiwe ubizwa ngokuthi umqophi. 

Izibonelo zokuqala ezingenakuphikiswa zezithombe eziqoshiwe zingezamasiko e-Aurignacian, eyayitholakala eYurophu naseningizimu-ntshonalanga ye-Asia futhi isebenza ekuqaleni kwe-Upper Paleolithic. Kanye nokukhiqiza ubuciko bakudala obaziwayo bomhume, abantu balesi siko benza amathuluzi amatshe aklanywe kahle, imihlobiso elengayo, amasongo, ubuhlalu bezinyo lendlovu, nemitshingo yamathambo, kanye nemifanekiso enezinhlangothi ezintathu.[86][87][88] 

Ngenxa yokuthi ukudweba kuhilela ukusetshenziswa kwezinto ezingabunjwa noma zilungiswe, kubhekwa njengenye yobuciko bepulasitiki. Iningi lobuciko bomphakathi i-sculpture. Izithombe eziningi eziqoshiwe ndawonye endaweni yasengadini zingase zibizwe ngokuthi ingadi ebaziwe. Abaqophi abazenzi ngaso sonke isikhathi izithombe eziqoshiwe ngesandla. Ngobuchwepheshe obukhulayo ekhulwini lama-20 kanye nokuduma kobuciko bomqondo ngaphezu kobuciko bobuchwepheshe, abaqophi abaningi baphendukela kubakhi bobuciko ukuze bakhiqize imisebenzi yabo yobuciko. Ngokwenziwa, umdwebi udala idizayini futhi akhokhele umenzi ukuthi awukhiqize. Lokhu kuvumela abaqophi ukuthi benze izithombe eziqoshiwe ezinkulu neziyinkimbinkimbi ngezinto ezifana nosimende, insimbi nepulasitiki, abangeke bakwazi ukuzidala ngesandla. Izithombe zingenziwa futhi ngobuchwepheshe bokuphrinta be-3-d. 

Incazelo ye-copyright yase-US yobuciko obubonakalayo 
E-United States, umthetho ovikela ilungelo lobunikazi phezu kocezu lobuciko obubonakalayo unikeza incazelo ekhawulelwe kakhulu "yobuciko obubonakalayo".[89] 

"Umsebenzi wobuciko obubonakalayo" uwu — 
(1) umdwebo, umdwebo, ukuphrinta noma ukubaza, okukhona ekhophini eyodwa, kuhlelo olulinganiselwe lwamakhophi angama-200 noma ngaphansi asayinwe futhi afakwe izinombolo ngokulandelana ngumbhali, noma, esimweni sokubaza, ekubunjweni okuningi, okuqoshiwe, noma okuqoshiwe okuqoshiwe okubhaliwe noma okubhaliwe okumbalwa noma okubhaliwe okubhaliwe noma okubhaliwe okubhaliwe noma okubhaliwe okumbalwa noma okusayiniwe olunye uphawu olukhomba umbhali; noma
(2) isithombe esinganyakazi esikhiqizwe ngezinhloso zombukiso kuphela, esikhona ekhophini eyodwa esayinwe umbhali, noma kushicilelo olulinganiselwe lwamakhophi angama-200 noma ambalwa asayinwe futhi afakwe izinombolo ngokulandelana ngumbhali. 

Umsebenzi wobuciko obubonakalayo awubandakanyi — 
(A)(i) noma iyiphi iphosta, imephu, iglowubhu, ishadi, umdwebo wobuchwepheshe, idayagramu, imodeli, ubuciko obusetshenziswayo, isithombe esinyakazayo noma omunye umsebenzi wokulalelwayo nokubukwayo, incwadi, iphephabhuku, iphephandaba, isizindalwazi, isevisi yolwazi lwe-elekthronikhi, ukushicilela ngogesi, noma ukushicilelwa okufanayo; 
  (ii) noma iyiphi into edayiswayo noma ukukhangisa, ukukhangisa, okuchazayo, okumbozayo, noma okupakishwayo noma okokufaka; 
  (iii) noma iyiphi ingxenye noma ingxenye yanoma iyiphi into echazwe esigatshaneni (i) noma (ii); 
(B) noma yimuphi umsebenzi owenzelwe ukuqashwa; noma 
(C) noma yimuphi umsebenzi ongekho ngaphansi kokuvikelwa kwe-copyright ngaphansi kwalesi sihloko.[89] 


Amahlaya yindlela esetshenziswa ukuveza imibono ngezithombe, evamise ukuhlanganiswa nombhalo noma olunye ulwazi olubukwayo. Ngokuvamile kuthatha uhlobo lokulandelana kwamaphaneli ezithombe. Amathuluzi ombhalo njengamabhaluni enkulumo, amagama-ncazo, ne-onomatopoeia angabonisa ingxoxo, ukulandisa, imiphumela yomsindo, noma olunye ulwazi. Akukho ukuvumelana phakathi kwama-theorists kanye nezazi-mlando mayelana nencazelo yamahlaya; ezinye zigcizelela inhlanganisela yezithombe nombhalo, ukulandelana okuthile noma okunye ubudlelwano bezithombe, nezinye izici zomlando ezifana nokuzalaniswa ngobuningi noma ukusetshenziswa kwezinhlamvu eziphindaphindayo. Ukwenza opopayi nezinye izinhlobo zemifanekiso kuyindlela evame kakhulu yokwenza izithombe kumahlaya. Amakhomikhi ezithombe yifomu elisebenzisa izithombe zezithombe. Amafomu ajwayelekile ahlanganisa imidwebo yamahlaya, opopayi bokuhlela kanye ne-gag, nezincwadi zamahlaya. Kusukela ngasekupheleni kwekhulu lama-20, amavolumu ahlanganisiwe afana namanoveli wezithombe, nama-albhamu amahlaya, ayanda kakhulu, kanye nama-webcomics.
 
Umlando wamahlaya ulandele izindlela ezahlukene emasikweni ahlukene. Izazi zenze umlando wangaphambi kwesikhathi emuva njengemidwebo yomhume waseLascaux. Maphakathi nekhulu lama-20, amahlaya adlondlobele, ikakhulukazi e-United States, entshonalanga yeYurophu (ikakhulukazi iFrance neBelgium) naseJapane. Umlando wamahlaya ase-Europe uvame ukulandelelwa emidwebeni yopopayi ka-Rodolphe Töpffer yama-1830s, kuyilapho u-Wilhelm Busch kanye no-Max wakhe no-Moritz nabo baba nomthelela emhlabeni wonke kusukela ngo-1865 kuqhubeke,[1][2][3][4] futhi baduma ngemva kwempumelelo ngeminyaka yawo-1930 yemigqa nezincwadi ezifana nethi The Adventures of Tintin. Amakhomikhi aseMelika avela njengengxenye enkulu ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20 ngokufika kwamapheshana amahlaya ephephandaba; izincwadi zamahlaya zohlobo lomagazini zalandelwa ngawo-1930, futhi uhlobo lweqhawe elivelele lwagqama ngemva kokuvela kukaSuperman ngo-1938. Imilando yamahlaya aseJapane (manga) iphakamisa imvelaphi ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-12. Amahlaya aseJapane ngokuvamile aphethwe ngokwehlukana nokuvela kwamahlaya ase-Euro-American, futhi ubuciko bamahlaya baseNtshonalanga cishe bavela e-Italy yekhulu le-17.[5] Imidwebo yamahlaya yaseJapane yanamuhla yavela ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, futhi ukukhishwa komagazini bamahlaya nezincwadi kwanda ngokushesha enkathini yangemva kweMpi Yezwe II (1945)– ngokuduma kwabadwebi bamakhathuni abafana no-Osamu Tezuka. Amahlaya abe nedumela eliphansi ngomlando wawo omningi, kodwa ngasekupheleni kwekhulu lama-20, aqala ukuthola ukwamukelwa okukhulu emphakathini nasezifundiswa. 

Igama lesiNgisi elithi amahlaya lisetshenziswa njengebizo elisebunyeni uma libhekisela esimweni ngokwaso (isb. "Amahlaya ayindlela yobuciko obubonakalayo."), kodwa njengobuningi lapho kubhekiselwa emisebenzini ngokuhlangene (isb. "Amahlaya ayizinto zokufunda ezidumile."). 

Imvelaphi namasiko

The Yellow Kid

Amasiko amahlaya ase-Europe, American, and Japanese alandele izindlela ezahlukene.[6] Abantu baseYurophu babone isiko labo njengeliqala ngo-Swiss Rodolphe Töpffer kusukela ekuqaleni kwawo-1827 futhi abantu baseMelika babone umsuka wabo emgqeni wephephandaba lika-Richard F. Outcault's 1890s, i-Yellow Kid, nakuba abantu abaningi baseMelika sebebona ukundulela kuka-Töpffer. U-Wilhelm Busch waba nomthelela ngokuqondile u-Rudolph Dirks kanye ne-Katzenjammer Kids yakhe.[7][8][9][10][11] I-Japan inomlando omude wezithombe ezihlekisayo namahlaya aholela enkathini yeMpi Yezwe II. Umdwebi we-ukiyo-e u-Hokusai wenza ukuthi igama lesi-Japanese lamahlaya nokudwetshwa kwekhathuni, i-manga, lidume ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19.[12] Ngawo-1930 u-Harry "A" Chesler waqala isitudiyo samahlaya, okwathi ekuphakameni kwaso saqasha amaciko angu-40 asebenzela abashicileli abahlukene abangu-50 abasiza ukwenza amahlaya aphumelele "nge-Golden Age of Comics" ngemva kweMpi Yezwe II.[13] Enkathini yangemva kwempi amahlaya esimanje aseJapane aqala ukuchuma lapho u-Osamu Tezuka ekhiqiza indikimba yemisebenzi eningi.[14] Ngasekupheleni kwekhulu lama-20, lawa masiko amathathu ahlangana ngendlela ebheke kumahlaya obude bencwadi: i-albhamu yamahlaya eYurophu, i-tankōbon[a] e-Japan, kanye nenoveli eyingcaca emazweni akhuluma isiNgisi.[6] 

Ngaphandle kwalezi zinhlu zozalo, osolwazi bamahlaya kanye nezazi-mlando baye babona izethulo zamahlaya emidwebeni yaseLascaux emigedeni [15] eFrance (eminye yayo ebonakala ilandelana ngokulandelana kwezithombe), imibhalo yasendulo yaseGibhithe, Ikholomu kaTrajan eRoma,[16] i-11th-century 370707 Tarasnis, Norman7 I-Protat woodcut, i-Ars moriendi ne-block yekhulu le-15, incwadi kaMichelangelo ethi The Last Judgment in the Sistine Chapel, [16] kanye nemibhalo eqoshiwe elandelanayo ka-William Hogarth yangekhulu le-18,[18] phakathi kokunye.[16][b] 

Umhlobiso omude kakhulu ohlotshiswe ngendwangu waseNgilandi ohola izehlakalo zendwangu yaseNgilandi ebonisa imicimbi yendwangu. 
Ama-Theorists aphikisana ngokuthi i-Bayeux Tapestry iyisandulela samahlaya. 
Amahlaya olimi lwesiNgisi 

"Umsindo othukuthele phakathi kobudlelwano bobungani" - Ukuphrinta okuhlekisayo kwezepolitiki ezungeze i-Caroline Affair (1840-1841) 

Endlini yengulube yokubhala. 
I-Upside Downs ye-Little Lady Lovekins kanye ne-Old Man Muffaroo, amahlaya ka-Gustave Verbeek aqukethe izibalo ezihlehliswayo kanye nemisho ye-ambigram (March 1904). 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Amahlaya waseBrithani, Umlando Wamahlaya aseMelika, kanye nencwadi yamahlaya yaseMelika
Amaphephandaba ahlekisayo anezithombe ayedumile eBrithani yekhulu le-19, eyokuqala yawo kwakuyi-Glasgow Looking Glass eyahlala isikhashana ngo-1825.[20] Eyaziwa kakhulu kwakuyi-Punch, [21] eyaduma igama elithi ikhathuni ngama-caricatures ahlekisayo.[22] Kwesinye isikhathi amakhathuni kulawa magazini ayevela ngokulandelana;[21] umlingiswa u-Ally Sloper owavela emculweni wamahlaya ochungechunge wakudala lapho umlingisi eqala ukubonakala kumagazini wakhe wamasonto onke ngo-1884.[23]

Amahlaya aseMelika avela komagazini abanjengePuck, Judge, neLife. Ukuphumelela kwezithasiselo zamahlaya anezithombe ku-New York World futhi kamuva ne-New York American, ikakhulukazi i-Outcault's The Yellow Kid, kuholele ekuthuthukisweni kwezinhlamvu zamahlaya zamaphephandaba. Imichilo yangeSonto lokuqala ibigcwele ikhasi[24] futhi ivame ukuba nemibala. Phakathi kuka-1896 no-1901 abadwebi bamakhathuni bahlola ukulandelana, ukunyakaza, namabhaluni enkulumo.[25] Isibonelo uGustave Verbeek, owabhala uchungechunge lwakhe lwamahlaya oluthi "The UpsideDowns of Old Man Muffaroo and Little Lady Lovekins" phakathi kuka-1903 no-1905. Lawa mahlaya enziwa ngendlela yokuthi umuntu akwazi ukufunda ikhomikhi enamaphaneli angu-6, aphenye incwadi futhi aqhubeke efunda. Wenza amahlaya anjalo angama-64 esewonke. Ngo-2012, ukwenziwa kabusha kokukhethwa kwamahlaya kwenziwa ngu-Marcus Ivarsson encwadini ethi 'In Uppåner med Lilla Lisen & Gamle Muppen'. (ISBN 978-91-7089-524-1) 

Umdwebo wamahlaya wamaphaneli amahlanu. 
U-Bud Fisher's Mutt kanye noJeff (1907-1982) kwaba umugqa wokuqala wamahlaya wansuku zonke oyimpumelelo (1907). 
Imicu emifushane, emnyama nokumhlophe yansuku zonke yaqala ukuvela ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, futhi yasungulwa emaphephandabeni ngemva kwempumelelo ka-1907 ka-Bud Fisher's Mutt noJeff.[26] EBrithani, i-Amalgamated Press yasungula isitayela esidumile sokulandelana kwezithombe ezinombhalo ngaphansi kwazo, okuhlanganisa ama-Illustrated Chips and Comic Cuts.[27] Ama-humor strips ayevame kakhulu ekuqaleni, futhi ngawo-1920s kanye nawo-1930s imicu enezindaba eziqhubekayo ezinhlotsheni ezifana ne-adventure nedrama nayo yaduma.[26] 

Amaphephandaba azacile abizwa ngezincwadi zamahlaya avela ngeminyaka yawo-1930s, ekuqaleni anyathelisa kabusha amapheshana amahlaya ephephandaba; ekupheleni kweminyaka eyishumi, okuqukethwe kwasekuqaleni kwaqala ukubusa.[28] Impumelelo yango-1938 ye-Action Comics kanye neqhawe layo eliphambili uSuperman yaphawula ukuqala kwe-Golden Age ye-Comic Books, lapho uhlobo lwe-superhero lwalugqame khona.[29] E-UK kanye naku-Commonwealth, i-DC Thomson-created Dandy (1937) kanye ne-Beano (1938) yaba yizihloko ezisekelwe kumahlaya eziphumelelayo, ngokusakazwa okuhlangene kwamakhophi angaphezu kwezigidi ezimbili ngeminyaka yawo-1950. Abalingisi babo, okuhlanganisa "uDennis the Menace", "Desperate Dan" kanye "The Bash Street Kids" bafundwe yizizukulwane zezingane zaseBrithani.[30] Amahlaya ekuqaleni azame amaqhawe amakhulu nezindaba zesenzo ngaphambi kokuthi axoxe ngamapheshana ahlekisayo anengxube ye-Amalgamated Press kanye nezitayela zencwadi yamahlaya yase-US.[31] 


Amaqhawekazi abe yinsada yezincwadi zamahlaya zaseMelika (Wonderworld Comics #3, 1939; isembozo: The Flame by Will Eisner).
Ukuthandwa kwezincwadi zamahlaya ezimangalisayo kwehla eminyakeni eyalandela iMpi Yezwe II,[32] kuyilapho ukuthengiswa kwezincwadi zamahlaya kwaqhubeka kwanda njengoba ezinye izinhlobo zanda, ezifana nezothando, ezasentshonalanga, ubugebengu, izinto ezesabekayo, namahlaya.[33] Kulandela inani eliphakeme lokuthengisa ekuqaleni kwawo-1950, okuqukethwe ezincwadini zamahlaya (ikakhulukazi ubugebengu kanye nokwesabeka) kwabhekwa emaqenjini abazali kanye nezinhlaka zikahulumeni, okwafinyelela umvuthwandaba ekulalelweni kweSigele okwaholela ekusungulweni kweSigungu Seziphathimandla ezizihlolayo.[34] Ikhodi isolwe ngokukhinyabeza ukukhula kwamahlaya aseMelika kanye nokugcina isimo sayo esiphansi emphakathini waseMelika ingxenye enkulu esele yekhulunyaka.[35] Amaqhawe anamandla azimisa kabusha njengohlobo lwencwadi yamahlaya evelele kakhulu ekuqaleni kwawo-1960.[36] Inhlanganisela engaphansi komhlaba inselele Ikhodi kanye nabafundi ngokuqukethwe kwabantu abadala, okungahambisani namasiko ngasekupheleni kwawo-1960 nasekuqaleni kwawo-1970.[37] Umshoshaphansi wazala omunye umnyakazo wamahlaya ngeminyaka yawo-1980 kanye nokuqukethwe kwawo okuvuthiwe, okuvamise ukuvivinywa ezinhlotsheni ezingezona zamaqhawe amakhulu.[38] 

Amahlaya e-US abe nedumela eliphansi elisukela ezimpandeni zawo emasikweni amaningi; abaholi bezamasiko ngezinye izikhathi babebona isiko elidumile njengesiko nomphakathi osongelayo. Engxenyeni yokugcina yekhulu lama-20, isiko elidumile lazuza ukwamukelwa okukhulu, futhi imigqa phakathi kwesiko eliphezulu neliphansi laqala ukufiphala. Amahlaya nokho aqhubekile nokucwaswa, njengoba le ncwadi ibibhekwa njengokuzijabulisa kwezingane nakubantu abangafundile.[39] 

Inoveli eyingcaca—amahlaya obude bencwadi—yaqala ukunaka ngemva kokuba u-Will Eisner ethakazelise leli gama ngencwadi yakhe ethi A Contract with God (1978).[40] Leli gama laziwa kabanzi emphakathini ngemuva kwempumelelo yezentengiselwano ye-Maus, Watchmen, kanye ne-Dark Knight Returns maphakathi nawo-1980s.[41] Ngekhulu lama-21 amanoveli ezithombe asungulwa ezitolo zezincwadi ezivamile[42] kanye nemitapo yolwazi[43] kanye nama-webcomics avamile.[44] 

Amahlaya kaFranco-Belgian kanye naseYurophu 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Amahlaya ase-Europe namahlaya aseFranco-Belgian 
I-francophone yase-Swiss Rodolphe Töpffer ikhiqize imicu yamahlaya eqala ngo-1827,[16] futhi yanyathelisa imibono engemuva kwaleli fomu.[45] U-Wilhelm Busch waqala ukunyathelisa i-Max and Moritz yakhe ngo-1865. [46] Opopayi bavela kabanzi emaphephandabeni nakomagazini kusukela ekhulwini le-19. [47] Impumelelo kaZig et Puce ngo-1925 yenza kwaduma ukusetshenziswa kwamabhaluni enkulumo kumahlaya ase-Europe, okwathi ngemva kwalokho amahlaya aseFranco-Belgian aqala ukubusa.[48] I-Adventures of Tintin, nesiginesha yesitayela somugqa ocacile, [49] yaqala ukukhiqizwa ezithasiselweni zamahlaya ephephandaba kusukela ngo-1929, [50] futhi yaba isithonjana samahlaya aseFranco-Belgian.[51]

Kulandela impumelelo ye-Le Journal de Mickey (est. 1934), [52] omagazini bamahlaya abazinikezele [53] njengo-Spirou (est. 1938) kanye no-Tintin (1946-1993), kanye nama-albhamu amahlaya anemibala egcwele aba inkundla yokuqala yamahlaya phakathi nekhulu lama-20.[54] Njengase-US, ngaleso sikhathi amahlaya ayebhekwa njengezinsana futhi esongela isiko nokufunda; abahlaziyi bathi "akekho obekezelela ukuhlaziya okuncane okubucayi",[c] nokuthi amahlaya "ayewukucekela phansi kwabo bonke ubuciko kanye nazo zonke izincwadi".[56][d] 

Ngeminyaka yawo-1960, igama elithi bandes dessinées ("imicu edwetshiwe") laqala ukusetshenziswa kakhulu ngesiFulentshi ukuze libonise indlela.[57] Abadwebi bamakhathuni baqala ukwenza amahlaya ezethameli ezivuthiwe,[58] kanye negama elithi "Ninth Art"[e] laqanjwa, njengoba amahlaya aqala ukuheha ukunaka komphakathi kanye nezemfundo njengobuciko.[59] Iqembu elihlanganisa u-René Goscinny kanye no-Albert Uderzo basungula iphephabhuku i-Pilote ngo-1959 ukuze banikeze abaculi inkululeko enkulu ngomsebenzi wabo. Ingoma ka-Goscinny no-Uderzo ethi The Adventures of Asterix yavela kuyo[60] futhi yaqhubeka yaba uchungechunge lwamahlaya oluthengiswa kakhulu lwesiFulentshi.[61] Kusukela ngo-1960, i-Hara-Kiri ehlambalaza futhi ephula umthetho wephula imithetho yokucwaninga ngomoya ophikisana namasiko owaholela ezenzakalweni zikaMeyi 1968.[62] 

Ukukhungatheka ngokucwaninga nokuphazamiseka kokuhlela kwaholela eqenjini labadwebi bamakhathuni be-Pilote ukuba bathole i-L'Écho des savanes yabantu abadala kuphela ngo-1972. Amahlaya ahloselwe abantu abadala kanye nawokuhlola achuma ngeminyaka yawo-1970, njengasenganekwaneni yokuhlola yesayensi kaMœbius nabanye ku-Métal streamat hurlant athatha ngisho nabashicileli abakhulu be-Métal. amahlaya.[63] 

Kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1980s, ukuzwela okujwayelekile kwaphindwa kwaphindwa kwaphindwa kwaphindwa kwaphindwa kwahlelwa futhi kwancipha kakhulu njengoba inani lamamagazini amahlaya lehla futhi amahlaya amaningi aqala ukushicilelwa ngokuqondile njengama-albhamu.[64] Abashicileli abancane njenge-L'Association[65] eyashicilela imisebenzi emide[66] ngamafomethi okungezona ezendabuko[67] ngabadali be-auteur-istic nabo bavame. Kusukela ngawo-1990, ukuhlanganiswa kwaholela ekubeni bambalwa abamemezeli abakhulu, kuyilapho abamemezeli abancane banda. Ukuthengisa kukonke kuqhubekile nokukhula naphezu kokuthambekela emakethe yokuphrinta enciphayo.[68] 

Amahlaya ase-Japanese 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Umlando we-manga ne-Manga 

Rakuten Kitazawa udale umdwebo wokuqala wesimanje wamahlaya wase-Japan. (Tagosaku to Mokube no Tōkyō Kenbutsu,[f] 1902) 
Amahlaya aseJapan kanye ne-cartooning (manga),[g] anomlando oye wabonwa kusukela kudala njengabalingiswa be-anthropomorphic ku-12th-to-13th-century Chōjū-jinbutsu-giga, i-17th-tobashi yezithombe kanye ne-woodblock yekhulu le-17 ukuphrinta okufana ne-ukiyo-e eyayidumile phakathi kwekhulu le-17 nelama-20. I-kibyōshi iqukethe izibonelo zezithombe ezilandelanayo, imigqa yokunyakaza,[73] nemisindo.[74]
 
Omagazini abanezithombe abaphuma kwamanye amazwe baseNtshonalanga bethula opopayi besitayela saseNtshonalanga eJapan ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19. Ukushicilelwa okusha kuzo zombili izitayela zaseNtshonalanga nezaseJapan kwaduma, futhi ekupheleni kweminyaka yawo-1890, izithasiselo zamahlaya zamaphephandaba esitayela saseMelika zaqala ukuvela eJapan,[75] kanye nakwamanye ama-comic strips aseMelika.[72] Ngo-1900 kwaqala ukuqalwa kwe-Jiji Manga ephephandabeni iJiji Shinpō—ukusetshenziswa kokuqala kwegama elithi "manga" ngomqondo walo wesimanje, [71] nalapho, ngo-1902, u-Rakuten Kitazawa aqala khona umdwebo wokuqala wamahlaya waseJapane wesimanje.[76] Ngawo-1930s, iziqephu zamahlaya zase zikhishwa ngochungechunge kumagazini wanyanga zonke wamantombazane nabafana futhi zaqoqwa zaba imiqulu eqinile.[77]
 
Inkathi yesimanje yamahlaya e-Japan yaqala ngemva kweMpi Yezwe II, igqugquzelwa impumelelo yamahlaya ahleliwe e-Osamu Tezuka [78] kanye nesiqephu samahlaya i-Sazae-san.[79] Izinhlobo nezethameli zihlukene phakathi namashumi eminyaka alandelayo. Izindaba zivame ukukhishwa kumagazini okuvamise ukuba ngamakhulu amakhasi awugqinsi futhi angase aqukathe izindaba ezingaphezu kweshumi nambili;[80] kamuva ahlanganiswe ezincwadini zefomethi ye-tankōbon.[81] Ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20 nelama-21, cishe ingxenye yesine yazo zonke izincwadi ezinyathelisiwe eJapane yayingamahlaya.[82] Ukuhumusha kwaduma kakhulu ezimakethe zakwamanye amazwe—kwezinye izimo kwalingana noma kwedlula ukuthengiswa kwamahlaya asekhaya.[83] 

Amahlaya ase-Korea 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: I-Manhwa 
Manhwa ( 만화 ) ibhekisela kumahlaya ase-Korea kanye nopopayi abanyathelisayo, negama elivame ukusetshenziswa emhlabeni wonke ukuze kuqondwe amahlaya adabuka e-Korea. Ngenkathi i-manhwa yabelana ngezimpande zamasiko nezilimi ne-manga yesi-Japanese kanye ne-Chinese manhua, ithuthukise ukuhlonza okuhlukile okuthonywa umlando, amasiko, kanye nobuciko bezwe lase-Korea. I-manhwa yesimanje isithole ukuthandwa emhlabeni jikelele, ngokwengxenye ngenxa yokwanda kwama-webtoon—amahlaya afomethwe ngokwedijithali aklanyelwe ukuskrola kumadivayisi eselula. Le mpumelelo iye yaba nesandla ekuzivumelaniseni namabhayisikobho, amadrama nochungechunge lwethelevishini. 

Umqondo we-manhwa wavela ngaphansi kwethonya le-manga yaseJapane ngesikhathi sokuhlala kwamaJapane eKorea ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20. Ubukhona obumisiwe buka-Manga e-Japan phakathi nalesi sikhathi zabombe kakhulu izitayela eziyisisekelo namafomethi amahlaya ase-Korea. Njengoba i-Korea ishintshela ekuzimele, i-manhwa yashintsha yaba indlela ehlukile, ilinganisa amathonya obuciko omakhelwane bayo nobuhle bendabuko baseKorea kanye nokuxoxa izindaba. 

Amahlaya ase-Argentina 

Ikhasi lokuqala le-Eternaut elanyatheliswa e-Hora Cero ngo-1957 
Ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, kwavela omagazini abaningi bamahlaya ezombusazwe ababequkethe imifanekiso yosopolitiki bendawo kanye nosaziwayo.Odume kakhulu kuwo yi-Caras y caretas, esaqhubeka nokushicilelwa namanje.[84]

Ngawo-1940 kanye nawo-1950, imboni yamahlaya yase-Argentina yadlondlobala ngokusebenzisa abalingisi abasha abaqondiswe ezinganeni kanye nentsha, abafana no-Patoruzú (i-tehuelche cacique ecebile yasePatagonia) kanye no-Isidoro Cañones (indoda ehlakaniphile yase-Buenos Aires), bobabili abadalwe ngu-Dante Quinterno] [85].[85] 

Phakathi kuka-1957 no-1959 i-El Eternauta yashicilelwa. Bekuwumzamo ohlonishwa umhlaba wonke wokudala izindaba zamahlaya ezivuthiwe e-Argentina. Yakhiwe ngu-Héctor Germán Oesterheld kanye noFrancisco Solano López njengendaba eqanjiwe yesayensi mayelana nokuhlasela kwabafokazi e-Buenos Aires, kanye neqhwa elinobuthi elingabulala noma ubani olithintayo. Kubhekwa njengokumela ubushiqela buka-1955 obushushisa ama-peronists (u-Oesterheld ngokwakhe eyi-peronist). U-Oesterheld nawo wonke umkhaya wakhe babezogcina sebenyamalele ubushiqela.[87]

Ngawo-1960, kwasungulwa umagazini wezingane i-Anteojito, lapho u-Manuel García Ferré ayezoqhubeka nokushicilela izindaba zabalingisi abaningi ababezoba amagama asekhaya, njengo-Hijitus (umfana ompofu nongenalwazi oyisigqoko sakhe samnika amandla amakhulu) kanye no-Larguirucho (umngane wakhe).[88] 

Phakathi kweminyaka yawo-1960 no-1970, kwavela omunye wabalingisi bamahlaya abadumile base-Argentina, uMafalda, odalwe nguQuino. Yayidumile kulo lonke elaseLatin America naseYurophu. UMafalda wayebhekwa njengenhlekisa emindenini yasemadolobheni esezingeni eliphakathi, futhi wabonisa ukuthambekela kwentsha kwezombusazwe okuthuthukayo.[89] 

Ngawo-1970 umlingisi wamahlaya ofanelekile kwakunguClemente, owadalwa nguCaloi. Kwakuyisilwane esiqanjiwe esingenazingalo namaphiko, esasidla iminqumo kuphela futhi siphuze umlingani. Naphezu kweminyaka yawo-1970 kwaba yisikhathi sezinxushunxushu zezombusazwe e-Argentina, uClemente wayengumkhohlisi futhi ethanda ibhola lenhlangano.[90] 

Amafomu namafomethi 
Ama-Comic strips ngokuvamile amafushane, amahlaya amaningi, kusukela ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, avame ukuvela emaphephandabeni. E-US, imichilo yansuku zonke ivame ukuthatha isigaba esisodwa, kanti imichilo yangeSonto inikezwe izigaba eziningi. Kusukela ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, imicu yamakhomikhi yamaphephandaba ansuku zonke iye yanyatheliswa ngamakhomikhi amnyama namhlophe nangeSonto ngokuvamile aye anyatheliswa ngombala futhi ngokuvamile athatha ikhasi eligcwele lephephandaba.[91] 

Amafomethi ezikhathi zamahlaya akhethekile ahluka kakhulu kumasiko ahlukene. Izincwadi zamahlaya, ngokuyinhloko ifomethi yaseMelika, zingamaphephandaba amancane[92] avame ukushicilelwa ngemibala.[93] Amahlaya aseYurophu nawaseJapane avame ukukhishwa komagazini—nyanga zonke noma masonto onke eYurophu,[71] futhi ngokuvamile okumnyama nokumhlophe kanye namasonto onke eJapane.[94] Omagazini bamahlaya baseJapane ngokuvamile bafinyelela emakhulwini amakhasi.[95] 


Ukuqhathaniswa kwamafomethi ezincwadi zamahlaya emhlabeni jikelele. Iqembu elingakwesokunxele livela e-Japan futhi libonisa i-tankōbon namafomethi we-bunkobon amancane. Labo abaseqenjini elimaphakathi lamahlaya aseFranco-Belgian bakufomethi ye-albhamu yamahlaya engusayizi ongu-A4 ojwayelekile. Iqembu elilungile lamanoveli ayingcaca livela emazweni akhuluma isiNgisi, lapho ingekho ifomethi evamile. 
Amakhomikhi obude bencwadi athatha izinhlobo ezahlukene emasikweni ahlukene. Ama-albhamu amahlaya ase-Europe ayimiqulu yemibala evame ukuphrintwa ngosayizi we-A4, usayizi wekhasi omkhulu kunokusetshenziswa kwamanye amasiko amaningi.[96][54] Emazweni akhuluma isiNgisi, ifomethi ye-paperback yohwebo evela ezincwadini zamahlaya eziqoqiwe nayo ikhethelwe okokusebenza koqobo. Uma kungenjalo, amavolumu ahlanganisiwe wamahlaya abizwa ngokuthi amanoveli ayingcaca futhi atholakala ngamafomethi ahlukahlukene. Naphezu kokuhlanganiswa kwegama elithi “inoveli”—igama elivame ukuhlotshaniswa nenganekwane—“inoveli eyingcaca” iphinde ibhekisele kokungelona iqiniso kanye namaqoqo emisebenzi emifushane.[97] Amahlaya aseJapan aqoqwa ngamavolumu abizwa nge-tankōbon elandelayo ukukhiqizwa komagazini.[98]

Opopayi be-Gag nabahleli ngokuvamile bahlanganisa iphaneli eyodwa, ngokuvamile ehlanganisa amagama-ncazo noma ibhaluni yenkulumo. Izincazelo zamahlaya agcizelela ukulandelana ngokuvamile akubandakanyi opopayi bephaneli elilodwa; zingafakwa ezincazelweni ezigcizelela inhlanganisela yegama nesithombe.[99] Opopayi be-Gag baqala ukwanda emaphepheni ashicilelwe eYurophu ngekhulu le-18 nele-19, futhi igama elithi "ikhathuni" [h] lasetshenziswa okokuqala ukuwachaza ngo-1843 kumagazini wamahlaya waseBrithani i-Punch.[22] 

Ama-Webcomics angamahlaya atholakala ku-inthanethi, aqala ukushicilelwa ngawo-1980. Bayakwazi ukufinyelela izethameli eziningi, futhi abafundi abasha ngokuvamile bangafinyelela kungobo yomlando yezitolimende zangaphambilini.[100] I-Webcomics ingasebenzisa ikhanvasi engapheli, okusho ukuthi ayivinjwa usayizi noma ubukhulu bekhasi lamahlaya eliphrintiwe.[101] 

Abanye babheka amabhodi wezindaba[102] kanye namanoveli angenamagama njengamahlaya.[103] Izitudiyo zamafilimu, ikakhulukazi ezopopayi, zivame ukusebenzisa ukulandelana kwezithombe njengemihlahlandlela yokulandelana kwefilimu. Lawa mabhodi wezindaba akuhlosiwe njengomkhiqizo wokugcina futhi awavamile ukubonwa umphakathi.[102] Amanoveli angenamagama ayizincwadi ezisebenzisa ukulandelana kwezithombe ezingenamagama-ncazo ukuletha ukulandisa.[104] 

Izifundo zamahlaya 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Izifundo zamahlaya 
"Amahlaya ... ngezinye izikhathi anemilenze emine futhi ngezinye izikhathi anemilenze emibili futhi ngezinye izikhathi ayandiza futhi ngezinye izikhathi awa ... ukusebenzisa isingathekiso njengoba sixutshwe ngendlela ngokwayo, ukuchaza amahlaya kuhlanganisa ukusika impicabadala enefindo lika-Gordian esongwe ngemfihlakalo ..." 
 
RC Harvey, 99][99]
Ngokufanayo nezinkinga zokuchazwa kwefilimu futhi akukho ncazelo efinyelelwe. amahlaya, [106] kanye nezincazelo nezincazelo ezizanyiwe ziye zaba izisulu zokuhlukile okuningi.[107] Amathiyori afana no-Töpffer,[108] RC Harvey, Will Eisner,[109] David Carrier,[110] Alain Rey,[106] kanye noLawrence Grove bagcizelela inhlanganisela yombhalo nemifanekiso,[111] nakuba kunezibonelo ezivelele zamahlaya e-pantomime kuwo wonke umlando wawo.[107] Abanye abagxeki, abafana noThierry Groensteen[111] kanye noScott McCloud, bagcizelele ukubaluleka kokulandelana kwezithombe.[112] Ngasekupheleni kwekhulu lama-20, ukutholwa kwamasiko ahlukene amasiko amahlaya womunye nomunye, ukutholwa kabusha kwamafomu amahlaya okuqala asekhohliwe, kanye nokwanda kwamafomu amasha kwenza ukuchaza amahlaya kwaba umsebenzi oyinkimbinkimbi.[113]

Izifundo zamahlaya ase-Europe zaqala ngemibono ka-Töpffer yomsebenzi wakhe ngeminyaka yawo-1840s, eyayigcizelela uguquko lwamaphaneli kanye nenhlanganisela yokubuka nokukhuluma. Ayikho enye inqubekelaphambili eyenziwe kwaze kwaba ngawo-1970.[114] U-Pierre Fresnault-Deruelle wabe esethatha indlela ye-semiotics ocwaningweni lwamahlaya, ehlaziya ubudlelwano bombhalo nesithombe, ubudlelwano bezithombe ezingeni lekhasi, nokungaqhubeki kwesithombe, noma lokho uScott McCloud akubiza kamuva ngokuthi "ukuvalwa".[115] Ngo-1987, u-Henri Vanlier wethula igama elithi multicadre, noma "multiframe", ukuze abhekisele ekhasini lamahlaya njengeyunithi ye-semantic.[116] Ngawo-1990s, ama-theorists afana no-Benoît Peeters kanye no-Thierry Groensteen baphendukela ekukhetheni amaciko ahlakaniphile.[115] U-Thierry Smolderen no-Harry Morgan babambe imibono ehambisanayo yencazelo yamahlaya, imidiya ethathe amafomu ahlukahlukene, avumelekile ngokulinganayo emlandweni wawo. UMorgan ubona amahlaya njengesethi engaphansi ye-"les littératures dessinées" (noma "izincwadi ezidwetshiwe").[113] Ithiyori yesiFulentshi isize ukuzonaka ngokukhethekile ikhasi, ngokwehlukana nemibono yaseMelika efana nekaMcCloud egxile ekushintsheni kwephaneli kuya kwephaneli.[116] Maphakathi nawo-2000, u-Neil Cohn waqala ukuhlaziya ukuthi amahlaya aqondwa kanjani kusetshenziswa amathuluzi asuka kusayensi yokuqonda, edlulela ngale kwethiyori ngokusebenzisa izivivinyo zangempela zengqondo nezengqondo. Lo msebenzi ubeke waphikisa ngokuthi izithombe ezilandelanayo nezakhiwo zekhasi zombili zisebenzisa "uhlelo lolimi" oluboshelwe emthethweni ukuze luqondwe ukuthi ludlulela ngale koshintsho lwephaneli-kuya-iphaneli kanye nokuhlukaniswa ngokwezigaba kwezinhlobo zezakhiwo, nokuthi ukuqonda kobuchopho kwamahlaya kuyafana nokuqonda ezinye izizinda, njengolimi nomculo.[117]

Ukulandisa okungokomlando kwe-manga kuvame ukugxila emlandweni wayo wakamuva, wangemva kwe-WWII, noma emizamweni yokubonisa izimpande ezijulile esikhathini esidlule, njengomqulu wesithombe we-Chōjū-jinbutsu-giga wekhulu le-12 nele-13, noma ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19 lekhulu le-Hokusai Manga.[118] Ukubuka kuqala komlando kwamahlaya ase-Japanese kwakuyi-Nihon Manga-Shi kaSeiki Hosokibara[i] ngo-1924.[119] Ukugxekwa kwaseJapan kwasekuqaleni kwangemva kwempi kwakungokwepolitiki engakwesokunxele kwaze kwaba yilapho kushicilelwa ngo-1986 i-Tomofusa Kure's Modern Manga: The Complete Picture,[j] eyayingagcizeleli ipolitiki ivuna izici ezisemthethweni, ezifana nesakhiwo kanye "nohlelo lolimi" lwamahlaya. Umkhakha wezifundo zemanga wanda ngokushesha, nenqwaba yezincwadi ezikhuluma ngale ndaba eyavela ngeminyaka yawo-1990. [120] Imibono esemthethweni ye-manga igxile ekuthuthukiseni "ithiyori yokusho i-manga",[k] ngokugcizelela ubudlelwano bendawo esakhiweni sezithombe ekhasini, ehlukanisa indlela nefilimu noma izincwadi, lapho ukuhamba kwesikhathi kuyisici sokuhlela esiyisisekelo.[121] Izifundo zezifundo zamahlaya zandile emanyuvesi ase-Japan, futhi i-Japan Society for Studies in Cartoon and Comics (ja)[l] yasungulwa ngo-2001 ukuze kuthuthukiswe umfundaze wamahlaya.[122] Ukushicilelwa kweManga kaFrederik L. Schodt! Manga! I-World of Japanese Comics ngo-1983 yaholela ekusabalaleni kokusetshenziswa kwegama elithi manga ngaphandle kwase-Japan ukuze lisho "amahlaya aseJapane" noma "amahlaya esitayela saseJapane".[123] 

Indoda endala enempandla efake izibuko. 
Indoda eneminyaka ephakathi ihlezi ngemva kwetafula, ibheke ikhamera. 
U-Will Eisner (kwesokunxele) no-Scott McCloud (kwesokudla) baphakamise izincazelo zamahlaya ezinethonya neziyimpikiswano.
U-Coulton Waugh uzame umlando wokuqala ophelele wamahlaya aseMelika nge-The Comics (1947).[124] I-Will Eisner's Comics and Sequential Art (1985) kanye ne-Understanding Comics ka-Scott McCloud (1993) kwakuyimizamo yakuqala ngesiNgisi yokwenza ngokusemthethweni ukufunda kwamahlaya. IkaDavid Carrier ethi The Aesthetics of Comics (2000) kwaba yindlela yokwelapha yokuqala yobude obugcwele yamahlaya ngokombono wefilosofi.[125] Imizamo evelele yaseMelika yokuchaza amahlaya ihlanganisa u-Eisner's, McCloud's, noHarvey's. U-Eisner uchaze lokho akubiza ngokuthi "ubuciko obulandelanayo" njengokuthi "ukuhlelwa kwezithombe noma izithombe namagama ukuze axoxe indaba noma enze idrama ngombono";[126] UScott McCloud uchaze amahlaya ngokuthi "izithombe ezihlanganisiwe nezinye izithombe ngokulandelana kwamabomu, okuhloswe ngazo ukudlulisa ulwazi kanye/noma ukukhiqiza impendulo yobuhle kumbukeli",[127] ngokwencazelo eqinile yezamasiko nencazelo yawo yomlando ehlanganisa amasiko nencazelo yawo yomlando, ehloselwe ukudlulisa ngamabomu kanye nezinye izithombe. izicupho.[128] U-RC Harvey uchaze amahlaya ngokuthi "izindaba ezilandiswayo eziyizithombe noma ukuvezwa lapho amagama (avame ukufakwa ngohlamvu endaweni yesithombe ngaphakathi kwamabhaluni enkulumo) ngokuvamile anengxenye encazelweni yezithombe futhi okuphambene nalokho".[129] Incazelo ngayinye ibe nabaphikisi bayo. U-Harvey wabona incazelo kaMcCloud njengengabandakanyi opopayi abanephaneli elilodwa, [130] futhi wamelana nezakhi zezwi zikaMcCloud ezingagcizeleli, egcizelela ukuthi "isici esibalulekile samahlaya ukuhlanganiswa kokuqukethwe kwamazwi".[116] U-Aaron Meskin wabona imibono kaMcCloud njengomzamo wokwenziwa wokwenza kube semthethweni indawo yamahlaya emlandweni wobuciko.[109] 

Ukufunda amahlaya ahlukene ngokwesiko kwenziwa nzima ngenxa yomehluko omkhulu encazelweni kanye nobubanzi bamagama asho "amahlaya" ezilimini ezahlukene.[131] Itemu lesiFulentshi lamahlaya, ama-bandes dessinées ("umcu odwetshiwe") ligcizelela ukuhlangana kwezithombe ezidwetshiwe njengento echazayo,[132] engasho ukukhishwa ngisho namahlaya ezithombe.[133] Igama elithi manga lisetshenziswa ngesi-Japanese ukukhombisa zonke izinhlobo zamahlaya, ukuqoshwa kwekhathuni,[134] kanye ne-caricature.[131] 

Itemu 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Uhlu lwamagama amahlaya 
Itemu elithi amahlaya lisho indlela yamahlaya lapho lisetshenziswa njengebizo elingenakubalwa futhi lithatha ubunye: "amahlaya iyisikhulumi" kunokuthi "amahlaya ayisisetshenziswa". Uma i-comic ivela njengebizo elibalekayo ibhekisela ezimweni ze-medium, njengemibhalo yamahlaya ngayinye noma izincwadi zamahlaya: "Amahlaya ka-Tom angaphansi kwendlu."[135]

Amaphaneli ayizithombe ngazinye eziqukethe ingxenye yesenzo,[136] ngokuvamile ezungezwe umngcele.[137] Izikhathi eziyinhloko endabeni zihlukaniswa zibe amaphaneli ngenqubo ebizwa ngokuthi i-encapsulation.[138] Umfundi uhlanganisa izingcezu ngenqubo yokuvala ngokusebenzisa ulwazi lwangemuva kanye nokuqonda ubudlelwano bephaneli ukuze ahlanganise amaphaneli ngokwengqondo enze izehlakalo.[139] Usayizi, umumo, nokuhlelwa kwamaphaneli ngalinye lithinta isikhathi nokuhamba kwezindaba.[140] Okuqukethwe kwephaneli kungase kuhambisane, futhi izehlakalo ezivezwe esithombeni esifanayo zingenzeki ngesikhathi esifanayo.[141] 
I-Etymology

Iphaneli yamahlaya. Phezulu kwesokunxele, amazwibela anengemuva eliphuzi afundeka kanje, "Kungazelelwe umgwaqo ugcwala abantu abathukuthele!" Kuphaneli enkulu, abalingiswa be-anthropomorphic bagcwala umgwaqo oseceleni. Inkawu, emi kwesokunxele emgwaqeni eceleni konqenqema, ithi, "Hawu! Bavelaphi bonke laba bantu?" Owesilisa oyisidudla osemgwaqweni ophakathi nendawo obheke kwesokudla uthi ephoyiseni, "Heyi! Iwashi lami linyamalele endaweni yami yokuphumula!" Intokazi eseduze ngezansi kwesokudla, ithi kowesilisa ngezansi kwesokudla, "Umgexo wami! Usukile etafuleni!!" 
Amazwibela (ibhokisi eliphuzi) anikeza umxoxi izwi. Ingxoxo yabalingiswa ivela emabhaluni enkulumo. Umsila webhaluni ubonisa isipikha. 
Umbhalo uvamise ukufakwa kumahlaya ngamabhaluni enkulumo, amagama-ncazo, nemisindo. Amabhaluni enkulumo abonisa inkhulumomphendvulwano (noma umcabango, endabeni yamabhaluni omcabango), anemisila ekhomba izikhulumi zawo.[142] Amagama-ncazo anganikeza izwi kumlandisi, adlulisele ingxoxo yabalingisi noma imicabango,[143] noma abonise indawo noma isikhathi.[144] Amabhaluni enkulumo ngokwawo ahlotshaniswa kakhulu namahlaya, kangangokuthi ukungezwa kweyodwa esithombeni kwanele ukushintsha isithombe sibe amahlaya.[145] Imiphumela yomsindo ilingisa imisindo engeyona eyephimbo ngokombhalo isebenzisa amagama omsindo we-onomatopoeia.[146] 

Ukwenza opopayi kuvame ukusetshenziswa kakhulu ekwenzeni amahlaya, ngokwesiko kusetshenziswa uyinki (ikakhulukazi uyinki waseNdiya) onamapeni okucwilisa noma amabhulashi ayinki;[147] imidiya exubile nobuchwepheshe bedijithali sekuyinsakavukela. Amasu opopayi afana nemigqa enyakazayo [148] kanye nezimpawu ezingabonakali zivame ukusetshenziswa.[149] 

Nakuba amahlaya ngokuvamile engumsebenzi womdali oyedwa, umsebenzi wokuwenza uvame ukuhlukaniswa phakathi kochwepheshe abambalwa. Kungase kube nababhali nabadwebi abahlukene, futhi amaciko angase agxile ezingxenyeni ezithile zomsebenzi wobuciko njengabalingiswa noma izizinda, njengoba kuvamile eJapane.[150] Ikakhulukazi ezincwadini zamakhomikhi eqhawe elinamandla laseMelika,[151] ubuciko bungahlukaniswa phakathi kwepensela, obeka umsebenzi wobuciko ngepensela;[152] inka, oqeda umsebenzi wobuciko ngoyinki;[153] umdwebi wemibala;[154] kanye nombhali, owengeza amagama-ncazo namabhaluni enkulumo.[155]

Itemu lesiNgisi elithi amahlaya lisuselwa emsebenzini ohlekisayo (noma "wamahlaya") owawudlangile emiculweni yamahlaya yamaphephandaba asekuqaleni aseMelika, kodwa ukusetshenziswa kwaleli gama sekuyinto evamile nemisebenzi engeyona eyamahlaya. Enye inhlanganisela yesipelingi - eyakhiwe ukunyakaza kwe-underground comix - ngezinye izikhathi isetshenziselwa ukubhekana nokungaqondakali okunjalo.[156] Igama elithi "incwadi yamahlaya" linomlando ofanayo odidayo njengoba ngokuvamile awawona amancoko futhi angamaphephandaba, awawona amabhuku avamile.[157] Kuvamile esiNgisini ukubhekisela kumahlaya amasiko ahlukene ngamagama asetshenziswa ezilimini zawo, njenge-manga yamahlaya aseJapane, noma ama-bandes dessinées amahlaya ase-French-language Franco-Belgian.[158] 

Amasiko amaningi athathe igama lawo lamahlaya esiNgisini, okuhlanganisa isiRashiya (комикс, komiks)[159] nesiJalimane (Amahlaya).[160] Ngokufanayo, igama lesiShayina elithi manhua[161] kanye nelesiKorea elithi manhwa[162] lisuselwa kuzinhlamvu zesiShayina okubhalwe ngazo igama lesi-Japanese elithi manga.[163] 




Umbhalo uyidokhumenti echaza ukulandisa kanye nengxoxo yencwadi yamahlaya ngokuningiliziwe. Liyincwadi yamahlaya elilingana nohlelo lwethelevishini oludlalwa ngethelevishini noma umdlalo wefilimu. 

Emakhomikhi, umbhalo ungase wandulelwe uhlaka lwesakhiwo, futhi cishe njalo ulandelwa imidwebo yekhasi edwetshwa umdwebi wamahlaya kanye noyinki, okulandelwa izigaba zokufaka imibala nezinhlamvu. Azikho izinhlobo ezinqunyiwe zemibhalo yamahlaya, kodwa kunezitayela ezimbili ezivelele embonini yamahlaya evamile, iskripthi esigcwele (esaziwa kakhulu ngokuthi "isitayela se-DC") kanye nombhalo wesakhiwo (noma "isitayela sendlu ye-Marvel").[1] 

Umdali wombhalo waziwa njengombhali wamahlaya.[a] 

Izitayela 
Umbhalo ogcwele wesitayela 
Ngalesi sitayela, umbhali wamahlaya uhlahlela indaba ngokulandelana, ikhasi nekhasi kanye nephaneli ngephaneli, echaza isenzo, abalingiswa, futhi ngezinye izikhathi isizinda kanye namaphuzu "wokubuka kwekhamera" wephaneli ngayinye, kanye nawo wonke amagama-ncazo nezingxoxo zengxoxo. Emashumini eminyaka, lena bekuyifomethi ethandwayo yezincwadi ezishicilelwe yi-DC Comics. 

U-Peter David wachaza ukusetshenziswa kwakhe okuqondile kwendlela yombhalo ogcwele: "Ngihlukanisa ikhasi ngalinye kuphaneli ngesisekelo sephaneli bese ngilebula ngele-PANEL A, PANEL B, njalonjalo. Bese ngichaza okusephaneli ngayinye, bese ngenza inkhulumomphendvulwano, ngibala amabhaluni. Ngiqoka amaphaneli anezinhlamvu kanye namabhaluni egama anezinombolo ukuze nginciphise ukudideka".[9] Ngaphezu kokubhala imibhalo, uJim Shooter udwebe izakhiwo zeciko emsebenzini wakhe wokuqala we-DC.[10] 

Iskripthi sesakhiwo
Embhalweni wesakhiwo umdwebi usebenza kusuka ku-synopsis yendaba evela kumbhali (noma umhleli), esikhundleni sombhalo ogcwele. Umdwebi uzenzela imininingwane yesakhiwo sekhasi nekhasi, ngemva kwalokho umsebenzi ubuyiselwa kumbhali ukuze kufakwe inkhulumomphendvulwano. Ngenxa yokusetshenziswa kwayo kabanzi e-Marvel Comics kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1960s, ngaphansi komhleli-wengxoxo uStan Lee kanye nababhali-maciko uJack Kirby noSteve Ditko, le ndlela yaziwa ngokuvamile ngokuthi indlela ye-Marvel noma isitayela sendlu ye-Marvel.[11] 
Okubi okubaluliwe kufaka phakathi:

Isazi-mlando samahlaya uMark Evanier sibhala ukuthi le "ndlela entsha yokusebenzisana . . . yazalwa ngenxa yesidingo—uStan wayesindwa umsebenzi—kanye nokusebenzisa ikhono elikhulu likaJack ngezindaba. . . . Ngezinye izikhathi uStan wayebhala uhlaka lwesakhiwo somculi. Ngezinye izikhathi, akunjalo".[12] Njengoba umhleli wencwadi yamahlaya uDennis O'Neil echaza, indlela yeMarvel "idinga ukuthi umbhali aqale ngokubhala isakhiwo bese engeza amagama lapho umsebenzi wobuciko obhalwe ipeni usuqediwe. . . . . Indaba, futhi ifake kuzo izifinyezo zengxoxo Ngakho-ke icebo leNdlela Eyisimangaliso lingasebenza lisuka ezigabeni ezimbalwa liye kokuthile ende futhi elinemininingwane eminingi." [13] 

Indlela ye-Marvel yayikhona okungenani neciko elilodwa ekuqaleni kuka-1961, njengoba u-Lee achaza ngo-2009 lapho ekhuluma "ngeziqephu zokugcwalisa ezimfishane, ezinamakhasi amahlanu" zika-Ditko ... ezibekwe kunoma yimaphi amahlaya ethu abenamakhasi ambalwa engeziwe okufanele agcwalise", egqame kakhulu ku-Amazing Fantasy kodwa ngisho nangaphambilini ku-Amazing Adventures kanye nezinye "pre-supersuperhero" yesayensi-i-Marvel. 

Ngingaphupha izinganekwane eziyinqaba ezine-twist yohlobo luka-O. Henry. Okwakufanele ngikwenze nje kwakuwukunikeza uSteve incazelo yomugqa owodwa wesakhiwo futhi wayezophuma egijima. Wayethatha lezo zinhlaka zamathambo engangimnike zona aziguqule zibe imisebenzi yobuciko emincane yakudala eyagcina isipholile kakhulu kunalokho engangingase ngikulindele.[14] 

Umagazini ka-Okthoba 2018 wephephabhuku lokubuka kuqala langaphakathi kwe-DC Comics, i-DC Nation, libonise ukubheka inqubo yokudala umlobi u-Brian Michael Bendis kanye namaciko uRyan Sook, u-Wade von Grawbadger no-Brad Anderson abaqashwe ku-Action Comics #1004, ehlanganisa amakhasi ombhalo we-Bendis ahlukaniswe iphaneli ngephaneli, noma kunjalo ngaphandle kwengxoxo.[15] 

Izinzuzo zendlela ye-Marvel phezu kwendlela ephelele yombhalo ecashunwe abadali nezingcweti zemboni ihlanganisa: 

Iqiniso lokuthi amaciko, aqashwe ukuze abone izigcawu ngeso lengqondo, angase ahlome kangcono ukunquma isakhiwo samaphaneli.[16][17] 
Inkululeko enkudlwana lokhu kuyinikeza abaculi.[16][17] 
Umthwalo ophansi othweswe umbhali.[16] 

Iqiniso lokuthi akuwona wonke amaciko angababhali abanekhono, futhi abanye bayazabalaza ngezinto ezifana nemibono yesakhiwo nokuhamba kancane.[16][18] 
Kusiza abaculi, ngokuvamile abakhokhelwa ubuciko bodwa nakuba empeleni besebenza njengababhali abakanye nabo.[18] 
Isitayela se-Kurtzman 
Enguqulweni yeskripthi sesakhiwo, esishiwo ngu-Harvey Kurtzman, umbhali uhlukanisa indaba ibe ama-rough amakhasi noma imidwebo yezithonjana, namagama-ncazo kanye nengxoxo ebhalwe phansi ngaphakathi kwezinkinga. Umdwebi (ovame ukuba ngumbhali wamahlaya futhi) ube esekhipha ama-rough ebhodini lobuciko elinosayizi ogcwele. Umbhali/abaculi uFrank Miller noJeff Smith bathanda lesi sitayela, njengoba kwenza u-Archie Goodwin.[1] 

Isitayela se-EC 
Sishiwo ku-William Gaines (umshicileli we-Kurtzman ku-EC Comics), isitayela se-EC siyefana nesitayela se-Kurtzman, ngaphandle kokuthi umbhali ehambise itulo eliqinile kumdwebi, elihlephula libe ngamaphaneli abekwe ebhodini lobuciko. Umbhali ubhala wonke amagama-ncazo nenkhulumomphendvulwano, enamathiselwe ngaphakathi kwala mapaneli, bese umdwebi edweba indaba ukuze ilingane nakho konke lokhu kunamathisela. Le ndlela ekhandlayo nenemingcele yokudala amahlaya ayisasetshenziswa; umculi wokugcina ukusebenzisa ngisho uhlobo oluhlukile lwesitayela se-EC kwakunguJim Aparo.[1]
