Incwadi isethulo esihlelekile sokwaziswa okurekhodiwe, ngokuyinhloko ngomlomo nangezithombe, kusetshenziswa indlela. Ekuqaleni, izincwadi ze-elekthronikhi nama-audiobook sezikhona. Izincwadi ezibonakalayo ziyizinto eziqukethe izinto eziphrintiwe, ikakhulukazi ezibhaliwe nemifanekiso. Izincwadi zesimanje ngokuvamile zakhiwa amakhasi amaningi ahlanganiswe ndawonye futhi avikelwe ngesembozo, lokho okwaziwa ngokuthi ifomethi ye-codex; amafomethi amadala ahlanganisa umqulu kanye nethebhulethi. 
 
Njengento ecatshangwayo, incwadi ivamise ukusho umsebenzi obhaliwe onobude obukhulu ngoyedwa noma ngaphezulu umbhali, ongasatshalaliswa ngokwedijithali njengencwadi ye-elekthronikhi (i-ebook). Lezi zinhlobo zemisebenzi zingahlukaniswa kabanzi zibe inganekwane (equkethe okuqukethwe okuqanjiwe, ngokuvamile ukulandisa) kanye nenganekwane (okuqukethe okuqukethwe okuhloswe njengokuyiqiniso). Kodwa incwadi ephathekayo akumele ibe nomsebenzi obhaliwe: isibonelo, ingaqukatha kuphela imidwebo, okuqoshiwe, izithombe, umculo weshidi, izindida, noma okuqukethwe okususwayo njengonodoli bephepha. 

Imboni yezincwadi yesimanje ibone izinguquko ezinkulu ezimbalwa ngenxa yobuchwepheshe obusha, okuhlanganisa ama-ebook nama-audiobook (okurekhodiwe kwezincwadi ezifundwa kuzwakale).Ukuqwashisa ngezidingo zabantu abakhubazekile ngokuphrinta kuholele ekwenyukeni kwamafomethi adizayinelwe ukufinyeleleka okukhudlwana njengokuphrinta kwe-braille kanye nokuhlelwa kwezinhlamvu ezinkulu.

I-Google Books yalinganiselwa ngo-2010 ukuthi cishe izigidi eziyi-130 seziphelele zezincwadi ezihlukile zase zishicilelwe. Inqubo yokushicilela incwadi iwuchungechunge lwezinyathelo ezihilelekile ekwakhiweni nasekusabalaliseni izincwadi. Izincwadi zithengiswa kuzo zombili izitolo ezijwayelekile kanye nezitolo zezincwadi ezikhethekile, kanye naku-inthanethi (ukuze zilethwe), futhi zingabolekwa emitatsheni yolwazi noma emakhabetheni ezincwadi zomphakathi. Ukwamukelwa kwezincwadi kuholele emiphumeleni eminingi yomphakathi, okuhlanganisa nokuhlolwa. 

Ngezinye izikhathi izincwadi ziqhathaniswa nezincwadi eziphuma ngezikhathi ezithile, njengamaphephandaba noma omagazini, lapho kunyatheliswa khona izinhlelo ezintsha ngokuvumelana nesimiso esivamile. Izinto ezihlobene, ezibuye zihlukaniswe kabanzi ngokuthi "izincwadi", zishiywa zingenalutho ukuze umuntu azisebenzisele yena: njengasendabeni yezincwadi ze-akhawunti, izincwadi ze-aphoyintimenti, izincwadi ze-autograph, izincwadi zokubhalela, idayari kanye ne-sketchbook. 

I-Etymology 
Igama elithi bhuku livela kwelesiNgisi Esidala elithi bōc, okungenzeka ukuthi livela empandeni yesiJalimane ethi *bōk-, ehambisana nelithi "beech".[1] Ngezilimi zesiSlavic njengesiRashiya, isiBulgaria, isiMacedonian буква bukva—"incwadi" ihambisana negama elithi "beech". Ngesi-Russian, isi-Serbian nesi-Macedonia, igama elithi букварь (bukvar') noma буквар (bukvar) lisho incwadi yesikole samabanga aphansi esiza izingane ezincane zikwazi kahle amasu okufunda nokubhala. Ngakho-ke kucatshangwa ukuthi imibhalo yokuqala yase-Indo-European kungenzeka iqoshwe okhunini lwe-beech.[2] Igama lesiLatini elithi codex, elisho incwadi ngomqondo wanamuhla (eboshiwe futhi enamaqabunga ahlukene), ekuqaleni lalisho “ibhulokhi lezinkuni”.[3] 

Umfundi oshisekayo noma umqoqi wezincwadi uyi-bibliophile, noma ngokwezwi nezwi "umsholozi wezincwadi".[4] 

Izincazelo 
Ekuguqulweni kwayo kwesimanjemanje, incwadi ngokuvamile yakhiwa amakhasi amaningi (ngokuvamile amaphepha, isikhumba, noma i-vellum) ahlanganiswe ndawonye onqenqemeni olulodwa futhi avikelwe isembozo. Ngokunwetshwa, incwadi isho okubhaliwe, okuphrintiwe, noma okuyingcaca kwencwadi.[5] Ingxenye eyodwa noma ukuhlukaniswa komsebenzi obhaliwe omude kungabuye kubizwe ngokuthi incwadi, ikakhulukazi eminye yemisebenzi eyaqanjwa kudala: ingxenye ngayinye ye-Aristotle's Physics, isibonelo, iyincwadi.[6] 

Kunzima ukwakha incazelo enembayo yencwadi eyichaza ngokucacile isuka kwezinye izinhlobo zezinto ezibhaliwe ngesikhathi namasiko. Incazelo yaleli gama ishintshe kakhulu ngokuhamba kwesikhathi ngokuvela kwemithombo yezokuxhumana.[7] Usomlando wezincwadi u-James Raven uye wasikisela ukuthi lapho kufundwa ukuthi izincwadi zisetshenziswe kanjani ukuxhumana, kufanele zichazwe ngendlela ehlanganisa kabanzi ngokuthi "izindlela eziphathekayo, ezihlala isikhathi eside, eziphindaphindekayo nezifundekayo" zokurekhoda nokusabalalisa ulwazi, kunokuncika ezicini ezibonakalayo noma ezingokomongo. Lokhu kuzobandakanya, isibonelo, ama-ebooks, amaphephandaba, kanye ne-quipus (uhlobo lokurekhoda okususelwe kufindo ngokomlando okwakusetshenziswa amasiko e-Andean South America), kodwa hhayi izinto ezimiswe endaweni efana nezikhumbuzo eziqoshiwe.[8][9]

Incazelo eqinile inikezwa yi-UNESCO: ngenhloso yokurekhoda izibalo zikazwelonke zokukhiqizwa kwezincwadi, incoma ukuthi incwadi ichazwe ngokuthi "ukushicilelwa okungaphrintiwe ngezikhathi ezithile okungenani okungamakhasi angama-49, okungahlanganisi amakhasi ekhava, ashicilelwe ezweni futhi enziwe atholakale emphakathini", iwahlukanise kwezinye izinto ezibhaliwe njengamapheshana.[5][10] Kovač et al. bayigxekile le ncazelo ngokuhluleka ukucabangela amafomethi amasha edijithali. Baphakamisa imibandela emine (ubude obuncane; okuqukethwe kombhalo; ifomu elinemingcele echaziwe; kanye "nesakhiwo solwazi" njengesakhiwo somugqa nezinye izici zombhalo) ezakha "isigaba sencwadi", lapho amafomethi agcwalisa imibandela eyengeziwe abhekwa njengefana kakhulu nencwadi evamile ephrintiwe.[11][12] 
Izindlela zokuqala zokubhala zaziqoshwe ezibhebheni, zishintsha zibe amahlamvu esundu ne-papyrus ezikhathini zasendulo. Isikhumba nephepha kamuva kwavela njengama-substrates abalulekile okwenza ubhuki, wethula ukuqina okukhulu nokufinyeleleka.[14] Kuzo zonke izifunda ezifana neShayina, iMpumalanga Ephakathi, iYurophu, neNingizimu Asia, kwavela izindlela ezihlukahlukene zokukhiqiza izincwadi. INkathi Ephakathi yabona ukwanda kwemibhalo yesandla ekhanyisiwe, exube ngokuyinkimbinkimbi umbhalo nemifanekiso, ikakhulukazi ngesikhathi sikaMughal eNingizimu ye-Asia ngaphansi kokusekelwa ngababusi abafana no-Akbar no-Shah Jahan.[15][16]

Nakuba ngolimi lwezemfundo i-monograph ingumsebenzi okhethekile esihlokweni esisodwa, kumtapo wolwazi kanye nesayensi yolwazi leli gama lisetshenziswa kabanzi ukuze lisho noma yikuphi ukushicilelwa okungeyona i-serial okuphelele kumqulu owodwa (incwadi ebonakalayo) noma inombolo eqondile yemiqulu (njengenoveli enevolumu eminingi), ngokungafani nokushicilelwa kwe-serial noma ngezikhathi ezithile.[13][6] 

Umlando 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umlando wezincwadi 

I-frontispiece eyinkimbinkimbi ye-Diamond Sutra evela ebukhosini base-Tang eShayina, okungukuthi 868 CE, incwadi endala kunazo zonke eyaziwayo enyathelisiwe emhlabeni (British Library) 
Umlando wezincwadi waba isiyalo semfundo esaziwayo ngeminyaka yawo-1980. Iminikelo kulo mkhakha iqhamuke kumfundaze wombhalo, i-codicology, i-bibliography, i-philology, i-palaeography, umlando wobuciko, umlando wezenhlalo kanye nomlando wamasiko. Ihlose ukukhombisa ukuthi incwadi njengento, hhayi nje umbhalo oqukethwe kuyo, iwumzila wokuxhumana phakathi kwabafundi namagama. Ukuhlaziywa kwengxenye ngayinye yencwadi kungadalula injongo yayo, ukuthi yayigcinwe kuphi futhi kanjani, yafundwa ubani, izinkolelo zemibono nezenkolo yangaleso sikhathi, nokuthi abafundi basebenzisana yini nombhalo ngaphakathi. Ngisho nokuntuleka kobufakazi obunjalo kungashiya imikhondo ebalulekile ngohlobo lwencwadi ethile. 
Imibhalo esemqoka: Ithebhulethi yobumba kanye nethebhulethi ye-Wax


Ngaphambi kokusungulwa komshini wokunyathelisa ngekhulu le-15, owaduma ngeBhayibheli likaGutenberg, umbhalo ngamunye wawuyisihloko esibalulekile esiyingqayizivele esenziwe ngesandla, esenziwe samuntu siqu ngezici zomklamo ezihlanganiswe umbhali, umnikazi, umdidiyeli wezincwadi, nomdwebi wezithombe.[17] Ukudalwa kwayo kuphawule isikhathi esibalulekile sokukhiqizwa kwencwadi. Ukuqamba okusha okufana nohlobo oluhambisekayo kanye nomshini wokunyathelisa osebenza ngesitimu kusheshise izinqubo zokukhiqiza futhi kube nomthelela ekwenyukeni kwamazinga okufunda nokubhala. Ukuvikelwa kwe-copyright nakho kwavela, kwavikela amalungelo ababhali futhi kwakha isimo sokushicilela.[18] Inkathi Yesimanje Sakamuva yethule izincwadi ze-chapbook, ezibhekelela abafundi abaningi, kanye nokwenziwa kwemishini yokunyathelisa kwathuthukisa ukusebenza kahle. 

Ikhulu lama-20 labona ukuvela kwemishini yokubhala, amakhompiyutha, nokunyathelisa ngedeskithophu, kwashintsha ukuklama nokunyathelisa imibhalo. Ukuthuthuka kwedijithali ekhulwini lama-21 kuholele ekwandeni kwama-ebook, okugqugquzelwa ukuduma kwezifundi nezici zokufinyeleleka. Nakuba izingxoxo ezimayelana nokwehla okungenzeka kwezincwadi zenyama ziye zavela, imidiya yokunyathelisa ibonakale ikwazi ukumelana nokuqina, iqhubeka ichuma njengemboni yezigidigidi zamadola.[19] Ukwengeza, imizamo yokwenza izincwadi zibandakanye kakhudlwana yavela, ngokuthuthukiswa kwe-Braille yabangaboni kahle kanye nokwakhiwa kwezincwadi ezikhulunywayo, okuhlinzeka ngezinye izindlela ukuze abantu ngabanye bathole futhi bajabulele izincwadi.[20] 


Izingcezwana Zemiyalo ye-Shuruppak, yasekuqaleni kwe-3rd millennium BC 
Ithebhulethi 
Imiqulu eyenziwe nge-papyrus yaqala ukusetshenziselwa ukubhala eGibhithe Lasendulo, mhlawumbe ekuqaleni koBukhosi Bokuqala, nakuba ubufakazi bokuqala buvela ezincwadini ze-akhawunti yeNkosi uNeferirkare Kakai Wobukhosi Besihlanu (cishe ngo-2400 BC). NgokukaHerodotus (Umlando 5:58), abaseFenike baletha ukubhala kanye ne-papyrus eGreece cishe ngekhulu le-10 noma lesi-9 BC. Kungakhathaliseki ukuthi yenziwa nge-papyrus, isikhumba, noma iphepha, imiqulu yayiwumthombo oyinhloko wokubhala emasikweni amaGreki, amaRoma, amaShayina, amaHebheru, namaMakedoniya. I-codex yayibusa ezweni lamaRoma kusukela kudala, kodwa imiqulu yaqhubeka isikhathi eside e-Asia.[catation needed]
Amanye amarekhodi alotshiwe okuqala enziwa ezibhebheni. Izibhebhe zobumba (izingcezu zobumba eziyisicaba ezigcizelelwe ngothi) zazisetshenziswa eMpumalanga Eseduze Yasendulo phakathi neNkathi Yethusi kanye naseNkathini Yensimbi, ikakhulukazi ekubhaleni nge-cuneiform. Amaphilisi e-wax (izingcezu zokhuni ezimbozwe ungqimba lwengcina) zazisetshenziswa ezikhathini zasendulo kanye nakuyo yonke iNkathi Ephakathi. 

Isiko lokuhlanganisa amaphilisi e-wax amaningana (ama-pugillare aseRoma) kuyisandulela sezincwadi zesimanje eziboshwe.[21] I-etymology yegama elithi codex (block of wood) isikisela ukuthi kungenzeka lavela ezibhebheni zengcina zokhuni.[22] 

Pheqa 
Isihloko esikhulu: 

Incwadi Yokuskrola Yabafileyo BaseHunefer; c. 1275 BC; uyinki nemibala e-papyrus; 45 × 90.5 cm; I-British Museum (London) 

I-Codex 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: 

Izincwadi ze-Codex Chinese bamboo zihlangabezana nencazelo yesimanje ye-codex. Le ncwadi ye-bamboo iyikhophi ye-Sun Tzu's The Art of War. 
I-codex ingukhokho wencwadi yesimanje, ehlanganisa amashidi anosayizi ofanayo aboshwe onqenqemeni olulodwa futhi ngokuvamile abanjwa phakathi kwekhava ezimbili ezenziwe ngezinto eziqinile. U-Isidore waseSeville (washona ngo-636) wachaza ubuhlobo obukhona ngaleso sikhathi phakathi kwe-codex, incwadi, kanye nomqulu encwadini yakhe ethi Etymologiae (VI.13): "I-codex yakhiwa izincwadi eziningi; incwadi iwumqulu owodwa. Ibizwa ngokuthi i-codex ngesingathekiso esivela eziqwini (codex) yezihlahla noma imivini, njengoba iqukethe inqwaba yezihlahla noma imivini, njengoba iqukethwe ngokhuni. babengamagatsha". 

Incwadi yokuqala okukhulunywa ngayo nge-codex njengohlobo lwencwadi ivela kuMartial, kweyakhe ethi Apophoreta CLXXXIV ekupheleni kwekhulu lokuqala, lapho etusa khona ukubumbana kwayo. Nokho, i-codex ayizange izuze ukuthandwa kakhulu ezweni lamaGreki, futhi emphakathini wamaKristu kuphela lapho yasetshenziswa khona kabanzi.[23] Lolu shintsho lwenzeka kancane kancane phakathi nekhulu lesi-3 nelesi-4, futhi izizathu zokwamukela uhlobo lwe-codex yale ncwadi zazimbalwa: ukuhleleka kwayo kwakuyonga kakhulu kunomqulu, njengoba kungasetshenziswa izinhlangothi zombili zezinto zokubhala; futhi ibiphatheka, isesheka, futhi kulula ukuyifihla. Ababhali abangamaKristu kungenzeka futhi babefuna ukuhlukanisa imibhalo yabo emibhalweni yobuqaba neyobuJuda eyayibhalwe emiqulwini. 

Amakhodi e-pre-Columbian Mesoamerica ayenesimo esifanayo ne-European codex, kodwa esikhundleni salokho enziwa ngemicu emide egoqiwe yegxolo lomkhiwane (amatl) noma imicu yezitshalo, ngokuvamile kusetshenziswa ungqimba olumhlophe olusetshenziswa ngaphambi kokubhala. Amakhodi ezwe Elisha abhalwa ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-16 (bheka amakhodi wamaMaya namakhodi wama-Aztec). Lawo abhalwa ngaphambi kokunqotshwa kweSpanishi kubonakala sengathi wonke kwakungamaphepha amade asongwe ngendlela yekhonsathi, ngezinye izikhathi ebhalwe nhlangothi zombili zephepha lendawo le-amatl. 

Umbhalo Wesandla 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umbhalo Wesandla 
Bheka futhi: Umbhalo wesandla weqabunga lesundu

I-Folio 14 recto yekhulu lesi-5 i-Vergilius Romanus iqukethe isithombe sombhali sika-Virgil. Qaphela isikhwama sezincwadi (i-capsa), indawo yokufunda kanye nombhalo obhalwe ngaphandle kwesikhala samagama ngosonhlamvukazi be-rustic.  
Imibhalo yesandla, imibhalo ebhalwe ngesandla futhi ekopishwe ngesandla, yayiwukuphela kwendlela yokubhala ngaphambi kokusungulwa nokwamukelwa kabanzi kokuphrinta. Kwenziwa intuthuko kumasu asetshenziswa ukuwadala.

Ekuqaleni koMbuso WaseRoma WaseNtshonalanga, izindlu zezindela zaqhubeka namasiko okubhala ngesiLatini ahlobene nobuKristu, futhi abefundisi babengabafundi nabakopishi abavelele. Inqubo yokwenza ubhuki yayiyinde futhi inzima. Ngokuvamile zazibhalwa esikhunjeni noma esikhunjeni, ezindaweni ezibhalwayo ezenziwe ngesikhumba sesilwane esigayiwe. Isikhumba kwakudingeka silungiswe, khona-ke amakhasi angaboshiwe ayehlelwa futhi abuswe ngethuluzi elibuthuntu noma umthofu, okwathi ngemva kwalokho umbhalo ubhalwa umbhali, owayevame ukushiya izindawo ezingenalutho ukuze kufanekiswe futhi kuxutshwe. Ekugcineni, yaboshwa umbhidi wezincwadi.[24] 

Ngenxa yobunzima obuhilelekile ekwenzeni nokukopisha izincwadi, zazibiza futhi ziyivelakancane. Izindela ezincane ngokuvamile zaziba nezincwadi ezimbalwa kuphela. Ngekhulu lesi-9, amaqoqo amakhulu ayephethe imiqulu engaba ngu-500 futhi ngisho nasekupheleni kweNkathi Ephakathi, umtapo wolwazi wopapa e-Avignon naseParis umtapo wezincwadi waseSorbonne wawunemiqulu engaba ngu-2,000 kuphela.[25] 

Ukwanda kwamanyuvesi ekhulwini le-13 kwabangela ukwanda kwesidingo sezincwadi, futhi kwavela isimiso esisha sokukopisha. Lezi zincwadi zahlukaniswa zaba amaqabunga angaboshiwe ( pecia ), ayebolekwa abakopishi abahlukahlukene, ngakho ijubane lokukhiqizwa kwezincwadi landa kakhulu. Lolu hlelo lwalunakekelwa izinhlangano zababhali bezwe, ezakhiqiza kokubili izinto ezingokwenkolo nezingezona ezenkolo.[26] 


Umbhali nombhali waseBurgundi uJean Miélot, wencwadi yakhe ethi Miracles de Notre Dame, yekhulu le-15 
ENdiya, imibhalo yesandla eboshiwe eyenziwe ngamagxolo e-birch noma iqabunga lesundu yayikhona kusukela kudala.[27] Umbhalo osemibhalweni yesandla yamaqabunga esundu wawuqoshwe ngepeni lommese emakhasini asikiwe angunxande futhi aphelisiwe amaqabunga esundu; Umbala wawube usufakwa phezulu bese wesulwa, ushiye uyinki emiseleni eqoshiwe. Ishidi ngalinye laliba nembobo okwakudlula kuyo intambo, futhi ngalezi amashidi ayehlanganiswa ngentambo ukuze ahlanganiswe njengencwadi. 

I-Woodblock printing 

Bagh print, indlela yokuphrinta ye-woodblock eyasungulwa e-Bagh, e-Madhya Pradesh, e-India 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukuphrinta kwe-Woodblock
Encwadini yokunyathelisa ye-woodblock, isithombe esiwusizo salo lonke ikhasi siqoshwa sibe amabhulokhi okhuni, anoyinki, bese sisetshenziselwa ukunyathelisa amakhophi alelo khasi. Yaqalwa esikhathini sobukhosi bakwaHan ngaphambi kuka-220 AD, yayisetshenziselwa ukuphrinta izindwangu kanye nephepha kamuva, futhi yayisetshenziswa kabanzi kulo lonke elaseMpumalanga Asia. Incwadi endala kunayo yonke eyanyatheliswa yile ndlela yi-The Diamond Sutra (868 AD). Indlela (ebizwa ngokuthi i-woodcut uma isetshenziswa kwezobuciko) yafika eYurophu ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-14. Izincwadi (ezaziwa ngokuthi i-block-books), kanye namakhadi okudlala nezithombe zenkolo, zaqala ukukhiqizwa ngale ndlela. Ukudala incwadi yonke kwakuyinqubo enzima, edinga ibhlokhi eqoshwe ngesandla ekhasini ngalinye, futhi izigxobo zokhuni zazikwazi ukuqhekeka uma zigcinwe isikhathi eside kakhulu. 

Uhlobo olunyakazayo kanye ne-incunabula 
Isihloko esikhulu: Iyashicilelwa 
Imibhalo esemqoka: Uhlobo olugudlukayo kanye neNgeke

Izimfundiso Ezikhethiwe Zezazi ZamaBuddha Nezazi ZeNdodana, incwadi yokuqala eyaziwayo eyanyatheliswa ngohlobo lwensimbi ehambayo, eyanyatheliswa eKorea, ngo-1377, i-Bibliothèque nationale de France 
Umsunguli waseShayina u-Bi Sheng wenza uhlobo lwezitsha zobumba ezigudlukayo c. 1045, kodwa azikho izibonelo ezaziwayo zokunyathelisa kwakhe. Cishe ngo-1450, uJohannes Gutenberg wasungula ngokuzimela uhlobo olunyakazayo e-Europe, kanye nezindlela ezintsha zokusakaza uhlobo olusekelwe ku-matrix nokubunjwa kwesandla. Lokhu kusungulwa kwenze ukuthi izincwadi zingabizi kakhulu ukuzikhiqiza futhi zatholakala kabanzi. Izincwadi zakuqala eziphrintiwe, amashidi angawodwa kanye nezithombe ezadalwa ngaphambi kuka-1501 e-Europe zaziwa njengezingalawuleki noma ezingalawuleki.[28] 


Ikhulu le-15 
Ikhulu le-19 elingenakunqotshwa ukwethula 
imishini yokunyathelisa ye-Steam yaqala ukuduma ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19. Le mishini ingaphrinta amashidi angu-1,100 ngehora,[29] kodwa izisebenzi zazikwazi ukusetha izinhlamvu ezingu-2,000 kuphela ngehora.[ecashunwa] Imishini yokuhlela yohlobo lwe-Monotype kanye ne-linotype yethulwa ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19. Bangakwazi ukusetha izinhlamvu ezingaphezu kwezi-6,000 ngehora kanye nomugqa wonke wohlobo ngesikhathi esisodwa. Kube nentuthuko eminingi emshinini wokunyathelisa. Maphakathi nekhulu lama-20, ukukhiqizwa kwezincwadi zaseYurophu kwase kukhuphuke kwaba nezihloko ezingaphezu kuka-200,000 ngonyaka. 

Phakathi nekhulu lama-20, imitapo yezincwadi ibhekene nezinga elikhula njalo lokunyathelisa, ngezinye izikhathi elibizwa ngokuthi ukuqhuma kokwaziswa. Ukufika kokushicilela nge-elekthronikhi kanye ne-inthanethi kusho ukuthi ulwazi olusha luvame ukushicilelwa ku-inthanethi kunasezincwadini eziphrintiwe, isibonelo ngomtapo wolwazi wedijithali. Ubuchwepheshe be-"Print on demand", okwenza kube nokwenzeka ukuphrinta nje ezimbalwa njengencwadi eyodwa ngesikhathi, buye benza ukuzishicilela (nokushicilela okuyize) kwaba lula kakhulu futhi kwafinyeleleka kakhudlwana, futhi buye bavumela abashicileli ukuthi bagcine izincwadi ezithengiswa kancane ziphrintiwe kunokuba bamemezele ukuthi aziphrintiwe. 

Ukushicilelwa kwamanje
Njengamanje, izincwadi zikhiqizwa inkampani yokushicilela ukuze zifakwe emakethe ngabasabalalisi nezitolo zezincwadi. Umshicileli uxoxisana ngesivumelwano somthetho esisemthethweni nababhali ukuze athole ilungelo lobunikazi elisebenzayo, bese ehlela ukuthi akhiqizwe futhi adayiswe. Izinyathelo ezinkulu zenqubo yokushicilela yilezi: ukuhlela nokuhlola umsebenzi ozoshicilelwa; ukuklama incwadi ephrintiwe; ukukhiqiza izincwadi; kanye nokuthengisa izincwadi, okuhlanganisa ukumaketha nokuphromotha. Ngasinye salezi zinyathelo ngokuvamile sithathwa izinkampani zezinkampani zangaphandle ezikhokhelwa umshicileli.[30] Lokhu kuphambene nokuzishicilela, lapho umbhali ekhokhela ukukhiqizwa nokusatshalaliswa komsebenzi wakhe futhi alawule ezinye noma zonke izinyathelo zenqubo yokushicilela.[31] 

Ukushicilela ngolimi lwesiNgisi okwamanje kubuswa abashicileli ababizwa ngokuthi "Ama-Big Five": i-Penguin Random House, i-Hachette Book Group, i-HarperCollins, i-Simon & Schuster, ne-Macmillan Publishers. Balinganiselwa ukuthi benze cishe amaphesenti angama-60 emakethe yezincwadi zokufunda okuvamile ngo-2021.[32] 

Idizayini 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Idizayini yencwadi 
Idizayini yencwadi iwubuciko bokufaka okuqukethwe, isitayela, ifomethi, umklamo, nokulandelana kwezici ezihlukahlukene zencwadi ibe yiyunithi ehambisanayo.[33] 

Isakhiwo 
Bheka futhi: Umdwebo wekhasi 


Umdwebo wencwadi Ibhande 
le-Belly 
I-Flap 
Endpaper 
Cover 
Head 
Fore edge 
Umsila 
Ikhasi kwesokudla (recto uma ukuphrinta kushiywe kwesokudla, verso uma kwesokudla kuye kwesokunxele) 
Ikhasi kwesokunxele (verso uma ukuphrinta kushiywe kwesokudla, recto uma kwesokudla kuya kwesokunxele) 
Umsele
Izincwadi zesimanje zihlelwa ngendlela ethile ebizwa ngokuthi isakhiwo sencwadi. Nakuba kunomehluko omkhulu ekuhlelweni, izincwadi zesimanje zivame ukunamathela eqoqweni lemithetho maqondana nokuthi ziyini izingxenye zesakhiwo nokuthi okuqukethwe kwazo ngokuvamile kuhlanganisani. Isakhiwo esiyisisekelo sizobandakanya ikhava yangaphambili, ikhava yangemuva kanye nokuqukethwe kwencwadi okubizwa ngokuthi ikhophi yayo yomzimba noma amakhasi okuqukethwe. Ikhava yangaphambili ivamise ukuba nesihloko sencwadi (kanye nesihlokwana, uma sikhona) kanye negama lombhali noma abahleli bayo. Ikhasi elingaphakathi lekhava elingaphambili livamise ukushiywa lingenalutho kuzo zombili izincwadi ezinoqwembe oluqinile namaphepha. Isigaba esilandelayo, uma sikhona, siwudaba oluphambili lwencwadi, oluhlanganisa konke okubhaliwe ngemva kwekhava yangaphambili kodwa hhayi ingxenye yokuqukethwe kwencwadi njengesandulelo, ukunikezelwa, uhlu lokuqukethwe kanye nedatha yomshicileli njengenguqulo yencwadi noma inombolo yokunyathelisa kanye nendawo eshicilelwe kuyo. Phakathi kwekhophi yomzimba nesembozo sangemuva kuhamba udaba lokugcina olungahlanganisa noma yiziphi izinkomba, amasethi amathebula, imidwebo, uhlu lwamagama noma uhlu lwemisebenzi ekhonjiwe (nakuba incwadi ehleliwe enababhali abaningana ngokuvamile ibeka imisebenzi ekhonjiwe ekupheleni kwesahluko ngasinye esigunyaziwe). Ikhasi lekhava elingaphakathi elingemuva, njengalelo elingaphakathi kwekhava yangaphambili, ngokuvamile alinalutho. Ikhava engemuva iyindawo evamile ye-ISBN yencwadi futhi mhlawumbe nesithombe sombhali(ababhali)/abahleli), mhlawumbe nesingeniso esifushane kubo. Futhi lapha kuvame ukuvela izifinyezo zesakhiwo, amabhakhodi kanye nokubuyekezwa okucashuniwe kwencwadi.[34] 

Indikimba yezincwadi imvamisa ihlukaniswe yaba izingxenye, izahluko, izigaba futhi kwesinye isikhathi izigatshana ezakhiwe okungenani isigaba noma ngaphezulu. 
Umdwebo wencwadi weqhude elikhala libheke elangeni eliphuma nendoda, egqoke i-nightcap nengubo yokulala, encike ngefasitela. Ingemuva libonisa abantu ababili abancane abahamba ngomgwaqo obiyelwe.
 
Usayizi 
Isihloko esikhulu: Usayizi wencwadi
Ubukhulu bencwadi ngokuvamile bulinganiswa ngobude obuqhathaniswa nobubanzi beqabunga, noma ngezinye izikhathi ukuphakama nobubanzi bekhava yayo.[35] Uchungechunge lwamagama avame ukusetshenziswa imitapo yolwazi yamanje nabashicileli kumasayizi ajwayelekile ezincwadi zamanje lusukela ku-folio (elikhulu kakhulu), kuye ku-quarto (elincane) kanye ne-octavo (esencane). Ngokomlando, la magama ayebhekisela kufomethi yencwadi, igama lobuchwepheshe elisetshenziswa abaphrinta nababhali bezincwadi ukukhombisa usayizi weqabunga ngokuya ngosayizi weshidi lokuqala. Isibonelo, i-quarto kwakuyincwadi enyatheliswe emakhasini ephepha eligoqwe kabili, eligoqelwe kuqala libe ngama-engeli angakwesokudla kuya kweyesibili, ukuze kukhiqizwe amaqabunga angu-4 (noma amakhasi angu-8), iqabunga ngalinye libe ingxenye yesine elilingana nephepha lokuqala eliphrintiwe - phawula ukuthi iqabunga libhekisela ephepheni elilodwa, kanti ikhasi liwuhlangothi olulodwa lweqabunga. Ngenxa yokuthi ukwakheka kwangempela kwezincwadi eziningi zanamuhla akunakutholakala ekuhloleni izincwadi, ababhali bezincwadi bangase bangawasebenzisi la magama ezincazelweni zezazi. 

Umfanekiso 
I-athikili eyinhloko: Umdwebo wencwadi 
Umdwebo ovela "Endlini Eyakhiwe UJack" kokuthi Iqoqo Eliphelele Lezithombe Nezingoma; ukuqoshwa nokuphrinta kuka-Edmund Evans, umfanekiso ka-Randolph Caldecott (1887) 
Nakuba uhlobo oluthile lomfanekiso wencwadi lukhona kusukela ekusungulweni kokubhala, isiko lesimanje laseNtshonalanga lemifanekiso laqala ngezincwadi zebhulokhi zekhulu le-15, lapho umbhalo wencwadi nemifanekiso kwasikwa ebhulokhini efanayo.[36] Amasu anjengokuqopha, i-etching, ne-lithography nawo abe nomthelela. 

Ukukhiqiza 

Izinhlamvu eziningana zezincwadi ezivezwe eshalofini 
Izindlela ezisetshenziselwa ukunyathelisa nokuhlanganisa izincwadi zaqhubeka zingashintshile kusukela ekhulwini le-15 kuya ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20. Nakuba kwakunemishini eyengeziwe, iphrinta yezincwadi ngo-1900 yayisasebenzisa uhlobo lwensimbi olugudlukayo oluhlanganiswe lube amagama, imigqa, namakhasi ukuze kwenziwe amakhophi. Izincwadi zamaphepha zanamuhla zinyatheliswa ephepheni eliklanyelwe ukuphrinta. Ngokwesiko, amaphepha ezincwadi angamaphepha amhlophe-mhlophe noma amhlophe kancane (afundeka kalula), ane-opaque ukuze kuncishiswe umbukiso wombhalo usuka kolunye uhlangothi lwekhasi uye kolunye futhi (ngokuvamile) enziwa ukuze aqine kakhulu ukucaciswa kwe-caliper noma ukujiya, ikakhulukazi ezincwadini ezinamakesi. Izimfanelo zephepha ezihlukene zisetshenziswa kuye ngohlobo lwencwadi: Amaphepha aqediwe ngomshini amboziwe, amaphepha angafakwanga ngamapulangwe angenalutho, amaphepha acolekile anamekiwe namaphepha amahle akhethekile angamamaki ephepha avamile. 


Inoveli yango-1870 ethi The Seven Brothers ka-Aleksis Kivi yaqale yashicilelwa ngemiqulu emine emifushane.
Namuhla, iningi lezincwadi linyatheliswa nge-offset lithography.[37] Lapho incwadi inyatheliswa, amakhasi abekwa epuletini ukuze ngemva kokuba ishidi eliphrintiwe seligoqiwe amakhasi azolandelana ngendlela efanele. Izincwadi zivame ukukhiqizwa namuhla ngamasayizi ambalwa ajwayelekile. Amasayizi ezincwadi ngokuvamile acaciswa "njengosayizi wokunquma": usayizi wekhasi ngemva kokuba ishidi ligoqwe futhi lisikwa. Osayizi abajwayelekile bavela kumasayizi amashidi (ngakho-ke osayizi bemishini) abaduma eminyakeni engama-200 noma engama-300 edlule, futhi sebezobusa imboni. Imihlangano yaseBrithani mayelana nalokhu idlangile kuwo wonke umhlaba okhuluma isiNgisi, ngaphandle kwase-US. Imboni yokukhiqiza izincwadi yaseYurophu isebenza ngesethi yezindinganiso ezihluke ngokuphelele. 

Izincwadi ezinoqwembe oluqinile zinesibopho esiqinile, kuyilapho izincwadi ezinoqwembe oluqinile zinekhava eshibhile, eguquguqukayo evame ukungahlali isikhathi eside. Abashicileli bangase bakhiqize amakhophi ashibhile angaphambi kokushicilelwa aziwa ngokuthi ama-galley noma "ubufakazi obubophekile" ngezinjongo zokuphromotha, njengokwenza izibuyekezo ngaphambi kokushicilelwa. Amagalaji ngokuvamile enziwa ngemali ephansi, njengoba engahloselwe ukudayiswa. 

Ukuphrinta 
 
Lesi sigaba sidinga izingcaphuno ezengeziwe ukuze siqinisekiswe. Sicela usize ukuthuthukisa lesi sihloko ngokwengeza izingcaphuno emithonjeni ethembekile kulesi sigaba. Izinto ezingatholakali zingaphikiswa futhi zisuswe. (Februwari 2024) (Funda ukuthi ungawususa kanjani futhi nini lo mlayezo)
Ezinye izincwadi, ikakhulukazi lezo ezinemijikelezo emifushane (okungukuthi ezinamakhophi ambalwa) zizophrintwa emshinini wokunyathelisa we-offset we-sheet-fed, kodwa izincwadi eziningi manje zinyatheliswa emishinini yokunyathelisa yewebhu, ephakelwa umqulu wephepha oqhubekayo, futhi ngenxa yalokho ingaphrinta amakhophi engeziwe ngesikhathi esifushane. Njengoba umugqa wokukhiqiza uzungeza, "incwadi" ephelele iqoqwa ndawonye esitakini esisodwa samakhasi, bese omunye umshini ufeza ukugoqa, ukuncenga, nokuhlanganisa amakhasi abe yinqwaba yesiginesha (izigaba zamakhasi) alungele ukungena emgqeni wokuqoqa. Amakhasi encwadi anyatheliswa amabili ngesikhathi, hhayi njengencwadi eyodwa ephelele. Izinombolo ezeqile ziphrintwa ukuze kulungiswe noma yikuphi ukumoshakala ngenxa yezinto ezenziwe kahle noma amakhasi okuhlola ukuze kuqinisekiswe ikhwalithi yokugcina yokuphrinta. 

I-make-ready umsebenzi wokulungiselela owenziwa abanyathelisi ukuze umshini wokunyathelisa ufinyelele izinga elidingekayo lokunyathelisa. Okufakiwe ekulungiseni isikhathi esithathwayo ukukhweza ipuleti emshinini, uhlanze noma yikuphi ukungcola emsebenzini wangaphambilini, futhi wenze umshini wokunyathelisa ube nesivinini. Ngokushesha nje lapho umshini wokunyathelisa enquma ukuthi ukunyathelisa kulungile, wonke amaphepha azilungiselayo azolahlwa, futhi umshini wokunyathelisa uzoqala ukwenza izincwadi. Ukulungisa okufanayo kwenzeka ezindaweni zokugoqa nezokubopha, ngayinye ebandakanya ukumoshakala kwephepha.
 
Intuthuko yakamuva ekukhiqizweni kwezincwadi ihlanganisa ukuthuthukiswa kokuphrinta kwedijithali. Amakhasi ezincwadi aphrintiwe, ngendlela efanayo naleyo esebenza ngayo umkopishi wasehhovisi, esebenzisa i-toner kunoyinki. Incwadi ngayinye inyatheliswa ngephasi eyodwa, hhayi njengamasiginesha ahlukene. Ukuphrinta kwedijithali kuye kwavumela ukwakhiwa kwezinto ezincane kakhulu kune-offset, ngokwengxenye ngenxa yokungabikho kwezinto ezilungiswayo kanye nokonakala. Ukuphrinta kwedijithali kuye kwavula ithuba lokuphrinta-ngokufunwa, lapho kungekho zincwadi eziphrintwa kuze kube ngemva kokutholwa kwe-oda elivela kukhasimende. 


Ukuphakama okungamamitha angu-12 (40 ft) umfanekiso oqoshiwe wenqwaba yezincwadi e-Berlin Walk of Ideas, okukhumbula ukusungulwa kokunyathelisa kwezincwadi zesimanje 
I-Binding 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukuhlanganisa izincwadi 
Ngemva kokuba amasiginesha esegoqiwe futhi aqoqwa, aya endaweni yokuhlanganisa izincwadi. Maphakathi nekhulu leminyaka elidlule kwakusenezinkampani eziningi ezihlanganisa ukuhweba—izinkampani ezibopha zodwa ezingazange zinyathelise, ezigxile ekubopheni zodwa. Ngaleso sikhathi, ngenxa yokubusa kokunyathelisa kwe-letterpress, ukuhlelwa kwezinhlamvu nokunyathelisa kwenzeka endaweni eyodwa, futhi kuhlanganiswe embonini ehlukile. Uma uhlobo kuyinsimbi yonke, inani lencwadi evamile lingaba likhulu, libe ntekenteke futhi libe nzima. Uma inyakaziswa kancane kulesi simo kuba ngcono: ngakho ukunyathelisa kwakuzokwenziwa endaweni efanayo nokuhlelwa kwezinhlamvu. Ngakolunye uhlangothi amashidi aphrintiwe ayenganyakaziswa kalula. Manje, ngenxa yokwanda kwekhompiyutha yokulungiselela incwadi yephrinta, ingxenye yokuhlela uhlobo yomsebenzi iye yakhuphuka yakhuphuka, lapho kwenziwa khona izinkampani ezihlukene ezisebenzela umshicileli, ngabashicileli ngokwabo, noma ngisho nababhali. Ukuhlanganiswa embonini yokukhiqiza izincwadi kusho ukuthi akusajwayelekile manje ukuthola umshini wokuhlanganisa izincwadi ongabandakanyeki ekunyatheliseni izincwadi (futhi okuphambene nalokho).

Uma incwadi iyi-hardback indlela yayo ngokusebenzisa i-bindery izobandakanya amaphuzu amaningi omsebenzi kunokuba ingemuva lephepha. Ukubophezela okungavaliwe manje kuya ngokuya kuvama. Amasiginesha encwadi angabuye abanjwe ndawonye ngokuthi "Ukuthunga okukaSmyth" kusetshenziswa izinaliti, "ukuthunga kukaMcCain", kusetshenziswa izimbobo ezibhoboziwe ezivame ukusetshenziswa ekuhlanganiseni izincwadi zesikole, noma "ukubopha i-notch", lapho amabhomu angaba yi-intshi ubude enziwa ngezikhathi ezithile ngokugoqa umgogodla wesiginesha ngayinye. Yonke enye inqubo yokubopha iyafana kuzo zonke izimo. Izincwadi ezithungiwe neziboshiwe zingaboshelwa njengama-hardback noma amaphepha. 

Ukuqeda 
Isihloko esikhulu se- : I-Ebook 
A Kindle e-reader 
"Ukwenza izimo" kwenzeka ungaxhunyiwe ku-inthanethi futhi ngaphambi kokufika kwebhuku emugqeni wokubopha. Ekwenziweni kwecala eliyisisekelo, izingcezu ezimbili zekhadibhodi zibekwe phezu kwendwangu enamathiselwe enesikhala phakathi kwazo okunamathiselwe kuso ibhodi elincanyana elisikwe ububanzi bomgogodla wencwadi. Imiphetho egqagqene yendwangu (cishe 5/8" nxazonke) igoqwe phezu kwamabhodi, futhi icindezelwe phansi ukuze ibambelele.Ngemuva kokwenza inqwaba yamacala izoya endaweni yokugxiviza ye-foil ukuze kwengezwe imihlobiso kanye nohlobo.

Ukudayisa nokusabalalisa 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukuthengisa Amabhuku 
Ukudayiswa kwezincwadi ukuhwebelana kwezincwadi okwenza ukuthengisa nokusabalalisa isiphetho senqubo yokushicilela. 

Ukushicilela okufinyelelekayo 
I-athikili eyinhloko: Ukushicilela okufinyelelekayo 
Isibonelo somuntu osebenzisa isifundi sesikrini ebonisa amadokhumenti angafinyeleleki, afundekayo futhi afinyelelekayo 
Ukushicilela okufinyelelekayo kuyindlela yokushicilela nokwakheka kwencwadi lapho izincwadi neminye imibhalo yenziwa itholakale ngezinye izindlela eziklanyelwe ukusiza noma ukufaka esikhundleni senqubo yokufunda. Kubaluleke kakhulu kubantu abayizimpumputhe, abangaboni kahle noma abakhubazeke ukuphrinta. 

Amanye amafomethi akhiwe ukuze asize abantu abahlukene ukuthi bawafunde afaka izinhlobonhlobo zamafonti amakhulu, amafonti akhethekile ezinhlobo ezithile zokukhubazeka kokufunda, i-braille, ama-ebook, nama-audiobook azenzakalelayo kanye nezincwadi zokukhuluma zedijithali ze-DAISY. 

Ukushicilela okufinyelelekayo kwenziwe kwaba lula ngentuthuko yezobuchwepheshe njengokuphrinta ngokufunwa, izifundi ze-ebook, ifomethi yedatha ehlelekile ye-XML, ifomethi ye-EPUB3 kanye ne-inthanethi. 

Ama-audiobooks 
Isihloko esikhulu: I-audiobook 
I-audiobook noma incwadi yokukhuluma iwukurekhodwa kwencwadi noma omunye umsebenzi ofundelwa phezulu. Ukufundwa kombhalo ophelele kuchazwa ngokuthi "okungafinyeziwe", kuyilapho ukufundwa kwezinguqulo ezifushane kuwukufinyeza. 

Umsindo okhulunywayo ubulokhu utholakala ezikoleni nasemitapo yolwazi yomphakathi futhi kancane kancane ezitolo zomculo kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1930s. Ama-albhamu amaningi akhulunywayo enziwa ngaphambi kweminyaka yamakhasethi, ama-compact disc, nomsindo olandekayo, ngokuvamile wezinkondlo nemidlalo kunezincwadi. Kwaze kwaba ngama-1980s lapho i-medium yaqala ukuheha abathengisi bezincwadi, kwase kuthi abathengisi bezincwadi baqala ukubonisa ama-audiobook emashalofini ezincwadi kunokuboniswa okuhlukile. 

I-Ebooks 

I-ebook (ifushane ngencwadi ye-elekthronikhi), nayo epelwe nge-e-book noma i-eBook, iyincwadi eshicilelwe etholakala ngendlela ye-elekthronikhi, ehlanganisa umbhalo, izithombe, noma kokubili, efundeka esibukweni sephaneli eyisicaba samakhompyutha noma ezinye izinto zikagesi.[38] Nakuba ngezinye izikhathi kuchazwa "njengenguqulo ye-elekthronikhi yencwadi ephrintiwe",[39] amanye ama-ebook akhona ngaphandle kokunyathelisa okulingana nawo. Ama-ebooks angafundwa kumadivayisi azinikele e-e-reader nakunoma iyiphi idivayisi yekhompyutha enesikrini sokubuka esilawulekayo, okuhlanganisa amakhompyutha edeskithophu, amakhompyutha aphathekayo, amathebulethi nama-smartphone. 

Kwezinye izimakethe, ukuthengiswa kwezincwadi eziphrintiwe kwehlile ngenxa yokwanda kokusetshenziswa kwama-ebook. Nokho, izincwadi eziphrintiwe zisadayisa kakhulu ama-ebooks, futhi abantu abaningi bathanda ukuphrinta.[40][41][42][43] 

Izincwadi eziyidumi 

Ugwayi ushushumbiswa nencwadi 
Izincwadi ze-Dummy (noma izincwadi zomgunyathi) ziyizincwadi eziklanyelwe ukulingisa incwadi yangempela ngokubukeka ukuze bakhohlise abantu, ezinye izincwadi zingase zibe namakhasi angenalutho, ezinye zingase zingenalutho noma kwezinye izimo, kungase kube nephaneli eliqoshwe ngomgogodla elibe selipendwe ukuze libukeke njengezincwadi, izihloko zezinye izincwadi nazo zingase zibe eziqanjiwe. 

Ziningi izizathu zokuthi kube nezincwadi ezibukwayo ezinjengalezi; ukubhekisela ezivakashini ngengcebo eningi yokwaziswa ezikuzo kanye nokwandisa ukubukeka komnikazi womcebo, ukufihla okuthile,[44] ukuze kuboniswe ezitolo noma ngezinjongo zokuhlobisa. 

Ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19 eGwrych Castle, eNyakatho Wales, uLloyd Hesketh Bamford-Hesketh wayaziwa ngeqoqo lakhe elikhulu lezincwadi emtatsheni wakhe wezincwadi, nokho, engxenyeni yakamuva yalelo khulu leminyaka, umphakathi waqaphela ukuthi izingxenye zomtapo wolwazi wakhe zaziyizinto eziqanjiwe, izincwadi eziyizidumi zakhiwa zase zikhiywa ngemuva kweminyango yengilazi ukuze kuvinjwe abantu ukuthi bazame ukuzifinyelela, kusukela kulo mtapo wezincwadi, ngaphandle".[45][46] 

Okuqukethwe 

Lesi sigaba sidinga izingcaphuno ezengeziwe ukuze siqinisekiswe. Sicela usize ukuthuthukisa lesi sihloko ngokwengeza izingcaphuno emithonjeni ethembekile kulesi sigaba. Izinto ezingatholakali zingaphikiswa futhi zisuswe. (Februwari 2024) (Funda ukuthi ungawususa kanjani futhi nini lo mlayezo) 

Amanoveli esitolo sezincwadi 
Imitapo yolwazi, izitolo zezincwadi, namaqoqo ngokuvamile ahlukanisa izincwadi zibe izinganekwane nezingezona izinganekwane, nakuba ezinye izinhlobo zikhona ngale kwalokhu. Ezinye izincwadi, ezihlala zingashicilelwe noma ezishicilelwe ngokuyinhloko njengengxenye yemisebenzi yebhizinisi ehlukene (njengezinhlu zezingcingo) akumele zithengiswe izitolo zezincwadi noma ziqoqwe imitapo yolwazi. Imibhalo yesandla, ama-logbook namanye amarekhodi angahlukaniswa futhi agcinwe ngendlela ehlukile ngamaqoqo akhethekile noma izinqolobane zomlando. Izincwadi 

ze-Fiction 
Fiction ziqukethe izinto eziqanjiwe, ngokuvamile ezilandisayo. Ezinye izinhlobo zemibhalo njengezinkondlo zifakiwe esigabeni esibanzi. Iningi lezinganekwane lihlukaniswa ngokwengeza ngohlobo lwemibhalo nohlobo.

Inoveli iwuhlobo olujwayeleke kakhulu lwencwadi yezinganekwane. Amanoveli ayimisebenzi enwetshiwe yenganekwane elandisayo, ngokuvamile enesakhiwo, isizinda, izingqikithi nabalingiswa. Inoveli ibe nomthelela omkhulu kwezokuzijabulisa kanye nezimakethe zokushicilela.[47][umthombo ongcono odingekayo] I-novella igama ngezinye izikhathi elisetshenziselwa iphrozi eqanjiwe ngokuvamile phakathi kwamagama ayi-17,500 nangu-40,000, kanye ne-novelette ephakathi kuka-7,500 no-17,500. Indaba emfushane ingaba yinoma yibuphi ubude bufike kumagama ayi-10,000, kodwa lawa magama ubude ayahluka. 

Izincwadi zamahlaya noma amanoveli ayingcaca ayizincwadi lapho kuboniswa khona indaba. Abalingiswa nabalandisi basebenzisa amabhamuza enkulumo noma emicabango ukuze baveze ulimi lomlomo. Izincwadi 

ezingezona 
 
Ikhasi elivela kusichazamazwi
izinganekwane zisekelwe eqinisweni, ezihlanganisa izifundo ezifana nomlando, ezombusazwe, izindaba zezenhlalo nezamasiko, kanye nemibhalo ephilayo kanye nezikhumbuzo. Cishe zonke izincwadi zemfundo azizona izinganekwane. 

Izikhombo 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umsebenzi oyireferensi 
Izincwadi eziyizinkomba ziyizincwadi ezingezona ezinganekwane ezihloselwe ukusheshe zibhekiselwe kuzo ukuze uthole ulwazi, kunokuba zifundwe ekuqaleni kuye ekugcineni. Isitayela sokubhala esisetshenziswe kule misebenzi siyafundisa; ababhali bagwema imibono kanye nokusetshenziswa komuntu wokuqala, futhi bagcizelele amaqiniso. 

I-almanaka iyincwadi eyireferensi evamile kakhulu, ngokuvamile eyivolumu eyodwa, enohlu lwedatha nolwazi ngezihloko eziningi. I-encyclopedia iyincwadi noma isethi yezincwadi eziklanyelwe ukuba nezindatshana ezijulile ngezihloko eziningi. Incwadi ebhala amagama, i-etymology yawo, izincazelo, nolunye ulwazi ibizwa ngokuthi isichazamazwi. I-atlas yincwadi equkethe iqoqo lamamephu. Incwadi yereferensi eyisipesheli enikeza ulwazi mayelana nenkambu ethile noma indlela yokusebenza, ngokuvamile ehloselwe ukusetshenziswa ngochwepheshe, ngokuvamile ibizwa ngokuthi ibhuku lesandla. Izincwadi ezizama ukwenza uhlu lwezikhombo nezifinyezo endaweni ethile ebanzi zingabizwa ngokuthi inkomba, njenge-Engineering Index, noma izifushaniso ezifana nezingcaphuno zamakhemikhali nezifushaniso zebhayoloji. 

I-Technical 
Bheka futhi: Ukubhala ngobuchwepheshe Izincwadi ze 

-atlas 
ezinolwazi lobuchwepheshe lokuthi kwenziwa kanjani okuthile noma indlela yokusebenzisa ezinye izinto ezisetshenziswayo zibizwa ngokuthi iziyalezo zeziqondiso. Ezinye izincwadi ezidumile zokuthi kwenziwa kanjani zifaka izincwadi zokupheka nezincwadi zokuthuthukisa ikhaya. Abafundi 

Bezemfundo 
bavame ukuphatha izincwadi nezincwadi zesikole ngezinjongo zokufunda. Izincwadi ze-Lap ziyithuluzi lokufunda elenziwe ngabafundi. Abafundi besikole samabanga aphansi bavame ukusebenzisa izincwadi zokusebenza, ezishicilelwa ezinezikhala noma izikhala ukuze zigcwaliswe yibo ukuze batadishe noma benze umsebenzi wesikole wasekhaya. Emfundweni ephakeme yase-US, kuvamile ukuba umfundi abhale isivivinyo esebenzisa incwadi eluhlaza okwesibhakabhaka. Isihloko esikhulu 

sezenkolo 
: Umbhalo wezenkolo
Imibhalo yezenkolo, okuhlanganisa nemibhalo, imibhalo izinkolo ezehlukene eziyithatha njengebalulekile esikweni lazo lezenkolo. Ngokuvamile zihlanganisa inhlanganisela noma ingxoxo yezinkolelo, imikhuba yemikhuba, imiyalo nemithetho yokuziphatha, ukuziphatha okuhle, izifiso ezingokomoya, neziyalezo zokukhuthaza umphakathi wenkolo. 

Amahubo izincwadi ezinamaqoqo ezingoma zomculo ngokuvamile ezingatholakala emasontweni. Izincwadi zomkhuleko noma imicibisholo ziyizincwadi eziqukethe imithandazo ebhaliwe futhi ngokuvamile ziphathwa izindela, izindela, nabanye abalandeli abazinikele noma abefundisi. 

Izincwadi Zezingane 
Lesi sigaba sicashunwe ezincwadini zezingane.[ hlela ]
 
Umama ufundela izingane zakhe phakathi nekhulu le-19 leminyaka le-lithograph kaJessie Willcox Smith.
Izincwadi zezingane noma izincwadi zezingane zihlanganisa izindaba, izincwadi, omagazini, nezinkondlo ezidalelwe izingane. Ukwengeza ezinhlotsheni zemibhalo ezijwayelekile, izincwadi zezingane zesimanje zihlukaniswa ngeminyaka ehlosiwe yomfundi, kusukela ezincwadini zezithombe zabancane kakhulu kuye kwezinganekwane zabantu abadala abancane kulabo abasondela ekuvuthweni. 

Izincwadi zezingane zingalandelelwa ezindabeni zendabuko ezifana nezinganekwane, ezihlonzwe kuphela njengezincwadi zezingane kusukela ngekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalombili, namaculo, ayingxenye yesiko elibanzi elidluliselwa ngomlomo, abantu abadala ababehlanganyela nezingane ngaphambi kokuba bashicilele. Ukuthuthukiswa kwezincwadi zezingane zakuqala, ngaphambi kokuba kusungulwe ukuphrinta, kunzima ukulandelela. Ngisho nangemva kokuba ukuphrinta kusabalele, izinganekwane eziningi zakudala "zezingane" zaqale zadalelwa abantu abadala futhi kamuva zaguqulelwa izethameli ezincane. Kusukela ngekhulu leshumi nanhlanu izincwadi eziningi beziqondiswe ikakhulukazi ezinganeni, ngokuvamile ezinomyalezo wokuziphatha noma wenkolo. Izincwadi zezingane ziye zalolongwa imithombo yezenkolo, njengamasiko amaPuritan, noma imibono eyengeziwe yefilosofi nesayensi ngemithonya kaCharles Darwin noJohn Locke.[48] Ekupheleni kwekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalolunye nasekuqaleni kwekhulu lamashumi amabili kwaziwa ngokuthi "Inkathi Yegolide Yezincwadi Zezingane" ngoba izincwadi eziningi zezingane zakudala zanyatheliswa ngaleso sikhathi. 

Ikhasi elivela ebhukwini lokubhalela elisetshenziswa njengedayari ebhalwe ngesandla 
Engashicilelwe 
Bheka futhi: Uhlu lwezincwadi ezingakashicilelwa 
Izincwadi eziningi zisetshenziselwa ukurekhoda imibono yomuntu siqu, amanothi, nama-akhawunti, njengezincwadi, izincwadi zokungena, izincwadi ezivamile, nedayari. Lezi zincwadi azivamile ukushicilelwa futhi zivame ukucekelwa phansi noma zihlale ziyimfihlo. 

Izincwadi zamakheli, amabhuku ocingo, kanye nekhalenda/amabhuku e-aphoyintimenti avame ukusetshenziselwa ukurekhoda ama-aphoyintimenti, imihlangano kanye nolwazi lokuxhumana lomuntu siqu. Amabhizinisi ngokomlando ayesebenzisa izincwadi zokubala ezifana namajenali namaleja ukuze aqophe idatha yezezimali ngendlela ebizwa ngokuthi ukugcinwa kwamabhuku (manje okuvamile okugcinwe kumakhompyutha esikhundleni sefomu elibhalwe ngesandla). 

Ukuqoqwa nokuhlelwa 

Lesi sigaba sidinga izingcaphuno ezengeziwe ukuze siqinisekiswe. Sicela usize ukuthuthukisa lesi sihloko ngokwengeza izingcaphuno emithonjeni ethembekile kulesi sigaba. Izinto ezingatholakali zingaphikiswa futhi zisuswe. (Agasti 2024) (Funda ukuthi ungawususa kanjani futhi nini lo mlayezo) 
Imitapo yolwazi yomuntu siqu neyomphakathi, izinqolobane zomlando nezinye izinhlobo zokuqoqwa kwezincwadi ziholele ekwakhiweni kwamasu amaningi ahlukene enhlangano nokuhlukanisa. Ngekhulu le-19 nelama-20, imitapo yolwazi kanye nezingcweti zemitapo yolwazi zahlela ukuqoqwa kwezincwadi kanye nezinhlelo zokuhlukanisa ngezigaba ukuze ziphendule embonini ekhulayo. Uhlelo olusetshenziswa kakhulu yi-ISBN, ehlinzeke ngezihlonzi ezihlukile zezincwadi kusukela ngo-1970. 

I-Libraries 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umtapowolwazi

Umtapo wolwazi kaCelsus e-Efesu, eTurkey, wakhiwa ngo-135 AD, futhi wawungathwala imiqulu engaba ngu-12,000. 
Umtapo wolwazi iqoqo lezincwadi, futhi mhlawumbe nezinye izinto kanye nemidiya, efinyeleleka ukuze isetshenziswe amalungu awo kanye namalungu ezikhungo ezihlangene. Imitapo yolwazi ihlinzeka ngezinto ezibonakalayo (amakhophi aqinile) noma edijithali (amakhophi athambile), futhi ingase ibe indawo ebonakalayo, indawo ebonakalayo, noma kokubili. Iqoqo lomtapo wezincwadi ngokuvamile lihlanganisa izinto eziphrintiwe ezingabolekwa, futhi ngokuvamile zihlanganisa nengxenye yereferensi yokushicilelwe engase isetshenziswe ngaphakathi kuphela kwezakhiwo. Izinsiza ezinjengokukhishwa kwezentengiso kwamafilimu, izinhlelo zikamabonakude, okunye okurekhodiwe kwevidiyo, umsakazo, umculo nokurekhodwa komsindo kungase kutholakale ngezindlela eziningi. Lokhu kufaka phakathi ama-DVD, ama-Blu-ray, ama-CD, amakhasethi, noma amanye amafomethi asebenzayo afana ne-microform. Bangase futhi banikeze ukufinyelela olwazini, umculo noma okunye okuqukethwe okugcinwe kusizindalwazi sezincwadi. 

Imitapo yolwazi ingahluka kakhulu ngobukhulu futhi ingase ihlelwe futhi inakekelwe inhlangano yomphakathi efana nohulumeni, isikhungo (njengesikole noma imnyuziyamu), inkampani, noma umuntu ozimele. Ukwengeza ekuhlinzekeni ngezinsizakusebenza, imitapo yolwazi iphinde ihlinzeke ngezinsizakalo zabasebenzi basemtapweni wolwazi abangochwepheshe abaqeqeshiwe ekutholeni, ekukhetheni, ekujikelezeni nasekuhleleni ulwazi ngesikhathi betolika izidingo zolwazi kanye nokuzulazula nokuhlaziya amanani amakhulu olwazi ngezinsiza ezihlukahlukene. 

Izakhiwo zomtapo wolwazi zivame ukuhlinzeka ngezindawo ezithule zokutadisha, kanye nezindawo ezivamile zokufunda njengeqembu nokusebenzisana, futhi zingase zinikeze izindawo zomphakathi zokufinyelela ezinsizeni zabo ze-elekthronikhi, njengamakhompyutha kanye nokufinyelela ku-inthanethi. 

Amakhasimende omtapo wolwazi kanye nezinsizakalo ezijwayelekile ezihlinzekwayo ziyahlukahluka kuye ngohlobo lwayo: abasebenzisi bomtapo wolwazi banezidingo ezihlukile kulezo zomtapo wolwazi okhethekile noma umtapo wolwazi, isibonelo. Imitapo yolwazi ingase futhi ibe izizinda zomphakathi, lapho kwenziwa khona izinhlelo futhi abantu bazibandakanye ekufundeni impilo yonke. Imitapo yolwazi yesimanje inweba izinkonzo zayo ngale kwezindonga ezibonakalayo zesakhiwo ngokuhlinzeka ngezinto ezifinyeleleka ngezindlela ze-elekthronikhi, kuhlanganise nasekhaya nge-inthanethi. 

Ukuhlonza kanye nezigaba 

ISBN ngebhakhodi
Ngo-2011, i-International Federation of Library Associations and Institutions (IFLA) yakha Incazelo Yebhayibhili Ejwayelekile Yamazwe Ngamazwe (ISBD) ukuze ilinganise izincazelo kumabhulobhu namakhathalogi omtapo wolwazi. Ibhuku ngalinye licaciswa INombolo Yencwadi Ejwayelekile Yamazwe Ngamazwe, noma i-ISBN, okuhloswe ukuthi ihluke kuzo zonke izinhlobo zencwadi ngayinye ekhiqizwa abashicileli ababamba iqhaza, emhlabeni wonke. Iphethwe yi-ISBN Society. I-ISBN inezingxenye ezine: ingxenye yokuqala ikhodi yezwe, eyesibili ikhodi yomshicileli, neyesithathu ikhodi yesihloko. Ingxenye yokugcina iyidijithi yesheke, futhi ingathatha amanani ukusuka ku-0–9 kanye no-X (10). Izinombolo ze-EAN Barcodes zezincwadi zithathwe ku-ISBN ngokufaka isiqalo 978, se-Bookland, kanye nokubala idijithi yesheke entsha. 

Abashicileli bezentengiselwano emazweni athuthukile ngokuvamile banikeza ama-ISBN ezincwadini zabo, ngakho abathengi bangase bacabange ukuthi i-ISBN iyingxenye yesistimu yamazwe ngamazwe ephelele, ngaphandle kokushiya. Nokho, abashicileli abaningi bakahulumeni, emazweni ezimboni kanye nasathuthuka, ababambi iqhaza ngokugcwele ohlelweni lwe-ISBN, futhi bashicilela izincwadi ezingenawo ama-ISBN. Iqoqo elikhulu noma elisesidlangalaleni lidinga ikhathalogi. Amakhodi abizwa ngokuthi "izinombolo zekholi" ahlobanisa izincwadi nekhathalogi, futhi anqume izindawo zawo emashalofini. Izinombolo zekholi zisekelwe ohlelweni lokuhlukaniswa kweLabhulali. Inombolo yocingo ibekwe emgogodleni wencwadi, ngokuvamile ibanga elifushane ngaphambi kwezansi, nangaphakathi. Amazinga esikhungo noma kazwelonke, afana ne-ANSI/NISO Z39.41 – 1997, asungula indlela efanele yokubeka ulwazi (njengesihloko, noma igama lombhali) kuma-spines ezincwadi, kanye nasezintweni "ezishelukayo" ezifana nencwadi, njengeziqukathi zama-DVD, amakhasethi evidiyo nesofthiwe. 


Izincwadi ezisemashalofini omtapo wezincwadi nezinombolo zezingcingo ezibonakala kuma-spines 
Enye yezinhlelo zokuqala nezaziwa kakhulu zekhathalogi yezincwadi i-Dewey Decimal System. Olunye uhlelo olwaziwa kabanzi yi-Library of Congress Classification system. Zombili lezi zinhlelo zichemile ezifundweni ezazimelwe kahle emitatsheni yolwazi yase-US ngenkathi zithuthukiswa, futhi ngenxa yalokho zinezinkinga zokusingatha izifundo ezintsha, njengekhompyutha, noma izifundo eziphathelene namanye amasiko.[49] Ulwazi olumayelana nezincwadi nababhali lungagcinwa kuzinqolobane ezifana nezizindalwazi eziku-inthanethi zenzuzo evamile. Imethadatha, okusho ukuthi "idatha emayelana nedatha" iwulwazi olumayelana nencwadi. Imethadatha emayelana nencwadi ingase ihlanganise isihloko sayo, i-ISBN noma enye inombolo yesigaba (bona ngenhla), amagama abanikeli (umbhali, umhleli, umdwebi) nomshicileli, idethi nosayizi walo, ulimi lombhalo, isihloko sawo, njll.

Amasistimu wokuhlukanisa 
I-Bliss bibliographic classification (BC) 
Ukuhlelwa Kwelabhulali YaseShayina (CLC) 
Ukuhlelwa Kwekholoni

sayo
Library of Congress Classification (LCC) 
Uhlelo Olusha Lokuhlukanisa Lwemitapolwazi YaseShayina 
I-Universal Decimal Classification (UDC) 
Ukongiwa kwe-Universal Decimal Classification (UDC) 

Uchwepheshe wezokongiwa kwemvelo ohlola umsebenzi wobuciko ngaphansi kwesibonakhulu e-Indianapolis Museum of Art 
Ukongiwa nokubuyiselwa kwezincwadi, imibhalo yesandla, imibhalo, kanye ne-ephemera kunikezelwe ekweluleni impilo yezinto zenani lomlando nezomuntu siqu ezenziwe ngokuyinhloko, ngephepha, isikhumba. Uma isetshenziswa kumagugu amasiko, imisebenzi yokongiwa kwemvelo ngokuvamile yenziwa umlondolozi. Umgomo oyinhloko wokongiwa kwemvelo uwukwelula ubude besikhathi bento kanye nokugcina ubuqotho bayo ngokugcina zonke izengezo zihlehliswa. Ukongiwa kwezincwadi nephepha kuhilela amasu okuhlanganisa izincwadi, ukubuyisela, amakhemikhali ephepha, nobunye ubuchwepheshe bezinto ezibonakalayo kuhlanganisa namasu okulondoloza kanye nokugcinwa komlando.[50] 

Ukongiwa kwezincwadi namaphepha kuhlose ukuvimbela futhi, kwezinye izimo, ukubuyisela emuva umonakalo ngenxa yokuphatha, ububi obungokwemvelo, kanye nemvelo.[51][52] Abalondolozi bama-Conservators banquma izindlela ezifanele zokugcina izincwadi namadokhumenti, okuhlanganisa amabhokisi namashalofu ukuze kuvinjelwe umonakalo owengeziwe futhi kukhuthaze ukugcinwa kwesikhathi eside.[53] Izindlela ezikhethwe ngokucophelela nezindlela zokulondoloza okusebenzayo zingahlehlisa kokubili umonakalo futhi zivimbele ukulimala okwengeziwe kumaqoqo noma ukwelapha into eyodwa ngokusekelwe enanini lencwadi noma idokhumenti.[54] 

Ngokomlando, amasu okubuyisela izincwadi ayengekho emthethweni futhi enziwa izindima ezihlukahlukene nezizinda zokuqeqesha. Kulezi zinsuku, ukulondolozwa kwemibhalo yephepha nezincwadi kuvame ukwenziwa umlondolozi ochwepheshile.[52][55] Abalondolozi abaningi bamaphepha noma bezincwadi bangamalungu enhlangano yochwepheshe, njenge-American Institute for Conservation (AIC) noma i-Guild of Bookworkers (kokubili e-United States), i-Archives and Records Association (e-United Kingdom nase-Ireland), noma i-Institute of Conservation (ICON) (e-United Kingdom).[56] 

Izindaba zomphakathi nezamasiko 
Ukwamukelwa 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukugxekwa kwemibhalo 
Umthelela wezincwadi ungahluka, futhi irekhodi lalokho kwamukelwa lifika ngezindlela eziningana: kuqala ngokwamukelwa komphakathi kokuqala emaphephandabeni angaleso sikhathi, isiko le-pop kanye nezincwadi, bese kuthuthukiswa ngezindlela ezihlukene zokugxekwa kwemibhalo ngabagxeki abangochwepheshe nabezemfundo. Embonini yokushicilela "ukubuyekezwa kwencwadi" kuyingxenye ebalulekile yokwandisa ukuqwashisa nokwamukelwa kwencwadi: ekwazi ukwenza noma ukwephula umbono womphakathi mayelana nencwadi entsha.[ecashunwa] 

Ukubuyekezwa kwencwadi 
Lesi sigaba siyingxenye yokubuyekezwa kwencwadi.[ hlela ] 
Ukubuyekezwa kwencwadi kuwuhlobo lokugxeka okubhaliwe lapho incwadi ichazwa nje (ukubuyekezwa okufingqiwe) noma ihlaziywe ngokusekelwe kokuqukethwe, isitayela kanye nesitayela.[5]

Ukubuyekezwa kwencwadi kungase kube umthombo oyinhloko, ucezu lwemibono, ukubuyekezwa okufingqiwe, noma umbono wezazi.[58] Izincwadi zingabuyekezwa emaphephandabeni anyathelisiwe, omagazini, namaphephandaba, njengomsebenzi wesikole, noma amawebhusayithi ezincwadi kuyi-Internet. Ubude bokubuyekezwa kwencwadi bungahluka kusuka endimeni eyodwa kuya endabeni enkulu. Ukubukeza okunjalo kungase kuhlole incwadi ngokusekelwe kulokho umuntu akuthandayo. Ababuyekezi bangasebenzisa isikhathi sokubuyekezwa kwencwadi ngendatshana enwetshiwe engahlotshaniswa eduze noma ngokukhululekile nesihloko sencwadi, noma baveze imibono yabo esihlokweni senganekwane noma umsebenzi ongelona iqiniso. 

Amanye amajenali anikelwe ekubuyekezweni kwezincwadi, futhi ukubuyekezwa kukhonjiswe kusizindalwazi esifana ne-Book Review Index kanye nokubuyekezwa kwe-Kirkus; kodwa ukubuyekezwa okuningi kwezincwadi kungatholakala emininingwaneni egciniwe yephephandaba kanye neyezazi ezifana ne-Arts and Humanities Citation Index, Inkomba Yokucaphuna Yesayensi Yezenhlalakahle, kanye nezingosi zolwazi eziqondene nesiyalo. 
Ukuhlolwa kwezincwadi nokuvinjelwa 
Ukuhlolwa kwezincwadi kuyisenzo seziphathimandla ezithile ezithatha izinyathelo zokucindezela imibono nolwazi olungaphakathi kwencwadi.[59] Ukuhlola "ukulawulwa kwenkululeko yokukhuluma nezinye izinhlobo zegunya eligxilile".[60] Amacense ngokuvamile akhomba njengomzali okhathazekile, amalungu omphakathi asabela kumbhalo ngaphandle kokufunda, noma izinhlangano zendawo noma zezwe.[61] Izincwadi ziye zahlolwa omashiqela abangondlovukayiphikiswa ukuze kuthuliswe abaphikisayo, njengePeople's Republic of China, iJalimane lamaNazi kanye neSoviet Union. Izincwadi zivame ukuhlolelwa ukufaneleka kweminyaka, ulimi oluhlambalazayo, okuqukethwe kwezocansi, phakathi kwezinye izizathu.[62] Ngokufanayo, izinkolo zingase zikhiphe uhlu lwezincwadi ezivinjelwe, njengesibonelo esingokomlando se-Index Librorum Prohibitorum yeSonto LamaKatolika kanye nokuvinjelwa kwezincwadi ezifana neka-Salman Rushdie ethi, The Satanic Verses ka-Ayatollah Khomeini,[63] ezingasebenzisi umthetho ngaso sonke isikhathi. Ukucwaninga kungenziwa ezingeni likazwelonke noma lamazwe angaphansi futhi, futhi kungathwala izinhlawulo ezingokomthetho. Ezimweni eziningi, ababhali balezi zincwadi bangabhekana nezigwebo ezinzima, ukudingiswa ezweni, noma ngisho nokubulawa.[64][65] 

Ukushiswa kwezincwadi 
Lesi sigaba siyingxenye yokushiswa kweNcwadi.[ hlela ] 

Ikhophi Yendlu Yamahlamvu eshiswayo 
Ukushiswa kwencwadi kuwukubhujiswa ngamabomu ngomlilo wezincwadi noma ezinye izinto ezilotshiwe, ngokuvamile ezenziwa emphakathini. Ukushiswa kwezincwadi kumelela ingxenye yokuhlolwa kwezincwadi futhi ngokuvamile kuvela ekuphikiseni kwamasiko, kwezenkolo, noma kwezombusazwe ezintweni okukhulunywa ngazo.[66] Ukushiswa kwezincwadi kungaba isenzo sokwedelela okuqukethwe yincwadi noma umbhali, okuhloswe ngaso ukudonsa ukunaka komphakathi kabanzi kulokhu kuphikiswa, noma ukufihla ukwaziswa okuqukethwe embhalweni ukuze kwaziswa obala, njengamadayari noma amaleja. Ukushiswa nezinye izindlela zokubhubhisa ndawonye zaziwa ngokuthi i-biblioclasm noma i-libricide.

Kwezinye izimo, imisebenzi ecekeleke phansi ayinakushintshwa futhi ukushiswa kwayo kusho ukulahlekelwa okukhulu kwamagugu amasiko. Izibonelo zifaka phakathi ukushiswa kwezincwadi nokungcwatshwa kwezazi ngaphansi kobukhosi baseChina bakwaQin (213-210 BCE), ukucekelwa phansi kweNdlu Yokuhlakanipha ngesikhathi sokuvinjezelwa kwamaMongol eBaghdad (1258), ukucekelwa phansi kwamakhodi ama-Aztec ngu-Itzcoatl (1430s), ukushiswa kwamakhodidi amaMaya 5 kanye no-Diego2 [1] [1] Umtapo Wolwazi Womphakathi waseJaffna eSri Lanka (1981).[68] 

Kwezinye izimo, njengokushiswa kwezincwadi zamaNazi, amakhophi ezincwadi ezibhujisiwe asekhona, kodwa isibonelo sokushiswa kwezincwadi siba uphawu lombuso onokhahlo nocindezelayo ofuna ukuhlola noma ukuthulisa isici esithile sesiko elibusayo.


"Okubhaliwe" kanye "Bhala" kuqondise kabusha lapha. Ukuze uthole ingxenye yeBhayibheli lesiHebheru, bheka i-Ketuvim. Ukuze uthole okunye ukusetshenziswa, bheka Bhala (disambiguation). 

I-Rosetta Stone (196 BC) ibhala ngemibhalo emithathu ehlukene. Ama-Hieroglyphs (phezulu) kanye ne-Demotic (maphakathi) aqopha umbhalo ofanayo ngolimi lwaseGibhithe, kuyilapho ingxenye efanayo yesiGrikhi isebenzisa izinhlamvu zezinhlamvu zesiGreki (ngezansi). Lezi zincwadi zaziyisihluthulelo ekuchazeni ama-hieroglyphs aseGibhithe ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19. 
Ukubhala kuyisenzo sokwakha ukumelwa okuphikelelayo kolimi. Uhlelo lokubhala luhlanganisa isethi ethile yezimpawu ebizwa ngokuthi umbhalo, kanye nemithetho abahlanganisa ngayo ulimi oluthile olukhulunywayo. Lonke ulimi olubhaliwe luvela olimini olukhulunywayo oluhambisanayo; kuyilapho ukusetshenziswa kolimi kwenzeka emhlabeni wonke emiphakathini yabantu, izilimi eziningi ezikhulunywayo azibhalwa.[1] 

Ukubhala kuwumsebenzi wokuqonda kanye nomphakathi ohlanganisa izinqubo ze-neuropsychological nezomzimba. Umphumela walo msebenzi, obuye ubizwe ngokuthi ukubhala (noma umbhalo) uchungechunge lwezimpawu ezibhalwe ngokoqobo, ezidluliswa ngomshini, noma ezimelelwe ngokwedijithali. Ukufunda kuyinqubo ehambisanayo yokuhumusha umbhalo obhaliwe, umhumushi abhekiselwe kuye njengomfundi.[2] 

Ngokuvamile, izinhlelo zokubhala azihlanganisi izilimi ngokwazo, kodwa ziyindlela yokuhlanganisa ulimi ukuze lufundwe ngabanye ngesikhathi nendawo.[3][4] Nakuba kungezona zonke izilimi ezisebenzisa uhlelo lokubhala, lezo ezilusebenzisayo zingagcwalisa futhi zandise amakhono olimi olukhulunywayo ngokwakha izinhlobo eziqinile zolimi ezingasakazwa endaweni yonke (isib. izincwadi ezibhaliwe) futhi zigcinwe ngokuhamba kwesikhathi (isib. imitapo yolwazi). Ukubhala kungase futhi kube nomthelela kulokho abantu abakutholayo, njengoba kuvumela abantu ukuba baveze ukucabanga kwabo ngaphandle ngezindlela okulula ukuzindla ngazo, ukuchaza kabanzi, ukucutshungulwa kabusha, nokuzibuyekeza.[6][7][8] 

Amathuluzi, izinto zokwakha, kanye nezisusa zokubhala 
Noma yisiphi isenzakalo sokubhala sihilela ukusebenzisana okuyinkimbinkimbi phakathi kwamathuluzi atholakalayo, izinhloso, amasiko angokwesiko, izindlela zokucabanga, izinhlobo, ulwazi olungasho lutho kanye nolwazi olusobala, kanye nezingqinamba kanye nemikhawulo yezinhlelo ezisetshenziswayo.[9] Izinsiza zokubhala ezisetshenziselwa ukwenza imibhalo ebonakalayo zihlanganisa iminwe, izitayela, amabhulashi ayinki, amapensela, amapeni, nezitayela eziningi ze-lithography; izindawo zokubhala okungabhalwa kuzo imibhalo zihlanganisa izibhebhe zamatshe, izibhebhe zobumba, iziliphu zoqalo, i-papyrus, izibhebhe ze-wax, i-vellum, isikhumba, iphepha, i-copperplate, nezileti.[10] 

Umshini wokubhala, kanye nephrosesa yamagama edijithali, kuvumela ababhali ngabanye ukuthi bakhiqize umbhalo obonakalayo ongaguquki besebenzisa ikhibhodi.[11]

Intuthuko ekucutshungulweni kolimi lwemvelo kanye nokukhiqizwa kolimi lwemvelo kuholele ekukhiqizeni isofthiwe ekwazi ukukhiqiza izinhlobo ezithile zokubhala ngefomula (isb. izibikezelo zesimo sezulu nokubikwa kwezemidlalo) ngaphandle kokubandakanyeka okuqondile kwabantu[12] ngemva kokucushwa kokuqala noma, ngokuvamile, okusetshenziselwa ukusekela izinqubo zokubhala ezifana nokukhiqiza okusalungiswa kokuqala, ukukhiqiza impendulo ngosizo lwerubrikhi,3 ukuhumusha, nokusiza ukukopisha].[12] 

Izisusa nezinjongo I 

-Bronze tympanum equkethe ukwenziwa samuntu Kokubhala - uThomas Jefferson Building, Washington, DC 
Ngokomlando, ukubhala kwavela ukuze kubhekelelwe izidingo zemiphakathi ekhula ebunzimeni bezomnotho nezenhlalo. Lapho sezithuthukisiwe, izinhlelo ezingase zisetshenziswe zazihlanganisa ukulandelela umkhiqizo kanye nomunye ingcebo, umlando oqoshiwe, ukugcinwa kwesiko, ukuhlanganisa ulwazi ngohlelo lwezifundo kanye nohlu lwamathekisthi athathwa njengonolwazi oluyisisekelo (isb. ICanon of Medicine) noma ukubaluleka kobuciko (isb. Izinsiza zokuphatha zazihlanganisa amakhodi omthetho, amarekhodi okubalwa kwabantu, izinkontileka, amatayitela obunikazi, intela, izivumelwano zohwebo, nezivumelwano. Njengoba uCharles Bazerman echaza, "ukumakwa kwezimpawu ematsheni, ubumba, ephepheni, futhi manje izinkumbulo zedijithali-ngasinye isikhathi esiphatheka kalula futhi esihamba ngokushesha kunesangaphambili-kuhlinzekele izindlela zokuqhubeka nokudidiyelwa kwesenzo esinwetshiwe kanye nenkumbulo kuwo wonke amaqembu amakhulu abantu ngokuhamba kwesikhathi nendawo."[14] Okunye okuqanjwe kabusha kwakuhlanganisa umfaniswano owengeziwe, ongabikezelwa, kanye nenguqulo yezinqubo zomthetho ezisatshalaliswa kabanzi, inguqulo yezinqubo ezingokomthetho ezisabalaliswayo ezisabalaliswa kabanzi. uphenyo lwesayensi nokuphathwa kolwazi, konke obekuncike kakhulu ezinhlotsheni eziphathwayo neziphindaphindeka kalula zolimi olulotshiwe. Umlando wokubhala ubanzi ngokuhambisana nokusetshenziswa kokubhala kanye nokucaciswa kwezinhlelo zemisebenzi ezidala kanye nezisabalalisa ukubhala.[15] 

Izisusa zomuntu ngamunye zokubhala zihlanganisa ikhono lokusebenza ngale kwemikhawulo yenkumbulo yomuntu siqu[16] (isb izinhlu zezinto okufanele zenziwe, izindlela zokupheka, izikhumbuzo, izincwadi zokungena, amamephu, izikhombisi-ndlela zemisebenzi eyinkimbinkimbi noma amasiko), ukusabalalisa imibono nokuxhumana (isb. ama-eseyi, ama-monographs, ama-broadsides, izinhlelo, izikhalazo, i-manifest yezindaba zomphakathi), ukugcinwa kwezindaba zomphakathi kanye nezindaba zomphakathi), amanethiwekhi,[17] izincwadi zebhizinisi mayelana nezimpahla namasevisi, kanye nokubhala impilo (isb. idayari noma iphephabhuku).[18]

Ukusabalala komhlaba wonke kwezinhlelo zokuxhumana zedijithali ezifana ne-imeyili kanye nenkundla yezokuxhumana kwenze ukubhala kwaba isici esibaluleke kakhulu ekuphileni kwansuku zonke, lapho lezi zinhlelo zixubana nobuchwepheshe obudala njengephepha, amapensela, amabhodi amhlophe, amaphrinta, namakhophi.[19] Amanani amakhulu okubhala kwansuku zonke abonakala ezindaweni eziningi zokusebenza emazweni athuthukile.[20] Emisebenzini eminingi (isib. umthetho, ukubalwa kwezimali, ukuklanywa kwesoftware, izinsiza zabantu), imibhalo ebhaliwe ayiyona nje into eyinhloko elethwayo kodwa futhi nendlela yokusebenza ngokwayo.[21] Ngisho nasemisebenzini engavamile ukuhlotshaniswa nokubhala, ukuphathwa kwamarekhodi okujwayelekile kwenza iningi labasebenzi libhale okungenani isikhathi esithile.[22] 

Ukusetshenziswa kwesimanje 
Abanye ubungcweti ngokuvamile bahlotshaniswa nokubhala, njengababhali bemibhalo, izintatheli, nababhali bezobuchwepheshe, kodwa ukubhala kugcwele ezinhlotsheni eziningi zesimanje zomsebenzi, ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi, ukuphathwa kwekhaya, kanye nemisebenzi yokuzilibazisa.[23] 

Ibhizinisi nezezimali 
Bheka futhi: Ukubhala kochwepheshe kanye nokuxhumana kochwepheshe 
Ukubhala kugcwele ezentengiselwano zansuku zonke. Isibonelo, ntambama, umthengisi angase athole umbuzo obhaliwe mayelana nokuba khona kolayini womkhiqizo, bese axhumane nabaphakeli nabakhi ngama-oda omsebenzi nezivumelwano zokuthenga, ahambisane nge-imeyili ukuze aqinisekise ukutholakala komkhumbi ngenkampani yedrayage, abhale i-invoyisi, futhi acele ubufakazi bokusithola ngendlela yesiginisha ebhaliwe. Ngezinga elikhulu, izinhlelo zesimanje zezimali, amabhange, kanye nebhizinisi zisekelwe emibhalweni ebhaliwe - okuhlanganisa imithethonqubo, izinqubomgomo, nezinqubo; ukwakhiwa kwemibiko kanye neminye imibhalo yokuqapha okufanele yenziwe, ihlolwe, futhi inikeze ukuziphendulela ngezinqumo nokusebenza; ukwakhiwa nokugcinwa kwamarekhodi; ukuxhumana okubhaliwe kwangaphakathi ngaphakathi kweminyango ukuze kudidiyelwe umsebenzi; ukuxhumana okubhaliwe okuhlanganisa imikhiqizo yomsebenzi eyethulwa kweminye iminyango nakumakhasimende; kanye nokuxhumana kwangaphandle kumakhasimende kanye nomphakathi.[24][ikhasi elidingekayo][25][ikhasi elidingekayo] Izinhlangano zebhizinisi nezezimali nazo zithembele emibhalweni eminingi yezomthetho ebhaliwe, njengezinkontileka, imibiko eya ezikhungweni zikahulumeni, amarekhodi entela, nemibiko yokubalwa kwezimali.[26] Izikhungo zezezimali nezimakethe eziphethe, ezithumelayo, ezihwebayo, eziqinisekisayo, noma ezilawula ukubanjwa kwamakhasimende noma ezinye izikhungo kuncike ikakhulukazi kumarekhodi abhaliwe (nakuba manje ngokuvamile asesimweni sedijithali) ukuze zigcine ubuqotho bezindima zazo.[27][ikhasi elidingekayo] 

Ukuphatha kanye nomthetho
Izimiso eziningi zanamuhla zikahulumeni zihlelwa futhi ingcweliswe ngemithetho-sisekelo ebhaliwe emazingeni kazwelonke futhi ngezinye izikhathi esifunda noma amanye enhlangano. Imithetho nezinqubo ezibhaliwe ngokuvamile ziqondisa ukusebenza kwamagatsha ahlukahlukene, iminyango, nezinye izindikimba zikahulumeni, ezivame ukukhiqiza imibiko namanye amadokhumenti njengemikhiqizo yomsebenzi futhi aziphendulele ngezenzo zawo. Ngaphezu kwezishayamthetho ezibhala futhi ziphasise imithetho, le mithetho ilawulwa yigatsha eliphezulu, elingase wethule eminye imithetho ebhaliwe ecacisa imithetho kanye nendlela eqhutshwa ngayo.[28] Ohulumeni emazingeni ahlukene futhi ngokuvamile bagcina amarekhodi abhaliwe ezakhamuzi mayelana nobunikazi, izehlakalo zempilo ezifana nokuzalwa, ukufa, imishado, nezehlukaniso, ukunikezwa kwamalayisensi emisebenzi elawulwayo, amacala obugebengu, amacala omgwaqo, nezinye izinhlawulo ezincane nezinkulu, kanye nesikweletu sentela nezinkokhelo.[29] 

Isayensi kanye ne-scholarship 
Ucwaningo olwenziwa emikhakheni yezemfundo ngokuvamile lushicilelwa njengama-athikili kumajenali noma ngaphakathi kwama-monographs obude bencwadi. Izimpikiswano, ukuhlola, idatha yokuqaphela, nobunye ubufakazi obuqoqwe phakathi nocwaningo bumelwe ngokubhaliwe, futhi busebenza njengesisekelo somsebenzi wakamuva. Ukuqoqwa kwedatha nokuhlelwa kwemibhalo yesandla kungase kusekelwe izibonelelo, ngokuvamile ezidinga iziphakamiso ezibonisa ukubaluleka kwalowo msebenzi kanye nesidingo soxhaso.[30] Idatha nezinqubo ngokuvamile ziqoqwa ezincwadini zamabhuku zelebhu noma kwamanye amafayela okuqalisa.[31][ikhasi elidingekayo] Ukuphrinta kusengaphambili okungase kushicilelwe kungase kwethulwe ezingqungqutheleni zezemfundo noma zokuqondiswa kwezigwegwe noma kumaseva ewebhu afinyeleleka esidlangalaleni ukuze athole impendulo kontanga futhi akhe isithakazelo emsebenzini. Ngaphambi kokushicilelwa okusemthethweni, le mibhalo ivame ukufundwa futhi ihlolwe ukubuyekezwa kontanga okuvela kochwepheshe abafanelekile, abanquma ukuthi umsebenzi unenani nekhwalithi eyanele okufanele ishicilelwe.[32] 

Ukushicilelwa akuqinisekisi izimangalo noma okutholwe komsebenzi njengokuyiqiniso eligunyaziwe, kuphela nje ukuthi kufanele ukunakwa abanye ochwepheshe. Njengoba umsebenzi uvela ezihlokweni ezibuyekezwayo, ezincwadini zezandla, ezincwadini zokufunda, noma kwezinye izilinganiso, nabanye bewucaphuna ekuthuthukiseni olwabo ucwaningo, ingabe uhlanganiswa njengolwazi oluthembeke ngokungaguquki.[33] 

Ubuntatheli
Izindaba nokubikwa kwezindaba kusemqoka ekubandakanyekeni kwezakhamizi kanye nolwazi lwemikhakha eminingi yemisebenzi abantu abangaba nentshisekelo kuyo mayelana nesimo somphakathi wabo, okuhlanganisa izenzo nobuqotho bohulumeni babo nezikhulu zikahulumeni, izitayela zezomnotho, izinhlekelele zemvelo nezimpendulo kuzo, imicimbi yezwe lomhlaba, okuhlanganisa izingxabano, kodwa nezemidlalo, ezokuzijabulisa, izincwadi, neminye imisebenzi yokuzilibazisa. Nakuba izindaba namaphephandaba kukhule ngokushesha kusukela ekhulwini leshumi nesishiyagalombili kuya kweleshumi nesishiyagalombili kuya kweleshumi nambili, ukushintsha kwezomnotho kanye nekhono lokukhiqiza nokusabalalisa izindaba kuye kwaletha izinselele ezinkulu nezisheshayo kubuntatheli kanye nenhlangano elandelanayo yolwazi lwesakhamuzi nokuzibandakanya.[34][35][ikhasi elidingekayo] Lezi zinguquko ziye zadala nezinselele zokuziphatha kobuntatheli eziye zathuthukiswa phakathi nekhulu leminyaka elidlule.[36] 

Izikhungo zemfundo nezemfundo 
Imfundo esemthethweni ingqikithi yezenhlalo ehlotshaniswa kakhulu nokufunda kokubhala, futhi abafundi bangase baphathe lezi zinhlangano isikhathi eside ngemva kokuqeda isikole.[37] Eceleni kokubhala abafundi abakufundayo (ngezinhlobo zezincwadi zokufunda, izincwadi abazinikeziwe, nezinye izinto zokufundisa kanye nezincwadi abazikhethele bona) abafundi babhala kakhulu ezikoleni kuwo wonke amazinga, ezivivinyweni zezifundo, ezindabeni, ekubhaleni amanothi, ekwenzeni umsebenzi wesikole, nasekuhloleni okuhlanganisayo nokufingqayo. Okunye kwalokhu kuqondiswe ngokusobala ekufundeni kokubhala, kodwa okuningi kugxile kakhulu ekufundeni izifundo.[38][39] 

Izindlela zokubhala 
Izinhlelo zokubhala zingahlukaniswa kabanzi ngokuya ngokuthi yimaphi amayunithi olimi avame ukumelwa yizimpawu zawo:[40][41] 

Amaphonografia amele imisindo yenkulumo - ngama-alfabhethi namagama kusetshenziswa izimpawu zamafonemi namalunga ngokulandelana kwawo. 
Ama-logographies amelela amayunithi encazelo yolimi (amagama noma ama-morphemes), nakuba asahlotshaniswa abafundi nokuphimisela okunikeziwe ngolimi oluhambisanayo olukhulunywayo. 
Ilogographies 

Ukuziphendukela kwemvelo ngokuqhathanisa ukusuka kuma-pictogram kuya ekubunjweni kwezinhlamvu ezingabonakali, kuma-cuneiform aseMesopotamiya, ama-hieroglyphs aseGibhithe kanye nezinhlamvu zesiShayina 
I-logography ibhalwa kusetshenziswa ama-logogram - izinhlamvu ezibhaliwe ezimelela amagama ngamanye noma ama-morphems.[40] Ama-logogramu amaningi anezakhiwo zangaphakathi, ezinezingxenye ezingamelela kokubili ifonographic kanye ne-ideographic (isb. ama-radicals wezinhlamvu zesiShayina, i-hieroglyphic determinatives) izici zemofimu.[42] 

Uhlelo oluyinhloko lwe-logographic olusetshenziswayo yizinhlamvu zesiShayina, ezisetshenziselwa ngokuyinhloko ukubhala izilimi zesiShayina nesiJapane, futhi ngokomlando ezinye ezivela ezifundeni ezithonywe isiko lamaShayina, njengesiKorea nesiVietnam. Ezinye izinhlelo ze-logographic zihlanganisa umbhalo we-cuneiform nesiMaya.[43]
 
Ama-syllabaries
I-syllabary iyisethi yezimpawu ezibhaliwe ezimele amalunga,[40] ngokuvamile ungwaqa olandelwa unkamisa, noma unkamisa yedwa. Kweminye imibhalo ama-syllables ayinkimbinkimbi (isb. ungwaqa–nkamisa–ungwaqa noma ungwaqa–ongwaqa–nkamisa) kungenzeka abe nama-glyphs akhethekile. Amagama afanayo ngefonetiki awabhalwa ngokufanayo.[40] 

Ama-syllabaries afaneleka kakhulu ezilimini ezinokwakheka kwamalunga alula, njengesi-Japanese. Ezinye izikripthi ze-syllabic zifaka u-Linear B kanye ne-Cherokee syllabary.[44] 

Ama-alfabhethi 
I-alfabhethi iyiqoqo lezimpawu ezibhaliwe ezimelela ongwaqa nonkamisa.[40] 

Ama-Abjads 
Alphabets ngokuvamile anezinhlamvu zongwaqa abizwa ngokuthi ama-abjad noma ongwaqa; nakuba ngokuzithandela, ama-abjad angase futhi asebenzise izimpawu zohlobo lwezinhlamvu ukuze acacise ukuthi yibaphi onkamisa abalandela ungwaqa ngamunye. Ama-alfabhethi okuqala kwakungama-abjad, athonywe izimpawu ezimelela ongwaqa abathile abasuka kuma-hieroglyphs aseGibhithe. Ama-abjad amaningi ngokufanayo nawo adabuka eMpumalanga Ephakathi, abonisa ukuhluka okulinganiselwe konkamisa ku-morphology yezilimi zamaSemite ezikhulunywa esifundeni.[40] 

Ama-Abugidas 
Ezinhlotsheni eziningi zezinhlamvu zaseNdiya naseNingizimu-mpumalanga ye-Asia, onkamisa baboniswa ngezinhlamvu zezinhlamvu noma ukuguqulwa kokuma kongwaqa. Lezi zibizwa ngokuthi ama-abugidas noma ama-alphasyllabaries.[40] Igama elithi abugida lisuselwa emagameni ezinhlamvu zokuqala embhalweni weGeʽez, enye i-abugida evelele eyasetshenziswa ekubhaleni izilimi eziningana e-Ethiopia nase-Eritrea.[45] 

Umlando nemvelaphi 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Umlando wokubhala 
Ukubhala kwaqala ukuvela ngeNkathi Yokuqala Yethusi ukuze kuhlangatshezwane nezidingo ezikhulayo zezomnotho zezifunda zedolobha laseSumeria, eziseningizimu yeMesophothamiya. Ngalesi sikhathi, inkimbinkimbi yezohwebo nokuphatha yadlula amandla enkumbulo, ne-cuneiform yaseSumeri esebenza njengendlela enokwethenjelwa yokurekhoda ukuthengiselana, ukugcinwa kwama-akhawunti ezezimali, nokugcina amarekhodi omlando, phakathi kwemisebenzi efanayo.[46] 

I-Cuneiform, esetshenziselwa ukubhala ulimi lwaseSumerian, yalandelwa ngokushesha ngokuqhathaniswa nemibhalo yaseGibhithe, nakho kokubili okuvela ezinhlelweni zokubhala ze-proto phakathi kuka-3400 no-3100 BC, nemibhalo yokuqala ehlangene kusukela c. 2600 BC.[47] Umbhalo we-Indus (c. 2600 - c. 2000 BC), otholakala ezinhlotsheni ezahlukene zezinto zobuciko ezikhiqizwe i-Indus Valley Civilization ezwenikazi lase-Indian, azikacaciswanga, nokuthi ngabe zasebenza njengokulotshwa kweqiniso akuvunyelwananga ngakho.[48] Nakuba umsuka wawo ungabonakali ngokusobala, ithuba lokusakazeka kwamasiko aseMesophothamiya lokwethula umqondo wokubhala kubantu base-Indus licacile.[49] 

eMesophothamiya
 
Globular eneqoqo lamathokheni wokubala, isikhathi sase-Uruk, esivela eSusa - Louvre Museum
Ngawo-1970, umvubukuli uDenise Schmandt-Besserat wethula inkolelo-mbono esungula ukuxhumana phakathi kwe-cuneiform kanye "namathokheni" obumba ayengahlukaniswanga, amadala kunawo wonke atholwe esifundeni saseZagros e-Iran. Cishe ngo-8000 BC, abantu baseMesopotamiya baqala ukusebenzisa amathokheni obumba ukubala izimpahla zabo zezolimo nezenziwe. Kamuva baqala ukufaka la mathokheni ngaphakathi kweziqukathi zobumba ezinkulu, ezingenalutho (i-bulla, noma izimvilophu ze-globular) ezazibe sezivaliwe. Ubuningi bamathokheni esitsheni ngasinye buvezwe ngokuhlaba umxhwele, ebusweni besiqukathi, isithombe esisodwa sesibonelo ngasinye sethokheni ngaphakathi. Ngokulandelayo bakhipha amathokheni, bethembele kuphela kuzimpawu zamathokheni, adwetshwe ezindaweni zobumba. Ukuze bagweme ukwenza isithombe sesenzakalo ngasinye sento efanayo (isibonelo: izithombe eziyi-100 zesigqoko ezimele izigqoko eziyi-100), babala izinto ngokusebenzisa amamaki amancane ahlukahlukene.[50] 

I-Cuneiform (kusuka ku-Latin cunius, lit. 'wedge') yavela c. 3200 BC kumongo walobu buchwepheshe bokugcina ama-akhawunti. Ekupheleni kwenkulungwane yesi-4 BC,[51] abaseMesophothamiya base besebenzisa ukuloba okumise okukanxantathu okucindezelwe odakeni oluthambile ukuze kuqoshwe izinombolo. Lesi simiso sanwetshwa kancane kancane kusetshenziswa usiba olucijile ukuze kuboniswe lokho okwakubalwa kusetshenziswa ama-pictograph. Izitayela zokuloba eziyindingilizi nezibukhali zashintshwa kancane kancane kwafakwa ama-stylus amise okwe-wedges, ekuqaleni amalogi aqopha kuphela - anezici zefonetiki ezethulwa ngekhulu lama-29 BC ukuze amele amalunga esiSumerian, okuholele ohlelweni lokubhala lwenjongo evamile.[52][53] 

Kusukela ngekhulu lama-26 BC, i-cuneiform yashintshwa ukuze kubhalwe ulimi lwase-East Semitic Akkadian (isi-Asiriya nesiBhabhiloni) olwalusakazekele eningizimu yeMesophothamiya - kwase kuba kwezinye ezinjenge-Elamite, Hattian, Hurrian kanye namaHeti. Imibhalo efana nalesi simiso sokubhala ihlanganisa naleyo yesi-Ugarit nesi-Old Persian. Ngokwamukelwa kwesi-Aramu njengolimi olusetshenziswa yiNeo-Assyrian Empire (911-609 BC), isi-Aramu Esidala saphinde sajwayelaniswa ne-cuneiform yaseMesophothamiya. Imibhalo yakamuva ye-cuneiform yesi-Akkadian etholwe kuze kube manje ingeyekhulu lokuqala AD.[54] 

I-Egypt 

I-Narmer Palette, ebonisa ama-serpopard amabili asabekayo amelela ukuhlanganiswa kwe-Upper and Lower Egypt, c. Ngo-3100 BC
Ama-hieroglyphs akudala kakhulu aziwayo (kusukela kusiGreki, okuhunyushwa ngokuthi 'umbhalo ongcwele') amalebula obumba ombusi we-Predynastic "Scorpion I", wango-c. ngekhulu lama-33 BC futhi walulama e-Abydos (i-Umm el-Qa'ab yesimanje) - noma ngenye indlela i-Narmer Palette, yango-c. 3100 BC.[55] Isikripthi se-hieroglyphic sasiyilogographic, sinezithasiselo zefonetiki ezihlanganisa izinhlamvu zamagama ezisebenzayo. Umusho omdala kunayo yonke ocutshunguliwe ufakazelwa ngophawu oluvela ethuneni likaSeth-Peribsen e-Abydos, esukela kuBukhosi Besibili (ngekhulu lama-28 noma lama-27 BC). Cishe ama-hieroglyphs angu-800 asetshenziswa ngezikhathi zoMbuso Omdala, Ophakathi, kanye Nomusha (2686–1077 BC); ngesikhathi samaGreki namaRoma (30 BC - 642 AD), kufakazelwa ama-glyphs ahlukene angaphezu kuka-5,000.[56] 

Ukubhala kwakubalulekile ekulondolozeni umbuso waseGibhithe, futhi ukufunda nokubhala ohlelweni olunzima lwemibhalo ebhalwe phansi kwakugxiliswe phakathi kwezicukuthwane ezifundile zababhali abakhonza ethempelini, iziphathimandla zefaro, nezempi.[57] 

I-Mesoamerica 
Kwemibhalo eminingana yangaphambi kwe-Columbian e-Mesoamerica, leyo ebonakala sengathi ithuthukiswe kangcono, futhi okuwukuphela kwayo okumele kuqondwe, umbhalo wesiMaya. Umbhalo wakuqala ohlonzwe njengeMaya ungowekhulu lesi-3 BC.[58] Ukubhala kwesiMaya kusetshenziswa cishe izimpawu ezihlukene ezingu-800 - ikakhulukazi ama-logogram, ahambisana neqoqo lama-syllabograms asetshenziselwa izinamathiselo, ukungaboni ngaso linye phakathi kokufundwa okuhlukene kwelogogram, noma ukushintshwa kwamalogo athile ngokuphelele.[59] 

EShayina 
Olunye ulwazi: I-Oracle bone script kanye nemibhalo yethusi yamaShayina 
Izibonelo zokuqala ezisekhona zokuloba eShayina - imibhalo emathanjeni e-oracle, ngokuvamile ama-plastron ofudu kanye ne-ox scapulae okwakusetshenziselwa ukubhula - kusukela ngo-c. 1200 BC, ngesikhathi seLate Shang. Inani elincane lemibhalo yethusi yangesikhathi esifanayo nayo isindile.[60] 

Imibhalo ye-Elamute 
Umbhalo we-Proto-Elamite, osetshenziswayo c. 3200 - c. 2900 BC, kufakazelwa ezibhebheni zobumba ezitholakala ezindaweni ezahlukene kulo lonke elase-Iran yanamuhla, kanti iningi limbiwe eSusa, idolobha lasendulo elisempumalanga yeTigris.[61] Umbhalo kucatshangwa ukuthi wawuyingxenye ye-logographic, uthuthukiswe kusukela ekuqaleni kwe-cuneiform, futhi wasebenzisa izimpawu ezingaphezu kwe-1,000 - nakuba imibhalo yawo "ibe, futhi izosala, iyinkinga enkulu engxoxweni yokubhala ngoba imele isikhathi esingacacile sokufunda nokubhala".[62] 

Umbhalo we-cuneiform wama-Elamu, osetshenziswe c. 2500 - 331 BC, yashintshwa isuka ku-cuneiform njengoba yayisetshenziselwa ukubhala isi-Akkadian. Kunoma isiphi isikhathi phakathi nalesi sikhathi, i-Elamite cuneiform yasebenzisa izimpawu ezingaba ngu-130 - kanye nesamba esingu-206 esisetshenziswa kuyo yonke impilo yayo yonke, ngaphansi kakhulu kweminye imibhalo eminingi ye-cuneiform.[40] 

Amasistimu e-Aegean 
Ngaphambi kokusungulwa kwezinhlamvu zezinhlamvu zesiGreki ngesikhathi se-Iron Age, ama-hieroglyphs e-Cretan afakazelwa ezintweni zobuciko ezivela eKrethe phakathi nenkulungwane yesibili kuya maphakathi BC. I-Linear B, uhlelo lokubhala lwamaGreki aseMycenaean, yasetshenziswa eKnossos eKrete kanye nezwe laseGreece c. 1450−1200 BC.[63] Umugqa A, osazochazwa, wawusetshenziswa e-Aegean Islands nasezwenikazi c. 1800–1450 BC.[64] 

Ukuthuthukiswa kwezinhlamvu 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umlando wezinhlamvu
