Ama-alfabhethi aziwa kuphela ukuthi aqanjwa kanye emlandweni wesintu, ngumphakathi wabavukuzi baseKhanani be-turquoise eNhlonhlweni yaseSinayi c. 1800 BC ukubhala izilimi zamaSemite zaseNtshonalanga,[65] "ngokwesimo sokuhwebelana kwamasiko phakathi kwabantu abakhuluma isiSemite abavela eLevant kanye nemiphakathi yaseGibhithe".[66] Leli fomu lokuqala elifakazelwe laziwa ngokuthi umbhalo we-Proto-Sinaitic, futhi liguqule imiqondo kanye namanye amagama alo okungenani abhaliwe asuka ekubhaleni kwe-Hieroglyphic yaseGibhithe; yamukela ngokuphelele izindinganiso zomsindo zaseNtshonalanga Semitic ezinhlamvu zayo, ngokuphambene nokuvumelana nezikhona zaseGibhithe.[67] Ukujola okunembile komsuka wayo, kanye nomsuka wesithombe wamafomu amaningi ezinhlamvu (uma ekhona) kuhlala kungacacile, futhi umbhalo uhlala ungacaciswanga.[68] Cishe imibhalo engcolile engama-30 itholwe endaweni yezimayini yaseGibhithe enezintaba eyaziwa ngokuthi i-Serabit el-Khadem, enezimpawu ezimele imisindo yongwaqa eyodwa esikhundleni samagama aphelele noma imiqondo - isisekelo sohlelo lwama-alfabhethi. Kwaze kwaba phakathi kwekhulu le-12 nelesi-9 BC lapho ukusetshenziswa kwezinhlamvu kwanda khona.[65] 

Izinhlamvu zezinhlamvu zaseFenike (c. 1050 BC) ziyinzalo eqondile ye-Proto-Sinaitic. AmaProto-Sinaitic namaFenike kwakungama-abjad anezinhlamvu ezimelela imisindo yongwaqa; IsiFenike ekugcineni saguqulelwa kuzinhlamvu zezinhlamvu zesiGreki (c. 800 BC), esokuqala ukumela imisindo yonkamisa, esakwenza ngokuphinda sisebenzise izimpawu zongwaqa zaseFenike ezingasetshenzisiwe.[69] Izinhlamvu ze-Cumae, okuhlukile kwezinhlamvu zamagama zesiGreki zakuqala, zaveza izinhlamvu ze-Etruscan kanye nenzalo yazo, njengezinhlamvu zesiLatini.[70] Ezinye izizukulwane zezinhlamvu zezinhlamvu zesiGreki zihlanganisa isiCyrillic, esisetshenziselwa ukubhala izilimi njengesiBulgaria nesiRashiya.[71] Izinhlamvu zamagama zaseFenike nazo zashintshwa zaba umbhalo wesi-Aramu, okuvela kuwo i-West Asian Square Hebrew, Arabic,[72] kanye nemibhalo ye-Brahmic yaseNingizimu Asia.[73] 

Imibhalo yezenkolo 
Emlandweni wokubhala, imibhalo yezenkolo noma ukubhala kube nendima ekhethekile. Isibonelo, ezinye izinhlanganisela zemibhalo yezenkolo kube ezinye zemibhalo yakudala edumile, noma okuwukuphela kwemibhalo ebhaliwe kwezinye izilimi, futhi kwezinye izimo kusadume kakhulu emhlabeni jikelele.[74][ikhasi elidingekayo][75][76] 



Ukuze uthole okunye ukusetshenziswa, bheka uMbhali (ukungaqondi). 

Lesi sihloko sinezinkinga eziningi. Sicela usize ukuyithuthukisa noma uxoxe ngalezi zinkinga ekhasini lenkulumo. (Funda ukuthi ungayisusa kanjani futhi nini le milayezo) 
Lesi sihloko sidinga izingcaphuno ezengeziwe ukuze siqinisekiswe. (Okthoba 2017)
Ithoni yalesi sihloko noma isitayela singase singabonisi ithoni ye-encyclopedic esetshenziswe ku-Wikipedia. (October 2022) 
Enkulumweni yomthetho, umbhali ungumdali wencwadi yokuqala eshicilelwe, kungakhathaliseki ukuthi lowo msebenzi ubhalwe, uyingcaca, ubonwa, noma urekhodiwe.[1] Isenzo sokudala umsebenzi onjalo sibizwa ngokuthi ubuqambi, okusho ukuthi umqophi, umdwebi, noma umqambi uthathwa njengombhali wezithombe eziqoshiwe, imidwebo, noma izingoma zomculo. Nakuba lisetshenziswa okuvamile, igama elithi “umbhali” livame ukuhlotshaniswa ngokuqondile nomlobi wencwadi, i-athikili, umdlalo, noma omunye umsebenzi obhaliwe.[2] Ezimeni ezihilela umsebenzi ozoqashwa, umqashi noma ithimba elithumayo lithathwa ngokomthetho njengomsunguli womsebenzi, ngisho noma wenziwe ngomunye umuntu.[1] 

Ngokuvamile, umnikazi wokuqala we-copyright ungumdali womsebenzi one-copyright, okungukuthi, umbhali. Uma abantu abangaphezu koyedwa abadale umsebenzi, khona-ke ubunikazi obuhlangene buye benza. Umthetho we-copyright uyahluka emhlabeni jikelele. Ihhovisi Lelungelo Lobunikazi Lase-United States, ngokwesibonelo, lichaza ilungelo lobunikazi “njengohlobo lokuvikela olunikezwa imithetho yase-United States (isihloko 17, Ikhodi yase-US) kubabhali ‘bemisebenzi yokuqala yobuqambi.’ [3][4] 

Eminye imisebenzi ibhekwa njengengenababhali, noma ibhalwe ngokungaziwa noma ngokuyimfihlo. Ingxabano ye-monkey selfie copyright ngeminyaka yawo-2010s yayiyingxabano ephawulekayo yobunikazi ehlanganisa izithombe ezithathwe ama-macaque ama-Celebes crested esebenzisa izinto zomthwebuli wezithombe zemvelo. Umthwebuli wezithombe wagomela ubunikazi bezithombe, ihhovisi le-copyright lase-United States eliziphikayo, lathi: "Ukuze ufaneleke njengomsebenzi 'wobunikazi' umsebenzi kufanele wenziwe umuntu."[5] Ukuthuthukiswa kobuhlakani bokwenziwa obukhiqizayo kuye kwaholela enkulumweni ephathelene nobunikazi bemidiya oyikhiqizayo. 

Ukubaluleka okusemthethweni kobunikazi 
Ukubamba isihloko "sombhali" phezu kwanoma iyiphi "imibhalo, idrama, umculo, ubuciko, [noma] eminye imisebenzi yobuhlakani" kunikeza amalungelo kulo muntu, umnikazi welungelo lobunikazi, ikakhulukazi ilungelo elikhethekile lokuzibandakanya noma ukugunyaza noma yikuphi ukukhiqizwa noma ukusatshalaliswa komsebenzi wabo.[3][4] Noma yimuphi umuntu noma inhlangano efisa ukusebenzisa impahla ebhaliwe yengqondo ephethwe ngaphansi kwelungelo lobunikazi kufanele ithole imvume kumnikazi we-copyright yokusebenzisa lo msebenzi, futhi ngokuvamile izocelwa ukuthi ikhokhele ukusetshenziswa kwezinto ezine-copyright.[4]

Amalungelo okushicilela omsebenzi wobuhlakani aphelelwa yisikhathi ngemva kwesikhathi esithile. Ingena endaweni yomphakathi, lapho ingasetshenziswa ngaphandle komkhawulo.[4] Imithetho ye-copyright ezindaweni eziningi - ikakhulukazi elandela ukuhola kwe-United States, lapho izimboni zezokuzijabulisa nezokushicilela zinamandla amakhulu okugqugquzela - iye yachitshiyelwa kaningi kusukela yasungulwa, ukuze kunwetshwe ubude balesi sikhathi esinqunyiwe lapho umsebenzi ulawulwa ngokukhethekile umnikazi welungelo lobunikazi. Ngobuchwepheshe, othile ungumnikazi womsebenzi wakhe kusukela ngesikhathi udalwa. Isici esiphawulekayo sobunikazi sivela ne-copyright ngokuthi, ezindaweni eziningi, singadluliselwa komunye, lapho umuntu efa. Umuntu othola ilungelo lobunikazi njengefa akayena umbhali, kodwa unokufinyelela ezinzuzweni ezingokomthetho ezifanayo. 

Imithetho yempahla yengqondo iyinkimbinkimbi. Imisebenzi yezinganekwane ibandakanya umthetho wezimpawu zokuhweba, amalungelo afanayo, amalungelo okusebenzisa ngendlela efanele aphethwe umphakathi (okuhlanganisa nelungelo lokubhuqa noma ukubhuqa), nezinye izinkinga eziningi ezithintanayo.[6] 

Ababhali bangase bahlukaniselane amalungelo ahlukene abanawo emaqenjini ahlukene ngezikhathi ezihlukene, nangezinhloso noma ukusetshenziswa okuhlukile, njengelungelo lokushintsha isiqephu sibe ifilimu, uchungechunge lwethelevishini, noma umdlalo wevidiyo. Uma omunye umuntu ekhetha ukulungisa umsebenzi, kungase kudingeke ukuthi aguqule izici zesakhiwo noma amagama abalingiswa ukuze agweme ukwephula ukushintshwa kwangaphambilini. Umbhali angase futhi angabi namalungelo lapho esebenza ngaphansi kwenkontileka abeyoba nawo, njengalapho enza umsebenzi ozoqashwa (isb, uqashelwe ukubhala incwadi yokuvakasha yedolobha kahulumeni kamasipala ongumnikazi wamalungelo okushicilela umsebenzi osuqediwe), noma lapho ebhala izinto zisebenzisa impahla yengqondo ephethwe abanye (njengalapho kubhalwa inoveli noma umdlalo wesikrini okuyisitolimende esisha ku-franchise yemidiya eseyisunguliwe). 

E-United States, I-Copyright Clause of the Constitution of the United States (I-athikili I, Isigaba 8, Isigaba somthetho 8) sinikeza ICongress amandla "okuthola Izikhathi Ezilinganiselwe Kubabhali Nabasunguli Ilungelo Elikhethekile Lemibhalo Yabo Ebhaliwe Nokutholwayo".[7] Ulimi oluphathelene nababhali lwasuselwa eziphakamisweni zikaCharles Pinckney, "zokuvikela ababhali amalungelo akhethekile isikhathi esilinganiselwe", kanye noJames Madison, "ukuvikela ababhali bombhalo amalungelo abo okukopisha isikhathi esilinganiselwe", noma, ngokunye, "ukukhuthaza, ngamaphrimiyamu afanele kanye Nezinhlinzeko, ukuthuthukiswa kolwazi oluwusizo nokutholakele".[8] Zombili lezi ziphakamiso zadluliselwa eKomidini Lemininingwane, elabika ngesiphakamiso esiqukethe ulimi lokugcina, esafakwa kuMthethosisekelo ngesivumelwano esivumelana ngazwilinye sengqungquthela.[8] 

Imibono yefilosofi yesimo sombhali
ISitatimende sika-Anne ngo-1710 sabeka isibonelo esingokomthetho esabeka izisekelo ze-copyright, futhi sasungula umbhali njengomqambi oyedwa womsebenzi wokubhala. Nakuba lo mthetho uvuma ukuthi amazwi ombhali ayimpahla yawo Yobuhlakani, awuzange uvikele imibono yalowo mbhali. Ngokwesibonelo, omunye umlobi wayengakopisha ngokusemthethweni isiqephu somunye umbhali, inqobo nje uma amagama ayengakopishwa njengezwi nezwi. Ngamanye amazwi, iSifanekiso sika-Anne sasivikela indlela yombhali yokukhuluma kodwa hhayi imicabango esekelwe kumazwi abo.[9] 


UJames Joyce wayengunoveli ovelele wase-Ireland, imbongi kanye nomhlaziyi wemibhalo phakathi nekhulu lama-20. 
Kuthiyori yemibhalo, abagxeki bathola izinkinga egameni elithi umbhali ngale kwalokho okuhlanganisa ubunikazi esimweni esisemthethweni. Ngemuva kwemibhalo yangemva kwesimanje, abagxeki abanjengoRoland Barthes noMichel Foucault baye bahlola indima nokuhlobana kombhali encazelweni noma ekuchazeni umbhalo wombhalo. 

U-Barthes uphonsela inselelo umbono wokuthi umbhalo ungabalelwa kunoma yimuphi umbhali oyedwa. Ubhala, endabeni yakhe ethi “Death of the Author” (1968), ukuthi “ulimi olukhulumayo, hhayi umbhali.”[10] Amagama nolimi lombhalo ngokwawo anquma futhi adalule incazelo kuBarthes, hhayi othile onomthwalo wemfanelo ongokomthetho ngenqubo yokukhiqizwa kwawo. Wonke umugqa wombhalo obhaliwe uwumfanekiso nje wezinkomba ezivela kunoma yiliphi inqwaba yamasiko, noma, njengoba uBarthes ekubeka, "umbhalo uyingqikithi yezingcaphuno ezithathwe ezikhungweni ezingenakubalwa zesiko"; akukona okoqobo.[10] Ngalokhu, umbono wombhali uyasuswa embhalweni, futhi imingcele eyayibekwe ngaphambili ngumqondo wezwi elilodwa elinegunya, incazelo eyodwa yokugcina neyomhlaba wonke, iyachithwa. Incazelo nencazelo yomsebenzi akudingekile ukuba kufunwe kulowo owawukhiqizayo, “njengokungathi njalo ekugcineni, ngokusebenzisa umfanekiso osobala noma osobala wenganekwane, izwi lomuntu oyedwa, umbhali ‘esithululela isifuba’ kithi.”[10] Umqondo, isiko, ukushiseka kombhali kungashaywa indiva lapho utolika amagama ngolimi olucebile ngokwalo, ngoba wona ngokwawo uhumusha umbhalo ocebile. Ukuveza izincazelo emsebenzini obhaliwe ngaphandle kokukhanga usaziwayo wombhali, abakuthandayo, abakuthandayo, okungalungile, kuBarthes, ukuvumela ulimi ukuba lukhulume, kunombhali.

UMichel Foucault uphikisa endabeni yakhe ethi "Uyini umbhali?" (1969) ukuthi bonke ababhali bangababhali, kodwa akubona bonke ababhali abangababhali. Uthi “incwadi yangasese ingase ibe nomuntu oyisayinileyo—ayinaye umbhali.”[11] Ukuze umfundi abele isihloko sombhali kunoma yimuphi umsebenzi obhaliwe uwukuchaza izindinganiso ezithile embhalweni lapho, ku-Foucault, esebenza ngokuhlanganyela nomqondo “womsebenzi wombhali.”[11] Umsebenzi wombhali we-Foucault uwumbono wokuthi umbhali osebenzayo akayona ingxenye yesakhiwo esibhaliwe kuphela, kodwa empeleni uyingxenye yesakhiwo esibhaliwe, kodwa uyingxenye yesakhiwo esibhaliwe kuphela. inqubo yokuhumusha. Igama lombhali "libonisa isimo senkulumo emphakathini namasiko," futhi ngesinye isikhathi lalisetshenziswa njengehange lokuhumusha umbhalo, umkhuba uBarthes ayengawuphikisa awuwona umzamo ofanele noma osebenzayo.[11] 

Enweba esikhundleni sikaFoucault, u-Alexander Nehamas ubhala ukuthi uFoucault uphakamisa ukuthi "umbhali [...] yinoma ubani okungaqondwa ukuthi ukhiqize umbhalo othile njengoba siwuhumusha," hhayi ukuthi ubani obhale umbhalo.[12] Yilo mehluko phakathi kokukhiqiza umsebenzi obhaliwe kanye nokukhiqiza incazelo noma incazelo encwadini ebhaliwe ukuthi bobabili uBarthes noFoucault banesithakazelo kuwo. UFoucault uxwayisa ngezingozi zokugcina igama lomlobi engqondweni ngesikhathi sokuhumusha, ngoba kungase kuthinte inani nencazelo umuntu asingatha ngayo incazelo. 

Abacusumbuli bezincwadi uBarthes noFoucault basikisela ukuthi abafundi akufanele bathembele noma babheke umbono wezwi elilodwa eliphakeme lapho behumusha umsebenzi obhaliwe, ngenxa yezinkinga ezikhona ngesihloko sombhali esithi "umbhali." Baxwayisa ngezingozi izincazelo ezingase zibe nazo lapho behlobanisa indaba yamagama nolimi olungokwemvelo nobuntu bezwi elilodwa elinegunya. Kunalokho, abafundi kufanele bavumele umbhalo ukuthi uhunyushwe ngokwemibandela yolimi ngokuthi "umbhali." 

Ubudlelwano nomshicileli 
Ukuzishicilela 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukuzishicilela 
Ukuzishicilela ngokwakho kulapho ababhali besebenza njengabashicileli bezincwadi zabo futhi bethatha umthwalo ogcwele kanye nokulawula izindleko. Lezo zindleko zihlanganisa ukuhlela, ukuphrinta, nokusabalalisa imisebenzi yabo. 

Ukushicilela kwendabuko 
Ngokushicilela okugunyaziwe, umshicileli wenza zonke izinhlelo zokushicilelwa futhi umbhali ukhokhela zonke izindleko.

Ababhali bangase banxeshezelwe ngephesenti lesamba sencwadi noma inani elithile, noma ngokuthola inani elingashintshi ngekhophi ngayinye ethengisiwe. Ukuze kuncishiswe ubungozi, ngezinye izikhathi abashicileli bahlehlisa izinkokhelo ezinjalo kuze kube yilapho inani elithile lamakhophi selidayisiwe. ECanada, le ndlela yavela ngawo-1890 kodwa ayizange isakazeke kwaze kwaba ngawo-1920. Ababhali abasunguliwe bangase banikezwe izinkokhelo kusengaphambili ngokumelene nezinzuzo zesikhathi esizayo, nakuba lo mkhuba usungavamile kakhulu. Abashicileli abaningi abazimele manje bakhokha izinzuzo njengephesenti lamarisidi engqikithi nakuba amarisidi engqikithi abalwa kanjani angahluka ngomshicileli. Ngaphansi kwalezi zivumelwano, umbhali akanasibopho sanoma yiziphi izindleko zokushicilela; umthwalo wezezimali uthwalwa ngokuphelele ngumshicileli, ogcina ingxenye enkulu yemali engenayo. Bheka futhi isihloko esithi Isinxephezelo.[13] 

I-Vanity publishing 
Isihloko esikhulu: I-Vanity press 
Vanity abashicileli ngokuvamile bakhokhisa imali ephansi ngokuhlela ukushicilelwa, banikeze inkundla yokuthengisa, bese bethatha iphesenti lokudayiswa kwayo yonke ikhophi yencwadi.[14] Umbhali uthola yonke imali eyenziwe.[14] Izinto eziningi ezishicilelwe ngale ndlela ezamaqembu e-niche hhayi izethameli eziningi.[15] 

Ukushicilela okuyize, noma ukushicilelwa komxhaso,[15] kucwaswa emhlabeni womsebenzi. Ngo-1983, uBill Henderson wachaza abashicileli abayize njengabantu “abazoshicilela noma yini umlobi azoyikhokhela, ngokuvamile kube ukulahlekelwa umbhali kanye nenzuzo enhle yomshicileli.”[16] Ekushicileleni koxhaso, ukuthengiswa kwezincwadi akuwona umthombo oyinhloko wemali engenayo yabashicileli, kodwa kunalokho izimali ezikhokhiswa ababhali ukuze bakhiqize incwadi ekuqaleni. Ngenxa yalokhu, abashicileli abayize akudingeki batshale imali ekwenzeni izincwadi zithengiseke njengoba kudingeka abanye abashicileli.[15] Lokhu kuholela ekutheni izincwadi ezisezingeni eliphansi zethulwe emakethe. 

Ubudlelwano nomhleli 
Ubudlelwano phakathi kombhali nomhleli, imvamisa okuwukuphela kwesixhumanisi sombhali nenkampani eshicilelayo, ngokuvamile bubonakala njengendawo yengxabano. Ukuze umbhali afinyelele izethameli zabo, ngokuvamile ngokushicilelwa, umsebenzi ngokuvamile kufanele udonse ukunaka komhleli. Umbono wombhali njengoyedwa owenza incazelo wesidingo ushintsha ukuze ufake amathonya omhleli kanye nomshicileli ukuze abandakanye izethameli ngokubhala njengesenzo somphakathi. 

Kunezinhlobo ezintathu eziyinhloko zokuhlela: 

Ukuqinisekisa (ukuhlola uhlelo lolimi nesipelingi, ukufuna amaphutha okubhala), 
Indaba (okungenzeka iyindawo ejulile yokucasuka kubo bobabili umbhali nomshicileli), kanye 
-Layout (ukuhlelwa kohlobo okudingekayo ukuze kulungiswe umsebenzi ozoshicilelwa ngokuvamile kudinga izinguquko ezincane zombhalo, ngakho-ke kuqashwa umhleli wesakhiwo ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukuthi lokhu akuwenzi umqondo wombhalo).
I-eseyi kaPierre Bourdieu ethi "The Field of Cultural Production" iveza imboni yokushicilela "njengendawo yokuthatha isikhundla sokufunda noma sobuciko," ebuye ibizwe ngokuthi "umkhakha wokuzabalaza," okuchazwa ukushuba kwesimo nokunyakaza okukhona phakathi kwezikhundla ezahlukahlukene kulo mkhakha.[17] U-Bourdieu uthi "umkhakha wokuthatha izikhundla [...] akuwona umkhiqizo wenhloso yokufuna ukubumbana noma ukuvumelana okunenjongo," okusho ukuthi imboni ebonakala ngokuthatha izikhundla ayiyona eyokuvumelana nokungathathi hlangothi.[18] Ikakhulukazi kumbhali, ubunikazi babo emsebenzini wabo benza umsebenzi wabo ube yingxenye yobunikazi babo, futhi kuningi okusengcupheni mathupha mayelana nokuxoxisana ngegunya ngalobo bunikazi. Nokho, ngumhleli "onamandla okubeka incazelo evelele yombhali ngakho-ke ukuhlukanisa inani labantu abanelungelo lokubamba iqhaza emzabalazweni wokuchaza umbhali".[19] "Njengabatshalizimali bezamasiko," abashicileli bancike esikhundleni somhleli ukuze bahlonze ukutshalwa kwezimali okuhle "kumali yamasiko" okungase kukhule kuveze imali enkulu yezomnotho kuzo zonke izikhundla.[20] 

Ngokocwaningo lukaJames Curran, uhlelo lwezindinganiso ezihlanganyelwe phakathi kwabahleli eBrithani selwenze ingcindezi phakathi kwababhali ukuba babhale ukuze kufanelane nalokho ababekulindele abahleli, kususe ukugxila ezilalelini zomfundi futhi kubeke ubunzima ebuhlotsheni phakathi kwababhali nabahleli kanye nasekubhaleni njengesenzo somphakathi. Ngisho nokubuyekezwa kwencwadi ngabahleli kunokubaluleka okukhulu kunokwamukelwa kwabafundi.[21] Ababhali 

Besinxephezelo 
bathembele ezinkokhelweni kusengaphambili, ezinkokhelweni zenkosi, ukulungiswa komsebenzi ukuze ufane nomdlalo wesikrini, nasezinkokhelweni eziqoqwe ekunikezeni izinkulumo.[22] 

Inkontileka evamile yombhali ngokuvamile izobandakanya ukuhlinzekwa kwenkokhelo ngendlela ye-advanced and royalties. 

I-Advance: isamba esikhokhwa ngaphambi kokushicilelwa. I-advanced kumele itholwe ngaphambi kokuthi kukhokhwe ama-royalties. Ingakhokhwa ngesamba sezimali ezimbili: inkokhelo yokuqala ngokusayinwa kwenkontileka, neyesibili lapho kulethwa umbhalo wesandla oqediwe noma lapho ushicilelwe. 
Inkokhelo yemali eyinzuzo: inani elikhokhelwa ababhali ngekhophi ngayinye yencwadi ethengiswayo futhi ngokuvamile lilinganiselwa ku-10–12%, kodwa ababhali abazishicilele ngokwabo bangathola izinzuzo ezingaba ngu-40% - 60% ngokuthengiswa kwencwadi ngayinye.[22] Inkontileka yombhali ingase icacise, isibonelo, ukuthi bazozuza u-10% yenani lokudayisa lencwadi ngayinye ethengisiwe. Ezinye izinkontileka zicacisa isilinganiso semali ekhokhwayo (isibonelo, lapho izinkokhelo ziqala ku-10% ekuthengisweni kokuqala okuyi-10,000, kodwa bese zikhuphukela kumaphesenti aphezulu ezilinganisweni zokuthengisa eziphezulu).
Ngokuvamile, ibhuku lombhali kufanele lizuze ngaphambi kwesikhathi ngaphambi kokuba kukhokhwe ezinye izinzuzo. Isibonelo, uma umlobi ekhokhelwa imali engaphambili engu-$2000, futhi isilinganiso sakhe senzuzo singu-10% wencwadi enenani elingu-$20 - okungukuthi, u-$2 incwadi ngayinye - incwadi izodinga ukuthengisa amakhophi angu-1000 ngaphambi kokuthi kwenziwe enye inkokhelo. Abashicileli ngokuvamile bagodla inkokhelo yephesenti lemali ezuziwe uma kuqhathaniswa nembuyiselo. 

Kwamanye amazwe, ababhali baphinde bathole imali engenayo ngohlelo lukahulumeni olufana ne-ELR (ilungelo lezemfundo lemalimboleko) kanye nezinhlelo ze-PLR (ilungelo lokuboleka umphakathi) e-Australia. Ngaphansi kwalezi zinhlelo, ababhali bakhokhelwa imali ngenani lamakhophi ezincwadi zabo emitatsheni yolwazi yezemfundo kanye/noma yomphakathi. 
 
Kulezi zinsuku, ababhali abaningi bengeza imali yabo engenayo ngokuthengiswa kwezincwadi ngokuzibandakanya okukhuluma esidlangalaleni,ukuvakasha kwezikole, izindawo zokuhlala, izibonelelo, kanye nezikhundla zokufundisa.

Ababhali be-Ghostwriters, ababhali bezobuchwepheshe, nababhali bezincwadi ngokuvamile bakhokhelwa ngendlela ehlukile: ngokuvamile inkokhelo emisiwe noma isilinganiso segama ngalinye esikhundleni samaphesenti okuthengisa. 

Ngonyaka wezi-2016, ngokusho kwe-US Bureau of Labor Statistics, cishe abantu abayi-130,000 basebenza ezweni njengababhali, okwenza isilinganiso sama- $ 61,240 ngonyaka. 

I-ebook (ifushane ngencwadi ye-elekthronikhi), futhi ebhalwe ngokuthi i-e-book noma i-eBook, iyincwadi eshicilelwe etholakala ngendlela ye-elekthronikhi, ehlanganisa umbhalo, izithombe, noma kokubili, efundeka kuphaneli eyisicaba yamakhompyutha noma ezinye izinto zikagesi.[1] Nakuba ngezinye izikhathi kuchazwa "njengenguqulo ye-elekthronikhi yencwadi ephrintiwe", [2] amanye ama-e-books akhona ngaphandle kokuphrinta okulinganayo. I-E-books ingafundwa kumadivayisi e-e-reader azinikele, nakunoma iyiphi idivayisi yekhompyutha enesikrini sokubuka esilawulekayo, okuhlanganisa amakhompyutha edeskithophu, amakhompyutha aphathekayo, amaphilisi nama-smartphone. 

Ngeminyaka yawo-2000s, bekunomkhuba wokuthengiswa kwezincwadi nama-e-book okuthuthela ku-inthanethi, [3] lapho abafundi bethenga khona izincwadi zendabuko zamaphepha nama-e-book kumawebhusayithi besebenzisa izinhlelo ze-e-commerce. Ngezincwadi eziphrintiwe, abafundi baya ngokuya bephequlula ezithombeni zamakhava ezincwadi kumawebhusayithi womshicileli noma wesitolo sezincwadi nokukhetha noku-oda izihloko ku-inthanethi. Izincwadi zamaphepha zibe sezilethwa kumfundi ngeposi nanoma iyiphi enye insiza yokudiliva. Ngama-e-books, abasebenzisi bangabhekabheka ngezihloko ku-inthanethi, bakhethe futhi ba-ode izihloko, bese i-e-book ingathunyelwa kubo nge-inthanethi noma umsebenzisi angadawuniloda i-e-book.[4] Ngasekuqaleni kwawo-2010, ama-e-books ayeseqale ukudlula ikhava eqinile ngezibalo ezishicilelwe e-US[5]
 
Izizathu eziyinhloko zokuba abantu bathenge ama-e-books kungenzeka kungenxa yamanani aphansi, ukunethezeka okwenyuka (njengoba bengathenga besekhaya noma besendleleni ngamadivaysi eselula) kanye nokukhethwa okukhulu kwezihloko.[6] Ngama-e-books, "amabhukhimakhi e-electronic enza ireferensi ibe lula, futhi izifundi ze-e-book zingavumela umsebenzisi ukuthi achaze amakhasi." "Nakuba izincwadi zezinganekwane nezingezona izinganekwane ziza ngamafomethi e-e-book, izinto zobuchwepheshe zifaneleka ngokukhethekile ukulethwa kwe-e-book ngoba zingaseshwa ngokwedijithali" ukuze uthole amagama angukhiye. Ngaphezu kwalokho, ezincwadini zokuhlela, izibonelo zamakhodi zingakopishwa.[7] E-US, inani lokufundwa kwe-e-book liyakhula. Ngo-2021, u-30% wabantu abadala base befunde i-e-book ngonyaka odlule, uma kuqhathaniswa no-17% ngo-2011.[8] Ngo-2014, u-50% wabantu abadala baseMelika babene-e-reader noma ithebhulethi, uma kuqhathaniswa nabangu-30% abangabanikazi bamadivayisi anjalo ngo-2013.[9] 

Ngaphandle kwezincwadi namamagazini ashicilelwe anokulingana kwedijithali, kukhona nezincwadi zokufunda zedijithali ezihloselwe ukusebenza njengombhalo wekilasi nosizo emfundweni esekelwe kubuchwepheshe. 

I-Teminology 
E-books nayo ibizwa ngokuthi "ama-ebooks", "e-books", "eBooks", "Ebooks", "e-Books", "e-journals", "e-editions", noma "digital books". Idivayisi eklanyelwe ngqo ukufunda i-e-books ibizwa nge-"e-reader", "ebook device", noma "eReader". 

Umlando 
The Readies (1930) 
Abanye balandelela umqondo we-e-reader, ithuluzi elizokwenza umsebenzisi akwazi ukubuka izincwadi esikrinini, ku-manifesto ka-1930 ka-Bob Brown, eyabhalwa ngemva kokubuka i-"talkie" yakhe yokuqala (ifilimu enomsindo). Wayiqamba ngokuthi The Readies, echitha umqondo we-"talkie".[10] Encwadini yakhe, uBrown uthi amamuvi ayenze yadlula le ncwadi ngokwakha "izingxoxo" futhi, ngenxa yalokho, ukufunda kufanele kuthole indlela entsha: 

Umshini wokufunda olula engingakwazi ukuwuphatha noma ukuwuhambisa,namathisela kunoma iyiphi ipulaki yesibani esidala futhi ufunde amanoveli amagama ayikhulu ngemizuzu eyi-10 uma ngifuna, futhi ngifuna.

Umbono kaBrown, nokho, wawugxile kakhulu ekuguquleni ukubhalwa kokubhalwa kwezincwadi kanye nesilulumagama, kunasemaphakathi. Uthi: "Sekuyisikhathi sokukhipha isivalo" futhi siqale "inguquko enegazi yegama," yethula izinombolo ezinkulu zezimpawu ze-portmanteau ukuze zithathe indawo yamagama avamile, nezimpawu zokuloba ukuze zilingise isenzo noma ukunyakaza, ngakho-ke akucaci ukuthi lokhu kuhambisana yini nomlando "wezincwadi ze-e-book" noma cha. Kamuva abafundi be-e abakaze balandele imodeli efana nekaBrown. Kodwa-ke, ubikezele ngokunembile ukuguqulwa okuncane nokuphatheka kwe-e-readers. Esihlokweni, uJennifer Schuessler uyabhala: “Umshini, uBrown wagomela, wawuzovumela abafundi ukuba balungise usayizi wohlobo, bagweme ukusikeka kwamaphepha futhi balondoloze izihlahla, kuyilapho besheshisa usuku lapho amazwi ‘angaqoshwa khona ngokuqondile ku-ether eshayayo.’” UBrown wayekholelwa ukuthi i-e-reader (kanye nemibono yakhe yokushintsha umbhalo ngokwawo) izoletha ukuphila okusha ngokuphelele ekufundeni. U-Schuessler uyihlobanisa no-DJ ophotha izingoma ezindala ukuze akhe isigqi noma ingoma entsha ngokuphelele, ngokuphambene ne-remix yengoma evamile.[11] 

Umsunguli 
Umsunguli we-e-book yokuqala akuvunyelwana ngayo kabanzi. Abanye abantu abazobhapathizwa bahlanganisa lokhu okulandelayo: 

URoberto Busa (1946-1970) 
I-e-book yokuqala ingase ibe i-Index Thomisticus, inkomba ye-elekthronikhi echazwe kakhulu emisebenzini kaThomas Aquinas, eyalungiselelwa uRoberto Busa, SJ kusukela ngo-1946 futhi yaqedwa ngawo-1970. Nakuba ekuqaleni yayigcinwe kuyi-computer eyodwa, inguqulo ye-CD-ROM esakazwayo yavela ngo-1989. Nokho, lo msebenzi ngezinye izikhathi uyayekwa. Mhlawumbe lokhu kungenxa yokuthi umbhalo ofakwe ekhompyutheni ubuyindlela yokufunda imibhalo ebhaliwe nokuthuthukisa amakhonkodensi ezilimi, kunokuba kube njengohlelo olushicilelwe ngokwalo.[13] Ngo-2005, i-Index yashicilelwa ku-inthanethi.[14] 

U-Ángela Ruiz Robles (1949) 
Ngo-1949, u-Ángela Ruiz Robles, uthisha waseFerrol, e-Spain, wagunyaza i-Enciclopedia Mecánica, noma i-Mechanical Encyclopedia, umshini owawusebenza emoyeni ocindezelwe lapho umbhalo nezithombe zaziqukethwe kuma-spools abasebenzisi ababezowalayisha kuwo azungezisayo. Umqondo wakhe kwakuwukwenza ithuluzi elizonciphisa inani lezincwadi ezithwalwa abafundi bakhe esikoleni. Umshini wokugcina wawuhlelelwe ukuba uhlanganise okurekhodiwe okulalelwayo, ingilazi yokukhulisa, umshini wokubala, nesibani sikagesi ukuze sifundwe ebusuku.[15] Idivayisi yakhe ayizange ifakwe ekukhiqizweni kodwa i-prototype iboniswa ku-National Museum of Science and Technology e-A Coruña.[16] 

UDouglas Engelbart no-Andries van Dam (1960s)
Kungenjalo, ezinye izazi-mlando zicabanga ukuthi izincwadi ze-elekthronikhi zaqala ekuqaleni kwawo-1960, kanye nephrojekthi ye-NLS eholwa nguDouglas Engelbart eStanford Research Institute (SRI), kanye neHypertext Editing System kanye namaphrojekthi we-FRESS aholwa ngu-Andries van Dam eBrown University.[17][18][19] Amadokhumenti e-FRESS asebenza kumafreyimu amakhulu e-IBM futhi ayegxile kusakhiwo kunokuba agxile emugqeni. Zazifomethwe ngendlela eguquguqukayo kubasebenzisi abahlukene, i-hardware yokubonisa, osayizi bewindi, njalonjalo, kanye nokuba namathebula azenzakalelayo wokuqukethwe, izinkomba, nokunye. Zonke lezi zinhlelo zinikeze nokuxhumana okubanzi, ihluzo, namanye amakhono. UVan Dam ngokuvamile kucatshangwa ukuthi waqamba igama elithi "incwadi kagesi",[20][21] futhi yasungulwa ngokwanele ukuze isetshenziswe esihlokweni se-athikili ngo-1985.[22] 

I-FRESS yayisetshenziselwa ukufunda imibhalo eyisisekelo ebanzi ku-inthanethi, kanye nesichasiselo nezingxoxo eziku-inthanethi ezifundweni ezimbalwa, ezihlanganisa i-English Poetry kanye ne-Biochemistry. Ubuhlakani bukaBrown basebenzise kakhulu i-FRESS. Ngokwesibonelo isazi sefilosofi uRoderick Chisholm wasisebenzisa ukuze akhiqize izincwadi zakhe ezimbalwa. Ngakho-ke ku-Preface to Person and Object (1979) uyabhala: "Le ncwadi ibingeke iqedwe ngaphandle kwe-File Retrieval and Editing System eyenza isikhathi eside..."[23] Umsebenzi weBrown University ezinhlelweni zezincwadi ze-elekthronikhi waqhubeka iminyaka eminingi, okuhlanganisa amaphrojekthi axhaswe yi-US Navy okulungisa ama-elekthronikhi; eyakha i-DynaText, uhlelo lokuqala lwe-e-reader olusekelwe ku-SGML; kanye nomsebenzi omkhulu we-Scholarly Technology Group ngezinga le-Open eBook. 

UMichael S. Hart (1971) 

uMichael S. Hart (kwesobunxele) kanye noGregory Newby (kwesokudla) beProject Gutenberg, ku-Hackers on Planet Earth (HOPE) Conference, 2006 
Naphezu komlando wangaphambili obanzi, izincwadi ezimbalwa zibika uMichael S. Hart njengomsunguli we-e-book.[26][27][28] Ngo-1971, opharetha be-Xerox Sigma V mainframe eNyuvesi yase-Illinois banikeze uHart isikhathi esiningi sekhompyutha. Efuna ukuwusebenzisa ngokufanelekile lo mthombo, wakha idokhumenti yakhe yokuqala ye-elekthronikhi ngokubhala I-United States Declaration of Independence kuyikhompyutha enombhalo ongenalutho. U-Hart uhlele ukudala amadokhumenti esebenzisa umbhalo ongenalutho ukuze awenze kube lula ngangokunokwenzeka ukulanda nokubuka kumadivayisi. Ngemva kokuba uHart eguqule okokuqala iSimemezelo Senkululeko sase-US sibe idokhumenti ye-elekthronikhi ngo-1971, i-Project Gutenberg yethulwa ukwenza amakhophi e-electronic emibhalo eyengeziwe, ikakhulukazi izincwadi.[29] 

Ukuqaliswa kwezingxenyekazi zekhompuyutha zakuqala
Imishini enikelwe yehadiwe yokufunda i-ebook yaqala ukuvela ngeminyaka yama-70s kanye nama-80s, ngaphezu kwezixazululo zohlaka oluyinhloko ne-laptop, kanye nokuqoqwa kwedatha ngayinye ngayinye. Ukuqaliswa kokuqala kwe-e-book kwakuyisibonelo sedeskithophu sekhompiyutha ehlongozwayo yamanothibhuku, i-Dynabook, ngeminyaka yawo-1970 e-PARC: ikhompuyutha yomuntu siqu ephathekayo enenhloso evamile ekwazi ukubonisa izincwadi ukuze zifundwe.[30] Ngo-1980, uMnyango Wezokuvikela wase-US waqala ukuthuthukiswa komqondo wedivayisi yokulethwa kwe-elekthronikhi ephathwayo yolwazi lokulungiswa kobuchwepheshe ebizwa ngokuthi iphrojekthi i-PEAM, i-Portable Electronic Aid for Maintenance. Ukucaciswa okuningiliziwe kwaqedwa ngo-FY 1981/82, futhi ukuthuthukiswa kwe-prototype kwaqala nge-Texas Instruments ngawo lowo nyaka. Ama-prototypes amane akhiqizwa futhi alethwa ukuze ahlolwe ngo-1986, futhi ukuhlolwa kwaqedwa ngo-1987. Umbiko wokugcina ofingqiwe wakhiqizwa ngo-1989 yi-US Army Research Institute for Behavioral and Social Sciences, eyabhalwa uRobert Wisher kanye no-J. Peter Kincaid.[31] Isicelo selungelo lobunikazi sedivayisi ye-PEAM,[32] enesihloko esithi "I-Apparatus yokuletha imiyalelo yohlobo lwenqubo", sathunyelwa yi-Texas Instruments ngomhla ka-4 Disemba 1985, ibala u-John K. Harkins no-Stephen H. Morriss njengabaqambi. 


Incwadi yokuqala ye-elekthronikhi ephathwayo, "Usizo Lwe-elekthronikhi Lomuntu Wokulondolozwa" loMnyango Wezokuvikela waseMelika 
Ngo-1992, u-Sony wethula i-Data Discman, umfundi wezincwadi we-elekthronikhi ongafunda ama-e-books agcinwe kuma-CD. Enye yezincwadi ze-elekthronikhi eyayingadlalwa kuyi-Data Discman yayibizwa ngokuthi i-Library of the Future.[33] Ama-e-books akudala ngokuvamile ayebhalelwa izindawo ezikhethekile kanye nezithameli ezilinganiselwe, okwakuhloswe ukuthi zifundwe kuphela ngamaqembu amancane nazinikele anentshisekelo. Ububanzi besihloko salezi zincwadi ze-e-book buhlanganisa imanyuwali yezobuchwepheshe yehadiwe, amasu okukhiqiza, nezinye izifundo. Ngawo-1990, ukutholakala okujwayelekile kwe-inthanethi kwenza ukudlulisa amafayela e-elekthronikhi kwaba lula kakhulu, okuhlanganisa nezincwadi ze-elekthronikhi.[catation] 

Ngo-1993, u-Paul Baim wakhulula isitaki se-HyperCard samahhala, esibizwa nge-EBook, esasivumela ukungeniswa kalula kwanoma yiliphi ifayela lombhalo ukudala inguqulo yekhasi efana nencwadi ye-electronic paperback. Isici esiphawulekayo kwaba ukulandelela okuzenzakalelayo kwekhasi lokugcina elifundwe ukuze lapho ubuyela 'ebhukwini' ubuyiselwe lapho ubuyeke ukufunda khona ngaphambilini. Isihloko salesi sitaki kungenzeka sisize ekwandiseni igama elithi 'ebook'.[34] 

Amafomethi e-e-book 
Bheka futhi: Ukuqhathaniswa kwamafomethi e-e-book
 
Owesifazane ufunda incwadi esebenzisa i-e-reader
Njengoba amafomethi e-e-book avela futhi anda,[okucashunwa] kwakudingeka ukusekelwa okuthile okuvela ezinkampanini ezinkulu zesofthiwe, njenge-Adobe nefomethi yayo ye-PDF eyethulwa ngo-1993.[35] Ngokungafani namanye amafomethi amaningi, imibhalo ye-PDF ivamise ukuboshelwa kubukhulu obuthile nesakhiwo, kunokuba ihambisane nekhasi lamanje, iwindi, noma omunye usayizi. Amadivaysi e-e-reader ahlukene alandela amafomethi ahlukene, iningi lawo lamukela izincwadi ngefomethi eyodwa noma ezimbalwa, ngaleyo ndlela ahlukanise imakethe ye-e-book nakakhulu. Ngenxa yokukhethekile nokufunda okulinganiselwe kwama-e-books, imakethe ephukile yabashicileli abazimele nababhali abakhethekile ayizange ibe nokuvumelana mayelana nendinganiso yokupakishwa nokudayiswa kwama-e-book.[catation needed] 

Ngaleso sikhathi, osolwazi basungule i-Text Encoding Initiative, eyathuthukisa imihlahlandlela yokuvumelana yombhalo wekhodi wezincwadi nezinye izinto ezisetshenziswayo zokufunda okuthakaselwayo. Inqwaba yemibhalo neminye imisebenzi yenziwe kusetshenziswa indlela ye-TEI. Ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yawo-1990, kwasungulwa umfelandawonye ukuze kuthuthukiswe ifomethi ye-Open eBook njengendlela yokuthi ababhali nabashicileli banikeze umbhalo womthombo owodwa ongaphathwa isoftware yokufunda izincwadi kanye nezinkundla zehadiwe. Izazi ezimbalwa ezivela ku-TEI zazibambe iqhaza kakhulu ekuthuthukisweni kokuqala kwe-Open eBook, okuhlanganisa u-Allen Renear, u-Elli Mylonas, noSteven DeRose, bonke abavela ku-Brown. Igxile ekuphathekeni, Vula i-eBook njengoba kuchazwe amasethi angaphansi adingekayo e-XHTML ne-CSS; isethi yamafomethi we-multimedia (amanye angasetshenziswa, kodwa futhi kufanele kube nokubuyela emuva kwelinye lamafomethi adingekayo), kanye ne-schema ye-XML ye-"manifest", ukuze kufakwe uhlu lwezingxenye ze-e-book enikeziwe, ukukhomba ithebula lokuqukethwe, ubuciko bekhava, njalonjalo.[catation] Le fomethi iholele kufomethi evulekile ye-EPUB. I-Google Books iguqule imisebenzi eminingi yomphakathi ibe yile fomethi evuliwe.[36] 

Ngo-2010, ama-e-books aqhubeka nokuzuza ngochwepheshe bazo kanye nezimakethe ezingaphansi komhlaba. Ngesikhathi esifanayo, ababhali abanezincwadi ezingamukelwanga abashicileli banikela ngemisebenzi yabo ku-inthanethi ukuze ibonwe abanye.[37] Izinhlu zezincwadi ezingagunyaziwe (futhi ngezikhathi ezithile ezingagunyaziwe) zatholakala kuwebhu, futhi izingosi ezinikelwe kuma-e-books zaqala ukusabalalisa ulwazi olumayelana nama-e-books emphakathini.[38] Cishe izingxenye ezimbili kwezintathu zemakethe yokushicilela ye-e-book yase-US ilawulwa yi-"Big Five". Abashicileli be-"Big Five" yilaba: Hachette, HarperCollins, Macmillan, Penguin Random House kanye noSimon & Schuster.[39]
 
Imitapo yolwazi
Imitapo yolwazi yase-US yaqala ukunikela ngama-e-books mahhala emphakathini ngo-1998 ngokusebenzisa amawebhusayithi awo kanye nezinsiza ezihambisanayo, [40] nakuba ama-e-books ayengowezifundiswa, ezobuchwepheshe, noma achwepheshile ngokwemvelo, futhi ayengalandwa. Ngo-2003, imitapo yolwazi yaqala ukunikeza umphakathi izincwadi ze-elekhthronikhi ezingalawulwa mahhala nezingezona izinganekwane, yethula imodeli yokuboleka ye-e-book eyasebenza ngempumelelo kakhulu emitatsheni yolwazi yomphakathi.[41] Inani labasabalalisi bezincwadi ze-e-book kanye namamodeli abolekisayo aqhubekile nokukhula eminyakeni embalwa ezayo. Kusukela ngo-2005 kuya ku-2008, imitapo yolwazi ibe nokukhula okungama-60% kumaqoqo e-e-book.[42] Ngo-2010, i-Public Library Funding and Technology Access Study eyenziwe yi-American Library Association[43] yathola ukuthi ama-66% emitapo yolwazi yomphakathi e-US ahlinzeka ngezincwadi ze-e-book, [44] futhi inhlangano enkulu embonini yomtapo wolwazi yaqala ukuhlola ngokujulile izindaba eziphathelene nokubolekwa kwe-e-book, ivuma "iphuzu elibalulekile" lapho ubuchwepheshe be-e-book5 buzosungulwa kabanzi.[4] Okuqukethwe okuvela emitapweni yolwazi yomphakathi kungadawunilodeka kuma-e-readers kusetshenziswa isofthiwe yohlelo lokusebenza njenge-Overdrive ne-Hoopla.[46] 

I-US National Library of Medicine sekuyiminyaka eminingi ihlinzeka nge-PubMed, ibhukwana eliphelele lezincwadi zezokwelapha. Ekuqaleni kuka-2000, i-NLM yasungula inqolobane ye-PubMed Central, egcina izinguqulo ze-e-book ezinombhalo ogcwele wezihloko eziningi zejenali yezokwelapha nezincwadi, ngokusebenzisana nezazi nabashicileli kulo mkhakha. I-Pubmed Central futhi manje isihlinzeka ngokugcina kungobo yomlando kanye nokufinyelela kuma-athikili angaphezu kwezigidi ezingu-4.1, agcinwe ngefomethi evamile ye-XML eyaziwa ngokuthi i-Journal Article Tag Suite (JATS).
 
Naphezu kokwamukelwa kabanzi kwama-e-books, abanye abashicileli nababhali abakawutusi umqondo wokushicilela nge-elekthronikhi, becaphuna izinkinga ngesidingo sabasebenzisi, ukwephulwa kwelungelo lobunikazi kanye nezinselelo ngemishini yobunikazi nezinhlelo.[47] Ocwaningweni lwabasebenzi bemitapo yolwazi ye-interlibrary loan (ILL), kutholwe ukuthi u-92% wemitapo yolwazi unama-e-books emaqoqweni awo nokuthi u-27% waleyo mitapo yolwazi uxoxisane ngamalungelo e-ILL kwamanye ama-e-book awo. Le nhlolovo ithole izithiyo ezinkulu ekukhokheleni izincwadi ze-e-books phakathi kwemitapo yolwazi.[48] I-Patron-driven acquisition (i-PDA) ibilokhu itholakala iminyaka eminingana emitapweni yolwazi yomphakathi, okuvumela abathengisi ukuthi benze lula inqubo yokutholwa ngokunikela ngokufanisa iphrofayela yokukhetha yelabhulali nezihloko ze-e-book zomthengisi. Ikhathalogi yelabhulali ibe isigcwaliswa ngamarekhodi awo wonke ama-e-book afana nephrofayela. Isinqumo sokuthenga isihloko sishiyelwa kubaxhasi, nakuba umtapo wolwazi ungasetha imibandela yokuthenga njengenani eliphezulu kanye nezikhwama zokuthenga ukuze izimali ezizinikele zisetshenziswe ngokuvumelana nesabelomali somtapo wolwazi.[49] Umhlangano ka-2012 we-Association of American University Presses wawuhlanganisa iphaneli ku-PDA yezincwadi ezikhiqizwe imishini yokunyathelisa yasenyuvesi, ngokusekelwe embikweni wokuqala kaJoseph Esposito, umxhumanisi wokushicilela wedijithali ofunde okushiwo yi-PDA ngesibonelelo esivela ku-Andrew W. Mellon Foundation.[50] 

Izinselele 
Nakuba isidingo sezinsiza ze-e-book emitatsheni yolwazi sikhule eminyakeni engamashumi amabili yokuqala yekhulu lama-21, ubunzima buvimba imitapo yolwazi ekunikezeni ama-e-book athile kumakhasimende. Abashicileli bazothengisa ama-e-book emitapo yolwazi, kodwa ezimweni eziningi bazonikeza imitapo yolwazi ilayisense elinganiselwe esihlokweni, okusho ukuthi umtapo wolwazi awunawo ubunikazi bombhalo we-elekthronikhi kodwa uvunyelwe ukuwusakaza isikhathi esithile, noma inombolo ethile yokuphuma, noma kokubili. Lapho umtapo wezincwadi uthenga ilayisense ye-e-book, izindleko okungenani ziphindwe kathathu kunalokho obekungaba kumthengi siqu.[51] Amalayisense e-e-book abiza kakhulu kunezinhlelo zefomethi yephepha ngoba abashicileli bakhathazekile ngokuthi i-e-book ethengiswayo ingase ifundwe futhi/noma ihlolwe inombolo enkulu yabasebenzisi, okungase kudale umonakalo. Nokho, ezinye izifundo zithole umphumela ophambene uyiqiniso (isibonelo, u-Hilton no-Wikey 2010).[52] 

Ukugcinwa kwemibhalo 
egciniwe Ingobo yomlando Ye-inthanethi kanye Nomtapo Wolwazi Ovulekile kunikeza ngaphezu kwezigidi eziyisithupha zama-e-book omphakathi afinyeleleka ngokugcwele. I-Project Gutenberg inama-e-books wesizinda somphakathi angaphezu kuka-52,000 atholakala mahhala. 

Izifundi zehardware ezizinikele kanye nesoftware ephathwayo 
Isihloko esikhulu: I-E-reader 
Bheka futhi: Ukuqhathaniswa kwama-e-readers 

I-BEBook e-reader
I-e-reader, ebizwa nangokuthi i-e-book reader noma i-e-book device, iyisisetshenziswa se-elekthronikhi ephathwayo eklanyelwe ngokuyinhloko inhloso yokufunda ama-e-books nama-digital periodicals. I-e-reader iyafana ngefomu, kodwa inenhloso elinganiselwe kunethebhulethi. Uma kuqhathaniswa namathebulethi, ama-e-readers amaningi angcono kunamathebulethi okufunda ngoba aphatheka kakhudlwana, afundeka kangcono ekukhanyeni kwelanga futhi anempilo yebhethri ende.[53] NgoJulayi 2010, umthengisi wezincwadi ku-inthanethi i-Amazon.com yabika ukuthengiswa kwe-e-books ye-Kindle yobunikazi bayo, yadlula ukuthengiswa kwezincwadi ezinoqwembe oluqinile okokuqala ngqa ngekota yesibili ka-2010, yathi ithengise ama-e-books angu-140 kuzo zonke izincwadi ezinoqwembe oluqinile eziyi-100, okuhlanganisa namakhava aqinile okwakungenawo uhlelo lwedijithali.[54] NgoJanuwari 2011, ukuthengiswa kwe-e-book e-Amazon kwase kudlule ukuthengiswa kwayo kwe-paperback.[55] Kuyo yonke imakethe yase-US, ukuthengiswa kwencwadi ye-paperback kusekukhulu kakhulu kunekhava eqinile noma i-e-book. I-American Publishing Association ilinganisela ukuthi ama-e-books amele u-8.5% wokuthengiswa kusukela phakathi no-2010, kusukela ku-3% ngonyaka odlule.[56] Ekupheleni kwekota yokuqala ka-2012, ukuthengiswa kwe-e-book e-United States kweqa ukuthengiswa kwezincwadi ezinoqwembe oluqinile okokuqala ngqa.[5] 

Kuze kube sekupheleni kuka-2013, ukusetshenziswa kwe-e-reader kwakungavunyelwe ezindizeni phakathi nokusuka nokuhlalisa yi-FAA.[57] NgoNovemba 2013, i-FAA yavumela ukusetshenziswa kwama-e-readers ezindizeni ngaso sonke isikhathi uma Isemodini Yendiza, okusho ukuthi yonke imisakazo icishiwe, futhi iYurophu yalandela lesi siqondiso ngenyanga elandelayo.[58] Ngo-2014, i-New York Times yabikezela ukuthi ngo-2018 ama-e-books azokwenza ngaphezu kuka-50% wesamba semali engenayo yokushicilela yabathengi e-United States nase-Great Britain.[59] 
Incazelo

Izicelo 

Izinhlelo zokufunda kumadivaysi ahlukene 
Abanye abathengisi abakhulu bezincwadi kanye nonjiniyela abaningi abavela eceleni banikela mahhala (futhi kwezinye izimo, ikhokhwe ikhokhwe) izinhlelo zokusebenza zesoftware ye-e-reader (izinhlelo zokusebenza) zamakhompyutha we-Mac ne-PC kanye ne-Android, Blackberry, iPad, iPhone, Windows Phone kanye ne-Palm OS amadivayisi ukuvumela ukufundwa kwe-e-books kanye neminye imibhalo ngaphandle kwemishini ye-ebook ezinikele. Izibonelo izinhlelo zokusebenza ze-Amazon Kindle,[60] i-Barnes & Noble Nook, i-iBooks, i-Kobo eReader ne-Sony Reader. 

Ukuhlelwa komtapo wolwazi kuwuhlelo olusetshenziswa ngaphakathi komtapo wolwazi ukuhlela izinto, okuhlanganisa izincwadi, okurekhodiwe komsindo nevidiyo, izinto zikagesi, njll., kokubili emashalofini nakumakhathalogi nezinkomba. Into ngayinye ngokuvamile inikezwa inombolo yocingo, ekhomba indawo yento ngaphakathi kwesistimu. Izinto ezisetshenziswayo zingahlelwa ngezinto eziningi ezihlukene, ngokuvamile ngesakhiwo sesihlahla esilandelanayo esisekelwe esihlokweni noma kusetshenziswa isistimu yokuhlukanisa ngezigaba ezihlukene, evumela ukwabiwa kwezigaba eziningi entweni, okuvumela izigaba ukuthi zi-odwe ngezindlela eziningi.[1] 
Umlando

Ukuhlukaniswa ngezigaba komtapo wolwazi kuyisici esibalulekile nesibalulekile kumtapo wolwazi kanye nesayensi yolwazi. Ihlukile ekuhlukaniseni ngokwesayensi ngoba inomgomo wayo wokuhlinzeka ngokuhleleka okuwusizo kwemibhalo esikhundleni senhlangano yethiyori yolwazi.[2] Nakuba inenjongo engokoqobo yokudala ukuhleleka okungokoqobo kwemibhalo, ngokuvamile izama ukunamathela olwazini lwesayensi olwamukelekayo.[3] Ukuhlukaniswa ngezigaba komtapo wolwazi kusiza ukwamukela zonke izincwadi ezisanda kunyatheliswa ngohlelo oseluvele lwenziwa ngokulandelana ngokulandelana.[4] 

Ukuhlukaniswa ngezigaba komtapo wolwazi kungachazwa njengokuhlelwa kwezincwadi emashalofini, noma incazelo yazo, ngendlela ewusizo kakhulu kulabo abafunda ngenjongo yokugcina yokuhlanganisa izinto ezifanayo ndawonye. Ukuhlukaniswa ngezigaba komtapo wezincwadi kuhloselwe ukufeza lezi zinhloso ezine: uku-oda imikhakha yolwazi ngendlela ehlelekile, ukuhlanganisa izinto ezihlobene ngokulandelana okuwusizo kakhulu, ukunikeza ukufinyelela okuhlelekile eshalofini, nokunikeza indawo yento ethile eshalofini.[5] 

Ukuhlukaniswa ngezigaba komtapo wolwazi kuhlukile ekusebenziseni izihloko zezifundo ngokuthi ukuhlukaniswa kuhlela ulwazi ngendlela ehlelekile, kuyilapho izihloko zezihloko zinikeza ukufinyelela ezintweni zobuhlakani ngokusebenzisa amagama esilulumagama angase ahlelwe noma angahlelwa njengohlelo lolwazi.[6] Izici ezidingwa ukuhlukaniswa kwezincwadi ukuze kufinyelelwe lezi zinhloso yilezi: ukulandelana okuwusizo kwezifundo kuwo wonke amazinga, amazwibela akhumbulekayo kafushane, kanye nenqwaba yamasu namathuluzi okuhlanganiswa kwezinombolo.[7] 
Ngemva kwenguquko yokunyathelisa ekhulwini leshumi nesithupha, ukwanda kwezinto ezinyathelisiwe ezitholakalayo kwenza ukuhlukaniswa okubanzi okunjalo kungasebenzi, futhi ukuhlukaniswa kwezigaba eziyimbudumbudu ezengeziwe zezinto zomtapo wolwazi kwadingeka kuthuthukiswe ekhulwini leshumi nesishiyagalolunye.[9]

Izigaba zomtapo wolwazi zandulelwa izigaba ezisetshenziswa ababhali bezincwadi abanjengoConrad Gessner. Izikimu zokuqala zokuhlukanisa umtapo wolwazi zazihlela izincwadi ngezigaba zezifundo ezibanzi. Uhlelo lwakudala olwaziwayo lokuhlukanisa umtapo wolwazi yiPinakes kaCallimachus, isazi saseMtapowolwazi wase-Alexandria ngekhulu lesithathu BC. Phakathi nenkathi yeRenaissance and Reformation, “Imitapo yolwazi yayihlelwa ngokuvumelana nokufisa noma ulwazi lwabantu abaphethe.”[8] Lokhu kwashintsha indlela okwakuhlukaniswa ngayo izinto ezihlukahlukene. Amanye amaqoqo ayehlukaniswa ngolimi kanti amanye ayehlukaniswa ngendlela ayenyatheliswa ngayo. 


Ngo-1627 uGabriel Naudé wanyathelisa incwadi ethi Advice on Establishing a Library. Ngaleso sikhathi, wayesebenza emtatsheni wezincwadi wangasese kaPresident à mortier Henri de Mesmes II. I-Mesmes yayinezincwadi eziphrintiwe ezingaba ngu-8,000 neminye imibhalo yesandla ebhaliwe yesiGreki, isiLatini nesiFulentshi eminingi. Nakuba wawungumtapo wezincwadi ozimele, izazi ezinezikhombo zazikwazi ukuwufinyelela. Injongo Yeseluleko Sokusungula Umtapo Wezincwadi kwakuwukuhlonza imithetho yabaqoqi bezincwadi ezizimele ukuze bahlele amaqoqo abo ngendlela ehleleke kakhudlwana ukuze kwandiswe ukuba wusizo nobuhle beqoqo. UNaudé wakha uhlelo lokuhlukanisa ngezigaba olusekelwe ezigabeni eziyisikhombisa ezihlukene: imfundiso yenkolo, imithi, umthetho wezomthetho, umlando, ifilosofi, izibalo, kanye nobuntu. Lamakilasi ayisikhombisa kamuva ayezokwengezwa abe ishumi nambili.[10] Iseluleko Sokusungula Umtapo Wezincwadi sasimayelana nomtapo wolwazi wangasese, kodwa ngaphakathi kwencwadi efanayo, uNaudé wakhuthaza umbono wemitapo yolwazi yomphakathi evulekele bonke abantu kungakhathaliseki ukuthi banamandla angakanani okukhokhela ukufinyelela eqoqweni. Omunye wemitapo yolwazi edume kakhulu uNaudé awusiza wayithuthukisa kwakuyi-Bibliothèque Mazarine eParis. UNaudé wachitha iminyaka eyishumi lapho njengonobhala wezincwadi. Ngenxa yenkolelo kaNaudé eqinile yokufinyelela mahhala emitatsheni yezincwadi kubo bonke abantu, i-Bibliothèque Mazarine yaba umtapo wolwazi wokuqala womphakathi eFrance cishe ngo-1644.[11] 

Yize imitapo yolwazi yakha ukuhleleka phakathi kwamaqoqo ayo kusukela ekuqaleni kwekhulu lesihlanu BC, [9] ukuhlukaniswa kweParis Bookseller, okwathuthukiswa ngo-1842 nguJacques Charles Brunet, ngokuvamile kubonakala njengesigaba sokuqala sezincwadi zesimanje. UBrunet unikeze amakilasi amahlanu amakhulu: imfundiso yenkolo, umthetho, isayensi nobuciko, i-belles-lettres, kanye nomlando.[12] Ukuhlelwa manje kungabonakala njengomhlinzeki wokufinyelela kwesihloko olwazini endaweni yenethiwekhi.[13] 

Izinhlobo 
Ziningi izinhlelo ezijwayelekile zokuhlukaniswa kwelabhulali ezisetshenziswayo, kanti ezinye eziningi ziye zahlongozwa ngokuhamba kweminyaka. Kodwa-ke, ngokuvamile, izinhlelo zokuhlukanisa zingahlukaniswa zibe izinhlobo ezintathu kuye ngokuthi zisetshenziswa kanjani: 

Izikimu Zomhlaba Wonke 
Zihlanganisa zonke izifundo, isb. I-Dewey Decimal Classification (DDC), I-Universal Decimal Classification (UDC), kanye ne-Colon Classification (CC). 
Izikimu zokuhlukanisa eziqondile 
Ihlanganisa izifundo ezithile noma izinhlobo zezinto, isib. I-Iconclass (ubuciko), Ikhathalogi YaseBrithani Yokuhlukaniswa Komculo, kanye nesigaba sika-Dickinson (umculo), noma Ukuhlelwa Kwe-NLM (umuthi). 
Izikimu zikazwelonke 
Ezakhelwe ngokukhethekile amazwe athile, isb uhlelo lokuhlukaniswa komtapo wolwazi waseSweden, i-SAB (Sveriges Allmänna Biblioteksförening). I-Library of Congress Classification yakhelwe ukuzungeza iqoqo le-US Library of Congress futhi inokuchema kwe-American, European, kanye nobuKristu. Noma kunjalo, isetshenziswa kakhulu emitatsheni yolwazi emikhulu yezemfundo nocwaningo. 
Mayelana nokusebenza, izinhlelo zokuhlukanisa zivame ukuchazwa ngokuthi: 

Izibalo 
Izihloko zezihloko zihlelwa ngokulandelana kwezinhlamvu, izinombolo ezinikezwe isihloko ngasinye ngokulandelana kwezinhlamvu. Izihloko 
ze-Hierarchical 
zihlukaniswa ngokohlelo, kusukela kokujwayelekile kuya kokuqondile kakhulu. Izihloko 
ezibhekene/ezihlaziyayo 
zihlukaniswe izingxenye ze-orthogonal ezikhethekile. 
Zimbalwa izinhlelo zokubala ngokuphelele noma amasistimu ahlukene; amasistimu amaningi ayingxube kodwa athanda uhlobo olulodwa noma olunye. Izinhlelo zokuhlukanisa ezivame kakhulu, i-LCC ne-DDC, ziyabala, nakuba zinezici ezithile ezilandelanayo nezihlukene (ikakhulukazi ku-DDC), ikakhulukazi ezingeni elibanzi nelivamile. Uhlelo lokuqala lweqiniso olunezinhlangothi kwaba ukuhlukaniswa kwekholoni ye-SR Ranganathan.[14] 

Izindlela noma ama-sys tems 
Izinhlobo zokuhlukanisa zikhomba ukuhlukaniswa ngezigaba ngokuya ngefomu noma izici noma izimfanelo zohlelo lokuhlukanisa noma izikimu. Indlela nesistimu inencazelo efanayo. Indlela noma izindlela noma uhlelo lusho izikimu zokuhlukanisa ezifana ne-Dewey Decimal Classification noma i-Universal Decimal Classification. Izinhlobo zokuhlukanisa zingokokuhlonza nokuqonda noma izinjongo zemfundo noma zocwaningo kuyilapho indlela yokuhlukanisa isho lezo zinhlelo zokuhlukanisa njenge-DDC, i-UDC. 

Amasistimu okuhlukanisa umhlaba wonke wesiNgisi 

I-Moys Classification Scheme njengoba isetshenziswa umtapo wezincwadi wezomthetho weNkantolo Ephakeme yase-Hong Kong 
Izinhlelo ezivame kakhulu emazweni akhuluma isiNgisi yilezi: 

I-Dewey Decimal Classification (DDC) 
Library of Congress Classification (LCC) 
Universal Decimal Classification (UDC) 
Ezinye izinhlelo zihlanganisa: 

I-Book Industry Standards and Communications (BISAC), isiye yathuthukiswa ekuqaleni kwencwadi yase-US. imitapo yolwazi.[15] 
I-Bliss bibliographic Classification esetshenziswa kweminye imitapo yolwazi yaseBrithani 
I-Colon classification (CC) 
I-Garside classification esetshenziswa emitapo yolwazi eminingi yase-University College London[16] 
I-Gladstone Library Classification, eklanywe ngu-WE Gladstone futhi yasetshenziswa kuphela eMtatsheni Wezincwadi wase-Gladstone[17] 
I-Harvard-Yenching Classification, uhlelo lokuhlukanisa isiNgisi lwezinsiza zolimi lwesiShayina 
Izindlela zokuhlukaniswa kwendawo yonke okungezona ezesiNgisi 
I-German Regensburger Verbundklassifikation (RVK) 
Uhlelo lokuhlukanisa izincwadi ngezigaba ze-Library yamaShayina' 
Izigaba ISikimu Semitapo Yolwazi YaseShayina 
I-Nippon Decimal Classification (NDC) I- 
Chinese Library Classification (CLC) I- 
Korean Decimal Classification (KDC) 
I-Russian Library-Bibliographical Classification (BBK) 
Uhlelo lokuhlukanisa umtapo wezincwadi wase-Swedish (SAB) 
Izinhlelo zokuhlukanisa umhlaba wonke ezincike ku-synthesis (amasistimu anezici) 
Ukuhlukaniswa ngezigaba kwe- 
bliss
I-Cutter Expansive Classification 
Universal Decimal Classification 
Izinhlelo ezintsha zokuhlukanisa zivame ukusebenzisa isimiso sokuhlanganisa (ukuhlanganisa amakhodi asuka ezinhlwini ezihlukene ukuze amele izimfanelo ezihlukene zomsebenzi) kakhulu, okushodayo ngokuqhathaniswa ku-LC noma ku-DDC. Ukuhlukaniswa ngezigaba 

komtapo 
wolwazi kuhlotshaniswa nekhathalogi (echazayo) ngaphansi kwerubhrikhi yokwenza ikhathalogi nokuhlukanisa, ngezinye izikhathi eqoqwe ndawonye njengamasevisi obuchwepheshe. Uchwepheshe womtapo wolwazi ozibandakanya nenqubo yokwenza ikhathalogi nokuhlukanisa izinto zomtapo wolwazi ubizwa ngokuthi ikhathalogi noma umsebenzi womtapo wolwazi. Amasistimu wokuhlukaniswa kwelabhulali angelinye lamathuluzi amabili asetshenziselwa ukwenza lula ukufinyelela kwesihloko. Enye iqukethe izilimi zokukhomba ngezinhlamvu zamagama njenge-Thesauri kanye nezinhlelo Zezihloko Zesihloko. 

Inqubo yokuhlukanisa umtapo wolwazi iwuhlobo lomsebenzi ojwayelekile wokuhlukanisa. Umsebenzi uqukethe izinyathelo ezimbili. Okokuqala, isihloko noma isihloko sendaba siyaqinisekiswa. Okulandelayo, inombolo yocingo (empeleni ikheli lencwadi) esekelwe ohlelweni lokuhlukanisa olusetshenziswa kumtapo wolwazi othile izonikezwa umsebenzi kusetshenziswa ukuphawula kwesistimu. 

Ngokungafani nesihloko sesihloko noma i-thesauri lapho amatemu amaningi angabelwa umsebenzi ofanayo, ezinhlelweni zokuhlukaniswa kwelabhulali, umsebenzi ngamunye ungabekwa ekilasini elilodwa kuphela. Lokhu kungenxa yezinjongo zokubeka amashelufu: Incwadi ingaba nendawo eyodwa kuphela ebonakalayo. Nokho, kumakhathalogi ahlukanisiwe umuntu angase abe nokufakiwe okuyinhloko kanye nokufakiwe okungeziwe. Amasistimu amaningi okuhlukanisa afana ne-Dewey Decimal Classification (DDC) kanye ne-Library of Congress Classification nazo zengeza inombolo yokusika emsebenzini ngamunye enezela ikhodi yokungena okuyinhloko (indawo yokufinyelela eyinhloko) yomsebenzi (isb umbhali). 

Amasistimu wokuhlukanisa emitapo yolwazi ngokuvamile adlala izindima ezimbili. Okokuqala, zenza kube lula ukufinyelela esihlokweni ngokuvumela umsebenzisi ukuthi athole ukuthi yini esebenzayo noma imibhalo umtapo wolwazi enawo ngesihloko esithile.[18] Okwesibili, bahlinzeka ngendawo eyaziwayo ukuze kutholakale umthombo wolwazi (isb. lapho ubekwe khona). 
Amanye amasistimu okuhlukanisa afaneleka kakhulu ekusizeni ukufinyelela esifundweni, esikhundleni sendawo yeshalofu. Isibonelo, I-Universal Decimal Classification, esebenzisa ukuphawula okuyinkimbinkimbi kwama-pluses namakholoni, kunzima kakhulu ukuyisebenzisela injongo yokuhlelwa kweshalofu kodwa kucace kakhulu uma kuqhathaniswa ne-DDC mayelana nokubonisa ubudlelwano phakathi kwezifundo. Izikimu zokuhlukanisa ezinohlangothi olufanayo zinzima kakhulu ukuzisebenzisa ekuhlelweni kweshalofu, ngaphandle uma umsebenzisi enolwazi lomyalelo wokucaphuna.

Kuze kube ngekhulu le-19, imitapo yolwazi eminingi yayivalile izitaki, ngakho-ke ukuhlukaniswa kwelabhulali kwasebenzela ukuhlela ikhathalogi yezihloko kuphela. Ngekhulu lama-20, imitapo yolwazi yavula izitaki zayo emphakathini futhi yaqala ukubeka emashalofini impahla yomtapo wolwazi ngokwawo ngokwezigaba ezithile zomtapo wolwazi ukuze kube lula ukuphequlula izifundo. 


Ngokuya ngosayizi weqoqo lelabhulali, amanye amalabhulali angase asebenzise amasistimu okuhlukanisa ngenjongo eyodwa noma enye kuphela. Ezimweni ezimbi kakhulu, umtapo wolwazi womphakathi oneqoqo elincane ungase usebenzise isistimu yokuhlukanisa indawo yezinsiza kodwa ungase ungasebenzisi isistimu yokuhlukanisa izifundo eyinkimbinkimbi. Kunalokho zonke izinsiza zingase zibekwe ezigabeni ezimbalwa ezibanzi (ukuvakasha, ubugebengu, omagazini njll.). Lokhu kwaziwa ngokuthi "uphawu nepaki" indlela yokuhlukanisa, ebizwa ngokusemthethweni ngokuthi "ukuhlelwa kwentshisekelo yomfundi".[19] 

Ukuqhathanisa izinhlelo zokuhlukanisa umtapo wolwazi 
Ngenxa yomehluko ekubhaleni, emlandweni, ekusetshenzisweni kokubala, ukulandelana kwezigaba, kanye nezici, izinhlelo zokuhlukanisa zingahluka ngalezi zindlela ezilandelayo: 

Uhlobo Lokuphawula: I-Notation ingaba msulwa (ihlanganisa izinombolo kuphela, isibonelo) noma ixutshwe (okuhlanganisa izinhlamvu nezinombolo, noma izinhlamvu, izinombolo, nezinye izimpawu). 
Ukugqama: Leli izinga lapho umbhalo ungaveza khona ubudlelwano phakathi kwemiqondo noma isakhiwo. 
Ukuthi bayayisekela yini i-mnemonics: Isibonelo, inombolo engu-44 kumbhalo we-DDC ngokuvamile isho ukuthi iphathelene nengxenye ethile ye-France. Isibonelo, kusigaba sika-Dewey esithi 598.0944 sithinta "Izinyoni eFrance", u-09 ubonisa ukuhlukaniswa kwendawo, kanti u-44 umele i-France. 
I-Hospitality: Izinga uhlelo olukwazi ngalo ukwamukela izifundo ezintsha. 
I-Brevity: Ubude benothi ukuveza umqondo ofanayo. 
Isivinini sezibuyekezo nezinga losekelo: Amasistimu wokuhlukanisa angcono avame ukubuyekezwa. 
Ukuvumelana 
Kokusebenziseka 
Kokulula 


Lesi sihloko simayelana nohlobo lokuqukethwe kwemidiya. Ukuze uthole okunye ukusetshenziswa, bheka Inganekwane (disambiguation). 
"Inganekwane" iqondisa kabusha lapha. Ngebhendi yesiJalimane, bona Inganekwane (ibhendi). 

Umfanekiso ovela kunoveli ka-Lewis Carroll ka-1865 ethi Alice's Adventures in Wonderland 

Lesi sihloko sidinga izingcaphuno ezengeziwe ukuze siqinisekiswe. Sicela usize ukuthuthukisa lesi sihloko ngokwengeza izingcaphuno emithonjeni ethembekile. Izinto ezingatholakali zingaphikiswa futhi zisuswe. 
Thola imithombo: "Inganekwane" - izindaba · amaphephandaba · izincwadi · isazi · JSTOR (August 2025) (Funda ukuthi ungawususa kanjani futhi nini lo mlayezo) 
Inganekwane inoma yimuphi umsebenzi wobuciko, ikakhulukazi noma yimuphi umsebenzi olandisayo, obonisa abantu, izehlakalo, noma izindawo ezicatshangelwayo noma ngezindlela ezicatshangwayo.[1][2][3] Ngakho-ke izithombe eziqanjiwe azihambisani neqiniso, umlando, noma ukukholeka. Ngomqondo wendabuko owumngcingo, inganekwane ibhekisela ekulandiseni okulotshiwe kwephrozi - ngokuvamile ikakhulukazi amanoveli, amanoveli, nezindaba ezimfushane.[4][5] Nokho, ngobubanzi, inganekwane ihlanganisa ukulandisa okucatshangwayo okuvezwa kunoma iyiphi indlela, okuhlanganisa hhayi nje imibhalo kodwa futhi nemidlalo yaseshashalazini ephilayo, amafilimu, izinhlelo zethelevishini, amadrama omsakazo, amahlaya, imidlalo yokulingisa, nemidlalo yevidiyo.
