 Literature portal 
vUmbhaloUmbhaloUmbhalo
Ngokuvamile, into eqanjiwe yomsebenzi ivezwa esidlangalaleni, ngakho izethameli zilindele ukuthi umsebenzi wenganekwane uchezukele ngezinga elikhulu noma elincane emhlabeni wangempela, kunokuba wethule ngokwesibonelo kuphela ukuvezwa okuyiqiniso okuyiqiniso noma abalingisi abangabantu bangempela.[6] Ngenxa yokuthi inganekwane ngokuvamile iqondwa njengenganamatheli emhlabeni wangempela, izingqikithi nomongo wencwadi eqanjiwe, njengokuthi uma futhi ihlobana kanjani nezindaba zomhlaba wangempela noma izehlakalo, zivulekele ukuchazwa.[7] Njengoba inganekwane inesikhathi eside yasungulwa emkhakheni wezincwadi (inganekwane elandisayo ebhaliwe), ukucwaninga okubanzi kwemvelo, umsebenzi, kanye nencazelo yenganekwane kubizwa ngokuthi ithiyori yemibhalo, futhi incazelo ewumngcingo yemibhalo ethile eqanjiwe ibizwa ngokuthi ukugxeka okubhaliwe (okunamagatshana afana nokugxeka ifilimu nokugxekwa kwetiyetha nakho manje osekunesikhathi eside kwasungulwa). Ngaphandle kokuxhumana komhlaba wangempela, eminye imisebenzi eqanjiwe ingase ibonise abalingisi nezehlakalo ngaphakathi komongo wazo, ezihluke ngokuphelele kumkhathi obonakalayo owaziwayo: indawo yonke yenganekwane ezimele. Ubuciko bokudala bokwakha umhlaba onjalo ocatshangelwayo baziwa ngokuthi wukwakha umhlaba. 

Umgxeki wezincwadi uJames Wood uthi "inganekwane iwubuciko kanye neqiniso", okusho ukuthi idinga kokubili okuqanjiwe okuqanjiwe kanye nezinga elithile elamukelekayo lokukholeka ezithamelini zayo,[8] umbono ovame ukufakwa emqondweni wembongi uSamuel Taylor Coleridge wokumisa ngokuzithandela kwezilaleli ukungakholwa. Imithelela yokubhekana nenganekwane, kanye nendlela izethameli ezishintshwa ngayo ulwazi olusha abalutholayo, sekungamakhulu eminyaka kuhlolisiswa. Futhi, amathuba angapheli enganekwane ngokwawo abonisa ukungenzeki kokwazi ngokugcwele okungokoqobo, okubonisa ngokucasulayo imibono yefilosofi, njengokuthi kungase kube khona umbandela wokulinganisa ukwakheka kwezinto ezingokoqobo.[9] 

Inganekwane nengokoqobo 
Inganekwane 
uma iqhathaniswa nenganekwane Ngokuphambene nenganekwane, abadali bezinganekwane bathwala isibopho sokwethula ulwazi (futhi ngezinye izikhathi imibono) olusekelwe eqinisweni elingokomlando neliyiqiniso. Naphezu kombono wendabuko wokuthi izinganekwane nezingezona eziyiqiniso ziphambene, eminye imisebenzi (ikakhulukazi esikhathini samanje) iwufiphalisa lo mngcele, ikakhulukazi imisebenzi ewela ngaphansi kwezinhlobo ezithile zokuxoxa zezindaba—kuhlanganise nenganekwane yangemva kwesimanje, indaba eqanjiwe,[10] noma inganekwane eqanjiwe njengamanoveli angelona iqiniso nama-docudramas—kanye nokuqamba amanga okuqamba amanga nokuqamba amanga okungelona iqiniso.[11]
 
Ngaphezu kwalokho, ngisho nezincwadi eziningi zezinganekwane ngokuvamile zinezakhi, noma ezisekelwe kuyo, iqiniso lohlobo oluthile, noma iqiniso ngokombono othile. Umehluko phakathi kwalokhu okubili ungase uchazwe kangcono ngokombono wezithameli, kuye ngokuthi umsebenzi ongeyona inganekwane uma abantu bawo, izilungiselelo, nesakhiwo sabo kuthathwa njengokungokoqobo ngokomlando noma okuyiqiniso, kuyilapho umsebenzi uthathwa njengenganekwane uma uchezuka ekubeni ngokoqobo kunoma iyiphi yalezo zindawo. Umehluko uqhubeka ufihlwa ukuqonda kwefilosofi, ngakolunye uhlangothi, ukuthi iqiniso lingethulwa ngemigudu ecatshangelwayo nezakhiwo, kuyilapho, ngakolunye uhlangothi, imisebenzi yomcabango futhi ingaletha imibono emisha ebalulekile, noma iziphetho mayelana, iqiniso kanye neqiniso. 

Zonke izinhlobo zezinganekwane zimema izithameli zazo ukuthi zihlole imibono yangempela, izingqinamba, noma okungenzeka kusetshenziswa indawo ecatshangwayo noma ukusebenzisa okuthile okufana neqiniso, nakuba kusahlukile kukho.[inothi 1][inothi 2] 

Inganekwane eqagelayo iqhathaniswa namaqiniso 
Uhlobo lwesambulela senganekwane eqagelayo lubonakala ngezinga elincane lokunamathela kubantu abangokoqobo noma abakholekayo, izehlakalo, noma indawo ewumlingiswa omkhulu, kuyilapho uhlobo olungokoqobo luwuhlobo oluthile. Ngokwesibonelo, inganekwane eqagelayo ingase ibonise indawo yonke ecatshangelwayo ngokuphelele noma leyo lapho imithetho yemvelo ingasebenzi khona ngokuqinile (ngokuvamile, uhlobo oluncane lwenganekwane). Noma, libonisa izikhathi zomlando zangempela, ngaphandle kokuthi ziphethe ngendlela ecatshangwe ngokuphelele noma zilandelwe izehlakalo ezinkulu ezintsha ezicatshangwayo ngokuphelele (uhlobo lomlando ohlukile). Noma, libonisa ubuchwepheshe obungenakwenzeka noma ubuchwepheshe obuphikisana nokuqondwa kwesayensi kwamanje noma amakhono (uhlobo lwenganekwane yesayensi). 

Ngokuphambene, inganekwane engokoqobo ihilela indaba lapho isilungiselelo sayo esiyisisekelo (isikhathi nendawo emhlabeni) singokoqobo futhi izehlakalo zazo zingenzeka ngokukholekayo kumongo womhlaba wangempela. Uhlu olulodwa oluncane lwenganekwane engokoqobo iyinganekwane yomlando, egxile ezenzakalweni zangempela ezinkulu kanye nezikhathi zesikhathi esedlule.[14] Umzamo wokwenza izindaba zizizwe zithembekile eqinisweni noma ukuchaza imininingwane ngokunembayo, kanye nomnyakazo wobuciko wangekhulunyaka le-19 owaqala ukukhuthaza ngamandla le ndlela, ubizwa ngokuthi i-literary realism, ehlanganisa imisebenzi ethile yakho kokubili inganekwane kanye nenganekwane. 

Umlando 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Umlando wezincwadi
Ukuxoxa izindaba kube khona kuwo wonke amasiko abantu, futhi isiko ngalinye lihlanganisa izici ezahlukene zeqiniso nenganekwane ekuxoxeni izindaba. Izinganekwane zakuqala zazihlotshaniswa eduze nomlando nenganekwane. Izimbongi zamaGreki ezinjengoHomer, uHesiod, no-Aesop zakha izindaba eziqanjiwe ezazixoxwa kuqala ngokuxoxwa kwezindaba ngomlomo bese zibhalwa phansi. Inganekwane yephrozi yathuthukiswa eGreece Yasendulo, yathonywa amasiko okuxoxa izindaba ase-Asia naseGibhithe. Umsebenzi oqanjiwe ocacile awuzange ubonwe njengehlukile ezindabeni zomlando noma zezinganekwane kuze kube yinkathi yombuso. Ukulandisa kwePlasmatic, okulandela abalingiswa nezenzakalo eziqanjwe ngokuphelele, kwathuthukiswa ngedrama yasendulo kanye namahlaya amasha.[15] Isakhiwo esisodwa esivamile phakathi kwezinganekwane zakuqala uchungechunge lwezigigaba eziyinqaba nezimangalisayo njengoba ababhali bokuqala behlola imikhawulo yokubhala izinganekwane. Izinganekwane zaseMilesi zaziyisibonelo sokuqala sokubhalwa kwezinganekwane eGreece Yasendulo nase-Italy. Njengoba ukubhalwa kwezinganekwane kuthuthukiswa eGreece Yasendulo, abalingiswa abahlobene nezimo ezizwakalayo zagcizelelwa ukuze kuxhunyanwe kangcono nezithameli, okuhlanganisa izici ezifana nezothando, ubugebengu bobugebengu, kanye nemikhosi yezenkolo. Ezothando zobuqhawe zathuthukiswa eYurophu yasendulo, ehlanganisa izici ezihlobene nenganekwane, okuhlanganisa izici ezingaphezu kwemvelo nobungane.[16] 

Isakhiwo senoveli yesimanje sathuthukiswa nguMiguel de Cervantes noDon Quixote ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-17. [17] Le noveli yaba umkhakha oyinhloko wezinganekwane ngekhulu le-18 nele-19. Babevame ukuhlotshaniswa nemibono Yokukhanyiselwa njenge-empiricism kanye ne-agnosticism. Amaqiniso athuthukile njengesitayela sokubhala ngalesi sikhathi.[18] Izinhlobo ezintsha zemithombo yezindaba zathuthukiswa ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19 nasekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, okuhlanganisa omagazini bezinganekwane ezidumile kanye nefilimu yokuqala.[19] Izinganekwane ezisebenzisanayo zathuthukiswa ngasekupheleni kwekhulu lama-20 ngemidlalo yevidiyo.[20] 

Izici 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Ukulandisa § Izakhi eziyisisekelo 
Izakhi ezithile eziyisisekelo zichaza yonke imisebenzi yokulandisa, okuhlanganisa yonke imisebenzi yenganekwane elandisayo. Okungukuthi, zonke izindaba ezixoxwayo zihlanganisa izici zomlingiswa, udweshu, imodi yokulandisa, isakhiwo, isizinda, nendikimba. Abalingiswa ngabantu abangaphakathi endabeni, ukungqubuzana kuwukushuba kwesimo noma inkinga eqhuba imicabango nezenzo zabalingisi, izindlela zokulandisa izindlela indaba exoxwa ngayo, iziqephu ziwukulandelana kwezenzakalo endabeni, izilungiselelo ziyizindawo zendaba ngesikhathi nesikhala, futhi izindikimba ziyimiyalezo ejulile noma izincazelo ezimayelana nendaba izethameli zayo okusala zixoxe ngazo futhi zizindle ngayo. 

Amafomethi 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Uhlu lwezinhlobo eziqanjiwe 

Ingxenye yesitolo sezincwadi
Ngokwesiko, izinganekwane zibandakanya amanoveli, izindaba ezimfishane, izinganekwane, izinganekwane, izinganekwane, izinganekwane, izinkondlo eziwumlando nezilandisayo, imidlalo (okuhlanganisa ama-opera, umculo, amadrama, imidlalo yopopayi, nezinhlobo ezehlukene zemidanso yaseshashalazini). Kodwa-ke, inganekwane ingase futhi ihlanganise izincwadi zamahlaya, kanye namakhathuni amaningi apopayi, ama-stop movements, i-anime, manga, amafilimu, imidlalo yevidiyo, izinhlelo zomsakazo, izinhlelo zethelevishini (amahlaya namadrama), njll. 

I-inthanethi ibe nomthelela omkhulu ekwakhiweni nasekusabalaliseni kwezinganekwane, ibeka kungabaza ukuba nokwenzeka kwe-copyright njengendlela yokuqinisekisa ukuthi izimali zikhokhwa kubanikazi be-copyright.[21] Futhi, imitapo yolwazi yedijithali efana ne-Project Gutenberg yenza imibhalo yesizinda somphakathi itholakale kalula. Inhlanganisela yamakhompiyutha asekhaya angabizi, i-inthanethi, nekhono lokusungula labasebenzisi bayo nakho kuye kwaholela ezinhlotsheni ezintsha zezinganekwane, njengemidlalo yekhompiyutha esebenzisanayo noma amahlaya akhiqizwe ngekhompiyutha. Izinkundla ezingenakubalwa zezinganekwane zabalandeli zingatholakala ku-inthanethi, lapho abalandeli abathembekile bezindawo eziqanjiwe ezithile bakha futhi basabalalisa izindaba eziphuma kokunye. I-inthanethi iphinde isetshenziselwe ukuthuthukiswa kwenganekwane yebhulogi, lapho indaba ilethwa ngebhulogi njengenganekwane ye-flash noma ibhulogi ye-serial, kanye nenganekwane ehlanganyelwayo, lapho indaba ibhalwa ngokulandelana ngababhali abahlukahlukene, noma wonke umbhalo ungabuyekezwa yinoma ubani osebenzisa i-wiki. 

Ukubhala izinganekwane  
Inganekwane yemibhalo 
Isihloko esikhulu: Inganekwane yombhalo
Incazelo yenganekwane yombhalo iyimpikiswano. Ingase ibhekisele kunoma yimuphi umsebenzi wenganekwane obhalwe ngendlela ebhaliwe. Nokho, ezinye izincazelo ezihlukahlukene zikhona, okuhlanganisa umsebenzi obhaliwe wenganekwane othi: 

awungeni kahle ohlotsheni olumisiwe (ngokuphambene nalokho okubizwa ngokuthi inganekwane yohlobo), lapho isetshenziswa njengelebula yokumaketha ekuhwebeni kwencwadi 
iqhutshwa ngabalingiswa kunokuba iqhutshwe ngesakhiwo 
ihlola isimo somuntu 
sisebenzisa ulimi ngendlela yokuhlola noma yezinkondlo 
ibhekwa njengento engathi sína njengomsebenzi wobuciko[22] 
umqondo womqondo ofanayo wombhalo osetshenziswa njenge-Litera. imibhalo ebhekwa ngokukhethekile njengohlobo lobuciko.[23] Yize izinganekwane zombhalo kwesinye isikhathi zithathwa njengeziphakeme kunezinganekwane zohlobo, zombili azihlukani, futhi izibalo ezinkulu zemibhalo zisebenzise izinhlobo zezinganekwane zesayensi, izinganekwane zobugebengu, ezothando, njll., ukwenza izincwadi. Ngaphezu kwalokho, ucwaningo lwezinhlobo zezinganekwane luthuthuke phakathi kwezemfundo emashumini eminyaka amuva nje.[24]

Leli gama ngezinye izikhathi lisetshenziswa njengokulinganisa inganekwane yemibhalo nemibhalo. Ukunemba kwalokhu kuyaphikiswana ngakho. U-Neal Stephenson uphakamise ukuthi, nakuba noma iyiphi incazelo izoba lula, namuhla kunomehluko ovamile wamasiko phakathi kwezinganekwane zombhalo kanye nohlobo. Ngakolunye uhlangothi ababhali bezincwadi kulezi zinsuku bavame ukusekelwa ngokusekelwa, ngokuqashwa enyuvesi noma esikhungweni esifanayo, futhi nokuqhubeka kwezikhundla ezinjalo ezinganqunywa ngokudayiswa kwezincwadi kodwa ngokutuswa okugxeka abanye ababhali bezincwadi abaziwayo nabagxeki. Ngakolunye uhlangothi, uphakamisa ukuthi, ababhali bezinganekwane zohlobo bavame ukuzisekela ngokuthengisa izincwadi.[25] Nokho, engxoxweni, uJohn Updike wakhala ngokuthi "umkhakha 'wezinganekwane zombhalo' usuqhamuke muva nje ukuze uhlukumeze abantu abafana nami abasanda kuqalisa ukubhala izincwadi, futhi uma noma ubani efuna ukuzifunda, kubi kakhulu, kuyanda kakhulu. ... Ngingumbhali wohlobo oluthile. Ngibhala inganekwane yombhalo, efana nenganekwane [2] noma i-chick6]". Ngokunjalo naku-The Charlie Rose Show, waveza ukuthi leli gama, uma lisetshenziswa emsebenzini wakhe, linciphisa kakhulu yena kanye nokulindela kwakhe okungase kufike ekubhaleni kwakhe, ngakho akakuthandi ngempela. Wasikisela ukuthi yonke imisebenzi yakhe ingeyemibhalo, ngenxa nje yokuthi “ibhalwe ngamagama”.[27] 

Izinganekwane zombhalo zivame ukubandakanya ukuphawula komphakathi, ukugxeka kwezombusazwe, noma ukucabanga ngesimo somuntu.[28] Ngokuvamile, igxile "ekucwaningweni kwabalingisi okujulile, okujulile" kwezinhlamvu "ezithakazelisayo, eziyinkimbinkimbi futhi ezithuthukisiwe". [28] Lokhu kuphambene nenganekwane yohlobo lapho indaba ibaluleke kakhulu.[29] Ngokuvamile ezinganekwaneni zombhalo kugxilwa "endabeni yangaphakathi" yabalingiswa abashayela isiqephu, benezisusa ezinemininingwane zokuvusela "ukubandakanyeka ngokomzwelo" kumfundi.[ecashunwa] Isitayela senganekwane yombhalo sivame ukuchazwa ngokuthi "ibhalwe ngobunyoninco, iphimbo lomculo, kanye ... neleya".[30] Ithoni yenganekwane yombhalo ingaba mnyama kunezinganekwane zohlobo,[31] kuyilapho ukuhamba kwenganekwane yombhalo kungase kube kancane kunenganekwane edumile.[31] Njengoba uTerrence Rafferty ephawula, "inganekwane yombhalo, ngokwemvelo yayo, izivumela ukuba ikhanye, ihlale kobuhle abaduka ngisho nasengozini yokulahlekelwa indlela yayo".[32] 

Indaba eqanjiwe yohlobo 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Inganekwane yohlobo 
Ngokusekelwe endleleni inganekwane echazwa ngayo, inganekwane yohlobo ingase ibe isethi encane (inganekwane ebhaliwe eqondana nohlobo oluthile), noma okuphambene nayo: ilebula yokuhlola yenganekwane ebhaliwe ehlanganisa isiko elidumile, njengobuciko noma ngobuhlakani obungaphansi kwesiko eliphakeme. Kungakhathaliseki ukuthi, izinganekwane zivame ukuhlukaniswa zibe izinhlobo ezihlukahlukene: izigaba zezinganekwane, ngasinye sihlukaniswa ithoni ethile ehlanganisayo noma isitayela; iqoqo lamasu okulandisa, ama-archetypes, noma amanye ama-tropes; okuqukethwe kwemidiya; noma omunye umbandela ochazwe ngokudumile.
 
Inganekwane yesayensi ibikezela noma icabanga ubuchwepheshe obungewona amaqiniso ngesikhathi sokudalwa komsebenzi: Inoveli kaJules Verne ethi From the Earth to the Moon yanyatheliswa ngo-1865, kodwa ngo-1969 kuphela lapho osomkhathi uNeil Armstrong noBuzz Aldrin baba abantu bokuqala ukufika eNyangeni. 

Inganekwane yomlando ibeka abalingiswa abacatshangelwayo ezenzakalweni zangempela zomlando. Encwadini yomlando ka-1814 ethi Waverley, umlingiswa oqanjiwe kaSir Walter Scott u-Edward Waverley uhlangana nomuntu ovela emlandweni, uBonnie Prince Charlie, futhi ubamba iqhaza eMpini yasePrestonpans. Eminye imisebenzi yezinganekwane icatshangwa kabusha kancane noma kakhulu ngokusekelwe endabeni ethile eyiqiniso kwasekuqaleni, noma i-biography eyakhiwe kabusha.[33] Ngokuvamile, ngisho nalapho indaba eqanjiwe isekelwe eqinisweni, kungase kube nokunezelwa nokukhipha endabeni yeqiniso ukuze ithakazelise. Isibonelo sika-Tim O'Brien sika-The Things They Carried, uchungechunge lwezindaba ezimfushane zango-1990 ngeMpi YaseVietnam. 


Isithombe sika-Harry Potter e-Leicester Square, e-London 
Fictional imisebenzi ehlanganisa ngokusobala izinto ezingaphezu kwemvelo, imilingo, noma izinto ezingenakwenzeka ngokwesayensi ngokuvamile zihlukaniswa ngaphansi kohlobo lwenganekwane, okuhlanganisa inoveli ka-Lewis Carroll ka-1865 ethi Alice's Adventures in Wonderland, ka-JRR Tolkien ethi The Lord of the Rings, nochungechunge luka-JK Harry Pottering.Abadali bemicabango ngezinye izikhathi bethula izidalwa ezicatshangelwayo kanye nezidalwa ezinjengamadragoni nama-fairies.[3]

Izinhlobo ngokubala kwamagama 
Izinhlobo zezinganekwane ezibhaliwe kuphrozi zihlukaniswa ngobude obuhlobene futhi zihlanganisa:[34][35] 

Indaba emfushane: umngcele phakathi kwendaba emfushane ende nenoveli awucacile,[36] nakuba indaba emfushane ngokuvamile iqukethe amagama angaphansi kuka-7,500 
i-Novela: ngokuvamile, amagama ayi-17,500 kuya kwangu-40,000 ubude ngobude; izibonelo zihlanganisa I-Strange Case ka-Robert Louis Stevenson sikaDkt Jekyll kanye noMnu Hyde (1886) noma Inhliziyo Yobumnyama kaJoseph Conrad (1899)[37] 
Inoveli: Amagama angu-40,000 noma ngaphezulu ngobude 
Inqubo yokubhala inganekwane 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukubhalwa kwenganekwane 
Ukubhala okuqanjiwe kuyinqubo umbhali noma umdali akhiqiza ngayo umsebenzi oqanjiwe. Ezinye izici zenqubo yokubhala zingahle zihlelwe kusenesikhathi, kanti ezinye zingazenzakalela. Ababhali bezinganekwane basebenzisa izitayela zokubhala ezihlukene futhi banamaphimbo ababhali abahlukene lapho bebhala izindaba eziqanjiwe.[38] 

Ukuqanjwa okuqanjiwe njengomqondo
 
Efilimini ehlekisayo yango-1940 ethi The Great Dictator, umlingisi oyiNgisi kanye nosomahlaya uCharlie Chaplin waveza i-Eccentric despot u-Adenoid Hynkel, okwakusobala kubabukeli ngaleso sikhathi njengenguqulo eqanjiwe ka-Adolf Hitler kanye nezenzakalo zangempela ezenzeka phakathi neMpi Yezwe Yesibili. 
Ukusetshenziswa kwezehlakalo zangempela noma abantu bangempela njengogqozi oluqondile lwezehlakalo ezicatshangelwayo noma abantu abacatshangelwayo kwaziwa njengokuqanjiwe. Isimo esiphambene, lapho umhlaba wenyama noma ukuphenduka kwangempela kwezehlakalo kubonakala kuthonywa inganekwane edlule, ngokuvamile kuchazwa inkulumo ethi "ubuciko bokulingisa impilo". Umusho wakamuva uwukuduma okuhlotshaniswa nomlobi wezinganekwane wase-Anglo-Irish u-Oscar Wilde.[39]

Ukuguqulwa kwezehlakalo zangempela zibe ifomethi eqanjiwe, lokhu okuhilela ukumelwa okumangalisayo kwezehlakalo zangempela noma abantu, kwaziwa njengokuyikho kokubili okuqanjiwe, noma, kancane kancane ekusebenzeni okubonakalayo kusebenza njengasetiyetha nasefilimini, ekulingiseni. Ngokwencwadi yezemfundo i-Oxford Reference, umsebenzi osungulwe ngale ndlela uzoba "nendatshana esekelwe ngokwengxenye noma ngokuphelele eqinisweni kodwa ebhalwe njengokungathi inganekwane" kangangokuthi "[f] amadrama namadrama asakazwayo alolu hlobo ngokuvamile anelebula 'esekelwe endabeni yeqiniso'." Ocwaningweni lobuhlakani, ukuhlola le nqubo kuyingxenye yezifundo zemidiya.[40] 

Izibonelo zezinganekwane ezivelele kwezobuciko bokudala zihlanganisa lezo ezisemongweni ojwayelekile weMpi Yezwe II ngesiko elidumile futhi ikakhulukazi abaholi baseJalimane abangamaNazi abafana no-Adolf Hitler ngesiko elidumile kanye no-Reinhard Heydrich esikweni elidumile. Isibonelo, umlingisi waseMelika kanye nosomahlaya uCharlie Chaplin uveze i-eccentric despot u-Adenoid Hynkel efilimini ehlekisayo yango-1940 ethi The Great Dictator. Umuntu ongaguquki, ongahlakaniphile waqamba izehlakalo zangempela ezivela eMpini Yezwe Yesibili eyayiqhubeka ngaleso sikhathi ngendlela eyethula abantu abangama-fascist njengabangenangqondo ngokuhlekisayo nabadabukisayo. Ezinye izigilamkhuba eziningi zithatha ugqozi oluqondile kubantu bangempela kuyilapho zinezinkulumo eziqanjiwe, ukubonakala, isizinda, amagama, nokunye.


Okungelona iqiniso (noma okungelona iqiniso) yinoma yimuphi umbhalo noma okuqukethwe kwemidiya okuzama, ngokwethembeka, ukudlulisa ulwazi mayelana nomhlaba wangempela kuphela, kunokuba kusekelwe emcabangweni.[1] Okungezona izinganekwane ngokuvamile kuhloswe ukwethula izihloko ngokususelwe olwazini lomlando, lwesayensi, nololwazi. Nokho, ezinye izinto ezingezona izinganekwane zifinyelela endaweni evumayo, okuhlanganisa nemibono eqotho ngezihloko zomhlaba wangempela.[2] 

Ngokuvamile kubhekiselwa ekubhalweni kwe-prose,[3] okungelona iqiniso kungenye yezindlela ezimbili ezibalulekile endabeni nokuxoxa indaba, ngokungafani nenganekwane elandisayo, egcwele abalingiswa abacatshangelwayo nezehlakalo.[1][4] Ababhali abangezona izinganekwane bangabonisa izizathu nemiphumela yezenzakalo, bangaqhathanisa, baqhathanise, bahlukanise, bahlukanise ngezigaba futhi bafingqe ulwazi, babeke amaqiniso ngokulandelana okunengqondo noma ngokulandelana kwezenzakalo, banqume futhi bafinyelele iziphetho mayelana namaqiniso, njll.[5] Bangasebenzisa izici zokubukeka okuyingcaca, kwesakhiwo nokuphrintiwe njengezithombe, amagrafu noma amashadi, imidwebo, amashadi agelezayo, izifinyezo, uhlu lwamagama, amabha aseceleni, imigqa yesikhathi, uhlu lokuqukethwe, izihloko, izihlokwana, amagama agqamile noma abhalwe ngomakhekeke, imibhalo yaphansi, amamephu, izinkomba, amalebula, amagama-ncazo, njll. ukuze basize abafundi bathole ulwazi.[5] 

Nakuba izimangalo ezithile emsebenzini ongaqanjiwe zingase zinganembile, umbhali oqotho uhlose ukuba neqiniso ngesikhathi sokubhala. I-akhawunti okungeyona eyiqiniso iwumsebenzi wokumela isihloko ngokunembile, futhi ihlala ihlukile kunoma yikuphi ukuvumela okushiwo. 

Umehluko
Izindlela zokulandisa eziningi ezisetshenziswa ngaphakathi kwenganekwane ngokuvamile zicatshangwa ukuthi azifaneleki ukuthi zisetshenziswe ezindabeni ezingezona izinganekwane. Zisekhona ikakhulukazi emisebenzini emidala, kodwa zivame ukuthuliswa ukuze zingasibekele ulwazi olungaphakathi komsebenzi. Ubulula, ukucaca, kanye nokuqondile ngezinye zezinto ezicatshangelwayo ezibaluleke kakhulu lapho kukhiqizwa inganekwane. Izithameli zibalulekile kunoma yimuphi umzamo wobuciko noma ochazayo, kodwa mhlawumbe kubaluleke kakhulu kwezinganekwane. Enganekwaneni, umbhali ukholelwa ukuthi abafundi bazokwenza umzamo wokulandela futhi bahumushe ukuqhubeka kwendikimba okwethulwa ngokungaqondile noma ngokusobala, kuyilapho ukukhiqizwa kwenganekwane kuhlobene kakhulu nokuhlinzekwa kolwazi ngokuqondile. Ukuqonda indlela abafundi abangase basebenzise ngayo umsebenzi kanye nolwazi lwabo olukhona lwesihloko kokubili kuyisisekelo sezinganekwane eziphumelelayo. Naphezu kokufuna iqiniso lenganekwane, ngokuvamile kudingekile ukuthonya umfundi ukuba avumelane nemibono ngakho-ke impikiswano elinganiselayo, ehambisanayo, nenolwazi ibalulekile. Kodwa-ke, imingcele phakathi kwezinganekwane nezingezona eziyiqiniso ihlale ifiphazwa futhi kuphikiswana ngayo, ikakhulukazi emkhakheni we-biography;[6] njengoba uVirginia Woolf asho: "Uma sicabanga ngeqiniso njengento eqinile njengegwalagwala nobuntu njengento engabambeki njengothingo futhi sibonisa ukuthi inhloso ye-biography iwukuhlanganisa lezi zinto ezimbili zibe yinye inkinga, sizobe sivumelana nalokho okubalulekile. akumangazi ukuthi ababhali bomlando wokuphila komuntu, ngokwengxenye enkulu baye bahluleka yini ukukuxazulula.”[7] 

Ukufaka ukwaziswa umbhali azi ukuthi akulona iqiniso ngaphakathi kwezincwadi ezinjalo ngokuvamile kubhekwa njengokungathembeki. Noma kunjalo, izinhlobo ezithile zemibhalo ebhaliwe ngokusemthethweni zingaba indaba eqanjiwe noma engeyona eqanjiwe, njengamajenali okuzichaza wena, izincwadi, izihloko zomagazini, nezinye izinkulumo zokuzicabangela. Nakuba ngokuvamile kungenye noma enye, inhlanganisela yakho kokubili kungenzeka. Enye inganekwane ingase ihlanganise izici ezingezona izinganekwane; I-semi-fiction iyinganekwane esebenzisa eziningi zezinganekwane,[8] (njengencazelo eqanjiwe esekelwe endabeni yeqiniso). Enye inganekwane ingase ihlanganise izici zokucatshangelwa okungaqinisekisiwe, ukubanjwa, noma umcabango ngenjongo yokusheshisa indaba exoxwayo, kodwa ukufakwa kwamanga asobala kuzoyihlambalaza njengomsebenzi ongelona iqiniso. Amabhizinisi okushicilela nawokudayisa ngezinye izikhathi asebenzisa igama elithi "inganekwane yobuciko" ukuze ahlukanise imisebenzi enombhalo noma ubuhlakani, ngokuphambene nenqwaba yezihloko ezingezona izinganekwane. 

Umdwebo ubuciko obubonakalayo obusebenzisa insimbi ukumaka iphepha noma enye indawo enezinhlangothi ezimbili, noma ukumelwa kwedijithali kwalokho. Ngokwesiko, amathuluzi asetshenziswa ukwenza umdwebo ahlanganisa amapensela, amakhrayoni, namapeni ayinki, kwesinye isikhathi kuhlanganiswe. Amathuluzi esimanje engeziwe afaka ama-stylus ekhompuyutha anamathebulethi ezithombe namaphedi wegeyimu kusofthiwe yokudweba ye-VR.

Ithuluzi lokudweba lidedela inani elincane lezinto endaweni, lishiye uphawu olubonakalayo. Ukusekela okuvame kakhulu ukudweba iphepha, nakuba ezinye izinto ezinjengamakhadibhodi, i-vellum, ukhuni, ipulasitiki, isikhumba, indwangu, kanye nebhodi, ziye zasetshenziswa. Imidwebo yesikhashana ingenziwa ebhodini noma ebhodini elimhlophe. Ukudweba bekuyindlela ethandwayo neyisisekelo yokuvezwa komphakathi kuwo wonke umlando wesintu. Ingenye yezindlela ezilula neziphumelela kakhulu zokudlulisela imibono.[1] Ukutholakala okubanzi kwezinsimbi zokudweba kwenza ukudweba kube omunye wemisebenzi yobuciko evamile. 

Ngaphezu kwamafomu ayo obuciko obuningi, ukudweba kuvame ukusetshenziswa emifanekisweni yezentengiselwano, ukugqwayiza, izakhiwo, ubunjiniyela, kanye nemidwebo yobuchwepheshe. Umdwebo osheshayo, okhululekile, ngokuvamile ongahlosiwe njengomsebenzi oqediwe, ngezinye izikhathi ubizwa ngokuthi umdwebo. Umdwebi ozijwayeza noma osebenza ngomdwebo wobuchwepheshe angase abizwe ngokuthi umdwebi, umdwebi, noma umdwebi.[2] 

Uhlolojikelele 

Madame Palmyre with Her Dog, 1897. 
Umdwebo ka-Henri de Toulouse-Lautrec ungenye yezindlela ezindala kakhulu zokukhuluma komuntu ngaphakathi kobuciko obubonakalayo. Ngokuvamile kuphathelene nokumaka imigqa nezindawo zethoni ephepheni/ezinye izinto, lapho ukumelwa okunembile komhlaba okubukwayo kuvezwa endaweni yendiza.[3] Imidwebo yomdabu yayiyi-monochrome, noma okungenani inombala omncane,[4] kuyilapho imidwebo yesimanje yamapensela anombala ingase isondele noma yeqe umngcele phakathi komdwebo nokudweba. Ngamagama aseNtshonalanga, ukudweba kuhlukile ekupendweni, nakuba imidiya efanayo ivame ukusetshenziswa kuyo yomibili imisebenzi. Imidiya eyomile, evame ukuhlotshaniswa nomdwebo, njengoshoki, ingasetshenziswa emidwebeni ye-pastel. Umdwebo ungenziwa nge-liquid medium, efakwe ngamabhulashi noma amapeni. Ukusebenzisa ibhulashi ekudwebeni kusakazeke kakhulu futhi nansi inqubo yokusebenzisa imigqa nokuchanyuselwa, ebonisa okuthile njengomdwebo. Izisekelo ezifanayo zingasebenza kokubili: ukudweba ngokuvamile kuhilela ukufaka upende owuketshezi kumaseyili noma amaphaneli alungisiwe, kodwa ngezinye izikhathi dwetshwa umdwebo ongaphansi kuqala kulokho kusekelwa okufanayo. 

Ukudweba kuvame ukuhlolisisa, kugcizelelwa kakhulu ekuqapheliseni, ekuxazululeni izinkinga nasekuqambeni. Umdwebo ubuye usetshenziswe njalo ekulungiseleleni umdwebo, okwenza kube nzima ukuhlukana kwawo. Imidwebo eyenzelwe lezi zinhloso ibizwa ngokuthi imidwebo. 

Kunezigaba ezimbalwa zokudweba, okuhlanganisa: 

umdwebo womdwebo 
we-cartooning 
doodling 
sketch 
freehand. 
Kukhona futhi izindlela eziningi zokudweba, ezifana nalezi: 

umdwebo womugqa 
ugxilisa 
shading 
entopic graphomania (indlela ye-surrealist lapho amachashazi enziwa khona ezindaweni zokungcola ephepheni elingenalutho, bese kwenziwa imigqa phakathi kwamachashazi) 
(ukudweba ephepheni elishintshashintshayo, njengephepha lokulandela umkhondo, uzungeza uhlaka lwamajamo asevele akhona abonakala ephepheni). 
Emikhakheni engaphandle kobuciko, imidwebo yezobuchwepheshe noma amapulani ezakhiwo, imishini, ukujikeleza kanye nezinye izinto zivame ukubizwa ngokuthi "imidwebo" ngisho nalapho zidluliselwe kwenye indlela ngokuphrinta. 

Umlando 
Ekuxhumaneni 
Umdwebo ungenye yezindlela ezindala kakhulu zokukhuluma komuntu, ezinobufakazi bokuba khona kwayo ngaphambi kokuxhumana okubhaliwe.[5] Kukholakala ukuthi umdwebo wawusetshenziswa njengendlela ekhethekile yokuxhumana ngaphambi kokusungulwa kolimi olubhalwayo, [5][6] olwaboniswa ukukhiqizwa kwemidwebo yomhume namadwala cishe eminyakeni engu-30,000 edlule (Art of the Upper Paleolithic).[7] Le midwebo, eyaziwa ngokuthi ama-pictograms, izinto eziveziwe kanye nemiqondo engabonakali.[8] Imidwebo nemidwebo ekhiqizwa izikhathi ze-Neolithic yagcina yenziwe isitayela futhi yenziwa lula yaba izinhlelo zezimpawu (i-proto-writing) futhi ekugcineni yaba izinhlelo zokuqala zokubhala. 

Emibhalweni yesandla 
Ngaphambi kokutholakala kabanzi kwephepha eYurophu, izindela ezigodlweni zezindela zaseYurophu zazisebenzisa imidwebo, njengemidwebo engaphansi yemibhalo yesandla ekhanyisiwe ebhalwe nge-vellum noma esikhumbeni, noma njengomfanekiso wokugcina. Umdwebo ubuye wasetshenziswa kakhulu emkhakheni wesayensi, njengendlela yokuthola, ukuqonda kanye nencazelo. 

Kwezesayensi 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umfanekiso wezobuchwepheshe 

Galileo Galilei, Izigaba Zenyanga, 1609 noma 1610, uyinki onsundu kanye nokuwasha ephepheni. 208 × 142 mm. I-National Central Library (Florence), Gal. 48, ifl. 28r 
Ukudweba imidwebo yokubhekwa yingxenye ebalulekile yocwaningo lwesayensi. 

Ngo-1609, isazi sezinkanyezi uGalileo Galilei sachaza izigaba ezishintshayo zeVenus kanye nama-sunspots ngemidwebo yakhe ye-telescopic yokubuka.[9] Ngo-1924, isazi se-geophysicist u-Alfred Wegener wasebenzisa imifanekiso ukuze abonise imvelaphi yamazwekazi.[9] 

Njengenkulumo yobuciko 
Ukudweba kungenye yezindlela ezilula zokubona ngeso lengqondo imibono kanye nokuveza ubuhlakani bomuntu; ngakho-ke iye yagqama emhlabeni wezobuciko. Kuwo wonke umlando, ukudweba bekubhekwa njengesisekelo sokwenza umsebenzi wobuciko.[10] Ekuqaleni, abadwebi babesebenzisa futhi baphinde basebenzise izibhebhe zokhuni ukuze benze imidwebo yabo.[11] Ngemva kokutholakala kabanzi kwephepha ekhulwini le-14, ukusetshenziswa kokudweba kwezobuciko kwanda. Kuleli qophelo, ukudweba kwakuvame ukusetshenziswa njengethuluzi lokucabanga nokuphenya, kusebenza njengendawo yokufunda ngenkathi amaciko elungiselela izingcezu zawo zokugcina.[12][13] I-Renaissance yaletha ubunkimbinkimbi kumasu okudweba, okwenza amaciko akwazi ukumela izinto ngendlela engokoqobo kunangaphambili, [14] futhi eveza isithakazelo ku-geometry nefilosofi.[15]

Ukusungulwa kohlobo lokuqala olutholakala kabanzi lokuthwebula izithombe kwaholela ekushintsheni kwesigaba sezigaba zezobuciko.[16] Ukuthwebula kunikeze enye indlela yokudweba njengendlela yokumelela ngokunembile izenzakalo ezibukwayo, futhi umkhuba wokudweba wendabuko wagcizelelwa kancane njengekhono elibalulekile kumaciko, ikakhulukazi emphakathini waseNtshonalanga.[9] 

Amaciko aphawulekayo nabadwebi 
Umdwebo waba obalulekile njengendlela yobuciko ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-15, enabaculi nabaqophi abachwepheshile abafana no-Albrecht Dürer noMartin Schongauer (c. 1448–1491), umqophi wokuqala waseNyakatho owaziwa ngegama. USchongauer uvela e-Alsace, futhi wazalelwa emndenini wabakhandi begolide. U-Albrecht Dürer, umpetha wesizukulwane esilandelayo, naye wayeyindodana yomkhandi wegolide.[17][18] 

Imidwebo Emidala Eyingcweti ivamise ukukhombisa umlando wezwe eyakhiqizwa kulo, kanye nezici ezibalulekile zesizwe ngaleso sikhathi. EHolland ekhulwini le-17, izwe lamaProthestani, cishe yayingekho imisebenzi yobuciko yenkolo, futhi, ngaphandle kweNkosi noma inkantolo, ubuciko obuningi babuthengwa ngasese. Imidwebo yezindawo noma izigcawu zohlobo ngokuvamile yayingabhekwa njengemidwebo kodwa njengemisebenzi yobuciko eqedwe kakhulu. Imidwebo yaseNtaliyane, nokho, ikhombisa ithonya lobuKatolika neSonto, eladlala indima enkulu ekuxhaseni kwezobuciko. Okufanayo kuvame ukuba njalo ngemidwebo yesiFulentshi, nakuba ngekhulu le-17 iziyalo ze-French Classicism[19] zazisho ukuthi imidwebo yayingaphansi kwe-Baroque kunezakwabo zase-Italy ezikhululekile, ezazidlulisela umuzwa omkhulu wokunyakaza.[20] 

Ekhulwini lama-20 i-Modernism yakhuthaza "imvelaphi ecatshangwayo"[21] futhi indlela yamanye amaciko ekudwebeni ayizange ibe ngokoqobo, ingabonakali. Amaciko adume umhlaba wonke afana no-Pablo Picasso, u-Andy Warhol kanye noJean-Michel Basquiat basize inselelo yesimo esikhona, ngokudweba kube maphakathi kakhulu nomsebenzi wabo, futhi ngokuvamile kuvame ukutolika kabusha amasu omdabu.[22] 

Imidwebo ye-Basquiat yakhiqizwa ngezindlela eziningi ezahlukene, ngokuvamile eyinki, ipensela, ithiphu elizwakalayo noma umaka, kanye nenduku kawoyela, futhi wayedweba kunoma iyiphi indawo etholakalayo, njengeminyango, izingubo zokugqoka, iziqandisi, izindonga nezigqoko ze-baseball.[23] 

Amakhulu eminyaka akhiqize uhlu lwabadwebi abaphawulekayo nabadwebi, ngamunye enolimi lwakhe oluhlukile lokudweba, okuhlanganisa:
