Ngo-19th: Aubrey Beardsley • Paul Cézanne • Jacques-Louis David • Honoré Daumier • Edgar Degas • Théodore Géricault • Francisco Goya • Jean-Auguste-Dominique Ingres • Pierre-Paul Prud'hon • Odilon Redon • John Ruskin • Georges Seuratuse0 Henri Goyat Henri Goyat Henri Goyat
20th: Max Beckmann • Jean Dubuffet • MC Escher • Arshile Gorky • George Grosz • Paul Klee • Oskar Kokoschka • Käthe Kollwitz • Alfred Kubin • André Masson • Alphonse Mucha • Jules Pascin • Pablo Picasso • Egon Schiele • Jean-Michel Warsquiat is the 
Material • Jean-Michel 
Warhoat umbala, noma umbala ulethwa endaweni yomdwebo. Imidiya eminingi yokudweba ingaba yomile (isb. i-graphite, amalahle, i-pastel, i-Conté, i-silverpoint), noma isebenzisa isixazululi esiwuketshezi noma isithwali (umaka, ipeni noyinki). Amapensela e-Watercolor angasetshenziswa omile njengamapensela ajwayelekile, bese aswakanyiswa ngebhulashi elimanzi ukuze athole imiphumela ehlukahlukene yokupenda. Akuvamile ukuthi abaculi badwebe ngoyinki ongabonakali (ovamise ukukhishwa amakhodi). Umdwebo we-Metalpoint ngokuvamile usebenzisa isiliva noma umthofu.[25] Okungavamile ukusetshenziswa igolide, iplatinum, ithusi, ithusi, ithusi, ne-tinpoint. 

Iphepha liza ngobukhulu obuhlukahlukene kanye nezimfanelo, kusukela ebangeni lephephandaba ukuya kukhwalithi ephezulu kanye nephepha elimba eqolo elithengiswa njengamashidi ngamanye.[26] Amaphepha ayahluka ngokwakheka, umbala, i-asidi, namandla uma emanzi. Iphepha elibushelelezi lihle ekunikezeni imininingwane emihle, kodwa iphepha "elinamazinyo" libamba umdwebo kangcono. Ngakho okokusebenza okumaholoholo kuyasiza ekukhiqizeni ukugqama okujulile. 

I-Newsprint kanye nephepha lokuthayipha kungase kube usizo ekuzilolongeni nasekudwebeni okumaholo. Iphepha lokulandela lisetshenziselwa ukuhlola umdwebo osuqedwe uhhafu, nokudlulisa umdwebo usuka kwelinye ishidi uya kwelinye. Iphepha le-Cartridge liwuhlobo oluyisisekelo lwephepha lokudweba elithengiswa ngamaphedi. Ibhodi le-Bristol kanye namabhodi anzima kakhulu angenayo i-asidi, ngokuvamile aneziphetho ezibushelelezi, asetshenziselwa ukudweba imininingwane emihle futhi angahlanekezeli lapho kusetshenziswa imidiya emanzi (uyinki, ukuwasha). I-Vellum ibushelelezi ngokwedlulele futhi ifanele imininingwane emihle kakhulu. Iphepha le-watercolor elicindezelwe lingase lithandeke ngomdwebo oyinki ngenxa yokuthungwa kwawo. 

Iphepha lekhwalithi elingenawo i-asidi, eligcina umlando walo kanye nokuthungwa kwalo lide kakhulu kunephepha elisekelwe ngokhuni elifana ne-newsprint, eliba phuzi futhi libe brittle ngokushesha. 

Amathuluzi ayisisekelo ibhodi lokudweba noma itafula, isiloli sepensela nesisula, kanye nokudweba uyinki, iphepha lokusula. Amanye amathuluzi asetshenziswa yikhampasi eyindilinga, irula, nesikwele sesethi. I-Fixative isetshenziselwa ukuvimbela amamaki epensela namakhrayoni ukuthi angangcoli. I-Drafting tape isetshenziselwa ukuvikela iphepha endaweni yokudweba, kanye nokuvala indawo ukuze igcine ingenazimpawu zengozi, njengezinto ezifafaziwe noma ezifafaziwe kanye nezinto zokugeza. Ithebula le-easel noma elitshekile lisetshenziselwa ukugcina indawo yokudweba isendaweni efanelekile, ngokuvamile evundlile kunendawo esetshenziswa ekudwebeni. 

Isu 

u-Antoine Watteau, indlela yamakhrayoni e-trois 
Cishe bonke abadwebi abadweba uhlaka basebenzisa izandla neminwe yabo ukuze bafake imidiya, ngaphandle kwabanye abakhubazekile abadweba ngomlomo noma ngezinyawo.[27]

Ngaphambi kokusebenza ngesithombe, iciko livamise ukuhlola ukuthi imidiya ehlukahlukene isebenza kanjani. Bangase bazame izinto ezisetshenziswayo ezihlukene zokudweba emashidini okuprakthiza ukuze banqume inani nokuthungwa, kanye nendlela yokuyisebenzisa ukuze kukhiqizwe imiphumela ehlukahlukene. 


U-Raphael, ukutadisha lokho okwaba yi-Alba Madonna, neminye imidwebo 
Ukukhethwa komdwebi kokudweba kuthinta ukubukeka kwesithombe. Imidwebo yepeni noyinki ivamise ukusebenzisa ukuchanyuselwa - amaqembu emigqa ehambisanayo.[28] I-cross-hatching isebenzisa ukuchanyuselwa ezindaweni ezimbili noma ngaphezulu ezihlukene ukuze kudaleke ithoni emnyama. Ukuchanyuselwa okuphukile, noma imigqa enqamuka ngezikhathi ezithile, yenza amathoni alula - futhi ukulawula ukuminyana kwezikhawu kufeza ukuhleleka kwethoni. I-Stippling isebenzisa amachashazi ukukhiqiza ithoni, ukuthungwa kanye nomthunzi. Ukuthungwa okuhlukene kungafinyelelwa kuye ngendlela esetshenziselwa ukwakha ithoni.[29] 

Imidwebo emithonjeni eyomile ivame ukusebenzisa amasu afanayo, nakuba amapensela nezinti zokudweba zingafinyelela ukuhlukahluka okuqhubekayo kwethoni. Ngokuvamile umdwebo ugcwaliswa ngokusekelwe ekutheni umdwebi uthanda siphi isandla. Umculi ongakwesokudla udweba ukusuka kwesokunxele ukuya kwesokudla ukugwema ukungcolisa isithombe. Amarabha angasusa imigqa engadingeki, akhanyise amathoni, futhi ahlanze izimpawu ezilahlekile. Emdwebeni odwetshiwe noma owuhlaka, imigqa edwetshiwe ivamise ukulandela umkhonto wesihloko, idale ukujula ngokubukeka njengethunzi elivela ekukhanyeni endaweni yeciko. 

Kwesinye isikhathi umdwebi ushiya ingxenye yesithombe ingakathintwa kuyilapho egcwalisa okusele. Ukuma kwendawo okumele kugcinwe kungapendwa nge-masking fluid noma kunqunywe ku-frisket futhi kusetshenziswe endaweni yokudweba, ukuvikela ubuso emamaki alahlekile kuze kube yilapho i-mask isusiwe. 

Enye indlela yokugcina ingxenye yesithombe ukusebenzisa isifutho sokulungisa phezulu. Lokhu kubamba okuxekethile kuqine kakhulu eshidini futhi kuvimbele ukuthi lingagcobi. Kodwa-ke isifutho esilungisayo sisebenzisa amakhemikhali angalimaza uhlelo lokuphefumula, ngakho-ke kufanele sisetshenziswe endaweni engenawo umoya njengangaphandle. 

Enye indlela umdwebo okhiphayo lapho umdwebo umbozwa nge-graphite noma amalahle bese uyasulwa ukuze kwenziwe isithombe.[30] 

Ithoni 

Isithombe sepensela sika-Henry Macbeth-Raeburn, esinokuchanyuselwa kanye nokufiphaza (1909) 
Ukufiphaza kuyindlela yokuguqula amanani ethoni ephepheni ukumela umthunzi wento kanye nokubekwa kwethunzi. Ukunakwa ngokucophelela ekukhanyeni okuveziwe, izithunzi nokugqamile kungaholela ekuhunyushweni okungokoqobo kwesithombe.

Ukuhlanganisa kusebenzisa ithuluzi ukuze kuthambise noma kusabalalise imivimbo yokudweba yasekuqaleni. Ukuhlanganisa kwenziwa kalula nge-medium engazilungiseli ngokushesha, njenge-graphite, ushoki, noma amalahle, nakuba uyinki osanda kufakwa ungacwiliswa, ube manzi noma wome, kweminye imiphumela. Ukuze kufakwe ukufiphaza nokuhlanganisa, umdwebi angasebenzisa isiphunzi esihlanganisayo, izicubu, irabha eligxotshiwe, ichopho lomunwe, nanoma iyiphi inhlanganisela yakho. Ucezu lwe-chamois luwusizo ekudaleni ukuthungwa okubushelelezi, kanye nokukhipha izinto ezibonakalayo ukuze kukhanye ithoni. Ithoni eqhubekayo ingafinyelelwa nge-graphite endaweni ebushelelezi ngaphandle kokuxubana, kodwa inqubo inzima, ehlanganisa imivimbo emincane eyindilinga noma eyisiyingi enephuzu elibuthuntu. 

Izindlela zokuthungatha ezethula nokuthungwa emdwebeni zihlanganisa ukuchanyuselwa kanye nokunyakazisa. Ezinye izindlela eziningi zikhiqiza ukuthungwa. Ngaphezu kokukhethwa kwephepha, izinto zokudweba kanye namasu kuthinta ukuthungwa. Ukuthungwa kungenziwa kubonakale kungokoqobo ngokwengeziwe uma kudwetshwa eduze nokuthungwa okuhlukile; ukuthungwa okumahhadla kubonakala kakhulu uma kubekwe eduze kwendawo ehlanganiswe kahle. Umphumela ofanayo ungafinyelelwa ngokudweba amathoni ahlukene eduze. Unqenqema olukhanyayo eduze kwengemuva elimnyama lugqama esweni, futhi lucishe lubonakale luntanta ngaphezulu kwendawo. 

Ukuqondiswa kanye nekhwalithi yokukhanya kudlala indima ebalulekile ekushiseni, kuthonya ukujula nobukhulu bomdwebo. Ukuqonda ukuthi ukukhanya kusebenzelana kanjani nezindawo ezihlukene kusiza amaciko akhe umuzwa wokwangempela, noma ngabe anikezela ngezinto ezibushelelezi, ezikhanyayo noma ama-rough, matte textures. Ukubuka izimo zokukhanya zomhlaba wangempela nokuzilolongela ukuphila kungathuthukisa ikhono leciko lokubonisa izithunzi ezikholisayo nokugqamisa. 

Ukwengeza, amasu okuthungatha athuthukile, njengokuqhafaza kanye nokuklolodela, avumela ukulawula okukhulu ekushintsheni kwethoni kanye nemininingwane yendawo. Ukweqa kuhlanganisa ukuhlukanisa imigqa enqamulayo ukuze kwakhiwe ukujula nephimbo, kuyilapho ukuklwebha kusebenzisa imivimbo eyindilinga noma edwetshiwe ukuze kwakheke ukufiphaza okuthambile, okuphilayo. Lezi zindlela, uma zihlanganiswe nokuhlanganisa ngokucophelela nokusetshenziswa kokuthungwa, zinikeza abaculi ikhithi yamathuluzi enemisebenzi eminingi ukuze bathole imiphumela eminingi, kusukela kuma-gradient athambile kuya ekuqanjweni okugqamile, okugqame kakhulu. 

Ifomu nengxenye 

Izilinganiso zomzimba womuntu 
Ukulinganisa ubukhulu besihloko ngenkathi kuvinjwa emdwebeni kuyisinyathelo esibalulekile sokukhiqiza ukuhumusha okungokoqobo kwesihloko. Amathuluzi anjengekhampasi angasetshenziswa ukukala ama-engeli ezinhlangothi ezihlukene. Lawa ma-engeli angaphinde akhiqizwe endaweni yomdwebo bese ehlolwa kabusha ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukuthi anembile. Olunye uhlobo lokulinganisa ukuqhathanisa osayizi abahlobene bezingxenye ezihlukene zesihloko nomunye nomunye. Umunwe obekwe endaweni ethile eduze kwesisetshenziswa somdwebo ungasetshenziswa ukuqhathanisa lobo bukhulu nezinye izingxenye zesithombe. Irula ingasetshenziswa kokubili njenge-straightedge kanye nedivayisi yokubala izilinganiso.


Ukwehluka kwesilinganiso nobudala 
Uma uzama ukudweba umumo oyinkimbinkimbi njengomfanekiso womuntu, kuyasiza ekuqaleni ukumela ifomu ngesethi yamavolumu akudala. Cishe noma yiluphi uhlobo lungamelwa yinhlanganisela ethile yekhiyubhu, imbulunga, isilinda, kanye nekhoni. Uma le miqulu eyisisekelo isiqoqwe ukuze ifane, khona-ke umdwebo ungacwengwa ube yifomu elinembe kakhudlwana neliphucuziwe. Imigqa yamavolumu akudala iyasuswa futhi ithathelwe indawo ngokufana kokugcina. Ukudweba ukwakhiwa okuyisisekelo kuyikhono eliyisisekelo lobuciko bokumelela, futhi lifundiswa ezincwadini nasezikoleni eziningi. Ukusebenza kwayo okulungile kuxazulula ukungaqiniseki okuningi mayelana nemininingwane emincane, futhi kwenze isithombe sokugcina sibukeke ngendlela efanayo.[31] 

Ubuciko obucwebe kakhudlwana bomdwebo wesithombe buncike kumdwebi onokuqonda okujulile kwe-anatomy kanye nenani labantu. Umdwebi oqeqeshiwe ujwayelene nesakhiwo samathambo, indawo ehlangene, ukubekwa kwemisipha, ukunyakaza kwe-tendon, nokuthi izingxenye ezihlukene zisebenza kanjani ndawonye ngesikhathi sokunyakaza. Lokhu kuvumela iciko ukuthi linikeze ukuma okungokwemvelo okwengeziwe okungabonakali kuqinile ngokokwenziwa. Umdwebi futhi ujwayelene nendlela izilinganiso ezihluka ngayo kuye ngeminyaka yesihloko, ikakhulukazi uma idweba isithombe esime ngobude. 

Umbono 
I-athikili eyinhloko: Umbono 

Umdwebo wombono onamaphuzu amabili 
Umbono womugqa uyindlela yokubonisa izinto endaweni eyisicaba ukuze ubukhulu bunciphe ngebanga. Iqoqo ngalinye lemiphetho ehambisanayo, eqondile yanoma iyiphi into, kungaba isakhiwo noma itafula, ilandela imigqa egcina ihlangana endaweni eshabalalayo. Ngokuvamile leli phuzu lokuhlangana lisendaweni ethile emkhathizwe, njengoba izakhiwo zakhiwe zisezingeni eliphansi. Uma izakhiwo eziningi ziqondaniswe nezinye, njengezakhiwo ezisemgwaqweni, iziqongo ezivundlile nezingezansi zezakhiwo ngokuvamile zihlangana endaweni yokushabalala. 

Lapho kudwetshwa izinhlangothi zombili nezinhlangothi, khona-ke imigqa ehambisanayo eyakha uhlangothi iyahlangana endaweni yesibili emkhathizwe (okungenzeka isuke ephepheni lomdwebo.) Lona umbono onamaphuzu amabili.[32] Ukuguqula imigqa eqondile ibe iphuzu lesithathu ngenhla noma ngaphansi komkhathizwe bese kukhiqiza umbono onamaphuzu amathathu.

 
Umdwebi odweba umfanekiso ngombono we-worm's-eye
Ukujula nakho kungavezwa ngamasu amaningana ngaphezu kwendlela yokubuka ngenhla. Izinto ezinosayizi ofanayo kufanele zibonakale zizincane kakhulu uma ziqhelelene nesibukeli. Kanjalo isondo langemuva lenqola libonakala lincanyana kunesondo langaphambili. Ukujula kungavezwa ngokusebenzisa ukuthungwa. Njengoba ukuthungwa kwento kuya ngokuya kuba matasa futhi kuba matasa, kuthatha uhlamvu oluhluke ngokuphelele kunalapho iseduze. Ukujula nakho kungavezwa ngokunciphisa ukugqama ezintweni ezikude kakhulu, nangokwenza imibala yazo ingagcwali kakhulu. Lokhu kukhiqiza kabusha umphumela wobungu basemoyeni, futhi kubangele iso ukuthi ligxile kakhulu ezintweni ezidwetshwe ngaphambili. Umdwebo wocwaningo 

lokuqamba 

onamaphuzu avelele amhlophe ka-William-Adolphe Bouguereau 
Ukwakheka kwesithombe kuyisici esibalulekile ekukhiqizeni umsebenzi othakazelisayo wokufaneleka kwezobuciko. Iciko lihlela ukubekwa kwesici kwezobuciko ukuze lixhumane nemibono nemizwa nombukeli. Ukwakheka kunganquma ukugxilwa kobuciko, futhi kuphumele ekupheleleni okuvumelanayo okukhangayo ngobuhle nokushukumisayo. 

Ukukhanya kwesihloko nakho kuyisici esibalulekile ekudaleni ucezu lobuciko, futhi ukuxhumana kokukhanya nesithunzi kuyindlela ebalulekile ebhokisini lamathuluzi lomdwebi. Ukubekwa kwemithombo yokukhanya kungenza umehluko omkhulu ohlotsheni lomlayezo owethulwayo. Imithombo eminingi yokukhanya ingageza noma imiphi imibimbi ebusweni bomuntu, ngokwesibonelo, futhi inikeze ukubukeka kobusha. Ngokuphambene, umthombo wokukhanya owodwa, njengokukhanya kwemini okuqinile, ungasebenza ukugqamisa noma yikuphi ukuthungwa noma izici ezithandekayo. 

Lapho edweba into noma umfanekiso, umdwebi onekhono unaka kokubili indawo engaphakathi kwe-silhouette nokuthi yini engaphandle. Ingaphandle libizwa ngokuthi yisikhala esingesihle, futhi singabaluleka ekumeleleni njengesibalo. Izinto ezibekwe ngemuva kwesithombe kufanele zivele zibekwe kahle noma kuphi lapho zingabukwa khona. 

Ucwaningo luwuhlaka lomdwebo owenziwa kulungiselelwa isithombe sokugcina esihleliwe. Izifundo zingasetshenziswa ukucacisa ukubukeka kwezingxenye ezithile zesithombe esiqediwe, noma ukuhlola indlela engcono kakhulu yokufeza umgomo wokugcina. Nokho isifundo esiklanywe kahle singaba ucezu lobuciko ngokwalo, futhi amahora amaningi okusebenza ngokucophelela angangena ekuqedeni isifundo. 

Inqubo 

Owesifazane osemusha edweba i-Barberini Faun eMunich 
Abantu ngabanye babonisa umehluko ekhonweni labo lokukhiqiza imidwebo enembile ngokubukeka,[33] lapho umdwebo onembile ngokubukeka "uqashelwa njengento ethile ngesikhathi esithile nasendaweni ethile, unikezwa ngokungezwa okuncane kwemininingwane ebonakalayo engabonakali entweni emelwe noma ngokususwa okuncane kwemininingwane ebonakalayo."[34]

Ucwaningo luhlose ukuchaza izizathu zokuthi kungani abanye abantu bedweba kangcono kunabanye. Olunye ucwaningo lwabeka amakhono amane abalulekile enqubweni yokudweba: amakhono ezimoto adingekayo ekwenzeni amamaki, umbono wedrowa ngokwalo ngomdwebo walo, umbono wezinto ezidwetshwayo, kanye nekhono lokwenza izinqumo zokumelela okuhle.[34] Ukulandela le nkolelo-mbono, izifundo eziningana ziye zafuna ukuphetha ngokuthi yiziphi lezi zinqubo ezibaluleke kakhulu ekuthinteni ukunemba kwemidwebo. 


Inqubo yokudweba ku-Academic Study of a Male Torso ka-Jean-Auguste-Dominique Ingres (1801, National Museum, Warsaw) Ukulawulwa 
kwezimoto 
Ukulawulwa kwezimoto kuyisici esibalulekile esibonakalayo 'Esigabeni Sokukhiqiza' senqubo yokudweba.[35] Kuye kwaphakanyiswa ukuthi ukulawula kwezimoto kudlala indima ekhonweni lokudweba, nakuba imiphumela yako ingabalulekile.[34] 

Umbono 
Kuye kwaphakanyiswa ukuthi ikhono lomuntu lokubona into ayidwebayo yisigaba esibaluleke kakhulu enqubweni yokudweba.[34] Lesi siphakamiso sisekelwa ukutholakala kobudlelwane obuqinile phakathi kokubona nekhono lokudweba.[36] 

Lobu bufakazi busebenza njengesisekelo sencwadi kaBetty Edwards ethi, Ukudweba Ngakwesokudla Kobuchopho.[37] U-Edward wayehlose ukufundisa abafundi bakhe indlela yokudweba, ngokusekelwe ekuthuthukisweni kwamakhono okuqonda omfundi. 

Ngaphezu kwalokho, umdwebi onethonya kanye nomhlaziyi wezobuciko uJohn Ruskin wagcizelela ukubaluleka kombono enqubweni yokudweba encwadini yakhe ethi The Elements of Drawing.[38] Wathi, "Ngoba cishe ngiyaqiniseka, ukuthi uma sesibona ngokucacile ngokwanele, kuncane kakhulu ubunzima ekudwebeni esikubonayo." 

Inkumbulo ebonakalayo 
Lokhu kuphinde kukhonjiswe ukuthi kunomthelela ekhonweni lomuntu lokudala imidwebo enembile ngokubukeka. Inkumbulo yesikhashana idlala indima ebalulekile ekudwebeni njengoba amehlo eshintsha phakathi kwento ayidwebayo kanye nomdwebo ngokwawo.[39] 

Ukuthatha izinqumo 
Ezinye izifundo eziqhathanisa abaculi nabangewona amaciko zithole ukuthi amaciko achitha isikhathi esiningi ecabanga ngendlela ehlelekile ngenkathi edweba. Ikakhulukazi, amaciko achitha isikhathi esiningi emisebenzini 'ye-metacognitive' efana nokucabangela izinhlelo ezihlukene zokucabanga ukuthi angathuthuka kanjani ngomdwebo. 

Isithombe (esaziwa nangokuthi isithombe, noma ngokuvamile okubhekiselwa kuso njengesithombe noma isithombe) isithombe esidalwe ukukhanya okuwela endaweni ezwelayo, ngokuvamile ifilimu yezithombe noma inzwa yesithombe sikagesi. Inqubo kanye nomkhuba wokudala izithombe ezinjalo kubizwa ngokuthi ukuthwebula izithombe. 

Izithombe eziningi manje zenziwa kusetshenziswa i-smartphone noma ikhamera, esebenzisa ilensi ukuze igxilise amaza okukhanya abonakalayo endaweni yesehlakalo ibe ukukhiqizwa kwalokho okungabonwa iso lomuntu. 

I-Etymology
Igama elithi isithombe laqanjwa ngo-1839 nguSir John Herschel futhi lisekelwe kwelesiGreki elithi φῶς (phos), elisho "ukukhanya," nelithi γραφή (graphê), elisho "ukudweba, ukubhala," ndawonye okusho "ukudweba ngokukhanya."[1] 

Umlando 
Isihloko Esiyinhloko: Umlando Wezithombe 
Isithombe sokuqala esihlala njalo, ikhophi edaluliwe yombhalo othi "182" wenziwa kusetshenziswa umbhalo othi "182" oqoshiwe osuselwe kothintana naye. inqubo eyenziwe ngu-Nicéphore Niépce. Izithombe zokuqala zesigcawu somhlaba wangempela, ezenziwe kusetshenziswa ikhamera obscura, zalandela eminyakeni embalwa kamuva e-Le Gras, eFrance, ngo-1826, kodwa inqubo kaNiépce yayingazwelani ngokwanele ukuba isebenze kuleso sicelo: kwakudingeka ukuchayeka kwekhamera okuthatha amahora amaningi noma izinsuku.[2] Ngo-1829, u-Niépce wangena ebudlelwaneni noLouis Daguerre, futhi bobabili babambisana ukuze benze inqubo efanayo, kodwa ebucayi kakhulu, futhi ngenye indlela ethuthukisiwe. 


Buka ngefasitela eLe Gras, 1826 nguJoseph Nicéphore Niépce 
Ngemva kokushona kuka-Niépce ngomhla ka-5 Julayi 1833 [3], u-Daguerre wagxila kwezinye izindlela ezisekelwe esiliva. Wadalula ishidi lethusi elinesiliva ku-iodine, okwenza ungqimba lwe-iodide esiliva ezwela ukukhanya; wayiveza kukhamera imizuzu embalwa; uthuthukise isithombe esifihlekile esingabonakali saba nomphumela wokubonakala ngentuthu ye-mercury; wabe esegeza ipuleti ngekhambi likasawoti oshisayo ukuze akhiphe iodide esiliva esele, okwenza imiphumela isheshe. Le nqubo yokuqala ewusizo yokwenza izithombe ngekhamera, i-daguerreotype, wayiqamba ngaye. Ukuba khona kwayo kwamenyezelwa emhlabeni ngomhlaka-7 Januwari 1839, kodwa imininingwane yokusebenza ayizange yenziwe esidlangalaleni kuze kube yi-19 Agasti ngalowo nyaka. Abanye abasunguli maduzane benza intuthuko enkulu enciphise inani elidingekayo lesikhathi sokuchayeka lisuka emaminithini ambalwa laya kumasekhondi ambalwa, okwenza ukuthwebula izithombe ngobude kusebenze ngempela futhi kudume kabanzi ngalesi sikhathi.

I-daguerreotype yayinokushiyeka, ikakhulukazi ubuthakathaka bendawo yesithombe esifana nesibuko kanye nezimo ezithile zokubuka ezidingekayo ukuze ubone isithombe ngendlela efanele. Ngayinye yayiyi-positive eyingqayizivele, ekhanyayo engaphinda iphindwe kuphela ngokuyikopisha ngekhamera. Abasunguli baqala ukusebenza ngezinqubo ezithuthukisiwe ezizoba usizo kakhulu. Ekupheleni kwawo-1850, i-daguerreotype yase ithathelwe indawo i-ambrotype ne-tintype engabizi kakhulu futhi ebukeka kalula, eyasebenzisa inqubo ye-collodion esanda kwethulwa. I-Glass plate collodion negatives esetshenziselwa ukwenza amaphrinta ephepheni le-albuden ngokushesha yaba indlela ethandwayo yezithombe futhi yahlala kuleso sikhundla iminyaka eminingi, ngisho nangemva kokwethulwa kwenqubo ye-gelatin elula kakhulu ngo-1871. Ukulungiswa kwenqubo ye-gelatin kuye kwahlala kuyinqubo eyinhloko yezithombe ezimnyama nezimhlophe kuze kube yilolu suku, okuhluke ngokuyinhloko ekuzweleni kwe-emulsion esetshenziswayo esetshenziswayo, okwakuyi-plastic esetshenziswayo, okwakuyi-flexible ye-emulsion yokuqala. amafilimu, kanye nezinhlobo ezahlukene zephepha lokuphrinta kokugcina. 


I-Market Square yase-Helsinki, ngeminyaka yawo-1890s 
Ukuthwebula ngemibala kucishe kube mdala ngokumnyama nokumhlophe, nokuhlola kwasekuqaleni okuhlanganisa nokuphrinta kwe-Anthotype ka-John Herschel ngo-1842, umsebenzi wokuphayona ka-Louis Ducos du Hauron ngeminyaka yawo-1860, kanye nenqubo ye-Lippmann eyambulwa ngo-1891, kodwa iminyaka eminingi yahlala iyilabhorethri yezithombe. Kwaqala kwaba yiqiniso lezentengiselwano elisakazekile ngokwethulwa kwamapuleti e-Autochrome ngo-1907, kodwa amapuleti ayebiza kakhulu futhi engafaneleki ukuthatha isifinyezo esivamile ngamakhamera aphethwe ngesandla. Maphakathi nawo-1930 kwethulwa i-Kodachrome ne-Agfacolor Neu, amafilimu ombala okuqala asebenziseka kalula ohlobo lwesimanje lwe-multi-layer chromogenic. Lezi zinqubo zakuqala zakhiqiza ukukhanya ukuze kusetshenziswe kuma-projektha amaslayidi namadivayisi wokubuka, kodwa ukuphrinta kwemibala kuye kwaduma kakhulu ngemva kokwethulwa kwephepha lokuphrinta lombala we-chromogenic ngawo-1940. Izidingo zomkhakha wezithombe ezinyakazayo zenze inani lezinqubo ezikhethekile namasistimu, mhlawumbe eyaziwa kakhulu inqubo ye-Technicolor enemigqa emithathu engasasebenzi. 

Izinhlobo zezithombe 

Isithombe sokuchayeka isikhathi eside seTheleskophu Enkulu Kakhulu[4] 
Izithombe ezingezona ezedijithali zikhiqizwa ngenqubo yamakhemikhali enezinyathelo ezimbili. Kunqubo yezinyathelo ezimbili, ifilimu ezwela ukukhanya ithwebula isithombe esibi (imibala nezibani/ubumnyama buhlanekezelwe). Ukukhiqiza isithombe esihle, okunegethivu kuvame ukudluliselwa ('okuphrintiwe') ephepheni lezithombe. Ukuphrinta okunegethivu kusitoko sefilimu esisobala kusetshenziswa ukwenza amafilimu ezithombe ezinyakazayo.

Kungenjalo, ifilimu iyacutshungulwa ukuze iguqule isithombe esibi, iveze obala okuhle. Izithombe ezinjalo ezinhle zivame ukufakwa kumafreyimu, abizwa ngokuthi ama-slides. Ngaphambi kwenqubekelaphambili yakamuva ekuthwebuleni izithombe zedijithali, obala bekusetshenziswa kakhulu ochwepheshe ngenxa yokucija kwabo nokunemba kokuhunyushwa kombala. Izithombe eziningi ezishicilelwe komagazini zithathwe ngefilimu ebonisa obala ngombala. 

Ekuqaleni, zonke izithombe zaziyi-monochromatic noma zipendwe ngesandla ngombala. Nakuba izindlela zokuthuthukisa izithombe ezinemibala zazitholakala kusukela ngo-1861, azizange zitholakale kabanzi kwaze kwaba ngawo-1940 noma 1950, futhi noma kunjalo, kwaze kwaba ngawo-1960, izithombe eziningi zazithathwa zimnyama nezimhlophe. Kusukela ngaleso sikhathi, ukuthwebula izithombe ngemibala kuye kwabusa ukuthwebula izithombe ezithandwayo, nakuba kusasetshenziswa umbala omnyama nomhlophe, kulula ukuwuthuthukisa kunombala. 

Izithombe zefomethi ye-panoramic zingathathwa ngamakhamera afana ne-Hasselblad Xpan kufilimu evamile. Kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1990s, izithombe ze-panoramic bezitholakala kufilimu ye-Advanced Photo System (APS). I-APS yathuthukiswa abakhiqizi bamafilimu abakhulu abaningana ukuze banikeze ifilimu enamafomethi ahlukene kanye nezinketho zekhompuyutha ezitholakalayo, nakuba ama-panorama e-APS adalwe kusetshenziswa imaski kumakhamera anekhono le-panorama, engathandeki kakhulu kunekhamera ye-panoramic yangempela, ezuza umphumela wayo ngefomethi yefilimu ebanzi. I-APS isithandwa kakhulu futhi iyekisiwe. 

Ukufika kwe-microcomputer kanye nezithombe zedijithali kuholele ekwandeni kokuphrinta kwedijithali. Lawa maphrinti adalwe kusuka kumafomethi wesithombe agciniwe njenge-JPEG, TIFF, ne-RAW. Izinhlobo zamaphrinta asetshenziswayo zifaka amaphrinta e-inkjet, amaphrinta we-dye-sublimation, amaphrinta we-laser, namaphrinta ashisayo. Ngezinye izikhathi amaphrinti e-inkjet anikezwa igama elihlanganisiwe elithi "Giclée". 

IWebhu ibilokhu iyindlela edumile yokugcina nokwabelana ngezithombe kusukela isithombe sokuqala sashicilelwa kuwebhu ngu-Tim Berners-Lee ngo-1992 (isithombe sebhendi ye-CERN house Les Horribles Cernettes). Namuhla, amasayithi adumile afana ne-Flickr, i-PhotoBucket, ne-500px asetshenziswa izigidi zabantu ukwabelana ngezithombe zabo. 

Eyokuqala ethi "selfie", noma ukuzithwebula, yathathwa nguRobert Cornelious emuva ngo-1839. [5] "Ama-Selfies" abe ngesinye sezithombe ezivame kakhulu, ikakhulukazi phakathi kwabantu abasha besifazane. Inkundla yezokuxhumana isiphenduke intuthuko yamasiko ngenxa yokuthatha izithombe. Abantu bayachuma ngenxa yezithombe ozishuthe zona osaziwayo babo abathandayo, abaningi bathola izigidi zokuthandwa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngenxa yesithombe ozishuthe sona esilula. 
Amafolda Ephepha 

Lokulondolozwa
Ukugcinwa kwesithombe okufanelekile kuhilela ukubeka isithombe ngasinye kufolda ngayinye eyakhiwe ngephepha elifakwe isivikelo, noma elingenayo i-asidi.[6] Amafolda ephepha ane-buffered atuswa ikakhulukazi ezimeni lapho isithombe besigxunyekwe ezintweni ezisezingeni eliphansi noma kusetshenziswa into enamathelayo ezoholela ekwakhiweni kwe-asidi eyengeziwe.[7] Gcina izithombe ezinobukhulu obungamayintshi angu-8x10 noma ezincane ngokuma ziqonde onqenqemeni olude lwesithombe kufolda yephepha eligcinwe endaweni yefa, ngaphakathi kwebhokisi lengobo yomlando elikhudlwana, bese ulebula ifolda ngayinye ngolwazi olufanele ukuze uyikhombe. Imvelo eqinile yefolda ivikela isithombe ekuweni noma ekuqhekekeni, inqobo nje uma ibhokisi lingapakishwanga liqine kakhulu noma lingagcwaliswanga ngaphansi. Izithombe ezinkudlwana zefolda noma izithombe eziphukayo zistakwe njengesicaba ngaphakathi kwamabhokisi okugcinwa kwengobo yomlando nezinye izinto ezinosayizi oqhathanisekayo.[8] 

Izindwangu ze-polyester
Amapulasitiki aqine kakhulu asetshenziswa ekulondolozweni kwezithombe, i-polyester, ayikhiqizi noma yiziphi izakhi zamakhemikhali eziyingozi, futhi ayinawo amandla okumunca ama-asidi akhiqizwa isithombe ngokwaso. Imikhono ye-polyester kanye ne-encapsulation iye yanconywa ngekhono layo lokuvikela isithombe ekumswakama nokungcoliswa kwemvelo, ibambezela ukusabela phakathi kwento nomkhathi. Lokhu kuyiqiniso, nokho i-polyester ivamise ukuvalela lezi zakhi eduze kwento ehloselwe ukuyivikela. Lokhu kuyingozi ikakhulukazi endaweni yokugcina ehlangabezana nokuguquguquka okukhulu komswakama noma izinga lokushisa, okuholela ekufakweni kwe-ferrotyping, noma ukunamathela kwesithombe epulasitiki.[6] Izithombe ezinemikhono noma ezifakwe ku-polyester azikwazi ukugcinwa ziqondile emabhokisini ngenxa yokuthi zizoshelela phansi eduze kwezinye ngaphakathi kwebhokisi, zigobe futhi zigoqe, futhi umgcini womlando akakwazi ukubhala ngokuqondile ku-polyester ukuze abone isithombe. Ngakho-ke, kuyadingeka ukupakisha izithombe ezivikelwe i-polyester zivundlile ngaphakathi kwebhokisi, noma uzibophe ku-binder ezintathu zamaringi. Ukupakisha izithombe ngokuvundlile ngaphakathi kwebhokisi eliyisicaba kuzonciphisa kakhulu ukufinyelela kalula, futhi izibophezelo zishiya izinhlangothi ezintathu zesithombe zivezwe emiphumeleni yokukhanya[9] futhi azisekeli isithombe ngokulinganayo nhlangothi zombili, okuholela ekuwohlokeni nasekugobeni ngaphakathi kwesibophezelo. Ipulasitiki esetshenziselwa ukuvaleka yenziwe ukuze ingakhuni ngangokunokwenzeka ukuze kuvinjelwe ukunwaya izithombe ngesikhathi sokufakwa emikhonweni. Ngeshwa, ukushelela kwendawo ebiyelwe kukhiqiza ugesi omile, oheha uthuli nezinhlayiya ze-lint. I-static ingadonsela uthuli ngaphakathi komkhono, futhi, lapho inganwaya khona isithombe.[6] Ngokunjalo, lezi zingxenye ezisiza ekufakweni kwesithombe, okubizwa ngokuthi ama-slip agents, zingakwazi ukudilika bese zidluliswa zisuka kupulasitiki ziye esithombeni, lapho zifaka khona njengefilimu enamafutha, zihehe okunye ulayini nothuli. Ngalesi sikhathi, akukho ukuhlolwa kokuhlola imiphumela yesikhathi eside yalezi zingxenye ezithombeni. Ngaphezu kwalokho, imikhono yepulasitiki ingakha ama-kinks noma ama-creases ebusweni, okuzoklwebha i-emulsion ngesikhathi sokuphatha.[9]
 
Ukuphatha nokunakekela
Kungcono ukushiya izithombe zilele phansi etafuleni uma uzibuka. Ungayithathi ekhoneni, noma ezinhlangothini ezimbili futhi uyibambe isezingeni lamehlo. Ngaso sonke isikhathi lapho isithombe sigoba, ngisho nakancane, lokhu kungabhidliza i-emulsion.[10] Yona kanye imvelo yokufaka isithombe ngepulasitiki ikhuthaza abasebenzisi ukuthi basithathe; abasebenzisi bathambekele ekuphatheni izithombe ezivalelwe zepulasitiki ngobumnene kunezithombe ezingavaliwe, ngoba nje bezwa ukuthi indawo ebiyelwe ngepulasitiki yenza isithombe singaphathwa kahle. Uma nje isithombe sikufolda yaso, asikho isidingo sokusithinta; mane nje ukhiphe ifolda ebhokisini, uyibeke phansi etafuleni, bese uvula ifolda. Uma ngesizathu esithile abacwaningi noma abagcini bomlando kudingeka baphathe isithombe sangempela, mhlawumbe ukuze bahlole i-verso ukuze babhale, bangasebenzisa amagilavu uma kubonakala kunengozi evela kumafutha noma ukungcola ezandleni. 

Izinganekwane nezinkolelo 
Bheka futhi: I-Aniconism 
Ngenxa yokuthi ama-daguerreotype ayehunyushwa endaweni eyisibuko, abantu abaningi abasebenzelana nemimoya nabo baba ochwepheshe balolu hlobo lobuciko olusha. Izazi zemimoya zingasho ukuthi isithombe somuntu esibukweni esibukiwe sasifana nokubheka umphefumulo womuntu. Abasebenzisa imimoya nabo babekholelwa ukuthi kwakuzovula imiphefumulo yabo futhi kungenise amademoni. Kwamanye amaSulumane, amakruh (okungathandwa) ukwenza isalah (ukukhulekela) endaweni ehlotshiswe ngezithombe.[11] Izithombe nezinto ezingaziwa zegumbi elimnyama kwesinye isikhathi ziholela ababukeli ukuthi bakholelwe ukuthi imimoya noma amademoni athwetshulwe ezithombeni. Abanye baye benza umsebenzi wabo ngokuthatha izithombe "zezipoki" noma "imimoya".[12] Kunezimo eziningi lapho abantu bakholelwa ukuthi izithombe zizoletha amashwa kumuntu othatha isithombe noma abantu abathwetshulwe esithombeni. Ngokwesibonelo, isithombe esithathwe owesifazane okhulelwe sizoletha amashwa enganeni esesibelethweni futhi izithombe zabantu abafile zizoqinisekisa ukuthi lowo muntu akaphumeleli ekuphileni kwangemva kokufa.[13] Isihloko Esiyinhloko 

Esisemthethweni 
: Ukuthwebula izithombe nomthetho 
Ukukhiqizwa noma ukusatshalaliswa kwezinhlobo ezithile zezithombe kwenqatshelwe ngaphansi kwemithetho yesimanje, njengaleyo yezakhiwo zikahulumeni,[14] izifunda ezisezingeni eliphezulu,[15] impahla yangasese, imisebenzi enamalungelo okukopisha,[16][17] izitho zangasese zezingane,[18] izithombe zobulili ezingcolile zezingane kanye nezithombe zobulili ezingcolile ezingavamile kakhulu.[19] Le mithetho ihluka kakhulu phakathi kwezindawo.

Kwezinye izindawo zomphakathi eziphethwe nguhulumeni, njengezinkantolo zomthetho,[20] izakhiwo zikahulumeni, imitapo yolwazi, izikhungo zomphakathi [21][22] kanye neminye iminyuziyamu e-Hong Kong, ukuthwebula izithombe akuvunyelwe ngaphandle kwemvume evela kuhulumeni. Akukho emthethweni ukuhlomisa noma ukuthatha izithombe nokuqoshwa endaweni yokuzijabulisa yomphakathi, njengamasinema kanye namathiyetha angaphakathi.[23][24] E-Hungary, kusukela mhla ziyi-15 kuNdasa wezi-2014 lapho kushicilelwa i-Civil Code okwase kuyisikhathi eside ilindelwe, umthetho waphinde washo lokho obekuyinto evamile, okungukuthi, ukuthi umuntu unelungelo lokwenqaba ukuthwetshulwa. Nokho, imvume ecatshangelwayo ikhona: akukho emthethweni ukuthwebula umuntu ongaphikisani ngokugcwele.[25][26] 

ENingizimu Afrika ukuthwebula abantu esidlangalaleni kusemthethweni.[27] Ukukhiqiza kabusha nokudayisa izithombe zabantu kusemthethweni ekuhleleni nasekusebenziseni okulinganiselwe izinjongo zezohwebo. Awukho umthetho wecala ongachaza ukuthi iyini imikhawulo ekusetshenzisweni kwezentengiso. E-United Kingdom ayikho imithetho enqabela ukuthwebula izithombe zendawo yangasese endaweni yomphakathi.[28] Ukuthwebula izithombe okuphikelelayo nokunolaka komuntu oyedwa kungase kube ngaphansi kwencazelo engokomthetho yokuhlukumeza.[29][30][31][32] Ilungelo lobumfihlo laba khona emthethweni wase-UK njengomphumela wokufakwa kweNgqungquthela YaseYurophu Yamalungelo Abantu emthethweni wasekhaya ngoMthetho Wamalungelo Abantu ka-1998. Lokhu kungaholela emigomeni ekushicilelweni kwezithombe. 

Umculo weshidi uwuhlobo olubhalwe ngesandla noma oluphrintiwe lwenothi yomculo esebenzisa izimpawu zomculo ukukhombisa ukuphakama, isigqi, noma izingoma zengoma noma ucezu lomculo wezinsimbi. Njengezifaniso zayo - izincwadi eziphrintiwe noma amapheshana esiNgisi, isi-Arabhu, noma ezinye izilimi - uhlobo lomculo weshidi ngokuvamile iphepha (noma, emakhulwini eminyaka angaphambili, i-papyrus noma isikhumba). Kodwa-ke, ukufinyelela emazwini omculo kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1980s kufake ukwethulwa kwezikolo ezikrinini zekhompuyutha kanye nokuthuthukiswa kwezinhlelo zekhompiyutha zombhali wamaphuzu akwazi ukuphawula ingoma noma ucezu nge-elektroniki, futhi, kwezinye izimo, "udlale emuva" umculo ophawuliwe usebenzisa i-synthesizer noma izinsimbi ezibonakalayo. 

Ukusetshenziswa kweshidi lamagama kuhloswe ukuhlukanisa izinhlobo zomculo ezibhaliwe noma eziphrintiwe kumsindo orekhodiwe (kurekhodi le-vinyl, ikhasethi, i-CD), ukusakazwa komsakazo noma i-TV noma ukudlala bukhoma okurekhodiwe, okungathwebula ifilimu noma ividiyo yokudlalwa kanye nengxenye yomsindo. Ekusetshenzisweni kwansuku zonke, umculo weshidi (noma umane nje umculo) ungabhekisela ekushicilelweni komculo weshidi lokuthengisa ngokuhambisana nokukhishwa kwefilimu entsha, uhlelo lwe-TV, i-albhamu erekhodiwe, noma omunye umcimbi oyingqayizivele noma odumile ohilela umculo. Umculo wokuqala ophrintiwe owenziwe ngomshini wokunyathelisa wenziwa ngo-1473.

Umculo weshidi uwuhlobo oluyisisekelo lapho kuphawulwa khona umculo we-Western classical ukuze ufundwe futhi wenziwa abaculi ababodwa, abadlali bezinsimbi noma ama-ensembles omculo. Izinhlobo eziningi zomculo wendabuko nodumile waseNtshonalanga zivame ukufundwa abaculi nabaculi "ngendlebe", esikhundleni sokusebenzisa umculo weshidi (yize ezimweni eziningi, umculo wendabuko nowe-pop ungase utholakale ngendlela yomculo weshidi). 

Igama elithi isikolo liyitemu elihlukile (futhi elejwayelekile) lomculo weshidi, futhi kunezinhlobo ezimbalwa zezikolo, njengoba kuxoxwe ngakho ngezansi. Igama elithi score lingabuye libhekisele emculweni wetiyetha, umculo wezinsimbi noma izingoma ezibhalelwe umdlalo, umculo, i-opera noma i-ballet, noma umculo noma izingoma ezibhalelwe uhlelo lwethelevishini noma ifilimu; okokugcina kwalokhu, bona isikolo sefilimu. Ikhasi lesihloko le 

-Elements 

lohlelo lokuqala lwezwi lomculo we-Béatrice et Bénédict ka 
-Hector Berlioz nomculo we-credit 
Sheet wangekhulunyaka lama-20 nelama-21 ngokuvamile ubonisa isihloko sengoma noma okuqanjwe ekhasini lesihloko, ikhava, noma phezulu ekhasini lokuqala lapho lingekho ikhasi lesihloko elihlukile. Uma iculo noma ucezu luvela ku-movie, umculo we-Broadway, noma i-opera, isihloko somsebenzi oyinhloko lapho ingoma/ucezu oluthathwe khona singakhonjiswa. 

Uma umbhali wengoma noma umqambi aziwa, igama lakhe ngokuvamile liboniswa kanye nesihloko. Umculo weshidi ungase futhi ubonise igama lombhali wezingoma, uma amagama engoma engomunye wababhali bezingoma noma abaqambi. Ingase futhi ifake negama lomhleli, uma ingoma noma ucezu luhlelelwe ukushicilelwa. Akukho mbhali wengoma noma igama lomqambi elingaboniswa kumculo wesintu wakudala, izingoma zendabuko ezinhlotsheni ezifana ne-blues ne-bluegrass, kanye namaculo endabuko amadala kakhulu kanye nezomoya, ngoba kulo mculo, ababhali ngokuvamile abaziwa; Ezimweni ezinjalo, igama elithi "indabuko" livame ukubekwa lapho igama lomqambi lalivame ukuya khona. 

Amakhasi ezihloko zezingoma angase abe nesithombe esibonisa abalingisi, isilungiselelo, noma izehlakalo ezivela emazwini awo. Amakhasi esihloko avela ezinsimbini angase ashiye umfanekiso, ngaphandle uma umsebenzi kuwumculo wohlelo onesihloko, noma amagama ezigaba zawo, ahlotshaniswa nesilungiselelo, abalingisi, noma indaba. 

Amanothi omculo 
Uhlobo lwenothi yomculo luhluka kakhulu ngohlobo noma isitayela somculo. Emculweni omningi we-classic, umculo nezingxenye ezihambisanayo (uma zikhona) ziphawulwa emigqeni yabasebenzi abasebenzisa amakhanda amanothi ayindilinga. Emculweni weshidi lakudala, abasebenzi ngokuvamile baqukethe: 


Ikhasi elisuka kumphumela we-autograph we-Fugue No. 17 ku-A♭ enkulu evela ku-JS Bach ethi The Well-Tempered Clavier 
a clef, njenge-bass clef bass clef noma i-treble clef treble clef 
isiginesha engukhiye ebonisa ukhiye—ngokwesibonelo, isiginesha eyinhloko esetshenziswa ukhiye omkhulu noma isignesha eyinhloko ethi A♯ omncane
isiginesha yesikhathi, ngokuvamile enezinombolo ezimbili eziqondaniswe ngokuqondile nenombolo engezansi ebonisa inani lenothi elimele isigqi esisodwa kanye nenombolo ephezulu ebonisa ukuthi mangaki amabhithi kubha—ngokwesibonelo, isiginesha yesikhathi engu-2 
4 ibonisa ukuthi kunamanothi ekota amabili (ama-crotchets) ibha ngayinye. 
Izingoma eziningi nezingcezu zenkathi Yakudala (c. 1750) kuqhubeke zibonisa i-tempo yocezu kusetshenziswa isisho—ngokuvamile esingesiNtaliyane—njenge-allegro (esheshayo) noma ithuna (ehamba kancane) kanye nokuguquguquka kwayo (umsindo omkhulu noma ukuthamba). Amazwi, uma ekhona, abhalwa eduze kwamanothi omculo. Kodwa-ke, umculo wenkathi ye-Baroque (c. 1600–1750) noma izinkathi zangaphambili ungase ungabi nokumaka kwetempo noma inkomba eguqukayo. Abaculi nabaculi bangaleso sikhathi bekulindeleke ukuthi bazi ukuthi isiphi isitephu nokuzwakala okuzodlalwa noma ukucula ingoma noma isiqeshana esithile ngenxa yesipiliyoni sabo somculo nolwazi. Esikhathini samanje somculo we-classical (ikhulu lama-20 nelama-21), futhi kwezinye izimo ngaphambili (njengenkathi yezothando ezifundeni ezikhuluma isiJalimane), abaqambi babevame ukusebenzisa ulimi lwabo lwendabuko ukuze babonise izinkomba ze-tempo, esikhundleni sesiNtaliyane (isb. 

Le mithetho ye-classical notation yomculo, futhi ikakhulukazi ukusetshenziswa kweziyalezo zetempo yesiNgisi, iphinde isetshenziselwe izinguqulo zomculo weshidi wezingoma zomculo ezidumile zekhulunyaka lama-20 nelama-21. Izingoma zomculo ezidumile zivame ukukhombisa kokubili i-tempo kanye nohlobo: i-slow blues noma i-uptempo rock. Izingoma ze-Pop zivame ukuqukatha amagama ezingoma ngaphezu kwezisebenzi zisebenzisa amagama ezinhlamvu (isb., C Maj, F Maj, G7, njll.), ukuze umdlali wesigingci se-acoustic noma umshayi wopiyano akwazi ukwenza ngcono ukuhambisana kwechord. 

Kwezinye izitayela zomculo, izindlela ezihlukene zokuphawula umculo zingasetshenziswa. Ku-jazz, isibonelo, ngenkathi abadlali abaningi abachwepheshile bekwazi ukufunda "i-classical" -style notation, izingoma eziningi ze-jazz ziphawulwa kusetshenziswa amashadi ezingoma, abonisa ukuqhubeka kweculo (isb., C, A7, D minor, G7, njll.) kanye nesimo sayo. Amalungu esigaba sesigqi se-jazz (umdlali wepiyano, isigingci se-jazz nomdlali we-bassist) asebenzisa ishadi lokucula ukuze aqondise izingxenye ezihambisana nazo ezithuthukisiwe, kuyilapho izinsimbi eziholayo eqenjini le-jazz, njengomdlali we-saxophone noma i-trumpeter, zisebenzisa izinguquko ze-chord ukuze ziqondise ukuthuthukiswa kwazo eyedwa. Njengezingoma zomculo ezidumile, izingoma ze-jazz zivame ukubonisa kokubili i-tempo kanye nohlobo: i-slow blues noma i-bop esheshayo.

Abaculi beseshini yomculo wezwe abangochwepheshe bavamise ukusebenzisa umculo obhalwe ku-Nashville Number System, okhombisa ukuqhubeka kwe-chord kusetshenziswa izinombolo (lokhu kuvumela abaqondisi bebhendi ukuthi bashintshe ukhiye ngokushesha nje). Amashadi ezingoma asebenzisa amagama ezinhlamvu, izinombolo, noma izinombolo zesiRoman (isb, I–IV–V) asetshenziswa kabanzi ekuqapheliseni umculo ngama-blues, i-R&B, umculo we-rock nabaculi be-heavy metal. Amanye amashadi e-chord awanikezi noma yiluphi ulwazi olunesigqi, kodwa amanye asebenzisa ama-slashs ukuze abonise amabhithi ebha kanye nesigqi ukuze abonise "amahithi" avumelanisiwe umqambi wengoma afuna ukuthi lonke ibhendi lidlale ndawonye. Abadlali besiginci abaningi nabadlali be-bass kagesi bafunda izingoma namashuni anothi besebenzisa i-tablature, ewumfanekiso oyingcaca okufanele udlale ngawo umculi. I-"Tab" isetshenziswa kakhulu umculo we-rock nabashayi besiginci esinzima nabadlali bebhesi. Abaculi bezitayela eziningi zomculo ezidumile bafunda ingoma besebenzisa ishidi lamagama kuphela, befunda umculo nesigqi "ngendlebe" ekurekhodeni. 

Injongo futhi usebenzise 

Umculo Weshidi wengoma ethi "Oregon, My Oregon" 
Umculo Weshidi ungasetshenziswa njengerekhodi, umhlahlandlela, noma indlela yokwenza, ingoma noma ucezu lomculo. Umculo weshidi uvumela abadlali bezinsimbi abakwazi ukufunda okubhaliwe komculo (oshaya upiyano, izidlali zezinsimbi ze-orchestra, ibhendi ye-jazz, njll.) noma abaculi ukuthi bacule ingoma noma ucezu. Abafundi bomculo basebenzisa umculo weshidi ukuze bafunde ngezitayela ezahlukene nezinhlobo zomculo. Inhloso ehlosiwe ye-edishini yomculo weshidi ithinta ukwakheka kwawo nesakhiwo. Uma umculo weshidi uhloselwe izinjongo zokufunda, njengasekilasini lomlando womculo, amanothi nabasebenzi bangenziwa babe bancane futhi umhleli akudingeki akhathazeke ngokuphenduka kwamakhasi. Ukuze uthole amaphuzu okusebenza, nokho, amanothi kufanele afundeke endaweni yomculo futhi umhleli kufanele agweme ukuphenduka kwamakhasi ngokweqile futhi aqinisekise ukuthi noma yiliphi ikhasi eliphendukayo libekwe ngemva kokuphumula noma ukumisa isikhashana (uma kungenzeka). Futhi, amaphuzu noma ingxenye esencwadini enogqinsi ngeke ihlale ivuliwe, ngakho-ke amaphuzu okusebenza noma ingxenye idinga ukuba ibe nokubopha okuncane noma isebenzise ifomethi ebophezelayo ezohlala ivuliwe endaweni yokubeka umculo. 

Emculweni we-classical, ulwazi lomculo olugunyaziwe mayelana nesiqephu lungatholwa ngokutadisha imidwebo ebhaliwe nezinguqulo zakuqala zezingoma umqambi okungenzeka ukuthi uzigcinile, kanye nemiphumela yokugcina ye-autograph kanye nezimpawu zomuntu siqu ebufakazini nezikolo eziphrintiwe.

Ukuqonda umculo weshidi kudinga uhlobo olukhethekile lokufunda nokubhala: ikhono lokufunda umbhalo womculo. Ikhono lokufunda noma ukubhala umculo akuyona imfuneko yokuqamba umculo. Sekube nedlanzana labaqambi nababhali bezingoma abakwazile ukukhiqiza umculo ngaphandle kwekhono lokufunda noma ukubhala ngombhalo womculo, inqobo nje uma i-amanuensis yohlobo oluthile itholakala ukuze babhale phansi izingoma abazicabangayo. Izibonelo zifaka umqambi oyimpumputhe wangekhulunyaka le-18 uJohn Stanley kanye nababhali bezingoma bekhulu lama-20 u-Lionel Bart, u-Irving Berlin no-Paul McCartney. Futhi, ezitayeleni zomculo wesintu ezifana nomculo we-blues nomculo wesintu, baningi ababhali bezingoma abanekhono ababengakwazi ukufunda umculo, kunalokho badlale futhi bacule umculo “ngendlebe”. 

Ikhono lokufunda ukubona yikhono lomculi lokwenza umsebenzi ongajwayelekile womculo lapho ebuka umculo weshidi okokuqala ngqa. Ikhono lokufunda lilindeleke kubaculi abangochwepheshe kanye nezimfundamakhwela ezidlala umculo wakudala, i-jazz nezinye izinhlobo ezihlobene. Ikhono elicwengisiswe nakakhulu ikhono lokubuka ucezu olusha lomculo futhi uzwe iningi noma yonke imisindo (imiculo, ama-harmonies, izinsimbi, njll.) ekhanda lomuntu ngaphandle kokulidlala ingoma noma ukuyizwa idlalwa noma iculwa. Abaqambi nabadidiyeli abanekhono banaleli khono, u-Beethoven eyisibonelo esiphawulekayo somlando. 


Isikolo somqhubi nenduku 
Abaculi bakudala abadlala imisebenzi ye-orchestra, umculo wegumbi, i-sonatas nemisebenzi eculayo yamakhwaya ngokuvamile baba nomculo weshidi phambi kwabo endaweni yesitendi yomculo lapho becula (noma abanjelwe phambi kwabo kufolda yomculo, uma kuyiqembu lekwaya), ngaphandle kokudlalwa kwezinsimbi okukodwa kwezingcezu eziyedwa, amakhonsathi, izingcezu, i-opera, izingoma ezicula ngazodwana, njll. kulindeleke. Ku-jazz, ethuthukisiwe kakhulu, umculo weshidi (obizwa ngokuthi i-lead sheet kulo mongo) usetshenziselwa ukunikeza izinkomba eziyisisekelo zemiculo, izinguquko zezingoma, namalungiselelo. Ngisho noma ibhendi ye-jazz ineshidi eliholayo, ishadi lokucula noma umculo ohleliwe, izici eziningi zokusebenza ziyathuthukiswa. 

Umculo obhalwe ngesandla noma ophrintiwe awubaluleki kangako kwamanye amasiko wokwenza umculo. Kodwa-ke, ezinhlotsheni ezinjengomculo wesintu nomculo wesintu, abaculi nabadlala izinsimbi ngokuvamile bafunda izingoma "ngendlebe" noma ekubeni nengoma noma ingoma abayifundiswa ngomunye umuntu. Nakuba umculo omningi odumile ushicilelwa ngendlela ethile, kuvamile ukuba abantu bafunde ingoma beyizwa ngendlebe. Kunjalo futhi ezinhlotsheni eziningi zomculo wesintu waseNtshonalanga, lapho izingoma nemidanso idluliswa ngomlomo - kanye nesiko lokuzwayo -. Umculo wamanye amasiko, owomdabu kanye nowakudala, uvamise ukudluliselwa ngomlomo, nakuba amanye amasiko angewona awaseNtshonalanga asungula ezawo izinhlobo zomculo nowomculo weshidi.

Nakuba umculo weshidi uvame ukucatshangwa njengenkundla yomculo omusha kanye nosizo lokuqamba (okungukuthi, umqambi "ubhala" umculo phansi), ungase futhi usebenze njengerekhodi elibukwayo lomculo osuvele ukhona. Izifundiswa nabanye benze okulotshiweyo ukuze kuhunyushwe umculo waseNtshonalanga nongewona owaseNtshonalanga ngendlela efundekayo ukuze kufundwe, kuhlaziywe futhi kusebenze kabusha. Lokhu akwenziwanga kuphela ngomculo wesintu noma wesintu (isb., imiqulu kaBartók yomculo wesintu waseMagyar nowaseRomania), kodwa futhi nangemisindo erekhodiwe yokuthuthukiswa kwabaculi (isb., upiyano lwe-jazz) kanye nemidlalo okungenzeka ukuthi isekelwe kancane ekuphawuleni. Isibonelo esiphelele salokhu kwakamuva ezikhathini zamuva iqoqo elithi The Beatles: Complete Scores (London: Wise Publications, 1993), elifuna ukuguqula libe izinti futhi lihlele zonke izingoma njengoba ziqoshwe ama-Beatles ngemininingwane yezinsimbi kanye nezwi. 

Izinhlobo 
Umculo weshidi lanamuhla ungase ufike ngezindlela ezahlukene. Uma ucezu lwenzelwa insimbi eyodwa noma izwi elilodwa (njengesiqephu sensimbi eyedwa noma eyezwi elicula yedwa i-cappella), wonke umsebenzi ungase ubhalwe noma uphrintwe njengocezu olulodwa lomculo weshidi. Uma ucezu lwezinsimbi luhloselwe ukuthi lwenziwe abantu abangaphezu koyedwa, umdlali ngamunye ngokuvamile uzoba nocezu oluhlukile lomculo weshidi, olubizwa ngokuthi ingxenye, azodlala kulo. Lokhu kunjalo ikakhulukazi ekushicilelweni kwemisebenzi edinga abadlali abangaphezu kwabane, nakuba njalo amaphuzu aphelele abuye ashicilelwe. Izingxenye eziculwa emsebenzini wephimbo azivamile ukukhishwa ngokwehlukana emisebenzini yesimanje, nakuba lokhu kwakunjalo ngokomlando, ikakhulukazi ngaphambi kokuba ukunyatheliswa komculo kwenze ukuthi umculo weshidi utholakale kabanzi. 

Umculo weshidi ungakhishwa njengezicucu zomuntu ngamunye noma imisebenzi (isibonelo, ingoma ethandwayo noma i-Beethoven sonata), emaqoqweni (ngokwesibonelo isebenza ngumqambi oyedwa noma abambalwa), njengezingcezu ezenziwe umculi onikeziwe, njll. 

Lapho izingxenye ezihlukene zezinsimbi nezezwi zomsebenzi womculo zinyatheliswa ndawonye, umculo weshidi owumphumela ubizwa ngokuthi amaphuzu. Ngokwejwayelekile, amaphuzu aqukethe amanothi omculo anengxenye ngayinye yezinsimbi noma yezwi ekuqondaneni okuqondile (okusho ukuthi izehlakalo ezifanayo kumbhalo wengxenye ngayinye zihlelwa ngokuhambisana). Igama elithi score liphinde lasetshenziselwa ukubhekisela kumculo weshidi obhalelwe umculi oyedwa kuphela. Umehluko phakathi kwamaphuzu nengxenye usebenza uma kunengxenye engaphezu kweyodwa edingekayo ekusebenzeni. 

Izikolo ziza ngamafomethi ahlukahlukene. 


Ikhasi lokuqala lamaphuzu agcwele e-Max Reger's Der 100. Ihubo lekwaya, i-orchestra ne-ogani 
Amaphuzu agcwele, okuhlukile, nokufingqa
Amaphuzu aphelele yincwadi enkulu ebonisa umculo wazo zonke izinsimbi noma amazwi ekwakhiweni akleliswe ngokulandelana okungashintshi. Inkulu ngokwanele ukuba umqhubi akwazi ukufunda ngenkathi eqondisa izivivinyo ze-orchestra noma i-opera kanye nokudlalwa. Ngokungeziwe ekusebenziseni kwabo ngendlela engokoqobo ama-conductor aholayo ama-ensembles, amaphuzu aphelele abuye asetshenziswe ochwepheshe bomculo, izazi zomculo, abaqambi kanye nabafundi bomculo abafunda umsebenzi othile. 

Isikolo esincane sifana nesikolo esigcwele kodwa esincishwe kakhulu ngosayizi. Incane kakhulu ukuthi ingasetshenziswa uma uqhuba, kodwa iwusizo ekufundeni ucezu lomculo, noma ngabe oweqoqo elikhulu noma umculi ohamba yedwa. Isikolo esincane singaqukatha amazwi ayisingeniso. 

Amaphuzu ocwaningo kwesinye isikhathi anosayizi ofanayo, futhi ngokuvamile awahlukaniseki, amaphuzu amancane, ngaphandle kwegama. Amanye amaphuzu ocwaningo awusayizi we-octavo ngakho-ke asendaweni ethile phakathi kosayizi bamaphuzu aphelele nabancane. Isikolo socwaningo, ikakhulukazi uma siyingxenye ye-anthology yocwaningo lwezemfundo, singafaka ukuphawula okwengeziwe mayelana nomculo nokumaka ngezinjongo zokufunda. 

Isikolo sepiyano (noma ukuncishiswa kwepiyano) ukulotshwa okungokoqobo okungaphezulu noma okuncane kwephiyano yocezu oluhloselwe izingxenye eziningi ezidlalwayo, ikakhulukazi imisebenzi ye-orchestra; lokhu kungafaka izingxenye zezinsimbi ngaphakathi kwemisebenzi emikhulu yezwi (bona amaphuzu ephimbo ngokushesha ngezansi). Amalungiselelo anjalo enzelwe i-piano solo (izandla ezimbili) noma i-duet yepiyano (ipiyano eyodwa noma ezimbili, izandla ezine). Izinti ezincane ezengeziwe ngezinye izikhathi zengezwa emaphuzwini athile kumaphuzu wepiyano ngezandla ezimbili ukuze kwenziwe isethulo siphelele, nakuba ngokuvamile kungenangqondo noma kungenzeki ukuzifaka ngenkathi udlala. 

Njengomphumela wephimbo (ngezansi), kudinga ikhono elikhulu ukwehlisa amaphuzu e-okhestra abe amafomu amancane kangako ngoba ukuncipha akudingi ukudlaleka kukhibhodi kuphela kodwa futhi nokucophelela ngokwanele ekwethulweni kwayo kokuvumelana okuhlosiwe, indlela yokwenza, imifanekiso, njll. Ngezinye izikhathi amamaki afakiwe ukuze abonise ukuthi yiziphi izinsimbi ezidlalayo kumaphuzu athile. 

Nakuba izikolo zepiyano ngokuvamile zingahloselwe ukusebenza ngaphandle kwesifundo nenjabulo (okulotshiweyo kwekhonsathi kaFranz Liszt yama-symphonies ka-Beethoven eyiqembu elilodwa lezinto ezihlukile eziphawulekayo), ama-ballet athola inzuzo ewusizo kakhulu kumaphuzu wepiyano ngoba ngomdlali wopiyano oyedwa noma ababili avumela i-ballet ukuthi yenze izivivinyo eziningi ngenani eliphansi kakhulu, ngaphambi kokuba i-orchestra iqashwe kabusha. Amaphuzu epiyano angasetshenziswa futhi ukuqeqesha abaqhubi bepiyano abaqalayo, abangakwazi ukuqhuba umdlali wopiyano odlala ukuncishiswa kwepiyano ye-symphony; lokhu kubiza kancane kakhulu kunokudlala i-orchestra ephelele. Izikolo zepiyano zama-opera azifaki izinti ezihlukene zezingxenye zezwi, kodwa zingangeza umbhalo oculwa nezikhombisi-ndlela zesiteji ngaphezu komculo.

Ingxenye iyisiqephu esisuka kumaphuzu aphelele ensimbi ethile. Isetshenziswa abadlali be-orchestra ekusebenzeni, lapho amaphuzu aphelele angaba nzima kakhulu. Kodwa-ke, ekusebenzeni, kungaba idokhumenti enkulu uma umsebenzi umude, futhi insimbi ethile idlala ingxenye enkulu yesikhathi sayo. 


Ingcaphuno yamaphuzu wephiyano-izwi le-opera ka-César Cui u-William Ratcliff. Dlalaⓘ 
Amaphuzu ephimbo 
Amaphuzu ephimbo (noma, ngokufanelekile, amaphuzu ephiyano) ukuncishiswa kwamaphuzu aphelele omsebenzi wezwi (isb, i-opera, umculo, i-oratorio, i-cantata, njll.) ukukhombisa izingxenye zephimbo (eyodwa nekhwaya) ezintini zazo kanye nezingxenye ze-okhestra ekuncishisweni kwepiyano (imvamisa yezandla ezimbili) ngaphansi; izingxenye ze-orchestra kuphela zesikolo nazo ziyancishiswa zepiyano. Uma ingxenye yomsebenzi i-cappella, ukuncishiswa kwepiyano kwezingxenye zezwi kuvame ukungezwa ukuze kusize ekuziqeqesheni (lokhu kuvame ukuba njalo ngomculo weshidi lezenkolo le-cappella). 

Izikolo zepiyano nezwi zisebenza njengendlela elula yokuthi abacula yedwa nabacula umculo bafunde umculo futhi bazilolonge ngokuhlukene ne-orchestra. Umphumela wezwi lomculo ngokuvamile awubandakanyi ingxoxo ekhulunyiwe, ngaphandle kwezimpawu. Izikolo zepiyano-vocal zisetshenziselwa ukuhlinzeka ngokuphelezelwa upiyano ngokudlalwa kwama-opera, umculo nama-oratorio ngamaqembu asebemnkantshubomvu kanye namaqembu athile asezingeni elincane. Lokhu kungenziwa ngumdlali wepiyano oyedwa noma abadlali bepiyano ababili. Ngomculo wenkathi yama-2000s, abadlali bekhibhodi bangase badlale ama-synthesizer esikhundleni sepiyano. 

Amaphuzu amakhwaya ahlobene kodwa angajwayelekile kakhulu aqukethe izingxenye zamakhwaya ezihambisana nokuncipha. 

Isilinganiso sezitho esiqhathanisekayo sikhona futhi, ngokuvamile ngokuhambisana nomculo wesonto wamaphimbo ne-orchestra, njengamalungiselelo (ngezandla zakamuva) kaMesiya we-Handel. Kufana nomculo wepiyano ngoba uhlanganisa izinti zezingxenye zezwi futhi unciphisa izingxenye ze-ochestra ezidlalwa umuntu oyedwa. Ngokungafani nemiphumela yephimbo, amaphuzu esitho ngezinye izikhathi ahloselwe umhleli ukuthi abambele i-orchestra ekusebenzeni uma kunesidingo. 

Iqoqo lezingoma zomculo othile ngokuvamile liphrintwa ngaphansi kwelebula yokukhetha amagama. Lokhu kuhlukile kumphumela wephimbo wohlelo olufanayo ngoba awethuli umculo ophelele, futhi okuhambisana nopiyano kuvame ukwenziwa lula futhi kufaka phakathi umugqa womculo. 

Ezinye izinhlobo
Isikolo esifushane siwukuncishiswa komsebenzi wezinsimbi eziningi ukuze kube izinti ezimbalwa. Kunokuba baqambe ngokuqondile amaphuzu aphelele, abaqambi abaningi benza uhlobo oluthile lwamaphuzu amafushane ngenkathi beqamba futhi kamuva banweba i-orchestration ephelele. I-opera, isibonelo, ingase ibhalwe kuqala ngamaphuzu amafushane, bese kuba amaphuzu aphelele, bese yehliselwa kumphumela wephimbo wokuprakthiza. Amaphuzu amafushane awavamile ukushicilelwa; zingase zijwayeleke kakhulu kwamanye ama-ensemble (isb, ibhendi) kunakwamanye. Ngenxa yobunjalo bawo bokuqala, amaphuzu amafushane ayiphoyinti eliyinhloko lenkomba yabaqambi abafisa ukuqedela umsebenzi ongakaqedwa womunye (isb. Ukunyakaza 2 kuya ku-5 kwe-10th Symphony ka-Gustav Mahler noma isenzo sesithathu se-opera Lulu ka-Alban Berg). 

Amaphuzu avulekile amaphuzu esiqeshana se-polyphonic esibonisa izwi ngalinye kubasebenzi abahlukene. Ezingcezu zekhibhodi ye-Renaissance noma ye-Baroque, amaphuzu avuliwe wezinti ezine ngezinye izikhathi ayesetshenziswa esikhundleni somhlangano wesimanje kakhulu womsebenzi oyedwa ngesandla ngasinye.[1] Kubuye futhi ngezinye izikhathi kufane namaphuzu aphelele (okungase kube nengxenye engaphezu kweyodwa ngabasebenzi). 

Emaphuzwini aseduze, zonke izingxenye zezwi zimelelwe ezintongeni ezimbili ezinkulu (i-treble ne-bass stick). 

Imiphumela yesikhathi se-Baroque (c.1600–1750) ivamise ukuba sesimweni somugqa webhesi ku-bass clef kanye nemiculo edlalwa insimbi noma eculwa phezulu (noma izinti) ku-treble clef. I-bass line ngokuvamile yayinezibalo ezibhalwe ngenhla kwamanothi e-bass abonisa ukuthi yiziphi izikhawu ezingenhla kwe-bass (isb., ama-chords) okufanele adlalwe, indlela ebizwa ngokuthi ama-bass figured. Izibalo zibonisa ukuthi yiziphi izikhawu umculi we-harpsichord, i-oganist yepayipi noma umdlali welute okufanele adlale ngaphezu kwenothi ngayinye yebhesi. 


Ishidi eliholayo lengoma ethi "Trifle in Pyjamas" libonisa kuphela izimpawu zomculo nezingoma. Ukuze udlale le ngoma, abaculi besigaba sesigqi sebhendi ye-jazz bangathuthukisa ukuphinyiswa kwezwi kanye ne-bassline besebenzisa izimpawu zokucula. Izinsimbi zomculo eziholayo, njenge-sax noma i-trumpet, zingathuthukisa imihlobiso ukuze zenze umculo uthakazelise, bese zithuthukisa ingxenye eyedwa. 
Umculo odumile 
Ishidi lokuhola licacisa kuphela umculo, amagama ezinhlamvu nokuvumelana, kusetshenziswa induku eyodwa enezimpawu zamaculo abekwe ngenhla namagama ezinhlamvu ngezansi. Ivamise ukusetshenziswa emculweni odumile kanye ne-jazz ukuze ithwebule izici ezibalulekile zengoma ngaphandle kokucacisa imininingwane yokuthi ingoma kufanele ihlelwe noma iculwe kanjani. 

Ishadi lokucula (noma kalula nje, ishadi) liqukethe ulwazi oluncane lomculo noma alunalo nhlobo kodwa linikeza ulwazi olubalulekile lwe-harmonic. Amanye amashadi e-chord aphinde abonise isigqi okufanele sidlalwe, ikakhulukazi uma kukhona uchungechunge oluvumelanisiwe "lokushaya" umhleli afuna ukuthi sonke isigaba sesigqi senze. Uma kungenjalo, amashadi e-chord angashiya isigqi singenalutho noma abonise ukusika kusigqi ngasinye.

Lolu uhlobo oluvame kakhulu lomculo obhaliwe olusetshenziswa abaculi baseseshini abangochwepheshe abadlala i-jazz noma ezinye izinhlobo zomculo odumile futhi kuhloselwe isigaba sesigqi (esivame ukuqukatha upiyano, isiginci, ibhesi nezigubhu) ukuze kuthuthukiswe okuhambisana nazo kanye nanoma yibaphi abacula yedwa abathuthukayo (isb, abadlali be-saxophone noma abadlali becilongo) ukuze basebenzise imigqa yabo njengereferensi. 

Incwadi mbumbulu iqoqo lezingoma ze-jazz namashuni anezici eziyisisekelo zomculo onikeziwe. Kunezinhlobo ezimbili zezincwadi zomgunyathi: (1) amaqoqo amashidi omthofu, ahlanganisa ingoma, izingoma zokucula, nezosha (uma zikhona), kanye (2) namaqoqo ezingoma namashuni anamaculo kuphela. Izincwadi zomgunyathi eziqukethe izingoma kuphela zisetshenziswa abadlali besigaba sesigqi (ikakhulukazi abaculi abadlala i-chord njengabashayi besigingci sikagesi nezidlali zepiyano kanye nomshayi webhesi) ukusiza ukuqondisa ukwenziwa kwabo ngcono kwezingxenye ezihambisana nengoma. Amabhuku mbumbulu anama-chords kuphela angasetshenziswa izinsimbi zomthofu (isb, i-saxophone noma i-trumpet) njengomhlahlandlela wokudlala kwawodwa okuthuthukisiwe. Njengoba ingoma ingafakiwe ezincwadini zomgunyathi ezinezingoma kuphela, abadlali bezinsimbi eziholayo kulindeleke ukuthi bawazi lowo mculo. 


Isilinganiso esikhulu ku-note evamile (ngenhla) kanye nethebula lethebula lesiginci (ngezansi) 
Ithebhulature (noma ithebhu) iwuhlobo olukhethekile lwamaphuzu omculo - ngokuvamile kakhulu ensimbini eyedwana - ebonisa ukuthi kufanele kudlalwa kuphi izingoma ensimbini enikeziwe kunokuba kukhiqizwe amaphimbo, anesigqi esibonisiwe futhi. I-Tablature isetshenziswa kakhulu ezingomeni zesiginci kanye ne-bass kagesi nezingcezu ezinhlotsheni zomculo ezidumile njengomculo we-rock nomculo we-heavy metal. Lolu hlobo lokubhala lwaqala ukusetshenziswa ngasekupheleni kweNkathi Ephakathi, futhi luye lwasetshenziselwa ikhibhodi (isb., isitho sepayipi) kanye nezinsimbi zomculo ezinezintambo (ilute, isiginci).[2] 

Amashidi ezingoma 
Amashidi ezingoma angamagama aphrintiwe ngaphandle kokuphawula komculo. Izifundo zezemfundo zomculo waseMelika zibiza lawa mashidi ngamaculo ezingoma.[3]: 25 Engxenyeni yokuqala yekhulu lama-20, amagama ezingoma ezingomeni anyatheliswa futhi athengiswa ngawodwana, ngamaqoqo emakhasini alingana nephephandaba, ahlanganiswe abe izincwajana, nakomagazini.[3]: 53–54 Amashidi ezingoma ngokuvamile ayehlanganisa izithombe zabajabulisi abadumile ezihlobene nengoma nomculo we-5 kanye nomculo we-5. 

Amashidi ezingoma aqashelwa njengokuncintisana kushidi lomculo yi-American Society of Composers, Authors and Publishers (ASCAP) ngo-1930, lapho ummeleli ethi, "Izinkulungwane manje zifunda izingoma ezidumile emsakazweni, abashicileli bathi. Njengoba amagama atholakalayo ngamasenti amahlanu noma ayishumi kanye nokucindezeleka okwaziwayo, umfutho wokuthenga umculo weshidi uyaqedwa." Nakuba umculo weshidi wengoma ungase ubize amasenti angamashumi amathathu noma angamashumi amathathu nanhlanu, ishidi lezingoma ngokuvamile lithengiswa nge-nickel noma i-dime. Izinhlangano zamakhwaya zingathengela umdlali wopiyano ikhophi eyodwa yomculo weshidi bese kuba amashidi ezingoma amaningi zabaculi.[3]: 55  

Uma amagama ezinhlamvu ephrintwa ngaphandle kwemvume evela kumnikazi welungelo lokukopisha, amashidi ezingoma abizwa ngokuthi amashidi ezingoma ze-bootleg. Ukubhucungwa kweshidi lezingoma kwabonwa njengenkinga encane e-Chicago ekuqaleni kwawo-1890, kodwa kwaba yinkinga ebalulekile kusukela ngo-1929 kuya ngawo-1930.[3]: 25–26 Abashicileli bokuqala nabasabalalisi bamashidi ezingoma ze-bootleg babekwe icala lokwephulwa kwelungelo lobunikazi ngo-February, 1930 Ngokusebenzisa Imizamo Yokushicilelwa Kwezomculo Ka-30 [3]: : 30: ukuphoqelelwa, kanye nokufika komagazini beshidi lezingoma ezisemthethweni, ukubhucungwa kweshidi lezingoma kwaphela ekuqaleni kwawo-1940.[3]: 39–40  

Omagazini bokuqala beshidi lengoma abasemthethweni baqala ngo-1934, kanye ne-Lyle Engel's Song Hits eyashicilelwa okokuqala ngo-1937 yaba yimpumelelo amashumi eminyaka yokukhangisa i-Songsp, 41 ukubuyekezwa, kanye nezincwadi zomlando ezikhangisayo zosaziwayo.[3]: 69  

Umlando 
Ozandulelayo kushidi lomculo 
Ukuqanjwa komculo kwasungulwa ngaphambi kokuba kusetshenziswe isikhumba noma iphepha ukuze kubhalwe. Indlela yokuqala yokuqanjwa komculo ingatholakala kuthebhulethi ye-cuneiform eyakhiwa e-Nippur, e-Sumer (i-Iraq yanamuhla), cishe ngo-2000 BC. Ithebhulethi imelela iziyalezo eziyizicucu zokudlalwa komculo, okubonisa ukuthi wenziwe ngokuvumelana kwengxenye yesithathu kusetshenziswa isikali se-diatonic.[4] 

Ithebhulethi cishe yango-1250 BC ikhombisa indlela yokubhala ethuthuke kakhulu.[5] Nakuba ukuchazwa kwesimiso sokubhalwa kwamagama kuseyimpikiswano, kusobala ukuthi le ncaphuno ibonisa amagama ezintambo kuhabhu, ukuhlelwa kwazo okuchazwe kwezinye izibhebhe.[6] Nakuba ziyizicucu, lawa maphilisi amelela imiculo yakudala eyaziwayo etholakala noma kuphi emhlabeni.[6] 


Itshe loqobo e-Delphi eliqukethe elesibili lamaculo e-Delphic aya ku-Apollo. I-notation yomculo iwumugqa wezimpawu zezikhathi ezithile ngenhla komugqa oyinhloko, ongaphazamiseki wezinhlamvu zesiGreki. 
Umbhalo wasendulo womculo wamaGreki wawusetshenziswa kusukela okungenani ekhulwini lesi-6 BC kuze kube cishe ngekhulu lesi-4 AD; ukuqanjwa okuningana okuphelele nezingcezwana zezingoma ezisebenzisa lesi sisho ziyasinda. I-notation iqukethe izimpawu ezibekwe ngenhla kwamagama ombhalo. Isibonelo sokwakheka okuphelele yi-Seikilos epitaph, eye yahlelwa ngokuhlukahluka phakathi kwekhulu lesi-2 BC kuya ekhulwini lokuqala AD.
 
Emculweni wamaGreki asendulo, amahubo amathathu kaMesomede waseKrethe akhona embhalweni wesandla. Esinye sezibonelo ezindala kunazo zonke ezaziwayo zenothi yomculo isiqeshana se-papyrus se-Hellenic era play i-Orestes (408 BC), equkethe amazwibela omculo we-choral ode. Imibhalo yasendulo yamaGreki ibonakala ingasasebenzi ngesikhathi sokuwohloka koMbuso WaseRoma. 

Imibhalo yesandla yaseNtshonalanga 
Ngaphambi kwekhulu le-15, umculo waseNtshonalanga wawubhalwa ngesandla futhi ulondolozwe emibhalweni yesandla, ngokuvamile eboshwe ngemiqulu emikhulu. Izibonelo ezaziwa kakhulu zenothi yomculo yeNkathi Ephakathi imibhalo yesandla yenkathi ephakathi yengoma ye-monophonic. I-Chant notation ibonise amanothi omculo wengoma, kodwa ngaphandle kwenkomba yesigqi. Endabeni ye-polyphony ye-Medieval, njenge-motet, izingxenye zazibhalwe ngezingxenye ezihlukene zamakhasi abheke. Le nqubo yasizwa ukufika kwe-mensural notation, ephinde yabonisa isigqi futhi yahambisana nomkhuba wenkathi ephakathi wokuhlanganisa izingxenye ze-polyphony ngokulandelana, kunokuba ngesikhathi esisodwa (njengasezikhathini zakamuva). Imibhalo yesandla ebonisa izingxenye ndawonye ngefomethi yamaphuzu ibingavamile futhi ilinganiselwe kakhulu ku-organum, ikakhulukazi leyo yesikole sase-Notre Dame. NgeNkathi Ephakathi, uma u-Abbess efuna ukuba nekhophi yokuqanjwa okukhona, okufana nokuqanjwa kuka-Abbess kwelinye idolobha, kwakuzodingeka aqashe umkopishi ukuze enze umsebenzi ngesandla, okwakuzoba inqubo ende futhi engaholela emaphutheni okulotshwa. 

Ngisho nangemva kokufika kokunyathelisa komculo maphakathi nawo-1400, umculo omningi waqhubeka ukhona emibhalweni yesandla ebhalwe ngesandla yabaqambi kwaze kwaba sekhulwini le-18. 

Ukuphrinta 
Bheka futhi: Umlando wokushicilela umculo kanye nokuqoshwa komculo 
ngekhulu le-15
Kube khona ubunzima obuningi ekuhumusheni ubuchwepheshe obusha bokunyathelisa emculweni. Encwadini yokuqala ephrintiwe ehlanganisa umculo, i-Mainz Psalter (1457), ingoma yomculo (kokubili imigqa yabasebenzi namanothi) yengezwe ngesandla. Lokhu kufana negumbi elishiywe kwamanye ama-incunabula osonhlamvukazi. I-psalter yanyatheliswa eMainz, eJalimane, nguJohann Fust noPeter Schöffer, futhi enye manje ihlala eWindsor Castle enye eMtatsheni Wezincwadi WaseBrithani. Kamuva, kwanyatheliswa imigqa yezisebenzi, kodwa ababhali basanezelwa kuwo wonke omunye umculo ngesandla. Ubunzima obukhulu bokusebenzisa uhlobo olunyakazayo ukuphrinta umculo ukuthi zonke izici kufanele zihambisane - ikhanda lenothi kufanele lihambisane kahle nabasebenzi. Emculweni wephimbo, umbhalo kufanele uhambisane namanothi afanele (nakuba ngalesi sikhathi, ngisho nasemibhalweni yesandla, lokhu bekungeyona into ebaluleke kakhulu). 

Ukuqoshwa komculo kuwubuciko bokudweba notation yomculo ngekhwalithi ephezulu ngenhloso yokukhiqiza kabusha ngomshini. Umculo wokuqala onyathelisiwe ngomshini wavela cishe ngo-1473, cishe eminyakeni engu-20 ngemva kokuba uGutenberg ethule umshini wokunyathelisa. Ngo-1501, u-Ottaviano Petrucci washicilela i-Harmonice Musices Odhecaton A, eyayiqukethe izingcezu ezingu-96 zomculo ophrintiwe. Indlela kaPetrucci yokunyathelisa yakhiqiza umculo ohlanzekile, ofundekayo, nonhle, kodwa kwakuyinqubo ende, enzima eyayidinga amaphasi amathathu ahlukene emshinini wokunyathelisa. Kamuva uPetrucci wenza inqubo eyayidinga amaphasi amabili kuphela emaphephandabeni. Kodwa bekusakhokhiswa intela njengoba iphasi ngalinye lalidinga ukuqondanisa okunembe kakhulu ukuze umphumela ufundeke (okungukuthi, ukuze izinhloko zenothi zikleliswe ngendlela efanele nemigqa yabasebenzi). Lona bekuwumculo wokuqala we-polyphonic owasatshalaliswa kahle. I-Petrucci iphinde yanyathelisa ithebhu yokuqala enohlobo olususwayo. Ukunyathelisa okunomfanekiso owodwa, lapho imigqa namanothi ezisebenzi kwakunganyatheliswa khona ngephasi elilodwa, kwaqala ukuvela eLondon cishe ngo-1520. UPierre Attaingnant waqala ukusetshenziswa kakhulu le nqubo ngo-1528, futhi ayizange ishintshe iminyaka engu-200. 


I-Frontispiece kuya ku-Petrucci's Odhecaton noma i-Harmonice Musices Odhecaton 
Ifomethi evamile yokukhipha umculo onezingxenye eziningi, wepholyphonic ngesikhathi seRenaissance kwakuyizincwadi. Kule fomethi, ingxenye yezwi ngayinye yeqoqo lama-madrigal anezingxenye ezinhlanu, ngokwesibonelo, izophrintwa ngokuhlukana encwadini yayo, ukuze kuzodingeka zonke izincwadi ezinhlanu ukuze kuculwe umculo. Ama-partbook afanayo angasetshenziswa abahlabeleli noma abadlali bezinsimbi. Izikolo zomculo onezingxenye eziningi zazingavamile ukuphrintwa ku-Renaissance, nakuba ukusetshenziswa kwefomethi yamaphuzu njengendlela yokuqamba izingxenye ngesikhathi esisodwa (kunokuba zilandelane, njengasekupheleni kweNkathi Ephakathi) kunikezwa u-Josquin des Prez, umqambi womculo wokuvuselela kabusha.

Umphumela womculo onyathelisiwe wawufana nomphumela wegama elinyathelisiwe, ngokuthi ukwaziswa kwasakazwa ngokushesha, ngokuphumelelayo, ngezindleko eziphansi, nakubantu abaningi kunokuba bekungenzeka ngemibhalo yesandla ekopishwe ngokuzikhandla. Kube nomthelela owengeziwe wokukhuthaza abaculi abayizimfundamakhwela abanekhono elanele, abase bekwazi ukucula umculo weshidi. Lokhu ngezindlela eziningi kwaba nomthelela kuyo yonke imboni yomculo. Abaqambi manje sebengakwazi ukubhala umculo owengeziwe wabaculi abayizimfundamakhwela, bazi ukuthi ungase usatshalaliswe futhi udayiselwe abantu abaphakathi. 

Lokhu kwakusho ukuthi abaqambi kwakungadingeki bathembele kuphela ekuxhasweni yizikhulu ezicebile. Abadlali abangochwepheshe bangaba nomculo owengeziwe futhi bangafinyelela umculo ovela emazweni ahlukene. Yandisa isibalo sezimfundamakhwela, ivumela abadlali abakhokhelwayo ukuthi bathole imali ngokubafundisa. Noma kunjalo, eminyakeni yokuqala, izindleko zomculo onyathelisiwe zanciphisa ukusatshalaliswa kwawo. Esinye isici esanciphisa ithonya lomculo onyathelisiwe ukuthi ezindaweni eziningi, igunya lokunyathelisa umculo lalinikezwa inkosi, futhi yilabo kuphela ababenesimiso esikhethekile ababevunyelwa ukuba benze kanjalo, okubenza babe bodwa. Lokhu kwakuvame ukuhlonishwa (kanye nenzuzo yezomnotho) enikezwa abaculi basenkantolo abathandwayo noma abaqambi. 

Ikhulu le-16 

Isibonelo somculo weshidi lekhulu le-16 kanye nokuphawula komculo. Ingcaphuno embhalweni wesandla othi "Muziek voor 4 korige diatonische cister".[7] 
Mechanical plate eqoshiwe yasungulwa ngasekupheleni kwekhulu leshumi nesithupha.[8] Nakuba ukuqoshwa kwepuleti kwakusetshenziswe kusukela ekuqaleni kwekhulu leshumi nanhlanu ekudaleni ubuciko obubonakalayo namamephu, akuzange kusetshenziswe emculweni kwaze kwaba ngu-1581.[8] Ngale ndlela, isithombe sesibuko sekhasi eliphelele lomculo sasiqoshwe epuletini lensimbi. Uyinki wabe esefakwa emiseleni, futhi umbhalo womculo wawudluliselwa ephepheni. Amapuleti ensimbi ayengagcinwa futhi asetshenziswe kabusha, okwakwenza le ndlela yaba inketho ekhangayo kubaqophi bomculo. Ithusi kwakuyinsimbi yokuqala ekhethwayo kumapuleti okuqala, kodwa ngekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalombili, i-pewter yaba into evamile ngenxa yokonakala kwayo nezindleko eziphansi.[9] 

Ukuqoshwa kwepuleti kwakuyindlela ekhethwayo yokunyathelisa umculo kwaze kwaba sekupheleni kwekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalolunye, lapho ukwehla kwawo kwasheshiswa ukuthuthukiswa kobuchwepheshe bezithombe.[8] Noma kunjalo, le nqubo isekhona nanamuhla futhi isasetshenziswa abashicileli abakhethiwe njengoG. Henle Verlag eJalimane.[10]

Njengoba ukuqanjwa komculo kwanda ngobunkimbinkimbi, kanjalo nobuchwepheshe obabudingeka ukuze kukhiqizwe amaphuzu anembile omculo. Ngokungafani nokunyathelisa kwezincwadi, okuqukethe ngokuyinhloko amagama aphrintiwe, umdwebo womculo udlulisela izinhlobo eziningana zokwaziswa ngesikhathi esisodwa. Ukuze kucace kubaculi, kubalulekile ukuthi amasu okuqopha avumele ukunemba okuphelele. Amanothi ezingoma, izimpawu eziguqukayo, nokunye ukuphawula kuhambisana nokunemba okuqondile. Uma umbhalo ufakiwe, uhlamvu ngalunye luhambisana ngokuqondile nomculo oluwabelwe. Ngokuvundlile, ukuhlukaniswa kwezingqimba akuphawulwa nje kuphela ngamafulege nemishayo, kodwa futhi nesikhala esihlobene phakathi kwakho ekhasini.[8] Ukuhleleka kokwenza amakhophi anembayo alethe izinkinga ezimbalwa kubaqophi bomculo bokuqala, futhi kuholele ekuthuthukisweni kobuchwepheshe bokuqopha umculo obuningi. 

Ikhulu le-19 
Ikhulu lama-20 nasekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-21
 
zesifunda sokushicilela umculo se-Tin Pan Alley eNew York City ngo-1910.[11]
Ngekhulu le-19, imboni yomculo yayibuswa abashicileli bomculo weshidi. Maphakathi nekhulu leminyaka, ukulawulwa kwe-copyright kwemiculo kwakungeqinile, futhi abashicileli babevame ukuphrinta izinguqulo zabo zezingoma ezazidumile ngaleso sikhathi. Abanye abaqambi, abafana no-JN Pattison, baphikisa ngokushicilela umculo wabo weshidi. UPattison ubesebenza egunjini lokuthengisa upiyano nezitho zomzimba e-Union Square edolobheni laseManhattan. Ngemuva kuka-1885, ukushicilelwa komculo waseNew York kwakubuswa iqembu lababhali bezingoma nabaqambi abaziwa ngokuthi i-Tin Pan Alley. Ngemithetho eqinile yokuvikela i-copyright ngasekupheleni kwekhulu leminyaka, ababhali bezingoma, abaqambi, abahlabeleli, nabashicileli baqala ukusebenza ndawonye ukuze bazuze bobabili ngokwezimali. Abashicileli baseNew York City bagxile emculweni wephimbo. Izindlu ezinkulu zomculo zazakhela eDolobheni laseNew York, kodwa abashicileli abancane bendawo - abavame ukuxhunyaniswa namaphrinta ezentengiselwano noma izitolo zomculo - baqhubeka nokuchuma ezweni lonke. Inani elingavamile labafuduki baseMpumalanga Yurophu laba abashicileli nababhali bezingoma ku-Tin Pan Alley—owayedume kakhulu u-Irving Berlin. Ababhali bezingoma abasebe ngabadidiyeli bezingoma abaphumelelayo baqashwa ukuthi babe ngabasebenzi bezindlu zomculo. 

E-United States, imboni yomculo weshidi yaphakama ngokuhambisana ne-blackface minstrelsy, kanye nomculo we-parlor. Ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19 kwaba nokuqhuma okukhulu komculo we-parlor, nobunikazi, nekhono lokudlala upiyano liba yi-de rigueur yomndeni wezinga eliphakathi. Ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19, uma umndeni wezinga eliphakathi ufuna ukuzwa iculo noma ucezu olusha oludumile, wawuthenga ishidi lomculo bese ucula ingoma noma ucezu ngendlela eyimfundamakhwela ekhaya lawo. Kodwa ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20 igilamafoni nomculo oqoshiwe kwakhula kakhulu. Lokhu, kuhlanganiswe nokwanda kokuthandwa kokusakaza emsakazweni kusukela ngawo-1920 kuqhubeke, kwehlisa ukubaluleka kwabashicileli bomculo weshidi. Imboni yokuqopha yagcina ithathe indawo yabashicileli bomculo njengamandla amakhulu embonini yomculo. 

Ngasekupheleni kwekhulu lama-20 kanye nekhulu lama-21, isithakazelo esibalulekile sesithuthukile ekumeleleni umculo weshidi ngefomethi efundeka ngekhompuyutha (bona isofthiwe yokuphawula umculo), kanye namafayela alandekayo. I-Music OCR, isofthiwe "yokufunda" umculo weshidi eliskeniwe ukuze imiphumela isetshenziswe, ibilokhu itholakala kusukela ngo-1991. 

Ngo-1998, umculo weshidi elibonakalayo waguqukela kulokho okwakuzobizwa ngokuthi umculo weshidi ledijithali, okwakungokokuqala ngqa wavumela abashicileli ukuthi benze umculo weshidi lelungelo lobunikazi utholakale ukuze uthengwe ku-inthanethi. Ngokungafani nozakwabo bamakhophi aqinile, lawa mafayela avumele ukukhohliswa okufana nokushintshwa kwezinsimbi, ukuguqulwa kanye nokudlala kwe-MIDI (Musical Instrument Digital Interface). Ukuduma kwalolu hlelo lokulethwa okusheshayo phakathi kwabaculi kukhuthaze ukukhula kwemboni entsha kusukela ngasekupheleni kwawo-1990.
 
Uhlelo lwangaphambili lwekhompuyutha olutholakala kumakhompyutha asekhaya kwakuyi-Music Construction Set, eyasungulwa ngo-1984 futhi yakhishelwa izinkundla eziningana ezahlukene. Yethula imiqondo engaziwa kakhulu kumsebenzisi wasekhaya wangaleso sikhathi, ivumele ukukhohliswa kwamanothi nezimpawu ngedivayisi yokukhomba njengegundane; umsebenzisi "angabamba" inothi noma uphawu kuphalethi futhi "aluwise" kubasebenzi endaweni efanele. Uhlelo lwaluvumela ukudlalwa komculo okhiqiziwe ngamakhadi omsindo ahlukahlukene asekuqaleni, futhi lungaphrinta amaphuzu omculo ephrinta yezithombe. 

Imikhiqizo eminingi yesofthiwe yesikhungo sokusebenza somsindo wedijithali yesimanje kanye nababhala amaphuzu kumakhompuyutha omuntu siqu avamile isekela ukukhiqizwa komculo weshidi kusukela kumafayela e-MIDI, kungaba ngomdlali odlala amanothi ngekhibhodi efakwe i-MIDI noma esinye isilawuli se-MIDI, noma ngokufaka ngesandla usebenzisa igundane noma enye idivayisi yekhompyutha. 

Ngo-1999, uhlelo nendlela yokuxhumanisa ukuboniswa komculo phakathi kwabadlali be-orchestra yayinelungelo lobunikazi ngu-Harry Connick Jr. [12] Kuyidivayisi enesikrini sekhompuyutha esetshenziselwa ukukhombisa umculo weshidi kubaculi be-orchestra esikhundleni sephepha elisetshenziswa kakhulu. U-Connick usebenzisa lesi simiso lapho evakasha neqembu lakhe elikhulu, isibonelo.[13] Ngokusabalala kwamanethiwekhi angenawaya nama-iPads, amasistimu afanayo athuthukile. Emhlabeni womculo we-classical, amanye amaqembu e-string quartet asebenzisa izingxenye ezisekelwe kusikrini sekhompyutha. Kunezinzuzo eziningana ezingxenyeni ezisekelwe kukhompyutha. Njengoba isikolo sikusikrini sekhompyutha, umsebenzisi angalungisa ukugqama, ukukhanya kanye nosayizi wamanothi ukuze enze ukufunda kube lula. Ngaphezu kwalokho, ezinye izinhlelo zizokwenza "ukuphenduka kwekhasi" zisebenzisa i-foot pedal, okusho ukuthi umculi akudingeki aphuthe ukudlala umculo ngesikhathi sokuvula ikhasi, njengoba kuvame ukwenzeka ngezingxenye zephepha. 

Okuthakasela kakhulu umphakathi jikelele i-Mutopia Project, umzamo wokwenza umtapo wolwazi womculo wesizinda somphakathi, oqhathaniswa nomtapo wezincwadi ka-Project Gutenberg wezincwadi zomphakathi. I-International Music Score Library Project (IMSLP) izama futhi ukudala umtapo wolwazi oqukethe wonke amaphuzu omculo wesizinda somphakathi, kanye nezikolo zabaqambi abazimisele ukwabelana ngomculo wabo nomhlaba mahhala.

Ezinye izinhlelo zekhompuyutha zombhali wamaphuzu zinesici esiwusizo kakhulu kubaqambi nabahleli: ikhono "lokudlala emuva" umculo ophawuliwe usebenzisa imisindo ye-synthesizer noma izinsimbi ezibonakalayo. Ngaphambi kokuba izinhlelo zekhompiyutha zibe khona, izindleko eziphezulu zokuqasha i-orchestra ye-symphony egcwele zazisho ukuthi abaqambi nabahleli abaningi babekwazi ukuzwa kuphela imisebenzi yabo ye-orchestra ngokuyihlelela upiyano, i-organ noma i-string quartet. Nakuba ukudlalwa kohlelo lwe-scorewiter kungenawo ama-nuances wokurekhodwa kwe-orchestra ephrofeshinali, lisadlulisa ithoni yemibala yocezu nokudlala kwezinsimbi. 

Ukungena kokuphawulwa kwabasebenzi baseNtshonalanga kwamanye amasiko
Ngaphandle kwamasiko esimanje aseNtshonalanga kunezinhlobonhlobo zezinhlelo zokuqanjwa komculo, ngayinye evumelana nezidingo ezithile zamasiko omculo okukhulunywa ngawo. Amanye amasiko akudala aguquke kakhulu, njengezinhlobo ze-khyal kanye ne-dhrupad zaseNyakatho ye-India, awasebenzisi nhlobo inothi noma amafomu angajwayelekile njengezinsiza ze-mnemonic. Amasistimu omculo we-Western notation awahlomele kahle ukuchaza umculo wezinye izinhlobo, njengezinhlobo zenkantolo ze-gagaku yesi-Japanese, i-Indian dhrupad, noma umculo we-percussive we-Ewe druming[catation]. Ukungena kwezaziso zabasebenzi baseNtshonalanga kula masiko kuchazwe isazi somculo u-Alain Daniélou[14] kanye noReebee Garofalo[15] njengenqubo ye-imperialism yamasiko. 

Indida ngumdlalo, inkinga, noma ithoyizi elihlola ubuhlakani bomuntu noma ulwazi. Ku-puzzle, umxazululi ulindeleke ukuthi ahlanganise izingcezu (noma azihlukanise) ngendlela enengqondo, ukuze kutholwe isixazululo sendida. Kunezinhlobo ezahlukene zamaphazili, njengeziphazili zamagama ahlukene, izindida zokusesha amagama, izindida zezinombolo, izindida eziphathelene nobudlelwano, namaphazili anengqondo. Ucwaningo lwezemfundo lwamaphazili lubizwa nge-enigmatology. 

Izindida zivame ukudalwa ukuze zibe uhlobo lokuzijabulisa kodwa futhi zingavela ezinkingeni ezinkulu zezibalo noma ezinengqondo. Ezimweni ezinjalo, isisombululo sabo singase sibe negalelo elikhulu ocwaningweni lwezibalo.[1] 

I-Etymology 
I-Oxford English Dictionary ibeka igama elithi iphazili (njengesenzo) kusukela ekhulwini le-16. Ukusetshenziswa kwayo kokuqala okubhalwe ku-OED kwakusencwadini enesihloko esithi The Voyage of Robert Dudley...to the West Indies, 1594–95, elandiswa nguCapt. Wyatt, ngokwakhe, kanye no-Abram Kendall, master (eyanyatheliswa cishe ngo-1595). Leli gama kamuva laqala ukusetshenziswa njengebizo, okokuqala njengebizo elingaqondakali elisho 'isimo noma isimo sokuxakeka', futhi kamuva lathuthukisa incazelo 'yenkinga edidayo'. Ingcaphuno yokuqala ecacile ye-OED ngomqondo 'wethoyizi elihlola ubuhlakani bomdlali' ivela inoveli kaSir Walter Scott ka-1814 ethi Waverley, ebhekisela ethoyizini elaziwa ngokuthi "i-reel ebhodleleni".[2] 

I-etymology yendida yesenzo ichazwa yi-OED ngokuthi "akwaziwa"; imibono engenabufakazi mayelana nomsuka wayo ihlanganisa isenzo sesiNgisi Esidala esithi puslian esisho 'khetha', kanye nokususelwa kwesenzo sokuma.[3]
