Lesi sigaba siqukethe ucwaningo lwangempela. Sicela uyithuthukise ngokuqinisekisa izimangalo ezenziwe futhi wengeze izingcaphuno ezisemgqeni. Izitatimende ezihlanganisa kuphela ucwaningo lwangempela kufanele zisuswe. (Novemba 2018) (Funda ukuthi ungawususa kanjani futhi nini lo mlayezo)

Izixazululo zezindida zivame ukudinga ukuqashelwa kwamaphethini kanye nokubambelela ohlotsheni oluthile lokuhleleka. Abantu abanezinga eliphezulu lokusebenzisa ukucabanga ngendlela efanele bangase babe ngcono ekuxazululeni izindida ezinjalo uma kuqhathaniswa nabanye. Kodwa izindida ezisuselwe ekubuzeni nasekutholeni zingaxazululwa kalula yilabo abanamakhono amahle okubamba. Ukucabanga okunciphisayo kuyathuthuka ngokuzijwayeza. Izindida zezibalo zivame ukubandakanya ama-BODMAS. I-BODMAS isifinyezo esimele i-Bracket, Of, Division, Ukuphindaphinda, Ukwengeza kanye Nokukhipha. Ezifundeni ezithile, i-PEMDAS (Abakaki, Ama-Exponents, Ukuphindaphinda, Ukwahlukanisa, Ukwengeza kanye Nokukhipha) ifana negama elithi BODMAS. Ichaza ukuhleleka kwemisebenzi yokuxazulula inkulumo. Ezinye izindida zezibalo zidinga ukuvumelana okusuka phezulu kuya phansi ukuze kugwenywe ukungaqondakali kohlelo lokusebenza. Kungumbono olula ngokumangalisayo oncike, njengoba kwenza i-sudoku, esidingweni sokuthi izinombolo zivele kanye kuphela zisuka phezulu ziye phansi njengoba ziyeza.[4] 

Abenzi bendida 
Abenzi bendida abantu abenza amaphazili. Ngokwemibandela evamile yomsebenzi, umdidiyeli noma uhlu lwendida ngumuntu oqamba kanye/noma oxazulula izindida.

Umlando wamaphazili 
Iphazili eyisishiyagalolunye ehlanganisiwe eyizindandatho, idivayisi yephazili ethuthukisiwe edinga ukubalwa kwezibalo ukuze ixazulule, yasungulwa eShayina ngesikhathi (24 BCE) Isikhathi Sempi [245 BCE] [24 BCE] Ama-Jigsaw puzzle asungulwa cishe ngo-1760, lapho u-John Spilsbury, umqophi waseBrithani nomdwebi wamabalazwe, ebeka imephu eshidini lokhuni, wabe eselisaha uhlaka lwezwe ngalinye kumephu. Wabe esesebenzisa izingcezu ezaba khona njengosizo ekufundiseni i-geography.[6] 

Ngemva kokuduma emphakathini, lolu hlobo lwensiza yokufundisa lwahlala luwukusetshenziswa okuyinhloko kwama-jigsaw puzzle kwaze kwaba ngu-1820.[7] 

Iphazili enkulu kunazo zonke (izingcezu ezingu-40,320) yenziwe inkampani yaseJalimane i-Ravensburger.[8] Iphazili encane kakhulu eyake yenziwa yadalwa e-LaserZentrum Hannover. Ingamamilimitha-skwele amahlanu kuphela, ubukhulu bohlamvu lwesihlabathi. 

Izindida ezabhalwa kuqala ziyizimfumbe. EYurophu, izinganekwane zamaGreki zazikhiqiza izimfumbe njengemfumbe yeSphinx. Izimfumbe eziningi zakhiqizwa nangeNkathi Ephakathi, futhi.[9] 

Ngasekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, omagazini namaphephandaba bathola ukuthi babengakhulisa ukufunda kwabo ngokushicilela imincintiswano ye-puzzle, eqala ngamagama ahlanganisayo futhi ezinsukwini zanamuhla i-sudoku.

Onodoli bephepha bayizibalo ezisikwe ephepheni noma ekhadini elincanyana elinezingubo ezihlukene, nazo ezenziwe ngephepha, ezivame ukubanjelwa onodoli ngamathebhu asongwayo ephepha.[1] Kungase kube umfanekiso womuntu, isilwane noma into engaphili.[2] 

Onodoli abangamaphepha baye basetshenziselwa ukukhangisa, ukuvela komagazini nasemaphephandabeni, futhi bahlanganisa izihloko ezihlukahlukene nezikhathi. Phakathi neminyaka edlule, ziye zasetshenziswa ukuqinisa izinkolelo zamasiko mayelana nokubukeka kwabesifazane abafanelekile.[3] 

Ezinye izibalo zepulasitiki eziyisicaba ziyefana nonodoli bephepha, njengezibalo ze-Colorforms nonodoli be-Flatsy, kodwa lokhu kuwukulingisa futhi akubhekwa njengophawu lobuciko bephepha lodoli.[4] Umfanekiso kamagazini we 

-History 

1919 womlingisi uNorma Talmadge kanye nezinye zezingubo zakhe zefilimu zisesimweni sikanodoli 
wephepha Onodoli bamaphepha bebelokhu baba khona kusukela kudala kunephepha, mhlawumbe amakhulu noma izinkulungwane zeminyaka ngokulinganiselwa okuthile. Ubuso noma ezinye izinto zazisetshenziswa ephepheni futhi zasetshenziswa phakathi nemikhuba yezenkolo nemikhosi emasikweni ase-Asia emakhulwini amaningi eminyaka adlule.[catation] AmaJapane ayesebenzisa iphepha le-origami, ubuciko bokugoqa iphepha, futhi aqala ngo-800 AD asonga imifanekiso yephepha ngendlela ye-kimono. Abantu baseBalinese benza iphepha nesikhumba kwaba onodoli kusukela ngaphambi kweNkathi yobuKristu. Amanye amasiko emhlabeni jikelele abe nokwakheka kwephepha noma ubuciko bephepha, kuhlanganise nasePoland, lapho ayebizwa khona ngokuthi iWycinanki. [ukucashunwa kuyadingeka] Lezi zinhlobo zakuqala zezibalo zephepha ziyehluka konodoli bephepha abavamile besimanje, njengoba zingekho izingubo ezazenziwe ukuze zisetshenziswe onodoli. 

Unodoli wephepha wokuqala owakhiwe kwakungu-“Little Fanny”, owakhiqizwa ngu-S&J Fuller, e-London, ngo-1810.[2] EYurophu, ikakhulukazi eFrance, onodoli bokuqala bephepha babedumile kusukela maphakathi nekhulu le-18. Ikhadi elidala elaziwayo likanodoli wephepha lisingathwa yiGermanisches Nationalmuseum futhi lanyatheliswa cishe ngo-1650 eSouthern Germany, libonisa abantu besifazane ababili abanenani lezingubo zokugqoka, izingcezu zezingubo zasekhanda, izinwele zezinwele kanye nezinsiza.[5] Leli phepha lahlanganiswa labizwa ngokuthi ama-pantin, okusho upopayi kajack wokudansa noma oweqa. Zazihloselwe ukujabulisa abantu abadala futhi zisakazekele emphakathini ophakeme. Babedwetshwa noma bapendwe njengabantu abanemfashini kunodoli ngamunye. Lawa ayefana kakhulu nonodoli bephepha baseNtshonalanga. Amasethi angajwayelekile apendwe ngesandla ezithombe zamaphepha asukela ngasekupheleni kwawo-1780s angatholakala kweminye iminyuziyamu.[6] 

"The History and Adventures of Little Henry", ka-J. Belcher kwakuyithoyizi lokuqala laseMelika elihlanganisa onodoli bephepha. Le ncwadi, eyanyatheliswa ngo-1812, yashukumisela izingane ukuba zilingise izigcawu ezihlukahlukene ngonodoli bephepha ababehlanganisiwe.[3]

Umkhiqizi omkhulu waseMelika wonodoli bephepha, uMcLoughlin Brothers, wasungulwa ekuqaleni kuka-1800 futhi wathengiswa kuMilton Bradley ngawo-1920. Ngalesi sikhathi onodoli bephepha baduma e-US base bekhula ngokuduma emashumini eminyaka alandelayo. Ukwanda kokukhiqizwa konodoli bephepha maphakathi nekhulu le-19 kuya maphakathi nekhulu lama-20 kwakungenxa yentuthuko yezobuchwepheshe eyenza ukunyathelisa kungabizi kakhulu.[3] 


Unodoli wephepha onezingubo 
Izinkampani ezishicilela izincwadi ezalandela ekukhiqizweni konodoli bephepha noma abasiki bengqephu kwakungoLowe, Whitman, Saalfield kanye noMerrill phakathi kwabanye. Izihlabani zamafilimu nosaziwayo baqala ukugxila kakhulu ezinsukwini zokuqala zonodoli abangamaphepha e-USA. Onodoli abangamaphepha basakhiqizwa futhi uWhitman noGolden Co. basashicilela onodoli bephepha. 

Ngaphandle kwezihlabani zamabhayisikobho, abesifazane bezokungcebeleka bavame ukuba yibo abavezwa efomini likanodoli wephepha. Njengoba abesifazane abengeziwe baqala ukusebenza ngekhulu lamashumi amabili, abakhiqizi bonodoli bephepha baqala ukukhiqiza onodoli ababemelela abesifazane bemisebenzi. Inhlangano elwela amalungelo abantu besifazane phakathi nekhulu lama-20 yayinecala ngokubangela lolu shintsho. Omakoti kwakungesinye isibalo esivamile esivame ukumelelwa ngonodoli bephepha. 

"Incwadi yokukhuluma" iqondisa kabusha lapha. Nge-albhamu, bheka Incwadi Ekhulumayo. Ukuze uthole okunye ukusetshenziswa, bheka Incwadi Ekhulumayo (i-disambiguation). 
I-audiobook (noma incwadi ekhulumayo) iwukurekhodwa kwencwadi noma omunye umsebenzi ofundelwa phezulu. Ukufundwa kombhalo ophelele kuchazwa ngokuthi "okungafinyeziwe", kuyilapho ukufundwa kwezinguqulo ezifushane kuwukufinyeza. 

Umsindo okhulunywayo ubulokhu utholakala ezikoleni nasemitapo yolwazi yomphakathi futhi kancane kancane ezitolo zomculo kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1930s. Ama-albhamu amaningi akhulunywayo enziwa ngaphambi kweminyaka yamakhasethi, ama-compact disc, nomsindo olandekayo, ngokuvamile wezinkondlo nemidlalo kunezincwadi. Kwaze kwaba ngama-1980s lapho i-medium yaqala ukuheha abathengisi bezincwadi, kwase kuthi abathengisi bezincwadi baqala ukubonisa ama-audiobook emashalofini ezincwadi kunokuboniswa okuhlukile. 

I-Etymology 
Igama elithi “incwadi yokukhuluma” laqala ukuvela ngawo-1930 ngezinhlelo zikahulumeni eziklanyelwe abafundi abangaboni, kuyilapho igama elithi “audiobook” laqala ukusetshenziswa phakathi nawo-1970 lapho amakhasethi alalelwayo eqala ukuthatha indawo yamarekhodi egilamafoni.[1] Ngo-1994, i-Audio Publishers Association yasungula igama elithi "audiobook" njengezinga lemboni.[1] 

I-History 

Caption ifundeka kanje: "Igilamafoni ekhaya ifunda inoveli." From Daily Graphic (New York), 2 April 1878. Ngaphansi konyaka ngemva kokusungulwa kwegilamafoni, lo mdwebo wawunikeza umbono wesikhathi esizayo. Amanoveli nokho azohlala engasebenzi kumagilamafoni kuze kube ngawo-1930.
Ukuqoshwa kwamagama akhulunywayo kwaqala kwenzeka ngokusungulwa kwegilamafoni nguThomas Edison ngo-1877.[1] "Izincwadi zegilamafoni" zazingezinye zezinhlelo zokusebenza zokuqala ezacatshangwa u-Edison "owayezokhuluma nabantu abayizimpumputhe ngaphandle komzamo wabo."[1] Amagama okuqala akhulunywa kugilamafoni kwakuyinkulumo ka-Edison ethi "UMariya WayeneWundlu Elincane", isibonelo sokuqala sevesi elirekhodiwe.[1] Ngo-1878, umboniso eRoyal Institution eBrithani wawuhlanganisa "Hey Diddle Diddle, the Cat and the Fiddle" kanye nomugqa wezinkondlo zikaTennyson ngaleyo ndlela wasungula kusukela ekuqaleni kobuchwepheshe ubudlelwane nezincwadi ezikhulunywayo.[1] 

E-United States 
Ekuqaleni kuya ku-1970 
Amarekhodi amaningi amafushane, akhulunywayo athengiswa kusilinda ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19 nasekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20;[2] nokho, amasilinda ayindilinga ayelinganiselwe cishe emaminithini angu-4 lilinye okwenza izincwadi zingasebenzi;[1] izingqwembe eziyisicaba zikhuphuke zaba yimizuzu eyi-12 kodwa nalokhu kwakungenzeki ekusebenzeni okude.[1] “Omunye umlaleli wakuqala wakhononda ngokuthi uzodinga ibhala ukuze aphathe izincwadi ezikhulumayo eziqoshwe kuma-diskhi anomthamo ongaka wokulondoloza.”[1] Ngawo-1930 amarekhodi asondelene akhula abe yimizuzu engu-20 okwenza kube nokulandisa okude.[1] 

Ngo-1931, i-American Foundation for the Blind (AFB) kanye ne-Library of Congress Books for the Adult Blind Project yasungula "Uhlelo Lwezincwadi Ezikhulumayo" (Izincwadi Zabayizimpumputhe), okwakuhloselwe ukuhlinzeka ngezinto zokufunda kumakadebona abalimala phakathi neMpi Yezwe I kanye nabanye abantu abadala abangaboni kahle.[1] Ukuhlolwa kokuqala okurekhodiwe ngo-1932 kwakuhlanganisa isahluko esivela ku-Midstream ka-Helen Keller kanye neka-Edgar Allan Poe ethi "The Raven".[1] Inhlangano ithole imvume yekhongolose yokukhululwa ku-copyright nasekusabalazweni kweposi mahhala kwezincwadi zokukhuluma.[1] Amarekhodi okuqala oHlelo Lwezincwadi Ezikhulumayo ngo-1934 ayehlanganisa izingxenye zeBhayibheli; Isimemezelo Senkululeko kanye neminye imibhalo yokushisekela izwe; imidlalo nezingoma zikaShakespeare; kanye nenganekwane kaGladys Hasty Carroll, EM Delafield, Cora Jarrett, Rudyard Kipling, John Masefield, kanye noPG Wodehouse.[1] Ukuze wonge izindleko futhi wakhe ngokushesha uhlu lwezincwadi ezilalelwayo, iBrithani ne-United States babelane ngokurekhodiwe kumakhathalogi abo. Ngokubheka amakhathalogi amadala, isazi-mlando u-Matthew Rubery "mhlawumbe" sihlonze i-audiobook yokuqala ekhiqizwe eBrithani njengeka-Agatha Christie ethi The Murder of Roger Ackroyd, efundwe ngu-Anthony McDonald ngo-1934.[3]

Ukuqopha i-Blind & Dyslexic (i-RFBD, kamuva eyaqanjwa kabusha ngokuthi i-Learning Ally) yasungulwa ngo-1948 ngu-Anne T. Macdonald, ilungu le-New York Public Library's Auxiliary's Women's Auxiliary, ephendula imibuzo eminingi evela kumasosha ayelahlekelwe umbono wawo empini phakathi neMpi Yezwe II. I-GI Bill of Rights esanda kuphasiswa iqinisekise imfundo yasekolishi kubo bonke omakadebona, kodwa imibhalo ibingafinyeleleki kakhulu kumakadebona abasanda kuphuphuthekiswa, abangazange bayifunde i-Braille futhi bengakwazi ukufinyelela kalula ukufunda bukhoma. UMacdonald ugqugquzele abesifazane boMsizi ngaphansi kwesiqubulo esithi “Imfundo iyilungelo, ayilona ilungelo”. Amalungu Omsizi aguqule i-attic ye-New York Public Library yaba isitudiyo, eqopha izincwadi esebenzisa amadiski egilamafoni angamayintshi ayisithupha e-SoundScriber ye-vinyl ye-SoundScriber ayedlala cishe imizuzu eyi-12 yento ngayinye ohlangothini ngalunye. Ngo-1952, uMacdonald wasungula izitudiyo zokuqopha emadolobheni angu-7 engeziwe kulo lonke elase-United States. 

I-Caedmon Records yayiyiphayona ebhizinisini le-audiobook. Bekuyinkampani yokuqala ezinikele ekuthengiseni umsebenzi orekhodiwe emphakathini futhi ibizwe ngokuthi "imbewu" yemboni yezincwadi ezilalelwayo.[4] ICaedmon yasungulwa eNew York ngo-1952 ngabafundi basekolishi uBarbara Holdridge noMarianne Roney. [4] Ukukhululwa kwabo kokuqala kwaba iqoqo lezinkondlo zikaDylan Thomas njengoba zifundwe umlobi.[4] I-LP's B-side iqukethe uKhisimusi Wengane e-Wales, owengezwe njengokucatshangwa kamuva. Indaba yayingacacile futhi uThomas ngokwakhe wayengasikhumbulanga isihloko sayo lapho ebuzwa ukuthi yini azoyisebenzisa ukuze agcwalise i-B-side—kodwa lokhu okuqoshiwe kwaqhubeka kwaba omunye wemisebenzi yakhe ayeyithanda kakhulu, futhi wethula uCaedmon enkampanini ephumelelayo.[4] Ukuqoshwa kwasekuqaleni kuka-1952 bekungokukhethwa kweRegistry National Recording Registry yase-United States yango-2008, ithi "inikwe udumo ngokwethula imboni ye-audiobook e-United States".[5] UCaedmon wasebenzisa amarekhodi e-LP, asungulwa ngo-1948, okwenza ukuqoshwa okude kufinyeleleke futhi kusebenze, nokho iningi lemisebenzi yabo kwakuyizinkondlo, imidlalo kanye neminye imisebenzi emifushane, hhayi izincwadi ezingafinyeziwe ngenxa yomkhawulo we-LP wesikhathi sokudlala esiyimizuzu engama-45 (izinhlangothi ezihlanganisiwe). 

Ilabhulali Elalelayo[6] futhi bekuyinkampani yokuqala, kwaba ngeyokuqala ukusabalalisa ama-audiobook ezingane ezikoleni, emitapo yolwazi nakwezinye izimakethe ezikhethekile, okuhlanganisa nezibhedlela ze-VA.[7] Yasungulwa ngu-Anthony Ditlow nomkakhe ngo-1955 ekhaya labo iRed Bank, eNew Jersey; UDitlow wayengaboni kahle.[7] Enye inkampani eyaqala ukuphayona kwakuyi-Spoken Arts eyasungulwa ngo-1956 ngu-Arthur Luce Klein nomkakhe, bakhiqiza okurekhodiwe okungaphezu kuka-700 futhi bayaziwa kakhulu ngezinkondlo nemidlalo eqoshiwe eyayisetshenziswa ezikoleni nasemitatsheni yezincwadi.[8] Njengo-Caedemon, Umtapo Wezincwadi Olalelayo kanye Nobuciko Obukhulunywayo bazuza kubuchwepheshe obusha be-LPs, kodwa futhi andisa uxhaso lukahulumeni lwezikole nemitapo yolwazi kusukela ngawo-1950 nawo-60s.[7]
 
1970 kuya ku-1996
Noma ukuqoshwa okukhulunyiwe kwakudumile ngefomethi yerekhodi ye-vinyl engu-33+1⁄3 yezikole nemitapo yolwazi ekuqaleni kwawo-1970, ukuqala kwemakethe yesimanje yokuthengisa yama-audiobook kungalandelelwa ekwamukelweni okubanzi kwamakhasethi ngamakhasethi ngeminyaka yawo-1970s.[9] Amakhasethi amakhasethi asungulwa ngo-1962 futhi imitapo yolwazi embalwa, njengeLibrary of Congress, yaqala ukusabalalisa izincwadi ezisekhasethi ngo-1969.[9] Kodwa-ke, ngeminyaka yawo-1970s, izinto ezintsha eziningi zobuchwepheshe zavumela ukusetshenziswa kabanzi kwekhasethi emitapo yolwazi futhi kwadala ukwakhiwa kwemakethe entsha yokuthengisa yezincwadi ezilalelwayo.[9] Lezi zindlela ezintsha zihlanganisa ukwethulwa kwabadlali abaphathekayo abancane nabashibhile njenge-Walkman, kanye nokusetshenziswa kabanzi kwamadekhi amakhasethi ezimotweni, ikakhulukazi amamodeli aseJapane angenisiwe agcwele imakethe phakathi nezinkinga eziningi zamandla zeminyaka eyishumi.[9] 

Ekuqaleni kwawo-1970, ukuqoshwa kweziyalezo kwakuphakathi kwemikhiqizo yokuqala yokuthengisa ethengiswa ngekhasethi.[9] Bekunezinkampani eziyisi-8 ezazisabalalisa izinto ezisekhasethini ezinezihloko ezinjengethi Managing and Selling Companies (amakhasethi angu-12, $300) kanye ne-Executive Seminar in Sound ochungechungeni lwamakhasethi emizuzu engu-60.[9] Emitapo yolwazi, izincwadi eziningi kukhasethi zazisalungiselelwa abantu abayizimpumputhe nabakhubazekile, nokho ezinye izinkampani ezintsha zabona ithuba lokwenza amabhuku alalelwayo enzelwe izethameli eziningi, njenge-Voice Over Books ekhiqize abathengisi abafinyeziweyo abadayiswa kakhulu nabalingisi abangochwepheshe.[9] Amaphayona akudala ahlanganisa owawina indondo yegolide wama-Olympic u-Duvall Hecht okwathi ngo-1975 wasungula i-California-based Books on Tape njengesevisi yokuqasha ye-oda leposi eliqondiswe kumthengi lama-audiobook angafingqiwe futhi wanweba izinsizakalo zabo zokudayisa imikhiqizo yabo emitatsheni yezincwadi kanye nezincwadi ezilalelwayo ezithola ukuduma kubagibeli nabahambi.[9] Ngo-1978, u-Henry Trentman, umdayisi ohambahambayo owalalela amakhasethi okuthengisa ngenkathi eshayela amabanga amade, waba nombono wokwenza ukuqoshwa kwekhwalithi okungafinyeziwe kwezincwadi zakudala ezifundwa abadlali abangochwepheshe.[10] Inkampani yakhe, i-Maryland-based Recorded Books, ilandele imodeli ye-Books on Tape kodwa enekhwalithi ephezulu yokuqoshwa kwestudiyo nabalingisi.[10] Izincwadi Ezirekhodiwe kanye ne-Chivers Audio Books kwaba ngabokuqala ukuthuthukisa amaqembu adidiyelwe adidiyelwe kanye nokusebenza nabalingisi abangochwepheshe.[11]

Ngo-1984, kwakunezinkampani eziyishumi nanye ezishicilela ama-audiobook, zazihlanganisa i-Caedmon, i-Metacom, i-Newman Communications, Izincwadi Ezirekhodiwe, I-Brilliance kanye ne-Books on Tape.[9] Izinkampani zazizincane, ezinkulu kunazo zonke zazinohlu lwezihloko ezingama-200.[9] Ezinye izihloko ezifushanisiwe bezithengiswa ezitolo zezincwadi, njenge-Waldenbooks, kodwa zinezibalo zokuthengisa ezingasho lutho, eziningi zazithengiswa ngokubhaliselwe kwe-oda leposi noma ngemitapo yolwazi.[9] Kodwa-ke, ngo-1984, i-Brilliance Audio yasungula indlela yokuqopha ngokuphindwe kabili ekhasethini elifanayo ngaleyo ndlela ivumele izinhlelo ezingabizi kakhulu ezingafinyeziwe.[9] Indlela yokwenza yayihilela ukuqoshwa esiteshini ngasinye kwezimbili zengoma ngayinye ye-stereo.[9] Lokhu kwavulela amathuba amasha emakethe futhi ngo-September 1985, Abashicileli Besonto ngalinye bahlonza abashicileli bezincwadi ezilalelwayo abangamashumi amabili nanye.[9] Lokhu kwakuhlanganisa abashicileli abasha abakhulu abafana noHarper noRow, Random House, kanye neWarner Communications.[9] 

Unyaka ka-1986 uhlonzwe njengenguquko embonini, lapho ikhula isuka elukulukuni lokuhlola.[9] Imicimbi eminingana yenzekile: I-Audio Publishers Association, inhlangano yohwebo engenzi nzuzo, yasungulwa abashicileli abajoyine ukugqugquzela ukuqwashisa ngomsindo wamagama akhulunywayo nokuhlinzeka ngezibalo zomkhakha.[9] I-Time-Life yaqala ukunikeza amalungu ama-audiobook.[9] Iklabhu ye-Book-of-the-Month yaqala ukunikela ngama-audiobook kumalungu ayo, njengoba kwenza i-Literary Guild. Amanye amakilabhu afana ne-History Book Club, i-Get Rich Club, i-Nostalgia Book Club, i-Scholastic club yezingane wonke aqala ukunikeza ama-audiobook.[9] Abashicileli baqala ukukhipha izihloko zezenkolo nezikhuthazayo ezitolo zezincwadi zobuKristu. Ngo-May 1987, iPublishers Weekly yaqala ikholomu evamile ukuze ihlanganise imboni.[9] Ekupheleni kuka-1987, imakethe ye-audiobook yayilinganiselwa emakethe yezigidi ezingu-200, futhi ama-audiobook ekhasethi ayethengiswa kuma-75% ezitolo zezincwadi zesifunda nezizimele ezihlolwe ngabashicileli Masonto onke.[9] Ngo-August 1988 kwase kunabashicileli bama-audiobook abangamashumi amane, cishe ngokuphindwe kane kunango-1984.[9] 

Maphakathi nawo-1990, ibhizinisi lokushicilela okulalelwayo lakhula lafinyelela ezigidini eziyizinkulungwane ezingu-1.5 zamaRandi ngonyaka ngenani lokudayisa.[12] Ngo-1996, i-Audio Publishers Association yasungula ama-Audie Awards ama-audiobook, alingana ne-Oscar embonini ye-audiobook. Abaqokiwe bamenyezelwa minyaka yonke ngoFebhuwari. Abawinile bamenyezelwa edilini elikhulu ngoMeyi, ngokuvamile elihambisana ne-BookExpo America.[13]
 
1996 ukwethula
Ngokusabalala kwe-inthanethi kubathengi ngeminyaka yawo-1990s, isivinini sokulanda ngokushesha ngobuchwepheshe be-broadband, amafomethi amasha omsindo acindezelwe kanye nezidlali zemidiya eziphathwayo, ukuthandwa kwama-audiobook kukhule kakhulu ngasekupheleni kwawo-1990 nawo-2000. Ngo-1997, i-Audible yaphayona isidlali semidiya yedijithali esinemakethe enkulu kunazo zonke emhlabeni, esiqanjwe "Isidlali Esizwakalayo", [14] sathengiswa ngo-$200, sabamba amahora angu-2 omsindo futhi kwathiwa "sincane futhi silula kune-Walkman", isidlali sekhasethi esidumile esasisetshenziswa ngaleso sikhathi.[15] Ama-audiobook edijithali abeyingqopha-mlando entsha ephawulekayo njengoba ayevumela izilaleli ukukhululeka emithonjeni yezindaba engokoqobo njengamakhasethi nama-CMP3sas ayedinga ukuthuthwa ngeposi, okuvumela esikhundleni salokho ukufinyelela kokudawuniloda okusheshayo okuvela emitapweni yolwazi eku-inthanethi yobukhulu obungenamkhawulo, nokuphatheka kusetshenziswa amadivaysi amancane nalula uma kuqhathaniswa. I-Audible.com yaba ngeyokuqala ukusungula iwebhusayithi, ngo-1998, okwakungathengwa kuyo ama-audiobook edijithali. 

Okunye okusha kwaba ukudalwa kwe-LibriVox ngo-2005 ngumlobi osekelwe eMontreal u-Hugh McGuire owabuza umbuzo kubhulogi yakhe: "Ingabe inetha ingasebenzisa inqwaba yamavolontiya ukusiza ukuletha izincwadi endaweni yomphakathi ekuphileni ngokusebenzisa i-podcasting?" Kwaqala kanjalo-ke ukwakhiwa kwama-audiobook esizinda somphakathi ngabalandisi abangamavolontiya. Ekupheleni kuka-2021, i-LibriVox yayinekhathalogi yemisebenzi engaphezu kuka-16,870.[16] 

Inguquko isuka ku-vinyl, iye kwikhasethi, iye kwi-CD, iye ku-MP3CD, iye ekulandisweni kwedijithali ibhalwe yi-Audio Publishers Association ocwaningweni lwaminyaka yonke (ushintsho lwangaphambili lusuka kwirekhodi luye kwikhasethi luchazwe esigabeni seminyaka yawo-1970). Unyaka wokugcina amakhasethi amele ngaphezu kuka-50% wesamba sokuthengiswa kwemakethe kwaba ngo-2002.[17] Amakhasethi athathelwa indawo ama-CD njengendawo ehamba phambili phakathi kuka-2003–2004. Ama-CD afinyelele inani eliphakeme lama-78% okuthengiswa ngo-2008, [18] aqala ukwehla avumela ukulandwa kwedijithali. Inhlolovo yango-2012 yathola ukuthi ama-CD abalwa "cishe uhhafu" wakho konke ukuthengiswa okusho ukuthi kwakungaseyona indlela ehamba phambili (i-APA ayizange ibike izibalo zokudawuniloda kwedijithali zango-2012, kodwa ngo-2011 ama-CD abalelwa ku-53% futhi ukudawuniloda kwedijithali kwaba ngu-41%).[19][20] I-APA ilinganisela ukuthi ukuthengiswa kwe-audiobook ngo-2015 ngefomethi yedijithali kukhuphuke ngo-34% ngo-2014.[21] 

Ukuvela kabusha kokuxoxwa kwezindaba ezilalelwayo kudalwe kabanzi ngenxa yentuthuko yobuchwepheshe beselula obufana nama-smartphone, amathebulethi, nezinhlelo zokuzijabulisa ze-multimedia ezimotweni, ezaziwa nangokuthi izinkundla zezimoto ezixhunyiwe.[22][23] Okurekhodiwe kwedrama yomsindo nakho manje kuyi-podcast ku-inthanethi.[24] 

Ngo-2014, u-Bob no-Debra Deyan be-Deyan Audio bavula i-Deyan Institute of Vocal Artistry and Technology, ikhampasi yokuqala emhlabeni kanye nesikole sokufundisa ubuciko nobuchwepheshe bokukhiqiza ama-audiobook.[25]

Ngo-2018, cishe ama-audiobook angama-50,000 aqoshwa e-United States ngokukhula kokuthengisa ngamaphesenti angama-20 unyaka nonyaka.[26] Ukuthengiswa kwe-audiobook yase-US ngo-2019 kwenza isamba semali eyizigidi eziyizinkulungwane ezingu-1.2, sikhuphuke ngo-16% kusukela ngonyaka odlule. Ngokungeziwe ekwenyukeni kokuthengiswa, inhlolovo kazwelonke ye-Edison Research yabalaleli bama-audiobook aseMelika abaneminyaka engu-18 kuya phezulu ithole ukuthi isilinganiso senani lama-audiobook alalelwayo ngonyaka sikhuphuke sisuka ku-6.8 ngo-2019 saya ku-8.1 ngo-2020.[27] 

Germany 
Ukuvela nokusetshenziswa kwezincwadi ezilalelwayo eJalimane (Hörbuch, "incwadi yokulalela") kufana kakhulu nalokho kwase-US. Isibonelo esikhethekile sokusetshenziswa kwayo iWest German Audio Book Library for the Blind, eyasungulwa ngo-1955. Abadlali baseshashalazini kamasipala eMünster baqopha ama-audiobook okuqala abantu abangaboni kahle esitudiyo esithuthukisiwe esifakwe amabhokisi amaqanda. Ngenxa yokuthi ama-tram aye anyakaza, le mikhiqizo yokuqala yenzeka ebusuku. Kamuva, imibhalo yarekhodwa izikhulumi eziqeqeshiwe ezitudiyo ezichwepheshile futhi yasakazwa kubasebenzisi ngeposi. Kuze kube yiminyaka yawo-1970 ukuqoshwa kwakukuma-tape reels, kwase kuba amakhasethi kamuva. Kusukela ngo-2004, iminikelo irekhodwe ku-DAISY Digital Talking Book MP3 ejwayelekile, ehlinzeka ngezici ezengeziwe kubasebenzisi abangaboni kahle ukuze balalele futhi bazulazule ezintweni ezibhaliwe ngokuzwakalayo.[28] 

I-India 
Audiobooks e-India yaqala ukuvela kamuva nje kunasemhlabeni wonke. Ngo-2010 kuphela lapho Ama-Audiobooks athola khona ukuduma okujwayelekile emakethe yaseNdiya. Lokhu ikakhulukazi kungenxa yokuntuleka kwemizamo ehleliwe yangaphambilini yabashicileli nababhali. Imizamo yokumaketha nokutholakala kwe-Audiobooks yenze i-India yaba ngenye yezimakethe ezikhula ngokushesha ze-Audiobooks emhlabeni.[catation needed] 

Indlela yokuphila yabantu base-Indian basemadolobheni kanye nesinye sezikhathi ezihamba phambili zansuku zonke zohambo lokuya emsebenzini emhlabeni nakho kusizile ekwenzeni ama-Audiobook adume esifundeni. Izincwadi Zebhizinisi Nezokuzisiza zikhanga kabanzi futhi bezidume kakhulu kunezinganekwane/okungezona izinganekwane.[catation needed] Lokhu kungenxa yokuthi ama-Audiobooks abonwa ngokuyinhloko njengendlela yokuzithuthukisa wena nokufunda, kunokuba ukuzijabulisa. 

Amabhuku alalelwayo akhululwa ngezilimi ezahlukene zaseNdiya. NgesiMalayalam, inoveli yokuqala yomsindo, enesihloko esithi Ouija Board, yakhululwa yiKathacafe ngo-2018. [29] 

INingizimu Korea 
Emkhakheni wokushicilela waseKorea, kusukela ibhizinisi lamabhuku alalelwayo laqala ngo-2000, selinyamalele ngenxa yokwehluleka kwalo ukuthola imiphumela ephusile. 

Cishe eminyakeni engama-20 kamuva, inzalo kumakhalekhukhwini yenyukile ngo-2019, kodwa kusenemisebenzi okufanele ixazululwe. 

Okokuqala, i-Audiobook ibintula ukwesekwa okuningi kwenqubomgomo okuhlobene nomkhakha, futhi okwesibili, ingqalasizinda yendawo yokukhiqiza i-Audiobook ibingenele. Okwesithathu, ucwaningo nokuthuthukiswa kobuchwepheshe, okufana nezemfundo, akukaze kusebenze ukuze kuqhubeke ukukhula njengemboni ye-Audiobook.[30]
 
Ukukhiqiza
Ukukhiqiza i-audiobook kuhlanganisa umxoxi ohlezi endaweni yokuqopha efunda umbhalo, kuyilapho unjiniyela wesitudiyo nomqondisi barekhoda futhi baqondise ukusebenza.[31] Uma kwenzeka iphutha ukurekhodwa kuyamiswa futhi umlandisi akufunde futhi.[31] Ngokuthuthuka kwakamuva kwezobuchwepheshe bokuqopha, ama-audiobook amaningi manje aseqoshwa ezitudiyo zasekhaya ngabalandisi abasebenza ngokuzimela.[32] Ama-audiobook akhiqizwe yizinkampani ezinkulu ezishicilelayo ahlolwa futhi ahlelwe ngemva kokuqoshwa kokulandisa. 

Abalandisi bavame ukukhokhelwa ngehora eliqoshiwe eliqediwe, okusho ukuthi uma kuthatha amahora angu-20 ukukhiqiza incwadi yamahora angu-5, umxoxi ukhokhelwa amahora angu-5, ngaleyo ndlela anikeze isisusa sokungenzi amaphutha.[31] Kuya ngombalisi bakhokhelwa u-US$150 ngehora eliqediwe ukuya ku-US$400 (kusukela ngo-2011).[31] Ababalisi abaningi baphinde basebenze njengabadidiyeli futhi balethe ama-audiobook akhiqizwe ngokugcwele, ahlelwe, afundiswa kahle, futhi afakazelwa. Bangase bakhokhise i-$75–$125 eyengeziwe ngehora eliqediwe ngaphezu kwemali yabo yokulandisa ukuze baxhumanise futhi bakhokhele izinsizakalo zangemuva kokukhiqiza. Izindleko eziphelele zokukhiqiza i-audiobook zingahluka kakhulu, njengoba izincwadi ezinde zidinga isikhathi esengeziwe se-studio futhi ababalisi abaziwayo beza ngeprimiyamu. Ngokusho kommeleli kwa-Audible, izindleko zokuqopha i-audiobook zehle zisuka cishe ku-US$25,000 ngasekupheleni kwawo-1990 zaya cishe ku-US$2,000-US$3,000 ngo-2014.[33] 

Amafomethi 
Bheka futhi: Umugqa wesikhathi wamafomethi alalelwayo 

Iqoqo le-audiobook emtatsheni wezincwadi. Ingxube yamakhasethi namafomethi e-CD-ROM. 
Ama-audiobook asakazwa kunoma iyiphi ifomethi yomsindo etholakalayo, kodwa ngokuyinhloko lawa amarekhodi, amakhasethi, ama-CD, ama-MP3 CD, amafomethi edijithali alandekayo (isb, i-MP3 (.mp3), i-Windows Media Audio (.wma), i-Advanced Audio Coding (.aac)), kanye namadivayisi edijithali alayishwe ngaphambilini lapho okuqukethwe komsindo kulayishwa futhi kuthengiswa ndawonye ne-hardware. 

Ngo-1955, umsunguli waseJalimane wethula isistimu yekhasethi yomsindo we-Sound Book esekelwe kufomethi ye-Tefifon lapho esikhundleni sekhasethi kazibuthe umsindo waqoshwa ku-loop eqhubekayo yeribhoni ye-vinylite egobile efana netheyiphu endala yamathrekhi angu-8. Ngisho noma i-Tefifon yokuqala eyayisekelwe kuyo yayisebenza ngo-19 CPS futhi yayikwazi ukubamba amahora angu-4, i-Sound Book eyodwa yayikwazi ukuqopha amahora ayisishiyagalombili njengoba yayigijima ngohhafu wejubane noma u-9.5 CPS. Nokho, njenge-Tefifon, ifomethi ayizange isabalale ekusetshenzisweni.[34] 

Inombolo encane yezincwadi irekhodelwa ukusakazwa komsakazo, ngokuvamile ngendlela efushanisiwe futhi ngezinye izikhathi i-serialized. Ama-audiobooks angase eze njengezinguqulo ezenziwe idrama ngokugcwele zencwadi ephrintiwe, ngezinye izikhathi ebiza abalingisi abaphelele, umculo, nemisindo. Amadrama alalelwayo asebenzayo, lawa ma-audiobook aziwa njengama-audiobook asakazwa ngokugcwele. Iziteshi zomsakazo ze-BBC iRadio 3, iRadio 4, kanye neRadio 4 Extra ziye zasakaza izinhlelo ezifana nenoveli kaWilliam Gibson ethi Neuromancer.[35]

Ukukhiqizwa komsindo kokuqala kuwumsebenzi womsindo wamagama akhulunywayo owumkhiqizo wangempela kodwa ongasekelwe encwadini. Izibonelo zifaka u-Joe Hill, indodana ka-Stephen King, owakhipha i-audiobook ye-Vinyl First ebizwa ngokuthi i-Dark Carousel ngo-2018. Ifike ngesethi ye-vinyl engu-2-LP, noma njenge-MP3 elandekayo, kodwa engenawo umbhalo oshicilelwe.[36] Esinye isibonelo sihlanganisa i-Spin, i-Audiobook Musical (2018), inguqulo yomculo ye-Rumpelstiltskin exoxwa nguJim Dale, futhi ehlanganisa izihlabani zomculo ze-Broadway.[37] 

Sebenzisa 

i-Audiobook esetshenziselwa ukusabalalisa ulwazi phakathi kwabalimi eKenya. 
Amabhuku alalelwayo asetshenziselwe ukufundisa izingane ukufunda nokwandisa ukuqonda kokufunda. Ziwusizo futhi kwabangaboni. I-National Library of Congress e-US kanye ne-CNIB Library e-Canada ihlinzeka ngezindleko zezinsiza zemtapo wezincwadi ezilalelwayo kwabangaboni kahle; izincwadi eziceliwe zithunyelwa ngeposi (ngaphandle kwenkokhiso) kumakhasimende. Yasungulwa ngo-1996, i-Assistive Media yakwa-Ann Arbor, eMichigan kwaba yinhlangano yokuqala ukukhiqiza nokuletha okuqoshiwe okukhulunywayo kwemisebenzi yobuntatheli ebhaliwe nemibhalo nge-inthanethi ukuze kusizwe abantu abangaboni kahle. 

Cishe amaphesenti angu-40 akho konke ukusetshenziswa kwe-audiobook kwenzeka kumalabhulali omphakathi, kanti okusele kunikezwa ikakhulukazi ezitolo zezincwadi. Izinhlelo zokulanda umtapo wolwazi okwamanje zikhula ngokushesha (imitapo yolwazi yomphakathi engaphezu kuka-5,000 inikezela ngama-audiobook angalandwa mahhala). Imitapo yolwazi iphinde ibe yizindawo ezidumile zokuhlola ama-audiobook akufomethi ye-CD.[38] Ngokusho kweNational Endowment for the Arts' study, "Reading At Risk: A Survey of Literary Reading in America" (2004), ukulalela kwe-audiobook kukhulisa ukufunda nokubhala okuvamile.[39] 

Izindlela zokulalela 
Bheka futhi: I-albhamu yamagama akhulunywayo 
Ngenxa yefomethi yayo, umuntu angalalela i-audiobook kuyilapho enza eminye imisebenzi, njengokuhlanza izingubo, ukuvocavoca umzimba, ukususa ukhula, neminye imisebenzi efanayo. Ukusetshenziswa okuvamile kwama-audiobook abantu abadala kulapho behamba ngemoto noma ngenkathi behamba ngezithuthi zomphakathi, njengenye indlela yomsakazo noma umculo. 

Inhlolovo yakamuva ekhishwe i-Audio Publishers Association ithole ukuthi iningi labasebenzisi be-audiobook balalela emotweni, futhi abathengi abangaphezu kwezingxenye ezimbili kwezintathu zamabhuku omsindo bachaze ama-audiobook njengaphumuza ingqondo nendlela enhle yokwenza izinto eziningi. Esinye isizathu esishiwo sokukhetha ama-audiobook ngaphezu kwamanye amafomethi ukuthi ukusebenza komsindo kwenza ezinye izincwadi zithandeke kakhulu.[40] 

Imikhuba evamile yokulalela ihlanganisa: 

Ukudlala kabusha: Ngokuya ngezinga lomuntu lokunaka kanye nentshisekelo, ngokuvamile kuyadingeka ukuthi ulalele izingxenye ze-audiobook izikhathi ezingaphezu kwesisodwa ukuze uvumele okuqukethwe kuqondwe futhi kugcinwe ngendlela egculisayo. Ukuphindaphinda kungenziwa ngokushesha noma ngemva kwesikhathi eside.
Ukufunda: Abantu bangase balalele i-audiobook (imvamisa engafinyeziwe) kuyilapho belandela encwadini yangempela. Lokhu kubasiza ukuba bafunde amagama abangase bangawafundi kahle uma befunda incwadi kuphela. Lokhu kungase futhi kube indlela ephumelela kakhulu yokufunda ulimi olusha. 
Ukwenza izinto eziningi: Abalaleli abaningi be-audiobook bakhetha ifomethi ngoba ivumela ukwenza izinto eziningi ngesikhathi semisebenzi engajwayelekile noma ejwayelekile njengokuzivocavoca, ukwenza ubuciko, noma ukupheka. 
Ukuzijabulisa: Ama-audiobook aseyindlela edumile yokuzijabulisa kwezokuvakasha emindenini noma kubagibeli.[41] 
Izinhlangano ezisiza umphakathi nezingenzi-nzuzo 

Isibonelo sestudiyo somsindo sokufundwa kochwepheshe. Isitudiyo sizungezwe ngamaphaneli e-baffle ukuze kuncishiswe ukuzwakala okuvela kusipika, okuvumela umbhobho ukuthi ubambe umsindo ocacile. 
Yasungulwa ngo-1948, i-Learning Ally isebenzela ngaphezu kuka-300,000 K–12, abafundi basekolishi nabaphothule, omakadebona kanye nabafundi bempilo yonke abanokukhubazeka kokuphrinta, okungukuthi abangakwazi ukufunda ukuphrinta okujwayelekile ngenxa yobumpumputhe, ukukhubazeka kokubona, i-dyslexia, noma okunye ukukhubazeka kokufunda. Iqoqo lokufunda lika-Ally lezincwadi zokufunda ezingaphezu kuka-80,000 ezilandiswa abantu nezihloko zezincwadi lingalandwa kuma-smartphones ajwayelekile namathebulethi, futhi lilikhulu kunawo wonke emhlabeni. 

Yasungulwa ngo-2002, i-Bookshare iwumtapo wezincwadi we-inthanethi wama-audiobook afundwa ngekhompuyutha ngamafomethi afinyeleleka kubantu abakhubazekile ngokuphrinta. 

Yasungulwa ngo-2005, i-LibriVox futhi iyilabhulali eku-inthanethi yama-audiobook alandekayo kanye nenhlangano yamahhala engenzi nzuzo eyakhiwe ngu-Hugh McGuire. Inama-audiobook esizinda somphakathi ngezilimi ezimbalwa.[42] 

I-Caliber Audio Library iyinhlangano esiza abantulayo yase-UK ehlinzeka ngensizakalo yamahhala yokubhalisa yama-audiobook angafingqiwe kubantu abanenkinga yokubona, i-dyslexia noma okunye ukukhubazeka, abangakwazi ukufunda ukuphrinta. Banomtapo wolwazi onezihloko ezingaphezu kwezi-8,550 zezinganekwane nezingezona izinganekwane ezingabolekwa ngeposi kuma-CD e-MP3 nama-memory stick noma ngokusakaza-bukhoma.[43] 

Izincwadi Zokulalela ziyinhlangano esiza abantulayo yase-UK enikeza ukusakazwa kwe-inthanethi, ukudawuniloda kanye nenkonzo yeposi kunoma ubani onokukhubazeka noma ogulayo okwenza kube nzima ukubamba incwadi, ukuphenya amakhasi ayo, noma ukufunda ngendlela evamile, lokhu kuhlanganisa abantu abanenkinga yokubona, ngokomzimba, yokufunda noma yengqondo. Banama-audiobook kokubili kokuzilibazisa nokufunda kanye nelabhulali enezihloko ezingaphezu kuka-7,500 eziqoshwe ezitudiyo zabo zedijithali noma ezitholakala ngokuthengisa. 

IRoyal National Institute of Blind People (RNIB) iyinhlangano esiza abantulayo yase-UK ehlinzeka ngenkonzo yomtapo wezincwadi ezikhulumayo. Ama-audiobook anikezwa ngefomethi ye-DAISY futhi alethwa endlini yomfundi ngeposi njenge-CD noma i-memory stick ye-USB. Kunama-audiobook angaphezu kuka-30,000 atholakalayo ongawabolekwa, amahhala ukuthi angaphrintwa amalungu omtapo wezincwadi akhubazekile. I-RNIB ixhasa insizakalo yezincwadi ezikhulumayo ngemali elinganiselwa ku-£4 million ngonyaka.

Umuntu okhubazekile wokuphrinta "umuntu ongakwazi ukufunda kahle okubhaliwe ngenxa yokukhubazeka okubonakalayo, ngokomzimba, kokuqonda, ukukhula, ukuqonda, noma ukufunda."[1] Ukukhubazeka kokuphrinta kuvimbela umuntu ekutholeni ulwazi ezintweni eziphrintiwe ngendlela evamile, futhi kumdinga ukuthi asebenzise ezinye izindlela zokufinyelela lolo lwazi. Ukukhubazeka kokuphrinta kuhlanganisa ukukhubazeka kokubona, ukukhubazeka kokufunda, noma ukukhubazeka ngokomzimba okuphazamisa ikhono lokukhohlisa incwadi.[2] Leli gama laqanjwa uGeorge Kerscher, iphayona ezincwadini zokukhuluma zedijithali.[3] I-DAISY isetshenziswa imitapo yolwazi njengendlela yokwenza izincwadi eziyinkimbinkimbi zifinyeleleke ngomsindo.[4] 

Ingqungquthela eyayihlelwe yi-World Intellectual Property Organisation (WIPO) e-Marrakesh, e-Morocco, ngoJuni 2013 yamukela isivumelwano esikhethekile esibizwa ngokuthi "Isivumelwano Sokusiza Ukufinyelela Imisebenzi Eshicilelwe ngabantu Abangaboni kahle kanye nabantu abanokukhubazeka kokuphrinta" (kafushane i-Marrakesh VIP Treaty).[5][6] 

ISivumelwano sase-Marrakesh simele ushintsho olubalulekile endleleni abenzi bomthetho abalinganisela ngayo izimfuno zabanikazi be-copyright ngokumelene nezintshisakalo zabantu abakhubazekile ikakhulukazi, kanye nephuzu elingaba khona lokuguquguquka kupolitiki yomhlaba wonke ye-copyright ngokuvamile kakhulu. 

Imizamo 
I-Accessible Books Consortium (ABC), eyasungulwa ngo-2014, yacatshangelwa "njengesinyathelo esisodwa esingase sibe khona, phakathi kokunye, ukufeza ngokuyikho imigomo yeSivumelwano saseMarrakesh".[7] I-ABC ihlose ukukhulisa inani lezincwadi emhlabeni wonke ngamafomethi afinyelelekayo—njenge-braille, umsindo nokuphrinta okukhulu—kanye nokuzenza zitholakale kubantu abayizimpumputhe, abangaboni kahle noma abakhubazeke ukuphrinta. 

Ukushicilela okufinyelelekayo kuyindlela yokushicilela kanye nokwakhiwa kwezincwadi lapho izincwadi neminye imibhalo yenziwa itholakale ngezinye izindlela eziklanyelwe ukusiza noma ukufaka esikhundleni senqubo yokufunda. Kubaluleke kakhulu kubantu abayizimpumputhe, abangaboni kahle noma abakhubazeke ukuphrinta. 

Amanye amafomethi akhiwe ukuze asize abantu abahlukene ukuthi bawafunde afaka izinhlobonhlobo zamafonti amakhulu, amafonti akhethekile ezinhlobo ezithile zokukhubazeka kokufunda, i-braille, i-e-books, nama-audiobook azenzakalelayo kanye nezincwadi zokukhuluma zedijithali ze-DAISY. 

Ukushicilela okufinyelelekayo kwenziwe kwaba lula ngentuthuko kwezobuchwepheshe njengokuphrinta ngokufunwa (i-POD), izifundi ze-e-book, ifomethi yedatha ehlelekile ye-XML, ifomethi ye-EPUB3 kanye ne-inthanethi. 

Inhloso 
Inhloso yokushicilela okufinyelelekayo ukwenza ukufunda kube lula kulabo abanobunzima bokwenza kanjalo. Leli qembu lihlanganisa abantu abayizimpumputhe noma abangaboni kahle, abanokukhubazeka ekufundeni, nabantu abafunda ulimi lwesibili. Ukushicilela okufinyelelekayo kuphinde kuhlose ukuvumela abantu ukuthi bafunde noma iyiphi ifomethi ebavumela ukuthi bafunde ngokushesha noma ebavumela ukuba bamunce ulwazi ngendlela engcono.

Ekhulwini lamashumi amabili nanye, inhloso yokushicilela okufinyelelekayo ukwenza yonke incwadi itholakale ngawo wonke amafomethi ukuze wonke umfundi akwazi ukufunda kalula nangobuchule. 

Imihlahlandlela nezindlela zokushicilela ngamafomethi afinyelelekayo zenziwe zatholakala izinhlangano nababhali abambalwa, okuhlanganisa: 

EDItEUR: "Ukushicilela Okufinyelelekayo - Izinkombandlela Zokusebenza Okungcono Kakhulu Yabashicileli".[1] 
U-Matt Garrish: "I-EPUB 3 Efinyelelekayo" (isahluko esitholakala mahhala esivela ku-EPUB 3 Imikhuba Enhle Kakhulu ka-Matt Garrish no-Markus Gylling, O'Reilly, 2013).[2] 
"Iziqondiso Zemidiya Efinyelelekayo Yedijithali" yiNational Center for Accessible Media (NCAM).[3] 
"Ukwenza amafayela e-PDF afinyeleleke: imihlahlandlela yesigaba sokudala i-DTP" nge-AcceDe PDF.[4] 
"Yenza idokhumenti ye-PDF ifinyeleleke ku-Adobe InDesign kanye ne-Acrobat Pro"[5] 
"Yenza idokhumenti ye-PDF itholakale ku-Microsoft Word"[6] 
Umlando 
Ngaphambi kwekhulu lama-21, imboni yokushicilela yayigxile ekukhiqizweni kwezincwadi eziphrintiwe. Ithiyori yokushicilela evelele, eyayigcizelela umnotho wesilinganiso, ijwayele ukwenza ifomethi eyodwa kuphela yencwadi enikeziwe. Ngale ndlela zingakhiqizwa ngobuningi futhi zenziwe zitholakale emphakathini jikelele. Le modeli ayizange ivumele noma iyiphi enye ifomethi ukuthi itholakale kabanzi, nokho. 

Kube nenani lentuthuko kwezobuchwepheshe okwandise ukufinyeleleka kwezincwadi. Esokuqala salokhu kwaba ukuthuthukiswa kwesistimu yokubhala ye-braille nguLouis Braille ngo-1821.[7] Kwabe sekuba nokwakhiwa kwama-audiobooks asuka kuKhongolose yase-United States ngo-1931[8] futhi aduma ngokuthuthuka ekurekhodeni nasekusetshenzisweni kwabalingisi bezwi. 

Ngo-1980, i-Thorndike Press yaba khona njengomshicileli wezincwadi ezinkulu eziphrintiwe.[9][10] U-Thorndike uthenge amalungelo ezinhlobo zokuphrinta ezinkulu zezincwadi kubashicileli wabe esezishicilela kabusha ngefomethi enkulu futhi efinyeleleka kalula yabantu abanenkinga yokufunda. 

Intuthuko yakamuva 
Abafundi abasha abaphathekayo, njengemikhiqizo ye-Victor Reader[11] kanye ne-Plextalk Pocket[12] baphatha izincwadi ezikhulumayo ngamafomethi ahlukahlukene ahlanganisa i-DAISY Digital Talking Book, i-MP3, umbhalo kuphela, nezinye eziningi. 

Ubuchwepheshe obusha, obufana nokwethulwa ku-Sony Reader[13] ka-2004 kanye ne-Amazon's Kindle[14] ngo-2007, bunikeze amandla okushintsha usayizi wefonti ngokuzenzakalelayo. 

I-ReadHowYouWant ingomunye umholi ekuthuthukiseni lobu buchwepheshe.[15] Isebenza ngokubambisana nabashicileli ukwenza izincwadi zitholakale kuwo wonke amafomethi emhlabeni wonke.[16] Lokhu kuhlanganisa amafonti aklanywe ngokukhethekile e-dyslexia, ukonakala kwe-macular kanye nezinkinga zokulandelela umugqa. 
Ukuphrinta okukhulu (futhi kuwuhlobo olukhulu noma ifonti enkulu) kubhekisela ekufomethweni kwencwadi noma omunye umbhalo lapho usayizi wefonti mkhulu kakhulu kunokuvamile ukuze kuhlaliswe abantu abangaboni kahle. Ngokuvamile i-medium nayo iyandiswa ngosayizi ukuze ivumelane nombhalo omkhulu. Imitapo yolwazi enezidingo ezikhethekile nemitapo yolwazi eminingi yomphakathi izogcina izinguqulo ezibhalwe ngamagama amakhulu, kanye nezinguqulo ezibhalwe nge-Braille.
 
Usayizi wefonti wokuphrinta okukhulu ngokuvamile okungenani unamaphuzu angu-18 ngosayizi, okulingana no-24px kusayizi wefonti yewebhu ye-CSS. Osayizi abahlukene benziwa ukuze bavumelane nezidingo ezihlukile zokubukwayo, nomthetho ovamile wesithupha wokuba okungenani ubuncane buphindwe kabili kunosayizi omncane we-acuity.[1] 


Izincwadi zokuphrinta ezinkulu 
Izindinganiso zokushicilela 
I-American National Association for Visually Handicapped (NAVH) inikeza i-NAVH Seal of Approval kubashicileli bezentengiselwano e-US, ngezincwadi ezihlangabezana nezindinganiso zabo zokuphrinta ezinkulu.[2] (I-Lighthouse International yathola i-NAVH ngo-2010.)[3] 

Amazinga[4] abiza: 

Imikhawulo ephezulu kusayizi, ukujiya, kanye nesisindo 
Imikhawulo ephansi kumamajini 
Usayizi wohlobo okungenani iphoyinti le-14, okungcono iphoyinti le-18[5] 
I-Sans serif noma ifonti eguquliwe ye-serif etuswayo 
Incwadi eyanele nesikhala samagama 
esituswayo ukuze i-House evuleleke imigqa yokubopha 

i 
-American Living I-blind ichaza osayizi befonti ngokuthi: 

12 pt = ukuphrinta okujwayelekile 
14–16 pt = ukuphrinta "okukhulisiwe" (okungabhekwa njengokuphrinta okukhulu) 
18 pt kanye nokukhudlwana = ukuphrinta okukhulu 
18 pt nangaphezulu kunezinye izinguquko zokufometha = ukuphrinta okuthuthukisiwe 
Ngaphezu kokukhulisa usayizi wohlobo, ukwakheka kwekhasi nezici zefonti kungaba nomthelela omuhle ekufundeni. Amafonti aklanyelwe ukufaneleka akwenza kube lula ukuhlukanisa uhlamvu olulodwa komunye. Ezinye izici eziyinhloko zamafonti anjalo yilezi:[6] 

Usonhlamvukazi "I" kanye nenombolo yesiRoman "I", inombolo "1", kanye nohlamvu oluncane "l" kufanele zonke zibukeke zihlukile kwenye. 
Ifonti kufanele ibe nomzimba obanzi nesikhala phakathi kohlamvu ngalunye. 
Izinhlamvu "ezinebhamuza" ngaphakathi kwazo (ezaziwa ngokuthi ikhawunta, njengokuthi o, d, g, e), kufanele zibe nesikhala esanele ngaphakathi kwekhawunta. 
Izimpawu zokuloba kufanele zibe yindilinga, zibe nkulu, futhi zibonakale kakhulu. 
Imivimbo yefonti kufanele iqine futhi ingabi nezikhala. 

Izibonelo zamafonti afundeka kalula i-Antique Olive, i-Tahoma, i-Tiresias, ne-Verdana. 

I-Ratios 
Izinkampani ezinikeza ukufometha kwezinhlamvu ezinkulu zisebenzisa amafomethi ahlukahlukene (abizwa nangokuthi ama-ratios) ukuze zisekele usayizi wefonti omkhulu.[7] Phakathi kwalezi zilinganiso, sithola: 

Isilinganiso 1:1, okuqukethwe kunwetshwa ekhasini elilodwa (1) lokuma ngobude futhi usayizi ovamile we-typological ungamaphuzu angu-18.
Isilinganiso 1:2, okuqukethwe kunwetshwa ekhasini le-landscape amabili (2) futhi usayizi we-typological ojwayelekile ungamaphuzu ayi-18. 
Izilinganiso zangokwezifiso, okuqukethwe kunwetshwa emakhasini amaningi okwakheka kwezwe futhi usayizi ojwayelekile we-typological ungamaphuzu angama-28. 
Umlando 
Omkhulu Wezilinganiso Zokuphrinta 
Isimo samanje siyasebenza
 
Phakathi kwabashicileli bokuqala bezincwadi ezinkulu eziphrintiwe, i-Clear Type Publishing Company yashicilela iqoqo lezincwadi ngohlobo lwamaphuzu angama-36, c. 1910.[8] Inkampani ezinze e-Ohio ekhetheke ngokuphrinta okukhulu, ishicilela izincwadi ngo-36pt kanye no-24pt.[9]

Ngo-1914 uRobert Irwin wakhiqiza uchungechunge lwezincwadi zokufunda ngamaphuzu angama-36, zezingane ezingaboni kahle ezikoleni zaseCleveland, e-Ohio. Lolu hlobo lubonakale lukhulu kakhulu futhi lwashiywa ngokushesha endaweni edume kakhulu yamaphoyinti angama-24. Ucwaningo olwaxhaswe ngu-Irwin ngo-1919 lwabonisa uhlobo lwamaphuzu angama-24 ukuthi lufundeka kakhulu kosayizi abahloliwe. Ucwaningo olwengeziwe olwenziwa ngabanye ngo-1952 nango-1959 lwasekela amaphuzu angu-18 noma uhlobo lwamaphuzu angu-24.[10] 

E-UK ngo-1964, uFrederick Thorpe waqala ukunyathelisa izihloko zokuphrinta ezijwayelekile ezinohlobo olucishe luphindwe kabili kunolokuqala olwalunyathelisiwe. Lezi zincwadi zanikezwa amabhantshi othuli angenalutho, anekhodi enemibala ukuze abonise izigaba ezinjengezimfihlakalo (ezimnyama), izinganekwane ezivamile (ezibomvu), ezothando (eziluhlaza okwesibhakabhaka), ezaseNtshonalanga (owolintshi), njll. Lezi zinhlelo ezinkulu ezibonakalayo kubikwe ukuthi zinzima kwabanye abafundi ukuzisingatha. 

Ngo-1969, inkampani kaThorpe, i-Ulverscroft, yaqala ukukhiqiza izincwadi ngohlobo lwamaphuzu ayi-16 kanye nezibopho ezinosayizi ojwayelekile, inkampani ethi kwandisa ukwamukelwa kwemibhalo emikhulu emitapo yolwazi yomphakathi. Uhlobo lwamaphuzu ayi-16 luncane kunenani eliphansi elinconywe uMkhandlu WaseMelika Wabangaboni,[11] otusa amaphoyinti angama-20, ngamaphoyinti ayi-18 njengokuncane okuphakanyisiwe.[12] 

Ngo-2008 i-W3.org yakhipha i-WCAG 2.0 amazinga okufinyeleleka kuwebhu, achaza umbhalo omkhulu ngokuthi 18pt, okungu-24px ku-CSS.[13] Ngaphezu kwalokho, izinga licacisa ukuthi abasebenzisi kufanele bakwazi ukukhulisa usayizi wefonti ngo-200% ngaphandle kokwephula okuqukethwe.[14] 

Namuhla izinhlelo zokuphrinta ezinkulu zezinye zezincwadi zamanje zinyatheliswa kanyekanye nezinguqulo eziphrintiwe ezijwayelekile ngabashicileli bazo futhi ngokuvamile zifaka amabhantshi anemibala egcwele efanayo nomklamo wamabhantshi. Imitapo yolwazi yomphakathi ivamise ukuba nezingxenye zokuphrinta ezinkulu, futhi izitolo zezincwadi eziningi ziphethe imibhalo emikhulu yokuphrinta. 

"I-Google Print" iqondisa kabusha lapha; akufanele kudidaniswe ne-Google Cloud Print. 
Lesi sihloko simayelana nenjini yokusesha yezincwadi ye-Google. Ngesevisi ye-e-book ye-Google, bona i-Google Play Books. Ngencwadi yezingane, bheka i-Google Book. 
Isithombe-skrini se- 
Google Amabhuku 
Uhlobo lwesayithi 
Umnikazi Welabhulali Yedijithali Umnikazi we-URL ye-Google 
books.google.com 
Ithulwe ngo-Okthoba 2004; Eminyakeni engu-20 edlule (njenge-Google Print)

I-Google Books (phambilini eyayaziwa ngokuthi Usesho lwe-Google Book, i-Google Print, futhi ngegama layo lekhodi elithi Project Ocean) [1] iyisevisi evela kwa-Google esesha umbhalo ogcwele wezincwadi namamagazini i-Google ewaskene, yaguqulelwa kumbhalo isebenzisa ukuqaphela uhlamvu olubonakalayo (OCR), futhi igcinwe kusizindalwazi sayo sedijithali.[2] Izincwadi zihlinzekwa ngabashicileli nababhali ngohlelo lukazakwabo we-Google Books, noma ozakwethu belabhulali ye-Google ngephrojekthi Yelabhulali.[3] Ukwengeza, i-Google ibambisene nenani labashicileli bamamagazini ukwenza ingobo yabo yomlando ibe yidijithali.[4][5] 

Uhlelo Lomshicileli lwaqala ukwaziwa nge-Google Print ngenkathi lwethulwa e-Frankfurt Book Fair ngo-Okthoba 2004. I-Google Books Library Project, eskena imisebenzi eqoqweni lozakwethu belabhulali bese ibangeza kuhlu lwedijithali, yamenyezelwa ngo-December 2004. 

Isinyathelo se-Google Books sanconywa ngamandla aso okunikeza ukufinyelela okungakaze kubonwe ngaphambili ku-inthanethi [7] engase ibe yinhlangano yabantu [7] ukwenziwa ngentando yeningi kolwazi.[8] Kodwa-ke, iphinde yagxekwa ngokwephulwa kwe-copyright okungenzeka,[8][9] kanye nokuntuleka kokuhlela ukulungisa amaphutha amaningi alethwe emibhalweni eskeniwe yinqubo ye-OCR. 

Kusukela ngo-Okthoba 2019, i-Google igubhe iminyaka engu-15 ye-Google Books futhi yanikeza inani lezincwadi eziskeniwe njengezihloko ezingaphezu kwezigidi ezingu-40.[10] I-Google yalinganisela ngo-2010 ukuthi kwakunezihloko ezihlukene ezingaba izigidi ezingu-130 emhlabeni, [11] futhi yathi ihlose ukuziskena zonke.[11] Kodwa-ke, inqubo yokuskena emitatsheni yolwazi yaseMelika yehlile kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-2000s.[12][13] Imizamo yokuskena ye-Google Book ibe ngaphansi kwecala, okuhlanganisa i-Authors Guild v. Google, icala lesenzo sekilasi e-United States, elinqunywe ngokuvumelana ne-Google (bona ngezansi). Lesi kwakuyicala elikhulu elasondela ekushintsheni izinqubo ze-copyright zemisebenzi yezintandane e-United States.[14] Ucwaningo lwango-2023 olwenziwa yizazi ze-University of California, Berkeley, kanye nezikole zebhizinisi zase-Northeastern University luthole ukuthi ukwenziwa kwezincwadi ngedijithali kwe-Google Books kuholele ekwenyukeni kokuthengiswa kwezinguqulo ezingokoqobo zezincwadi.[15] 

Imininingwane 
Imiphumela evela ku-Google Books ibonakala kukho kokubili Usesho lwe-Google olutholakala emhlabeni wonke kanye nakuwebhusayithi yokusesha ye-Google Books ezinikele (books.google.com). 

Ukuphendula imibuzo yosesho, i-Google Books ivumela abasebenzisi ukuthi babuke amakhasi aphelele ezincwadini lapho amagama okusesha avela khona uma incwadi ingaphandle kwe-copyright noma uma umnikazi we-copyright enikezile imvume. Uma i-Google ikholelwa ukuthi ibhuku lisengaphansi kwe-copyright, umsebenzisi ubona "amazwibela" ombhalo eduze kwamagama osesho abuziwe. Zonke izimo zamagama okusesha embhalweni wencwadi zivela nokugqamile okuphuzi. 

Amaleveli amane okufinyelela asetshenziswa ku-Google Books yilawa:[16]

Ukubuka okugcwele: Amabhuku esizindeni somphakathi ayatholakala ukuze "ubukwe ngokugcwele" futhi angadawunilodeka mahhala. Izincwadi eziphrintiwe ezitholwe ngohlelo lukazakwethu nazo ziyatholakala ukuze zibukwe ngokugcwele uma umshicileli enike imvume, nakuba lokhu kuyivelakancane. 
Ukuhlola kuqala: Ezincwadini eziphrintiwe lapho imvume inikiwe khona, inombolo yamakhasi abukekayo ikhawulelwe "ekubukeni kuqala" okusethwe imikhawulo eyahlukene yokufinyelela nezinyathelo zokuphepha, ezinye zisekelwe ekulandeleni komsebenzisi. Ngokuvamile, umshicileli angasetha iphesenti lencwadi elitholakalayo ukuze lihlolwe kuqala.[17] Abasebenzisi bavinjelwe ukukopisha, ukulanda noma ukuphrinta ukuhlola kuqala kwebhuku. I-watermark efundwayo ethi "Copyrighted material" ivela phansi emakhasini. Wonke amabhuku atholwe ngohlelo lukazakwethu ayatholakala ukuze abukwe kuqala. 
Ukubuka amazwibela: "Ukubuka amazwibela" - imigqa emibili kuya kwemithathu yombhalo ezungeze igama lokusesha elibuzwayo - kuboniswa ezimeni lapho i-Google ingenayo imvume yomnikazi we-copyright yokubonisa ukuhlola kuqala. Lokhu kungenxa yokuthi i-Google ayikwazi ukuhlonza umnikazi noma umnikazi wenqabe imvume. Uma igama lokusesha livela izikhathi eziningi encwadini, i-Google ayibonisi amazwibela angaphezu kwamathathu, ngaleyo ndlela ivimbele umsebenzisi ukuthi abuke incwadi eningi kakhulu. Futhi, i-Google ayibonisi amazwibela ezincwadi ezithile eziyisethenjwa, njengezichazamazwi, lapho ukuvezwa kwamazwibela angalimaza imakethe yomsebenzi. I-Google imile ekutheni ayikho imvume edingekayo ngaphansi komthetho we-copyright ukuze kuboniswe amazwibela.[18] 
Akukho ukubuka kuqala: I-Google iphinde ibonise imiphumela yosesho yezincwadi ezingafakwanga kwidijithali. Njengoba lezi zincwadi zingaskenwanga, umbhalo wazo awusesheki futhi imethadatha kuphela efana nesihloko, umbhali, umshicileli, inombolo yamakhasi, i-ISBN, isihloko kanye nolwazi lwe-copyright, futhi kwezinye izimo, kutholakala ithebula lokuqukethwe nesifinyezo sencwadi. Empeleni, lokhu kufana nekhathalogi yamakhadi omtapo wezincwadi aku-inthanethi.[3] 
Ukuphendula ukugxekwa okuvela emaqenjini afana ne-American Association of Publishers kanye ne-Authors Guild, i-Google yamemezela inqubomgomo yokuphuma ngo-August 2005, lapho abanikazi be-copyright bengahlinzeka ngohlu lwezihloko abangafuni ukuthi ziskenwe, futhi isicelo sizohlonishwa. Inkampani iphinde yathi ngeke iskene noma yiziphi izincwadi ze-copyright phakathi kuka-Agasti no-1 Novemba 2005, ukuze inikeze abanikazi ithuba lokunquma ukuthi yiziphi izincwadi abangazikhipha kuPhrojekthi. Ngakho, abanikazi bamalungelo okukopisha banezinketho ezintathu maqondana nanoma yimuphi umsebenzi:[18] 

Ingabamba iqhaza Kuhlelo Lozakwethu ukwenza incwadi itholakale ukuze ibukwe kuqala noma ibukwe ngokugcwele, lapho izokwabelana ngemali engenayo etholakala ekubonisweni kwamakhasi asuka emsebenzini iphendula imibuzo yabasebenzisi. 
Ingavumela i-Google ukuthi iskene ibhuku ngaphansi Kwephrojekthi Yelabhulali futhi ibonise amazwibela ekuphenduleni imibuzo yabasebenzisi.
Ingaphuma Kuphrojekthi Yelabhulali, lapho i-Google ingeke iskene incwadi. Uma ibhuku seliskeniwe kakade, i-Google izosetha kabusha izinga layo lokufinyelela njengokuthi 'Akukho ukuhlola kuqala'.  
Imisebenzi eminingi eskeniwe ayisanyathelisiwe noma ayisatholakali ngokwentengiso.[19]

Ngokungeziwe ekuthengeni izincwadi emitapweni yolwazi, i-Google iphinde ithole izincwadi kubashicileli bayo, ngokusebenzisa "Uhlelo Lozakwethu" - oluklanyelwe ukusiza abashicileli nababhali baphromothe izincwadi zabo. Abashicileli nababhali bahambisa ikhophi yedijithali yencwadi yabo ngefomethi ye-EPUB noma ye-PDF, noma ikhophi ephrintiwe ku-Google, eyenziwa yatholakala ku-Google Books ukuze ibukwe kuqala. Umshicileli angakwazi ukulawula iphesenti lebhuku elitholakalayo ukuze libukwe kuqala, ubuncane bube ngu-20%. Bangaphinde bakhethe ukwenza incwadi ibukeke ngokugcwele, futhi baze bavumele abasebenzisi ukuthi badawunilode ikhophi ye-PDF. Izincwadi zingenziwa futhi ukuthi zitholakale ukuze zithengiswe ku-Google Play.[3] Ngokungafani neProjekthi Yelabhulali, lokhu akuphakamisi noma yikuphi ukukhathazeka ngelungelo lobunikazi njengoba kwenziwa ngokuvumelana nesivumelwano nomshicileli. Umshicileli angakhetha ukuhoxa esivumelwaneni nganoma yisiphi isikhathi.[18] 

Ezincwadini eziningi, i-Google Books ibonisa izinombolo zamakhasi okuqala. Kodwa-ke, u-Tim Parks, ebhala ku-New York Review of Books ngo-2014, waphawula ukuthi i-Google iyekile ukunikeza izinombolo zamakhasi ezincwadini eziningi zakamuva (cishe lezo ezitholwe ngoHlelo Lozakwethu) "ngokunokwenzeka ngokubambisana nabashicileli, ukuze kuphoqwe thina esidinga ukulungiselela imibhalo yaphansi ukuthi sithenge izinhlelo zephepha."[20] 

Ukuskena kwezincwadi 
Iphrojekthi20 iqale ngaphansi kwekhodi ye-Ocean. Umsunguli we-Google u-Larry Page ubehlale enentshisekelo yokwenza izincwadi zibe yidijithali. Ngenkathi yena noMarissa Mayer beqala ukuzama ukuskena izincwadi ngo-2002, kwabathatha imizuzu engama-40 ukuthi bafake kudijithali incwadi enamakhasi angama-300. Kodwa ngokushesha ngemva kokuba ubuchwepheshe sebuthuthukisiwe kangangokuthi ama-opharetha athwebulayo akwazi ukuskena amakhasi afinyelela kwangu-6000 ngehora.[14]

I-Google isungule izikhungo zokuskena eziqokiwe lapho izincwadi zithuthwa khona ngamaloli. Iziteshi zingafaka idijithali ngesilinganiso samakhasi ayi-1,000 ngehora. Izincwadi zibekwe kumbeleko owakhelwe ngokwezifiso olungisa umgogodla webhuku endaweni ngenkathi izibani eziningi nezinsimbi ezibonakalayo ziskena amakhasi amabili avuliwe. Ikhasi ngalinye lizoba namakhamera amabili aqondiswe kulo athwebula isithombe, kuyilapho isitholi sebanga i-LIDAR simboze igridi ye-laser enezinhlangothi ezintathu endaweni yencwadi ukuze ithwebule ukugoba kwephepha. Umuntu wayevula amakhasi ngesandla, esebenzisa inyathela ukuze athathe izithombe. Ngaphandle kwesidingo sokucaba amakhasi noma ukuwaqondanisa kahle, isistimu ye-Google ayifinyelelanga nje kuphela ukusebenza kahle nesivinini kodwa futhi yasiza ukuvikela amaqoqo abuthaka ekuphathweni ngokweqile. Ngemuva kwalokho, izithombe ezingcolile zidlule emazingeni amathathu okucubungula: okokuqala, ama-algorithms e-de-warping asebenzisa idatha ye-LIDAR ukulungisa ukugoba kwamakhasi. Bese, isofthiwe ye-optical character recognition (OCR) yaguqula izithombe ezingahluziwe zaba umbhalo, futhi, ekugcineni, omunye umjikelezo we-algorithms wakhipha izinombolo zekhasi, imibhalo yaphansi, imidwebo nemidwebo.[14] 

Eziningi zezincwadi ziskenwa kusetshenziswa ikhamera eyenziwe ngokwezifiso ye-Elphel 323[21][22] ngenani lamakhasi ayi-1,000 ngehora.[23] Ilungelo lobunikazi elinikezwe i-Google ngo-2009 liveze ukuthi i-Google iqhamuke nohlelo olusha lokuskena amabhuku olusebenzisa amakhamera amabili kanye nesibani se-infrared ukuze silungise ngokuzenzakalelayo ukugoba kwamakhasi encwadini. Ngokwakha imodeli ye-3D yekhasi ngalinye bese "iyisusa-i-warping", i-Google iyakwazi ukwethula amakhasi abukeka eyisicaba ngaphandle kokwenza amakhasi abe sicaba, okudinga ukusetshenziswa kwezindlela ezilimazayo ezifana nokuqaqa noma amapuleti engilazi ukuze enze isicaba ekhasini ngalinye, okuyinto engasebenzi kahle ukuskena ngezinga elikhulu.[24][25] 

I-Google inqume ukushiya imininingwane yombala ukuze ivune ukulungiswa okungcono kwendawo, njengoba izincwadi eziningi ezazingaphandle kwe-copyright ngaleso sikhathi zazingenayo imibala. Isithombe ngasinye sekhasi sidluliselwe kuma-algorithms ahlukanisa umbhalo nezifunda zemifanekiso. Izifunda zombhalo bese zicutshungulwa kusetshenziswa i-OCR ukuze kunikwe amandla ukusesha kombhalo ogcwele. I-Google isebenzise izinsiza ezinkulu ekuqhamukeni namasu aphelele okucindezela, okuhloswe ngawo ukuba nekhwalithi ephezulu yesithombe kuyilapho igcina osayizi befayela beyingcosana ukuze ivumele ukufinyelela kubasebenzisi be-inthanethi abanomkhawulokudonsa ophansi.[26] 

Ukusebenza kwewebhusayithi
Kumsebenzi ngamunye, i-Google Books ikhiqiza ngokuzenzakalelayo ikhasi lokubuka. Leli khasi libonisa ulwazi olukhishwe encwadini—imininingwane yayo yokushicilela, imephu yamagama ephindaphindwayo, uhlu lokuqukethwe—kanye nezinto zesibili, njengezifinyezo, ukubuyekezwa kwabafundi (okungafundeki kunguqulo yeselula yewebhusayithi), kanye nezixhumanisi zeminye imibhalo efanele. Isivakashi sekhasi, isibonelo, singabona uhlu lwezincwadi ezabelana ngohlobo olufanayo nendikimba, noma singabona uhlu lwezifundo zamanje encwadini. Ngaphezu kwalokho, lokhu okuqukethwe kunikeza amathuba okusebenzelana kubasebenzisi abangene ngemvume ku-akhawunti yabo ye-Google. Bangakwazi ukuthekelisa idatha ye-bibliographic nezingcaphuno ngamafomethi avamile, babhale ukubuyekezwa kwabo, bakwengeze emtapweni wabo wolwazi ukuze amakwe, ahlelwe, futhi kwabelwane ngawo nabanye abantu.[27][28] Ngakho-ke, i-Google Books iqoqa lezi zici ezitolikayo kusukela kuhlu lwemithombo, okuhlanganisa abasebenzisi, amasayithi ezinkampani zangaphandle njenge-Goodreads, futhi ngokuvamile umbhali nomshicileli wencwadi.[29] 

Eqinisweni, ukukhuthaza ababhali ukuthi balayishe ezabo izincwadi, i-Google yengeze imisebenzi embalwa kuwebhusayithi. Ababhali bangavumela izivakashi ukuthi zilande i-ebook yazo mahhala, noma zingasetha intengo yazo yokuthenga. Bangakwazi ukushintsha intengo baye phambili naphambili, banikeze izaphulelo noma nini lapho ibafanele. Futhi, uma umbhali wencwadi ekhetha ukwengeza inombolo yerekhodi ye-ISBN, i-LCCN noma i-OCLC, isevisi izobuyekeza i-url yebhuku ukuze iyifake. Bese, umbhali angasetha ikhasi elithile njengehange lesixhumanisi. Le nketho yenza incwadi yabo itholakale kalula.
 Isihloko esikhulu se- 
Ngram Viewer 
: I-Google Ngram Viewer
I-Ngram Viewer iyisevisi exhunywe ku-Google Books ebonisa imvamisa yokusetshenziswa kwamagama kulo lonke iqoqo lawo lezincwadi. Le nkonzo ibalulekile kosomlando kanye nezazi zezilimi njengoba inganikeza ukubukeka kwangaphakathi kwesiko lomuntu ngokusebenzisa amagama phakathi nenkathi yesikhathi.[30] Lolu hlelo lugxekwe ngenxa yamaphutha kumethadatha esetshenziswe kuhlelo.[31] 

Izinkinga zokuqukethwe nokugxekwa 
Le phrojekthi ithole ukugxekwa ngokuthi inhloso yayo eshiwo yokugcina imisebenzi yezintandane nengashicilelwe isengcupheni ngenxa yedatha eskeniwe enamaphutha kanye nezinkinga ezinjalo ezingaxazululeki.[32][33] 

Amaphutha okuskena 

Isandla esiskenwe encwadini ye-Google 
Inqubo yokuskena ingaphansi kwamaphutha. Isibonelo, amanye amakhasi angase angafundeki, abheke phansi, noma ahleleke ngendlela engafanele. Izazi ziye zabika ngisho namakhasi ashwabene, izithupha neminwe engabonakali, kanye nezithombe ezigcotshiwe noma ezilufifi.[34] Kulolu daba, isimemezelo esivela ku-Google ekupheleni kwezincwadi eziskeniwe sithi: 
Amaphutha kumethadatha

Ukwenziwa kwedijithali ezingeni eliyisisekelo kakhulu kusekelwe ezithombeni zamakhasi ezincwadi ezibonakalayo. Ukuze senze leli bhuku litholakale njengefayela elifomethiwe ye-ePub sithathe lezo zithombe zekhasi futhi sakhipha umbhalo sisebenzisa ubuchwepheshe be-Optical Character Recognition (noma i-OCR ngamafuphi). Ukukhishwa kombhalo ezithombeni zekhasi kuwumsebenzi onzima wobunjiniyela. Ama-smudges emakhasini ezincwadi ezibonakalayo, amafonti amahle, amafonti amadala, amakhasi adabukile, njll. konke kungaholela emaphutheni embhalweni okhishiwe. I-OCR engaphelele iyinselelo yokuqala kuphela emgomweni wokugcina wokusuka emaqoqweni ezithombe zekhasi uye ezincwadini ezisuselwe kumbhalo okhishiwe. Ama-algorithms ekhompuyutha yethu nawo kufanele anqume ngokuzenzakalelayo ukwakheka kwencwadi (ziyini izihloko nonyaweni, lapho izithombe zibekwe khona, noma ngabe umbhalo uyivesi noma iphrozi, njalonjalo). Ukuthola leli lungelo kusivumela ukuba sinikeze incwadi ngendlela elandela ifomethi yencwadi yokuqala. Ngaphandle kwemizamo yethu emihle kakhulu ungase ubone amaphutha esipelingi, izinhlamvu zikadoti, izithombe ezingavamile, noma amakhasi angekho kule ncwadi. Ngokusekelwe ezilinganisweni zethu, lawa maphutha akufanele akuvimbele ekujabuleleni okuqukethwe yincwadi. Izinselele zobuchwepheshe zokwakha ngokuzenzakalelayo incwadi ephelele ziyethusa, kodwa siyaqhubeka nokwenza izithuthukisi ku-OCR yethu kanye nobuchwepheshe bokukhipha isakhiwo sebhuku.[35] 

Ngo-2009, i-Google yathi izoqala ukusebenzisa i-reCAPTCHA ukusiza ukulungisa amaphutha atholakala kumaskeni we-Google Book. Le ndlela izothuthukisa kuphela amagama askeniwe okunzima ukuwabona ngenxa yenqubo yokuskena futhi ayikwazi ukuxazulula amaphutha anjengamakhasi aphendukile noma amagama avinjiwe.[36] 

Amaphutha okuskena akhuthaze imisebenzi yobuciko efana namaqoqo ashicilelwe amakhasi angavamile kanye nebhulogi ye-Tumblr.[37] 

Izazi zivame ukubika amaphutha adlangile kulwazi lwemethadatha ku-Google Amabhuku - okuhlanganisa ababhali abangabaluliwe kanye nezinsuku eziyiphutha zokushicilelwa. UGeoffrey Nunberg, isazi sezilimi esicwaninga ngezinguquko ekusetshenzisweni kwamagama ngokuhamba kwesikhathi waphawula ukuthi ukusesha izincwadi ezishicilelwe ngaphambi kuka-1950 futhi eziqukethe igama elithi “internet” kuveze imiphumela ebingalindelekile engama-527. UWoody Allen kukhulunywa ngaye ezincwadini ezingama-325 ngokusobala ezishicilelwe ngaphambi kokuba azalwe. I-Google iphendule uNunberg ngokusola inqwaba yamaphutha kosonkontileka bangaphandle.[31] 

Amanye amaphutha emethadatha abikiwe ahlanganisa nezinsuku zokushicilelwa ngaphambi kokuzalwa kombhali (isb. 182 isebenza nguCharles Dickens ngaphambi kokuzalwa kwakhe ngo-1812); ukuhlukaniswa kwezihloko okungalungile (uhlelo lwe-Moby Dick olutholakala ngaphansi "kwamakhompyutha", umlando we-Mae West obekwe ngaphansi "kwenkolo"), izigaba ezingqubuzanayo (izinguqulo ezingu-10 ze-Whitman's Leaves of Grass zonke zihlukaniswa ngokuthi "inganekwane" kanye "nokungelona iqiniso"), izihloko ezipelwe ngokungalungile, ababhali, nabashicileli (i-Moby Dick ene-app engalungile, i-White metall yencwadi eyodwa engalungile: noma i-Ward Dick engalungile) incwadi ehluke ngokuphelele (imethadatha yomsebenzi wezibalo wango-1818 iholela enovelini yothando yango-1963).[38] [39]

Ukubuyekezwa kombhali, isihloko, umshicileli, nama-elementi emethadatha onyaka wokushicilelwa kwamarekhodi angu-400 akhethwe ngokungahleliwe e-Google Books yenziwe. Imiphumela ibonisa u-36% wezincwadi eziyisampula kuphrojekthi yokwenza idijithali iqukethe amaphutha emethadatha. Leli zinga lephutha lingaphezulu kwalokho umuntu angalindela ukulithola kukhathalogi ye-inthanethi yomtapo wolwazi.[40] 

Isilinganiso samaphutha sisonke esingu-36.75% esitholwe kulolu cwaningo siphakamisa ukuthi imethadatha ye-Google Books inezinga eliphezulu lephutha. Nakuba amaphutha "amakhulu" kanye "namancane" angumehluko ozimele osuselwe kumqondo othize onganqunyiwe "wokutholakala", amaphutha atholakala kuzakhi ezine zemethadatha ezihlolwe kulolu cwaningo kufanele wonke abhekwe njengokukhulu.[40] 

Amaphutha emethadatha asekelwe kumadethi okuskeniwe okungalungile enze ucwaningo kusetshenziswa isizindalwazi sephrojekthi ye-Google Books lwaba nzima. Ngokwendatshana ka-2009 ka-Geoffrey Nunberg, i-Google yayiwazi lawa maphutha futhi isebenzela ukuwalungisa.[41] 
 
Izinkinga zolimi 
Abanye osopolitiki kanye nezihlakaniphi zase-Europe bawugxekile umzamo we-Google ngezizathu ze-imperialism yolimi. Baphikisa ngokuthi ngenxa yokuthi iningi lezincwadi ezihlongozwayo ukuba askeniwe ngezesiNgisi, kuzoholela ekumelelekeni okungafani kwezilimi zemvelo emhlabeni wedijithali. IsiJalimane, isiRashiya, isiFulentshi, neSpanishi, isibonelo, izilimi ezidumile ekufundiseni. Ukugcizelelwa kwe-inthanethi okungalingani kwesiNgisi, nokho, kungabumba ukufinyelela kumfundaze womlando, futhi, ekugcineni, ukukhula nokuqondisa komfundaze wesikhathi esizayo. Kulaba bagxeki kukhona uJean-Noël Jeanneney, owayengumongameli we-Bibliothèque nationale de France.[42][43] 

I-Google Books iphikisana ne-Google Scholar
Yize i-Google Books ifake kudijithali izinombolo ezinkulu zezindaba ezibuya kujenali, ukuskena kwayo akufaki imethadatha edingekayo ukuze kutholakale ama-athikili athile ezindabeni ezithile. Lokhu kuholele ekutheni abakhi be-Google Scholar baqale olwabo uhlelo lokufaka kudijithali futhi babambe ama-athikili amajenali amadala (ngokuvumelana nabashicileli bawo).[44] 

Ozakwethu belabhulali 
I-Google Books Library Project ihloselwe ukuskena nokwenza amaqoqo emitapo yolwazi eminingana emikhulu asesheke.[45] Kanye nolwazi lwe-bibliographic, amazwibela ombhalo ophuma encwadini ngokuvamile ayabukeka. Uma incwadi ingaphandle kwelungelo lobunikazi futhi isendaweni yomphakathi, le ncwadi itholakala ngokugcwele ukuthi ifundwe noma ilandwe.[16] 

Izincwadi ze-copyright eziskeniwe nge-Library Project zenziwa zitholakale ku-Google Books ukuze zibukwe amazwibela. Mayelana nekhwalithi yokuskena, i-Google iyavuma ukuthi "ayihlali inekhwalithi ephezulu ngokwanele" ukuthi ingathengiswa ku-Google Play. Futhi, ngenxa yezinkinga ezicatshangelwayo zobuchwepheshe, i-Google ayifaki izikena ngezinguqulo zekhwalithi ephezulu ezingase zinikezwe abashicileli.[46] 

Le phrojekthi iyisihloko secala le-Authors Guild v. Google, elafakwa ngo-2005 futhi lavuna i-Google ngo-2013, futhi, ngesikhalazo, ngo-2015. 

Abanikazi be-copyright bangafuna amalungelo ebhuku eliskeniwe futhi balenze litholakale ukuze libukwe kuqala noma libukwe ngokugcwele ("ngokulidlulisela" ku-akhawunti yabo yoHlelo Lukazakwabo), noma bacele i-Google ukuthi ivimbele umbhalo wencwadi oseshweni.[4] 

Isibalo sezikhungo ezibambe iqhaza kuPhrojekthi Yemitapo Yezincwadi ikhulile kusukela yasungulwa.[47] 

Ozakwethu bokuqala 

Lesi sigaba sidinga ukubuyekezwa. Sicela usize ukubuyekeza lesi sihloko ukuze sibonise izehlakalo zakamuva noma ulwazi olusha olutholakalayo. (Novemba 2024) 

Isaziso mayelana nephrojekthi yase-Michigan University Library 
Harvard University, Harvard University Library[48]
I-Harvard University Library kanye ne-Google yenze uvivinyo unyaka wonke ka-2005. Le phrojekthi yaqhubeka, ngenhloso yokwandisa ukufinyelela ku-inthanethi ku-Harvard University Library, ehlanganisa imiqulu engaphezu kwezigidi ezingu-15.8. Nakuba ukufinyelela ngokomzimba ezintweni zomtapo wezincwadi we-Harvard ngokuvamile kukhawulelwe kubafundi bamanje base-Harvard, ubuhlakani, nabacwaningi, noma kwizazi ezingeza eCambridge, Massachusetts, I-Harvard-Google Project yakhelwe ukunika amandla womabili amalungu omphakathi wase-Harvard nabasebenzisi yonke indawo ukuthola imisebenzi eqoqweni le-Harvard. 
University of Michigan, University of Michigan Library[49] 
Kusukela ngo-March 2012, imiqulu eyizigidi ezingu-5.5 iskenwa.[50] 
Ilabhulali Yomphakathi YaseNew York[51] 
Kulolu hlelo lokuhlola, i-NYPL isebenza ne-Google ukuze inikeze iqoqo lezincwadi zayo zesizinda somphakathi, ezizoskenwa ziphelele futhi zenziwe zitholakale mahhala emphakathini ku-inthanethi. Abasebenzisi bazokwazi ukusesha futhi baphequlule umbhalo ogcwele wale misebenzi. Uma inqubo yokuskena isiqediwe, izincwadi zingafinyelelwa kokubili kuwebhusayithi ye-New York Public Library kanye nasenjinini yokusesha ye-Google.[51] 
I-University of Oxford, I-Bodleian Library[52] 
I-Stanford University, I-Stanford University Libraries (SULAIR)[53] 
Ozakwethu abengeziwe 
Abanye ozakwethu bezikhungo bajoyine iphrojekthi kusukela kwamenyezelwa okokuqala ubudlelwano:[54] I 

-Austrian National Library[55] 
I-Bavarian State Library[56]
