I-University of Lanne yase-California, i-University of Lanne California yaseLausanne[56][67] 
University of Mysore, Mysore University Library 
Ubambiswano bekuwukwenza imibhalo engu-800,000 kudijithali, kuhlanganise nemibhalo yesandla ebhalwe emakhasini esundu ahlehlela emuva ekhulwini lesishiyagalombili.[68][69] 
Inyuvesi yase-Texas e-Austin, eNyuvesi yase-Texas Imitapo yolwazi[70] 
Ubambiswano bekuwukwenza kudijithali iqoqo lomtapo wezincwadi waseLatin America - imiqulu engaba ingxenye yesigidi.[50] 
University of Virginia, University of Virginia Library[71] 
University of Wisconsin-Madison, University of Wisconsin Libraries[72] 
Kusukela ngo-March 2012, cishe 600,000 imiqulu yayisikeniwe.[50] 
Umlando
2002: Iqembu lamalungu eqembu kwa-Google lethula ngokusemthethweni "iphrojekthi 'yezincwadi' eyimfihlo."[73] Abasunguli be-Google u-Sergey Brin no-Larry Page baqhamuke nombono wokuthi kamuva baba yi-Google Books ngenkathi besathweswa iziqu e-Stanford ngo-1996. Ikhasi lomlando kuwebhusayithi ye-Google Books lichaza umbono wabo wokuqala wale phrojekthi: "ezweni elizayo lezincwadi, abantu bazosebenzisa iqoqo elikhulu lezincwadi khomba okuqukethwe kwezincwadi futhi uhlaziye ukuxhumana phakathi kwazo, unquma noma iyiphi incwadi ehlotshaniswa nokufaneleka nokuba wusizo kwayo ngokulandelela inombolo nekhwalithi yezingcaphuno ezivela kwezinye izincwadi."[73] Leli thimba livakashele izingosi zeminye yemizamo emikhulu yokwenza idijithali ngaleso sikhathi okuhlanganisa i-American Memory Project ye-Congress yeCongress, i-Project Gutenberg, kanye ne-Universal Library ukuze lithole ukuthi zisebenza kanjani, isisekelo seNyuvesi, kanye ne-Michigan. amaphrojekthi afana ne-JSTOR kanye ne-Making of America. Engxoxweni noMongameli wangaleso sikhathi weNyuvesi uMary Sue Coleman, lapho uPage ethola ukuthi isilinganiso samanje senyuvesi sokuskena wonke amavolumu omtapo wolwazi sasiyiminyaka eyinkulungwane, kubikwa ukuthi u-Page watshela u-Coleman ukuthi "ukholelwa ukuthi i-Google ingasiza ukuthi kwenzeke ngezinyanga eziyisithupha. 

" "ezinye izici ezingalindelekile."[73] 

Disemba 2004: I-Google isayine isandiso kuhlelo lwayo lwe-Google Print olwaziwa nge-Google Print Library Project.[47] I-Google imemezele ubudlelwano namanyuvesi ambalwa asezingeni eliphezulu kanye nemitapo yolwazi yomphakathi, okuhlanganisa i-University of Michigan, i-Harvard (i-Harvard University Library), i-Stanford (i-Green Library), i-Oxford (i-Bodleian Library), kanye ne-New York Public Library. Ngokwemibiko yabezindaba kanye nabaphathi bamalabhulali basenyuvesi, i-Google ihlele ukwenza idijithali futhi yenze itholakale ngesevisi yayo Yezincwadi ze-Google cishe imiqulu eyizigidi eziyi-15 phakathi neminyaka eyishumi. Lesi simemezelo maduzane savusa impikiswano, njengoba izinhlangano zabashicileli nababhali ziphonsela inselelo izinhlelo ze-Google zokwenza, hhayi nje izincwadi ezisesizindeni somphakathi, kodwa nezihloko ezisengaphansi kwe-copyright. 

Septhemba–Okthoba 2005: Amacala amabili abhekene ne-Google athi inkampani ayizange ihloniphe amalungelo okukopisha futhi yehlulekile ukunxephezela ngendlela efanele ababhali nabashicileli. Enye iyisimangalo sekilasi egameni lababhali (I-Authors Guild v. Google, Septhemba 20, 2005) kanti enye iyicala lombango elilethwe abashicileli abakhulu abahlanu kanye ne-Association of American Publishers. (McGraw Hill v. Google, Okthoba 19, 2005)[9][74][75][76][77][78] 

Novemba 2005: I-Google yashintsha igama lale sevisi lisuka ku-Google Print laya ku-Google Book Search.[79] Uhlelo lwayo oluvumela abashicileli nababhali ukuthi bafake izincwadi zabo kusevisi luqanjwe kabusha ngokuthi Uhlelo Lozakwethu Lwe-Google Books,[80] kanye nokusebenzisana namalabhulali kube yi-Google Books Library Project.

2006: I-Google yengeze inkinobho "yokulanda i-pdf" kuzo zonke izincwadi zayo ezingaphandle kwe-copyright, zesizinda somphakathi. Iphinde yengeza isixhumi esibonakalayo esisha sokuphequlula kanye namakhasi amasha "Mayelana nale Ncwadi".[73] 

Agasti 2006: I-University of California System yamemezela ukuthi izojoyina iphrojekthi yokwenza i-Books digitization. Lokhu kubandakanya ingxenye yemiqulu eyizigidi ezingama-34 phakathi kwemitapo yolwazi ecishe ibe yi-100 ephethwe Uhlelo.[81] 

Septhemba 2006: I-Complutense University of Madrid ibe umtapo wolwazi wokuqala wolimi lwesi-Spanish ukujoyina i-Google Books Library Project.[82] 

Okthoba 2006: Inyuvesi yaseWisconsin–Madison yamemezela ukuthi izojoyina iphrojekthi yokwenza i-Book Search kanye ne-Wisconsin Historical Society Library. Sekuhlangene, imitapo yolwazi inempahla eyizigidi ezingu-7.2.[83] 

Novemba 2006: Inyuvesi yaseVirginia yajoyina lo msebenzi. Imitapo yolwazi yayo iqukethe imiqulu engaphezu kwezigidi ezinhlanu kanye nemibhalo yesandla engaphezu kwezigidi ezingu-17, izincwadi eziyivelakancane nezinqolobane zomlando.[84] 

NgoJanuwari 2007: Inyuvesi yaseTexas e-Austin yamemezela ukuthi izojoyina iphrojekthi yokwenza i-Book Search digitization. Okungenani imiqulu eyisigidi izofakwa ekhompyutheni ezindaweni eziyi-13 zale nyuvesi. 

Mashi 2007: I-Bavarian State Library yamemezela ubudlelwano ne-Google ukuze iskene izizinda zomphakathi ezingaphezu kwesigidi nemisebenzi engaphandle kokuphrinta ngesiJalimane kanye nesiNgisi, isiFulentshi, isiNtaliyane, isiLatini, neSpanishi.[85] 

Meyi 2007: Ubambiswano lwephrojekthi yokwenza izincwadi ngedijithali lwamenyezelwa ngokuhlanganyela yi-Google kanye ne-Cantonal kanye ne-University Library yase-Lausanne.[86] 

Meyi 2007: I-Boekentoren Library yase-Ghent University yamemezela ukuthi izobamba iqhaza ne-Google ekwenzeni izinguqulo ezenziwe ngedijithali zezincwadi zekhulu le-19 ngezilimi zesiFulentshi nesi-Dutch zitholakale ku-inthanethi.[87] 

May 2007: I-Mysore University imemezela ukuthi i-Google izofaka kudijithali izincwadi nemibhalo yesandla engaphezu kuka-800,000–okuhlanganisa nemibhalo yesandla engaba ngu-100,000 ebhalwe ngesi-Sanskrit noma ngesi-Kannada kuwo womabili amahlamvu esundu namaphepha.[68] 

NgoJuni 2007: IKomidi Lokubambisana Kwezikhungo (eliqanjwe kabusha ngokuthi iBig Ten Academic Alliance ngo-2016) lamemezela ukuthi imitapo yolwazi engamalungu ayo ayishumi nambili izobamba iqhaza ekuhloleni izincwadi eziyizigidi eziyi-10 phakathi neminyaka eyisithupha ezayo.[58] 

Julayi 2007: Inyuvesi yase-Keio yaba nguzakwethu wokuqala welabhulali ye-Google e-Japan ngesimemezelo sokuthi izofaka kudijithali okungenani izincwadi zesizinda somphakathi eziyi-120,000.[88] 

Agasti 2007: I-Google yamemezela ukuthi izofaka kudijithali izinto ezifinyelela ku-500,000 zombili ezinamalungelo okukopishwa kanye nezisesidlangalaleni ezivela ku-Cornell University Library. I-Google izophinde ihlinzeke ngekhophi yedijithali yayo yonke imisebenzi eskeniwe ukuze ifakwe ohlelweni lwelabhulali yenyuvesi. [89] 

Septhemba 2007: I-Google yengeze isici esivumela abasebenzisi ukuthi babelane ngamazwibela ezincwadi ezisesizindeni somphakathi. Amazwibela angase avele ncamashi njengoba enza ekuskeneni kwencwadi, noma njengombhalo ongenalutho.[90]

Septhemba 2007: I-Google ikhiphe isici esisha esibizwa ngokuthi "Ilabhulali Yami" evumela abasebenzisi ukuthi benze amalabhulali enziwe ngokwezifiso zabo siqu, izinketho zezincwadi abangazilebula, bazibuyekeze, bazilinganise, noma baseshe umbhalo ogcwele.[91] 

Disemba 2007: Inyuvesi yase-Columbia yengezwa njengozakwethu ekwenzeni imisebenzi yesizinda somphakathi kudijithali.[92] 

Meyi 2008: I-Microsoft yaphazamiseka futhi yahlela ukuqeda iphrojekthi yayo yokuskena, eyayifinyelele izincwadi ezingu-750,000 kanye nezihloko zamajenali eziyizigidi ezingu-80.[93] 

Okthoba 2008: Kwafinyelelwa kusixazululo phakathi kwemboni yokushicilela ne-Google ngemva kweminyaka emibili yezingxoxo. I-Google yavuma ukunxephezela ababhali nabashicileli ukuze ithole ilungelo lokwenza izigidi zezincwadi zitholakale emphakathini.[9][94] 

Okthoba 2008: I-HathiTrust "Inqolobane Yedijithali Ehlanganyelwe" (kamuva eyaziwa ngokuthi i-HathiTrust Digital Library) yethulwa ngokuhlanganyela yiKomidi Lokubambisana Kwesikhungo kanye namalabhulali angu-11 enyuvesi ohlelweni lweNyuvesi yaseCalifornia, wonke obekuyimitapo yolwazi ebambisene ne-Google, ukuze kugcinwe kungobo yomlando futhi kunikeze ukufinyelela kwezemfundo ezincwadini eziskeniwe yi-Google99. 

Novemba 2008: I-Google yafinyelela uphawu lwebhuku oluyizigidi ezingu-7 ezintweni eziskenwe yi-Google kanye nozakwethu bokushicilela. Ezingu-1 million bezikumodi yokubuka kuqala okugcwele kanti eziyizigidi ezingu-1 bezibukelwa ngokugcwele futhi zilandeke imisebenzi yesizinda somphakathi. Cishe izigidi ezinhlanu zazinganyatheliswa.[19][96][97] 

Disemba 2008: I-Google imemezele ukufakwa kwamamagazini ku-Google Books. Izihloko zifaka i-New York Magazine, i-Ebony, ne-Popular Mechanics[98][99] 

February 2009: I-Google yethule inguqulo yeselula ye-Google Book Search, evumela abasebenzisi befoni be-iPhone ne-Android ukuthi bafunde imisebenzi yomphakathi engaphezu kwesigidi esingu-1.5 e-US (nangaphezulu kuka-500,000 ngaphandle kwase-US) isebenzisa isiphequluli seselula. Esikhundleni sezithombe zamakhasi, kuboniswa umbhalo ongenalutho wencwadi.[100] 

May 2009: Emhlanganweni waminyaka yonke we-BookExpo eNew York, i-Google yasayina inhloso yayo yokwethula uhlelo oluzokwenza abashicileli bakwazi ukuthengisa izinguqulo zedijithali zezincwadi zabo ezintsha ngqo kubathengi nge-Google.[101] 

Disemba 2009: Inkantolo yaseFrance yavala ukuskenwa kwezincwadi ezinama-copyright ezishicilelwe eFrance, yathi lokhu kwephula imithetho ye-copyright. Bekuwukulahlekelwa okusemthethweni kokuqala okukhulu kwephrojekthi yokuskena.[102] 

Ephreli 2010: Amaciko abonakalayo awazange afakwe ecaleni langaphambilini nasekuxazululeni, angamaqembu abamangali kwelinye icala, futhi athi ahlose ukuletha okungaphezu nje kokuthi Izincwadi ze-Google zicutshungulwe. "Isenzo esisha sekilasi," sifunda isitatimende, "sedlula Iphrojekthi Yelabhulali Ye-Google, futhi sihlanganisa nokunye ukwephulwa kwe-Google okuhlelekile nokugcwele kwamalungelo abathwebuli bezithombe, abadwebi bezithombe nabanye abaculi ababonakalayo."[103]

Meyi 2010: Kwabikwa ukuthi i-Google izovula isitolo sezincwadi zedijithali esibizwa nge-Google Editions.[104] Izoqhudelana ne-Amazon, Barnes & Noble, Apple kanye nabanye abathengisi bezincwadi ze-elekthronikhi ngesitolo sayo se-e-book. Ngokungafani nezinye, i-Google Editions izoba ku-inthanethi ngokuphelele futhi ngeke idinge idivayisi ethile (efana ne-kindle, Nook, noma iPad). 

Juni 2010: I-Google yaphasisa izincwadi eziskeniwe eziyizigidi ezingu-12.[11] 

Agasti 2010: Kwamenyezelwa ukuthi i-Google ihlose ukuskena zonke izincwadi ezikhona kakade ezingu-129,864,880 phakathi neminyaka eyishumi, ezingaba amakhasi edijithali angaphezu kwezigidigidi ezi-4 namagama angu-2 trillion esewonke.[11] 

Disemba 2010: I-Google eBooks (Google Editions) yethulwa e-US.[105] 

Disemba 2010: I-Google yethula i-Ngram Viewer, eqoqa futhi igrafu idatha ekusetshenzisweni kwamagama kulo lonke iqoqo layo lebhuku.[30] 

Mashi 2011: Ijaji likahulumeni linqabe ukuxazululwa okufinyelelwe phakathi komkhakha wokushicilela ne-Google.[106] 

Mashi 2012: I-Google yaphasisa izincwadi eziyizigidi ezingu-20 eziskeniwe.[107][108] 

Mashi 2012: I-Google yafinyelela isivumelwano nabashicileli.[109] 

Januwari 2013: Idokhumentari ethi Google and the World Brain yaboniswa kuSundance Film Festival.[110] 

Novemba 2013: Ukubusa ku-Authors Guild v. Google, Ijaji Lesifunda lase-US u-Denny Chin lisekela i-Google, ecaphuna ukusetshenziswa okufanele.[111] Ababhali bathi bazosidlulisela phambili icala. [112] 

Okthoba 2015: Inkantolo yokudlulisa amacala icheme ne-Google, imemezela ukuthi i-Google ayizange iphule umthetho we-copyright.[113] Ngokwe-New York Times, i-Google isikene izincwadi ezingaphezu kwezigidi ezingu-25.[12] 

Ngo-April 2016: INkantolo Ephakeme yase-US yenqabile ukulalela isikhalazo se-Authors Guild, okusho ukuthi isinqumo senkantolo ephansi simile, futhi i-Google izovunyelwa ukuskena amabhuku omtapo wezincwadi futhi ibonise amazwibela emiphumeleni yosesho ngaphandle kokwephula umthetho.[114] 

Isimo 
i-Google ibiyimfihlo kakhulu mayelana nezinhlelo zayo ngekusasa lephrojekthi ye-Google Books. Imisebenzi yokuskena ibilokhu yehla kusukela okungenani ngo-2012, njengoba kuqinisekiswe abasebenzi basemtapweni wezincwadi ezikhungweni ezimbalwa zozakwethu be-Google. ENyuvesi yaseWisconsin, isivinini sase sehlile saba ngaphansi kwesigamu salokho esasiyikho ngo-2006. Kodwa-ke, osolwazi bathe ukuncipha kwejubane kungaba umphumela ongokwemvelo wokuvuthwa kwephrojekthi - ekuqaleni izitaki zezincwadi zathathwa zathathwa ukuze ziskenwe kanti manje yizihloko kuphela ezazingakaskenwa kakade okwakudingeka zicatshangelwe.[50] Ikhasi lenkampani lomugqa wesikhathi we-Google Books alizange likhulume lutho ngemva kuka-2007 ngisho nango-2017, futhi ibhulogi ye-Google Books yahlanganiswa yaba kubhulogi Losesho Lwe-Google ngo-2012.[115]

Naphezu kokuwina icala leminyaka eyishumi ngo-2017, i-Atlantic ithe i-Google "ivaliwe ukusebenza kwayo kokuskena." [14] Ngo-Ephreli 2017, i-Wired ibike ukuthi bekunabasebenzi abambalwa be-Google abasebenza kule phrojekthi, futhi izincwadi ezintsha zisaskenwa, kodwa ngezinga eliphansi kakhulu. Iphawule ukuthi impi yezomthetho eyathatha iminyaka eyishumi yenze i-Google yalahlekelwa isifiso sayo.[115] 

Izinkinga zomthetho 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: I-Authors Guild, Inc. v. Google, Inc. 
Ngale phrojekthi, izincwadi zomtapo wezincwadi bezifakwa kudijithali ngokungakhethi ngokunganaki isimo se-copyright, okuholele emacaleni amaningi aphikisana ne-Google. Ekupheleni kuka-2008, kubikwa ukuthi i-Google yayisifake kudijithali izincwadi ezingaphezu kwezigidi eziyisikhombisa, okuyisigidi esisodwa kuphela okwakuyimisebenzi emphakathini. Kokunye, isigidi esisodwa sasinamalungelo okukopisha futhi sanyatheliswa, kanti izigidi ezinhlanu zazinamalungelo okukopisha kodwa zanganyatheliswa. Ngo-2005, iqembu lababhali nabashicileli bamangalela i-Google icala elikhulu lokwephula imisebenzi ene-copyright. U-Google waphikisa ngokuthi igcina "imisebenzi eyizintandane" - izincwadi ezisengaphansi kwe-copyright, kodwa abanikazi bama-copyright abatholakalanga.[116] 

I-Authors Guild kanye ne-Association of American Publishers yamangalela i-Google ngokuhlukene ngo-2005 ngephrojekthi yayo yencwadi, icaphuna "ukwephulwa kwelungelo lobunikazi okukhulu."[117] I-Google iphikise ngokuthi iphrojekthi yayo imele ukusetshenziswa okulungile futhi iminyaka yedijithali elingana nekhathalogi yamakhadi enawo wonke amagama ekushicilelweni anenkomba.[9] Amacala ahlanganiswa, futhi ekugcineni kwahlongozwa isixazululo. Lesi sivumelwano sithole ukugxekwa okubalulekile ngezizathu ezihlukahlukene, okuhlanganisa ukungathembeki, ubumfihlo, kanye nokunganeli kwezigaba ezihlongozwayo zababhali nabashicileli. Ukulungiswa kwagcina kwenqatshiwe,[118] futhi abashicileli bazinza ne-Google maduze nje. I-Authors Guild yaqhubeka necala layo, kwathi ngo-2011 ikilasi labo elihlongozwayo lagunyazwa. I-Google yafaka isikhalazo ngaleso sinqumo, ngenani elithile le-amici eligomela ukuntuleka kwekilasi, futhi Isifunda Sesibili yenqaba isitifiketi sekilasi ngoJulayi 2013, yabuyisela icala eNkantolo Yesifunda ukuze kucutshungulwe ukuvikela ukusetshenziswa okufanele kwe-Google.[119] 

Ngo-2015 Inhlangano Yababhali yafaka esinye isikhalazo ngokumelene ne-Google ukuze sicatshangelwe Inkantolo Yezikhalo Yesifunda yesi-2 yase-US eNew York. I-Google iwine icala ngazwi linye ngokusekelwe empikiswano yokuthi bebengabonisi abantu imibhalo egcwele kodwa amazwibela, futhi abavumeli abantu ukuthi bafunde incwadi ngokungemthetho.[120] Embikweni, izinkantolo zathi aziphuli imithetho ye-copyright, njengoba zazivikelwe ngaphansi kwesigatshana sokusetshenziswa okufanele.[121]

I-Authors Guild yazama futhi ngo-2016 ukuphikisa isinqumo futhi kulokhu yathatha udaba lwabo ukuze lucutshungulwe yiNkantolo Ephakeme. Icala lanqatshwa, kwashiya isinqumo Sesifunda Sesibili ecaleni sinjalo, okusho ukuthi i-Google ayizange yephule imithetho ye-copyright.[122] Leli cala liphinde labeka isibonelo kwamanye amacala afanayo ngokuphathelene nemithetho yokusetshenziswa ngendlela efanele, njengoba laqhubeka licacisa umthetho futhi lawandisa. Ukucaciswa okunjalo kuthinta amanye amaphrojekthi okuskena afana ne-Google.[120] 

Amanye amacala alandela ukuhola kwe-Authors Guild. Ngo-2006 icala laseJalimane, elafakwa ngaphambilini, lahoxiswa.[123] NgoJuni 2006, u-Hervé de la Martinière,[124] umshicileli ongumFulentshi owaziwa nge-La Martinière kanye ne-Éditions du Seuil,[125] umemezele inhloso yakhe yokumangalela i-Google France.[126] Ngo-2009, iNkantolo Yombango YaseParis yaklomelisa u-300,000 EUR (cishe u-430,000 USD) ngomonakalo nenzalo futhi yayala i-Google ukuthi ikhokhe u-10,000 EUR ngosuku kuze kube yilapho ikhipha izincwadi zomshicileli kusizindalwazi sayo.[125][127] Inkantolo ibhale ukuthi, "I-Google yephule imithetho ye-copyright yababhali ngokukhiqiza kabusha ngokugcwele nokwenza kufinyeleleke" izincwadi uSeuil anazo ngaphandle kwemvume yayo[125] nokuthi i-Google "yenze izenzo zokwephulwa kwe-copyright, ezilimaza abashicileli".[124] I-Google ithe izokhalaza. [125] I-Syndicat National de l'Edition, ejoyine icala, ithe i-Google ihlole cishe imisebenzi yesiFulentshi engu-100,000 ngaphansi kwe-copyright.[125] 

Ngo-December 2009, umbhali waseShayina uMian Mian wafaka icala lombango ngo-$8,900 ngokumelene ne-Google ngokuskena inoveli yakhe, Abathandi be-Acid. Leli yicala lokuqala elinjalo ukufakwa ku-Google eShayina.[128] Futhi, ngoNovemba ngalowo nyaka, i-China Written Works Copyright Society (CWWCS) yasola i-Google ngokuskena izincwadi eziyi-18,000 ngababhali abangamaShayina abangama-570 ngaphandle kokugunyazwa. I-Google yavuma ngoNovemba 20 ukuhlinzeka ngohlu lwezincwadi zesiShayina eyayiziskeniwe, kodwa inkampani yenqaba ukuvuma ukuthi "yephulile" imithetho ye-copyright.[129][umthombo ongathembekile?] 

NgoMashi 2007, uThomas Rubin, ummeli ojwayelekile we-copyright, uphawu lokuhweba, nezimfihlo zohwebo kwa-Microsoft, wasola i-Google ngokwephula umthetho we-copyright ngesevisi yabo yokusesha izincwadi. U-Rubin ugxeke ngokuqondile inqubomgomo ye-Google yokukopisha ngokukhululekile noma yimuphi umsebenzi kuze kube yilapho etshelwa umnikazi welungelo lobunikazi ukuthi ayeke.[130] 

Ukunikezwa kwelayisense kwe-Google kwemisebenzi yesizinda somphakathi nakho kuyindawo ekhathazayo ngenxa yokusebenzisa amasu e-digital watermarking nezincwadi. Eminye imisebenzi eshicilelwe esesidlangalaleni, njengayo yonke imisebenzi edalwe uhulumeni wase-US Federal, isaphathwa njengeminye imisebenzi engaphansi kwelungelo lobunikazi, ngakho ikhiywa ngemva kuka-1922.[131] 

Kusukela okungenani ngo-2014, i-Google ivumele ababhali nabashicileli ukuthi basuse ukuhlola kuqala kwebhuku ku-Google Books uma beceliwe.[132]
 
Amaphrojekthi afanayo
I-Project Gutenberg ingumzamo wokuvolontiya wokwenza idijithali kanye nokugcina imisebenzi yamasiko, "ukukhuthaza ukudalwa nokusabalalisa ama-eBooks". Yasungulwa ngo-1971 nguMichael S. Hart futhi ingumtapo wolwazi wedijithali omdala kunayo yonke. Kusukela ngomhla zi-3 kuMfumfu wezi-2015, i-Project Gutenberg ifinyelele izinto ezingu-50,000 eqoqweni layo. 
Ingobo yomlando ye-inthanethi iyinhlangano engenzi nzuzo eyenza kudijithali izincwadi ezingaphezu kuka-1000 ngosuku, kanye nezibuko zezincwadi ezivela ku-Google Books neminye imithombo. Kusukela ngoMeyi 2011, isingathe izincwadi zesizinda somphakathi ezingaphezu kwezigidi ezingu-2.8, ezinkulu kunezincwadi ezilinganiselwa esigidini esisesidlangalaleni ku-Google Books.[133] I-Open Library, iphrojekthi engudadewabo ye-Internet Archive, iboleka angu-80,000 ama-ebook askeniwe futhi athengwe ezivakashini zamamitapo wolwazi angu-150.[134] 
I-HathiTrust inakekela i-HathiTrust Digital Library kusukela ngo-Okthoba 13, 2008,[135] egcina futhi ehlinzeka ngokufinyelela kokubalulekile okuskenwe yi-Google, ezinye zezincwadi ze-Internet Archive, futhi ezinye eziskenwa endaweni yizikhungo zozakwethu. Kusukela ngoMeyi 2010, ihlanganisa imiqulu eyizigidi eziyisi-6, engaphezu kwesigidi esisodwa okuyisizinda somphakathi (okungenani e-US). 
I-ACLS Humanities E-Book, iqoqo eliku-inthanethi lezincwadi ezingaphezu kuka-5,400 zeqophelo eliphezulu kubuntu kanye nesayensi yezenhlalo ehlobene, efinyeleleka ngokubhalisela isikhungo. 
I-Microsoft ixhase ngezimali ukuskenwa kwezincwadi ezingu-300,000 ukuze zenze i-Live Search Books ngasekupheleni kuka-2006. Yaqhubeka kwaze kwaba nguMeyi 2008, lapho iphrojekthi iyekwa[136] futhi izincwadi zenziwa zitholakale mahhala ku-Internet Archive.[137] 
I-National Digital Library of India (NDLI) iwumsebenzi ongaphansi koMnyango Wokuthuthukiswa Kwabasebenzi, e-India. Inhloso ukuhlanganisa imitapo yolwazi yedijithali kazwelonke nakwamanye amazwe kwingosi eyodwa yewebhu. I-NDLI inikeza ukufinyelela mahhala kwezindleko zezincwadi eziningi zesiNgisi nezilimi zaseNdiya. 
I-Europeana ixhumanisa cishe nezinto zedijithali eziyizigidi eziyi-10 kusukela ngo-2010, okuhlanganisa ividiyo, izithombe, imidwebo, okulalelwayo, amamephu, imibhalo yesandla, izincwadi eziphrintiwe, namaphephandaba asuka eminyakeni eyizi-2,000 edlule yomlando wase-Europe kusukela ezinqolobaneni ezingaphezu kuka-1,000 e-European Union.[138][139] 
I-Gallica evela ku-French National Library ixhumanisa nezincwadi ezifakwe kwidijithali ezingaba ngu-4,000,000, amaphephandaba, imibhalo yesandla, amamephu nemidwebo, njll. Idalwe ngo-1997, umtapo wezincwadi wedijithali uyaqhubeka nokukhula ngenani lamadokhumenti amasha angaba ngu-5000 ngenyanga. Kusukela ekupheleni kuka-2008, iningi lamadokhumenti amasha askeniwe atholakala ngefomethi yezithombe nemibhalo. Iningi lale mibhalo libhalwe ngesiFulentshi.

Ukushicilela kuyinqubo yokwenza ulwazi, izincwadi, umculo, isofthiwe, nokunye okuqukethwe, ngokomzimba noma kwedijithali, kutholakale emphakathini ukuze kudayiswe noma mahhala.[1] Ngokwesiko, igama elithi ukushicilela libhekise ekwakhiweni nasekusatshalalisweni kwezincwadi eziphrintiwe, njengezincwadi, izincwadi zamahlaya, amaphephandaba kanye nomagazini emphakathini. Ngokufika kwezinhlelo zolwazi lwedijithali, ububanzi buye banda ukuze bafake ukushicilelwa kwedijithali okufana ne-e-books, omagazini bedijithali, amawebhusayithi, inkundla yezokuxhumana, umculo, nokushicilela imidlalo yevidiyo. 

Imboni yokushicilela yezohwebo isuka kuma-conglomerates amakhulu ezizwe ngezizwe njenge-News Corp, i-Pearson, i-Penguin Random House, ne-Thomson Reuters[2] kuye kumabhrendi amakhulu kanye nezinkulungwane zabashicileli abancane abazimele. Inezigaba ezihlukahlukene ezifana nokushicilela/ukuthengisa okudayiswayo kwezinganekwane nezingezona izinganekwane, ukushicilela okufundisayo, nokushicilela kwezemfundo nesayensi.[3] Ukushicilela futhi kwenziwa ngohulumeni, izinhlangano zomphakathi, nezinkampani ezizimele ngezidingo zokuphatha noma zokuhambisana, ibhizinisi, ucwaningo, ukumela, noma izinjongo ezithakaselwa umphakathi.[4] Lokhu kungafaka imibiko yonyaka, imibiko yocwaningo, ucwaningo lwemakethe, ukwaziswa ngenqubomgomo, nemibiko yezobuchwepheshe. Ukuzishicilela sekuyinto evamile kakhulu. 

Ukushicilela kushintshile kusuka koluncane, ohlotsheni lwakudala olunqunyelwe umthetho noma inkolo kuya embonini yesimanjemanje, enkulu esakaza zonke izinhlobo zolwazi.[5] 

"Umshicileli" angabhekisa enkampanini eshicilelayo, inhlangano, noma umuntu ohola inkampani yokushicilela, imprint, iphephabhuku, noma iphephandaba. 

Izigaba zokushicilela 
Inqubo yokushicilela ehlanganisa iningi labashicileli bamamagazini, ijenali, kanye nabashicileli bezincwadi ihlanganisa: (Izigaba ezihlukene ziyasebenza ezinhlotsheni ezahlukene zabashicileli)[6] 
Ukubhala 
Ngokugunyaza Ukuhlela 

Ikhophi 
Ukuhlelwa Kokubhala 
Ukubhala 
Ukusetha 
Ukuhlola 
Ukuhlola 
Ukulungisa Imijikelezo Ukulungisa 
Izinkomba 
Izilungiso zokugcina 
Ukushicilela Iwebhu Ukushicilela I-Web 
Prepress 
Printing 
Post press

publisher 
Newspapers
Amaphephandaba noma amawebhusayithi ezindaba angukushicilelwa kwemibiko yamanje, izindatshana, nezici ezibhalwe izintatheli. Zimahhala, ngezinye izikhathi zine-edishini ye-premium, noma zikhokhelwe, ngazodwana noma ngokubhalisa. Agcwele izithombe noma enye imidiya futhi ngokuvamile axhaswa ngokukhangisa. Ngokuvamile, bahlanganisa izindaba zendawo, zezwe, nezamazwe ngamazwe noma bafaka imboni ethile. Ezinye izinhlangano zikhokhisa imali ekhokhwayo uma zinolwazi nolwazi olukhethekile. Imboni yezindaba yenzelwe ukusiza umphakathi, ukwenza abantu namabhizinisi baziphendulele, futhi ikhuthaze inkululeko yolwazi nokukhuluma.[7] Abahleli baphatha ithoni yezwi lokushicilelwe kwabo; ngokwesibonelo, izihloko ezingezinhle uma ziqhathaniswa nezakhayo zingathinta umbono womfundi.[8] 

Ukushicilela ijenali 
Ijenali iwukushicilelwa kwezemfundo noma kobuchwepheshe okutholakala ngefomethi yedijithali kanye(noma) yokuphrinta, equkethe ama-athikili abhalwe abacwaningi, osolwazi, kanye nabantu abangochwepheshe. Lezi zincwadi ziqondene ngqo nomkhakha othile futhi zivame ukweqa imingcele emisiwe kule mikhakha. Ngokuvamile banezinqubo zokubuyekeza kontanga ngaphambi kokushicilela ukuze kuhlolwe ukufaneleka nekhwalithi yokuqukethwe.[9] 

Ukushicilelwa komagazini 
Iphephabhuku lishicilelwa ngezikhathi ezithile. Ihlanganisa izakhiwo zobuciko, ukuthwebula izithombe, nemifanekiso ehlanganisa isihloko noma intshisekelo ethile. Omagazini batholakala ngamafomethi aphrintiwe noma edijithali futhi angathengwa ezinhlelweni zokusebenza noma kumawebhusayithi afana ne-Readly noma afinyelelwe mahhala ezinhlelweni zokusebenza noma kumawebhusayithi afana ne-Issuu. 

Ukushicilelwa kwezincwadi 
Imboni yomhlaba wonke yokushicilela izincwadi iqukethe izincwadi ezihlukaniswe njengezinganekwane noma ezingezona ezinganekwane kanye nokuphrinta, i-e-book, noma i-audiobook. Imakethe yezincwadi inkulu, inabantu abangaba yizigidi eziyizinkulungwane ezingu-1.5 abakhuluma isiNgisi.[10] Amasevisi okuhumusha ayatholakala ukuze enze le mibhalo ifinyeleleke ngezinye izilimi. Ukuzishicilela ngokwakho kwenza ukushicilela kufinyeleleke kabanzi ngokusebenzisa ukuphrinta okuncane kwedijithali okuphrintiwe noma izinkundla zokuzishicilela eziku-inthanethi. Ubuchwepheshe besikrini se-E-reader buyaqhubeka buthuthuka ngokugqama okukhulayo nokulungiswa okubenza bakhululeke kakhudlwana ukufunda. Incwadi ngayinye ine-ISBN ebhalisiwe yokuyikhomba. 

Inkomba yokushicilela 
uhla lwemibhalo luqukethe idatha eseshekayo ekhonjiwe mayelana namabhizinisi, imikhiqizo, namasevisi. Zanyatheliswa esikhathini esidlule kodwa manje sezitholakala kakhulu ku-inthanethi. Izikhombisi ziyatholakala njengohlu oluseshekayo, kumephu, njengengosi eqondene nomkhakha othile, njengendawo yokubuyekeza (uchwepheshe noma umthengi), noma njengesayithi lokuqhathanisa. Nakuba amanye amabhizinisi engase angaziboni njengabashicileli, indlela idatha eboniswa ngayo iyashicilelwa. 

Ukushicilelwa kwezincwadi zokufunda
Incwadi iyincwadi efundisayo, noma i-e-book, equkethe ukwaziswa ngesihloko esithile futhi isetshenziswa abantu abafunda leso sihloko.[11] Isidingo sokushicilelwa kwezincwadi siyaqhubeka ngenxa yesidingo semfundo emhlabeni wonke.[12][13] Izincwadi zokufunda ezivela kubashicileli abakhulu zihlanganiswa nezinkundla zokufunda eziku-inthanethi ukuze uthole ulwazi lochwepheshe kanye nokufinyelela kumtapo wolwazi wezincwadi ezinokuqukethwe kwedijithali.[14] Umshini wokushicilela wasenyuvesi ungumshicileli wezemfundo ophethwe inyuvesi. I-Oxford University Press inkulu kakhulu emhlabeni futhi igxile ocwaningweni, emfundweni, nasekufundiseni isiNgisi ngolimi lwamazwe ngamazwe.[15] 

Ikhathalogi yokushicilela 
Ikhathalogi wuhla lwemibhalo olubonakalayo noma uhlu lohlu olukhulu lwemikhiqizo olukuvumela ukuthi upheqa futhi uthenge enkampanini ethile.[16] Ngokuphrinta, lokhu kuvamise ukuba kufomethi yencwadi ethambile noma uhla lwemibhalo. Amakhathalogi amancane abonakalayo angaziwa njengezincwajana. Nge-inthanethi, iguqukele kusizindalwazi esiseshekayo semikhiqizo eyaziwa ngaphansi kwetemu le-e-commerce. Amakhathalogi asebenzisanayo nezincwajana ezifana ne-IKEA[17] ne-Avon[18] avumela amakhasimende ukuthi aphequlule uhla olugcwele uma enganqumanga ngokuthenga kwawo. Iwebhu ephendulayo kanye nedizayini yohlelo lokusebenza izovumela ukuhlanganiswa okwengeziwe phakathi kokubonwa kwekhathalogi esebenzisanayo kanye nesizindalwazi somkhiqizo oseshekayo. 

Ukushicilela ngewebhu 
Kuze kube muva nje, izincwadi ezibonakalayo beziwumthombo oyinhloko wolwazi lokurekhoda. Ukuze ufinyeleleke futhi ufinyelele umhlaba wonke, lokhu okuqukethwe kungahlelelwa kabusha iwebhu. Ngokwesibonelo, uMtapo Wezincwadi WaseBrithani uphethe izinto ezingaphezu kwezigidi ezingu-170 ezinezengezo ezintsha eziyizigidi ezintathu unyaka ngamunye.[19] Ngemvume, okuqukethwe kungashicilelwa ku-inthanethi ngama-e-books, amabhuku alalelwayo, amawebhusayithi asekelwe ku-CMS, izinkundla zokufunda ku-inthanethi, amavidiyo, noma izinhlelo zokusebenza zeselula. Ku-inthanethi, ababhali nabahleli bamakhophi baziwa njengababhali bokuqukethwe nabahleli bokuqukethwe, nakuba izindima zabo zihluka kozakwabo abasekelwe ezincwadini. Ukukhangisa 

Ukukhangisa 
kunganikeza imali engenayo noma imali engenayo exhaswe ngabashicileli. Uma ukukhangisa kunembuyiselo ku-investimenti (i-ROI), umshicileli angakhuphula imali engenayo ngokukhuphula ukusetshenziswa kwemali. I-ROI efika ku-£10 nge-£1 ngayinye etshaliwe ingenzeka, njengoba kubonakala emikhankasweni kaKhisimusi ka-John Lewis & Partners.[20][21] Ngokufanayo, noma yikuphi ukonga kwezindleko okulimaza ikhasimende/umthengi kungaba nomthelela kumkhiqizo ngokuhamba kwesikhathi. Ukumaketha kweziteshi eziningi kungabiza kakhulu ekudaleni umuzwa ojulile ongenakuphindwa ngesiteshi esisodwa. Isibonelo, uma ucubungula imali yokumaketha, isitolo esinemali encane (noma engekho nhlobo) uma siqhathaniswa newebhusayithi sibiza kakhulu ngoba sisebenza njengebhodi elikhulu elinikeza ulwazi lokuphequlula oluvumela abathengi ukuthi benze izinqumo zokuthenga. Kubenza bazizwele ngophawu, babe khona emphakathini, futhi kudaleke namathuba emisebenzi. Futhi, ukusebenzisa ukushicilela kwenkundla yezokuxhumana ukukhangisa kune-ROI enhle uma okuthrendayo, okuqukethwe kwekhwalithi ephezulu kwakhiwa okubonisa kahle umkhiqizo.

Ukushicilela okuhlanganisayo 
I-athikili eyinhloko: I-Tie-in 
Film, ithelevishini, umsakazo, kanye nezikhangiso zishicilela ulwazi kubabukeli bazo. Imidlalo yamakhompiyutha, izinhlelo zokusebenza zokusakaza-bukhoma, nenkundla yezokuxhumana ishicilela okuqukethwe ngezindlela ezihlukene ezingagcina izethameli zihlanganyele kakhulu. Ukuthengisa imikhiqizo eyengeziwe ehlobene eduze nefilimu enkulu, njenge-Star Wars, kuyisibonelo sokushicilela okuhlangene. Le mikhiqizo ihlanganisa kodwa ayikhawulelwe ezincwadini eziphuma phambili, amanoveli ayingcaca, ama-albhamu ezingoma, imidlalo yekhompyutha, amamodeli namathoyizi, okuthunyelwe kwenkundla yezokuxhumana, nokushicilelwe kokuphromotha. Izibonelo zokushicilela okuhambisanayo okusekelwe ezincwadini ama-franchise ka-Harry Potter kanye no-James Bond. 

Bheka futhi: Ukushicilelwa ngezikhathi ezithile 
Izigatshana zokushicilela incwadi 

Bheka futhi: Umlando wezincwadi 
"Inkampani yokushicilela izincwadi" uqondisa kabusha lapha. Ngomshicileli obizwa nge-Book Publishing Company, bheka Ipulazi (Tennessee). 
Isimo sokushicilela sithuthuka ngokuqhubekayo. Njengamanje kunezinhlobo ezine ezinkulu zabashicileli ekushicilelweni kwezincwadi:[22] 

Abashicileli abavamile 
Lezi zinkampani ngokuvamile zikhiqiza izincwadi ezingamakhophi ngamaphepha amakhulu. Basungule amanethiwekhi abasabalalisa lezo zincwadi ezitolo zezitini kanye nodaka nemitapo yolwazi. 

Uma umshicileli ovamile amukela incwadi ukuze ishicilelwe, badinga ukuthi umbhali asayine inkontileka enikezela amalungelo athile kumshicileli. Ngokushintshana, umshicileli uzonakekela zonke izici zokushicilela incwadi ngezindleko zomshicileli. Bathembele ngokuphelele ekuthengisweni kwencwadi ukuze babuyise lezo zindleko futhi benze inzuzo. Umbhali uthola inzuzo ekuthengisweni ngakunye (futhi ngesinye isikhathi nemali ekhokhwa kusengaphambili uma incwadi yamukelwe[23]). Ngenxa yobungozi bezezimali, abashicileli abavamile bakhetha kakhulu ukuthi bazokushicilela ini, futhi bayayinqaba imibhalo yesandla eminingi ethunyelwe kubo.[24] 

Ngo-2013, iPenguin (ekaPearson) kanye neRandom House (ekaBertelsmann) yahlanganiswa, okwanciphisa imboni yokushicilela evamile yaba yidlanzana labashicileli abakhulu njengoba ijwayelana nemidiya yedijithali.[25] Ukuhlanganiswa kwakha umshicileli wezincwadi zabathengi abakhulu kunawo wonke emhlabeni jikelele, ngesabelo semakethe yomhlaba wonke esingaphezu kwamaphesenti angu-25.[26] Kusukela ngo-2022, cishe amaphesenti angu-80 emakethe yohwebo yase-United States yezincwadi yayilawulwa yizinkampani zokushicilela ze-"Big Five": i-Penguin Random House, i-Hachette, i-HarperCollins, i-Simon & Schuster, ne-Macmillan.[27]

NgoNovemba 2020, i-ViacomCBS yavuma ukudayisela uSimon & Schuster, umshicileli wezincwadi wesithathu ngobukhulu e-United States, kuPenguin Random House ngesivumelwano, ukube sasidlulile, sasiyokwakha inkampani enkulu yokushicilela emhlabeni.[25] Ngomhla zi-2 kuNovemba 2021, uMnyango Wezobulungiswa wase-United States wafaka icala (i-US v. Bertelsmann SE & CO. KGaA, et al.) ukuze uvimbele ukuhlanganiswa ngezizathu zokungathembeki, [28] futhi ngo-Okthoba 31, 2022, iNkantolo Yesifunda yase-DC yakhipha isinqumo esivuna uMnyango Wezobulungiswa, yafaka isivimbelo esingunaphakade.[29] 

Nakuba izinkampani zamaphephandaba nomagazini zisavame ukuba nemishini yokunyathelisa nezincwadi ezihlanganisayo, abanyathelisi bezincwadi abavamile ukuba nazo.[ecashunwa] Ngokufanayo, uhwebo ngokuvamile luthengisa imikhiqizo eqediwe ngomsabalalisi ogcina futhi asabalalise izimpahla zomshicileli ngenani elithile noma azidayise ngokuthengisa noma ukubuya. 

Abanye abashicileli abakhulu banezigaba eziphelele ezinikelwe ku-franchise eyodwa, isb, i-Ballantine Del Rey LucasBooks inamalungelo akhethekile e-Star Wars e-United States; I-Random House UK (Bertelsmann)/Century LucasBooks inamalungelo afanayo e-United Kingdom. Imboni yegeyimu yevidiyo izishicilela yona nge-BL Publishing/Black Library (Warhammer) kanye Nabathakathi Basogwini (Dragonlance, Realms Forgotten, njll.). I-BBC inomkhakha wayo wokushicilela owenza kahle kakhulu ngochungechunge olunesikhathi eside olufana noDokotela Who. Le misebenzi ye-multimedia imakethwa ngokuhlaselayo, futhi ukuthengisa kuvame ukwedlula umsebenzi oshicilelwe ozimele wodwa, okuwenza ukugxila kwentshisekelo yebhizinisi.[30] 

Ukufika kwe-inthanethi kunikeze enye indlela yokusabalalisa izincwadi futhi abashicileli abaningi abajwayelekile nabo banikela ngezincwadi zabo ngefomethi ye-ebook. Ukulungiselela ibhuku lokushicilelwa kwe-e-book kuyefana nokushicilelwa, okunokuhluka okuncane kuphela kwenqubo yokulandisa ngezindlela ezihlukene zokushicilela; Ukushicilelwa kwe-E-book kuphinda kuqede izindleko ezithile njengesaphulelo esinikezwa abathengisi (imvamisa cishe amaphesenti angama-45).[31] 

Imishini yokunyathelisa emincane 
Abashicileli abancane, ababuye babizwe ngokuthi abashicileli abazimele noma be-indie,[32] basebenzisa imodeli evamile (okungukuthi umbhali udela amalungelo athile ukuze athole umshicileli othwala zonke izindleko zokushicilela), kodwa imigomo yawo enembile ingahluka kakhulu.[33] Ngokuvamile, abakhokhi imali kusengaphambili. 

Ukushicilela okuxubile 
Umshicileli oyingxubevange wabelana ngezindleko zokushicilelwa (ngakho-ke ubungozi) nombhali. Ngenxa yale ngozi yezezimali, bayakhetha kulokho abakushicilelayo. Inkontileka iyahlukahluka kuye ngokuthi yini okuxoxiswene ngayo phakathi kombhali nenkampani, kodwa iyohlala ihlanganisa ukunikezela kwamanye amalungelo kumshicileli.[34] Ukushicilela okuxubile kuwumthombo wenkulumompikiswano embonini yokushicilela, ngenxa yokuthambekela kwemishini eyize ukuze izenze ingxubevange. 

Imishini yeze
Umshini wokunyathelisa oyize uzoshicilela noma iyiphi incwadi. Ngokubuyisela, umbhali kufanele akhokhe zonke izindleko zokushicilelwa, anikeze amalungelo athile kumshicileli, futhi akhokhe izinzuzo ngokuthengisa. Imishini yokunyathelisa eyize ivame ukuhileleka emikhubeni ekhohlisayo noma inikeze izinsizakalo ezibizayo, zekhwalithi engeyinhle nezinsiza ezilinganiselwe ezitholakala kumlobi. E-US, lezi zinqubo ziphawulwe yi-Better Business Bureau njengemibiko engathandeki yabathengi.[35] Uma kubhekwa idumela elibi lokushicilela okuyize, imishini eminingi ye-vanity izibiza ngokuthi ingabashicileli abayingxube. I-Society of Authors (SoA) kanye Nenhlangano Yababhali Yase-Great Britain (WGGB) bacele ukuguqulwa komkhakha wokushicilela okhokhelwayo. Lezi zinyunyana, ezimele ababhali abangu-14,800, zishicilele ngokuhlanganyela umbiko wokudalula imikhuba emibi esabalele ezinkampanini ezikhokhisa ababhali ukuthi bashicilele umsebenzi wabo bebe bephuca amalungelo abo. 

Ukuzishicilela 
Uma umbhali ezishicilele ngokwakhe incwadi, ugcina wonke amalungelo futhi athwale umthwalo wazo zonke izigaba zokulungiselela, ukushicilela kanye nokusabalalisa incwadi. Umbhali angase aqashe ochwepheshe ngesisekelo senkokhelo yesevisi njengoba kudingeka, (isb umhleli, umklami wekhava, isihloli sokuhlola) noma abandakanye inkampani ukuze inikeze iphakheji ehlanganisiwe.[36] 

Intuthuko yakamuva 
Ukushicilela okufinyelelekayo kusebenzisa ukufakwa kwezincwadi ngedijithali ukuze kumake ku-XML futhi kukhiqizwe amafomethi amaningi ukuze adayiselwe amakhasimende, ngokuvamile aqondise labo abanenkinga yokufunda. Amafomethi ahlanganisa osayizi abahlukahlukene bokuphrinta abakhulu, amafomethi okuphrinta akhethekile e-dyslexia,[37] izinkinga zokulandelela iso, nokonakala kwe-macular, kanye ne-Braille, DAISY, amabhuku alalelwayo, nama-e-book.[38] 

Ukushicilela okuluhlaza kusho ukulungisa inqubo yokushicilela ukuze kuncishiswe umthelela wendawo. Isibonelo esisodwa umqondo wokuphrinta okudingekayo, kusetshenziswa ubuchwepheshe bedijithali noma bokuphrinta okudingekayo. Lokhu kunciphisa isidingo sokuthumela izincwadi ngoba zenziwa eduze nekhasimende ngesikhathi esifanele.[39] 

Okunye okuthuthukile ukukhula kokushicilelwa kwe-inthanethi, lapho kungakhiqizi izincwadi ezibonakalayo. Umbhali wenza i-e-book futhi ayilayishe kuwebhusayithi, lapho noma ubani angayilanda futhi ayifunde. 

Inani elandayo lababhali lisebenzisa i-niche marketing ku-inthanethi ukuze bathengise izincwadi eziningi ngokuxhumana nabafundi babo ku-inthanethi.[40] 

Ukumisa 
Bheka izigaba ze-ISO ze-ICS 01.140.40 kanye ne-35.240.30 ukuze uthole ulwazi olwengeziwe.[41][42] 

Izindaba zomthetho 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukushicilelwa
Ukushicilelwa ukusatshalaliswa kwamakhophi noma okuqukethwe emphakathini.[43][44] I-Berne Convention idinga ukuthi lokhu kungenziwa kuphela ngemvume yomnikazi welungelo lobunikazi, okunguye ohlale engumbhali.[43] Ku-Universal Copyright Convention, "ukushicilelwa" kuchazwa ku-Article VI njengokuthi "ukukhiqizwa kabusha ngendlela ephathekayo kanye nokusatshalaliswa okuvamile emphakathini kwamakhophi omsebenzi ongafundwa kuwo noma obonwa ngenye indlela ngokubukeka."[44]
 
Privishing
Ukushicilela okuyimfihlo (ukushicilela kwangasese, kodwa akufanele kudidaniswe nokuzishicilela) igama lesimanje lokushicilela incwadi kodwa kunyatheliswe amakhophi ambalwa kakhulu noma ngenxa yokuntuleka kokusekelwa kokumaketha, ukukhangisa, noma ukuthengisa kangangokuthi kungafinyeleli emphakathini.[45] Le ncwadi, nakuba ishicilelwe ngegama, cishe akunakwenzeka ukuyithola ngemigudu evamile njengezitolo zezincwadi, ngokuvamile ayikwazi uku-oda ngokukhethekile, futhi inokuntuleka kokusekelwa okuphawulekayo okuvela kumshicileli wayo, okuhlanganisa nokwenqaba ukuphinda kunyatheliswe isihloko. Incwadi eyimfihlo ingase kuthiwe "ibulewe." Kuye ngesisusa, ukuhlonishwa kungase kuhlanganise ukwephulwa kwenkontileka, ukucwaninga,[46] noma umkhuba omuhle webhizinisi (isb., ukungaphrinti izincwadi eziningi kunalokho umshicileli akholelwa ukuthi zizothengiswa ngobude besikhathi obunengqondo). Iphrinta 

Yomlando 

esebenza ngomshini wokunyathelisa wokuqala we-Gutenberg kusukela ngekhulu le-15 (umdwebo ka-1877) 
Ukushicilela kwaba nokwenzeka ngokusungulwa kokubhala futhi kwaba usizo nakakhulu lapho kwethulwa ukuphrinta. Ngaphambi kokunyathelisa, izincwadi ezisabalalisiwe zazikopishwa ngesandla ababhali. Ngenxa yokuphrinta, ukushicilelwa kwaqhubela phambili ngokubambisana nokuthuthukiswa kwezincwadi. 

Umsunguli waseShayina u-Bi Sheng wenza uhlobo olugudlukayo lwezitsha zobumba c. 1045, kodwa azikho izibonelo ezaziwayo ezisekhona zomsebenzi wakhe. Isisebenzi sikahulumeni saseKorea u-Ch'oe Yun-ŭi, owaphila ngesikhathi soBukhosi baseGoryeo, wasungula uhlobo lokuqala lwensimbi olunyakazayo ngo-1234-1250 AD.[47] 

EYurophu, 
uJohannes Gutenberg wasungula uhlobo lwezinhlobo ezinyakazayo e-Europe cishe ngo-1450, kanye nezindlela ezintsha zokwenza uhlobo olusekelwe ku-matrix kanye nesikhunta sesandla. Ukusungulwa kwemishini yokunyathelisa kancane kancane kwenza izincwadi zangabizi kakhulu futhi zatholakala kabanzi. 

Izincwadi zakuqala eziphrintiwe, amashidi angawodwa, kanye nezithombe ezadalwa ngaphambi kuka-1501 eYurophu zaziwa ngokuthi ama- incunable noma incunabula. "Umuntu owazalwa ngo-1453, unyaka wokuwa kweConstantinople, wayekwazi ukubheka emuva kusukela onyakeni wakhe wamashumi amahlanu ekuphileni lapho kwakunyatheliswe khona izincwadi ezingaba yizigidi eziyisishiyagalombili, mhlawumbe ngaphezu kwabo bonke ababhali baseYurophu ababekhiqizwe kusukela uConstantine asungula idolobha lakhe ngo-AD 

330. 

" yekhulu leshumi nesishiyagalombili lohwebo lwezincwadi lwaseJalimane njengenkathi ye-Sturm und Drang, isiJalimane “yesivunguvungu nengcindezi.”[49] 

Izithunywa zevangeli zaletha imishini yokunyathelisa e-Afrika eseningizimu yeSahara phakathi nekhulu le-18.[50] 

Ngokomlando, ukushicilela bekusingathwa abashicileli, nakuba abanye ababhali bezishicilela ngokwabo.[51] 

I-United States 
Ulwazi Olwengeziwe: Izincwadi E-United States kanye Nomlando Wencwadi eMelika
Imboni yokushicilela yase-US yaqala ngomshini wokunyathelisa eMassachusetts ngo-1638, yasungula iNew England njengendawo yokuqala. I-Philadelphia nayo yaba yinto ebalulekile, lapho uWilliam Bradford esungula umshini wokuqala wokugaya amaphepha kwathi uBenjamin Franklin evula owakhe umshini. Maphakathi nekhulu le-19, iDolobha laseNew York laba isikhungo semboni, esiphawulwa ukwanda kwezindlu ezinkulu zokushicilela ezifana noHarper, Wiley, Putnam, kanye noScribner, abahlomule emithethweni yamalungelo okushicilela nezindlela ezintsha zokusabalalisa. Ekuqaleni, bathembela kakhulu emisebenzini yaseBrithani engubugebengu kwaze kwaba yilapho kumiswa imithetho yamazwe ngamazwe yamalungelo okukopisha ngo-1891.[52] Maphakathi nekhulu le-19 futhi wabona izinto ezintsha ezifana ne-paperback "dime novels" eyenza izincwadi zitholakale kalula.[53] Inkathi yangemva kweMpi Yezwe I yaba yimpumelelo ekushicileleni kwaseMelika ngababhali abasha nabashicileli abafana noSimon & Schuster kanye neRandom House abasafufusa. Ukuwohloka Okukhulu Kwezomnotho kwabangela ukuhlehla, kodwa imboni yabuya ngemva kwempi. Kusukela ngawo-1960s, kube khona umkhuba wokuhlanganisa nokuhlanganiswa, okusheshisa ukukhula kwabathengisi abaku-inthanethi nama-ebook, nakuba iNew York City isalokhu iyisikhungo sokushicilela esikhulu emhlabeni wonke, ikhaya labashicileli be-"Big Five" (okuhlanganisa i-HarperCollins, i-Penguin Random House, no-Simon & Schuster, abashicileli bezemfundo, i-Mcmillan Learner, Mcmillan I-Scholastic, kanye no-Wiley, kanye nabashicileli abaningi abazimele.[54] Kusukela nge-Cornell University Press ngo-1869 kanye ne-Johns Hopkins University Press ngo-1878, amanyuvesi amaningi asungula izindlu zokushicilela ukuze ashicilele izincwadi zezazi namajenali alolu hlobo akhiqizwa ubuhlakani babo nabafundi abathweswe iziqu. Nokho, ekhulwini lama-21, izingcindezi zezimali. bebelokhu behlisa umkhiqizo wabo.[55] 

Ucwaningo olusekelwe e-US ngo-2016 olwahlola abashicileli abangu-34 lwathola ukuthi abesifazane abaqondile, abanamandla, abamhlophe bamele kakhulu imboni yokushicilela e-US.[56] I-Salon ichaze lesi simo ngokuthi "ukuntuleka kokuhlukahluka ngemuva kwezigcawu emhlabeni wezincwadi."[57] Inhlolovo yango-2020 eyenziwa yiqembu elifanayo yathola ukuthi alukho ushintsho olubalulekile lwezibalo ekuntulekeni kokuhlukahluka kusukela ngocwaningo lwango-2016.[58] Ukuntuleka kokuhlukahluka embonini yokushicilela yaseMelika bekuyinkinga iminyaka. Ngaphakathi embonini, inani elincane lokuhlukahluka lalisezikhundleni zokuhlela ezisezingeni eliphezulu.[59] 

Inkathi Ye-inthanethi 
Ukusungulwa kwe-World Wide Web ngo-1989 ngokushesha kwaqhubekisela phambili le webhusayithi endaweni ehamba phambili yokushicilela. Ama-Wiki namabhulogi athuthukiswa ngokushesha, alandelwa izincwadi eziku-inthanethi, amaphephandaba aku-inthanethi, nomagazini abaku-inthanethi. Lokhu kuphinde kwasiza nokuhlangana kobuchwepheshe kokuqukethwe kwezohwebo nokuzishicilele kanye nokuhlangana kokushicilela nokukhiqiza kube ukukhiqizwa ku-inthanethi ngokuthuthukiswa kokuqukethwe kwe-multimedia.

Ukuphrinta kuyinqubo yokukhiqiza kabusha umbhalo nezithombe ngobuningi kusetshenziswa ifomu eliyinhloko noma isifanekiso. Imikhiqizo yokuqala engeyona eyephepha ehlanganisa ukuphrinta ihlanganisa izigxivizo zamasilinda nezinto ezifana neCyrus Cylinder kanye namaCylinders kaNabonidasi. Indlela yokuqala eyaziwayo yokunyathelisa yavela ekukhuhleni kukayinki okwenziwe ephepheni noma endwangu emibhalweni ezibhebheni zamatshe, eyasetshenziswa phakathi nekhulu lesithupha.[1][a] Ukuphrinta ngokucindezela isithombe esinoyinki ephepheni (kusetshenziswa ukuphrinta kwe-woodblock) kwavela kamuva kulelo khulu leminyaka.[3] Intuthuko yakamuva kubuchwepheshe bokuphrinta ihlanganisa uhlobo olunyakazayo olwasungulwa ngu-Bi Sheng cishe ngo-1040[4][5] kanye nomshini wokunyathelisa owasungulwa nguJohannes Gutenberg ngekhulu le-15. Ubuchwepheshe bokunyathelisa badlala indima ebalulekile ekuthuthukisweni kweRenaissance kanye neScientific Revolution futhi babeka isisekelo esiphathekayo somnotho wesimanje osekelwe olwazini kanye nokusabalala kokufunda kubantu abaningi.[6] 

Umlando 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Umlando wokunyathelisa 
Ukuphrinta kwe-Woodblock 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukuphrinta i-Woodblock 
Ukuphrinta i-Woodblock kuyindlela yokunyathelisa umbhalo, izithombe noma amaphethini ayesetshenziswa kabanzi kulo lonke elaseMpumalanga Asia. Yavela eShayina emandulo njengendlela yokunyathelisa ezindwangu futhi kamuva ephepheni.[3] 

EMpumalanga Asia 

I-frontispiece eyinkimbinkimbi ye-Diamond Sutra evela ebukhosini base-Tang e-China, AD 868 (British Library), yatholwa e-Library Cave of Mogao Caves e-Dunhuang, kodwa cishe yanyatheliswa ngesi-Sichuan.[7] 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umlando wokunyathelisa e-East Asia 
Izibonelo zokuqala zokukhuhlwa kukayinki kanye namabhulokhi okuphrinta amatshe angaba khona avela maphakathi nekhulu lesithupha eShayina. Uhlobo lokuphrinta olubizwa nge-mechanical woodblock printing ephepheni lwaqala phakathi nekhulu lesi-7 ebukhosini baseTang, [3][1] futhi kamuva lwasakazeka kulo lonke elaseMpumalanga Asia. I-Nara Japan yanyathelisa i-Hyakumantō Darani ngobuningi cishe ngo-770, futhi yayisabalalisa emathempelini kulo lonke elaseJapane. E-Korea, isibonelo sokunyathelisa kwe-woodblock kusukela ngekhulu lesi-8 satholwa ngo-1966. Ikhophi ye-Buddhist Dharani Sutra ebizwa ngokuthi i-Pure Light Dharani Sutra (isiKorea: 무구정광대다라니경; Hanja: 無垢淨光大陀 Muguda jeong: 無垢淨光大陀 Muguda jeong: 無垢淨光大陀 Muguda jeong: darani-gyeong), etholwe eGyeongju, endaweni yobukhosi baseSilla eyalungiswa ngo-751, [8] yayingenasuku kodwa kumele ukuthi yadalwa esikhathini esithile ngaphambi kokwakhiwa kabusha kweShakyamuni Pagoda yeThempeli laseBulguk, eSifundazweni saseKyongju ngo-751.[9][10][11][12][13] Umbhalo kulinganiselwa ukuthi wakhiwe ngaphambi kuka-704.[8] 

Ngekhulu lesi-9, ukunyathelisa ephepheni kwase kuqalile, futhi incwadi yokuqala eyasinda ngokuphelele i-Diamond Sutra (British Library) ka-868, eyambulwa eDunhuang.[14] Ngekhulu leshumi, kwase kunyatheliswa amakhophi angu-400 000 ezinye ze-sutra nezithombe, futhi kwase kunyatheliswa izincwadi zakudala zobuConfucius. Umshicileli onekhono angaphrinta amashidi anamakhasi amabili angaba ngu-2,000 ngosuku.[15]

Ukunyathelisa kwasakazeka kusenesikhathi eKorea naseJapane, nayo eyayisebenzisa ama-logogram aseShayina, kodwa le ndlela yasetshenziswa naseTurpan naseVietnam kusetshenziswa inqwaba yezinye izincwadi. Le nqubo yabe isisakazekela ePheresiya naseRussia.[16] Le nqubo yadluliselwa eYurophu cishe ngonyaka we-1400 futhi yasetshenziswa ephepheni kuma-master prints amadala namakhadi okudlala.[17]351-367 



EMpumalanga Ephakathi 
Ukunyathelisa kweBlock, okubizwa ngokuthi i-tarsh ngesi-Arabhu, kwathuthukiswa ngesi-Arabhu saseGibhithe phakathi nekhulu lesishiyagalolunye neleshumi, ikakhulukazi emithandazweni nezigqizo. Kunobunye ubufakazi obubonisa ukuthi la mabhuloki okuphrinta ayenziwe ngezinto ezingezona zokhuni, mhlawumbe ithini, umthofu, noma ubumba. Amasu asetshenziswayo awaqinisekile. Ukunyathelisa kwe-block kamuva kwayeka ukusetshenziswa phakathi ne-Timurid Renaissance.[18] Indlela yokunyathelisa e-Egypt yamukelwa ngokukhiqiza kabusha imibhalo emigqeni yamaphepha futhi inikezwe ngamakhophi ahlukene ukuze ihlangabezane nesidingo.[19][20] 

EYurophu 

I-woodcut yokuqala eyaziwayo, i-1423, i-Buxheim, enemibala ye- 
Block printing yaqala ukufika eYurophu njengendlela yokunyathelisa endwangu, lapho yayivame khona ngo-1300. Lapho iphepha selitholakala kalula, cishe ngo-1400, le nqubo yadluliselwa ngokushesha ezithombeni zenkolo ezincane eziqoshwe ngokhuni kanye namakhadi okudlala anyatheliswe ephepheni. Lawa maphrinti akhiqizwa ngamanani amakhulu kakhulu kusukela ngo-1425 kuya phambili.978-0-495-09705-1 

Phakathi nekhulu leshumi nanhlanu, izincwadi ze-blockcut, izincwadi ze-woodcut ezinombhalo nemifanekiso, ngokuvamile ziqoshwe kubhlokhi efanayo, zavela njengendlela engabizi kakhulu kunemibhalo yesandla nezincwadi eziphrintiwe ngohlobo olunyakazayo. Yonke lena kwakuyimisebenzi emifushane, enemifanekiso eminingi, eyayithengiswa kakhulu ngaleso sikhathi, eyayiphindwa ezinguqulweni eziningi ze-block-book: i-Ars moriendi ne-Biblia pauperum kwakuyizona ezazivame kakhulu. Kusenempikiswano phakathi kwezazi mayelana nokuthi isingeniso sazo sandulela yini noma, ngokombono weningi, silandele ukwethulwa kohlobo olugudlukayo, nenani elilinganiselwe lezinsuku liphakathi kuka-1440 no-1460.[21]

i-Jikji, "Izimfundiso Ezikhethiwe Zezazi ZamaBuddha Nezazi ZeNdodana" yaseKorea, incwadi yokuqala eyaziwayo eyanyatheliswa ngohlobo lwensimbi enyakazayo, 1377. I-Bibliothèque 
type 
Types i-typography isebenzisa izingcezu ezinyakazayo zohlobo lwensimbi, ezenziwe ngokusakazwa kumatrices ashaywe ama-letterpunch. Uhlobo olunyakazayo luvunyelwe izinqubo eziguquguqukayo kakhulu kunokukopisha ngesandla noma ukuphrinta kwebhulokhi.

Cishe ngo-1040, isistimu yokuqala eyaziwayo yohlobo olunyakazayo yadalwa eShayina ngu-Bi Sheng nge-porcelain.[5] U-Bi Sheng wasebenzisa uhlobo lobumba, olwaphuka kalula, kodwa u-Wang Zhen ngo-1298 wayeseqophe uhlobo oluhlala isikhathi eside ngokhuni. Wakha nesimiso esiyinkimbinkimbi samatafula ajikelezayo kanye nokuhlotshaniswa kwezinombolo nezinhlamvu zesiShayina ezibhaliwe okwenza ukuhlela nokunyathelisa kuphumelele kakhudlwana. Noma kunjalo, indlela eyinhloko eyayisetshenziswa lapho yahlala inyathelisa i-woodblock (xylography), “eyabonakala ishibhile futhi iphumelela kangcono ekunyatheliseni isiShayina, nezinkulungwane zezinhlamvu zaso”.[22] 

Ukunyathelisa kwezinhlamvu zethusi ezinyakazayo kwaqala eShayina ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-12. Yayisetshenziswa ekunyatheliseni imali enkulu yephepha eyayikhishwe ubukhosi beNgoma YaseNyakatho. Uhlobo olunyakazayo lwasakazekela eKorea ngesikhathi sobukhosi bakwaGoryeo. 

Cishe ngo-1230, amaKorea asungula uhlobo lwensimbi lokunyathelisa olugudlukayo lisebenzisa ithusi. I-Jikji, eyanyatheliswa ngo-1377, iyincwadi yokuqala eyaziwa ngensimbi. Kwasetshenziswa uhlobo lokulingisa, lwashintshwa kusukela endleleni yokuphonsa izinhlamvu zemali. Lo mlingiswa wayesikwa ngokhuni lwe-beech, olwalube selucindezelwa odakeni oluthambile ukuze lube isikhunta, bese luthelwa ithusi esikhunjeni, futhi ekugcineni lolo hlobo lwapholishwa.[23] Uhlobo lwensimbi yaseMpumalanga olunyakazayo lwasakazwa eYurophu phakathi kwekhulu le-14 nasekuqaleni kwekhulu le-15.[24][25][26][27][28] Uhlobo lwesiKorea lohlobo lwensimbi olunyakazayo lwachazwa isazi esingumFulentshi uHenri-Jean Martin ngokuthi "lufana kakhulu nelikaGutenberg".[29] Izazi-mlando ezigunyaziwe uFrances Gies noJoseph Gies zathi "Ukubaluleka kwase-Asia kokusungulwa kwezinhlobo ezinyakazayo manje sekuqinisekisiwe ngokuqinile, nokuthi indlela yesiShayina-Korean, noma umbiko wayo waya ngasentshonalanga cishe uqinisekile."[30] 
Icala 


lezingcezu zohlobo lwensimbi ecijile kanye nodaba lohlobo lwento 
entongeni 
yokuqamba IPlantin-Moretus Museum 
Cishe ngo-1450, uJohannes Gutenberg wethula isimiso sokuqala sokunyathelisa ngomshini eYurophu. Uthuthuke emasu okulingisa okusekelwe ku-matrix nesikhunta sesandla, ukujwayela ukucindezela isikulufu, ukusetshenziswa kukayinki osekelwe kuwoyela, nokudalwa kwephepha elithambile nelimunca kakhulu.[31] UGutenberg waba ngowokuqala ukudala izingcezu zakhe zohlobo ngengxubevange yomthofu, ithini, i-antimony, ithusi ne-bismuth - izingxenye ezifanayo ezisasetshenziswa nanamuhla.[32] UJohannes Gutenberg waqala umsebenzi emshinini wakhe wokunyathelisa cishe ngo-1436, ebambisene no-Andreas Dritzehen - ayemyalele ngaphambili ukusika amagugu - kanye no-Andreas Heilmann, umnikazi womshini wokugaya amaphepha.[33][ikhasi elidingekayo]


Uma kuqhathaniswa nokunyathelisa kwe-woodblock, ukulungiselelwa kwamakhasi ohlobo olususwayo nokunyathelisa kusetshenziswa umshini wokunyathelisa kwakushesha futhi kuhlala isikhathi eside. Futhi, izingcezu zohlobo lwensimbi zaziqinile futhi izinhlamvu zifana kakhulu, okuholela ekubhaleni nasekubhaleni amafonti. Izinga eliphezulu kanye nenani eliphansi leBhayibheli likaGutenberg (1455) lasungula ukuphakama kwezinhlobo ezinyakazayo zezilimi zaseNtshonalanga. Umshini wokunyathelisa wasabalala ngokushesha kulo lonke elaseYurophu, kwaholela eNkathini Yenguquko, futhi kamuva emhlabeni wonke.[34] 


Igumbi lokuhlela ikhasi – c. 1920 
Umagazini i-Time Life wabiza izinto ezintsha zikaGutenberg ekunyatheliseni kwezinhlamvu ezinyakazayo njengokuqanjwa okubaluleke kakhulu kwenkulungwane yesibili yeminyaka.[35] 

Umshini wokunyathelisa we-Rotary 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Umshini wokunyathelisa we-Rotary 
Umshini wokunyathelisa we-rotary osebenza ngesitimu, owasungulwa ngo-1843 e-United States ngu-Richard M. Hoe,[36] ekugcineni wavumela izigidi zamakhophi ekhasi ngosuku olulodwa. Ukukhiqizwa ngobuningi bemisebenzi ephrintiwe kwachuma ngemva kokushintshela ephepheni eligoqiwe, njengoba ukudla okuqhubekayo kwavumela imishini ukuba isebenze ngesivinini esikhulu. Umklamo wokuqala kaHoe wawusebenza ngokushintshashintsha okungafika ku-2,000 ngehora lapho inguquko ngayinye ifaka izithombe zamakhasi angu-4, okunikeza umshini wokunyathelisa umphumela wamakhasi angu-8,000 ngehora.[37] Ngo-1891, i-New York World kanye ne-Philadelphia Item zase zisebenza ngomshini wokunyathelisa zikhiqiza amaphepha angu-90,000 anamakhasi angu-4 ngehora noma angu-48,000 anamakhasi angu-8.[38] 

Umshini wokunyathelisa we-rotary usebenzisa okuvelayo okugobe eduze kwesilinda ukuze uphrinte kumaroli amade aqhubekayo ephepha noma amanye ama-substrates. Ukunyatheliswa kwezigubhu ezijikelezayo kamuva kwathuthukiswa kakhulu nguWilliam Bullock. Kunezinhlobo eziningi zobuchwepheshe bemishini yokunyathelisa ye-rotary ezisasetshenziswa nanamuhla: i-sheetfed offset, i-rotogravure, ne-flexographic printing.[39] 

Amandla okuphrinta 
Ithebula libala inani eliphezulu lamakhasi imiklamo ehlukahlukene yokunyathelisa engaphrintwa ngehora.

History=400 ukuphrinta 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukuphrinta i-Woodblock 
Ukuphrinta i-Woodblock kuyindlela yokunyathelisa umbhalo, izithombe noma amaphethini ayesetshenziswa kabanzi kulo lonke elaseMpumalanga Asia. Yavela eShayina emandulo njengendlela yokunyathelisa ezindwangu futhi kamuva ephepheni.[3] 

E-East Asia 

I-frontispiece eyinkimbinkimbi ye-Diamond Sutra evela ebukhosini base-Tang e-China, AD 868 (British Library), yatholwa e-Library Cave of Mogao Caves e-Dunhuang, kodwa cishe yanyatheliswa ngesi-Sichuan.[45] 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umlando wokuphrinta eMpumalanga Asia
Izibonelo zakuqala zokukhuhlwa kokucindezela kukayinki kanye namabhulokhi okuphrinta amatshe angaba khona avela maphakathi nekhulu lesithupha e-China. Uhlobo lokuphrinta olubizwa nge-mechanical woodblock printing ephepheni lwaqala phakathi nekhulu lesi-7 ebukhosini baseTang, [3][1] futhi kamuva lwasakazeka kulo lonke elaseMpumalanga Asia. I-Nara Japan yanyathelisa i-Hyakumantō Darani ngobuningi cishe ngo-770, futhi yayisabalalisa emathempelini kulo lonke elaseJapane. E-Korea, isibonelo sokunyathelisa kwe-woodblock kusukela ngekhulu lesi-8 satholwa ngo-1966. Ikhophi ye-Buddhist Dharani Sutra ebizwa ngokuthi i-Pure Light Dharani Sutra (isiKorea: 무구정광대다라니경; Hanja: 無垢淨光大陀 Muguda jeong: 無垢淨光大陀 Muguda jeong: 無垢淨光大陀 Muguda jeong: darani-gyeong), etholwe eGyeongju, endaweni yobukhosi baseSilla eyalungiswa ngo-751, [8] yayingenasuku kodwa kumele ukuthi yadalwa esikhathini esithile ngaphambi kokwakhiwa kabusha kweShakyamuni Pagoda yeThempeli laseBulguk, eSifundazweni saseKyongju ngo-751.[9][46][47][48][49] Umbhalo kulinganiselwa ukuthi wakhiwe ngaphambi kuka-704.[8] 

Ngekhulu lesi-9, ukuphrinta ephepheni kwase kuqalile, futhi incwadi yokuqala eyasinda ngokuphelele i-Diamond Sutra (British Library) ka-868, eyambulwa eDunhuang.[50] Ngekhulu leshumi, kwase kunyatheliswa amakhophi angu-400 000 ezinye ze-sutra nezithombe, futhi kwase kunyatheliswa izincwadi zakudala zobuConfucius. Umshicileli onekhono angaphrinta amashidi anamakhasi amabili angaba ngu-2,000 ngosuku.[15] 

Ukunyathelisa kwasakazeka kusenesikhathi eKorea naseJapane, nayo eyayisebenzisa ama-logogram aseShayina, kodwa le ndlela yasetshenziswa naseTurpan naseVietnam kusetshenziswa inqwaba yezinye izincwadi. Le nqubo yabe isisakazekela ePheresiya naseRussia.[16] Le nqubo yadluliselwa eYurophu cishe ngo-1400 futhi yasetshenziswa ephepheni kuma-master prints amadala kanye namakhadi okudlala.[51]351-367 



EMpumalanga Ephakathi 
Ukunyathelisa kweBlock, okubizwa ngokuthi i-tarsh ngesi-Arabhu, kwathuthukiswa ngesi-Arabhu saseGibhithe phakathi nekhulu lesishiyagalolunye neleshumi, ikakhulukazi emithandazweni nezigqizo. Kunobunye ubufakazi obubonisa ukuthi la mabhuloki okuphrinta ayenziwe ngezinto ezingezona zokhuni, mhlawumbe ithini, umthofu, noma ubumba. Amasu asetshenziswayo awaqinisekile. Ukunyathelisa kwe-block kamuva kwayeka ukusetshenziswa phakathi ne-Timurid Renaissance.[52] Indlela yokunyathelisa e-Egypt yamukelwa ngokukhiqiza kabusha imibhalo emigqeni yamaphepha futhi inikezwe ngamakhophi ahlukene ukuze ihlangabezane nesidingo.[53][20] 

EYurophu 

I-woodcut yokuqala eyaziwayo, i-1423, i-Buxheim, enemibala ye- 
Block printing yaqala ukufika eYurophu njengendlela yokunyathelisa endwangu, lapho yayivame khona ngo-1300. Lapho iphepha selitholakala kalula, cishe ngo-1400, le nqubo yadluliselwa ngokushesha ezithombeni zenkolo ezincane eziqoshwe ngokhuni kanye namakhadi okudlala anyatheliswe ephepheni. Lawa maphrinti akhiqizwa ngamanani amakhulu kakhulu kusukela ngo-1425 kuya phambili.978-0-495-09705-1

Maphakathi nekhulu leshumi nanhlanu, i-block-books, izincwadi eziqoshwe ngokhuni ezinombhalo nemifanekiso, ngokuvamile eziqoshwe endaweni eyodwa, zavela njengenye indlela eshibhile kunemibhalo yesandla nezincwadi eziphrintwe ngezinhlamvu ezinyakazayo. Yonke lena kwakuyimisebenzi emifushane, enemifanekiso eminingi, eyayithengiswa kakhulu ngaleso sikhathi, eyayiphindwa ezinguqulweni eziningi ze-block-book: i-Ars moriendi ne-Biblia pauperum kwakuyizona ezazivame kakhulu. Kusenempikiswano phakathi kwezazi mayelana nokuthi isingeniso sazo sandulela yini noma, ngokombono weningi, silandele ukwethulwa kohlobo olugudlukayo, nenani elilinganiselwe lezinsuku liphakathi kuka-1440 no-1460.[54] 

Ukuphrinta kohlobo olunyakazayo I- 

Copperplate engu-1215–1216 5000 yemali yephepha engukheshi enezinhlobo eziyishumi zethusi ezihambayo 

i-Jikji, "Izimfundiso Ezikhethiwe Zezazi ZamaBuddha Nezazi ZeNdodana" yaseKorea, incwadi yokuqala eyaziwayo eyanyatheliswa ngohlobo lwensimbi enyakazayo, 1377. I-Bibliothèque 
type 
Types i-typography isebenzisa izingcezu ezinyakazayo zohlobo lwensimbi, ezenziwe ngokusakazwa kumatrices ashaywe ama-letterpunch. Uhlobo olunyakazayo luvunyelwe izinqubo eziguquguqukayo kakhulu kunokukopisha ngesandla noma ukuphrinta kwebhulokhi. 

Cishe ngo-1040, isistimu yokuqala eyaziwayo yohlobo olunyakazayo yadalwa eShayina ngu-Bi Sheng nge-porcelain.[5] U-Bi Sheng wasebenzisa uhlobo lobumba, olwaphuka kalula, kodwa u-Wang Zhen ngo-1298 wayeseqophe uhlobo oluhlala isikhathi eside ngokhuni. Wakha nesimiso esiyinkimbinkimbi samatafula ajikelezayo kanye nokuhlotshaniswa kwezinombolo nezinhlamvu zesiShayina ezibhaliwe okwenza ukuhlela nokunyathelisa kuphumelele kakhudlwana. Noma kunjalo, indlela eyinhloko eyayisetshenziswa lapho yahlala inyathelisa i-woodblock (xylography), “eyabonakala ishibhile futhi iphumelela kangcono ekunyatheliseni isiShayina, nezinkulungwane zezinhlamvu zaso”.[55] 

Ukunyathelisa kwezinhlamvu zethusi ezinyakazayo kwaqala eShayina ekuqaleni kwekhulu le-12. Yayisetshenziswa ekunyatheliseni imali enkulu yephepha eyayikhishwe ubukhosi beNgoma YaseNyakatho. Uhlobo olunyakazayo lwasakazekela eKorea ngesikhathi sobukhosi bakwaGoryeo. 

Cishe ngo-1230, amaKorea asungula uhlobo lwensimbi lokunyathelisa olugudlukayo lisebenzisa ithusi. I-Jikji, eyanyatheliswa ngo-1377, iyincwadi yokuqala eyaziwa ngensimbi. Kwasetshenziswa uhlobo lokulingisa, lwashintshwa kusukela endleleni yokuphonsa izinhlamvu zemali. Lo mlingiswa wayesikwa ngokhuni lwe-beech, olwalube selucindezelwa odakeni oluthambile ukuze lube isikhunta, bese luthelwa ithusi esikhunjeni, futhi ekugcineni lolo hlobo lwapholishwa.[56] Uhlobo lwensimbi yaseMpumalanga olunyakazayo lwasakazwa eYurophu phakathi kwekhulu le-14 nasekuqaleni kwekhulu le-15.[57][58][59][60][61] Uhlobo lwesiKorea lohlobo lwensimbi olususekayo lwachazwa isazi esingumFulentshi uHenri-Jean Martin ngokuthi "lufana kakhulu nelikaGutenberg".[62] Izazi-mlando ezigunyaziwe u-Frances Gies no-Joseph Gies zathi "Ukubaluleka kwase-Asia kokusungulwa kwezinhlobo ezinyakazayo sekuqinisekisiwe ngokuqinile, futhi indlela yesiShayina-Korean, noma umbiko wayo owaya ngasentshonalanga cishe uqinisekile."[30]


Ikesi lezingcezu zohlobo lwensimbi ecijile kanye nodaba lwesethi othini lokuhlanganisa Umshini 
wokunyathelisa 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umshini wokunyathelisa 

Ukusungulwa kokunyathelisa, okungaziwa, okuklanywe ngu-Stradanus, iqoqo I-Plantin-Moretus Museum 
Cishe ngo-1450, u-Johannes Gutenberg wethula uhlelo lokuqala lokunyathelisa lwezinhlobo ezihambayo eYurophu. Uthuthuke kakhulu ohlotsheni lokulingisa olusekelwe ku-matrix nesikhunta sesandla, ukujwayela ukucindezela isikulufu, ukusetshenziswa kukayinki osuselwa kuwoyela, nokudalwa kwephepha elithambile nelimunca kakhulu.[63] UGutenberg waba ngowokuqala ukudala izingcezu zakhe zohlobo ngengxubevange yomthofu, ithini, i-antimony, ithusi ne-bismuth - izingxenye ezifanayo ezisasetshenziswa nanamuhla.[64] UJohannes Gutenberg waqala umsebenzi emshinini wakhe wokunyathelisa cishe ngo-1436, ebambisene no-Andreas Dritzehen - ayemyale ngaphambili ekusikeni amagugu - kanye no-Andreas Heilmann, umnikazi womshini wokugaya amaphepha 

. Futhi, izingcezu zohlobo lwensimbi zaziqinile futhi izinhlamvu zifana kakhulu, okuholela ekubhaleni nasekubhaleni amafonti. Izinga eliphezulu kanye nenani eliphansi leBhayibheli likaGutenberg (1455) lasungula ukuphakama kwezinhlobo ezinyakazayo zezilimi zaseNtshonalanga. Umshini wokunyathelisa wasabalala ngokushesha kulo lonke elaseYurophu, kwaholela eNkathini Yenguquko, futhi kamuva emhlabeni wonke.[65] 


Igumbi lokuhlela ikhasi – c. 1920 
Umagazini i-Time Life wabiza izinto ezintsha zikaGutenberg ekunyatheliseni kwezinhlamvu ezinyakazayo njengokuqanjwa okubaluleke kakhulu kwenkulungwane yesibili yeminyaka.[66] 

Umshini wokunyathelisa we-Rotary 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Umshini wokunyathelisa we-Rotary 
Umshini wokunyathelisa we-rotary osebenza ngesitimu, owasungulwa ngo-1843 e-United States ngu-Richard M. Hoe,[36] ekugcineni wavumela izigidi zamakhophi ekhasi ngosuku olulodwa. Ukukhiqizwa ngobuningi bemisebenzi ephrintiwe kwachuma ngemva kokushintshela ephepheni eligoqiwe, njengoba ukudla okuqhubekayo kwavumela imishini ukuba isebenze ngesivinini esikhulu. Umklamo kaHoe wangempela wawusebenza ngokushintshashintsha okungafika ku-2,000 ngehora lapho inguquko ngayinye ifaka izithombe zamakhasi angu-4, okunikeza umshini wokunyathelisa umphumela wamakhasi angu-8,000 ngehora.[67] Ngo-1891, i-New York World kanye ne-Philadelphia Item zase zisebenza ngomshini wokunyathelisa zikhiqiza amaphepha angu-90,000 anamakhasi angu-4 ngehora noma angu-48,000 anamakhasi angu-8.[68] 

Umshini wokunyathelisa we-rotary usebenzisa okuvelayo okugobe eduze kwesilinda ukuze uphrinte kumaroli amade aqhubekayo ephepha noma amanye ama-substrates. Ukunyatheliswa kwezigubhu ezijikelezayo kamuva kwathuthukiswa kakhulu nguWilliam Bullock. Kunezinhlobo eziningi zobuchwepheshe bemishini yokunyathelisa ye-rotary ezisasetshenziswa nanamuhla: i-sheetfed offset, i-rotogravure, ne-flexographic printing.[69]

Ezivamile izindawo 
zokuphrinta 
ezimbili eziphathelene nenqubo yokuphrinta yohlobo lokugcina 
indawo (izindawo zokunyathelisa) 
Indawo okungezona izithombe (izindawo okungezona zokunyathelisa) 
Ngemva kokuba ulwazi selulungiselelwe ukukhiqizwa (isinyathelo sangaphambi kokushicilela), inqubo ngayinye yokunyathelisa inezindlela eziqondile zokuhlukanisa isithombe ezindaweni ezingezona izithombe. 

Ukuphrinta okuvamile kunezinhlobo ezine zenqubo: 

I-Planographics, lapho izindawo zokunyathelisa nezingaphrinti zisendaweni efanayo yendiza futhi umehluko phakathi kwazo ugcinwa ngamakhemikhali noma ngezakhiwo ezibonakalayo, izibonelo yilezi: i-offset lithography, i-collotype, nokuphrinta okungenasici. 
I-Relief, lapho izindawo zokunyathelisa zisendaweni yendiza futhi izindawo ezinganyathelisi zingaphansi kwendawo, izibonelo: i-flexography ne-letterpress. 
I-Intaglio, lapho izindawo ezingaphrintiwe zisendaweni yendiza futhi indawo yokunyathelisa igxiliwe noma iqoshwe ngaphansi kwendawo, izibonelo: i-steel die engraving, i-gravure, i-etching, i-collagraph. 
I-Porous noma i-Stencil, lapho izindawo zokunyathelisa zisezikrinini ze-mesh emihle lapho u-inki angangena khona, futhi izindawo ezingaphrinti ziyi-stencil phezu kwesikrini ukuvimba ukugeleza kukayinki kulezo zindawo, izibonelo: ukuphrinta kwesikrini, i-stencil duplicator, i-risograph. 
Amamaki wokunqampuna 
Ukuze uphrinte isithombe ngaphandle kwendawo engenalutho ezungeze isithombe, izindawo ezingaphrintiwe kufanele zisikwe ngemva kokuphrinta. Izimpawu zokunqampuna zingasetshenziswa ukuze kuboniswe iphrinta lapho indawo yokuphrinta iphelela khona, nendawo yokungaphrinti iqala.[71] Ingxenye yesithombe esikiwe ibizwa ngokuthi yi-bleed. 

I-Letterpress 

Miehle iphrinta iphephabhuku i-Le Samedi. Montreal, 1939. 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukuphrinta kwe-Letterpress 
I-Letterpress printing iyindlela yokunyathelisa yokusiza. Isisebenzi siqamba futhi sikhiye uhlobo lomshini womshini wokunyathelisa, siwufake uyinki, bese sicindezela iphepha ukuze sidlulise uyinki ohlotsheni oludala isithombe ephepheni. Kunamaphepha ahlukene emisebenzi eyahlukene izinga lephepha likhombisa uyinki ohlukene ozosetshenziswa. 

Ukunyathelisa nge-Letterpress kwakuyindlela evamile yokunyathelisa yombhalo kusukela eyasungulwa nguJohannes Gutenberg phakathi nekhulu le-15 futhi yaqhubeka isetshenziswa kakhulu ezincwadini nakwezinye izinto kwaze kwaba sengxenyeni yesibili yekhulu lama-20, lapho kuthuthukiswa ukunyathelisa nge-offset. Muva nje, ukuphrinta kwe-letterpress kubone imvuselelo ngendlela yobuciko. I-athikili eyinhloko 

ye-Offset 
: Cindezela i-Offset 
Imishini yokunyathelisa engamathani angu-910 e-Las Vegas Review-Journal yayimikhulu kakhulu emhlabeni ngesikhathi ifakwa ngo-2000.
Ukuphrinta kwe-Offset kuyinqubo yokuphrinta yesimanje esetshenziswa kakhulu. Lobu buchwepheshe buchazwa kangcono njengalapho isithombe esihle (esifundwa kwesokudla) epuleti lokuphrinta sifakwa uyinki futhi sidluliswa (noma "i-offset") sisuka epuletini siye kwembethe yenjoloba. Isithombe sengubo siba isithombe sesibuko sesithombe sepuleti. Ukudluliswa kwe-offset kuhambisa isithombe ku-substrate yokuphrinta (imvamisa eyiphepha), okwenza isithombe sifundeke kahle futhi. Ukuphrinta kwe-Offset kusebenzisa inqubo ye-lithographic esekelwe ekwakhiweni kukawoyela namanzi. Inqubo ye-offset isebenzisa isithwali sesithombe esiyisicaba (i-planographic) (ipuleti) esigxunyekwe kusilinda sokucindezela. Isithombe esizophrintwa sithola uyinki kumarola ayinki, kuyilapho indawo engaphrinteki iheha ifilimu yamanzi (e-acidic), egcina izindawo ezingezona izithombe zingena-inki. Imishini eminingi yokunyathelisa ye-offset isebenzisa amasilinda amathathu: Ipuleti, ingubo yokulala, okugxilile. Njengamanje, izincwadi eziningi namaphephandaba anyatheliswa kusetshenziswa i-offset lithography. I-athikili eyinhloko 

ye-Gravure 
: 
Ukuphrinta kwe-Rotogravure Gravure kuyindlela yokuphrinta ye-intaglio, lapho isithombe esinyatheliswayo sakhiwe ama-depression amancane ebusweni bepuleti lokuphrinta. Amaseli agcwaliswa ngoyinki, futhi okungaphezu kwalokho kukhishwa phezulu ngensingo kadokotela. Khona-ke irola elimbozwe ngenjoloba licindezela iphepha phezu kwepuleti futhi lithintane noyinki osemaseli. Amasilinda okuphrinta ngokuvamile enziwa ngensimbi ene-copper plated, kamuva efakwe i-chrome, futhi ingase ikhiqizwe ngokuqoshwa kwedayimane; i-laser ablation, noma i-etching. 

Ukuphrinta kwe-Gravure kwaziwa ngekhono lakhona lokukhiqiza izithombe ezisezingeni eliphezulu, ezinesinqumo esiphezulu ngokuzalanisa umbala onembile kanye nokusebenzisa imishini yokulawula i-viscosity ngesikhathi sokukhiqiza. Ukulawula ukuhwamuka kukayinki kuthinta ushintsho kumbala wesithombe esiphrintiwe. 

Ukuphrinta kwe-Gravure kusetshenziselwa ukuphrinta okude, kwekhwalithi ephezulu okufana namamagazini, amakhathalogi a-oda ngeposi, ukupakisha nokuphrinta endwangu nasesithombeni sangemuva. Ibuye isetshenziselwe ukuphrinta izitembu zokuposa kanye nama-laminates epulasitiki okuhlobisa, njengezindawo zokusebenza zasekhishini. 

I-Flexography 
I-Flexography iwuhlobo lokuphrinta impumuzo. Amapuleti okusiza ngokuvamile enziwa ngama-photopolymers. Inqubo isetshenziselwa ukupakisha okuguquguqukayo, ibhodi likathayela, amalebula, amaphephandaba nokunye. Kule makethe iqhudelana nokuphrinta i-gravure ngokubamba u-80% wemakethe e-US, 50% eYurophu kodwa kuphela u-20% e-Asia.[72] 

Amanye amasu okuphrinta 
Amanye amasu okuphrinta abalulekile ahlanganisa: 

Iphrinta ye-Dye-sublimation 
Inkjet, esetshenziselwa ukuphrinta inombolo encane yezincwadi noma ukupakisha, kanye nokuphrinta izinto ezihlukahlukene: kusukela kumaphepha ekhwalithi ephezulu alingisa ukuphrinta kwe-offset, kuya kumathayela aphansi. I-inkjet iphinde isetshenziselwe ukusebenzisa amakheli okuposa ukuqondisa izingcezu zemeyili 
Ukuphrinta nge-laser (ukuphrinta kwe-toner) okusetshenziswa kakhulu emahhovisi kanye nokuphrinta kohwebo (izikweletu, imibhalo yasebhange). Ukuphrinta nge-laser kuvame ukusetshenziswa izinkampani zemeyili eziqondile ukuze zenze izinhlamvu zedatha eziguquguqukayo noma amakhuphoni. 
Ukuphrinta kwephedi, okudumile ngekhono lakhona lokuphrinta endaweni eyinkimbinkimbi enezinhlangothi ezintathu 
Ukuphrinta kosizo, okusetshenziselwa ikakhulukazi amakhathalogi
Ukuphrinta isikrini kwezinhlelo zokusebenza ezihlukahlukene kusukela kuzikibha kuya kumathayela aphansi, nasezindaweni ezingalingani 
i-Intaglio, esetshenziswa kakhulu kumadokhumenti yenani eliphezulu njengezinhlobo zemali. 
Ukuphrinta okushisayo, okwaduma ngeminyaka yawo-1990 ukuphrinta ngefeksi. Isetshenziswa namuhla ukuphrinta amalebula afana namathegi emithwalo yendiza namalebula amanani angawodwana ezibalini zezitolo ezinkulu. 
Umthelela womshini wokunyathelisa wohlobo olunyakazayo lwesiJalimane 

Izici zobuningi 

Ukukhishwa kwezincwadi zase-Europe eziphrintwe ngohlobo olususekayo ukusuka ku-c. 1450 kuya ku-1800[73] 
Isihloko Esiyinhloko: Umlando Wokunyathelisa 
Kulinganiselwa ukuthi ngemva kokusungulwa komshini wokunyathelisa kaGutenberg, ukukhishwa kwezincwadi zaseYurophu kwenyuka kusuka ezigidini ezimbalwa kuya kumakhophi acishe abe yizigidi eziyinkulungwane phakathi nenkathi engaphansi kwamakhulu amane eminyaka.[73] 

Umthelela ongokwenkolo 
uSamuel Hartlib, owadingiselwa eBrithani futhi eshisekela izinguquko kwezenhlalo namasiko, wabhala ngo-1641 ukuthi “ubuciko bokunyathelisa buyosakaza ulwazi kangangokuthi abantu abavamile, bewazi amalungelo nenkululeko yabo, ngeke babuswe ngendlela yokucindezela”.[74][75] 


I-Replica yomshini wokunyathelisa we-Gutenberg e-International Printing Museum e-Carson, eCalifornia 
Ezweni lamaSulumane, ukuphrinta, ikakhulukazi ngemibhalo yesi-Arabhu, kwaphikiswa kakhulu phakathi nenkathi yesimanjemanje, ngokwengxenye ngenxa yodumo oluphezulu lobuciko lobuciko be-calligraphy bendabuko. Nokho, ukunyathelisa ngezinhlamvu zesiHeberu noma zesi-Armenia ngokuvamile kwakuvunyelwe. Ngakho, ukunyathelisa kwezinhlamvu zokuqala ezinyakazayo eMbusweni Wase-Ottoman kwaba ngesiHeberu ngo-1493, okwathi ngemva kwalokho imibhalo yenkolo nengeyona eyenkolo yanyatheliswa ngesiHeberu.[76] Ngokusho kwenxusa lombuso e-Istanbul phakathi nekhulu leshumi nesithupha, kwakuyisono kubantu baseTurkey, ikakhulukazi amaSulumane aseTurkey, ukunyathelisa izincwadi zenkolo. Ngo-1515, uSultan Selim I wakhipha isimemezelo sokuthi umsebenzi wokunyathelisa wawuyoba nesijeziso sokufa. Ekupheleni kwekhulu leshumi nesithupha, uSultan Murad III wavumela ukudayiswa kwezincwadi ezinyathelisiwe ezingezona ezenkolo ngezinhlamvu zesi-Arabhu, kodwa eziningi zazivela e-Italy. U-Ibrahim Muteferrika wasungula umshini wokuqala wokunyathelisa owawuzonyatheliswa ngesi-Arabhu eMbusweni Wase-Ottoman, ngokumelene nokuphikiswa ngabadwebi be-calligrapher nezingxenye ze-Ulama. Yasebenza kwaze kwaba ngu-1742, ikhiqiza yonke imisebenzi eyishumi nesikhombisa, yonke eyayiphathelene nezindaba ezingezona ezenkolo, eziwusizo. Ukunyathelisa akuzange kube yinto evamile ezweni lamaSulumane kwaze kwaba sekhulwini le-19. [77]

Abanyathelisi bolimi lwesiHeberu bavinjelwa ezinhlanganweni zokunyathelisa kwezinye izifundazwe zaseJalimane; ngenxa yalokho, ukunyatheliswa kwesiHeberu kwachuma e-Italy, kusukela ngo-1470 eRoma, kwase kusakazekela nakwamanye amadolobha ahlanganisa iBari, iPisa, iLivorno, neMantua. Ababusi bendawo babenegunya lokunikeza noma ukuhoxisa amalayisense okushicilela izincwadi zesiHebheru,[78] futhi eziningi zalezo eziphrintiwe ngalesi sikhathi zinamagama athi 'con licenza de superiori' (okubonisa ukunyathelisa kwazo kunikezwe ilayisense ngokusemthethweni) emakhasini azo ezihloko. 

Kwakucatshangwa ukuthi ukwethulwa kokunyathelisa ‘kwakuzoqinisa inkolo futhi kuthuthukise amandla amakhosi.’[79] Iningi lezincwadi lalingezenkolo, isonto nomqhele olawula okuqukethwe. Imiphumela yokunyathelisa izinto 'ezingalungile' yayidlulele. UMeyrowitz[79] wasebenzisa isibonelo sikaWilliam Carter owathi ngo-1584 wanyathelisa ipheshana elisekela ubuKatolika eNgilandi eyayibuswa amaProthestani. Umphumela wesenzo sakhe wawulenga. 

Umthelela wenhlalo 
Ukuphrinta kunikeze ububanzi obubanzi babafundi ukufinyelela olwazini futhi kwavumela izizukulwane zakamuva ukuba zakhele ngokuqondile ezimpumelelweni zobuhlakani zezangaphambili ngaphandle kwezinguquko ezivele ngaphakathi kwamasiko omlomo. Ukuphrinta, ngokuka-Acton enkulumweni yakhe ethi On the Study of History, yango-1895, kwanikeza "isiqinisekiso sokuthi umsebenzi we-Renaissance wawuyohlala njalo, ukuthi lokho okulotshiwe kwakuyofinyeleleka kubo bonke, ukuthi ukuthakatha okunjalo kolwazi nemibono njengoba kwakucindezele iNkathi Ephakathi kwakungeke kuphinde kuvele, ukuthi akukho mbono owawuzolahleka." [74] 


Ukuphrinta izincwadi ngekhulu le-16 
Ukuphrinta kwaba nesandla ekuguquleni isimo somphakathi sokufunda. 

U-Elizabeth Eisenstein uveza imiphumela emibili yesikhathi eside yokusungulwa kokunyathelisa. Uthi ukuphrinta kwakha inkomba eqhubekayo nefanayo yolwazi futhi kwavumela ukuqhathaniswa kwemibono engahambelani.[80] 

U-Asa Briggs noPeter Burke bahlonza izinhlobo ezinhlanu zokufunda ezathuthukiswa maqondana nokwethulwa kokuphrinta: 

Ukufundwa okubucayi: Ngenxa yokuthi imibhalo yagcina ifinyeleleka kubantu abaningi, ukufundwa okuhlolisisayo kwavela lapho abantu bekwazi ukuzakhela eyabo imibono ngemibhalo. 
Ukufunda okuyingozi: Ukufunda kwakubhekwa njengento eyingozi ngoba kwakubhekwa njengokuvukelayo nokungahlangani, ikakhulukazi kwabesifazane, ngoba ukufunda kwakungavusa imizwelo eyingozi enjengothando, futhi uma abesifazane bekwazi ukufunda, babekwazi ukufunda amanothi othando. 
Ukufunda ngobuciko: Ukuphrinta kwavumela abantu ukuthi bafunde imibhalo futhi bayihumushe ngobuciko, ngokuvamile ngezindlela ezihluke kakhulu kunezihloswe umlobi.  
Ukufunda kabanzi: Lapho ukuphrinta sekwenze imibhalo eminingi yatholakala, imikhuba yangaphambili yokufunda ngokujulile imibhalo kusukela ekuqaleni kuya ekugcineni yaqala ukushintsha, futhi abantu baqala ukufunda izingcaphuno ezikhethiwe, okuvumela ukufundwa okunabile okwengeziwe ngezihloko eziningi.
Ukufunda ngasese: Ukufunda kwakuxhunyaniswa nokwanda kobuntu ngenxa yokuthi, ngaphambi kokunyatheliswa, ukufunda kwakuvame ukuba umcimbi weqembu lapho umuntu oyedwa efundela iqembu. Ngokuphrinta, kokubili ukufunda nokutholakala kwemibhalo kwanda, futhi ukufunda uwedwa kwaba inkambiso.
Ukusungulwa kokunyathelisa kwashintsha nendlela yokusebenza kwamadolobha aseYurophu. Abaphrinta baqhamuke njengeqembu elisha lezingcweti ezazibalulekile kubo ukufunda nokubhala, kuyilapho umsebenzi onzima kakhulu wombhali wehla ngokwemvelo. Ukulungiswa kobufakazi kwavela njengomsebenzi omusha, kuyilapho ukwanda kwenani labathengisi bezincwadi nabasebenzi basemitatsheni yezincwadi ngokwemvelo kulandele ukuqhuma kwezinombolo zezincwadi. 

Umthelela wezemfundo 
Umshini wokunyathelisa kaGutenberg ube nomthelela omkhulu nasemanyuvesi. Amanyuvesi athonywa "olimini lwawo lwezifundo, imitapo yolwazi, ikharikhulamu, [kanye] ne-pedagogy"[81] 

Ulimi lwezifundo 
Ngaphambi kokusungulwa komshini wokunyathelisa, izinto eziningi ezibhaliwe zazingesiLatini. Nokho, ngemva kokusungulwa kokunyathelisa inani lezincwadi ezinyathelisiwe lanwetshwa kanjalo nezilimi zomdabu. IsiLatini asizange sithathelwe indawo ngokuphelele, kodwa sahlala siwulimi lwamazwe ngamazwe kwaze kwaba sekhulwini leshumi nesishiyagalombili.[81] 

Imitapo yolwazi yamanyuvesi 
Ngalesi sikhathi, amanyuvesi aqala ukusungula imitapo yolwazi ehambisana nayo. "I-Cambridge yenza umfundisi ophethe umtapo wezincwadi ngekhulu leshumi nanhlanu kodwa lesi sikhundla saqedwa ngo-1570 futhi ngo-1577 uCambridge wasungula ihhovisi elisha lomtapo wezincwadi wasenyuvesi. Nakuba, iNyuvesi yaseLeuven ayizange ibone isidingo somtapo wezincwadi waseyunivesithi ngokusekelwe embonweni wokuthi uprofesa wayengumtapo wezincwadi.
