Imitapo yolwazi nayo yaqala ukuthola izincwadi eziningi kangaka ezivela izipho, nokukhishwa kwe-18 kwaqala ukuxazululwa. indoda egama layo linguMerton eyanquma ukuthi izincwadi kufanele zigcinwe emashalofini avundlile esikhundleni se-lecterns [81] 

Umshini wokunyathelisa 
washintsha imitapo yolwazi yaseyunivesithi ngezindlela eziningi oSolwazi ekugcineni bakwazi ukuqhathanisa imibono yababhali abahlukene kunokuba baphoqwe ukuba babheke umbhali oyedwa kuphela noma ababili abakhethekile nabo babenyatheliswa emazingeni ahlukene obunzima bencwadi eyodwa 


kuphela i-comic ishicilelwe equkethe ubuciko bamahlaya ngendlela yamaphaneli alandelanayo amele izigcawu ngazinye zivame ukuhambisana nephrozi echazayo kanye nendaba ebhaliwe, ngokuvamile inkhulumomphendvulwano equkethwe ngamabhaluni egama, afanekisela uhlobo lobuciko bamahlaya kwakuyikhomikhi 

yaseBrithani eyanyatheliswa kusukela ngo-1890 kuya ku-1953 . (1884), ephawuleka ngokusebenzisa kwayo opopayi abalandelanayo ukuze iveze ukulandisa. Lawa makhomikhi aseBrithani ayekhona eduze kwe-lurid "i-penny dreadfuls" ethandwayo (njenge-Spring-heeled Jack), "amaphepha endaba" yabafana kanye nomagazini ohlekisayo we-Punch, obengowokuqala ukusebenzisa igama elithi "ikhathuni" ngomqondo walo wesimanje ohlekisayo.

Incwadi yamahlaya yokuqala yesimanje yaseMelika, ethi, Famous Funnies: A Carnival of Comics, yakhululwa e-US ngo-1933 futhi yayiwukunyatheliswa kabusha kwamapheshana ahlekisayo ephephandaba angaphambili, eyayisungule amathuluzi amaningi okuxoxa izindaba asetshenziswa kumahlaya.[1] Igama elithi incwadi yamahlaya lisuselwa ezincwadini zamahlaya zaseMelika yake yaba inhlanganisela yezinhlamvu zamahlaya zethoni ehlekisayo; nokho, lo mkhuba wathathelwa indawo ngokubonisa izindaba zazo zonke izinhlobo, ngokuvamile ezingezona ezihlekisayo ngephimbo. 

Imakethe enkulu yezincwadi zamahlaya yiJapan. Ngo-1995, imakethe yama-manga e-Japan yayilinganiselwa ku-¥586.4 billion ($6–7 billion),[2] ngokuthengiswa konyaka kwezincwadi zama-manga eziyizigidi eziyizinkulungwane eziyi-1.9 (imiqulu ye-tankōbon nomagazini be-manga) e-Japan, okulingana nezindaba eziyi-15 umuntu ngamunye.[3] Ngo-2020, imakethe yama-manga e-Japan yafinyelela inani elirekhodiwe elisha lamabhiliyoni angu-¥612.5 ngenxa yokukhula ngokushesha kokuthengiswa kwe-digital manga kanye nokwenyuka kwezindali zokuphrinta.[4][5] Imakethe yezincwadi zamahlaya e-United States naseCanada yalinganiselwa ku-$1.09 billion ngo-2016.[6] Kusukela ngo-2017, umshicileli omkhulu wencwadi yamahlaya e-United States umsabalalisi wama-manga i-Viz Media, elandelwa yi-DC Comics kanye ne-Marvel Comics equkethe ama-franchise amahlaya afana no-Superman, u-Batman, i-Wonder Woman, i-Spider-Man, i-Incredible Hulk, ne-X-Men.[7] Izigaba zamabhuku amahlaya athengiswa kakhulu e-US kusukela ngo-2019 izinganekwane zezingane eziku-41%, ama-manga angu-28% kanye namahlaya angu-superhero ku-10% emakethe.[8] Enye imakethe enkulu yezincwadi zamahlaya yiFrance, lapho amahlaya aseFranco-Belgian kanye ne-Japanese manga ngayinye imele u-40% wemakethe, ilandelwa amahlaya aseMelika ngesabelo semakethe esingu-10%. [9] 

Isakhiwo 
I-athikili eyinhloko: Amahlaya § Amagama 
Izincwadi zamahlaya zaseMelika 
Isihloko esikhulu: Incwadi yamahlaya yaseMelika
 
Ikhasi 76 lenoveli eyingcaca ethathelwe ka-Tristram Shandy, edwetshwe umdwebi wamakhathuni waseBrithani uMartin Rowson.
Izincwadi zamahlaya zithembele kakhulu enhlanganweni yazo kanye nesethulo esibukwayo. Ababhali banikezela ukunaka okubalulekile ezicini ezifana nesakhiwo sekhasi, usayizi, umumo, nokuma kwamaphaneli. Lezi zici zibalulekile ekudluliseni ngempumelelo okuqukethwe nemilayezo ngaphakathi kwencwadi yamahlaya. Izingxenye ezibalulekile zezincwadi zamahlaya zihlanganisa amaphaneli, amabhamuza enkulumo (owaziwa nangokuthi amabhaluni), imigqa yombhalo, nezinhlamvu. Amabhaluni enkulumo ngokuvamile athatha uhlobo lweziqukathi zeconvex ezibamba ingxoxo yomlingiswa futhi zixhunywe kumlingisi ngesici somsila. Umsila uhlanganisa umsuka, indlela, ithiphu, nendawo eqondisayo. Ukwakhiwa kwezincwadi zamahlaya kuhilela izinyathelo ezimbalwa ezibalulekile: ukubhala, ukudweba, nokufaka imibala. Kusetshenziswa amathuluzi nezindlela zobuchwepheshe ezihlukene ukwenza izincwadi zamahlaya, ezihlanganisa imiqondo efana nezikhombisi-ndlela, izimbazo, idatha, namamethrikhi. Ngokulandela lezi ziqondiso zokufometha, inqubo iqhubeka ngokubhala, ukudweba, kanye nemibala.[10] E-United States, igama elithi "incwadi yamahlaya", ngokuvamile lisetshenziselwa izincwadi zamahlaya namaphepha okuhweba kuyilapho "inoveli eyingcaca" kuyigama elisetshenziselwa izincwadi ezizimele.[11][12]

Amahlaya njengendlela yokuphrinta abe khona e-United States kusukela kwanyatheliswa i-Adventures kaMnu. Obadiah Oldbuck ngo-1842 enoqwembe oluqinile, [13] okuyenza ibe yincwadi yamahlaya yokuqala eyaziwayo yaseMelika. Ama-Proto-comics periodicals aqala ukuvela ngasekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20, kanti i-comic yokuqala enosayizi ojwayelekile yamahlaya ithi i-Funnies on Parade. I-Funnies on Parades yayiyincwadi yokuqala eyasungula ubukhulu, ubude besikhathi, kanye nefomethi yencwadi yamahlaya yesimanje. Okulandela lokhu kwaba, i-Dell Publishing's Famous Funnies: A Carnival of Comics enamakhasi angama-36 njengencwadi yamahlaya yaseMelika yokuqala yeqiniso; UGoulart, isibonelo, ukubiza ngokuthi "itshe legumbi legatsha elinenzuzo kakhulu lokushicilela omagazini".[14] Ngo-1905 i-GW Dillingham Company yanyathelisa iziqephu ezikhethiwe ezingu-24 zomdwebi wamakhathuni u-Gustave Verbeek encwadini ye-anthology ebizwa ngokuthi 'The Incredible Upside-Downs of Little Lady Lovekins and Old Man Muffaroo'.[15] Ukwethulwa kukaJerry Siegel kanye noJoe Shuster's Superman ngo-1938 kwaguqula izincwadi zamahlaya zaba imboni enkulu[16] futhi kwangenisa iGolden Age of Comic Books. I-Golden Age yasungula i-archetype ye-superhero. Ngokwesazi-mlando uMichael A. Amundson, abalingiswa bencwadi yamahlaya abakhangayo basiza ekudambiseni ukwesaba kwabafundi abasebasha impi yenuzi futhi banciphisa ukukhathazeka ngemibuzo ebuzwa amandla e-athomu.[17]

Osomlando ngokuvamile bahlukanisa umugqa wesikhathi wencwadi yamahlaya yaseMelika ibe yizinkathi. I-Golden Age of Comic Books yaqala ngo-1938, lapho kuqalwa khona i-Superman in Action Comics #1, eyanyatheliswa ngabakwaDetective Comics (umanduleli we-DC Comics), ngokuvamile ebhekwa njengesiqalo sencwadi yamahlaya yesimanje njengoba yaziwa namuhla.[18] I-Silver Age of Comic Books ngokuvamile ibhekwa njengeyamanje kusukela ekuvuselelweni kokuqala okuyimpumelelo kwefomu leqhawe elase lithule ngaleso sikhathi, ngokuqala kwe-Flash ku-Showcase #4 (Oct. 1956).[19][20] I-Silver Age yadonsa ngasekupheleni kwawo-1960 noma ekuqaleni kwawo-1970, ngaleso sikhathi i-Marvel Comics yashintsha okuphakathi ngamaqhawe emvelo afana no-Stan Lee kanye ne-Fantastic Four kaJack Kirby kanye no-Lee kanye ne-Spider-Man kaSteve Ditko. Ukuhlukaniswa phakathi kweSilver Age kanye nenkathi elandelayo, i-Bronze Age of Comic Books, akucaciswanga kahle, neNkathi Yebhulonzi eqala ekuqaleni kwawo-1970 kuya maphakathi nawo-1980.[21] I-Modern Age of Comic Books iqala maphakathi nawo-1980 kuze kube namuhla.[22] 

Isenzakalo esibalulekile emugqeni wesikhathi wezincwadi zamahlaya zaseMelika senzeka lapho udokotela wengqondo uFredric Wertham ezwakalisa ukugxeka kwakhe le ndaba ngencwadi yakhe ethi Seduction of the Innocent (1954). Lokhu kugxeka kuholele ekubandakanyekeni kweKomidi Elincane LeSigele SaseMelika mayelana Nokuhlukunyezwa Kwezingane, elaqala uphenyo ezincwadini zamahlaya. U-Wertham wagomela ngokuthi izincwadi zamahlaya zinesibopho sokwanda kobuhlongandlebe bentsha futhi zibe nomthelela ongaba nomthelela ebuhlotsheni bobulili bengane nezindinganiso zokuziphatha.[23] Isabela ekunakeni kukahulumeni nakwabezindaba, imboni yezincwadi zamahlaya yase-US yasungula i-Comics Magazine Association of America.[24] I-CMAA yafaka i-Comics Code Authority ngo-1954 futhi yabhala i-self-censorship Comics Code ngalowo nyaka, eyayidinga ukuthi zonke izincwadi zamahlaya zidlule inqubo yokugunyazwa. Kwaze kwaba ngawo-1970 lapho izincwadi zamahlaya zingashicilelwa ngaphandle kokuhlolwa kwe-CMAA.[25] Ikhodi yenziwe yashabalala ngokusemthethweni ngoNovemba 2011. 

Izincwadi zamahlaya ezingaphansi komhlaba 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: I- Underground comix 
Ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yawo-1960 nasekuqaleni kwawo-1970, kwavela umfutho wokusungula kulokho okwaziwa ngokuthi i- underground comix. Eshicilelwa futhi asatshalaliswa ngokuzimela embonini yamahlaya esunguliwe, iningi lalawo mahlaya abonisa indlela intsha ephikisana ngayo nesiko lezidakamizwa yangaleso sikhathi. Ingxubevange engaphansi komhlaba "ibonise futhi yaphawula ngokuhlukana komphakathi kanye nokungezwani komphakathi waseMelika". [26] Abaningi babenesitayela esingavinjiwe, esivame ukungahloniphi; imifanekiso yabo engagwegwesi yobunqunu, ubulili, inhlamba, nepolitiki yayingenakho ukufana ngaphandle kwezandulela zabo, “amabhayibheli eTijuana” ezithombe zobulili ezingcolile futhi angaqondakali nakakhulu. Amahlaya angaphansi komhlaba cishe awazange athengiswe ezindaweni zokudayisa, kodwa kunalokho ezitolo ezigxile entsheni njengezitolo ezinkulu nezitolo zamarekhodi, kanye nangeposi. Amahlaya angaphansi komhlaba akhuthaze abadali ukuthi bashicilele umsebenzi wabo ngokuzimela ukuze babe namalungelo aphelele obunikazi kubalingiswa babo.[26] 

Incwadi kaFrank Stack ethi The Adventures of Jesus, eshicilelwe ngaphansi kwegama elithi Foolbert Sturgeon, [27] [28] ibizwa ngokuthi i-comix yokuqala engaphansi komhlaba; [27] [28] kuyilapho u-R. Crumb kanye neqembu labadwebi bamakhathuni ababesebenza ku-Zap Comix benza leli fomu laduma. 

Amanye amakhomikhi 
Isihloko esikhulu: Amanye amahlaya
Ukukhula kwezitolo ezikhethekile zezincwadi zamahlaya ngasekupheleni kwawo-1970 kwadala futhi kwafana nemakethe ezinikele "yamahlaya azimele" noma "amanye amahlaya" e-US. Amahlaya okuqala anjalo ahlanganisa uchungechunge lwe-anthology i-Star Reach, eyanyatheliswa umbhali wencwadi yamahlaya uMike Friedrich kusukela ngo-1974 kuya ku-1979, kanye ne-American Splendor kaHarvey Pekar, eyaqhubeka nokushicilelwa okungavamile ekhulwini lama-21 futhi uShari Springer Berman noRobert Pulcini baguqulela ifilimu yango-2003. Amanye amahlaya azimele aqhubeka nesiko lamahlaya angaphansi komhlaba. Nakuba okuqukethwe kwabo ngokuvamile kuhlale kungacacile kangako, okunye kufana nokuphumayo kwabashicileli abavamile ngefomethi nohlobo kodwa kwashicilelwa izinkampani ezincane eziphethwe amaciko noma abaculi abangabodwa. Imbalwa (ikakhulukazi i-RAW) imele imizamo yokuhlola yokusondeza amahlaya esimeni sobuciko obuhle. 

Ngawo-1970 isiko "lokunyathelisa elincane" lakhula futhi lahlukahluka. Ngawo-1980, abashicileli abaningana abazimele - njenge-Pacific, Eclipse, First, Comico, kanye ne-Fantagraphics - base beqalile ukukhipha izinhlobonhlobo zezitayela namafomethi-kusuka ku-color-superhero, umphenyi, kanye nezincwadi zamahlaya eziqanjiwe zesayensi kuya ezindabeni zefomethi yomagazini omnyama nomhlophe wamaqiniso omlingo waseLatin America. 

Idlanzana labashicileli abancane ngeminyaka yawo-1990, lashintsha ifomethi nokusatshalaliswa kwamahlaya abo ukuze afane kakhulu nokushicilela okungewona wamahlaya. Ifomu elithi "minicomics", inguqulo engakahleleki kakhulu yokuzishicilela, yavela ngeminyaka yawo-1980 futhi yaduma kakhulu phakathi kwamaciko ngawo-1990s, [29] naphezu kokufinyelela izethameli ezilinganiselwe kunomshini wokunyathelisa omncane. 

Abashicileli abancane abavame ukukhulula izihloko bahlanganisa i-Avatar Press, Hyperwerks, Raytoons, kanye ne-Terminal Press, ekhuthazwa intuthuko enjalo kubuchwepheshe bokuphrinta njengokufunwa kwedijithali. 

Amanoveli ezithombe 

ICenters for Disease Control and Prevention yashicilela le noveli eyingcaca yokufundisa ngo-2018 ukufundisa intsha ukuyeka ukusabalalisa izifo ezithathelwanayo. 
Isihloko esikhulu: inoveli yezithombe 
Ngo-1964, u-Richard Kyle waqamba igama elithi "inoveli eyingcaca".[30] 

Izanduleli zefomu zazikhona ngeminyaka yawo-1920s, okubone ukuvuselelwa kwesiko lenkathi ephakathi yokugunda ngokhuni ngu-Belgian Frans Masereel,[31] American Lynd Ward nabanye, kuhlanganise no-Stan Lee. 

Ngo-1947, i-Fawcett Publications yashicilela "Inoveli Yamahlaya No. 1", njengeyokuqala ochungechungeni oluhlosiwe lwalawa "manoveli amahlaya". Indaba ekushicilelo lokuqala ibithi "Anarcho, Dictator of Death", indaba yenhloli yezahluko ezinhlanu eyabhalwa u-Otto Binder futhi yadwetshwa u-Al Carreno. Iyafundeka ku-inthanethi ku-Digital Comic Museum.[32] Lo magazini awuzange ufinyelele ngisho nakumagazini wesibili.
 
Ngo-1950, i-St. John Publications yakhiqiza "inoveli yesithombe" elingana nenhlabamkhosi, ethambekele kubantu abadala ethi, I-Rhymes with Lust, inhlabamkhosi enamakhasi ayi-128 yombhali ongaziwa u-"Drake Waller" (u-Arnold Drake no-Leslie Waller), umbhali wepensela u-Matt Baker kanye no-inker uRay Osrinanthleng "enovelini yokuqala" ebhalwe encwadini yakhe yokuqala. I-"It Rhymes with Lust" iyatholakala futhi ukuthi uyifunde ku-inthanethi ku-Digital Comic Museum.[33] 

Ngo-1971, umbhali ongumdwebi u-Gil Kane nabahlanganyeli basebenzise ifomethi ye-paperback "kunoveli yabo yamahlaya" i-Blackmark. U-Will Eisner wakhulisa igama elithi "inoveli eyingcaca" lapho elisebenzisa esembozweni sohlelo olusephepheni lomsebenzi wakhe othi A Inkontileka NoNkulunkulu, kanye Nezinye Izindaba ZeTenement ngo-1978 futhi, kamuva, ukusetshenziswa kwaleli gama kwaqala ukwanda. 

Amahlaya edijithali Bheka futhi: 
Usayizi Wemakethe 
yamahlaya edijithali 
Ngo-2017, usayizi wemakethe yezincwadi zamahlaya eNyakatho Melika wawungaphezudlwana nje kuka-$1 bhiliyoni ngokuthengiswa kwedijithali okuyisicaba, izitolo zezincwadi zibe nokwehla ngo-1%, kanye nezitolo zezincwadi zamahlaya zibe nokwehla ngo-10% ngo-2016.[34] Imakethe yezincwadi zamahlaya emhlabeni wonke ikhule ngo-12% ngo-2020, yafinyelela inani eliphelele lama-US $ 8.49 billion. Lo mkhondo omuhle uqhubekile ngo-2021, inani lemakethe laminyaka yonke lenyuka laya ku-US$9.21 billion. Ukuthandwa okukhulayo kwezincwadi zamahlaya kungase kubangelwe ekuthakaselelweni okuphezulu komhlaba wonke, okuqhutshwa kakhulu imizamo yokuhlanganyela phakathi kwemikhiqizo ehlukahlukene. Lokhu kubambisana kuhloselwe ukukhiqiza okuqukethwe kwamahlaya okuhehayo nokukhangayo, okunomthelela ekukhuleni okuqhubekayo kwemboni.[35] 
Ukuqoqwa kwezincwadi zamahlaya 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Ukuqoqwa kwencwadi yamahlaya 
Eminyakeni yawo-1970 yabona ukuvela kwezitolo ezikhethekile zezincwadi zamahlaya. Ekuqaleni, izincwadi zamahlaya zazimakethwa abashicileli ezinganeni ngoba izincwadi zamahlaya zazithathwa njengokuzijabulisa kwezingane. Nokho, ngokwandayo ukuqashelwa kwamahlaya njengendlela yobuciko kanye nokukhula kwesiko le-pop lemihlangano yezincwadi zamahlaya, manje semukelwe abantu abadala abaningi.[24]


Abaqoqi bamabhuku amahlaya bavame ukukhombisa uthando lwempilo yonke lwezindaba ezingaphakathi kwamahlaya, imvamisa egxile kumaqhawe athile futhi belwela ukuqoqa iqoqo eliphelele lochungechunge oluthile. Amahlaya anikezwa izinombolo ezilandelanayo, futhi ukukhishwa kokuqala kochungechunge lwencwadi yamahlaya oluhlala isikhathi eside kuvame ukuba yindlala kakhulu futhi efiswa kakhulu phakathi kwabaqoqi. Ukwethulwa kohlamvu olusha kungase kwenzeke phakathi kwesihloko esikhona. Isibonelo, ukubonakala kokuqala kwe-Spider-Man kwenzeka ku-Amazing Fantasy #15. Abalingiswa abasha babevame ukwethulwa ngale ndlela, belinda izethameli eziqavile ngaphambi kokuba bethule izihloko zabo. Ngakho-ke, amahlaya abonisa ukubonakala kokuqala komlingiswa obalulekile kwesinye isikhathi angaba inselele nakakhulu ukuyithola kunodaba lokuqala lochungechunge oluzimele lwalowo mlingiswa. 

Ezinye zezincwadi zamahlaya ezingavamile zihlanganisa amakhophi e-Motion Picture Funnies Weekly #1 engakhishiwe kusukela ngo-1939. Amakhophi ayisishiyagalombili, kanye nelilodwa elingenayo ikhava, avela endaweni yomshicileli oshonile ngo-1974. "Ikhophi Yokukhokha" yale ncwadi ithengiswe ngo-$43,125 endalini yefa lika-2005.[36] 

Amahlaya ayigugu kakhulu aseMelika ahlanganise ukutholakala nekhwalithi nokuvela kokuqala kwabalingisi abadumile nabahlala njalo. Amabhuku amahlaya amane athengiswe ngaphezulu kwesigidi esingu-US$1 kusukela ngo-December 2010, okuhlanganisa izibonelo ezimbili ze-Action Comics #1, ukubonakala kokuqala kuka-Superman, [37][38] womabili athengiswa ngasese ngomthengisi we-inthanethi i-ComicConnect.com ngo-2010, kanye ne-Detective Comics #27, ukubonakala kokuqala kuka-Batman, endalini yomphakathi. 

Ukubuyekeza inani elingenhla elitholwe i-Action Comics #1, ukubonakala kokuqala kuka-Superman, ukuthengiswa okuphezulu kakhulu okurekhodiwe kwaleli bhuku kungu-$3.2 wezigidi, ngekhophi engu-9.0.[39] 

Ama-Misprints, ukuphrinta komthengisi wamahlaya okukhangisa, kanye nezinkinga ezinokusabalalisa okuphansi kakhulu kuvame ukuba nenani lokushoda emakethe yamabhuku amahlaya. Izincwadi zamahlaya zesimanje eziyivelakancane zifaka phakathi uchungechunge lwangempela lwabezindaba lwe-The League of Extraordinary Gentlemen #5, isikhulu se-DC u-Paul Levitz asikhumbula futhi wasishaya indiva ngenxa yokuvela kwesikhangiso senkathi yama-Victori ye-"Marvel Douche", umshicileli ayithatha njengecasulayo;[40] amakhophi ayi-100 kuphela akhona, amaningi awo afakwe esigabeni se-CGC. (Bheka amahlaya Akhunjuziwe ukuze uthole amahlaya amaningi, akhunjulwayo, nayiphutha.)

Ngo-2000, inkampani ebizwa ngokuthi i-Comics Guaranty (CGC) yaqala umkhuba "wokushaya" amahlaya, okubandakanya ukuwafaka ngaphakathi kwamakesi epulasitiki aqinile futhi iwanikeze ibanga lezinombolo. Le ndlela igqugquzele ukuvela Kwesevisi Yesitifiketi Sencwadi Yamahlaya. Uma kubhekwa ukubaluleka kwesimo ekunqumeni ukubaluleka kwamahlaya angavamile, umqondo wokuhlelwa kwenkampani engachemi, engazibandakanyi nokuthenga noma ukuthengisa amahlaya, ubonakale uthembisa. Noma kunjalo, kunenkulumompikiswano eqhubekayo mayelana nokuthi izindleko eziphakeme uma kuqhathaniswa zale sevisi yokugreda ziyafaneleka yini nokuthi ingabe zifeza izithakazelo zabaqoqi noma ikakhulukazi abaqageli abafuna inzuzo esheshayo, okufana nokuhweba ngezitoko noma ubuciko obuhle. Ukuhlelwa kwamahlaya kubambe iqhaza ekusunguleni izindinganiso zokulinganisa, ezisetshenziswa imihlahlandlela yamanani e-inthanethi njenge-GoCollect kanye ne-GPAnalysis ukuze inikeze ulwazi lwesikhathi sangempela senani lemakethe. 
 
Abaqoqi baphinde bafune amakhasi oqobo obuciko ezincwadini zamahlaya, okungenzeka ukuthi yizinto ezingavamile kakhulu endaweni yokuqoqwa kwamabhuku amahlaya. Lawa makhasi anokuntuleka okungenakuqhathaniswa ngenxa yokuthi kunekhasi elilodwa kuphela eliyingqayizivele lomsebenzi wobuciko kuwo wonke amakhasi aphrintiwe futhi ashicilelwa.

Ukwakhiwa kwalawa makhasi omsebenzi wobuciko wangempela kuhilela umzamo wokubambisana: umbhali udweba indaba, umdwebi wepensela uklama amaphaneli alandelanayo ekhasini, ingcweti ye-inki idlula ipeni noyinki, umbhali unikeza inkhulumomphendvulwano nokulandisa ngokubhala ngesandla, futhi ekugcineni, umdwebi wombala wengeze umbala njengokuthinta kokugcina ngaphambi kokuba amakhasi athunyelwe kuphrinta. 

Uma iphrinta ibuyisela amakhasi oqobo omsebenzi wobuciko, ngokuvamile abuyiselwa kumaciko ngokwawo. Laba baculi kwesinye isikhathi bakhetha ukuthengisa lawa makhasi emihlanganweni yezincwadi zamahlaya, kumagalari, nasemibukisweni yobuciko egxile kubuciko bencwadi yamahlaya. Amakhasi oqobo avela ku-DC kanye ne-Marvel, abonisa ukuvela kokuqala kwezinhlamvu zesithonjana ezifana noSuperman, u-Batman, i-Wonder Woman, i-Flash, uCaptain Marvel, u-Spider-Man, i-Incredible Hulk, i-Iron Man, i-Captain America kanye ne-Mighty Thor athathwa njengamagugu ayigugu emhlabeni wencwadi yamahlaya. 

Umlando wohlanga ezincwadini zamahlaya zaseMelika 

Lesi sigaba singadinga ukuhlanzwa ukuze kuhlangatshezwane namazinga ekhwalithi ye-Wikipedia. Inkinga ethile ithi: bhala kabusha ukuze wenze kunciphe ukuncika kumakhwothi, uvumelane kangcono nesitayela se-WP. Sicela usize ukuthuthukisa lesi sigaba uma ukwazi. (Julayi 2019) (Funda ukuthi ungawususa kanjani futhi nini lo mlayezo)
Ukuphindwaphindwa okuningi kwasekuqaleni kwezinhlamvu ezimnyama kumahlaya "kube ukuhlukahluka 'esithombeni esisodwa esivamile se-Sambo'."[41] I-Sambo yayihlobene eduze ne-coon stereotype kodwa inomehluko othile ocashile. Zombili ziyindlela edelelayo yokuveza abalingiswa abamnyama. "Igama ngokwalo, isifinyezo se-raccoon, lilulaza ubuntu. NjengoSambo, i-coon yavezwa njengevila, ethukile kalula, engenzi lutho, engaqondakali, i-buffoon."[42] Lesi sithombe "impela bekungomunye umzamo wokuqinisa ukwehla kobuhlakani bohlanga olumnyama ngokusebenzisa isiko elidumile."[4194] Nokho, kwakukhona ushintsho kumfanekiso omnyama. abalingiswa. "Ukubuka nje kancane...kungase kunikeze umbono wokuthi izimo zase zithuthukile kubantu base-Afrika baseMelika kumahlaya."[41] Emakhomikhi amaningi akhiqizwa ngalesi sikhathi kwakukhona ukucindezela okukhulu kokubekezelelana phakathi kwezinhlanga. "Lawa maqhawe acabanga ngokulingana aqala ukwenza okuthile njengoba nje abantu base-Afrika baseMelika babecelwa ukuba babambe iqhaza emzamweni wempi." [41]
 
Phakathi nalesi sikhathi, uhlelo oluqhutshwa uhulumeni, Ibhodi Lempi Yababhali, lahileleka kakhulu kulokho okwakuzoshicilelwa kumahlaya. "Ibhodi Lempi Yababhali lasebenzisa izincwadi zamahlaya ukuze lilolonge imibono edumile yobuhlanga nobuzwe..."[43] Babengagcini nje ngokusebenzisa izincwadi zamahlaya njengendlela yokuqasha bonke abantu baseMelika, futhi babezisebenzisa njengenkulumo-ze "[ukwakha] isizathu senzondo esekelwe ngokobuhlanga yezitha zamazwe angaphandle zaseMelika."[43] Ibhodi Lempi Yababhali lakha izincwadi zamahlaya "[3] ezichaza ubuhlanga"[3] Kodwa-ke, "lokhu kulandisa okuvumelana nokubekezelelana kuzabalaza ukunqoba izintambo ezingezinhle ezidumile neziqondwa kabanzi ezisetshenziswe amashumi eminyaka esikweni labantu abaningi baseMelika...".[43] Nokho, babengayifezi le ajenda kuwo wonke amahlaya abo.

Ochungechungeni lwamahlaya uCaptain Marvel Adventures, bekunomlingisi ogama lakhe linguSteamboat ohlanganisa iqoqo lemibono engemihle edlangile ngaleso sikhathi. Ibhodi Lempi Yababhali alizange licele noma yiziphi izinguquko kulo mlingisi ngaphandle kokuvezwa okuyinkinga. Ukususwa kwe-Steamboat ochungechungeni lwenzeka kuphela ngenxa yokuphikelela kweqembu lentsha emnyama elizinze eDolobheni laseNew York.[43] Isicelo sabo ekuqaleni sanqatshwa abantu abasebenza ehlaya bethi, "UCaptain Marvel Adventures uhlanganise izinhlobo eziningi zama-caricature 'ngenxa yokuhlekisa'."[43] Iqembu lentsha emnyama liphendule ngokuthi "lokhu, kodwa akusona isigidi somfundi wakho ozocabanga ukuthi u-Negro." ngakho."[43] Ngemva kwalokho, uSteamboat wanyamalala kumahlaya ndawonye. Kube khona ikhomikhi edaliwe mayelana ne-99th Squadron, eyaziwa nangokuthi i-Tuskegee Airmen, ibutho lezempi elimnyama. Esikhundleni sokwenza umdlalo ohlekisayo ngendaba yabo, umdlalo wamahlaya wawukhuluma ngo-Hop Harrigan. Umshayeli wendiza omhlophe othwebula amaNazi, wambonisa amavidiyo akhe eqembu lamaNazi embula amadoda akhe eqembu le-99 ngaleso sikhathi. ehlulwe abantu base-Afrika baseMelika okwamcasula njengoba ebabona njengohlanga olungcono kakhulu futhi akakholwa ukuthi babenze kahle kakhulu abantu bakhe." I-Tuskegee Airmen, kanye nezithombe zabashayeli bezindiza abamnyama zivela kumaphaneli amathathu nje kwamashumi amahlanu nantathu... enze amaqembu amnyama alwela ukulingana ayelwela ukulingana e-US "Spider-Man 'wakwenza kwacaca ukuthi amandla amnyama aphikisayo ayengelona ikhambi lokungabi nabulungisa kwezinhlanga'."[41] "I-Falcon yakugxeka obala ukuziphatha kwabantu abamnyama ithi' mhlawumbe kubalulekile kithi ukuthi sehlise izinto phansi-ukuze sikwazi ukuvikela amalungelo esinawo ukuze sibe umlingisi omnyama"[41] ngokwengxenye kusolwa iqiniso lokuthi, ngalesi sikhathi, "kwakuqabukela ukuba kube khona iciko noma umbhali omnyama ovunyelwe enkampanini enkulu yamahlaya."[41]

Abalingiswa base-Asia ezincwadini zamahlaya bahlangabezane nokucwaswa okufanayo njengoba kwenza abalingisi abamnyama. Babekhonjiswe emifanekisweni eyehlisa isithunzi, nezindaba ezixoxwayo ezivame ukubaveza “njengabangakwazi futhi abangaphansi komuntu.”[43] Ohlelweni lwango-1944 lwencwadi ethi United States Marines, kwakukhona indaba enesihloko esithi The Smell of the Monkeymen. Lokhu kulandisa kufanekisela amasosha aseJapane njengabafana abanonya, futhi kubonisa izikhundla zabo ezicashile zikhashelwa iphunga lemizimba yabo elenyanyekayo.[43] Izinhlamvu zesiShayina zithole impatho efanayo. "Ngesikhathi i-United States ingena ku-WWII, imibono engemihle yamaShayina yayiyingxenye emisiwe yesiko labantu abaningi...."[43] Nokho, ngenxa yokukhathazeka ngokuthi amaJapane angasebenzisa izinto ezimelene namaShayina aseMelika njengenkulumo-ze aqala "ukwethula isithombe esihle kakhulu sabalingani baseMelika baseShayina..."[43] Njengoba nje bezama ukubonisa ukumelela okungcono kwabantu abamnyama kumahlaya benza okufanayo kubantu base-Asia. Nokho, "Izinhlamvu zesi-Japanese nesi-Filipino zazingabonakali kahle. Womabili la maqembu anama-bucktees asabekayo, izingubo ezidabukile, nesikhumba esiphuzi esikhanyayo."[43] "Abashicileli babonise abalingani baseMelika base-Asia ngezithombe ezihlambalazayo nolimi oluhlonishwe emashumini eminyaka adlule."[43] Abalingiswa base-Asia ngaphambili babevezwe njengamademoni angu-41. Phakathi neMpi Yezwe II, "[wonke] amaqhawe amakhulu alingana ne-spandex yakhe azinikele ekuqothulweni kwabahlaseli base-Asia."[41] Kwakukhona "umjaho oqhubekayo wokudluliselana kwabantu lapho isiko elithile lase-Asia lavele lanikeza induku yenzondo kwelinye ngaphandle kwezinguquko ezizwakalayo endleleni abalingiswa ababezovezwa ngayo."[41] 

"I-superpuction ye-endopic eyodwa kuphela eyaxoxwa ngayo engaqondile." kahle. Ngo-1975, uMarvel wasinika uHector Ayala (owaziwa nangokuthi Ingwe Elimhlophe)."[41] "Nakuba alwe iminyaka eminingana ehambisana namaqhawe aziwa kakhulu anjengoSpider-Man noDaredevil, wahlala iminyaka eyisithupha kuphela ngaphambi kokuthengiswa kwamahlaya ahambisana naye kwaba kubi kangangokuthi uMarvel wamenza ukuba ashiye phansi [41] Umlingiswa wakhe odumile 

waseBain Ukumelelwa kwaboMdabu baseMelika ezincwadini zamahlaya "kungafingqwa ngenkolelo-mbono enonya"[41] " indikimba ephindaphindayo...inxuse amaNdiya aseMelika ukuthi alahle inzondo yawo yendabuko ebhekiswe e-United States. Yiwona apendwe njengabangabekezeleli futhi abangahloniphi ukukhathazeka okuvelele kwabamhlophe baseMelika".[41] 

Amahlaya ase-East Asia 
Ama-Japanese manga 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: I-Manga 
Manga (漫画) izincwadi zamahlaya noma amanoveli ayingcaca aphuma e-Japan. Ama-manga amaningi ahambisana nesitayela esakhiwe e-Japan ngasekupheleni kwekhulu le-19, nakuba uhlobo lobuciko lunomlando omude kubuciko bangaphambili baseJapane. Igama elithi manga lisetshenziswa eJapane ukubhekisela kukho kokubili amahlaya kanye ne-cartooning ngokuvamile. Ngaphandle kweJapan,leli gama ngokuvamile lisetshenziselwa ukubhekisela kumahlaya ashicilelwe ekuqaleni ezweni. 

I-Dōjinshi 
Isihloko esikhulu: Dōjinshi
I-Dōjinshi (同人誌, umagazini wabalandeli), amahlaya enziwe abalandeli baseJapane, asebenza emakethe enkulu kakhulu e-Japan kunemakethe yaseMelika "ye-underground comix"; umbukiso omkhulu we-dōjinshi, i-Comiket, uheha izivakashi ezingu-500,000 kabili ngonyaka.[44] 

I-Korean manhwa 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: I-Manhwa 
Manhwa (만화) izincwadi zamahlaya noma amanoveli ayingcaca aphuma e-Korea. Igama elithi manhwa lisetshenziswa e-Korea ukubhekisela kukho kokubili amahlaya kanye ne-cartooning ngokuvamile. Ngaphandle kweKorea, leli gama ngokuvamile libhekisela kumahlaya ashicilelwe eKorea. I-Manhwa ithonywa kakhulu amahlaya e-Japanese Manga nakuba ihlukile ku-manga ne-manhua enezici zayo ezihlukile. 

Ama-Webtoons 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ama-Webtoon 
Webtoons asedumile eSouth Korea njengendlela entsha yokufunda amahlaya. Sibonga ngokwengxenye emithethweni ehlukene yokucwaninga, umbala nemiphumela ehlukile yokubuka, kanye nokwenza kahle ukuze kufundwe kalula kuma-smartphone namakhompyutha. I-manhwa engeziwe yenze ukushintsha kusuka ku-manhwa yokuphrinta yendabuko kuya kuma-webtoon aku-inthanethi ngenxa yenkokhelo engcono kanye nenkululeko eyengeziwe kune-manhwa yokuphrinta yendabuko. Ifomethi ye-webtoon iphinde yanda nakwamanye amazwe angaphandle kwe-Korea njenge-China, Japan, Southeast Asia, kanye namazwe aseNtshonalanga. Abasabalalisi abakhulu be-webtoon bahlanganisa i-Lezhin, i-Naver, ne-Kakao. 

Chinese manhua 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Manhua 
Vietnamese truyện tranh 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Truyện tranh 
Amahlaya ase-Europe 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Amahlaya ase-Europe 
Amahlaya kaFranco-Belgian 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Bande dessinée 

René Goscinny (1926-1977), umbhali wencwadi yamahlaya yase-Astérix, izincwadi zamahlaya 
zaseBelgium ezivame ukubizwa ngokuthi uchungechunge lwezincwadi zamahlaya zase-France kanye ne-BD (isifinyezo sama-bandes dessinées, okusho ukuthi ngokwezwi nezwi "imicu edwetshiwe")[45] ngesiFulentshi, nemicu ngesi-Dutch noma isi-Flemish. Izincwadi zamahlaya zaseBelgian ekuqaleni ezibhalwe ngesi-Dutch zibonisa ithonya lamahlaya e-Francophone "Franco-Belgian" kodwa anesitayela sawo esihlukile.[ecashunwa] 

Amahlaya aseBrithani 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Amahlaya waseBrithani 

Ikhava eya ku-27 December 1884 edition of Ally Sloper's Half Holiday. U-Ally Sloper uthathwa njengomlingiswa wokuqala ophindelelayo kumahlaya.[46]
Nakuba i-Half Holiday ka-Ally Sloper (1884) yayihloselwe imakethe yabantu abadala, abashicileli basheshe bakhomba abantu abasha, okuholele ekutheni iningi lokushicilelwa kube okwezingane futhi lidale ukuhlangana emqondweni womphakathi wamahlaya njengabantwana. I-Guardian ibiza u-Ally Sloper "njengomunye wabalingisi bopopayi bokuqala abayisithonjana emhlabeni", futhi "owaduma e-Victorian Britain njengo-Dennis the Menace kwakuzoba ikhulunyaka kamuva." [47] Amahlaya waseBrithani ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-20 ngokuvamile avela ezithombeni ezimbi ze-penny zenkathi yama-Victori (okuhambisana no-Dickney Turney, u-Dickney Turney, u-Dickney, u-Dickney, no-Dr. I-vampire).[48] Kwaqala ukushicilelwa ngeminyaka yawo-1830s, ama-penny dreadfuls "ayewukunambitheka kokuqala kweBrithani kwesiko elidumile elikhiqizwe ngobuningi labasha."[49] 


Isithombe sikaMinnie the Minx, umlingiswa wase-The Beano, eDundee, eScotland. Yethulwa ngo-1938, i-The Beano yaziwa ngamahlaya ayo axakile, kuvela uDennis the Menace kukhava. 
Izincwadi ezimbili zamahlaya zaseBrithani ezaziwa kakhulu, i-The Beano nethi The Dandy, zaqala ukushicilelwa ngu-DC Thomson ngeminyaka yawo-1930. Ngo-1950 ukusakazwa kwamasonto onke kokubili kwafinyelela ezigidini ezimbili.[50][51] Echaza ngokuduma okukhulu kwamahlaya e-UK ngalesi sikhathi, u-Anita O'Brien, umnakekeli womqondisi eCartoon Museum yaseLondon, uthi: "Lapho amahlaya afana ne-Beano ne-Dandy asungulwa emuva ngawo-1930 - futhi kuze kube yiminyaka yawo-1950 kanye nama-60s - lawa mahlaya cishe ayewukuphela kwendlela yokuzijabulisa eyayitholakala ku-Dennis." 1950s, lapho ukuthengiswa kwe-The Beano kwanda. [52] Ubonakala kukhava ye-The Beano, lapho i-BBC imbiza ngokuthi "umfana ogangile wasemhlabeni wamahlaya."[52] 

Ngo-1954, amahlaya we-Tiger wethula u-Roy of the Rovers, uchungechunge lwebhola oludumile olulandisa ngempilo ka-Roy Race neqembu alidlalela, i-Melchester Rovers. Inkulumo yabezindaba yesitoko ethi "izinto 'zangempela ze-Roy of the Rovers'" ivame ukusetshenziswa ababhali bebhola, abahlaziyi nabalandeli lapho bechaza ukukhonjiswa kwekhono elikhulu, noma imiphumela emangalisayo engqubuzana nezingqinamba, kubhekiselwa ezindabeni ezimangalisayo ezaziwuphawu lokuhweba lomugqa.[53] Ezinye izincwadi zamahlaya ezifana noKhozi, iValiant, Warrior, Viz kanye no-2000 AD nazo zachuma. Amanye amahlaya, afana neJudge Dredd nezinye izihloko zango-2000 AD, ashicilelwe ngendlela ye-tabloid. Amahlaya angaphansi komhlaba kanye nezihloko "zezindaba ezincane" nazo zivele e-UK, ikakhulukazi i-Oz ne-Escape Magazine.

Okuqukethwe kwe-Action, esinye isihloko esihloselwe izingane futhi saqalwa maphakathi nawo-1970, kwaba isihloko okuxoxwa ngaso e-House of Commons. Nakuba ngezinga elincane kunophenyo olufanayo e-US, ukukhathazeka okunjalo kuholele ekulinganisweni kokuqukethwe okushicilelwe ngaphakathi kwamahlaya waseBrithani. Ukulinganisela okunjalo akuzange kwenziwe kube semthethweni kwaze kwafika ezingeni lokumenyezelwa kwekhodi, futhi akuzange kuhlale isikhathi eside. I-UK iphinde yasungula imakethe enempilo ekuphrinteni kabusha nasekupakishweni kabusha kwezinto ezibonakalayo, ikakhulukazi izinto ezivela e-US. Ukuntuleka kwezinto ezinokwethenjelwa zezincwadi zamahlaya zaseMelika kuholele ekuprintweni kabusha okuhlukahlukene okumnyama nokumhlophe, okuhlanganisa amahlaya e-Marvel's monster of the 1950s, uCaptain Marvel kaFawcett, nabanye abalingiswa abafana noSheena, uMandrake the Magician, kanye noPhantom. Izinkampani eziningi zokuphrinta kabusha zabamba iqhaza ekupakisheni kabusha izinto zaseMelika ezimakethe yaseBrithani, ikakhulukazi umthengisi kanye nomsabalalisi uThorpe & Porter. I-Marvel Comics yasungula ihhovisi lase-UK ngo-1972. I-DC Comics kanye ne-Dark Horse Comics nayo yavula amahhovisi ngawo-1990. Ukupakishwa kabusha kwezinto zaseYurophu akwenzekanga njalo, nakuba uchungechunge lwe-Adventures of Tintin ne-Asterix luhunyushwe ngempumelelo futhi lwapakishwa kabusha ezincwadini ezinoqwembe oluthambile. Inani lamahlaya aseYurophu atholakala e-UK lenyukile kule minyaka engamashumi amabili edlule. Inkampani yaseBrithani iCinebook, eyasungulwa ngo-2005, ikhiphe izinguqulo ezihunyushwe ngesiNgisi zochungechunge oluningi lwase-Europe. 
NgoKhisimusi, abashicileli bapakisha kabusha futhi bathumele izinto zeminyaka yamahlaya, eziphrintiwe futhi ziboshwe njengezincwadi ezinoqwembe oluqinile ezinosayizi ongu-A4; "I-Rupert" inikeza isibonelo esidumile sonyaka wamahlaya waseBrithani.U-DC Thomson uphinde apakishe imicu ethi The Broons kanye ne-Oor Wullie ezincwadini ezinosayizi ongu-A4 ezinoqwembe oluthambile ngesikhathi samaholide.

Ngawo-1980, ukuvela kabusha kwababhali namaciko baseBrithani kwazuza ukuvelela ezincwadini zamahlaya ezivamile, ezazibizwa ngokuthi "Ukuhlasela KwaseBrithani" emlandweni wencwadi yamahlaya.[54] Laba babhali namaciko beza nezindikimba zabo ezivuthiwe kanye nefilosofi efana nesiyaluyalu, izingxabano kanye nepolitiki evamile kwabezindaba baseBrithani. Lezi zici zingavula indlela yezincwadi zamahlaya "ezimnyama nezinhle kakhulu" futhi zigxume ziqale iNkathi Yesimanje Yamahlaya.[55] Ababhali babehlanganisa u-Alan Moore, odume nge-V yakhe ethi Vendetta, From Hell, Watchmen, Marvelman, kanye ne-League of Extraordinary Gentlemen;[56] uNeil Gaiman ngezinganekwane ze-Sandman kanye ne-Books of Magic; Warren Ellis, umdali weTransmetropolitan and Planetary; nabanye abafana no-Mark Millar, umdali we-Wanted ne-Kick-Ass. Uchungechunge lwezincwadi zamahlaya u-John Constantine, i-Hellblazer, olusethwe kakhulu eBrithani futhi oludlala isangoma u-John Constantine, lwavulela indlela ababhali baseBrithani abafana noJamie Delano.[57] 

Umculi waseNgilandi u-Peter Gabriel wakhipha ngo-2000 Indaba Ye-OVO eyakhululwa encwadini yamahlaya emise okwe-CD njengengxenye ye-CD edition enesihloko esithi "OVO The Millennium Show". I-2000 Millennium Dome Show esekelwe kuyo.[58] 


Ngomhla ziyi-19 kuNdasa 2012, isevisi yeposi yaseBrithani, iRoyal Mail, yakhipha isethi yezitembu ezibonisa abalingiswa bencwadi yamahlaya yaseBrithani nochungechunge.[59] Iqoqo liqukethe i-The Beano, i-Dandy, i-Eagle, i-Topper, i-Roy of the Rovers, i-Bunty, i-Buster, i-Valiant, i-Twinkle kanye no-2000 AD.[59] 

Amahlaya aseSpain 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Amahlaya aseSpain 
Kuye kwashiwo ukuthi ikhulu le-13 i-Cantigas de Santa María ingabhekwa njenge-"comic" yokuqala yaseSpanishi, nakuba izincwadi zamahlaya (ezaziwa nangokuthi eSpain ngokuthi historietas noma i-tebeos) zenza ukuqala kwazo cishe ngo-1857. Umagazini i-TBO waba nethonya ekwandiseni indlela. Ngemuva kweMpi Yombango YaseSpain, umbuso kaFranco wabeka uphenyo oluqinile kuyo yonke imidiya: amahlaya amaqhawe ayenqatshelwe futhi ngenxa yalokho, amaqhawe amahlaya asekelwe ezinganekwaneni zomlando (ngo-1944 iqhawe lenkathi ephakathi u-El Guerrero del Antifaz ladalwa nguManuel Gago kanye nelinye iqhawe lenkathi ephakathi elidumile, uCapitán Trueno, wadalwa ngu-Migur Velgo 1956 ngu-Amraío 56 u-Amraíbro). Izindlu ezimbili zokushicilela - I-Bruguera yokuhlela kanye ne-Editor Valenciana - yayibusa imakethe yamahlaya aseSpain ngesikhathi sayo segolide (1950-1970). Amahlaya adume kakhulu abonise isitayela esibonakalayo sokuhlekisa nge-slapstick (ethonywe ababhali base-Franco-Belgian abafana no-Franquin): I-Carpanta ka-Escobar kanye no-Zipi y Zape, ka-Vázquez's Las hermanas Gilda kanye no-Anacleto, i-Ibáñez's Mortadelo y.13 Percebel's Filemón kanye ne-Jan. Ngemva kokuphela kwenkathi yamaFrancoist, kwaba nesithakazelo esikhulu kumahlaya abantu abadala anomagazini abanjengoTotem, El Jueves, 1984, no-El Víbora, kanye nemisebenzi efana neParacuellos kaCarlos Giménez.
 
Abaculi baseSpain ngokwesiko basebenza kwezinye izimakethe bethola impumelelo enkulu, kungaba kwabaseMelika (isb., abawine Indondo ye-Eisner uSergio Aragonés, uSalvador Larroca, uGabriel Hernández Walta, uMarcos Martín noma uDavid Aja), amaNgisi (isb., uCarlos Ezquerra, umdidiyeli we-Judge Dredd-Belgi noma owine i-Francos eyodwa ye-Fardo uJulio Ribera [fr; fy; 

Amahlaya ase-Italian 
Isihloko esiyinhloko: Amahlaya ase-Italy 

u-Hugo Pratt (1927-1995), umbhali wochungechunge lwencwadi yamahlaya yase-Corto Malta 
E-Italy, amahlaya (owaziwa ngesi-Italian ngokuthi fumetti) enze ukuqalwa kwawo njengamahlaya ekupheleni kwekhulu le-19, futhi kamuva aguqukela ezindabeni zokuzijabulisa. Nokho, ngemva kweMpi Yezwe II, abaculi abafana no-Hugo Pratt kanye no-Guido Crepax badalula amahlaya ase-Italy kubabukeli bamazwe ngamazwe. Izincwadi zamahlaya ezidumile ezifana noDiabolik noma umugqa weBonelli—okungukuthi u-Tex Willer noma uDylan Dog—zihlala zithengiswa kakhulu.[60] 

Amahlaya avamile ngokuvamile ashicilelwa nyanga zonke, ngefomethi yosayizi wenhlabamkhosi emnyama nomhlophe, cishe namakhasi ayi-100 kuya kwayi-132. Amaqoqo ezinto zakudala zezinhlamvu ezidume kakhulu, ngokuvamile ezinamakhasi angaphezu kuka-200, nazo zivamile. Amahlaya ombhali ashicilelwa ngefomethi ye-French BD, isibonelo nge-Corto Maltese kaPratt. 

Abadwebi bopopayi base-Italy babonisa ithonya lamahlaya avela kwamanye amazwe, ahlanganisa iFrance, iBelgium, iSpain, ne-Argentina. I-Italy nayo idume ngokuba ngomunye wabakhiqizi abahamba phambili bezindaba zamahlaya ze-Walt Disney ngaphandle kwase-US; I-superhero alter ego ka-Donald Duck, i-Paperinik, eyaziwa ngesiNgisi ngokuthi i-Superduck, yadalwa e-Italy. 

Amahlaya akwamanye amazwe 
Bheka futhi: Uhlu lwamahlaya ngezwe 
Ukusatshalaliswa 
Imboni yezincwadi zamahlaya ithwele kanzima ngezinkinga zokusabalalisa kuwo wonke umlando wayo, njengoba abathengisi abaningi abavamile bebemanqikanqika ukulondoloza amanani amakhulu amahlaya ahehayo nafunwa kakhulu. I-smartphone kanye ne-tablet sekuphenduke indlela ekahle yokusabalalisa ku-inthanethi.[61] 

Ukusatshalaliswa kwedijithali 
Ngomhla ziyi-13 kuNovemba 2007, i-Marvel Comics yethula i-Marvel Digital Comics Unlimited, isevisi yokubhalisa evumela abafundi ukuthi bafunde amahlaya amaningi emlandweni we-Marvel ku-inthanethi. Le sevisi ifaka phakathi amahlaya amasha akhishwa ngezikhathi ezithile angatholakali kwenye indawo. Ngokukhishwa kwe-Aveng Spider-Man #1, uMarvel uphinde waba umshicileli wokuqala ukunikeza amakhophi edijithali mahhala njengengxenye yekhophi ephrintiwe yencwadi yamahlaya.[62]
 
Ngokuthandwa okukhulayo kwama-smartphone namathebulethi, abashicileli abaningi abakhulu sebeqalile ukukhipha izihloko ngendlela yedijithali. Inkundla edume kakhulu yi-comiXology. Ezinye izinkundla, njenge-Graphicly, zivaliwe. 

Amaqoqo amahlaya kulabhulali
Imitapo yolwazi eminingi ineqoqo elibanzi lamahlaya ngendlela yamanoveli ayingcaca. Lokhu kusebenza njengendlela elula yokuthi umphakathi ujwayelane nolimi.[63] 

I-Guinness World Records 
Ngo-2015, umculi we-manga wase-Japan u-Eiichiro Oda waklonyeliswa ngesihloko se-Guinness World Records ngokuba "namakhophi amaningi ashicilelwe ochungechungeni lwencwadi yamahlaya ngumbhali oyedwa". Uchungechunge lwakhe lwe-manga i-One Piece, alubhalayo futhi alubonisayo, lukhishwe uchungechunge kumagazini wesiJapane i-Weekly Shōnen Jump kusukela ngoDisemba 1997, futhi ngo-2015, amavolumu aqoqiwe angama-77 ayesekhishiwe. IGuinness World Records ibike esimemezelweni sayo ukuthi imiqulu eqoqiwe yalolu chungechunge isidayise isamba esingu-320,866,000. I-One Piece iphinde ibe nesihloko se-Guinness World Records "samakhophi amaningi ashicilelwe ochungechungeni lwe-manga olufanayo". [64] 

Ngomhla zi-5 Agasti 2018, isihloko se-Guinness World Records "sencwadi yamahlaya enkulu kunawo wonke ake ashicilelwa" saklonyeliswa ngencwadi yamahlaya yase-Brazil i-Turma da Mônica — O Maior Gibi do Mundo!, eshicilelwe yi-Panini Comics Brasil kanye no-Mauricio de Sousa Produções. Incwadi yamahlaya ikala 69.9 by 99.8 centimeters (2 feet 3.5 amayintshi by 3 feet 3.3 amayintshi). Incwadi yamahlaya enamakhasi ayi-18 inamakhophi ayi-120.[65] 

Ngokushicilelwa kwangoJulayi 2021 kwevolumu yochungechunge lwama-201 eqoqwe lochungechunge lwakhe lwe-manga i-Golgo 13, umculi we-manga wase-Japan u-Takao Saito waklonyeliswa ngesihloko se-Guinness World Records esithi "Amavolumu amaningi ashicilelwe ngochungechunge olulodwa lwe-manga."[66] I-Golgo 13 ishicilelwe ngokuqhubekayo kumagazini waseJapane i-Big Comic8, nayo eyenza ibe yindala manga kusukela ngo-Okthoba 196. 

Iphephandaba ibhuku lezikhathi ezithile eliqukethe ulwazi olubhaliwe mayelana nemicimbi yamanje futhi livamise ukuthayipha ngoyinki omnyama onomlando omhlophe noma ompunga. Amaphephandaba angafaka imikhakha ehlukahlukene njengepolitiki, ibhizinisi, ezemidlalo, ezobuciko nesayensi. Ngokuvamile zihlanganisa izinto ezifana namakholomu emibono, izibikezelo zesimo sezulu, ukubuyekezwa kwezinsizakalo zasendaweni, izingcwabo, izaziso zokuzalwa, amagama aphikisanayo, izindida ze-sudoku, opopayi abahlelayo, imicu yamahlaya, namakholomu ezeluleko.
 
Amaphephandaba amaningi angamabhizinisi, futhi akhokha izindleko zawo ngengxube yemali engenayo yokubhaliselwe, ukuthengiswa kwesitolo sezindaba, nemali engenayo yokukhangisa. Izinhlangano zobuntatheli ezishicilela amaphephandaba zona ngokwazo zivame ukubizwa ngokuthi amaphephandaba. Ngokuvamile amaphephandaba ashicilelwe ngokuphrinta (imvamisa emaphepheni ashibhile, asezingeni eliphansi abizwa nge-newsprint). Kodwa-ke, namuhla amaphephandaba amaningi nawo ashicilelwa kumawebhusayithi njengamaphephandaba aku-inthanethi, futhi amanye aze ashiya izinguqulo zawo zokuphrinta ngokuphelele.

Amaphephandaba athuthukiswa ngekhulu le-17 njengamaphepha okwaziswa abathengisi. Ngasekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19, amadolobha amaningi aseYurophu, kanye naseNyakatho neNingizimu Melika, anyathelisa amaphephandaba. Amanye amaphephandaba anokuzimela okuphezulu kokuhlela, ikhwalithi ephezulu yobuntatheli, kanye nokusakazwa okukhulu abhekwa njengamaphephandaba aqoshiwe. Ngokuduma kwe-inthanethi, amaphephandaba amaningi manje asedijithali, izindaba zawo ezethulwa ku-inthanethi njengendlela eyinhloko esetshenziswa iningi labafundi, kanti ushicilelo lokuphrinta lungolwesibili (kwidlanzana lamakhasimende akhetha ukulikhokhela) noma, kwezinye izimo, liye layeka ukusebenza. Ukwehla kwamaphephandaba ekuqaleni kwekhulu lama-21 ekuqaleni kwahunyushwa kakhulu njengomncintiswano nje wokuphrinta uqhathanisa nedijithali lapho amabhithi edijithali ephrinta khona. Okungokoqobo kuhlukile futhi ku-multivariate, njengoba amaphephandaba manje evame ukuba khona ku-intanethi; noma ubani ozimisele ukubhalisa angazifunda ngedijithali ku-inthanethi. Izinto ezifana nezikhangiso ezihlukanisiwe ezingaseyona isikhungo esikhulu semali engenayo (ngenxa yezinye izindlela zokuthenga nokudayisa ku-inthanethi) kanye nemibono yezikhangiso manje esisakazwa kuyo yonke imidiya eminingi okokufaka. 

Uhlolojikelele 

Ikhasi langaphambili le-New York Times ngoSuku Lwe-Armistice, 
Amaphephandaba ka-1918 ashicilelwa nsuku zonke noma masonto onke. Omagazini bezindaba bakhona bamasonto onke, kodwa banendlela yomagazini. Amaphephandaba anentshisekelo evamile ngokuvamile ashicilela izindatshana zezindaba futhi afake ama-athikili ezindabeni zikazwelonke nezamazwe ngamazwe kanye nezindaba zasendaweni. Lezi zindaba zihlanganisa izehlakalo zezombangazwe nosopolitiki.", ibhizinisi nezezimali, ubugebengu, isimo sezulu, nezinhlekelele zemvelo; ezempilo nemithi, isayensi, amakhompiyutha nobuchwepheshe; ezemidlalo; nezokuzijabulisa, umphakathi, ukudla nokupheka, izingubo zokugqoka nemfashini yasekhaya, nobuciko. 

Ngokuvamile, leli phepha lihlukaniswe laba izigaba zeqembu ngalinye lalawo amakhulu (abhalwe A, B, C, njalonjalo, anezinombolo ezibhalwe ekhasini 1B-20, ikhasi B1B, isiqalo A C1-C20, njalo njalo). Amaphepha amaningi endabuko aphinde abe nekhasi lokuhlela eliqukethe izihloko ezibhalwe umhleli (noma ibhodi lokuhlela lephepha) futhi eveza umbono ngodaba olusesidlangalaleni, izihloko zemibono ezibizwa ngokuthi "op-eds" ezibhalwe ngababhali bezivakashi (okuyinto ngokuvamile eba esigabeni esifanayo nesokuhlela), namakholomu aveza imibono yomuntu siqu yabahleli bamakholomu ngokuvamile anikeza ukwaziswa okubhaliwe ukuze ahumushe amakholomu edatha, ahumushe imininingwane ebhaliwe. umfundi "ukuthi kusho ukuthini" futhi ebanxenxa ukuthi bavumelane namaphepha angenawo ama-athikili abhalwe ngababhali bezisebenzi.
 
Kushicilelwe inhlobonhlobo yezinto emaphephandabeni. Ngaphandle kwezindaba ezishiwo ngenhla, ulwazi nemibono, kuhlanganisa izibikezelo zesimo sezulu kanye nobuciko bethelevishini (kuhlanganise nobuciko befilimu, ukugxeka kwefilimu; imidlalo yaseshashalazini, ezobuciko, nezokwakha) kanye nezinkonzo zasendaweni ezifana nezindawo zokudlela, izaziso zokuzalwa kanye nezimemezelo zokuthweswa iziqu ezifana namagama ahlukene, ama-horoscopes, amakhathuni, amakholomu ezeluleko, ukudla, nezinye izinhlaka zomsakazo kanye nezinhlelo zethelevishini ezikhangiswayo; ka-2013, ukwanda kwamawebhusayithi e-inthanethi okuthengisa izimpahla, njenge-Craigslist ne-eBay kuholele ekuthengisweni kwezikhangiso okufakwe esigabeni esingaphansi kwamaphephandaba.[catation needed]

Amaphephandaba amaningi angamabhizinisi, futhi akhokha izindleko zawo ngenhlanganisela yemali engenayo yokubhalisela, ukuthengiswa kwesitolo sezindaba, kanye nemali engenayo yokukhangisa (amanye amabhizinisi noma abantu ngabanye bayakhokha ukuze babeke izikhangiso emakhasini, okuhlanganisa izikhangiso ezibukwayo, izikhangiso ezihlukanisiwe, kanye nezilinganiso zazo eziku-inthanethi). Amanye amaphephandaba aphethwe uhulumeni noma okungenani axhaswe uhulumeni; ukuthembela kwabo emalini engenayo yokukhangisa kanye nenzuzo akubalulekile kangako ekusindeni kwabo. Ngakho-ke, ukuzimela kokuhlela kwephephandaba kuhlala kuncike ezithakazelweni zothile, kungakhathaliseki ukuthi abanikazi, abakhangisi noma uhulumeni. Amanye amaphephandaba anokuzimela okuphezulu kokuhlela, ikhwalithi ephezulu yobuntatheli, kanye nokusakazwa okukhulu abhekwa njengamaphephandaba aqoshiwe. 
 
Amaphephandaba amaningi, ngaphandle kokuqasha izintatheli ngenkokhelo yazo, aphinde abhalisele izinhlangano zezindaba (izinkonzo zocingo) (njenge-Associated Press, Reuters, noma i-Agence France-Presse), eziqasha izintatheli ukuba zithole, zihlanganise, futhi zibike izindaba, bese zidayisela okuqukethwe emaphephandabeni ahlukahlukene. Lena indlela yokugwema ukuphindaphinda izindleko zokubika ezivela emhlabeni wonke. c. Ngo-2005, bekunezihloko zamaphephandaba zansuku zonke ezingaba ngu-6,580 emhlabeni wonke ezithengisa amakhophi anyathelisiwe ayizigidi ezingu-395 ngosuku (e-US, izihloko ezingu-1,450 ezithengisa amakhophi ayizigidi ezingu-55).[1] Ngasekupheleni kwawo-2000-ekuqaleni kwawo-2010 ukwehla komnotho emhlabeni wonke, kuhlangene nokukhula ngokushesha kwezindlela ezihlukile ezisekelwe kuwebhu, kuye kwasiza ekubangeleni ukwehla kwezokukhangisa nokusatshalaliswa kwezimali, njengoba amaphepha amaningi kwadingeka adilize imisebenzi ukuze aqede ukulahlekelwa.[2] Imali engenayo yonyaka emhlabeni wonke ifinyelele ku-$100 billion ngo-2005-7, yase ingena phakathi nenhlekelele yezimali ka-2008. Imali engenayo ngo-2016 yehle yafinyelela ku-$53 billion kuphela, yalimaza wonke umshicileli omkhulu njengoba imizamo yabo yokuthola imali engenayo nge-inthanethi yehla kakhulu emgomweni.[3]

Ukwehla kwemali engenayo yokukhangisa kuthinte kokubili imidiya yokunyathelisa ne-inthanethi kanye nazo zonke ezinye izindlela; ukukhangisa kokuphrinta kwake kwaba nenzuzo enkulu kodwa kwehle kakhulu, futhi izintengo zokukhangisa ku-inthanethi ngokuvamile ziphansi kunalezo ezandulelayo zokuphrinta. Ngaphandle kokulungisa kabusha ukukhangisa, i-inthanethi (ikakhulukazi iwebhu) iphinde yaphonsela inselelo amamodeli ebhizinisi enkathi yokuphrinta kuphela ngokuqoqa kokubili ukushicilela ngokujwayelekile (ukwabelana ngolwazi nabanye) kanye, ikakhulukazi, ubuntatheli (umsebenzi wokuthola, ukuhlanganisa, nokubika izindaba). Ngaphandle kwalokho, ukukhuphuka kwama-aggregator wezindaba, ahlanganisa izindatshana ezixhunyiwe ezivela emaphephandabeni amaningi aku-inthanethi neminye imithombo, kuthonya ukuhamba kwethrafikhi yewebhu. Ukwenyuka kwe-paywalling kwamaphephandaba aku-inthanethi kungase kuphikisana naleyo miphumela. Iphephandaba elidala elisashicilelwe yi-Ordinari Post Tijdender, eyasungulwa e-Stockholm ngo-1645. 

Izincazelo 
Amaphephandaba ngokuvamile ahlangabezana nemibandela emine:[4][5] 

Ukufinyeleleka komphakathi: Okukuqukethe kufinyeleleka ngokunengqondo emphakathini, ngokwesiko ngephepha elithengiswayo noma lisatshalaliswa ezindaweni zokudayisa, izitolo, kanye nemitapo yolwazi, futhi, kusukela nge-intanethi, yenziwe yatholakala nge-inthanethi eyi-199. Nakuba amaphephandaba e-Internet aye anda ukufinyelela emaphephandabeni ngabantu abane-Internet, abantu abangenayo i-Internet noma i-computer (isb., abantu abangenamakhaya, abantulayo kanye nabantu abahlala ezindaweni ezikude noma zasemaphandleni) bangase bangakwazi ukungena ku-inthanethi, futhi ngenxa yalokho ngeke bakwazi ukufunda izindaba eziku-inthanethi. Ukufunda nokubhala kuyisici esivimbela abantu abangakwazi ukufunda ukuthi bakwazi ukuzuza ngokufunda amaphephandaba (iphepha noma ku-inthanethi). 
I-Periodicity: Zishicilelwa ngezikhathi ezithile, ngokuvamile nsuku zonke noma masonto onke. Lokhu kuqinisekisa ukuthi amaphephandaba angahlinzeka ngolwazi ngezindaba ezisanda kuvela noma izehlakalo. 
Imali: Ulwazi lwayo lungolwakamuva njengoba uhlelo lwayo lokushicilela luvuma. Izinga lokwaziswa kwamuva kwephephandaba eliphrintiwe lilinganiselwe isidingo sesikhathi sokuphrinta nokusabalalisa iphephandaba. Emadolobheni amakhulu, kungase kube nohlelo lwasekuseni kanye noshicilelo lwakamuva lwephepha losuku olufanayo, ukuze uhlelo lwakamuva luhlanganise izindaba ezisematheni ezenzeka kusukela kwanyatheliswa uhlelo lwasekuseni. Amaphephandaba aku-inthanethi angabuyekezwa kaningi njengoba ulwazi olusha lutholakala, ngisho nezikhathi ezimbalwa ngosuku, okusho ukuthi izinhlelo eziku-inthanethi zingaba ngezakamuva kakhulu. 
I-Universality: Amaphephandaba ahlanganisa izihloko eziningi, kusukela ezindabeni zezepolitiki nezamabhizinisi kuya kuzibuyekezo zesayensi nobuchwepheshe, ezobuciko, amasiko, nezokuzijabulisa. AmaGazethi 
Omlando 
kanye namanqampunqampu 
ERoma Lasendulo, kwakhishwa i- Acta Diurna, noma izimemezelo zikahulumeni. Ayeqoshwa ngensimbi noma ngetshe futhi abekwe ezindaweni zomphakathi. EShayina, amakhasi ezindaba akhiqizwa uhulumeni wakuqala, abizwa ngokuthi i-Dibao, ayesakazwa phakathi kwezikhulu zenkantolo phakathi nobukhosi bamaHan ongasekho (ngekhulu lesibili nelesithathu AD). Phakathi kuka-713 no-734, i-Kaiyuan Za Bao ("Bulletin of the Court") yobukhosi base-Chinese Tang yashicilela izindaba zikahulumeni; yayibhalwe ngesandla kusilika futhi ifundwe yizikhulu zikahulumeni. Ngo-1582, kwaba khona inkomba yokuqala emaphephandabeni ashicilelwe ngasese e-Beijing, ngesikhathi sobukhosi bamaMing ongasekho.[6] 

Ekuqaleni kweYurophu yanamuhla, ukwanda kokuxhumana kwemingcele kwadala isidingo esikhulayo solwazi esahlangatshezwa ngamashidi wezindaba abhalwe ngesandla amafushane. Ngo-1556, uhulumeni waseVenice waqala washicilela i-notizie scritte yanyanga zonke, eyabiza igazetta eyodwa, uhlamvu lwemali oluncane.[7] Lawa ma-avvisi kwakuyizincwadi zezindaba ezibhalwe ngesandla futhi ayesetshenziselwa ukudlulisa izindaba zezombusazwe, ezempi, nezomnotho ngokushesha nangempumelelo emadolobheni ase-Italy (1500–1700)—ukwabelana ngezici ezithile zamaphephandaba nakuba ngokuvamile engabhekwa njengamaphephandaba eqiniso.[8] Kodwa-ke, akukho nokukodwa kwalokhu kushicilelwa okuhlangabezana ngokugcwele nemibandela yakudala yamaphephandaba afanelekile, njengoba ngokuvamile bekungahloselwe umphakathi ovamile futhi kukhawulelwe kuhlu oluthile lwezihloko. 

Amaphephandaba 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umlando wokushicilela amaphephandaba 
Bheka futhi: Uhlu lwamaphephandaba okuqala kanye nenqubo yokukhiqizwa kwamaphephandaba 
eYurophu 
Bheka futhi: Umlando Wamaphephandaba aseBrithani 

Ikhasi lesihloko likaJohann Carolus' Relation from 1609, the first newspaper 

Josef Danhauser's portrait Newspaper readers, 1840
Umshini wokuqala wokunyathelisa wezinhlamvu ezinyakazayo owawuvumela ukukhiqizwa ngobuningi bezincwadi ezinyathelisiwe wasungulwa ngu-Johann Gutenberg cishe ngonyaka we-1450. Eminyakeni engu-50 ngemva kokuba uGutenberg eqale ukunyathelisa, kwakulinganiselwa ukuthi izincwadi ezingu-500 000 zazisakazwa, zanyatheliswa emishinini yokunyathelisa engaba ngu-1 000 kulo lonke izwekazi. Ukusungulwa kukaGutenberg kwakuwumshini olula, kodwa kwaqala uguquko oluphawuleka ngokuthuthuka okuphindaphindiwe kwezobuchwepheshe, ngenxa yalokho, kwanda izimiso zenkululeko nenkululeko yokushintshisana ngolwazi.[9] 
 
Ukuvela kwemithombo yezindaba emisha ekhulwini le-17 kufanele kubonakale ngokuseduze nokusabalala komshini wokunyathelisa lapho umshini wokushicilela uthola khona igama lawo.[10] I-German-language Relation aller Fürnemmen und gedenckwürdigen Historien, eyanyatheliswa kusukela ngo-1605 kuya phambili ngu-Johann Carolus eStrasbourg eMbusweni Ongcwele WaseRoma Wesizwe SaseJalimane, ivame ukuqashelwa njengephephandaba lokuqala.[11][12] Iphephandaba lesibili, i-German Avisa, lanyatheliswa kusukela ngo-1609 eWolfenbüttel. Womabili amaphephandaba ayezehlukanisa kwezinye izinto ezinyathelisiwe ngokunyatheliswa njalo. Babike ngezinhlobonhlobo zezenzakalo zamanje ezithamelini ezibanzi zomphakathi. Phakathi namashumi ambalwa eminyaka, amaphephandaba ayengase atholakale kuwo wonke amadolobha amakhulu aseYurophu, kusukela eVenice kuya eLondon.

I-Dutch Courante uyt Italien, Duytslandt, njll. ("Courant from Italy, Germany, etc.") ka-1618 kwaba ngeyokuqala ukuvela ku-folio- kunosayizi we-quarto. I-Amsterdam, isikhungo sezohwebo emhlabeni, ngokushesha yaba ikhaya lamaphephandaba ngezilimi eziningi, ngokuvamile ngaphambi kokuba anyatheliswe emazweni akubo.[13] Iphephandaba lokuqala lesiNgisi, i-Corrant out of Italy, Germany, njll., lanyatheliswa e-Amsterdam ngo-1620. Ngawo lowo nyaka, iphephabhuku lase-Antwerp elithi Nieuwe Tijdinghen[14] lanyatheliswa ngu-Abraham Verhoeven.[15] Ngo-1621, i-Corante, noma izindaba zamasonto onke ezivela e-Italy, eJalimane, eHungary, e-Poland, e-Bohemia, e-France nase-Low Countreys yanyatheliswa eNgilandi yi-"NB" (ngokuvamile okucatshangwa ukuthi uNathaniel Butter noma u-Nicholas Bourne) kanye no-Thomas Archer.[16] Iphephandaba lokuqala eFrance lashicilelwa ngo-1631, i-La Gazette (ekuqaleni eyanyatheliswa njengeGazette de France).[7] Iphephandaba lokuqala e-Italy, ngokuhambisana nomagazini omdala kunawo wonke osalondoloziwe, kwakuyi-Di Genova eyanyatheliswa ngo-1639 eGenoa.[17] Iphephandaba lokuqala ePortugal, A Gazeta da Restauração, lanyatheliswa ngo-1641 eLisbon.[18] Iphephandaba lokuqala leSpanishi, iGaceta de Madrid, lanyatheliswa ngo-1661. 

I-Post-och Inrikes Tidningar (eyasungulwa njenge-Ordinari Post Tijdender) yanyatheliswa okokuqala eSweden ngo-1645, futhi iyiphephandaba elidala kunawo wonke elisekhona, nakuba manje linyatheliswa ku-inthanethi kuphela.[19] I-Opregte Haarlemsche Courant yase-Haarlem, eyashicilelwa okokuqala ngo-1656, iyiphepha elidala kunawo wonke elisanyatheliswa. Yaphoqeleka ukuthi ihlangane nephephandaba i-Haarlems Dagblad ngo-1942 ngesikhathi iJalimane idla iNetherlands. Kusukela lapho i-Haarlems Dagblad iye yavela nesihlokwana esithi Oprechte Haerlemse Courant 1656. 

Americas 
Bheka futhi: Umlando Wamaphephandaba aseMelika 

Umdwebo othakazelisayo wesitolo sikaMarguerite Martyn eSt. Louis Post-Dispatch ngo-Okthoba 21, 1906. Kwesokunxele kude, iqembu lamadoda lihlanganyela ngokufunda iphephandaba.
E-Boston ngo-1690, uBenjamin Harris washicilela i-Publick Occurrences Both Forreign and Domestick. Leli phephandaba lithathwa njengephephandaba lokuqala emakoloni aseMelika nakuba kwashicilelwa uhlelo olulodwa ngaphambi kokuba leli phephandaba licindezelwe uhulumeni. Ngo-1704, umbusi wavumela ukuthi i-Boston News-Letter ishicilelwe futhi yaba iphephandaba lokuqala elishicilelwe njalo emakoloni. Ngokushesha ngemva kwalokho, amaphepha amasonto onke aqala ukushicilelwa eNew York nasePhiladelphia. Lawa maphephandaba okuqala ayelandela indlela yaseBrithani futhi ngokuvamile ayenamakhasi amane ubude. Ikakhulukazi bebephatha izindaba ezivela eBrithani futhi okuqukethwe kuncike kulokho okuthakaselwa ngumhleli. Ngo-1783, iPennsylvania Evening Post yaba eyokuqala yaseMelika nsuku zonke.[21] 

Ngo-1752, uJohn Bushell washicilela i-Halifax Gazette, ethi "iphephandaba lokuqala laseCanada". Nokho, inzalo yayo esemthethweni, i-Royal Gazette, iyincwadi kahulumeni yezaziso ezingokomthetho nezimemezelo esikhundleni sokuba iphephandaba elifanele; Ngo-1764, iQuebec Gazette yanyatheliswa okokuqala mhla zingama-21 kuJuni 1764 futhi iseyiphephandaba elidala kunawo wonke elishicilelwe ngokuqhubekayo eNyakatho Melika njengeQuebec Chronicle-Telegraph. Njengamanje ishicilelwa njengolimi lwesiNgisi lwamasonto onke emahhovisi ayo e-1040 Belvédère, suite 218, Quebec City, Quebec, Canada. Ngo-1808, iGazeta do Rio de Janeiro [22] yaba nohlelo lwayo lokuqala, yanyatheliswa ngamathuluzi alethwe ivela eNgilandi, ishicilela izindaba ezivuna uhulumeni wase-United Kingdom yasePortugal, eBrazil kanye nase-Algarves njengoba yakhiqizwa yinkonzo yabezindaba esemthethweni yomqhele wamaPutukezi. 

Ngo-1821, ngemva kokuphela kokuvinjelwa kokusakazwa kwephephandaba elizimele, kuvela incwadi yokuqala enyathelisiwe engeyona yombuso, i-Diário do Rio de Janeiro, nakuba yayivele ikhona iCorreio Braziliense, eyanyatheliswa nguHipólito José da Costa ngesikhathi esifanayo neGazeta, kodwa kusukela eLondon futhi ngokugcizelela ngokunamandla ukudalula imibono yezombangazwe kanye nokudalula imibono yezombangazwe nokugxeka. Iphephandaba lokuqala ePeru kwaba El Peruano, eyasungulwa ngo-October 1825 futhi esanyatheliswa nanamuhla, kodwa nezinguquko amagama ambalwa. 

I-Asia 
Izihloko Eziyinhloko: Imidiya yokuphrinta e-India, amaphephandaba aseJapane, kanye nomlando wamaphephandaba aseShayina
Ngesikhathi sobukhosi baseTang eChina (618-906), iKaiyuan Za Bao yashicilela izindaba zikahulumeni; yayinyatheliswe ephepheni. Ngezinye izikhathi libhekwa njengelinye lamaphephandaba okuqala kakhulu ukushicilelwa. Umzamo wokuqala oqoshiwe wokuthola iphephandaba lohlobo lwanamuhla eNingizimu ye-Asia kaWilliam Bolts, umDashi owayeqashwe yiNkampani YaseBrithani East India ngo-September 1768 eCalcutta. Nokho, ngaphambi kokuthi aqale iphephandaba lakhe, wadingiswa wabuyela e-Europe. Ngo-1780 iphephandaba lokuqala elivela kulesi sifunda, i-Hicky's Bengal Gazette, lanyatheliswa indoda yase-Ireland, uJames Augustus Hicky. Wayisebenzisa njengendlela yokugxeka ukubusa kwamaNgisi ngokusebenzisa ubuntatheli.[23] I-Jobo, okwaxoxwa ngayo kuyi-Annals of the Joseon Dynasty, yanyatheliswa ngo-1577 ngabefundisi beNkosi uSeonjo. Njengoba iNkosi yayingayinikezanga imvume yokunyathelisa izindaba zezindaba, uJobo wayekwa, futhi izikhonzi ezingu-30 zagwetshwa “isijeziso esinzima”. Yayinyatheliswa nsuku zonke, futhi ihlanganisa izihloko ezihlukahlukene, ezihlanganisa isimo sezulu, imilaza nezindaba zamuva. Ngo-2017, indela yaseKorea yathi ithole ikhophi eyayisekhona yeJobo.[24][25] 

Middle East 
Isihloko esikhulu: Umlando wamaphephandaba aseMpumalanga Ephakathi  
Umlando wamaphephandaba aseMpumalanga Ephakathi uhlehlela emuva ekhulwini le-19. Abahleli abaningi bebengezona izintatheli kuphela kodwa nababhali, izazi zefilosofi nosopolitiki. Ngamajenali angekho emthethweni, lezi zihlakaniphi zazikhuthaza izinkulumo zomphakathi ngezombangazwe eMbusweni Wase-Ottoman nasePheresiya.Izincwadi zokubhala zazo zonke izinhlobo zahlukaniswa futhi zashicilelwa nakumaphephandaba.

Amaphephandaba okuqala eMbusweni Wase-Ottoman ayengawabantu bakwamanye amazwe ababehlala lapho ababefuna ukwenza inkulumo-ze ngezwe laseNtshonalanga.[26] Eyokuqala yanyatheliswa ngo-1795 yiPalais de France ePera. Ubuntatheli bomdabu baseMpumalanga Ephakathi baqala ngo-1828, lapho u-Muhammad Ali, uKhedive wase-Egypt, eyala ukusungulwa kwendawo yegazethi i-Vekâyi-i Mısriyye (Izindaba ZaseGibhithe).[27] Kwakuyiphepha lokuqala elabhalwa ngesi-Ottoman Turkish kanye nesi-Arabhu emakhasini aphikisanayo, futhi kamuva ngesi-Arabhu kuphela, ngaphansi kwesihloko esithi "Al-Waqāʾiʿ al-Miṣriyya".[28] 

Iphephandaba lokuqala laseTurkey elingelona elisemthethweni, i-Ceride-i Havadis (Irejista Yezehlakalo), yanyatheliswa yiNgisi, uWilliam Churchill, ngo-1840. Iphephandaba lokuqala langasese elashicilelwa izintatheli zaseTurkey, u-Tercüman-ı Ahvâl (Umhumushi Wezehlakalo), lasungulwa ngu-İbrahim Şinasi kanye no-Agah 986 kanye no-Agah 986. Iphephandaba lokuqala e-Iran, Kaghaz-e Akhbar (Iphephandaba), ladalelwa uhulumeni uMirza Saleh Shirazi ngo-1837.[30] Amajenali okuqala eNhlonhlweni Yase-Arabia avela e-Hijaz, lapho isizimele ekubuseni kwe-Ottoman, ngasekupheleni kweMpi Yezwe I. Omunye wabesifazane bokuqala ukusayina izihloko zakhe emaphephandabeni ama-Arab kwakungudokotela wesifazane uGalila Tamarhan, owanikela ngezindatshana ephephabhukwini lezokwelapha elibizwa ngokuthi "Ya'asub al-Tib" (Umholi we-38 kwezokwelapha). 

I-Industrial Revolution 

Ikhasi langaphambili le-Helsingin Sanomat (Helsinki Times) ngoJulayi 7, 1904 
Ngasekuqaleni kwekhulu le-19, amadolobha amaningi aseYurophu, kanye naseNyakatho neNingizimu Melika, anyathelisa izincwadi ezinjengamaphephandaba nakuba kungezona zonke ezathuthukiswa ngendlela efanayo; okuqukethwe kwakheke kakhulu okuthandwayo kwesifunda namasiko.[32] Intuthuko yobuchwepheshe bokunyathelisa ehlobene neNguquko Yezimboni yenza amaphephandaba abe yindlela yokuxhumana esakazwa kabanzi, njengoba ubuchwepheshe obusha bokunyathelisa benza ukunyathelisa kungabizi futhi kuphumelele ngokwengeziwe. Ngo-1814, i-Times (yaseLondon) yathola umshini wokunyathelisa owawukwazi ukwenza izinhlamvu ezingu-1 100 ngehora.[33] Ngokushesha, lo mshini wokunyathelisa washintshwa ukuze uphrinte nhlangothi zombili zekhasi ngesikhathi esisodwa. Lokhu kusungulwa kwenza amaphephandaba ashibhile futhi ngaleyo ndlela atholakale engxenyeni enkulu yabantu. 

Ngo-1830, iphephandaba lokuqala elishibhile elithi "i-penny press" lafika emakethe: I-Boston Transcript kaLynde M. Walter. [34] Amaphepha okushicilela kaPenny abiza cishe ingxenye eyodwa kwesithupha yenani lamanye amaphephandaba futhi anxusa izethameli eziningi, kuhlanganise nabantu abangafundile nabahola kancane.[35] E-France, u-Émile de Girardin waqala i-La Presse ngo-1836, wethula amaphephandaba ashibhile, asekelwa ukukhangisa e-France. Ngo-1848, u-August Zang, wase-Austrian owayazi u-Girardin eParis, wabuyela e-Vienna eyokwethula izindlela ezifanayo nge-Die Presse (eyaqanjwa futhi yakopisha ngokungananazi incwadi ka-Girardin).[36] 

Izigaba 
Nakuba amaphephandaba amaningi ehloselwe abafundi abahlukahlukene, ngokuvamile achazwa ngokwendawo, amanye agxila emaqenjini abafundi achazwe kakhulu ngezintshisakalo zabo kunendawo abakuyo: isibonelo, kukhona amaphephandaba ebhizinisi ansuku zonke namasonto onke (isb, I-Wall Street Journal kanye ne-India Today) kanye namaphephandaba ezemidlalo. Ochwepheshe abengeziwe basengamaphephandaba amasonto onke, ngokuvamile amahhala futhi asakazwa ezindaweni ezilinganiselwe zesifunda; lezi zingase zisebenzele imiphakathi ngendlela eqondile njengabantu abathile bokufika, umphakathi wendawo wezitabane noma abathanda i-indie rock ngaphakathi kwedolobha noma isifunda. 

I-Frequency 
Daily 
"Iphepha lansuku zonke" liqondisa kabusha lapha. Mayelana nomkhiqizo, bheka i-Daily Paper (izingubo). 
"Izinguqulo zangeSonto" ziqondisa kabusha lapha. Ukuze uthole okunye ukusetshenziswa, bheka i-Sunday Edition (disambiguation). 
Iphephandaba lansuku zonke linyatheliswa nsuku zonke, ngezinye izikhathi ngaphandle kwamaSonto futhi ngezinye izikhathi ngeMigqibelo (namanye amaholide amakhulu). NgoMgqibelo futhi, lapho ekhona, ushicilelo lwangeSonto lwamaphephandaba ansuku zonke luvame ukuba lukhudlwana, luhlanganisa izigaba ezikhethekile (isb, ezobuciko, amafilimu, ezokuzijabulisa) nokufakwa kokukhangisa, futhi kubiza ngaphezulu. Ngokuvamile, iningi lezisebenzi zala maphephandaba lisebenza kusukela ngoMsombuluko kuya kuLwesihlanu, ngakho ushicilelo lwangeSonto nolweMsombuluko luncike kakhulu kokuqukethwe okwenziwe kusengaphambili noma okuqukethwe okuthengiswayo.

Amaphephandaba amaningi ansuku zonke athengiswa ekuseni. Amaphepha antambama noma kusihlwa, ake avamile kodwa manje ayivelakancane, aqondiswe kakhulu kubagibeli nabasebenzi basehhovisi. Empeleni (nakuba lokhu kungase kuhluke ngokwezwe), iphephandaba lasekuseni litholakala ngohlelo lwasekuseni kusukela ngaphambi kwaphakathi kwamabili ngobusuku bangaphambi kosuku lwalo lwekhava, ezinye izinhlelo zinyatheliswa futhi zisatshalaliswe ebusuku. Izinhlelo zakamuva zingabandakanya izindaba eziphambili ezavezwa okokuqala ngalolo suku, ngemva kokuba uhlelo lwasekuseni selunyathelisiwe kakade. Ukuhlola kuqala amaphephandaba akusasa ngokuvamile kuyisici sezinhlelo zezindaba zasebusuku, njenge-Newsnight yase-United Kingdom. Ngo-1650, kwavela iphephandaba lokuqala lansuku zonke, i-Einkommende Zeitung, [37] elanyatheliswa nguTimotheus Ritzsch eLeipzig, eJalimane.[38] 
 
E-United Kingdom nakwamanye amazwe e-Commonwealth, ngokungafani namanye amazwe amaningi, amaphephandaba ansuku zonke awanyathelisi ngamaSonto. Phambilini bekunamaphephandaba angeSonto azimele; namuhla umshicileli ofanayo uvame ukukhiqiza iphephandaba langeSonto, elihluke ngezindlela eziningi kwelansuku zonke, ngokuvamile elinegama elihlobene nalo; isb, i-Times kanye ne-Sunday Times amaphephandaba ahlukene aphethwe yinkampani efanayo, futhi indatshana eshicilelwe ekugcineni ngeke inikezwe i-Times.

Kwezinye izimo uhlelo lwangeSonto luwuhlelo olwandisiwe lwephephandaba oluphuma kumshicileli ofanayo; kwezinye izimo, ikakhulukazi eBrithani, kungaba ibhizinisi elihlukile, isb, i-Observer, elingahlangene nephephandaba lansuku zonke kusukela ekusungulweni kwalo ngo-1791 laze latholwa yi-The Guardian ngo-1993. Imvamisa, iwuhlelo olwandiswe ngokukhethekile, ngokuvamile oluphindwe kaningana ubukhulu nesisindo sezinhlelo zezinsuku zaphakathi nesonto futhi ezitholakala ezigabeni ezivamile zangeSonto kanye nezihloko ezinjengamaviki. (njengeThe New York Times Magazine kanye neThe Sunday Times Magazine). 

Kwamanye amazwe amaphephandaba ansuku zonke awashicilelwa ngoSuku LukaKhisimusi, kodwa amaphephandaba aphuma masonto onke angalushintsha usuku lwawo isib. Amaphephandaba angeSonto ashicilelwa ngoMgqibelo zingama-24 kuZibandlela, olwandulela olwandulela uKhisimusi lapho usuku lukaKhisimusi luba ngeSonto. 

Ngamaviki onke 
Amanye amaphephandaba ashicilelwa kabili ngeviki futhi aziwa njengezincwadi zamasonto onke. 

Kathathu Ngeviki 
Njengoba igama liphakamisa, i-triweekly ishicilela kathathu ngesonto. I-Meridian Star iyisibonelo sencwadi enjalo.[39] 
Isihloko esikhulu 

samasonto onke : Iphephandaba lamasonto onke 
Amaphephandaba amasonto onke ashicilelwa kanye ngesonto, futhi avame ukuba mancane kunamaphepha ansuku zonke. 
Njalo ngeviki 
Okunye okushicilelwe kushicilelwe, ngokwesibonelo, ngemva kwamasonto amabili (noma kabili ngeviki ngolimi lwaseMelika). Bangase babe noshintsho osukwini oluvamile lwesonto lwesonto phakathi nesikhathi sikaKhisimusi kuye ngokuthi usuku lwesonto lukaKhisimusi luwela ngalo. 
Ububanzi bendawo nokusatshalaliswa 
Kwendawo noma kwesifunda 
Lesi sigaba asisho noma yimiphi imithombo. Sicela usize ukuthuthukisa lesi sigaba ngokungeza izingcaphuno emithonjeni ethembekile. Izinto ezingatholakali zingaphikiswa futhi zisuswe. (Disemba 2018) (Funda ukuthi ungawususa kanjani futhi nini lo mlayezo) 
Iphephandaba lendawo lisebenzela indawo efana nedolobha, noma ingxenye yedolobha elikhulu. Cishe zonke izimakethe zinephephandaba elilodwa noma amabili agcwele indawo. Amaphephandaba amadolobha amakhulu avame ukuba namanethiwekhi amakhulu okusabalalisa, futhi angatholakala ngaphandle kwendawo yawo evamile, ngezinye izikhathi ngokubanzi, ngezinye izikhathi emithonjeni embalwa.




Kuzwelonke 
Bheka futhi: Uhlu lwamaphephandaba kazwelonke 

Amaphephandaba amazwe ngamazwe athengiswayo eParis 
Main article: Printing press 
Izizwe eziningi zinephephandaba okungenani elilodwa elizungeza ezweni lonke: iphephandaba kazwelonke. Amanye amaphephandaba kazwelonke, njenge-Financial Times kanye ne-Wall Street Journal, akhethekile (kulezi zibonelo, ezindabeni zezezimali). Kunamaphephandaba amaningi kazwelonke e-United Kingdom, kodwa ambalwa kuphela e-United States naseCanada. E-Canada, i-The Globe and Mail ithengiswa ezweni lonke. E-United States, ngaphezu kwamaphephandaba kazwelonke anjalo, i-New York Times itholakala kulo lonke izwe.[40]

Kukhona neqeqebana lamaphephandaba elingabonakala njengamaphephandaba omhlaba. Amanye, njenge-New York Times International Edition, (eyayiyi-International Herald Tribune) ibilokhu igxile kulokho, kanti amanye amaphephandaba kazwelonke apakishwa kabusha noma "ama-edishini aphesheya" kwamaphephandaba ezwe noma amakhulu edolobhakazi. Kwezinye izimo, iziqephu zendatshana ezingase zingathakazelisi ububanzi obubanzi babafundi zikhishiwe ezinhlelweni zamazwe ngamazwe; kokunye, okuthakasela abakwamanye amazwe, izindaba ezibalulekile zezwe ziyagcinwa. Njengoba isiNgisi saba ulimi lwamazwe ngamazwe kwezamabhizinisi nobuchwepheshe, amaphephandaba amaningi ngaphambilini abeshicilelwa ngezilimi okungezona isiNgisi nawo asungule izinhlelo zolimi lwesiNgisi. Ezindaweni ezihlukahlukene njenge-Jerusalem ne-Mumbai, amaphephandaba anyatheliselwa umphakathi wasekhaya nowamazwe ngamazwe okhuluma isiNgisi, kanye nezivakashi. Ukufika kwe-inthanethi kuvumele namaphephandaba angelona isiNgisi ukuthi akhiphe inguqulo yesiNgisi esehlisiwe ukuze iphephandaba lawo lifinyelele umhlaba wonke. 

Ngokufanayo, emazweni amaningi anabantu abaningi abakhuluma olunye ulimi noma izivakashi eziningi, amaphephandaba anezilimi ezingezona ezolimi lwesizwe anyatheliswa kokubili kuleli futhi athunyelwe kwamanye amazwe. Ngokwesibonelo, amaphephandaba nomagazini abavela emazweni amaningi, namaphephandaba anyatheliswa endaweni ngezilimi eziningi, sekumi ngomumo ukutholakala ezindlini zezindaba enkabeni yeLondon. Esifundazweni sase-US saseFlorida, izivakashi eziningi ezivela esifundazweni sase-Canada e-Quebec ezikhuluma isiFulentshi zivakashela ukuhlala isikhathi eside ebusika ("izinyoni zeqhwa") kangangokuthi ezinye izindawo zokudayisa nezitolo zithengisa amaphephandaba esiFulentshi njenge-Le Droit. 

Isihloko 
Amaphephandaba jikelele ahlanganisa zonke izihloko, ngokugcizelela okuhlukile. Nakuba okungenani kukhulunywa ngazo zonke izihloko, ezinye zingase zibe nokuhlanganisa kahle izenzakalo zamazwe ngamazwe ezibalulekile; abanye bangase bagxile kakhulu kwezokuzijabulisa kazwelonke noma zendawo noma ezemidlalo. Amaphephandaba akhethekile angase agxile kakhulu, ngokwesibonelo, ezindabeni zezezimali. Kunezincwadi ezikhuluma ngezemidlalo kuphela, noma imidlalo ethile, imijaho yamahhashi, 

imidlalo yaseshashalazini nokunye, nakuba kungase kungabe kusabizwa ngokuthi 
amaphephandaba 

.
Emakhulwini eminyaka amaphephandaba ayenyatheliswa ephepheni futhi enikezwa ngokoqobo kubafundi ngokusatshalaliswa kwendawo noma kwezinye izimo ngeposi, isibonelo kwabangaphandle baseBrithani abahlala eNdiya noma eHong Kong ababhalisele amaphephandaba aseBrithani. Amaphephandaba angalethwa ezindlini zababhalisile kanye/noma amabhizinisi ngabantu abathunyelwa ngephepha, athunyelwe ngeposi, athengiswe ezitolo zezindaba, ezitolo zegrosa, nasezitolo ezithengisa izinto ezilula, futhi alethwe emitatsheni yolwazi nezitolo zezincwadi. Izinhlangano zamaphephandaba zidinga uhlelo olukhulu lokusabalalisa ukuze zilethe amaphepha azo kulaba basakazi abahlukene, okuvamise ukubandakanya amaloli okudiliva kanye nabantu abadilivayo. Eminyakeni yakamuva, amaphephandaba kanye neminye imithombo yezindaba ijwayelane nesimo sobuchwepheshe esishintshayo ngokuqala ukunikeza izinhlelo eziku-inthanethi ukuze zihlangabezane nezidingo zomphakathi. Ngokuzayo, inkambiso yokulethwa kwezindaba nge-elekthronikhi izoqhubeka ngokugcizelela kakhulu i-inthanethi, inkundla yezokuxhumana kanye nezinye izindlela zokulethwa kwe-elekthronikhi. Kodwa-ke, ngenkathi indlela yokulethwa ishintsha, iphephandaba kanye nemboni kusene-niche emhlabeni. I-athikili eyinhloko 

eku-inthanethi 
: Iphephandaba eliku-inthanethi 
Kusukela ngo-2007, cishe wonke amaphephandaba amakhulu aphrintiwe akhiqiza izinhlelo eziku-inthanethi ezisatshalaliswa nge-inthanethi, okuthi, kuye ngezwe, lilawulwe izinhlangano zobuntatheli njengeKhomishana Yezikhalazo Zabezindaba e-UK.[41] Kodwa njengoba abanye abashicileli bethola ukuthi amamodeli abo asekelwe ezincwadini aya ngokuya engathandeki,[42] "amaphephandaba" asekelwe kuwebhu nawo aseqalile ukuvela, njengeSouthport Reporter e-UK kanye neSeattle Post-Intelligencer, eyayeka ukushicilela ngokuphrinta ngemva kweminyaka engu-149 ngoMashi 2009 futhi yaba yiphepha eliku-inthanethi kuphela. 

Kusukela ngo-2005 e-UK amaphephandaba esifunda angaphezu kuka-200 avaliwe okuholele ekwehleni kwenani lezintatheli zesifunda ngo-50%. Ucwaningo olwenziwa ngo-2016 olwenziwa i-King's College, eLondon, lwathola ukuthi amadolobha alahlekelwe amaphephandaba awo asendaweni ayehlehla ezimisweni zentando yeningi futhi alahlekelwa ukholo lomphakathi eziphathimandleni.[43] 

Umkhuba omusha ekushicilelweni kwamaphephandaba ukwethulwa kokwenza kube ngokwakho ngobuchwepheshe bokuphrinta obufunwa kakhulu noma ngamawebhusayithi ahlanganisa izindaba aku-inthanethi njengezindaba ze-Google. Amaphephandaba enziwe ngokwezifiso avumela umfundi ukuthi enze iphephandaba lakhe ngalinye ngokukhetha amakhasi ngamanye avela ezincwadini eziningi. Le ndlela "Engcono Kakhulu" ivumela ukuvuselelwa kwemodeli esekelwe ekuphrintiwe futhi ivule isiteshi esisha sokusabalalisa ukuze kwandiswe ukutholakala ngaphansi kwemingcele evamile yokusabalalisa. Amaphephandaba enziwe ngokwezifiso aku-inthanethi anikezwe i-MyYahoo, I-Google, CRAYON, ICurrent.com, Kibboko.com, Twitter. izikhathi nezinye eziningi. Ngala maphephandaba aku-inthanethi, umfundi angakhetha ukuthi ingakanani ingxenye ngayinye (ezombangazwe, ezemidlalo, ezobuciko, njll.) afisa ukuyibona ezindabeni zabo. 

Inhlangano kanye nabasebenzi 

Indlu yokunyathelisa yeTelegraph eMacon, Georgia, c. 1876

Umfanyana wezindaba othengisa i-Toronto Telegram e-Canada ngo-1905 

Igumbi lezindaba lase-Gazeta Lubuska e-Zielona Góra, e-Poland 

Ibhilidi lehhovisi lase-Tyrvään Sanomat e-Sastamala, e-Finland 
Ubusuku engosini yezindaba e-Daily Nebraskan 
E-US, umphathi jikelele noma isikhulu esiphezulu sephephandaba ngumshicileli.[44] Emaphephandabeni amancane, umnikazi wokushicilelwe (noma umnikazi wamasheya omkhulu kunabo bonke enkampanini engumnikazi wokushicilelwe) ngokuvamile ungumshicileli [okucashunwa] Iningi lamaphephandaba aneminyango emine eyinhloko enikelwe ekushicileleni iphephandaba ngokwalo— elokuhlela, elokukhiqiza/lokunyathelisa, elisakazwayo, kanye nokukhangisa, nakuba evame ukubizwa ngamagama ahlukahlukene. Amaphepha amaningi aphinde abe neminyango engaqondene nephephandaba etholakala kwamanye amabhizinisi anosayizi ofanayo, njenge-accounting, ukumaketha, izinsiza zabantu, kanye ne-IT. 

Kuwo wonke umhlaba okhuluma isiNgisi, umuntu okhetha okuqukethwe kwephephandaba uvame ukubizwa ngokuthi umhleli. Ukwehluka kulesi sihloko okufana nomhleli oyinhloko, umhleli omkhulu, nokunye kuvamile. Emaphephandabeni amancane, umhleli oyedwa angaba nesibopho kuzo zonke izindawo zokuqukethwe. Emaphephandabeni amakhulu, umhleli ophezulu kakhulu nguyena ophethe ukushicilelwa, kuyilapho abahleli abancane abaphezulu bangagxila endabeni eyodwa yesihloko, njengezindaba zendawo noma ezemidlalo. Lezi zigaba zibizwa ngokuthi amahhovisi ezindaba noma "amadeski", futhi ngayinye igadwe umhleli oqokiwe. Abahleli abaningi bamaphephandaba bakopisha ukuhlela izindaba engxenyeni yabo yephephandaba, kodwa bangase babelane ngomsebenzi wabo nabahloli bamaphutha nabahloli bamaqiniso. 

Izintatheli yizintatheli ezibika ngokuyinhloko amaqiniso eziwaqoqile, futhi labo ababhala izindatshana ezinde, ezigxile kakhulu ezindabeni bangase babizwe ngokuthi ababhali bezindaba. Abathwebuli bezithombe nabadwebi bezithombe bahlinzeka ngezithombe nemifanekiso ukuze basekele ama-athikili. Izintatheli zivame ukuba ngochwepheshe endabeni ethile, ebizwa ngokuthi isigqi, njengezemidlalo, inkolo, noma isayensi. Ababhali bamakholomu yizintatheli ezibhala izindatshana ezivamile ezixoxa ngemibono yazo kanye nolwazi lwazo. Amaphrinta nabanyathelisi banyathelisa iphephandaba. Ukunyathelisa kukhishwa amaphephandaba amaningi, ngokwengxenye ngenxa yezindleko zomshini wokunyathelisa we-offset (uhlobo oluvame kakhulu lomshini wokunyathelisa osetshenziswa ukunyathelisa amaphephandaba), nangenxa yokuthi umshini wokunyathelisa wephephandaba elincane ungase udinge ukusebenza okungaphansi kwehora, okusho ukuthi uma iphephandaba linowalo umshini belizohlala lingenzi lutho isikhathi esiningi. Uma iphephandaba linikeza ulwazi ku-inthanethi, abaphathi bewebhu kanye nabaklami bewebhu bangaqashwa ukuze balayishe izindaba kusizindalwazi sephephandaba.

Abasebenzi bomnyango wezokujikeleza baxhumana nezitolo ezidayisa leli phephandaba; thengisa okubhaliselwe; futhi yengamele ukusatshalaliswa kwamaphephandaba anyathelisiwe ngeposi, ngabathwali bamaphephandaba, ezitolo, nangemishini yokudayisa. Amaphephandaba amahhala awawathengisi amaphephandaba, kodwa asenomnyango osakaza amaphephandaba obhekele ukusabalalisa amaphephandaba. Izisebenzi zokuthengisa emnyangweni wokukhangisa azithengisi nje kuphela indawo yesikhangiso kumakhasimende afana namabhizinisi endawo, kodwa futhi zisiza amakhasimende aklame futhi ahlele imikhankaso yawo yokukhangisa. Amanye amalungu omnyango wokukhangisa angase ahlanganise abaklami bezithombe, abaklama izikhangiso ngokuya ngokucaciswa kwamakhasimende kanye nezinqubomgomo zomnyango. Ephephandabeni elingenazo ukukhangisa, awukho umnyango wokukhangisa. 

Ama-Zoned kanye nezinye izinhlelo 

Iphephandaba lansuku zonke lase-Israel i-Haaretz ezinhlelweni zalo zesiHebheru nesiNgisi 
Amaphephandaba avame ukwenza ngcono ukusatshalaliswa kwezikhangiso nezindaba ngokuklama nokuhlela. Ukuklama kwenzeka lapho ukukhangisa nokuqukethwe kokuhlela kushintsha ukuze kubonise indawo lapho umkhiqizo ulethwa khona.
