Okuqukethwe kokuhlela ngokuvamile kungase kushintshe ukuze nje kubonise izinguquko ekukhangiseni—inani nesakhiwo esithinta isikhala esitholakalayo sokuhlela—noma singaqukatha izindaba eziqondene nesifunda esithile. Ezimweni ezingavamile, ukukhangisa kungase kungashintshi ukusuka kwenye indawo kuya kwenye, kodwa kuzoba nokuqukethwe okuhlukile kokuhlela okuqondene nesifunda. Njengoba okuqukethwe kungahluka kakhulu, izinhlelo eziklanyiwe zivame ukukhiqizwa ngokuhambisana. Ukuhlelwa kwenzeka ezigabeni eziyinhloko njengoba izindaba zibuyekezwa ubusuku bonke. Ukukhangisa kuvame ukufana ku-edishini ngayinye (ngaphandle kwezifunda eziklanyiwe, lapho kuvame ukuba yingxenye ethi 'B' yezindaba zasendaweni ebhekana nezinguquko zokukhangisa). Njengoba uhlelo ngalunye lumelela izindaba zakamuva ezitholakalayo ekunyatheliseni okulandelayo, lezi zinhlelo zikhiqizwa ngokulandelana, ngohlelo olulodwa oluqediwe luyakopishwa futhi lubuyekezelwe uhlelo olulandelayo. Uhlelo lwangaphambilini luhlala lukopishwa ukuze kugcinwe iPhephandaba Lokurekhodiwa kanye nokubuyela emuva uma kudingeka ukulungiswa ngokushesha kwabezindaba. Isibonelo, zombili i-The New York Times kanye ne-Wall Street Journal zinikeza uhlelo lwesifunda, oluphrintwe ngosonkontileka wasendaweni, futhi oluqukethe okuqukethwe okuthile kwendawo. Ikhadi lezinga lokukhangisa lejenali linikeza isibonelo esihle sokuhlela.[45] 

Bheka futhi izigaba zasemadolobheni e-Los Angeles Times. 
Ifomethi ye- 

Yomiuri Shimbun, i-broadsheet e-Japan ehlonishwa ngokuba nephephandaba elisakazwa kakhulu emhlabeni wonke 
Amaphephandaba amaningi esimanje[46] akwenye yosayizi abathathu:
 
Ama-Broadsheets: 600 mm × 380 mm (23+1⁄2 in × 15 in), ngokuvamile ehlotshaniswa namaphephandaba ahlakaniphe kakhulu, nakuba amaphephandaba eshintsha leli phephandaba. Izibonelo zifaka i-Daily Telegraph yase-United Kingdom.
Ama-Tabloids: uhhafu kasayizi wama-broadsheet ngo-380 mm × 300 mm (15 ku-× 11+3⁄4 in), futhi ngokuvamile abonwa njengashukumisa ingqondo ngokungafani nama-broadsheet.[catation] Izibonelo zifaka i-The Sun, The National Enquirer, The Star Magazine, New York Post, Chicago Sun-Times, kanye ne-The Grounds. 
I-"Microdaily" ayivamisile ukusetshenziselwa ukubhekisela ephephandabeni lansuku zonke lamahhala elingasayizi we-tabloid elinikeza amanani aphansi ezikhangiso kunabaqhudelana nabo be-broadsheet.[catation] Okuqukethwe kwe-microdaily kungasukela ekusakazweni kwezindaba zasendaweni okujulile kuye kwinhlanganisela yezindaba zasendaweni nezikazwelonke.[catation edingekayo] 
Berliner noma i-Midi: 470 mm × 8+15 ⁄1 × 2 × 2 mm ⁄1 mm ⁄1 ⁄1 ⁄1 × 15 mm in) esetshenziswa amaphepha ase-Europe afana ne-Le Monde e-France, i-La Stampa e-Italy, i-El País e-Spain futhi, kusukela ngo-2005 kuze kube ngu-2018, i-Guardian e-United Kingdom. 
I-Brazilian Vossa Senhoria ithi iphephandaba elincane kunawo wonke emhlabeni, elikala u-1.4 in. x 1 in (3.5 cm x 2.5 cm). 

Amaphephandaba ajwayele ukuphrintwa ephepheni elishibhile, elingekho mhlophe elaziwa ngokuthi yi-newsprint. Kusukela ngeminyaka yawo-1980, imboni yamaphephandaba iye yasuka kakhulu ekunyatheliseni kwe-letterpress yekhwalithi ephansi yaya ekunyatheliseni kwekhwalithi ephezulu, ngemibala emine, ukuphrinta kwe-offset. Ngaphezu kwalokho, amakhompiyutha edeskithophu, isofthiwe yokucubungula amagama, isofthiwe yezithombe, amakhamera edijithali kanye nobuchwepheshe bokunyathelisa kwangaphambili kanye nokuhlelwa kwezinhlamvu kuyiguqule kakhulu inqubo yokukhiqiza amaphephandaba. Lobu buchwepheshe buye benza amaphephandaba akwazi ukushicilela izithombe ezinemibala kanye nemifanekiso, kanye nezakhiwo ezisha kanye nomklamo ongcono. 

Ukuze izihloko zawo zigqame ezitolo zezindaba, amanye amaphephandaba anyatheliswa emaphephandabeni anemibala. Isibonelo, i-Financial Times iphrintwe ephepheni elipinki elihlukile le-salmon, futhi ukushicilelwa kwezemidlalo kwamasonto onke kwe-Sheffield kuthole igama layo, i-Green 'Un, kumbala wendabuko wephepha layo. Iphephandaba lezemidlalo lase-Italy i-La Gazzetta dello Sport nalo liphrintwe ephepheni elibomvana kuyilapho i-L'Équipe (eyake yabizwa ngokuthi i-L'Auto) iphrintwe ephepheni eliphuzi. Yomibili le yakamuva ikhuthaze imijaho emikhulu yamabhayisikili futhi imibala yayo yephephabhuku ibonakale ngemibala yamajezi asetshenziswa ukukhombisa umholi womjaho; isibonelo umholi we-Giro d'Italia ugqoka ijezi eliphinki. 

Ukujikeleza nokufunda 
Izihloko eziyinhloko: Uhlu lwamaphephandaba ngokusakazwa, Ukusatshalaliswa kwamaphephandaba, kanye nokuguga kokufunda amaphephandaba
Inani lamakhophi asakazwayo, kungaba ngosuku oluyisilinganiso noma ngezinsuku ezithile (ngokuvamile ngeSonto), libizwa ngokuthi ukusakazwa kwephephandaba futhi lingenye yezinto eziyinhloko ezisetshenziselwa ukusetha amanani okukhangisa. Ukusakazwa kwezincwadi akufani ngempela namakhophi athengiswayo, njengoba amanye amakhophi noma amaphephandaba asakazwa ngaphandle kwezindleko. Izibalo zokufunda zingase zibe phezulu kunezibalo ezisatshalaliswayo, ngoba amakhophi amaningi afundwa abantu abangaphezu koyedwa, nakuba lokhu kuncishiswa inani lamakhophi asabalalisiwe kodwa angafundiwe (ikakhulukazi lawo asakazwa mahhala). E-United States, i-Alliance for Audited Media igcina idatha yomlando neyamanje ekusakazeni okumaphakathi kwamaphephandaba ansuku zonke naweviki onke kanye namanye amaphephandaba. 

Ngokwe-Guinness Book of Records, ukusakazwa kwansuku zonke kwephephandaba laseSoviet i-Trud kweqa izi-21 500 000 ngo-1990, kuyilapho i-Argumenty i Fakty yamasonto onke yaseSoviet yaziqhayisa ngokusakazwa kwezingu-33 500 000 ngo-1991. izigidi. I-Bild yaseJalimane, esakazwa izigidi ezingu-1.15, kwakuyilona kuphela elinye iphepha kuleso sigaba. E-United Kingdom, iThe Sun yilona elihamba phambili ngokudayisa, njengoba kunamakhophi alinganiselwa ezigidini ezingu-1.2 asakazwa nsuku zonke. E-US, i-Wall Street Journal isakazwa nsuku zonke cishe ezigidini ezingu-2.02, okuyenza ibe yiphepha elisakazwa kakhulu ezweni.[47] 

Nakuba ukufunda okukhokhelwayo kwamaphephandaba aphrintiwe kwehla kancane kancane emazweni athuthukile e-OECD, bekulokhu kukhuphuka emazweni amakhulu asathuthuka (iBrazil, i-India, i-Indonesia, i-China kanye neNingizimu Afrika), ukusakazwa kwawo okukhokhelwayo nsuku zonke kudlula okwamazwe athuthukile okokuqala ngqa ngo-2008. [48] E-India,[49] I-Times of India iphephandaba lesiNgisi elisakazwa kakhulu kunawo wonke, elinamakhophi ayizigidi ezingu-3.14 nsuku zonke. Ngokocwaningo lwe-Indian Readership lwango-2009, i-Dainik Jagran iphephandaba elifundwa kakhulu, elibhalwe ngolimi lwendawo (isi-Hindi), elinabafundi abayizigidi ezingama-55.7.[50] Ngokuka-Tom Standage we-Economist, i-India njengamanje inamaphepha asakazwa nsuku zonke angamakhophi ayizigidi eziyi-110.[51]

Isilinganiso esivamile sempilo yephephandaba ukungena ezimakethe, okushiwo njengephesenti lemizi ethola ikhophi yephephandaba uma kuqhathaniswa nenani eliphelele lemizi endaweni yemakethe yephepha. Ngeminyaka yawo-1920, kuzwelonke e-US, amaphephandaba ansuku zonke azuza ukungena emakethe ngamaphesenti angu-123 (okusho ukuthi i-avareji yomndeni wase-US yathola amaphephandaba angu-1.23). Njengoba eminye imithombo yezindaba iqala ukuncintisana namaphephandaba, futhi njengoba ukunyathelisa kuba lula futhi kungambi eqolo okudala ukuhlukahluka okukhulu kwezincwadi, ukungena ezimakethe kwaqala ukwehla. Kwaze kwaba sekuqaleni kwawo-1970, nokho, lapho ukungena kwemakethe kwehle ngaphansi kwamaphesenti ayi-100. Ngonyaka ka-2000, kwase kumaphesenti angama-53 futhi zisawa.[52] Amaphephandaba amaningi akhokhelwe anikeza izinhlelo ezihlukahlukene zokubhalisa. Ngokwesibonelo, othile angase afune iphepha langeSonto kuphela, noma mhlawumbe ngeSonto nangoMgqibelo kuphela, noma mhlawumbe isikhokhelo sesonto lomsebenzi kuphela, noma mhlawumbe isikhokhelo sansuku zonke. Amaphephandaba amaningi anikeza okunye noma konke okuqukethwe kwawo kuyi-Internet, ngaphandle kwenkokhiso noma ngemali ekhokhwayo. Kwezinye izimo, ukufinyelela kwamahhala kutholakala kuphela ngendaba yezinsuku noma amasonto, noma inombolo ethile yezihloko ezibukiwe, ngemva kwalokho abafundi kufanele babhalise futhi banikeze idatha yomuntu siqu. Kwezinye izimo, izingobo zomlando zamahhala zinikezwa. 

Umthengisi wamaphephandaba, Paddington, London, February 2005 
Umdayisi wamaphephandaba, Paddington, London, February 2005 
 
Ubude besikhathi: 40 seconds.0:40 
Ukuzama ukuthenga iphephandaba 
Ukukhangisa 
 
Newspaper kanye nesikhangiso, Argentina
Iphephandaba ngokuvamile likhiqiza u-70–80% wemali engenayo ngokukhangisa, kanye nensalela ekuthengisweni nasekubhaliseni.[53] Ingxenye yephephandaba engakhangisi ibizwa ngokuthi okuqukethwe kokuhlela, indaba yokuhlela, noma nje indaba yokuhlela, nakuba igama lokugcina lisetshenziselwa ukubhekisela ngokuqondile kulezo zihloko lapho iphephandaba nababhali balo abayizivakashi beveza imibono yabo. (Lokhu mehluko, nokho, wathuthukiswa ngokuhamba kwesikhathi - abashicileli bokuqala abafana no-Girardin (France) no-Zang (Austria) abazange bahlale behlukanisa izinto ezikhokhelwayo kokuqukethwe kokuhlela.). Imodeli yebhizinisi yokuba nokukhangisa isekela izindleko zokunyathelisa nokusabalalisa amaphephandaba (futhi, kuhlale kuthenjwa ukuthi, ukwenza inzuzo) kunokuba ababhalisile bakhokhe izindleko eziphelele senziwa okokuqala, kubonakala sengathi, ngo-1833 yi-Sun, iphepha lansuku zonke elanyatheliswa eNew York City. Kunokuba bakhokhise amasenti angu-6 ikhophi ngayinye, inani lentengo evamile yansuku zonke yaseNew York ngaleso sikhathi, babekhokhisa isenti elingu-1, futhi kwakuncike ekukhangiseni ukuze benze umehluko.[54]

Amaphephandaba emazweni anokufinyelela kalula kuwebhu alinyazwe ukwehla kwabakhangisi abaningi bendabuko. Izitolo zomnyango nezitolo ezinkulu bekungathenjelwe kuzo esikhathini esidlule ukuthi zithenge amakhasi ezikhangiso zamaphephandaba, kodwa ngenxa yokuhlanganiswa kwezimboni mancane kakhulu amathuba okuthi zenze kanjalo manje.[55] Ukwengeza, amaphephandaba abona abakhangisi bendabuko beshintshela ezinkundleni ezintsha zemidiya. Isigaba esihlukanisiwe sishintshela kumasayithi afaka i-Craigslist, amawebhusayithi okuqashwa, namasayithi ezimoto. Abakhangisi kazwelonke bashintshela ezinhlotsheni eziningi zokuqukethwe kwedijithali okuhlanganisa amawebhusayithi, izinkundla zemidiya enothile, kanye neselula. 

Eminyakeni yamuva, i-advertorial yavela. Izikhangisi zivame ukubonwa njengomhleli ophambene lapho abantu besithathu bakhokha imali ukuze bayifake ephepheni. Abakhangisi bavamise ukukhangisa ngemikhiqizo emisha noma amasu, njengedizayini entsha yezinto zegalofu, uhlobo olusha lokuhlinzwa nge-laser, noma izidakamizwa zokwehlisa isisindo. Ithoni ivamise ukuthi isondele kuleyo yokukhishwa kwabezindaba kunendaba yezindaba eyinhloso. Izindatshana ezinjalo zivame ukuhlukaniswa ngokucacile kokuqukethwe kokuhlela ngokusebenzisa idizayini nesakhiwo sekhasi noma ngelebula ememezela i-athikili njengesikhangiso. Nokho, kube nokukhathazeka okukhulayo ngokufiphala komugqa phakathi kokuqukethwe kokuhlela kanye nokukhangisa.[56] 

Ngo-1938 iphephandaba lesiDashi isikhangiso sezingubo zabesifazane ezithengiswa ezitolo ze-C&A 
1938 iphephandaba lesiDashi isikhangiso sezingubo zabesifazane ezithengiswa ezitolo ze-C&A ezitolo 
 
zamaphephandaba ase-US imali yokukhangisa yephephandaba—I-Newspaper Association of America yashicilela idatha[57] 
Imali yokukhangisa yephephandaba lase-US—I-Newspaper Association of America yanyathelisa idatha[57] 
I-Journalism 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ubuntatheli 
 
Thenyil0 staff in Seroslav Kray
Kusukela amaphephandaba aqala ukwenza izenzakalo zamanje amaphephandaba aqala ukubizwa ngokuthi ubuntatheli. Enkathini yobuntatheli ephuzi yekhulu le-19, amaphephandaba amaningi e-United States ayethembele ezindabeni ezivusa amadlingozi ezazihloselwe ukucasula noma ukujabulisa umphakathi, kunokuba zazise. Isitayela esivinjelwe sokubika esincike ekuhloleni amaqiniso nokunemba siphinde saduma ngeMpi Yezwe II. Ukugxekwa kobuntatheli kuhlukene futhi kwesinye isikhathi kushubile. Ukuthembeka kuyabuzwa ngenxa yemithombo engaziwa; amaphutha emaqinisweni, isipelingi, nohlelo lolimi; ukuchema kwangempela noma okucatshangwayo; kanye namahlazo ahlanganisa ukukopela nokuqamba amanga.
 
Esikhathini esedlule, amaphephandaba abevame ukuba ngabanikazi bamaphephandaba, futhi ayesetshenziselwa ukuthola izwi lezombusazwe. Ngemuva kuka-1920 amaphephandaba amaningi amakhulu aba izingxenye zamaketanga aphethwe yizinkampani ezinkulu zemidiya ezifana ne-Gannett, The McClatchy Company, Hearst Corporation, Cox Enterprises, Landmark Media Enterprises LLC, Morris Communications, The Tribune Company, Hollinger International, News Corporation, Swift Communications, njll. Amaphephandaba, emhlabeni wanamuhla, adlale indima ebalulekile ekusebenziseni inkululeko yokukhuluma. Izimpimpi, kanye nalabo “abaputshuza” izindaba zenkohlakalo emibuthanweni yezepolitiki bavame ukukhetha ukwazisa amaphephandaba ngaphambi kwezinye izindlela zokuxhumana, bethembele ekuzimiseleni okucatshangwa ngabahleli bamaphephandaba ukuveza izimfihlo namanga alabo abangathanda ukuwabhala. Kodwa-ke, kube nezimo eziningi zokuncishiswa kokuzimela kwezepolitiki kwamaphephandaba. Ucwaningo lwakamuva luhlole imiphumela yokuvala kwephephandaba ekuqokweni kabusha kwabazongena ezikhundleni, ukuphuma kwabavoti, kanye nezindleko zomkhankaso.[58] 

Imibono yabanye ababhali nabafundi ichazwa ku-op-ed ("okuphambene nekhasi lokuhlela") kanye nezincwadi eziya ezigabeni zabahleli zephepha. Ezinye zezindlela amaphephandaba azame ngazo ukuthuthukisa ukwethembeka kwawo yilezi: ukuqoka ombudsmen, ukuthuthukisa izinqubomgomo zezimiso zokuziphatha nokuqeqeshwa, ukusebenzisa izinqubomgomo zokulungisa eziqinile, ukuxhumana nezinqubo zabo kanye nezizathu ezizwakalayo nabafundi, nokucela imithombo ukuthi ibuyekeze izihloko ngemva kokushicilelwa. 

Umthelela wethelevishini ne-inthanethi 
Isihloko esikhulu: Ukwehla kwamaphephandaba 
Ulwazi olwengeziwe: Amaphephandaba aku-inthanethi 

Umshini wokunyathelisa wamaphephandaba e-Limoges, eFrance
Ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yawo-1990, ukutholakala kwezindaba ngeziteshi zethelevishini zamahora angama-24 kanye nokutholakala okulandelayo kobuntatheli be-inthanethi kwabeka inselele eqhubekayo kumodeli yebhizinisi yamaphephandaba amaningi emazweni athuthukile. Ukusatshalaliswa kwamaphephandaba akhokhelwayo kwehlile, kuyilapho imali eqoqwayo yokukhangisa—imali eningi etholwa ngamaphephandaba—isuke isuka enyathelisiwe iye ezinkundleni zokuxhumana kanye namawebhusayithi ezindaba, okubangele ukwehla okuvamile. Enye yezinselelo ukuthi inqwaba yamawebhusayithi ezindaba aku-inthanethi atholakala mahhala. Amanye amasayithi ezindaba aku-inthanethi ane-paywall futhi adinga ukubhalisa okukhokhelwayo ukuze afinyelele. Emazweni angathuthukile, ukunyathelisa nokusabalalisa okushibhile, ukwanda kokwazi ukufunda nokubhala, ukukhula kwesigaba esiphakathi, nezinye izici kuye kwanxephezela ukuvela kwezinto zobuchwepheshe, futhi ukusakazwa kwamaphephandaba kuyaqhubeka kukhula.[59]

Ngo-April 1995, iThe American Reporter yaba iphephandaba lokuqala lansuku zonke elisekelwe ku-inthanethi elinezintatheli zalo ezikhokhelwayo kanye nokuqukethwe kwangempela.[60] Ikusasa lamaphephandaba emazweni anamazinga aphezulu okufinyelela ku-inthanethi kuye kwaphikiswana ngakho kabanzi njengoba imboni iye yabhekana nokwehla kwamanani entengo ephephabhuku, ukwehla kokuthengiswa kwezikhangiso, ukulahleka kokukhangisa okuhlukaniswa kakhulu, kanye nokwehla okukhulu kokusatshalaliswa. Kusukela ngasekupheleni kwawo-1990, inani lamaphephandaba okubhekwe ukuthi livalwe, ukuqothuka, noma ukuncishiswa okunzima liye lenyuka—ikakhulukazi e-United States, lapho le mboni iye yakhipha ingxenye yesihlanu yezintatheli zayo kusukela ngo-2001.[61] Umbiko kaJuni 2022 ulinganisela ukuthi amaphephandaba ama-2 afa isonto ngalinye, futhi wembula ukuthi i-US yehla isuka kumaphephandaba ayi-8,891 ngo-2005 yaya ku-6,377 ekupheleni kukaMeyi 2022. Imisebenzi yobuntatheli yehla isuka ku-75,000 ngo-2006 yaya ku-31,000 ngo-2022. [62] 

Inkulumo-mpikiswano isiphuthuma kakhulu muva nje, njengoba ukwehla komnotho ngo-2008-2009 kwaphuca inzuzo yamaphephandaba futhi njengoba ukukhula okwake kwaba nokuqhuma kwenzuzo yewebhu sekwehlile, kwavimbela lokho imboni eyayinethemba lokuthi kuzoba umthombo obalulekile wemali engenayo.[63] Okubangwayo ukuthi imboni yamaphephandaba ibhekene ne-cyclical trough (noma idiphu), noma ukuthi ubuchwepheshe obusha buye benza amaphephandaba angasebenzi. Kusukela ngo-2017, amaphesenti akhulayo ezinkulungwane zeminyaka athola izindaba zawo kumawebhusayithi ezokuxhumana. Ngawo-2010, amaphephandaba amaningi endabuko aseqalile ukunikeza "izinhlelo zedijithali", ezifinyeleleka ngamakhompyutha namadivayisi eselula. Ukukhangisa ku-inthanethi kuvumela amawebhusayithi ezindaba ukuthi abonise izikhangiso eziphakelwayo, ngokusekelwe kulokho okuthakaselwayo yisivakashi. 

Izingobo zomlando 
Bheka futhi: Uhlu lwezingobo zomlando zamaphephandaba kanye Namaphephandaba e-United States § Izingobo zomlando 
Esikhathini sewebhu, izinqolobane zedijithali bezilokhu zithatha indawo yokugcinwa kwemibhalo emincane yangaphambili kanye namakhophi aqinile, futhi lezi zindaba ezimbili zokugcina ziye zafakwa kakhulu kwidijithali ngokuskena izithombe, ngokuvamile ngekhonsathi enokubonwa kohlamvu olubonakalayo.
